[1,i]	vimukta āvaraṇa kleśam dīpta akhila guṇa śriyam sva eka vedya ātma sampattim namasyāmi mahā munim svayam api kṛtinām mahadbhiḥ anyaiḥ api gamitaḥ bahu vistaraiḥ nna yoyam tat api ca sugamaḥ na madvidhānām iti vivṛti chalataḥ karomi cintām aham api na nija eka lābha lubdhaḥ na ca para kṛtya rasa abhilāṣa muktaḥ phalati punar iyam para arthavān śāvratatiḥ abhīṣṭa phalāni puṇya bhājām 
[1,ii_1,iv]	śāstra ādau avidhnena tad samāpti artham bhagavati prasāda janane śrotṛ jana anugraha arthañca stuti pūrvakam ācāryaḥ namaskāraślokam āha vidhūta kalpanā jāla gambhīra udāra mūrtaye namaḥ samantabhadrāya samanta spharaṇa tviṣe vidhūtam vidhvastam anutpattika dharma tām āpāditam kalpanā grāhya grāhaka adhyāropaḥ sā eva jālam bandhana hetu tvāt yāsām tāḥ vidhūta kalpanā jālāḥ etena dharma kāyaḥ uktaḥ dvaya śūnyatāyāḥ dharmadhātu tvāt tad adhigamasya dharma kāya tvāt gambhīrāḥ ca khaḍga śrāvaka ādya viṣaya tvāt udārāḥ ca sakala jñeya satva artha vyāpanāt iti gambhīra udārāḥ ābhyām sa ambhogika nairmmāṇika kāyau uktau tayoḥ eva svarūpa tvāt vidhūta kalpanā jālāḥ gambhīra udārāḥ mūrttayaḥ yasya sa vidhūta kalpanā jāla gambhora udāram arttiḥ etena sva artha sampad uktā trikāya lakṣaṇa tvāt tasyāḥ 
[2,i]	samantam niravaśeṣam bhadram kalyāṇam para artha sampad sambhāra lakṣaṇam yasmāt asau samantabhadraḥ anayā bhagavat nāma vyutpattyā para artha sampad abhihitā samantataḥ spharanti iti samanta spharaṇyaḥ tviṣaḥ tāvat tviṣaḥ deśanā yasya sa samanta spharaṇa tviś vastu tattva avabhāsana upāya tā ca tu iṣ deśanayoḥ sādharmyam anena para artha sampad upāyaḥ darśitaḥ deśanā dvāreṇa bhagavatā jagat artha karaṇāt etena stutiḥ uktāḥ asādhāraṇānām sva para artha sampatti tad upāyānām upadarśanāt sarvatra namaḥ śabda yogāt caturthī anena namaskāra ubhihitaḥ yadā tu samantabhadra śabdaḥ rūḍhyā bodhisattva viśeṣe vartate tadā api pada vyākhyānam pūrvavat eva ayantu viśeṣaḥ vidhūta kalpanā jāla tvam bodhisattva bhūmi āvaraṇa prahāṇataḥ veditavyam gāmbhīryantu khaḍga śrāvakā viṣaya tvāt audāryantu darśa bhūm īśvara bodhisattva māhātmya atiśayataḥ kāyatrayantu bodhisattvānām api asti prakarṣa niṣṭha āgamanāt tu bhagavatām vyavasthāpyate deśanā ca prasiddhā eva teṣām 
[2,ii_2,iii]	śrotṛ doṣa bāhulyāt śāstreṇa para upakāram apaśyan sūkta abhyāsa bhāvita citta tām eva ātmanaḥ śāstra ārambha kāraṇandarśayan vakra uktyā doṣa tāpa nayanena śāstre śrotṛt pravartayitum āha prāyas prākṛta saktiḥ apratibala prajñaḥ janaḥ kevalam na anarthyeva su bhāṣitaiḥ parigatāḥ vidveṣṭi apīrṣya amalaiḥ tena ayam na para upakāraḥ iti naḥ cintā api cetaḥ tatas sūkta abhyāsa vibarddhita vyasanam iti atra anubaddha spṛham 
[2,iv_3,i]	prāyas bhūyān bāhulyena vā janaḥ prākṛteṣu bahis śāstreṣu saktiḥ abhiṣvaṅgaḥ yasya sa prākṛta saktiḥ anena kuprajña tvam śrotṛ doṣaḥ uktaḥ apratibalā śāstra artha grahaṇam pratyaśaktā prajñā yasya asau apratibala prajñaḥ anena ajña tvam uktam kevalam na anarthyeva sūbhāṣitaiḥ kintu su bhāṣita abhidhāyinam īrṣyā para saṃpattau cetasaḥ vyāroṣaḥ sā eva malaḥ citta malinīkaraṇāt taiḥ parigataḥ yuktaḥ san vidveṣṭi api īrṣyā malaiḥ iti vyakti apekṣayā bahuvacanam anena yathākramam anarthi tvam amādhyasthi añca uktam tena śrotṛ doṣa kalā arpena ayam āripsitaḥ vārttika ākhyaḥ granthaḥ param upakaroti iti para upakāraḥ iti naḥ asmākañcintā api na asti kathantarhi śāstra karaṇe pravṛttiḥ iti āha cetaḥ ciram dīrgha kālam sūktasya abhyāsena vivarddhita vyasanam vistārita abhiṣvaṅgam iti hetoḥ atra vārtika karaṇe anubaddha spṛham jāta abhilāṣam etena kuprajña tā ādi doṣa jātam ātmanaḥ bodhitāḥ śrotāraḥ tad parihāreṇa śāstre pravartitāḥ eva bhavanti ayam ācā ryaḥ bṛhat ācāryīya pramāṇa samuccaya śāstre vārttikam cikīrṣuḥ svatas kṛta bhagavat namaskāraḥ tad śāstra ārambha samaye tad ācārya kṛta bhagavat namaskāra ślokam vyākhyātu kāmaḥ prathamam pramāṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇam āha 
[3,ii_3,v^1]	pramāṇam avisaṃvādi jñānam jñānam pramāṇaṃna ajñānam indriya artha sannikarṣa ādi kīdṛśam avisaṃvādi visaṃvādanam visaṃvādaḥ vañjanam tad yogāt visaṃvādi na tathā asau avisaṃvādi avisamvādanam uktam iti arthaḥ kim punar iti āha artha kriyā sthitiḥ avisaṃvādanam yathā upadarśita arthasya kriyāyāḥ sthitiḥ pramāṇa yogya tā avisaṃvādanam atas ca yatas jñānāt artham paricchidya api na pravartate pravṛttaḥ vā kutaścid pratibandha ādeḥ artha kriyāt na adhigacchati tat api pramāṇam eva pramāṇa yogya tā lakṣaṇasya avisaṃvādasya sattvāt sā eva pramāṇa yogya tā katham asatyām artha kriyā prāptau niścīyate iti ced yat tāvat asakṛt vyavahāra abhyāsāt darśana mātreṇa upalakṣita bhrama vivikta svarūpa viśeṣam sādhana adhyakṣam tasya svatas eva pramāṇa yogya tā niścayaḥ kṛtrima akṛtrima m aṇiḥ upyādi tatva niścaya vat aṃnumānasya ca sādhya pratibaddha janmanaḥ 
[3,v^2]	vyabhicāra āśaṅkā virahāt artha kriyā nirbhāsantu pratyakṣam svatas eva artha kriyā anubhava ātmakam na tatra para artha kriyā apekṣyate iti tat api svatas niścita prāmāṇyam atas eva artha kriyā paraṃpara anusaraṇāt anavasthā doṣa upi dusthaḥ eva yat tu a nabhyastad aśāyām saṃdigdha prāmāṇyam utpattau tasya artha kriyā jñānāt anumānāt vā prāmāṇyam niścīyate etat ca avisaṃvādanam bāhya artha itara vādayoḥ samānam pramāṇa lakṣaṇam vi jñāḥ na nayepi sādhana nirbhāsa jñāna anantaram arthaṃkriyā nirbhāsa jñānam eva saṃvādaḥ atas vijñaptimātra tve pramāṇa itara vibhāga vyavahāraḥ asaṃkīrṇṇaḥ 
[4,i_4,iii]	nanu śabda gandha rasa sparśān citra rūpañca paśyataḥ jñānasya param artha kriyā jñānam na asti iti tad pramāṇat na syāt iti āha śābdepi abhiprāya nivedanāt śābde śabda janite jñāne api śabdāt gandha ādi viṣaye api abhiprāyasya abhipreta artha kriyāyāḥ nivedanāt pratipādanāt prāmāṇyam artha kriyā hi kvacid svarūpa pratipattiḥ eva kvacid tatas anyāḥ yathāsambhavam vyavahāra viṣayaḥ tad prāpaṇañca prāmāṇyam iti na avyāpakam pramāṇa lakṣaṇam 
[4,iv_4,vi]	nanu śabdasya artha pratibandha abhāvāt na prāmāṇyam syāt iṣyate ca anumāna tvāt iti āha vaktṛ vyāpāra viṣayaḥ yorthaḥ buddhau prakāśate prāmāṇyam tatra śabdasya na artha tattva nibandhanam vaktṛḥ vyāpāraḥ vivakṣā tasya viṣayaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ samāropita bahī rūpaḥ jñāna ākāraḥ prakāśate buddhau vivakṣā ātmikāyām tatra śabdasya prāmāṇyam liṅga tvam śabdāt uccaritāt vivakṣita artha pratibhāsī vikalponumīyate iti arthaḥ tad kārya tvāt tad śabdasya na punar artha tattva nibandhanam tad pratibandha abhāvāt 
[4,vii_5,ii]	nanu ghaṭoyam iti ādi jñānāt pravartamānasya sambandha usti eva iti tat pramāṇam syāt iti āha gṛhīta grahaṇāt na iṣṭam sāṃvṛtam dhī pramāṇa tā pravṛtteḥ tad pradhāna tvāt heya upādeya vastuni gṛhīta grahaṇāt na iṣṭam sāṃvṛtam darśana uttara kālam sāṃvṛtam vikalpa jñānam pramāṇam na iṣṭam darśana gṛhītasya eva grahaṇāt tena eva ca prāpayitum śakya tvāt sāṃvṛtam akiñcitkaram eva kasmāt punar ddhiyaḥ pramāṇatā iṣyate na indriya ādeḥ heya upādeya vastu viṣayāyāḥ pravṛtteḥ tad pradhāna tvāt jñāna pradhāna tvāt dhiyaḥ eva prāmāṇyam na hi indriyam asti iti eva pravṛttiḥ kintarhi jñāna sadbhavāt sādhakatamañca pramāṇam tasya avyavahita vyāpāra tvāt 
[5,iii_5,v]	evam phala arthinām pravṛtti vyavahāra kāri tvena dhiyaḥ prāmāṇyam pratipāditam sāmpratam adhigama phala vibhāga kāri tvam āha viṣaya ākāra bhedāt ca dhiyodhi gama bhedataḥ dhiyaḥ viṣayasya iva ākāraḥ viṣaya ākāraḥ nīla ādiḥ tasya bhedāt viśeṣāt adhigamasya artha pratīteḥ bhedāt viśeṣāt hiyaḥ eva prāmāṇyam nīla svarūpam hi jñānam nīlapratītiḥ anyādṛśam anyathā iti dhīḥ eva pramāṇam 
[5,vi_5,ix]	nanu yathā adhigama sādhanam ākāraḥ tathā indriyam api tat utpatteḥ atas āha bhāvāt eva asya tad bhāve tasya ākārasya bhāve asya adhigamasya bhāvāt eva sādhanam avyavahita tvāt na tu indriya ādi tad bhāvepi jñāna anutpattau adhi gama abhāvāt kaścid āha sarva jñānānām abādhita tva lakṣaṇam prāmāṇyam svatas eva sidhyate bādha kāraṇa doṣa jñānābhyām kvacid tat apohyate yathā śuktikāyām rajata jñāne candra dvaya darśane vā tat ca idam ayuktam yatas svarūpasya svatas gatiḥ 
[6,i]	svarūpasya svatas gati rna prāmāṇyasya svatas hi prāmāṇyasya abhivyaktiḥ vaktavyā na tu utpattiḥ jñāna ātma bhūtasya svasmāt utpatti virodhāt yadi ca svatas abādhita tvam prāmāṇyam abhivyaktyā vyavasthāpitam na tasya bādhakānām sahasreṇa api bādhaḥ yuktaḥ atha sambhavati bādhake bādhaka adarśanam yatra tatra ābādhita tvam apodyate bādhaka darśanena evantarhi bādhakā darśanāt na ābādhita tvam kintarhi bādhaka abhāvāt tasya ca adarśanāt anyat na sādhanam tad ced asādhanam na ābādhita tvam nāma prāmāṇyam na api asya svatas siddhiḥ atas prathamam bādhaka adarśanāt prasaktam abādhita tvam bādha darśanāt apodyate iti kim atra ayuktam īdṛśaḥ eva bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ sarvatas 
[6,ii]	kīdaśaḥ atra prasaṅga arthaḥ kim sattvam uta sattva niścayau sambhāvanā mātramvā tatra na tāvat anayoḥ pakṣayoḥ apavādaḥ yuktaḥ sataḥ kenacid api bādhitum aśakyatvāt antyepi na svatas abādhita tva niścayaḥ tad viruddha tvāt sambhāvanāyāḥ aniścitam eva tatra ābādhita tvam katham anyathā utpadyate iti ced na tarhi svatas prāmāṇya niścayaḥ iti yatra api bādha darśanam na asti tatra api anāśvāsaḥ eva evañca bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ sat asat tā pa kṣaya uḥ asaṅgataḥ veditavyaḥ 
[6,iii_6,iv^1]	prāmāṇyam vyavahāreṇa yadi svarūpa mātram svatas gamyate na prāmāṇyam kathantarhi tat avagamyam iti āha prāmāṇyam vyavahāreṇa artha kriyā jñānena yasya sādhana jñānasya tādātmyāt anubhūtepi prāmāṇye sa āśaṅkā vyavaharttāraḥ anabhyāsa vaśāt anutpanna anurūpa niścayāḥ tatra artha kriyā jñānena prāmāṇya niścayaḥ anyatra tu vibhrama śaṅkā saṅkocāt utpattau eva svarūpasya prāmāṇyasya svatas gatiḥ iti uktam athavā cakṣuḥ vijñānena rūpakṣaṇaḥ ekaḥ dṛśyate na bhāvī prāpyaḥ na api sparśaḥ tad kayam anya darśanam anya prāptyā pramāṇam evam hi ati prasaṅgaḥ syāt anumānañca vyāpti grahaṇa sāpekṣam vyāptiḥ ca pratyakṣeṇa
[6,iv^2]	puras vartti rūpa mātra grāhiṇā kathaṃśakyagrahā deśa kāla vyakti vyāptyā ca vyāptiḥ ucyate yatra yatra dhūmaḥ tatra tatra agniḥ iti pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha jaḥ ca vikalpaḥ na pramāṇam pramāṇa vyāpāra anukārī tvasā āviṣyate yatra ayam adhyakṣavya apāram atikramya adhikam āropayati tatra na pramāṇam amūlaka tvāt tasya pramāṇa prameyasya vijātīya vyāvṛtteḥ adhyakṣeṇa dṛṣṭa tvāt asti eva mūlam iti ced na sajātīya vyāvṛttyā viśeṣita tvāt tasyāḥ anyathā śābaleyanā śam pratiyatā pratyakṣeṇa go mātra nāśaḥ vyavasthāpyeta anumānāt ca vyāpti grahaṇe anavasthāpattiḥ atas āha svarūpasya svatas gatiḥ 
[7,i_7,ii]	sva rūpa mātram svatas gamyate na prāpya rūpa sāpekṣam prāmāṇyat nāma kiñcid asti kathantarhi tad vyavasthā iti āha prāmāṇyam vyavahāreṇa sāṃvyavahārikasya idam pramāṇasya lakṣaṇam saṃvyavahāraḥ ca bhāvi bhūta rūpa ādi kṣaṇānām ekatvena saṃvāda viṣayonavagītaḥ sarvasya sādhya sādhanayoḥ eka vyakti darśanesamasta tad jātīya tathā tva vyavasthānam samvā dam avadhārayanti vyavaharttāraḥ tad anurodhāt prāmāṇyam vyavasthāpyate tattvataḥ tu sva samvedana mātram apravṛtti nivṛttikam 
[7,iii_7,v]	nanu yatra tāvat abhyasta sādhana jñāna ādiṣu nirasta bhramāḥ vyavahāriṇaḥ teṣām svatas eva prāmāṇya niścayaḥ yat tu a nabhyasta sādhanam jñānam tasya api vyavahāreṇa iti niṣphalam śāstra praṇayanam iti āha śāstram moha nirtanam yadi vyavahārataḥ pramāṇa svarūpa siddhiḥ paraspara virodhīni lakṣaṇa śāstrāṇi na syuḥ tasmāt śāstreṇa lakṣaṇa upadarśanāt tad viṣayaḥ saṃmohaḥ nivartanīyaḥ yena para loka niḥśreyasa ādeḥ vyavahāra aprasiddhasya siddhiḥ bhavati 
[7,vi_8,ii]	tat evam avisamvādanam pramāṇa lakṣaṇa mukta bhidānīm anyat āha ajñāta artha prakāśaḥ vā prakāśanam prakāśaḥ ajñā tasya arthasya prakāśaḥ jñānam tad pramāṇam artha grahaṇena dvi candra ādi jñānasya nirāsaḥ ajñāta grahaṇena sāmvṛtasya avayavi ādi viṣayasya pṛthak gṛhītānām eva rūpa ādīnām ekatvena vikalpanāt smaraṇañca pūrva gṛhīta artha vikalpa rūpa tvāt na adhika grāhi gṛhīte ca prāktanam eva pramāṇam idānīntu smaraṇam apra vartakam tasya eva sandehāt 
[8,iii_8,iv]	nanu avisamvādāt eva ajñāta artha prakāśaḥ jñātavyaḥ anyathā pīta śaṃkha jñānam api pramāṇam syāt tathā ca avisamvādi tvam eva pramāṇam astu kim anena abhi hitena syāt etat yadi sambhavitva mātre lakṣaṇam syāt kim nu uddiṣṭa tvena anyathā jñāna tva sattva ādikam api lakṣaṇam syāt nanu avisamva ādibhyaḥ ajñāta artha prakāśakam jñāyate na tu jñāna tva ādibhyaḥ iti pūrvasya apekṣaṇīyatā lakṣaṇena na tu pareṣām iti viśeṣaḥ yadi evam tadā avisamvādi tvepya jñāta artha prakāśanam apekṣate eva na anyathā sāṃvṛtasya nirāsaḥ śakyaḥ karttum tasmāt ubhayam api paraspara sa apekṣam eva lakṣaṇamba uddhavyam 
[8,v_9,iv]	nanu sva lakṣaṇa pratīteḥ ūrddhvam sāmā nyaviṣayam jñānam ajñāta artha prakāśaka tvāt pramāṇam prāptam tat eva āha svarūpa adhigateḥ param prāptam sāmānya vijñānam pramāṇam iti śeṣaḥ atra āha avijñāte sva lakṣaṇe yat jñānam iti abhiprāyāt ajñāta sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam yat jñānam tad pramāṇam na jñāta viṣayam iti abhiprāyāt na atiprasa ṅgaḥ evantarhi anumānam api sāmānya viṣaya tvāt pramāṇam na syāt na etat asti tat api ca lakṣa ṇam eva anityādi rūpa tayā viṣayīkaroti kim punar adhigata sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam eva pramāṇam iṣṭam sva lakṣaṇa vicārataḥ sva lakṣaṇa vicārataḥ artha kriyā arthibhiḥ sva lakṣaṇa meva pramāṇena anviṣyate tasya eva artha kriyā sādhana tvāt yat eva ca taiḥ anviṣyate tat eva śāstre vicāryate sāṃvyavahārika pramāṇa adhikārāt 
[9,v_10,iii]	yathā ukta dvividha lakṣaṇam uktam yat pramāṇam tadvat pramāṇam bhagavān tadvat bhagavān pramāṇam yathā abhihitasya satya catuṣṭayasya avisamvādanāt tasya eva paraiḥ ajñātasya prakāśanāt ca yadi evam namaskāra śloke pramāṇāya iti eva astu pragāṇa bhūtāya iti kimartham iti āha abhūta vinivṛttaye bhūta unktiḥ bhūta śabda nirdeśaḥ abhūtasya nityasya nivṛtti artha nityam pramāṇam na asti iti arthaḥ sādhana apekṣā tatas yuktām pramāṇa tā tatas sādhana apekṣā pramāṇatā yuktāḥ bhagavataḥ ca prāmāṇya sādhanam vakṣyamāṇam 
[10,iv_10,vii]	nityam pramāṇam na eva asti prāmāṇyāt kasmāt punar nityam pramāṇam na eva asti āha vastunā urtha kriyā kāriṇaḥ sataḥ gateḥ jñānasya prāmāṇyāt na asti nityam pramāṇam atra eva kāraṇam āha vastu saṃgateḥ jñeya anityatayā tasyāḥ adhrauvyāt jñeyasya vastunaḥ artha kriyā kāri tvena anitya tvāt tasyāḥ vastu saṅgateḥ api tad janyāyāa dhrauvyādanitya tvāt 
[10,viii_10,x]	syāt etat anitya viṣayam anityam eva jñānam kevalam yasya tat jñānam sa jñātā nityaḥ bhaviṣyati iti āha krama janmanām nityāt utpatti viśleṣāt apekṣāyāḥ ayogataḥ jñānasya nityāt jñātuḥ utpatteḥ vi śleṣāt nityam hi sadā eka rūpam yadi krama janmanām jñānānām arjana samartham sakṛt eva tāni kuryyāt atha samartham api nityam krami sahakāryi apekṣayā krameṇa karoti tat ayuktam apekṣāyāḥ ayogāt 
[10,xi_11,iv]	kasmāt sahakāri apekṣā na yuktā iti āha kathañcid na upakārya tvāt nityasya sarvadā aviśiṣṭa svabhāvasya paraiḥ saha kāribhiḥ kathañcid na upakārya tvāt kva tad apekṣā tatas sarva jñānāni sakṛt eva kuryyāditya vāryyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ syāḥ detat santāna viśeṣāt nisarga siddhāṃpara aparakṣaṇa ātmakam sādhana apekṣā śūnyam anityam eva pramāṇam bhaviṣyati iti āha anityepya pramāṇa tā anityepi api śabdāt nityepya pramāṇa tā sādhana abhāvaḥ iti arthaḥ 
[11,v]	nanu santi eva sādhanāni yathā sthitvā pravṛtteḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣāt artha kriyā sādhana tvāt kārya tva ādeḥ ca vimati adhikaraṇāni tanu bhuvana karaṇa ādīni upādāna ādi abhijña buddhimat pūrvakāṇi turyya ādi vat prāsāda ādi vat vā asya ādi vat ghaṭa ādi vat ce ti evamādīni sthitvā pravṛtti ādayaḥ turī tantu ādiṣu upādāna ādi abhijña buddhimat pūrvakatva mātreṇa upalabdha vyāpta yodhi karaṇa siddhānta nyāyena nitya vyāpi sarvajña nitya buddhi āśraya ātma viśeṣa viśiṣṭam eva pakṣe sādhyam upanayanti dhūmaḥ iva parvata varttinam dahanam na hi anityena avyāpinā vā nānā deśa kāla kārya jātam śakya kriyam na api sarvasya kāryasya upādāna kāraṇāni asarva vid veditum samarthaḥ na api anityayā buddhyā atīta anāgata kāla vartti vastu jātam jñātum śakyam tad vedanāt ca sarva vid na ca ete hetavaḥ asiddhāḥ dharmiṇi sattva niścayāt na ca viruddhāḥ sa pakṣe sattvāt na anaikāntikāḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ vyāpti niścayāt na ca kāla atyaya apadiṣṭāḥ sādhya sādhana bādhana abhāvāt na api prakaraṇa samāḥ viparyaya sādhaka hetu abhāvāt iti atra āha 
[11,vi_12,i]	sthitvā pravṛttiḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣa artha kriyā ādiṣu iṣṭa siddhiḥ sthitvā pravṛttiḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣa artha kriyā artha kriyā ādiṣu sādhaneṣu upādāna ādi abhijña buddhimat pūrvaka tve sādhye iṣṭa siddhiḥ asmākam vayam api sādhāraṇā sādhāraṇa cetanā lakṣaṇa karma nirmitam jagat vicitram icchāmaḥ tad sādhayatā ca pareṇa sāhāyyakam anuṣṭhitam yena sādhya gatena viśeṣeṇa vinā dharmiṇi liṅgam anupapannam tasya eva adhikaraṇa siddhāntena pratītiḥ yathā parvata varttinaḥ dhūmāt vahneḥ parvata vartti tvasya na hi anya deśa sthena agninā janyamānasya dhūmasya parvata vartti tvam upapadyate na tu evam nitya tva sarvajñatva vyāpi tvā ādi vinā cetanasya tanu bhuvana ādi gatam sthitvā pravṛtti ādikam anupapannam nitya tva ādi viparyaya yoginā api cetanena kriyamāṇam tat ghaṭataḥ eva 
[12,ii]	nanu uktam eva anitya avyāpinaḥ sarva deśa kāla vartti kāryam akāryam asarva vidaḥ ca sarva upādāna ādi abhijña tā na asti ityādinā satyam uktam ayuj tantu uktam karttuḥ eka tva asiddheḥ ekasya karttuḥ aneka deśa kālam kāryam kurvāṇasya tad upādāna ādikam jānān asya nitya tva ādikam antareṇa sthitvā pravṛtti ādi na upapadyate iti syāt api tādṛśasya adhikaraṇa siddhāntena pratipattiḥ anekena api tu nānā deśa kāla varttinā sva sva kāryasya upādāna ādi jānatā kriyamāṇam sthitvā pravṛtti ādi saṅgatam eva atas eva eka tvasya api tatas eva siddhiḥ ayuktā anekasya api hetu tva yogāt pakṣā yoga vyavacchedaḥ eva tu sādhyasya adhikaraṇa siddhāntena sidhyatu na tu tad adhikaḥ vahneḥ iva ca andana tva ādiḥ 
[12,iii]	nanu anekaḥ eva te cetanauvantobhimatāḥ na ca upādāna ādikam tanu ādīnām te jānate na api tad kartṛ tvam ātmanaḥ manyante tat katham amī karttāraḥ atha ādhipatya mātreṇa eṣām karttṛ tvam na tu upakaraṇa ādya ayojanena vyāpāreṇa yathā candrasya candra kānta drutau tena upādāna ādi abhijña tā kartṛ tva abhimānaḥ ca na eṣām evantarhi upādāna ādi abhijña cetana pūrvaka tve sādhye na iṣṭa siddhiḥ vaktavyā yadi evam bhavataḥ eva sūkṣmekṣikā tadā cetanā pūrvakatva mātram sādhaya dṛṣṭānte ca kumbhakāra tva vat sat api upādāna ādi abhijña tvam aprayojakam manyasva 
[12,iv_13,ii]	sat katham pariharttavyam iti ced tat kim kumbhakāra tvam aparihārya aprayojaka tvāt tyajyate iti ced upādāna ādi abhijña tvepi samānam etat upādāna ādikam ajānatā upi buddhim ataḥ anekasya adhiṣṭhāna mātreṇa api kāryyāṇām utpatti yogāt asiddhiḥ vā dṛṣṭānte saṃśayaḥ athavā atha nitya tva ādi viśiṣṭa puruṣa pūrvaka tvam eva sādhyam tadā asiddhiḥ dṛṣṭānte sādhya śūnyaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti arthaḥ na hi kvacid dṛṣṭānte tādṛśam sādhyam upalabdham yena vyāptiḥ pratīyeta asiddha vyāptikaḥ ca hetuḥ anaikāntikaḥ eva sthitvā pravṛtteḥ artha kriyā samartha tvāt iti hetvoḥ saṃśayaḥ athavā anaikāntika tvam tena eva tu abhimata puruṣeṇa na hi asau sthitvā pravartamānaḥ kāryyeṣu artha kriyākārī vā tathā puruṣa adhiṣṭhitaḥ anavasthā prasaṅgāt 
[13,iii_13,v]	siddham yādṛś adhiṣṭhātṛ bhāva abhāva anuvṛttimat sanniveśa ādi athavā yādṛśa buddhimat pūrvakam sanniveśa ādi dṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭam tasya dharmiṇya siddhiḥ iti āha ghaṭe dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sanniveśa ādi yādṛśam pṛthu budhnā udara ādi dṛṣṭa eka vyākti jātyā viśeṣitam adhiṣṭhātuḥ puṃsaḥ anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna vat vyavahāra pragalbha puruṣāṇām tad siddhānta anurodha rahitānām pratyakṣa balena anurūpa niścaya utpādāt siddham niścitam tat yuktam tasmāt yat anumīyate 
[13,vi]	tasmāt sanniveśāt aparatra anupalabdha puruṣa janmani ghaṭe yat buddhimat adhiṣṭhānam anumīyate tat yuktam tasya eva puruṣa kārya tvena niścayāt asanniveśa vyāvṛttam sanniveśa mātram tu sat api na tad kārya tayā pratyakṣam upasthāpayati pratyakṣa vyāpāra vivāde ca paṭu pracārāḥ vyavahāriṇaḥ śaraṇam na hi kaścid vyavahārī ghaṭam puruṣa kṛtam paśyan śarāva ādi parvata ādikam vā tat kṛtam avadhārayati yadā tu śarāva ādīn api tatas udayam āsādayataḥ paśyati tadā tān api tad kṛtān avaiti atas sanniveśa viśeṣaṃpuruṣa kāryam dṛṣṭavataḥ sanniveśa mātrāt tad anumānam ayuktam 
[14,i_14,iii]	etat eva āha vastu bhede prasiddhasya śabda sāmyāt abhedinaḥ na yukta anumitiḥ pāṇḍu dravya ādi vat hutāśane vastu bhede ghaṭe prasiddhasya puruṣa pūrvaka tvasya sanniveśaḥ iti śabda sāmyāt abhedinaḥ sanniveśa mātrāt parvata ādau na yukta anumitiḥ pāṇḍu dravya ādi vat hutāśane yathā pāṇḍu viśeṣasya dhūmasya kāraṇa tvena dṛṣṭe vahnau pāṇḍu śabda sāmyāt abhedinaḥ yatas kutaścid pāṇḍu dravyād dhūma ādeḥ anumānam anucitam atas yat tat buddhimat vyāptam sanniveśāḥ di tad harbhiṇi na asti iti asiddhiḥ hetūnām 
[14,iv_14,vi]	nanu sanniveśa ādi sāmānyāt asanniveśa ādi vyāvṛttyā hetavaḥ bhaviṣyanti iti atas āha anyathā kumbhakāreṇa mṛd vikārasya kasyacid ghaṭa ādeḥ karaṇāt sidhyet valmīkasya api tad kṛtiḥ anyathā yadi sādhya vyāptam viśeṣam tyaktvā sāmānyam liṅgam kriyate tadā kumbhakāreṇa kasyacid ghaṭa ādeḥ mṛd vikārasya karaṇāt valmīkasya api mṛd vikāra tvāt tena kumbhakāreṇa kṛtiḥ karaṇam sidhyeta 
[14,vii]	syāt etat na mṛd vikāra tvam kumbhakāra vyāptam tam antareṇa api valmīkasya utpatteḥ yadi evam buddhimantam antareṇa etat tanu ādi jāyate iti tat api pakṣaḥ na syāt atha pakṣeṇa na vyabhicāraḥ valmīkepyayam nyāyaḥ samānaḥ tasmāt sanniveśa ādi sāmānyam vyāpti asiddheḥ anaikāntikam eva na ca etad kārya samam dūṣaṇam yatas 
[14,viii_14,ix]	sādhyena anugamāt kārye sāmānyena api sādhane sambandhi bhedāt bheda ukti doṣaḥ kārya samaḥ mataḥ sādhyena anitya tvena anugamāt vyāpanāt kārye kṛtaka tve sāmānyena api sādhane kṛte sambadhinoḥ sādhya dharmi dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇoḥ bhedāt sambaddhasya sādhanasya bheda uktyā yadi sādhya dharmi gatam kārya tvam hetuḥ tadā na anvaya siddhiḥ atha dṛṣṭānta gatam tadā asiddhaḥ hetuḥ iti yaḥ doṣaḥ sa kārya samaḥ mataḥ 
[14,x_15,ii]	atra tu sanniveśa ādi sāmānyam na sādhya vyāptam siddham iti viśeṣe asiddha tvam sāmānye ca anaikāntika dūṣaṇam na jāti uttaram nanu sanniveśa ādi śabda vācyaḥ arthaḥ kumbhe buddhimat vyāptaḥ pratītaḥ sa ca tanu ādiṣu api dṛśyate tatas viśeṣe vikalpaḥ na yuktaḥ iti āha jāti antare prasiddhasya śabda sāmānya darśanāt na yuktam sādhanam go tvāt vāc ādīnām viṣāṇi vat 
[15,iii]	jāti antare jāti viśeṣe ghaṭa sanniveśa ādau prasiddhasya sādhyasya buddhimat pūrvaka tvasya tam viśeṣam parityajya śabda sāmānya darśanāt sanniveśa ādi mātreṇa na yuktam sādhanam vāc ādīnām go tvāt go śabda vācya tvāt viṣāṇi vat viṣāṇi tvasya iva na yuktam sādhanam viśiṣṭa jāteḥ eva viṣāṇa vyāpti upalabdheḥ 
[15,iv_15,vi]	kiñca vivakṣā paratantra tvāt na śabdāḥ santi kutra vā tad bhāvāt artha siddhau tu sarvam sarvasya sidhyati vivakṣā paratantra tvāt na śabdāḥ santi kutra vā sarvatra eva santi tasya śabdasya bhāvāt artha siddhau satyām sarva yathāsamīhitam sādhyam sarvasya puṃsaḥ sidhyati uktam īśvara sādhanasya dūṣaṇam 
[15,vii_15,ix]	amum eva nyāyam anyatra api atidiśan āha etena kāpila ādīnām acaitanya ādi cintitam anitya ādeḥ ca caitanya maraṇāt tvac apohataḥ etena śabda sāmānya mātrasya artha śūnyasya ahetutva kathanena yat kāpila ādeḥ bbuddhi sukha ādīnām anitya tva utpattimat tva ādi hetutaḥ acetana tvam iṣṭam tathā digambarāṇām caitanyam tarūṇām sarvasyāḥ tvacaḥ apohataḥ apagateḥ maraṇāt abhimatam tat cintitam veditavyam yathā hi apracyuta prācya rūpasya tirodhānam anitya tvam sāṃkhya syeṣṭam bauddhasya tu niranvaya vināśi tvam tasya yathākramam upādāne prativādya siddha tā vādya siddha tā ca 
[16,i]	nanu ubhayā siddham anitya tvam asti kiñcid ṛte śabda sāmyāt tathā vijñāna indriya āyuḥ nirodha lakṣaṇam maraṇam iṣṭam bauddha siddhānte tasya ca taruṣva siddhiḥ cetana tu asyai va sādhya tvāt na hi asiddheṣu tad nirodhaḥ yuktaḥ śoṣa m ātrantu taruṣu maraṇam upacārāt ucyate yadi ca maraṇa vācya tva mātram hetuḥ tadā taila ādiṣu api tat sattvāt sādhāraṇa anaikāntika tā 
[16,ii_16,iv]	nanu evam kṛtaka tva ādikam api hetu rnna syāt ākāśa guṇaḥ śabdasya dharmaḥ bauddhasya asiddhaḥ anyathā ca anyasya iti atas āha vastu svarūpe asiddhe ayam nyāyaḥ siddhe viśeṣaṇam abādhakam asiddhau api ākāśa āśraya vat dhvaneḥ vastu svarūpe asiddhe ayat nyāyaḥ yathā ukta asiddhi codanā lakṣaṇaḥ vastu svarūpe tu dharmiṇi hetau siddhe viśe ṣaṇam asiddhau api abādhakam kim iva ākāśa āśraya vat dhvaneḥ yathā śabdasya ākāśa guṇa tvam viśeṣaṇam api na bādhakam dharmitāyāḥ kṛtaka tva ādi hetoḥ vā viśeṣaṇa asiddhau api hi śabdaḥ dharmī pratyakṣa siddhaḥ kṛtaka tva ādi ca anumāna siddham tāvatā eva ca sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ nirvirodhaḥ 
[16,v_16,vii]	yatra śabda upya siddhaḥ vastu tu siddham tatra katham iti āha asiddhau api śabdasya siddhe vastuni sidhyati aulūkyasya yathā bauddhena uktam mūrti ādi sādhanam asiddhau api śabdasya siddhe vastuni sādhana abhimate sidhyati sādhyorthaḥ yathā aulūkyasya vai śeṣikasya paramāṇūnām anitya tva sādhana artham bauddhena mūrtti ādi sādhanam uktam śabda asiddhau api sidhyati tathā hi vaiśeṣikasya asarva gatam dravya parimāṇam mūrttiḥ iṣṭā bauddhasya sparśavati sā prasiddhā tatas na ubhaya sampratipannā mūrtti śabda vṛttiḥ vācya bhedāt 
[17,i_17,iii]	śabdasya asiddhau api ca sparśavat tva lakṣaṇa ūrthaḥ dvayoḥ api siddhaḥ saḥ eva hetu tvena abhipretaḥ iti bhavati sādhanamatas ca tasya eva vyabhicāra ādau śabdepya vyabhicāriṇi doṣavat sādhanam jñeyam vastunaḥ vastu siddhitaḥ tasya eva arthasya vyabhicāra ādau ādi śabdāt asiddha tve viparyyaya vyāptau ca śabdepya vyabhicāriṇi doṣavat sādhanam jñeyam kasmāt vastunaḥ hetoḥ vastunaḥ sādhyasya siddhitaḥ evam sādhya vyāpta artha śūnya śabda mātra kāṇi īśvara sādhanāni doṣavanti boddhavyāni 
[17,iv_17,vi]	nanu kim punar īśvarasya bādhakam pramāṇam iti āha yathā tat kāraṇam vastu tathā eva tat akāraṇam yadā tat kāraṇam kena matam na iṣṭam akāraṇam yathā sadṛśena svabhāvena tadī śvara ākhyam vastu kāraṇam iṣṭam sargga avasthāyām tathā eva tena eva svabhāvena sa rggāt prāk tat na kāraṇam kena viśeṣeṇa matam na tu akāraṇam iṣṭam kāraṇa tvam hi akāraka avasthā viśiṣṭa tvena vyāptam tad abhāvāt kāraṇa tva abhāvaḥ 
[17,vii_18,i]	yadi punar akāraka avasthā aviśiṣṭa upīśvaraḥ kāraṇam ucyate tadā śastra auṣadha abhisambandhāt caitrasya vraṇa rohaṇe asambaddhasya kim sthāṇoḥ kāraṇa tvam na kalpyate caitrasya śastra auṣadhayoḥ sambandhāt vraṇe vraṇa rohaṇe ca vṛtte asambaddhasya vyāpāra dvāreṇa apratyāsannasya sthāṇoḥ kim kāraṇa tvam na kalpyate nimittasya samāna tvāt 
[18,ii_18,vii]	nanu akāraṇa avasthātaḥ vyāpāra samāveśāt asti viśeṣaḥ kāraṇavasthāyām iti āha svabhāva bhedena vinā vyāpāropi na yujyate svabhāva bhedena vinā na kevalam kāraka tvam vyāpāropi nirvyāpārasya nityasya na yujyate kiñca nityasya avyatireki tvāt sāmarthyañca duranvayam nityasya avyatireki tvāt sāmarthyañca duranvayam duravagamam na hi asti iti kāraṇam api tu yat abhāvāt kārya abhāvaḥ sa tad kāraṇam anyathā akāśa ādīnām api hetu tva prasaṅgaḥ 
[18,viii_18,x]	api ca yeṣu satsu bhavati eva yat tebhyaḥ anyasya kalpane tad hetu tvena sarvatra hetūnām anavasthitiḥ yeṣu kāraṇeṣu satsu yad kāryam bhavati eva tebhyaḥ kāraṇebhyonyasya padārthasya tad kārya hetu tvena kalpane sarvatra kārya hetūnām anavasthitiḥ prāpnoti aparāpara kalpanayā tasmāt dṛṣṭa sāmarthyāḥ eva kṣiti bīja ādayaḥ kāraṇam aṅkurasya na īśvara ādiḥ adṛṣṭa sāmarthyaḥ 
[18,xi_18,xiii]	nanu kṣiti ādiḥ api akāraka avasthātaḥ na viśiṣṭasva bhāvaḥ kāraṇa avasthāyām aṅkurasya iti āha svabhāva pariṇāmena hetuḥ aṅ kurajanmani bhūmi ādiḥ tasya saṃskāre tad viśeṣasya darśanāt upasarpaṇa pratyayāt adṛṣṭa saha kāriṇaḥ prāpta kārya utpāda anuguṇa atiśayā bhūmi ādiḥ svabhāva pariṇāmena kārya anuguṇa atiśaya tāratamya m uktā apara aparakṣaṇa lakṣaṇena antya avasthā prāptā aṅkura janmani hetuḥ bhavati sa tu pūrva para eka rūpaḥ krama ākramayoḥ artha kriyā virodhāt kutas etat iti ced tasya bhūmi ādeḥ karṣaṇa pāṃsu prakṣepa ādinā saṃskāre tasya aṅakurasya puṣṭatara ādi viśeṣasya darśanāt 
[19,i_19,ii]	yathā viśeṣeṇa vinā viṣaya indriya saṃhatiḥ buddheḥ hetuḥ taṃtha idam ced na tatra api viśeṣataḥ nanu yathā viśeṣeṇa vinā viṣaya indriya saṃhatiḥ akṣepa kriyā dharmiṇī buddheḥ hetuḥ bhavati tathā idam īśvara ādi vastu viśeṣa mvinā sahakāri sannidhānena kāryam karoti iti ced na tatra api viṣaya indriya ādi saṃhatau prāc avasthāvat upasarppaṇa pratyaya janitāt vijñāna janana śaktakṣaṇa prajñā lakṣaṇāt viśeṣāt 
[19,iii_19,v]	anyathā pṛthak pṛthak aśaktānām svabhāva atiśaye asati saṃhatau api asāmarthyam syāt siddhaḥ atiśayaḥ tatas pṛthak pṛthak aśaktānām viṣaya indriyāṇām svabhāva atiśaye asati saṃhatau apya sāmarthyam syāt jñāna arjanam prati svarūpa abhedāt utpadyate ca jñānam siddhotiśayaḥ tatas jñāna utpādāt 
[19,vi_19,vii]	tasmāt pṛthak aśakteṣu yeṣu saṃbhāvyate guṇaḥ saṃhatau hetu tā teṣām na īśvara ādeḥ abhedataḥ tasmāt pṛthak aśakteṣu yeṣu sambhāvyate guṇaḥ svarūpa antara utpāda lakṣaṇam saṃhatau hetu tā teṣām kṣaṇikānām na īśvara ādera bhedataḥ īśvara pradhāna puruṣa ādeḥ akāraka abhinna svarūpa tvāt na hetu tvam iti upasaṃhāraḥ uktam īśvara ādi dūṣaṇam 
[19,viii_20,ii]	bhagavatā upi sādhana abhāvāt aprāmāṇyam para matena āśaṅkate prāmāṇyañca parokṣa artha jñānam tad sādhanasya ca abhāvāt na asti anuṣṭhānam iti kecid pracakṣate prāmāṇyañca parokṣa artha jñānam na sarvasya iṣyate tad sādhanasya abhāvāt anuṣṭhānam kasyacid na asti iti kathan tathāvidha pramāṇa upapattiḥ iti kecid jai mi nī yāḥ pracakṣate 
[20,iii_20,v]	atra āha jñānavān mṛgyate kaścid tad ukta pratipattaye ajña upadeśa karaṇe vipralambhana śaṅkibhiḥ na khalu vyasani tayā pramāṇam anviṣyate prekṣāvadbhiḥ api tu svargga apavarga pradhāna puruṣa artham prepsubhiḥ tad viṣaya jñānavān kaścid anviṣyate tat uktasya upāyasya pratipattaye anuṣṭhāna artham ajña upadeśa karaṇe vipralambhana śaṅkibhiḥ visamvādam sambhāvayadbhiḥ 
[20,vi_20,vii]	tasmāt anuṣṭheya gatam jñānam asya vicāryatām kīṭa saṃkhyā parijñānam tasya naḥ kva upayujyate duḥkha upaśama upāya upadeṣṭuḥ jñānam mṛgyate yatas tasmāt anuṣṭheya gatam saṃsāra duḥkha praśama upāyam jñānam asya pramāṇapuruṣasya vicāryatām anupayogi kīṭa saṃkhyā parijñānantasya upadeṣṭuḥ naḥ asmākam na kvacid puruṣa arthe upayujyate iti na tat vicāryam iti pratijñā pratyupakāra ādi apekṣā samam sarva satveṣu tasmāt yat evam prekṣāvatām anuṣṭheyantadviṣayam upadeṣṭum jñānam upayuktam na anya viṣayam 
[20,viii_20,ix]	heya upādeya tattvasya sa abhyupāyasya vedakaḥ yaḥ pramāṇam asau iṣṭaḥ na tu sarvasya vedakaḥ tasmāt heya tattvasya duḥkha satyasya sa abhyupāyasya samudaya satya anvitasya upādeya tattvasya nirodha satyasya sa abhyupāyasya mārgga satya sahitasya pramāṇa pariśuddhasya yaḥ vedakaḥ sa pramāṇam iṣṭaḥ na tu sarvasya yasya kasyacid vivedakaḥ na khalu sakala jñānāt ārya satya catuṣṭaya deśanā api tu tad jñāna tvāt tad upadeṣṭṛ tayā eva ca prāmāṇyam iṣyate 
[20,x_21,ii]	tat eva āha dūram paśyatu vā mā vā tattvam iṣṭantu paśyatu pramāṇam dūra darśī ced eta gṛdhrān upāsmahe duḥ ram paśyatu vā mā vā drākṣīt tatvam iṣṭantu ārya satya catuṣṭayam paśyati tāvatā eva bhagavān pramāṇam anyathā atattvadarśī api pramāṇam dūra darśī ced iṣyate etāgacchata mumukṣavaḥ gṛdhra an upāsmahe dūra darśinaḥ dīrghaśrutīn ca varāhān iti upahasati uktam abhimatam prāmāṇyam 
[21,iii_22,i]	nanu īdṛśasya pramāṇasya kim sādhanam iti āha sādhanam karuṇā abhyāsāt sā buddheḥ deha saṃśrayāt asiddhā abhyāsaḥ iti ca id na āśraya pratiṣedhataḥ sādhanam karuṇā duḥkha aduḥkha hetoḥ ca samuddharaṇa kāma tā karuṇā sā bhagavataḥ prāmāṇyasya sādhanam sā eva karuṇā iti atas āha abhyāsāt sā gautra viśeṣāt kalyāṇa mitra saṃsarggāt anuśaya darśanāt ca kaścid mahāsattvaḥ kṛpāyām upajāta spṛhaḥ sā dara nirantara aneka janma paramparā prabhava abhyāsena sa ātmībhūta kṛpayā preryamāṇaḥ sarva sattvānām samudaya hā anyā duḥkha hānāya mārga bhāvanayā nirodha prāpaṇāya ca deśanām kartu kāmaḥ svayam asākṣātkṛtasya deśanāyām vipralambha sambhāvanāt catur ārya satyāni sākṣāt karoti iti bhagavati sādhanam kṛpā prāmāṇyasya buddheḥ deha saṃśrayāt asiddhaḥ abhyāsaḥ iti ced buddhiḥ deham āśritā kāryatvāt pradīpam iva prabhā śakti rūpa tvāt vā madyam iva mada śaktiḥ guṇa tvāt vā paṭam iva śukla tā tredhā api āśraya vināśe tasya nāśāt kutas janma antarāṇi katham vā teṣu abhyāsaḥ kṛpā ādeḥ iti cārvākāḥ tat etat na yuktam āśraya pratiṣedhataḥ buddheḥ buddhi rahitaḥ kāyaḥ na āśrayaḥ kāraṇa tvāt guṇi tvāt śaktimat tvāt vā 
[22,ii_22,iv]	tatra kāraṇa tvam pratiṣeddhum āha prāṇa apāna indriya dhiyām dehāt eva na kevalāt sajāti nirapekṣāṇām janma janma parigrahe atiprasaṅgāt prāṇaḥ vāyuḥ ūrdhva ga tad viparītaḥ apānaḥ indriyāṇi cakṣuḥ ādīni dhīḥ buddhiḥ tāsām sa jāti nirapekṣāṇām kāraṇa bhūta pūrva sa jāti prāṇa ādi puñja nirapekṣāṇām dehāt eva kevalāt na janma bhavati kutas iti āha janma parigrahe ati prasaṅgāt yadi mahābhūtebhyaḥ eva kevalebhyaḥ prāṇa ādīnām janma grahaḥ tadā sarvasmāt bhaveyuḥ iti sarvam prāṇi mayam jagat syāt na ca asti etat tasmāt pūrva sajāti sāpekṣāṇām eva akṣa ādīnām dehāt janma iti pūrva janma pratibandha siddhiḥ 
[22,v_22,vii]	bhāvi janma paramparā siddhi artham api āha yat dṛṣṭam pratisandhāna śaktimat kim āsīt tasya yat na asti paścāt yena na sandhimat yad prāṇa apāna ādi madhya avasthāyām prāṇa ādīnām utpādana śakti yuktam dṛṣṭam tasya kim āsīt pratisandhāna kāle adhikam yat paścāt maraṇa kāle na asti yena tad vaikalyāt tadā na sandhimat samagra apratibaddha kāraṇa tvāt pratisandhānam prāptam iti arthaḥ 
[22,viii_23,i]	syāt etat pūrva sajāti hetukam indriya ādi na bhavati kintu deha hetukam eva idam na ca atiprasaṅgaḥ keṣāñcid eva bhūta pariṇāmānām deha ātmakānām tad hetu tvāt anyeṣān ca tad viruddha svabhāvānām ahetu tvāt suvarṇṇa bīja abījapāṣāṇa vat atra āha na sa kaścid pṛthivī ādeḥ aṃśaḥ yatra na jantavaḥ saṃsveda ja ādyāḥ jāyante sarvam bīja ātmakam tatas 
[23,ii]	na sa kaścid pṛthivī ādeḥ aṃśaḥ pradeśaḥ yatra jantavaḥ saṃsveda ja ādyāḥ ādya śabdāt jarāyu jāṇḍaja prabhṛtayaḥ na jāyante tatas sarvam bhūta pariṇati jātam prāṇa ādi janane bīja ātmakam iti na asti bīja viruddha svabhāva tā kasyacid suvarṇṇa asuvarṇṇa bīja tvantu pāṣāṇa ādīnām suvarṇṇa paramāṇūnām eva sat asat tvābhyām iti viṣamaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ 
[23,iii_23,iv]	nanu bhūtamātra hetuka tva aviśeṣepi pariṇāmasya yathā viśeṣaḥ suvarṇṇa paramāṇu maya tva itarābhyān tathā prāṇa ādi hetu tvā hetu tvābhyām api syāt uktam eva atra sarvatra prāṇinām dṛṣṭeḥ sarva tat bīja ātmakam iti na asti eva abīja ātmaka tā kasyacid pariṇāmasya atra api vā tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ yadi bhūtamātra hetukaḥ ayam bīja pariṇāmaḥ sarvaḥ tathā syāt hetu aviśeṣe kārya viśeṣa ayogāt 
[23,v_23,vi]	nanu bhūtāni api avāntara aneka vividha viśeṣa bhāñji vicitrāḥ pariṇatīḥ janayanti iti na samāna tā prasaṅgaḥ na tāvat sa viśeṣaḥ bhūtamātrāt sarvatra prasaṅgāt na ca anyatas anyasya abhāvāt asmākantu karma api sahakāri sammatam tad vaicitryāt vicitram kārya jātam ucitam śakti pakṣam niṣeddhum āha tat sva jāti anapekṣāṇām akṣa ādīnām samudbhave pariṇāmaḥ yathā ekasya syāt sarvasya aviśeṣataḥ 
[23,vii]	tat tasmāt bhūtamātra hetu tvāt sva jāti anapekṣāṇām akṣa ādīnām samudbhave svīkriyamāṇe pariṇāmaḥ yathā ekasya dehasya atad bhūta prāṇa apāna indriya caitanya śakti tayā tathā sarvasya loṣṭa ādeḥ api syāt hetoḥ aviśeṣataḥ atas eva hi prasaṅgāt guṇa pakṣa upi pratikṣiptaḥ boddhavyaḥ tasmāt āśraya tvam api na asti anindriyasya kāyasya kāraṇa tva śaktima tve guṇa tvānām ayogataḥ 
[23,viii_24,iv]	sa indriyopi kāyaḥ buddheḥ āśrayaḥ na yuktaḥ iti vaktum āha pratyekam upaghāte api na indriyāṇām manaḥ mateḥ upaghāta usti indriyāṇām pratyekam yathāsvam pratyayaiḥ upaghāta īpi sati manaḥ mateḥ vikalpa buddheḥ upaghātaḥ paṭu manda tā ādi lakṣaṇaḥ na asti yat hi yat āśritam tad tad vikāre vikriyate yathā ghaṭasya dāha ādau tad śukla tva ādi tasmāt na tad āśritā buddhiḥ viparyayam eva ākhyātum āha bhaṅge asyāḥ teṣām bhaṅgaḥ ca dṛśyate bhaya śoka ādibhiḥ asyāḥ manaḥ buddheḥ bhaṅge vikāre sati teṣām indriyāṇām bhaṅgaḥ vikāraḥ ca dṛśyate 
[24,v_24,vi]	tasmāt sthiti āśrayaḥ buddheḥ buddhim eva samāśritaḥ kaścid nimittam akṣāṇām tasmāt akṣāṇi buddhitaḥ harṣa ādinā ca paripuṣṭiḥ iti vikalpa buddhi vikāra vikāri tvāt indriyāṇi eva tad āśritāni tasmāt buddheḥ sthiteḥ āśrayaḥ samāna jātīyaḥ kaścid na sa indriyaḥ kāyaḥ sa tarhi tad āśritaḥ bhaviṣyati na sa ca buddhim eva samāśritaḥ nimit tañca akṣāṇām tasmāt akṣāṇi buddhitaḥ na buddhiḥ tebhyaḥ 
[24,vii_25,iii]	yādṛśyākṣepikā sā asīt paścāt api astu tādṛśī tatas janma ādau yādṛśī dṛṣṭā atma graha yoginī buddhiḥ ākṣepikā buddhīndriya ādīnām āsīt paścāt api maraṇa avasthāyām api tādṛ śyākṣepikā bhavatu janma antarasya śarīra antara sambaddha buddhīndriya ādi utpādana lakṣaṇasya iti pūrva ukta nigamanam nanu kāya āśrita tvam manasā upyuktam bhagavatā anyonya anuvidhāyi tvam kāya manasoḥ iti vadatā tat katham iti āha tad jñānaiḥ upakārya tvāt uktam kāya āśritam manaḥ tad jñānaiḥ kāya viṣayaiḥ jñānairūpa ādi grāhibhiḥ upakārya tvāt manasaḥ sukha utsāha ādi rūpeṇa uktam bhagavatā kāya āśritam manaḥ vijñānam na sākṣāt tad utpatteḥ 
[25,iv_25,vi]	na nu indriyāṇi vinā na buddhi riti yuktam āśraya tvam eṣām iti āha yadi api akṣaiḥ vinā buddhiḥ nna tāni api tayā vinā tathā api anyonya hetu tvam tatas api anyonya hetuke yadi api akṣaiḥ vinā buddhiḥ na bhavati tāni api akṣāṇi tayā vinā na bhavanti bhūtamātrāt utpatteḥ sarvasmāt utpatti prasaṅgāt iti ukteḥ tathā api anyonya hetu tvam uktam bhavati tata upi anyonya hetuke kāya manasī madhya avasthāvat anāditādṛś pravāhavatī iti siddhaḥ para lokaḥ 
[25,vii_26,i]	kiñca na akramāt kramiṇaḥ bhāvaḥ na api apekṣā aviśeṣiṇaḥ kramāt bhavantī dhīḥ kāyāt kramam tasya api śaṃsati na akramāt kramiṇaḥ kāryasya bhāvaḥ krama rahita tvāt kāraṇasya te nniṣpādyāni kāryāṇi sakṛt jāyeran kramavataḥ sahakāriṇaḥ apekṣya kramāt janayiṣyati iti ced na api aviśeṣiṇaḥ sthira eka rūpasya paraiḥ anādheya viśeṣasya pareṣām sahakāriṇām apekṣā asti tasmāt kramāt bhavantī dhīḥ kāyāt kramantasya api kāyasya śaṃsati 
[26,ii_26,iv]	tatas ca pratikṣaṇam apūrvasya pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ kṣaṇaḥ bhavet tasya hetuḥ atas hetuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ eva astu sarvadā pratikṣaṇam apūrvasya buddhīndriya kāya samudāyasya kāryasya pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ kṣaṇaḥ tādṛśaḥ hetuḥ bhavet atas kāraṇāt anantarasya buddhīndriya ādeḥ hetuḥ madhya avasthāvat dṛṣṭaḥ eva buddhīndriya ādi kalāpaḥ sarvadā aihika janma ādau vāmutrika janma ādau ca astu 
[26,v_26,vii]	nanu yadi sa vijñāna kāya tvāt tathābhūta janana anumānena para loka siddhiḥ tadā maraṇa citta tvāt citta antara apratisandhānam arhat caram acitta vat iti kasmāt na anumīyate iti āha citta antarasya sandhāne kaḥ virodha untya cetasaḥ tadvat api arhataḥ cittam asandhānam kutas matam citta antarasya sandhāne kaḥ virodhaḥ antya cetasaḥ maraṇa cittasya na kaścid tathā hi na tāvat maraṇa cittena citta antara sandhānasya saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇaḥ virodhaḥ nivartti a nivartaka tva abhāvāt na api paraspara parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇaḥ ama raṇa citta vyavacchedena maraṇa cittasya avasthānāt tadvat api arhataḥ cittam asandhānam kutas pramāṇāt matam yena dṛṣṭāntaḥ syāt na hi arhan bhavatāṃsiddhaḥ tad bādhanāya yatnāt 
[26,viii_27,ii]	atha abhyupagamyate tadā tasya kleśa visaṃyoga kṛtam asandhānam na anyathā sa ca na pṛthagjanānām iti kathanteṣām maraṇa cittam asandhānam kleśa visaṃyogaḥ hi pratisandhāna virodhī lakṣyate na maraṇa cittam syāt etat bhavat siddhānta siddham arhat cittam asandhā anantataḥ eva dṛṣṭānta siddhiḥ atra āha asiddhārthaḥ pramāṇena kim siddhāntaḥ anugamyate hetoḥ vaikalyataḥ tat ced kinta devā atra na uditam 
[27,iii]	asiddha arthaḥ aniścita arthaḥ pramāṇena kim siddhāntaḥ anugamyate tad anurodhena para lokasya abhyupagama prasaṅgāt atha hetoḥ āśvāsa praśvāsa indriya pāṭa vā ādeḥ vaikalyataḥ bharaṇa cittasya tad apratisandhānam iti ced kintadeva hetuva eka lya matra apratisandhāne sādhana tve na uditam dṛṣṭānta vikalantu maraṇa cittam uktam āśvāsa ādi hetu tva niṣedhan ca vakṣyati 
[27,iv_27,v]	tat dhīvat grahaṇa prāpteḥ manaḥ jñānam na sa indriyāt jñāna utpādana sāmarthya bhedāt na sakalāt api kāyaḥ ca hetuḥ bhavan sa indriyaḥ vā syāt anindriyaḥ vā sa indriyopi pratyekam indriyaiḥ sahitaḥ samastaiḥ vā tatra prathama pakṣe tasyāḥ indriya dhiyaḥ iva vikalpyamāneṣu rūpa ādiṣu spaṣṭatarasya grahaṇasya prāpteḥ manaḥ jñānam na sa indriyāta kāyāt indriya janyasya spaṣṭa tayā abhra anta jñāna ādiṣu vyāpti dṛṣṭeḥ dvitīya pakṣepya āha pratyekam indriyāṇām rūpa ādi grahaṇa pratiniyata jñāna utpādana sāmarthya bhedāt dṛṣṭāt na sakalāt api indriya kalāpāt pratiniyata viṣaya āgrāhiṇaḥ manaḥ vijñānasya sambhavaḥ eka indriya vaikalyepi anutpāda prasaṅgāt ca 
[27,vi_28,iii]	na api anindriyaḥ hetuḥ iti āha acetana tvāt na anyasmāt acetana tvāt na anyasmāt anindriyāt keśa nakha ādeḥ iva manaḥ jñānam nanu acetana tvam kim indriya jñāna rahita tvam uta manaḥ jñāna vimukta tvam tatra ādyam iṣṭam eva indriyasya abhāve tad jñāna abhāvāt antye sādhya aviśiṣṭa tvam hetoḥ manaḥ jñānasya eva sādhya tvāt ucyate yathā sparśa ādayaḥ sparśa jñānena cetayante na tathā nakha keśa ādayaḥ iti acetanāḥ cetanā pratibaddhañca manaḥ vijñānam tad abhāve na syāt nanu yadi na kāyaḥ āśrayaḥ katham saha sthitiḥ iti atas āha hetu abhedāt saha sthitiḥ akṣa vat rūpa rasa vat artha dvāreṇa vikriyā 
[28,iv]	hetoḥ karmma saṃjñitasya abhedāt eka sāmagrī pratibaddha tvāt saha sthitiḥ na tu āśraya āśrayi bhāvāt akṣa vat rūpa rasavat yathā akṣāṇi rūpa rasa ādayaḥ ca parasparam anāśraya āśrayi bhūtāḥ api ekasāmagrī adhīna tvāt saha sthitimantaḥ nanu yaḥ yat vikāreṇa vikriyate sa tad āśritaḥ yathā cakṣuḥ ādi vikāreṇa vikriyam āṇantat jñānam cakṣuḥ ādi āśritam viṣa śleṣma ādinā kāya vikāre ca vikriyate manaḥ vijñānam atas tat āśritam iti āha tad jñānaiḥ upakārya tva ādinā uktam api artha dvāreṇa vikriyāḥ ālamvyamānāḥ hi śastra prahāra ādayaḥ vikārayanti mānasam na tu āśraya tvena 
[28,v_28,vi]	satta upakāriṇaḥ yasya nityam tad anubandhataḥ sa hetuḥ saptamī tasmāt utpādāt iti ca ucyate na ca upakārakaḥ iti eva āśrayaḥ kintu nirvartakaḥ tat āha yasya sattā nirvartyasya upakāriṇī sa hetuḥ saḥ eva āśrayaḥ katham upakāriṇī nityam tasya nirvartti asya anubandhataḥ anuvartanāt yasya tu kadā cit upakāraka tvam asau viśeṣasya eva hetuḥ na dharmiṇaḥ tad abhāve api tad bhāvāt cittamātra pratibaddhañca cittam tad viśeṣaḥ tu kāya ādi hetukaḥ atas na ayam hetuḥ na ca tat nivṛ ttyā nivṛttiḥ cittasya nitya anubandhi tayā hetu tvam abhipretya ca asmin sati idam bhavati iti saptamī ucyate tasmāt iti ca pañcamī tad hetu anuvaddhām kārya tāñca abhipretya utpādāt iti ca ucyate 
[29,i_29,iii]	nanu hetuḥ upakārakaḥ kathañcid upakurvan dṛśyate ca kadācid dehaḥ cittam atas āha astu upakārakaḥ vā api kadācid citta santateḥ vahni ādi vat ghaṭa ādīnām vinivṛttiḥ na tāvatā astu upakārakaḥ vā api kadācid citta santateḥ dehaḥ vahni ādi vat ghaṭa ādīnām na ca tāvatā upakāraka nivṛttyā upakāryasya nivṛttiḥ na hi vahniḥ ghaṭasya apākam upakāram kurvan api sva nivṛttyā nivartakaḥ 
[29,iv_29,ix]	kiñca anivṛtti prasaṅgaḥ ca dehe tiṣṭhati cetasaḥ anevṛtti prasaṅgaḥ ca dehe tiṣṭhati cetasaḥ sva jāti nirapekṣasya deha mātra hetukasya avikala hetoḥ anutpatti ayogāt tatas yāvat hetuḥ tāvat na maraṇam bhavet prāṇa apānau api citta kāraṇam tayoḥ vaikalyāt maraṇa avasthāyāt na citta utpādaḥ iti ced āha tad bhāva bhāvāt vaśya tvāt prāṇa apanau tatas na tat tasya cittasya bhāve bhāvāt prāṇa apāḥ nau tatas bhavataḥ citta vaśya tvāt ca tatas eva tau na tu tābhyām tat cittam viparyayāt 
[30,i_30,vi]	etat hetu dvaya siddhi artham āha preraṇa ākarṣaṇaḥ vāyoḥ prayatnena vinā kutas bahis antar ca preraṇa ākarṣaṇe vāyoḥ yathākramam prāṇa apānau puruṣasya buddhi lakṣaṇam prayatnamvinā kutas sambhavataḥ tasmāt tad adhīnau kiñca nirhrāsa atiśaya āpatti nirhrāsa atiśayāt tayoḥ yadi prāṇa apāna hetu kañcitam tadā cittasya nirhrāsa atiśaya āpattiḥ apakarṣa utkarṣa āpattiḥ nirhrāsa atiśayāt tayoḥ prāṇa apānayoḥ kāraṇa viśeṣa anukāri tvāt kārya viśeṣasya 
[30,vii_30,ix]	tulyaḥ prasaṅga upi tayoḥ api ca tayoḥ api prāṇa apānayoḥ dehe tiṣṭhati anivṛtti prasaṅgaḥ tulyaḥ tad hetu tvāt tayoḥ tatas maraṇa kāle prāṇa apāna vaikalya abhāvāt cittā nivṛtti prasaṅgaḥ tad avasthaḥ syāt etat citta kāraṇe api citte svīkriyamāṇe maraṇa samaye citta anapāyāt citta utpattau yāvat dehe anivṛtti prasaṅgaḥ iti āha 
[30,x_30,xi]	na tulyam citta kāraṇe sthiti āvedhakam anyat ca yatas kāraṇam iṣyate na tulyam citta kāraṇe caitanye prasañjanam na khalu anuvartakam eva kāraṇam iṣṭam yena nityam tasmin āśraye syāt kintarhi sthiti āvedhakam anyat ca karmma ākhyam kāraṇam yatas iṣyate tasmāt tena karmaṇā yāvat kālam tad dehe sthitiḥ ākṣiptā tatas ūrdhva hetu apāyāt na pravartate deha antare tu vartate iti asamāna tvam 
[31,i_31,ii]	na doṣaiḥ viguṇaḥ dohaḥ hetuḥ varti ādi vat yadi mṛte śamīkṛte doṣe punar ujjīvanam bhavet dauṣaiḥ vāta ādibhiḥ viguṇīkṛtaḥ dehaḥ na hetuḥ caitanyasya prāṇa apāna ādeḥ ca vartti ādi vat yadi yathā viguṇīkṛtaḥ vartti ādiḥ na dīpasya hetuḥ tadā mṛte śarīre caitanya ādi nāśān mṛtasya śamībhavanti doṣāḥ iti śamīkṛte doṣe vikāra vikāriṇī ārogya lābhāt hetoḥ dehasya punar ujjīvanam prāṇāḥ pānam caitanya utpatti lakṣaṇambha vet 
[31,iii_31,iv]	nivṛtta īpi anale kāṣṭha vikāra avinivṛtti vat tasyāḥ anivṛttiḥ iti ced na cikitsā prayogataḥ nivṛtta īpi anale hetau kāṣṭha vikārasya aṅgārādeḥ anivṛtti vat tasya caitanya ādi nirodhasya anivṛttiḥ nivṛttiḥ na bhavati tad doṣe mṛta śarīrāt nivṛttā ipi iti ced na cikitsā prayogataḥ 
[31,v_31,viii]	syāt etat yadi anivarttyāḥ doṣāṇām vikārāḥ syuḥ dṛśyante ca cikitsyamānāḥ doṣa vikārāḥ jvara ādayaḥ etat eva āha apunarbhāvataḥ kiñcid vikāra jananam kvacid kiñcid viparyayāt agniḥ yathā kāṣṭha suvarṇayoḥ kiñcid vastu kvacid vikārye vikārasya jananam janakamapunarbhāvataḥ yathā vikāryasyā punarbhāvaḥ nirvikāra tvam punar na bhavati yathāgni kāṣṭhe kiñcid eva tad viparyyayāt yathāgni suvarṇṇe 
[31,ix_32,i]	ādyasya alpa upya saṃhāryaḥ pratyāneyaḥ tu yatkṛtaḥ vikāraḥ syāt punarbhāvaḥ tasya hemni khara tva vat tatra ādyasya vikārasya alpa upi vikāraḥ śyāma tā ādikaḥ asaṃhāryaḥ anivartanīyaḥ pratyāneyaḥ nivartanīyaḥ tu yad kṛtaḥ vikāraḥ tasya vikāryasya punarbhāvaḥ syāt vikāra nivṛttyā pūrva avasthāpattiḥ vahni kṛte drava tve nivṛtte hemni khara tva vat dṛḍha tvam iva 
[32,ii_32,iv]	nanu yadi nivartanīyaḥ doṣa vikāraḥ tadā na kaścid asādhyaḥ vidhiḥ syāt iti āha durlabha tvāt samādhātuḥ asādhyam kiñcid īritam āyuḥ kṣayāt vā doṣe tu kevale na asti asādhya tā yat kiñcit asādhyam vyādhi jātam uktam tad samādhātuḥ sadyas doṣa śamana auṣadha rasāyana ādeḥ durlabha tvāt karmmā ākṣiptasya āyuṣaḥ tad śarīra sahacara caitanya ādi sthiti hetoḥ vā kṣayāt bhūta mātra vādinaḥ kevale doṣe tu svīkriyamāṇe na asti asādhya tā kasyacid vyādheḥ bhūtamātra ārabdhasya doṣasya cikitsā dṛṣṭeḥ viśeṣa kāriṇaḥ ca hetoḥ abhāvāt 
[32,v_32,vii]	tathā mṛte viṣa ādi saṃhārāt tad daṃśa chedataḥ api vā vikāra hetoḥ vigame sa na ucchvasiti kim punar viṣa ādinā mṛte prāṇini sati daṃśa sthāne viṣa ādeḥ saṃhārāt saṃgaṇanāt tasya daṃśa sthānasya ccheda topi vā vikāra hetoḥ maraṇa hetoḥ viṣa ādeḥ vigamāt sa mṛtaḥ punar na ucchvasiti kasmāt caitanya hetoḥ dehasya vikāra tvāt yuktam ucchvasitum 
[32,viii_32,x]	kiñca upādāna avikāreṇa na upādeyasya vikriyā karttum śakyā avikāreṇa mṛdaḥ kuṇḍādinaḥ yathā yadi apādānam dehaḥ cittasya tadā upādānasya dehasya avikāreṇa vikāram vinā upādeyasya cittasya vikriyā na karttum śakyā syāt yathā kuṇḍa ādi upādāna bhūtāyāḥ mṛdaḥ vikāreṇa vinā kuṇḍādinaḥ vikāraḥ karttu bhaśakyaḥ 
[33,i_33,iii]	kasmāt evam iti āha avikṛtya hi yat vastu yaḥ padārthom vikāryate upādānam na tat tasya yuktam gogavaya ādi vat hiḥ yasmāt avikṛtya yat vastu kiñcid yaḥ padārthaḥ vikāryate upādānan na tat tasya padārthasya yuktam gogavaya ādi vat go ga vayayoḥ iva na upādāna upādeya bhāvaḥ ekasya avikāreṇa aparasya vikārāt 
[33,iv_33,v]	cetaḥ śarīrayoḥ evam tad hetoḥ kārya janmanaḥ cetaḥ śarīrayoḥ evam śarīram avikṛtya eva bhaya śoka ādinā samanantara pratyaya vikāra mātreṇa cetasaḥ vikāra utpatteḥ na upādāna upādeya bhāvaḥ yadi nāma dehaḥ api kathañcid upakārakaḥ cittasya avasthā viśeṣa hetu tvāt tathā api santāna hetu tva abhāvāt na upādānam atas tad nivṛttyā na caitanya nivṛttiḥ avasthā viśeṣaḥ eva nivarteta 
[33,vi_33,viii]	kathantarhi saha avasthānam cetaḥ śarīrayoḥ iti āha sahakārāt saha sthānam agni tāmra drava tva vat tasya cetasaḥ śarīrasya ca hetoḥ pūrva cit takṣaṇasya kalala ādeḥ ca sahakārāt saha kāraṇāt kāryayoḥ citta dehayoḥ janmanaḥ utpādāt tayoḥ saha sthānam bhavati yathā agni tāmra janmanoḥ vahni tāmra drava tvayoḥ saha avasthitiḥ 
[33,ix_33,xi]	nanu dehaḥ cittasya āśrayaḥ tatas saha sthitiḥ syāt iti āha anāśrayāt sat asatoḥ na āśrayaḥ sthiti kāraṇam sataḥ ced āśrayaḥ na asyāḥ sthātuḥ avyatirekataḥ anā śrayāt sat asatoḥ na āśrayaḥ na hi akāraṇam āśrayaḥ atiprasaṅgāt sataḥ ca niṣpanna tvāt na āśrayaḥ kaścid asataḥ api vā kāraṇam kiñcid syāt na tu āśrayaḥ svarūpasya eva abhāvāt sataḥ sthiti kāraṇam āśrayaḥ ced iṣyate na etat api yuktam asyāḥ sthātuḥ avyatirekataḥ na hi sthitiḥ nāma sthātuḥ padārthāt bhinnā yām kurvataḥ āśraya tvam 
[34,i_34,iv]	vyatireke api tad hetuḥ tena bhāvasya kim kṛtam vyatireke api vā svīkriyamāṇe tad hetuḥ āśrayaḥ syāt tena ca āśraya abhimatena bhāvasya sthitimataḥ kim kṛtam yena asau āśrayaḥ syāt etat bhāva sambandhinī sthitiḥ bhāvam sthāpayati tena tad karttuḥ āśraya tvam irti āha avināśa prasaṅgaḥ sa nāśa heta ūḥ mataḥ yadi tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ tatra api 
[34,v_34,vi]	yadi sthityā utpannayā bhāvaḥ sthāpyate tadāna kadācid asya bhāvasya vināśaḥ syāt sa nāśa hetoḥ mudgara ādeḥ matas yadi tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ tatra api nāśaḥ api na tāvat bhāvāt avyatiriktaḥ kriyate tasya utpanna tvāt vyatirikte api nāśe kṛte bhāvaḥ tad avasthaḥ iti prāgvat upalambha ādi prasaṅgaḥ kiñca 
[34,vii_34,viii]	kim punar sthiti hetunā ā na aśaka āgamāt sthānam tatas ced vastu dharma tā nāśāsya yadi nāśa hetunā nāśaḥ kriyate tadā kim punar sthiti hetunā āśrayeṇa yāvat nāśa hetuḥ na āpatati tāvat svayam eva sthāsyati āpatitāt ca tasmāt na eṣa rakṣaṇa kṣamaḥ iti kim anena svīkṛtena ā na aśaka āgamāt hi na aśaka āgamanam yāvat tatas āśrayāt sthānañcet iṣyate evantarhi vastu dharmatā nā śasya 
[35,i_35,iii]	yadi naśvaraḥ bhāvaḥ tad āśrayeṇa nāśa kopa nipātam yāvat sthāpi eta anyathā tu svayam eva sthitimān kim āśrayeṇa satyabādhosau iti kim sthiti hetunā yathā jala ādeḥ ādhāraḥ iti ced tulyam atra ca evam satyabādhaḥ asau iti kim sthiti hetunā vidyamāne vastuni svabhāva tvāt abādhaḥ bādhara hita ūsau nāśaḥ iti kim sthiti hetunā svīkṛtena api yathā jala ādeḥ sataḥ eva ādhāraḥ ghaṭa ādiḥ tathā cittasya dehaḥ iti ced tulyam atra ca prāk uktam sakalam 
[35,iv_35,vi]	kathantarhi ādhāra vyavahāraḥ samarthanīyaḥ ityāḥ ha pratikṣaṇa vināśe hi bhāvānām bhāva santateḥ tathā utpatteḥ sa hetu tvāt āśrayaḥ ayuktam anyathā bhāvānām hi vinaśvara svabhāva tayā pratikṣaṇa vināśe yaḥ bhāvaḥ sahakārī bhavāsantateḥ tathā tādṛśyāḥ sva upādāna deśāyāḥ utpatteḥ nnimittam sa hetu tvāt āśrayaḥ na tu anyathā ayukta tvāt 
[35,vii_35,ix]	evam sāmānyena āśraya āśrayi bhāva dūṣaṇam abhidhāya dravya dūṣaṇa ādau viśeṣe dūṣaṇam vaktum āha syāt ādhāraḥ jala ādīnām gamana pratibandhataḥ agatīnām kimādhāraiḥ guṇa sāmānya karmaṇām syāt ādhāraḥ jala ādīnām prasarpaṇa dharmaṇām gamana pratibandhataḥ kuṇḍādiḥ agatīnām niṣkriya tvāt kimādhāraiḥ guṇi vyakti ādibhiḥ guṇa sāmānya karmaṇām padārthānām 
[36,i_36,ii]	etena samavāyaḥ ca samavāyi ca kāraṇam vyavasthita tvam jāti ādeḥ nirastam anapāśrayāt etena āśraya āśrayi bhāva pratiṣedhena samavāyaḥ ayuta siddhānāmādhārya ādhāra bhūtānām iha iti pratyaya hetuḥ yathā vyakti sāmānyayoḥ samavāyikāraṇañca sva samaveta kārya janakam yathā ātmā ādi buddhi ādīnām vyavasthita tvam jāti ādeḥ kāsucid eva vyaktiṣu go tvam vartate keṣu cit eva ca deha ākāra pariṇateṣu caitanyamityā di nirastam anapāśrayāt āśraya pratiṣedhāt tad mūla tvāt ca āsām vyavasthānām 
[36,iii_36,v]	uktam artham śloka trayeṇa saṃgṛhṇan āha paratas bhāva nāśaḥ ced tasya kim sthiti hetunā sa vinaśyet vinā api anyaiḥ aśaktāḥ sthiti hetavaḥ paratas mudgara ādeḥ bhāvasya anaśvarasya na aśaḥ ced tasya kim sthiti hetunā āśrayeṇa svayam anaśvara tvāt eva na nakṣyati atha naśvara svabhāva ūsau tadā sa vinaśyeta vinā api anyaiḥ nāśa hetubhiḥ aṃśaktāḥ sthiti hetavaḥ bhāvam naśvaram sthāpayitum naśva vara svabhāvasya avaśyam nāśāt 
[36,vi_37,iii]	kiñca sthitimān sa āśrayaḥ sarvaḥ sarva utpattau ca sa āśrayaḥ sthitimān sa āśrayaḥ sarvaḥ bhāvaḥ tatra yaḥ nāma kaścid niti a āśrayaḥ yathā sukha ādiḥ ātma āśritaḥ sarvaḥ sa nityam sthitimān syāt sthāpakasya sadā sthiteḥ kaścid anitya āśrayaḥ yathā śukla tva ādiḥ kārya dravya āśritaḥ sarva utpattau asarvaḥ ca utpadyamānaḥ sa āśrayaḥ iti dravya ādiḥ api sa āśrayaḥ tad āśrayopi kapāla ādiḥ khaṇḍovayaviṣu samavetaḥ te ca anyeṣu iti yāvat paramāṇavaḥ āśraya avadhayaḥ teṣām nitya tvāt tad āśritam dvi aṇukam nityam iti anayā paramparayā guṇa upi nityaḥ sāditya āha tasmāt sarvasya bhāvasya na vināśaḥ kadācana tasmāt sarvasya bhāvasya buddhi ādeḥ śukla ādeḥ ca na vināśaḥ kadācana prāpnoti 
[37,iv_37,vi]	kiñca svayam vinaśvara ātmā ced tasya kaḥ sthāpakaḥ paraḥ svayam na naśvara ātmā ced tasya kaḥ sthāpakaḥ paraḥ svayam vinaśvara ātmā ced bhāvaḥ tasya kaḥ sthāpakaḥ paraḥ āśraya abhimataḥ na kaścid asāmārthyāt svayam na naśvara ātmā ced tasya kaḥ sthāpakaḥ paraḥ svayam avināśi tayā eva sthiteḥ vaiyarthyāt sthāpakasya 
[37,vii_37,ix]	punar citta śarīrayoḥ upādāna upādeya tām niṣeddhum āha buddhi vyāpāra bhedena nirhrāsa atiśayau api prajñā ādeḥ bhavataḥ deha nirhrāsa atiśayau vinā buddhi vyāpāra bhedena na manaḥ jñānasya abhyāsa viśeṣeṇa nirhrāsa atiśayau upacaya apacayau api prajñā āderādi śabdāt maitrī karuṇā vairāgya ādīnām bhavataḥ dehasya nirhrāsa atiśayau vinā tasmāt buddhiḥ eva upādāna kāraṇam tad vikāra vikāri tvāt na dehaḥ viparyayāt 
[37,x_38,iii]	idam dīpa prabhā ādīnām āśritānām na vidyate idam āśraya vikāram vinā api vikāri tvam dīpa prabhā ādīnām āśritānām na vidyate tad vikāra vikāri tvāt atha dehāt api svasthāt prajñā ādeḥ utkarṣaḥ dṛśyate iti tad vikāra vikāri tvam asti eva iti āha syāt tatas api viśeṣaḥ asya na citte anupakāriṇi syāt tatas dehāt api viśeṣaḥ sya prajñā ādeḥ na citte anupakāriṇi cittam hi svastha deha upakṛta saumanasyam abhyāsa viśeṣa vat prajñā ādikam utkarṣayati na guṇepi citte dehaḥ eva 
[38,iv_38,vi]	amum eva nyāyam rāgāt ā āha rāga ādi vṛddhiḥ puṣṭi ādeḥ kadācid sukha duḥkha jā tayoḥ ca dhātu sāmya ādeḥ antar arthasya sannidheḥ yā api rāga ādi vṛddhiḥ puṣṭayādeḥ sā api na sarvadā api tu kadācid prakṛtyāḥ manda rāgasya pratisaṃkhyāna balinaḥ ca puṣṭasya api rāgāvṛddheḥ yadā api bhavati tadā api na kevalāt puṣṭi ādeḥ kintu sukha duḥkha jā sukhāt rāgaḥ duḥkhāt dveṣaḥ iti na citta nirapekṣaḥ rāga ādi hetuḥ dehaḥ tayoḥ ca sukha duḥkhayoḥ ddhātu sāmya ādeḥ antar arthasya anugrāhakasya antar spraṣṭavya viśeṣasya antarasya sparśa jñāna viṣayīkṛtasya sannidheḥ janma sukha duḥkha jñāne api viśiṣṭa viṣaya pūrva jñāna sāpekṣe eva na deha mātra janye iti arthaḥ 
[38,vii_38,viii]	etena sannipāta ādeḥ smṛti bhraṃśa ādayaḥ gatāḥ vikārayati dhīḥ ā iva hi antarartha viśeṣa jā etena antara ukta nyāyena sannipāta ādeḥ ādi grahaṇāt jvara ādeḥ smṛti bhraṃśa ādayaḥ gatāḥ vyākhyātāḥ dhīḥ ā iva hi pūrvikā antarartha viśeṣāt dhātu vaiṣamyāt jātā tad grāhiṇīm citta santatim vikārayati smṛti pramoṣa ādi upahatām karoti 
[38,ix_39,i]	śārdūla śoṇita ādīnām santāna atiśaye kvacid moha ādayaḥ sambhavanti śravaṇa īkṣaṇataḥ yathā yathā śārdū laśoṇita ādīnām yathākramam śravaṇa īkṣaṇataḥ santāna atiśaye kvacid bhīrutame moha ādayaḥ ādi śabdāt bhaya roma harṣa ādayaḥ viṣaya vikṛta buddhi dvāreṇa eva sambhavanti na hi moha ādīnām śārdūla śoṇita ādayaḥ upādānakāraṇāni kintu viṣayāḥ saṃntaḥ paramparayā upakārakāḥ tathā rāga smṛti bhraṃśāt ayopi boddhavyāḥ 
[39,ii_39,iii]	tasmāt svasya eva saṃskāram niyamena anuvartate tat na antarīyakam cittam atas citta samāśritam tasmāt svasya eva saṃskāram niyamena anuvartate tat na antarīyakam cittam eṣitavyam atas cittam āśritam cittam citta saṃskārasya eva anuvartanāt deha saṃskārantu vyabhicarati pratisaṃkhyāna balinām iti uktam 
[39,iv_39,vi]	cetaḥ śarīrayoḥ bheda pakṣeṇa āśraya āśrayi bhāvaḥ ayuktaḥ iti pratipādya śaktipakṣepya bheda ātmake doṣam āha yathā śruta ādi saṃskāraḥ kṛtaḥ cetasi cetasi kālena vyajyate abhedāt syāt dehepi tatas guṇaḥ yathā śruta ādi saṃskāraḥ kṛtaḥ cetasi punar yathā prabodha pratyayam cetasi kālena krama bhāvinā vyajyate tathā abhedāt citta śarīrayoḥ syāt dehepi tatas saṃskāra prabodhakāt pratyayāt guṇaḥ abhivyaktaḥ tatas ca deham paśyatā śruta ādi saṃskāra upi tad ātma bhūtaḥ dṛśyaḥ dṛśyeta tasmāt dehasya āśraya tva pratiṣedhāt tad vināśe citta vināśaḥ na iti janma paramparāsu yuktaḥ kṛpā abhyāsaḥ 
[39,vii_40,i]	katham punar janma parigrahaḥ iti āha ananya satvaneyasya hīna sthāna parigrahaḥ ātma snehavataḥ duḥkha sukha tyāga āpti vāñchayā ananya satvaneyasya īśvara pratiṣedhāt hīna sthāna parigrahaḥ garbhasya āśraya tvena svīkāraḥ ātma snehavataḥ sa tṛṣṇasya duḥkhe sukham iti viparyāsaḥ tasya duḥkha sukhayoḥ yathākramam tyāga āpti vāñchayā sa tṛṣṇaḥ hi duḥkhe sukham iti viparyastaḥ ātmani snigdhaḥ janma ākṣepaka karma vaśāt sukha hetum garbha sthānam manyamānaḥ parigṛhṇāti 
[40,ii_40,iv]	tatas ca duḥkhe viparyāsa matiḥ tṛṣṇā ca ābandha kāraṇam janminaḥ yasya te na staḥ na sa janma adhigacchati duḥkhe viparyāsa matiḥ tṛṣṇā ca ābandha kāraṇam āśleṣa hetuḥ janminaḥ tṛṣṇayā ātma sneha upyākṣiptaḥ hetu vat veditavyaḥ yasya tu unmūlita ātma grahasya te viparyāsaḥ tṛṣṇā ca na staḥ na vidyete na sa janma adhigacchati 
[40,v_40,vi]	gati āgatī na dṛṣṭe ced indriyāṇām apāṭavāt adṛṣṭiḥ manda netrasya tanudhūma āgatiḥ yathā bhāvi janmani atītāt ca janmanaḥ yathākramam gati āgatī na dṛṣṭe ced indriyāṇām apāṭa vāt sāḥ adṛṣṭiḥ adarśanam te sūkṣmasya antarābhava śarīrasya manda netrasya puṃsa stana dhūmasyā gatiḥ adarśanam yathā na hi adṛśyasya adarśanāt abhāvaḥ 
[40,vii_41,i]	nanu mūrttam na mūrttāntaram anupraviśati pratighātāt mūrttañca antara abhava śarīram iti atas āha tanu tvāt mūrtam api tu kiñcid kvacid aśaktimat jala vat sūta vat hemni na adṛṣṭena asat eva vā tanu tvāt mūrttam api tu kiñcid kvacid mūrtte aśakti mat a pratighāta vat jala vat ghaṭe sūta vat hemni jala sūtau hi mūrttau api ghaṭa hemnī bhindantau dṛśyete antarābhava śarīram aśaktimat na dṛṣṭam iti ced nādaṣṭena asat eva vā bhavati tādṛśam antarābhava śarīram 
[41,ii_41,iii]	kiñca śarīram upādānam buddheḥ bhavat ekam avayavi rūpam vā syāt anekam paramāṇu sañcaya svabhāvam vā tatra avayavi rūpam kim avayavāḥ eva hasta ādayaḥ uta tebhyaḥ anyat dvayam api pratiṣeddhum āha pāṇi ādi kampe sarvasya kampa prāpteḥ virodhinaḥ ekasmin karmaṇaḥ ayogāt syāt pṛthak siddhiḥ anyathā 
[41,iv]	pāṇi ādi kampe sarvasya kampa prāpteḥ yadi pāṇi ādayaḥ avayavāḥ eva avayavi eka rūpaḥ tadā pāṇi ādeḥ kampe sati sarvasya pāda ādeḥ api kampaḥ prāpnoti ekasmin tasmin karmaṇaḥ kampasya virodhinaḥ akampasya ayogāt ekantu dravyam tad samavetaḥ ca kampaḥ iti sarvam kampeta avayavānām eka avayavi rūpa tvam hetuḥ para abhyupagama siddhaḥ sarvasya kampa prasaṅgaḥ na ca kamposti iti sādhya abhāvena eka avayavi rūpa tva abhāva prasaṅga viparyayaḥ evam vakṣyamāṇau api prasaṅga tad viparyayau veditavyau atha avayavebhyaḥ bhinnaḥ avayavī atas eva ekasmin avayave kampamāne na avayava antarasya kampaḥ tadā api syāt pṛthak siddhiḥ anyathā avayava avayavinoḥ bhede pṛthakkampamānāt avayavāt akampamānasya āvayavinaḥ samavetasya bhedena tatra eva avayave siddhiḥ syāt vastra udaka vat atra api avayava avayavinoḥ bhedaḥ para abhyupagama siddhaḥ hetuḥ pṛthak siddhiḥ prasajyate sādhya abhāve sādhana abhāvaḥ viparyayaḥ evam vakṣyamāṇau ca prasaṅga viparyayau 
[41,v_42,i]	ekasya ca āvṛtau sarvasya āvṛtiḥ syāt anāvṛtau dṛśyeta rakte ca ekasmin rāgaḥ araktasya vā agatiḥ atha abheda pakṣe ekasya avayavasya āvṛtau sarvasya āvṛtiḥ ca syāt iti prasaṅgaḥ bheda pakṣam āśritya anā ṛtau ca avayavinaḥ svīkriyamāṇa āyām āvṛtaḥ eva avayave anāvṛtaḥ saudṛśyeta iti prasaṅgaḥ atha abheda pakṣe rakte ca ekasmin avayave sarvatra avayave rāgaḥ dṛśyeta iti prasaṅgaḥ bheda pakṣe tu raktaḥ eva avayave araktasya ca avayavinaḥ vā agatiḥ syāt iti prasaṅgaḥ 
[42,ii_42,v]	sarvatra sādhya abhāvena sādhana abhāvaḥ prasaṅga viparyayaḥ tam āha na asti eka samudāyaḥ asmāt aneka tve api pūrvavat na asti ekasmin na asti ekaḥ avayavī samudāyaḥ avayavānām asmāt kampa ādi sādhya abhāvāt avayava avayavinoḥ aneka tvepi pūrvavat abheda pakṣaḥ iva sādhya abhāvena sādhana abhāvaḥ viparyayaḥ aviśeṣāt aṇu tvāt ca na gatiḥ ced na sidhyati aviśeṣaḥ 
[42,vi_42,vii]	atha śarīra ādau pratyakṣa dṛṣṭe dharmiṇi kampā kampa ādi viruddha dharmma adhyāsāt svatantra hetoḥ eka tva pratiṣedhaḥ sādhanīyaḥ iti avayavinaḥ abhāvāt paramāṇu puṃja rūpam śarīra ādi tat api paraspara saṅgama avasthātaḥ puñjā avasthāyām a viśeṣāt viśeṣa abhāvāt aṇu tvāt ca darśana anarha sūkṣma tayā api śarīra ādeḥ na gatiḥ ced na sidhyati aviśeṣaḥ viśiṣṭānām aindriya tvam atas anaṇuḥ 
[42,viii_43,ii]	paraspara asaṅga tebhyaḥ paramāṇubhyaḥ adṛṣṭa saha kāribhyaḥ dṛśyānām eva anyonya saṃhatānām utpatteḥ teṣām viśiṣṭānām aindriya tvam indriya grāhya tvam atas aindriya tvāt anaṇuriṣṭaḥ indriya agocareṣu aṇu tvam prasiddham tat eva tu hetu kṛtam puñjībhūtāḥ tu dṛśyamānāḥ na aṇavaḥ ucyante kintu śarīra ādi vyapadeśyāḥ yathā tantavaḥ paṭa avasthāḥ na tantavaḥ ucyante api tu paṭaḥ iti asiddhau hetū etena āvaraṇa ādīnām abhāvaḥ ca nirākṛtaḥ etena paramāṇūnām pūrva avasthātaḥ viśiṣṭa tva kathanena āvaraṇa ādhāra ādīnām abhāvaḥ paraiḥ asaṃhata avasthāyām iva yaḥ pratipāditataḥ sa ca nirākṛtaḥ boddhavyaḥ kecid paramāṇavaḥ saṃhatāḥ jātāḥ āvaraṇa dhāraṇa ādi kṣamāḥ bhavanti na anye 
[43,iii_43,iv]	katham vā sūta hema ādi miśram tapta upala ādi vā dṛśyam pṛthak aśaktānām akṣa ādīnām gatiḥ katham katham vā sūta hema ādi miśram piṣṭikā avasthāyām tejaḥ paramāṇu sañcaya rūpe tapta upala ādi vā miśram katham dṛśyam vijātīyānām dravya anārambhāt na tad avayavi dravyam paramāṇavaḥ ca tvad mate na dṛśyāḥ iti na teṣām darśanam syāt yadi ca paramāṇavaḥ pṛthak avasthāyām jñāna janane aśaktā iti puñjā avasthā api tathā tadā pṛthak aśaktānām akṣa ādīnām jñāna janane saṃhatau gatiḥ jñānam katham 
[43,v_43,vi]	saṃyogāt ced samānaḥ atra prasaṅgaḥ hema sūtayoḥ dṛśyaḥ saṃyogaḥ iti ced kutas adṛśī āśraye gatiḥ tasmāt anaikāntikam api hetu dvayam na indriya ādeḥ jñāna janma kintu saṃyogāt tadīyāt iti ced samānaḥ atra prasaṅgaḥ yathā pṛthak indriya ādayaḥ saṃyogat na janayanti tathā āmilitāḥ api na janayeyuḥ hema sūtayoḥ dṛśyaḥ saṃyogaḥ dṛśyate iti ced kutas adṛśyāśraye gatiḥ hema sūta paramāṇavaḥ hi saṃyogasya āśrayāḥ teṣām adṛśya tve kathantad āśritasya saṃyogasya darśanam na hi kaścid piśācayoḥ saṃyogam upalabhate kiñca nānā dravya ārabdha pānaka ādiḥ api saṃyogaḥ guṇaḥ eṣitavyaḥ tasmin mṛṣṭam pānakam svarūpam pānakam iti nirguṇa tvāt guṇānām viruddhaḥ 
[43,vii_44,i]	rasa rūpa ādi yogaḥ ca saṃyogaḥ upacārataḥ iṣṭaḥ ced buddhi bhedaḥ astu paṃktiḥ dīrgha iti vā katham nānā guṇi dravyeṣu saṃyogaḥ rasa rūpa ādayaḥ ca samavetāḥ iti ekārtha samavāyāt tad dharmasya pānaka ādiṣu upacārataḥ rasa rūpa ādi yogaḥ iṣṭaḥ ced tarhi kṣīra ādau pānaka ādau ca mukhyā mukhya tvena spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa tayā mṛṣṭa ādi buddheḥ bhedaḥ syāt na hi māṇavake agni buddhiḥ upacāra adagnau iva bhavati paṃktiḥ dīrgha iti vā katham paṃktiṣu samavetā paṅktiḥ saṃkhyā guṇaḥ vā syāt na ca tatra dairdhyam asti nirguṇa tvāt guṇānām na api paṅktiṣu dairdhyam asti yena eka artha samavāyāt upacāraḥ syāt 
[44,ii_44,iv]	etat ca abhyupagamya uktam na tu saṃkhyā ādayaḥ santi tat āha saṃkhyā saṃyoga karma ādeḥ api tadvat svarūpataḥ abhilāpāt ca bhedena rūpam buddhau na bhāsate saṃkhyā saṃyoga karmma ādeḥ ādi śabdāt vibhāga paratva aparatva sāmānya ādeḥ api tadvat svarūpataḥ dravya svabhāvāt bhedena abhilāpāt ca saṃkhyā saṃyogaḥ iti ādikāt buddhau dravya grāhiṇyām rūpam na bhāsate abhāsamānañca dṛśya abhimatam dṛśya anupalabdhayā bādhitam 
[44,v_44,vii]	yadi saṃkhyā ādayaḥ na santi katham ekaḥ ghaṭaḥ saṃyuktaḥ mahān patati ityādi vyapadiśyate artha bheda abhāve paryyāyatā prāpnoti iti atas āha śabda jñāne vikalpena vastu bheda anusāriṇā guṇa ādiṣu iva kalpya arthe naṣṭa ajāteṣu vā yathā śabda jñāne ekaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti ādike kalpyā arthe kalpita arthe vikalpena kīdṛśena vastu bheda anusāriṇā vastunaḥ bhedaḥ vijātīyāt vyāvṛttiḥ tām viṣaya tvena anusaratā guṇa ādiṣu iva yathā paṅkti ādau ekā mahatī gacchati ityādi śabda jñāne na hi tatra saṃkhyā ādayaḥ santi nirguṇa tvāt guṇānām naṣṭa ajāteṣu vā yathā ekaḥ dvau bahavaḥ naṣṭāḥ bhaviṣyanti vā iti śabda jñāna vat naṣṭam ajā tañca svayam eva na asti kim punar tatra saṃkhyā ādayaḥ bhaviṣyanti 
[45,i_45,ii]	mataḥ yadi upacāraḥ atra saḥ iṣṭaḥ yat nibandhanaḥ saḥ eva sarva bhāveṣu hetuḥ kim na iṣyate tayoḥ mataḥ yadi upacārotra guṇa ādiṣu saṃkhyā ādi vyapadeśasya saḥ upacāraḥ iṣṭaḥ yat nibandhanaḥ guṇa ādiṣu saṃkhyā ādi upacārasya hetuḥ yaḥ saḥ eva sarva bhāveṣu hetuḥ kinneṣyate tayoḥ śabda jñānayoḥ yena saṃkhyā ādayaḥ kalpyante pramāṇa bādhitāḥ 
[45,iii_45,iv]	upacāraḥ na sarvatra yadi bhinna viśeṣaṇam mukhyam iti eva ca kutas abhinne abhinna artha tā iti ced upacāraḥ na sarvatra yadi mukhye sati upacāraḥ bhavatina tu sarvatra eva asau bhinna viśeṣaṇam mukhyam yatra bhinnam viśeṣaṇam asti tat mukhyam anyatra upacāraḥ bhinna viśeṣaṇam mukhyam iti etat eva kutas niścitam abhinne abhinna artha tā iti ced 
[45,v_45,vii]	yadi saṃkhyā ādi bhinnam na asti tadā ghaṭaḥ ekaḥ saṃyuktaḥ mahān gacchati iti śabdānām paryāyatā syāt na ca asti anartha antara hetu tvepi a paryāyaḥ sita ādiṣu saṃkhyā ādi yoginaḥ śabdāḥ tatra api artha antaram yadi nanu anartha antara hetu tvepi a paryāyaḥ sita ādi guṇeṣu saṃkhyā ādi yoginaḥ śabdāḥ dṛśyante atra api artha antaram yadi sita ādau saṃkhyā ādi tiṣṭhati tatas tad śabdānām aparyāyatā āpattiḥ 
[46,i_46,ii]	guṇa dravya aviśeṣaḥ syāt bhinnaḥ vyāvṛtti bhedataḥ syāt anartha antara artha tvepya karmā dravya śabda vat evañca sati guṇānām dravya aṇāñcā viśeṣaḥ syāt saṃkīrṇṇa lakṣaṇa tvāt kriyāvat guṇavat samavāyi kāraṇam dravyam iti lakṣaṇasya dvayoḥ api bhāvāt katham punar abhinna artha tvepya paryāya tvam iti āha vijātīyebhyaḥ aneka asaṃyukta ādibhyaḥ vyāvṛtteḥ bhedāt bhinnaḥ pratyayaḥ ca ekaḥ ghaṭaḥ saṃyuktaḥ ghaṭaḥ ityādi akarma dravyam adravyam karma iti śabdau iva bhinnaḥ vyatirikta artha abhāvepi na hi tvad mata īpya karma dravya śabdayoḥ arthaḥ dravya karmabhyām bhinnaḥ vastu bhūta usti 
[46,iii_46,v]	yadi na santi saṃkhyā ādayaḥ katham ghaṭasya ekatvam saṃyogaḥ vā ityādi vyapadeśaḥ iti āha vyatirekī iva yat ca api sūcyate bhāva vācibhiḥ saṃkhyā ādi tadvataḥ śabdaiḥ tad dharma antara bhedakam vyatirekī iva bheda vat iva yat ca api saṃkhyā ādi tadvataḥ dravyāt bhāva vācibhiḥ dravya abhidhāyibhiḥ śabdaiḥ sūcyate ghaṭasya ekatvam ityādi tat sūcyamānam eka tva ādi dharmmāntarasya śukla tva ādeḥ bhedakam yadi api ghaṭa ana eka tva ādayaḥ bhinnāḥ vastutas tathā api ekatva śukla tva ādayaḥ ghaṭāt parasparam ca anuvṛtti ananu vṛttibhyām kalpita bhedāḥ 
[46,vi_46,vii]	śrutiḥ tanmātra jijñā sorana ākṣiptā akhila aparā bhinnam dharmam iva ācaṣṭe yogaḥ aṅgulyā iti kvacid teṣu yadā ekaḥ dharmaḥ pratipitsitaḥ tadā bhedena nirdiṣṭaḥ sa dharma antara pratikṣepakaḥ bhavati ghaṭasya ekatvam ityādi tadā tanmātrasya eka dharma mātra pratipitsoḥ pratipādyasyānrodhena ca tathā saṃketa vaśāt prayuktā śrutiḥ anākṣiptaḥ aviṣayīkṛtaḥ aparokhilaḥ dharmaḥ vyavacchedakam yathāsambhavī yayā sā tādṛśī dharmiṇaḥ dharmma antarebhyaḥ ca bhinnam niṣkṛṣṭa bhiva dharmam ācaṣṭe yathā aṅgulyā yogaḥ iti 
[46,viii_47,i]	yukta aṅgulī iti sarveṣām ākṣepāt dharmi vācinī khyāta eka artha abhidhāne api tathā vihita saṃsthitiḥ yadā tu saḥ eva dharmaḥ dharma antara sambandha yogaḥ jijñāsitaḥ tadā tathā saṃketāt yukta aṅgulī iti śrutiḥ sarveṣām dharmma antarāṇām ākṣepāt dharmi vācinī khyātā ekasya vijātīya vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇasya arthasya abhidhāna ipyayam vibhāgaḥ yuktaḥ yasmāt tena prakāreṇa vihita saṃsthitiḥ kṛta vyavasthā sā śrutiḥ saṃketena 
[47,ii_47,v]	tat evam dharma vācinī api śrutiḥ ddharma antara pratikṣepa apratikṣepābhyām dharma vācinī dharmi vācinī vā iti nirdiṣṭam idānīm samu dāya vācinīm darśayati rūpa ādi śakti bheda anām anākṣepeṇa varttate tad samāna phalā ahetu vyavacchede ghaṭa śrutiḥ ghaṭa vyapadeśa bhājām rūpa ādīnām avāntara raṃjana ādi śakti bheda anām anākṣepeṇa teṣām rūpa ādīnām yat samānam phalam udaka āharaṇa ādi tasya ahetoḥ aśva ādeḥ vyavacchede pratipādye ghaṭa śrutiḥ vartate udaka āharaṇa ādya hetu vyāvṛttim samudāya vācī ghaṭa śabdaḥ āha iti arthaḥ 
[47,vi_47,vii]	atas na rūpam ghaṭaḥ iti eka adhikaraṇa śrutiḥ bhedoyam i īdṛśaḥ jāti samudāya abhidhāyinoḥ atas samudāyā abhidhāyi tvāt na rūpam ghaṭaḥ iti eka adhikaraṇā śrutiḥ rūpa śabdaḥ hi dharma vācī ghaṭa śabdaḥ tu samudāya abhidhāyī katham anayoḥ eka artha tā bhedaḥ ayam īdṛśaḥ jāti samudāya abhidhāyinoḥ ghaṭa tva ghaṭa śabdayoḥ ca jñeyaḥ 
[47,viii_48,i]	samudāya abhidhāyī ca apratikṣipta dharma antaraḥ eva bhavati iti sauvarṇṇaḥ ghaṭaḥ ityādi sāmānādhikaraṇyam sa ca dvividhaḥ aneka vṛttiḥ anyathā ca tathā ghaṭa ādi śabda uvindhya adri śabdaḥ ca yadi rūpa ādayaḥ kevalā na asti avayavī tadā katham ghaṭasya rūpa ādayaḥ iti sambandha iti āha rūpa ādayaḥ ghaṭasya iti tad sāmānya upasarjanāḥ tad śakti bhedāḥ khyāpyante vācyaḥ anyopi diśā anayā 
[48,ii]	rūpa ādayaḥ ghaṭasya iti sambandha vācinyā śrutyā tad sāmānya upasarjanāḥ ghaṭa tva sāmānya viśeṣitāḥ teṣām rūpa ādīnām śakti bhedāḥ rañjana ādayaḥ khyāpyante ghaṭa vyapadeśa viṣaya samudāya antarggatam rañjana kṣama rūpam niṣkṛṣya ucyate iti arthaḥ anyopi candanasya gandhaḥ ityādi vyapadeśaḥ anayā diśā vācyaḥ vistaraḥ tṛtīya paricchedaḥ eva asya tat evam avayavi ādīnām pratiṣedhāt pānaka ādiḥ iva paramāṇu puñja rūpaḥ eva dehaḥ pratyakṣeṇa īkṣyate iti sthitam 
[48,iii_48,v]	na ca asya buddhi hetu tvam yuktam iti prakṛtam anubandham paramāṇūnām samuditānām pratyekam buddhi hetu tva abhāvam vaktum āha hetu tve ca samastānām ekāṅga vikalepi na pratyekam api sāmarthye yugapad bahu sambhavaḥ yadi samastānām deha paramāṇūnām hetu tvam tadā avayava cheda ādinā eka aṅga vikalepi dehe na syāt buddhiḥ na ca etat asti atha pratyekam te samarthāḥ tadā pratyekam api sāmarthye svīkriyamāṇe yugapad bahu sambhavaḥ paramāṇu saṃkhyāni jñānāni yugapad jāyaret sarveṣām pratyekam sāmarthyāt 
[48,vi_48,viii]	atha prāṇa apānābhyām niyāmakābhyām ekam eva jñānam abhivyajyate tatas na yugapad anekā vyaktiḥ iti atas āha na aneka tvasya tulya tvāt prāṇa apānau niyāmakau ekatve api bahu vyaktiḥ tad hetoḥ nitya sannidheḥ tat na paramāṇu sañcaya ātmaka tvena deha vat prāṇa apānayoḥ api aneka tvasya tulya tvāt teṣām pratyekam abhivyañjaka tve yugapad aneka abhivyakti prasaṅgāt eka jñāna abhivyaktau prāṇa apānau niyāmakau na yuktau ekatvepi prāṇasya apānasya ca bahūnām nānā kāla bhāvinām jñānānām yugapad abhivyaktiḥ syāt tasya abhivyakteḥ hetoḥ prāṇa ādeḥ nityam sannidheḥ 
[49,i_49,iii]	na aneka hetuḥ iti ca id na aviśeṣāt kramāt api na eka prāṇepi aneka artha grahaṇāt niyamaḥ tatas yugapanna anekasya abhivyakti hetuḥ prāṇa ādiḥ iti ced na syāt hetuḥ aviśeṣāt kramāt api kiñca ekasmin api prāṇe anekeṣām arthānām grahaṇāt anekābhiḥ bbuddhibhiḥ ekaḥ prāṇaḥ ekām buddhim abhivyanakti iti na ayantataḥ eka prāṇān niyamaḥ 
[49,iv_49,v]	ekayā aneka vijñāne buddhyā astu sakṛt eva tat avirodhāt krameṇa api mā bhūt tad aviśeṣatas ekayā buddhyā aneka vijñāne ca svīkriyamāṇe astu sakṛt eva tat yāvat grahītavya grahaṇam avirodhāt yadi ekasyāḥ aneka grahaṇam virudhyate katicid padārtha grahaṇam api ekadā na syāt na virudhyate ced yāvat grahītavyam gṛhṇīyāt anyathā krameṇa api mā bhūt aneka grahaṇam tat aviśeṣatas buddheḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt 
[49,vi_49,vii]	bahavaḥ kṣaṇikāḥ prāṇāḥ asvajātīya kālikāḥ tādṛśām eva cittānām kalpyante yadi kāraṇam baha vaḥ kṣaṇikāḥ prāṇāḥ asvajātīya kālikāḥ asahabhāvinaḥ tādṛśām eka kṣaṇikānām bahūnām asahabhāvinām cittānām kalpyante yadi kāraṇam 
[50,i_50,ii]	kramavantaḥ katham te syuḥ krama vat hetunā vinā pūrva sva jāti hetu tve na syāt ādyasya sambhavaḥ tadām kramavantaḥ kathante prāṇāḥ syuḥ krama vat hetunā vinā śarīram teṣām hetuḥ tat ca ākramam na ca akramāt krami kāryam yuktam pūrva sva jāti hetu tve na syāt ādyasya prāṇasya sambhavaḥ 
[50,iii_50,v]	na hi para loka āgataḥ prāṇa usti yaḥ ādyasya śarīra sambandhinaḥ hetuḥ syāt etat eva āha tad hetuḥ tādṛśaḥ na asti sati vā akanetāḥ dhruvam prāṇānām bhinna deśa tvāt sakṛt janma dhiyāmatas tad hetuḥ tādṛśaḥ na asti sati ca tat hetau aneka tā dhruvam prāṇānām bhinna deśa tvāt deśa bhedāt prāṇāḥ pratideśam bhinnā atas aneka tvāt prāṇānām pratyekam samarthānām tebhyaḥ vyañcakaḥ aneka tvāt atas dhiyām janma sakṛt syāt iti prasaṅgaḥ 
[50,vi_50,vii]	yadi eka kālikaḥ anekaḥ api eka caitanya kāraṇam ekasya api na vaikalye syāt manda śvasita ādiṣu yadi ekakālikaḥ anekaḥ prāṇa eka caitanya kāraṇam iṣyate tadā ekasya api prāṇasya manda śvasita ādiṣu vā ekaḥ lye sati na syāt caitanyam kāraṇānām asamagra tvāt 
[50,viii_50,ix]	atha hetuḥ yathābhāvam jñāne api syāt viśiṣṭa tā na hi tat tasya kāryam yat yasya bhedāt na bhidyate atha hetuḥ yathābhāvam yathāsambhavam prāṇānām hetu tvam syāt tadā jñānepi syāt viśiṣṭa tā prāṇānām upacaya apacayābhyām jñānam api tādṛśam syāt na hi tat tasya kāryaṃyuktam yat i asya bhedāt na bhidyate 
[50,x_51,v]	tvad matepi dhiyām sakṛt janma kasmāt na bhavati iti āha vijñānam śakti niyamāt ekam ekasya kāraṇam vijñānam śakti niyamāt ekaṃvijñāname kam śakteḥ sva kāraṇa kṛtāyāḥ niyamāt ekasya vijñānasya kāraṇam iti na sakṛt dhiyām janma kutas evat iti ced āha anya artha āsakti viguṇe jñāne na artha antara āgrahāt anyasmin arthe āsaktyā punar punar pravṛti ātmikayā viguṇe viṣaya antara sañcāri jñāna utpāda virodhāni jñāne pūrvake sati viṣaya antarasya agrahaṇāt aviguṇe tu grahaṇāt tasmāt jñāna kāryam jñānam tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt 
[51,vi_51,vii]	śarīrāt sakṛt utpannā dhīḥ sva jātyā niyamyate paratas ced samarthasya dehasya viratiḥ kutas atha śarīrā tsakṛt prathamam utpannā dhīḥ sva jātyā niyamyate paratas ekasyāḥ buddheḥ ekā buddhiḥ bhavati iti na sakṛt janma prasaṅgaḥ nanu buddhi janane prathamam samarthasya dehasya paścāt viratiḥ tad jananāt kutas yena buddhiḥ nniyāmikā syāt paratas 
[51,viii_51,ix]	anāśrayāt nivṛtte syāt śarīre cetasaḥ sthitiḥ kevalasya iti ced citta santāna sthiti kāraṇam nanu yadi buddheḥ na dehaḥ āśrayaḥ tadā anāśrayāt āśraya abhāvāt nivṛtte śarīre kevalasya cetasaḥ sthitiḥ syāt iti ced syāt etat śarīreṇa saha citta santānasya sthiti kāraṇam dṛṣṭaṃsa hāyam yat karma
[51,x_52,iii]	tad hetu vṛtti lābhāya na aṅga tām yadi gacchati tat yadi tasya pāralaukikasya dehasya hetuḥ aihikam antyam pañcāyatanam tasya vṛttiḥ pāralaukika deha janana ādi a abhimukhyam tasya lābhāya prāptaye aṅga tām sahakāritām na gacchati tadā kevalam cittam tiṣṭhati yathā virūpe dhātau kaḥ punar āmutrika deha hetuḥ yasya cittam sahakārī iti āha hetuḥ deha antara utpattau pañcāyatanam aihikam hetuḥ deha antara utpattau pañca āyatanam pañca indriyāṇi aihikam idam janma bhavam 
[52,iv_52,v]	tad aṅga bhāva hetutva niṣedhe anupalambhanam aniścaya karam proktam indriya ādi api śeṣavat yat ca tayoḥ karma aihika pañcāya tanayoḥ yathākramam aṅga bhāva hetu tvayoḥ saha kārita upādāna tvayoḥ niṣedhe karttavye anupalambhanam paraiḥ ucyate tad aniścaya karam anaikāntikam adṛśya viṣaya tvāt proktam indriya ādi api śeṣavat yajapi indriya ādi śarīra antara sambandhi indriya ādi pratisandhātṛ na bhavati indriya tva ādeḥ iti tat api śe ṣa vat anaikāntikam boddhavyam ādi śabdāt prāṇa apāna tva ādi jñāna tva ādi ca 
[52,vi_52,viii]	viruddha tvam api darśayati dṛṣṭā ca śaktiḥ pūrveṣām indriyāṇām sva jātiṣu vikāra darśanāt siddham apara apara janma ca dṛṣṭā ca śaktiḥ pūrveṣām indriyāṇām sva jātiṣu karttavyeṣu madhya avasthāyām tatas indriya ādi tvāt sva jāti pratisandhātṛ tvam eva eṣām yuktam madhya avasthāyāñca pūrva avasthātaḥ pāṭava ādi vikāra darśanāt siddham pratikṣaṇam apara apara janma ca indriya ādīnām iti na adṛṣṭāntaḥ hetuḥ 
[52,ix_53,i]	nanu śarīrāt eva indriya ādīnām janma iti āha śarīrāt yadi tad janma prasaṅgaḥ pūrvavat bhavet cittāt ced tatas eva astu janma deha antarasya ca śarīrāt yadi teṣām indriya ādīnām janma tadā pūrvavat he tutve ca samastānām ityādinā uktaḥ prasaṅgaḥ bhavet cittāt ced indriya citta ādīnām janma śarīrāt janmani doṣa darśanāt iṣyate tadā antya avasthāyām api avikala tvāt cittasya tatas eva astu janma deha antarasya pañcāyatana rūpasya ana gatasya 
[53,ii_53,iii]	tasmāt na hetu vaikalyāt sarveṣām antya cetasām asandhiḥ īdṛśam tena śeṣavat sādhanam matam yatas cittam eva cittasya hetuḥ tṛṣṇā karma sahāyañca pañcāyatanasya tasmāt na hetu vaikalyāt sarveṣām antya cetasām asandhiḥ cittasya pañcāyatanasya ca hetu avaikalyāt kārya utpādasya avaśyambhāvi tvāt tena īdṛśam antya citta tva ādi śeṣavat anaikāntikam sādhanam matam 
[53,iv_53,vi]	tat evam cittamātra pratibaddha tvāt citta janmanaḥ deha nivṛttau api janma paramparā sambhave yuktaḥ kṛpā abhyāsaḥ iti abhyāsāt sā iti samarthitam abhyāsena viśeṣe api laṅghana udaka tāpa vat svabhāva atikramaḥ mā bhūt iti ced nanu abhyāsena viśeṣepi sati alpīyasi svabhāvasya kṛpā ādeḥ tad vipakṣa saṃkīrṇa tvasya atikramaḥ vipakṣa avyavakīrṇṇa svarasa pravṛtta kṛpā ādi maya tā sā ātmībhāvaḥ mā bhūt laṃghana udaka tāpa vat 
[53,vii_53,viii]	na hi puruṣoti artham laṅghane kṛta abhyāsaḥ yojanam arddha yojanam vā laṅghayati na api udakam ekāntam tāpyamānam dahanībhavati kintu prakṛti siddhāt laṅghanāt sparśāt ca viśeṣa mātram bhavati yathā tathā utkarṣa mātram syāt kṛpayā na tu sā ātmībhāvaḥ iti ced atra āha āhitaḥ sa ced punar yatnam apekṣeta yadi syāt ca asthiḥ āśrayaḥ viśeṣaḥ na eva varddheta svabhāvaḥ ca na tādṛśaḥ 
[54,i]	āhitaḥ sa ced viśeṣaḥ ādhāyaka nivṛttau ātma lābhāya punar yatnam apekṣeta na svarasa vāhī syāt laṅghanam yathā abhyastam api punar yatna apekṣayā eva pravartate na svarasa vāhi yadi syāt ca asthiḥ āśrayaḥ udaka tāpa vat kvāthyamānam hi adakam kṣīya te eva iti asthira āśrayaḥ udaka tāpaḥ punar yatna apekṣī ca svarasa vāhi tva abhāvāt tadā viśeṣaḥ na eva varddheta prakarṣa niṣṭhām na gacchet tādṛśaḥ ca viśeṣaḥ na eva svabhāvaḥ prakṛtiḥ viśeṣa vat hetu sannidhāna vyavadhāna sāpekṣa tvāt pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ 
[54,ii_54,iv]	tathā ca tatra upayukta śaktīnām viśeṣa anuttarān prati sādhanānām asāmarthyān nityañcāna āśraya sthiteḥ tatra pūrva dṛṣṭaḥ eva viśeṣe upayukta śaktīnām sādhanānām yatna ādīnām punar api viśeṣa anuttarān pratyasāmarthyāt nityañcāna āśraya sthiteḥ 
[54,v_54,vi]	viśeṣasya asvabhāva tvāt vṛddhau api āhitaḥ yadā na apekṣeta pūnaryatnam yatna unyaḥ syāt viśeṣa kṛt āśraya sthiti abhāvāt tādṛśasya viśeṣasya asvabhāva tvāt vṛddhau api vyavasthita utkarṣa tā eva punar yatna apekṣi tvena asthiḥ āśraya tvena vyavasthita utkarṣatā vyāptā iti arthaḥ yadā tu viśeṣaḥ āhitaḥ na apekṣeta punar yatnam prāk utpannasya ātmanaḥ lābhāya api tu svarasa vāhī bhavati tadā yatnaḥ anyaḥ kriyamāṇaḥ viśeṣa kṛt yathā abhyāsam uttarottara viśeṣa ādhāyī bhavati 
[54,vii_54,viii]	kāṣṭha pārada hema ādeḥ agni ādeḥ iva cetasi abhyāsa jāḥ pravarttante svarasena kṛpā ādayaḥ kāṣṭha pāra deham ādeḥ agni ādeḥ iva yathā agninā hema cāraṇa jāraṇa ādinā puṭapāka ādinā yathākramam kāṣṭhe pārade hemnī va daradāhaḥ rupya rañjana sāmarthya varṇṇikā vṛddhaye āhitāḥ svarasa vāhinyaḥ na punar yatna sāpekṣāḥ teṣu yadā punar vahni ādayaḥ vyāpriyante tadā samadhikam aṅgārāḥ diviśeṣam ādadhati tathā abhyāsa jāḥ kṛpā ādayaḥ punar yatna anapekṣi tvāt sthira āśraya tvāt ca svarasena pravartante 
[55,i_55,ii]	tasmāt sa teṣām utpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ jāyate guṇaḥ tat uttarottaraḥ yatnaḥ viśeṣasya vidhāyakaḥ tasmāt svarasa vāhi tvāt sa teṣām abhyāsavatām puṃsām utpannaḥ guṇaḥ kṛpā ādiḥ svabhāvaḥ jāyate manasaḥ prakṛtiḥ bhavati tat uttarottaraḥ yatnaḥ pūrva pūrva abhyāsāt aparāparaḥ prayatnaḥ viśeṣa kṛt bhavati pūrva prayatna kṛtasya viśeṣasya susthita tvāt ādhikya ādhānam eva aparayatnāt 
[55,iii_55,iv]	yasmāt ca tulya jātīya pūrva bīja pravṛddhayaḥ kṛpā ādi buddhayaḥ tāsām sati abhyāse kutas sthitiḥ yasmāt ca kāraṇāt tulya jātīyāt pūrvasmāt bījāt vāsanā garbha samanantara pratyayāt pravṛddhiḥ utkarṣaḥ yāsa antāḥ tathā kṛpā ādi buddhayaḥ tāsām sati abhyāse kutas sthitiḥ vyavasthita utkarṣatā 
[55,v_55,vi]	na ca evam laṃghanāt eva laṃghanam balayatnayoḥ tad hetvoḥ sthita śakti tvāt laṃghanasya sthita ātma tā na ca evam laṃghanāt eva laṃghanam yathā kṛpā ādibhyaḥ eva kṛpā ādayaḥ tathā na laṃghanāt eva laṃghanam api tu bala yatnābhyām bala yatnayoḥ tad hetvoḥ sthita śakti tvāt sāmarthya niyamāt laṃghanasya sthita ātma tā vyavasthita utkarṣatā bhavati 
[55,vii_55,ix]	yadi bala yatnābhyām eva laṃghanam na svabhāva jātīyāt tadā abhyāsāt prāk api tāvat parimāṇam syāt iti āha tasya ādau deha vaiguṇyāt paścāt vada vilaṃghanam śanais yatnena vaiguṇye niraste sva bale sthitiḥ tasya laṃghayituḥ ādau abhyāsāt pūrvam deha vaiguṇyāt śleṣma ādi kṛta gauravāt paścāt vat abhyāsa anantaram iva avilaṃghanam śanais yatnena vyāyāma ādinā vaiguṇye niraste sva bale sthitiḥ śarīrasya bhavati tena pūrvasmāt laṃghanam viśiṣyate bala anurūpa sthiti kañca
