[55,x_56,ii]	manaḥ guṇāḥ tu sati abhyāse vipakṣān abhyāse ca prakarṣaṃniṣṭām gacchanti tadāhe kṛpā sva bīja prabhavā sva bīja prabhavaiḥ na ced vipakṣaiḥ bādhyate citte prayāti atyanta sātma tām kṛpā sva bīja prabhavā bhūyas abhyasta sva jā tīya saṃskāra vat samanantara pratyaya prasūta artha bīja prabhavaiḥ na ced vipakṣaiḥ dveṣa ādibhiḥ bbādhyate sva utpattyā vyāhanyate citte citta santāne prayāti atyanta sātma tām vipakṣa asaṃkīrṇṇa sātmatām prakṛti tām 
[56,iii_56,iv]	tathā api mūlam abhyāsaḥ pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ parasya tu kṛpā vairāgya bodha ādeḥ citta dharmasya pāṭave tathā hi mūlam kāraṇam abhyāsaḥ pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ parasya uttarasya kṛpā vairāgyabaḥ dhādeḥ citta dharmasya manaḥ guṇasya pāṭave prakarṣe na tu utpattau tasyāḥ sambhavāt 
[56,v_56,vii]	tatas kṛpā ātmaka tvam abhyāsāt ghṛṇauvairāgya rāga vat niṣpanna karuṇa utkarṣa para duḥkha kṣamestiḥ kṛpā ātmaka tvam abhyāsāt bhavati ghṛṇābaiḥ āgya rāga vat yathā abhyāsāt ghṛṇā kvacid viṣaye vairāgyam rāgaḥ ca sā ātmībhavati tat evam abhyāsāt kṛpā prakarṣa viśeṣavatī niṣpadyate iti samarthitarmi yatā ca jagat hita eṣitvañca vyākhyātam kṛpāyāḥ prāmāṇya sādhana tvam 
[56,viii_56,x]	śāstṛ tva vya ākhyānāya dayām darśayitum āha dayāvān duḥkha hāna artham upāyeṣu abhiyujyate parokṣa upeya tad hetoḥ tat ākhyānam hi duṣkaram dayāvān bodhisattvaḥ para duḥkham śamayitu kāmaḥ duḥkha hāna artham ātmanaḥ upāyeṣu duḥkha śamana upāyeṣu abhiyujyate kasmāt punar para duḥkha śamana upāyeṣu yujyate iti āha parokṣaḥ upeyaḥ duḥkha praśamaḥ tad hetuḥ ca mārgaḥ yasya tasya tad ākhyām nam yasmāt duṣkaram 
[57,i_57,iii]	tatra sākṣātkaraṇe parīkṣaṇam aṅgam tat āha yukti āgamābhyām vimṛśan duḥkha hetum parīkṣate tasyānityādi rūpam ca duḥkhasya eva viśeṣaṇaiḥ yu kti āgamābhyām anumāna pravacanābhyām parasparam aviruddhābhyām vimṛśan vicārayan duḥkhasya janmanaḥ hetum parīkṣate mumukṣuḥ tasya duḥkha hetoḥ anitya ādi rūpam ādi śabdāt nivartana yogyatā ādi kañca parīkṣate katham iti āha duḥkhasya eva viśeṣaṇaiḥ kādācitka tva ādibhiḥ 
[57,iv_57,viii]	kasmāt punar duḥkhasya hetoḥ anitya tva ādi parīkṣaṇīyam iti āha yatas tathā sthite hetau nivṛttiḥ na iti paśyati phalasya hetoḥ hāna artham tat vipakṣam parīkṣate yatas tathā sthite hetau nitya tvāt sadāsthite hetau phalasya duḥkhasya nivṛttiḥ na iti paśyati jānāti tasmāt duḥkhasya hetoḥ hāna arthañca tasyāḥ vipakṣam parīkṣate duḥkha hetu biruddham yasya abhyāsāt duḥkha hetuḥ apaiti sādhyate tad vipakṣopi hetoḥ rūpa avabodhataḥ ātma ātmīya graha kṛtaḥ snehaḥ saṃskāra gocaraḥ sādhyate niścīyate tad vipakṣopi hetoḥ rūpa avabodhataḥ jñāte hi he tau tad virodhī boddhum śakyaḥ ātma ātmīya grahābhyām kṛtaḥ snehaḥ saṃskāra gocaraḥ 
[58,i_58,ii]	hetu virodhi nairātmya darśanam tasya bādhakam bahuśas bahudhā upāyam kālena bahunā asya ca adhyātma skandheṣu tad upakārakeṣu ca bāhyeṣu sneha usya hetuḥ duḥkhasya ātmā ātmīya grahavataḥ snigdhasya tṛṣṇayā janma parigrahāt tasya nairātmya darśanam virodhi viparīta ālambana ākāra tvāt bādhakam vipakṣaḥ etam duḥkha hetum tad vipakṣañca āgamāt upaśrutya anumānāt niścitya bahuśas anekaśas bahudhā upāyam aneka prakāram kālena ca bahunā asya bodhisattvasya 
[58,iii_58,v]	gacchanti abhyasyataḥ tatra guṇa doṣāḥ prakāśatām buddheḥ ca pāṭavāt hetoḥ vāsanātaḥ prahīyate abhyasyataḥ bhāvayataḥ tatra duḥkha hetau tad vipakṣe ca guṇa doṣāḥ yathāyogaṃprakāśa tām gacchanti abhyāsa adhīnaḥ hi bhāvyamāna buddhi ākāra viśadībhāvaḥ atas abhyāsāt buddheḥ ca pāṭavāt hetoḥ ātma grahasya tṛṣṇāyāḥ ca vāsanā kāya vāc buddhi vaiguṇya hetutaḥ śakti leśaḥ prahī yate niḥśeṣam apaiti 
[58,vi_58,x]	para artha vṛtteḥ khaṅga ādeḥ viśeṣaḥ ayam mahā muneḥ ayam eva vāsanāhā ni lakṣaṇaḥ khaṅgaḥ pratyekabuddhaḥ ādiḥ yasya śrāvakasya tasmāt sakāśāt mahā muneḥ samyaksambuddhasya viśeṣaḥ sva artha sampatteḥ nanu evam upāya abhyāsaḥ darśitaḥ na śāstṛ tvam tasya upadeṣṭṭha tvāt iti āha upāya abhyāsaḥ eva ayam tādarthyāt śāsanam matam upāya abhyāsaḥ eva ayam śāsanam matam tādarthyāt śāsana artha tvāt kāraṇe kārya upacārāt 
[59,i_59,vi]	niṣpatteḥ prathamam bhāvāt hetuḥ uktam idam dvayam sugatattvasya phalasya niṣpatteḥ prathamam bhāvāt tāvat etat dvayam hi hita eṣi tvam śāstṛ tvam hetuḥ uktam hetu avasthāyāḥ abhidhānāt sugata tvam vyāci khyāsurāha hetoḥ prahāṇam triguṇam sugata tvam aniśrayāt hetoḥ samudāyasya prahāṇam nirodhaḥ sugata tvam tat ca triguṇam guṇatraya yuktam su śabdasya trividhaḥ arthaḥ praśasta tā surūpa vat apunarāvṛttiḥ anaṣṭa jvara vat niḥśeṣa tā ca apūrṇṇa ghaṭa vat tatra praśastam bhagavān jñātavān sugataḥ iti praśasta artham āha aniḥśrayāt anāśrayaṇāt 
[59,vii_59,xi]	duḥkhasya śastam nairātmya dṛṣṭeḥ ca yuktitaḥ api vā duḥkhasya śastam sugata tvam tat punar duḥkhān āśrayaṇam nairātmya dṛṣṭeḥ ātma darśī hi ātmani snihyan tad duḥkha sukha parihāra prāpti icchayā janma duḥkha rūpam ādatte prahīṇa ātma darśanaḥ tu na etādṛśaḥ iti prahīṇa duḥkha upāyaḥ yuktitopi vā yukti paridṛṣṭena upāyena vā gamanāt tad suga tattvam praśastam athavā apunarāvṛttyā gamanam sugata tvam tat ākhyātum āha punarāvṛttiḥ iti uktau janma doṣa samudbhavau janmanaḥ rāga ādeḥ ca doṣasya samudbhavau punar punar āvartanāt punarāvṛttiḥ iti uktau
[59,xii_60,ii]	ātma darśana bījasya hānāda punarāgamaḥ tad bhūta bhinna ātma tayā nairātmya bhāvanā sātmye tu ātma darśanasya janma prabandha bījasya hānāda punar āgamaḥ apunarāvṛttiḥ tat punar ātma darśana bījasya hānam bhūtā tsatyāt nairātmyāt bhinna ātma tayā anya tvāt na hi sa ātmībhūta pratipakṣasya vipakṣa bīja sambhavaḥ niḥśeṣam va āgamanāt sugata tvam tat āha śeṣam akleśa nirjvaram kāya vāc buddhi vaiguṇyam mārgoṃktyapaṭu tā api vā aśeṣa hānam abhyāsāt 
[60,iii]	kāya vaiguṇyam acā apalepī utplutya gamana ādi vāc vaiguṇyam māna abhāvepi vṛṣalī vāda ādi buddhi vaiguṇyam nitya asamādhānāt avyākṛta citta avasthānam etat trayam śeṣam sakala kleśa upakleśa praśamāt akleśam nirjvarañcā doṣa mūla tvāt mārggasya kṣaṇika nairātmya bhāvana ādeḥ uktau apaṭutā api vā śeṣam tad parityāgāt aśeṣa hānam abhyāsāt iti niḥśeṣa gamanāt sugata tvam 
[60,iv_60,viii]	darśitam triguṇam sugata tvam tat evam sarvajñasya sambhava anumānam pratipādya tat bādhakam dūṣayitum āha ukti ādeḥ doṣa saṃkṣayaḥ na iti eke vyatirekosya saṃdigdhaḥ vyabhita cāryataḥ akṣayitvam ca doṣāṇām nitya tvāt anupāyataḥ eke jaiminīyāḥ ukti ādeḥ hetoḥ rathyā puruṣa vat rāga ādi doṣa saṃkṣayaḥ kasyacid na asti iti āhuḥ vyatirekaḥ vipakṣāt vyāvṛttiḥ asya vaktṛ tva ādi hetoḥ saṃdigdhaḥ atas vyabhicārya naikānti koyam iti vistarataḥ vipañcayiṣyate kiñca akṣayitvam doṣāṇām yaḥ manyate sa nitya tvāt vā akāśavatanupāyate upāya abhāvāt vā naṣṭasya punar unmajjana vat 
[60,ix_61,ii]	eṣām trayāṇām api hetūnām asiddha tvam darśayati upāyasya aparijñānāt api vā parikalpayet hetumat tvāt viruddhasya hetoḥ abhyāsataḥ kṣayāt t upāyasya aparijñānāt vā mūrkhasya śabda jñāna vat pari kalpayet hetumat tvāt viruddhasya hetumat tvāt doṣāṇām anitya tvam tatas asiddham nitya tvam doṣāṇām hetoḥ ātma darśanasya viruddhasya nairātmyasya abhyāsataḥ kṣayāt upāya abhāva upya siddhaḥ 
[61,iii_61,iv]	hetu svabhāva jñānena tat jñānam api sādhyate hetoḥ ātma darśanasya svabhāva jñānena tat jñānam api tad nivṛtti upāyasya tad viparyaya rūpasya jñānañca sādhyate yathā dāne jñāte tad viparyaya rūpa tvāt mātsaryasya tad vipakṣatā avasīyate iti tṛtīya upya siddhaḥ pratyuktam sarvajñasya bādhanam 
[61,v_61,vii]	tāyi tvam vyākhyātum āha tāyaḥ sva dṛṣṭa mārga uktiḥ vaiphalyāt vakti na anṛtam duḥkha hetu nivartaka tvena svayam dṛṣṭasya mārggasya ukteḥ deśanā tāyaḥ kāraṇe kārya upacārāt tayā hi sattvān tāyate tad yogāt tāyi tvam sa ca vaiphalyāt vakti na anṛtam ātma sukha ādi abhilāṣa ādinā kaścid asatyam vadati ajñānāt vā prahīṇa ātma darśanasya sākṣātkṛta tattvasya tat ubhayam na asti 
[61,viii_62,iii]	viśeṣataḥ satya abhidhāna hetuḥ eva kṛpā asti iti āha dayālu tvāt parārthañca sarva ārambha abhiyogataḥ tasmāt pramāṇam dayālu tvāt ca parārthañca sarvasya mārgga abhyāsa ādeḥ ārambhe abhiyogataḥ para artham eva uddiśya bhagavān abhisaṃbuddhaḥ kathantasya mithyā abhidhānena sattva vañcana āśaṅkā api tasmāt tāyi tvāt pramāṇam bhagavān yathā dṛṣṭa artha pravaktṛ tvam hi samvādi tvam eva iti prathama pramāṇa lakṣaṇa yogāt prāmāṇyam anena uktam dvitīya lakṣaṇa yogam api āha tāyaḥ vā catur satya prakāśanam tāyaḥ vā catur satya prakāśanam paraiḥ ajñātasya satya catuṣṭayasya prakāśanam vā tāyaḥ tad yogāt tāyī pramāṇam bhagavān uktaḥ 
[62,iv_62,ix]	ārya satyeṣu duḥkham āha duḥkham saṃsāriṇaḥ skandhāḥ rūpa vedanā saṃjñā saṃskāra vijñāna ākhyāḥ pañca skandhāḥ janma maraṇa prabandhaḥ saṃsāraḥ tadvantaḥ duḥkham tisṛbhiḥ duḥ khatābhiḥ nanu yadi skandhāḥ eva pratītyasamutpannā na tu kaścid sattvaḥ yaḥ saṃsarati tadā rāga ādayaḥ yādṛcchikā ahetavaḥ syuḥ iti āha rāga ādeḥ pāṭava īkṣaṇāt abhyāsāt na yadṛcchātaḥ ahetoḥ janma virodhataḥ abhyāsāt rāga ādeḥ pāṭavasya īkṣaṇāt abhyāsāt eva te bhavanti na tu yadṛcchātaḥ na hi akāraṇāt viśeṣa sambhavaḥ na api ahetukā rāga ādayaḥ ahetoḥ heturahitasya janma virodhataḥ na hi ākāśam kadācid jāyate 
[62,x_63,ii]	syāt etat vāta prakṛtiḥ mohavān pitta prakṛtiḥ dveṣavān śleṣma prakṛtiḥ rāgavān iti vāta ādi dharmaḥ doṣa gaṇaḥ iti āha vyabhicārāt na vāta ādi dharmaḥ prakṛti saṃkarāt adoṣaḥ ca tad anyaḥ api dharmaḥ kim tasya na īkṣyate na vyabhicārāt vāta ādi dharmaḥ rāga ādiḥ vāta prakṛtiḥ api na moha bahulaḥ pitta prakṛtiḥ api na paṭu dveṣaḥ śleṣma prakṛtiḥ ca na udbhūta rāga viśeṣaḥ kaścid dṛśyate iti vāta ādi vyabhicāriṇaḥ moha ādayaḥ na tad hetavaḥ prakṛti saṃkārāt adoṣaḥ ced saṃkīrṇṇa prakṛtayaḥ hi puruṣāḥ pratyekam vāta pitta śleṣmaṇām sattvāt atas doṣāṇām na kāraṇa vyabhicāraḥ yadi evam tasyādveṣa ādeḥ anyaḥ dharmaḥ khara tva ādiḥtasya vāta ādeḥ kinnekṣyate 
[63,iii_63,v]	atha pratyekam sarveṣām rāgādiḥ dharmaḥ tatas na vyabhicāraḥ iti āha na sarva dharmaḥ sarveṣām sama rāga prasaṅgataḥ rūpa ādi vat adoṣaḥ ceta tulyam tatra api codanam na sarva dharmaḥ sarveṣām samasya rāgasya prasaṅgāt nānā prakṛtika tvepi rāga ādi hetoḥ samāna tvāt rūpa ādi vat adoṣaḥ ced yathā bhūtamātra hetuka tvepi rūpa ādayaḥ utkṛṣyante ayakṛṣyante ca kvacid tathā rāgādayopī iti ced tulyam tatra rūpa ādau api codanam samatvasya 
[63,vi_64,i]	ādhipatyam viśiṣṭānām yadi tatra na karmaṇām ādhipatyam viśiṣṭānām karmaṇām śruta aśruta lakṣaṇānām yadi tatra rūpa ādau kārye na iṣyate bhūta sahakāriṇām karmaṇām vaiśiṣṭyāt rūpa ādi viśeṣaḥ iti arthaḥ syāt etat na doṣa mātrāt rāga ādayaḥ api tu teṣām pariṇāma viśeṣāt yathā vyādhayaḥ tatas na samara āgata ādi prasaṅgaḥ iti āha viśeṣepi ca doṣāṇām aviśeṣāt viśeṣepi ce doṣāṇām prakopa ādinā aviśeṣāt rāga ādīnām na doṣa pariṇāma hetu tā 
[64,ii_64,iv]	nanu aviśeṣa āditya siddhaḥ hetuḥ kapha ādi utkarṣe rāga ādi utkarṣa dṛṣṭa īrityāḥ ha asiddha tā na vikārāt vikāreṇa sarveṣām na ca sarvajāḥ na asiddha tā aviśeṣasya tathā hi sarveṣām kapha ādīnām vikāreṇa utkarṣeṇa pīḍayā vikārāt dveṣaḥ bhavati na rāga ādayaḥ sarvaja tvāt adoṣaḥ iti ced na ca sarvajāḥ samara āgata ādi prasaṅgāt iti ukteḥ 
[64,v_64,viii]	kiñca kāraṇe varddhamāne ca kārya hāniḥ na yujyate tāpa ādiṣu iva sannipāta avasthāyām kāraṇe kapha ādike varddhamāne kāryasya rāga ādeḥ hāniḥ na yujyate tāpa ādiṣu iva tāpa ādīnām iva pitta ādi vṛddhau syāt etat doṣāṇām sāmye rāga ādayaḥ bhavanti vaiṣamye tu dveṣa ādayaḥ tatas viśeṣepi doṣāṇām na viśiṣyante rāga ādayaḥ iti asiddhaḥ hetuḥ iti āha 
[64,ix_64,xiv]	rāga ādeḥ vikāraḥ api sukha ādi jaḥ rāga ādeḥ doṣa sāmya avasthāyām vikāra upi vṛddhi lakṣaṇaḥ yaḥ sa sukha ādi jaḥ āntara dhātu sāmya sparśa prabhavena sukha ādinā varddhante rāga ādayaḥ vaiṣamya jena duḥkhena rāga āsya anudbhavaḥ yadi vācyam kena udbhavaḥ sāmyāt mada vṛddhiḥ smaraḥ tatas vaiṣamya jena duḥkhena dveṣasya utpādanāt tad viruddhasya rāga āsya anudbhavaḥ yadi mataḥ tadā vācyam kena hetūnā rāgasya udbhavaḥ sāmyāt doṣāṇām madasya śukrasya vṛddhiḥ smaraḥ rāgaḥ śukra vṛddheḥ yat i iṣṭam etat api ayuktam yatas rāgī viṣama doṣaḥ api dṛṣṭaḥ sāmye api na aparaḥ rāgī viṣama doṣaḥ api rāga caritaḥ kaścid dṛṣṭaḥ sāmya īpi na aparaḥ pratisaṃkhyāna balī manda rāga prakṛtiḥ vā dṛṣṭaḥ 
[65,i_65,vii]	kṣayāt asṛka srutaḥ api anye kṣayāt śukrasya asuka srutaḥ raktam kṣaranta upyanye rāga bahulā dṛṣṭāḥ iti śukram api na rāga hetuḥ kiñca na eka strī niyataḥ madaḥ na eka strī niyataḥ madaḥ na hi ekām striyam apekṣya śukram śukrībhavati api tu sarvāḥ tena ekasyām na tīvraḥ syāt aṅga rūpa ādi api iti ced tena sādhāraṇa tvena śukrasya tat janyaḥ rāgaḥ ekasyām striyām na tīvraḥ syāt kintu sādhāraṇaḥ aṅga rūpa ādi api iti ced 
[65,viii_65,x]	rūpa yauvana upacāra ādi ca sahakāri rāga vṛddheḥ iti ced na sarveṣām anekāntān na ca api aniyataḥ bhavet aguṇa grāhiṇaḥ api syāt aṅgam saḥ api guṇa grahaḥ na yuktam etat sarveṣām rūpa ādīnām anekānta tvāt rūpa ādi rahiteṣu api rāga utkarṣa dṛṣṭeḥ kiñca yadi śukram rūpa ādi ca striyāḥ kāraṇam rāgasya tadā na ca api aniyataḥ aviṣayīkṛta strī viśeṣaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ rāgaḥ na bhavet rūpa ādi sahakāriṇaḥ avyāpārāt tathā rūpavatyā guṇam aśubha abhāvanā bhāvitam gṛhṇatopi rāgaḥ syāt śukra rūpayoḥ tad hetvoḥ sadbhāvāt aṅgat nimittam sa upi guṇa grahaḥ tatas aśubhām bhāvayataḥ na syāt rāgaḥ 
[65,xi_65,xv]	yadi sarvaḥ guṇa grāhī syāt hetoḥ aviśeṣatas yadi sarvaḥ śubha aśubha bhāvakaḥ guṇa grāhī syāt guṇa grahasya hetoḥ rūpa ādeḥ sarvān pratyaviśeṣatas kiñca yad avasthaḥ mataḥ rāgī na dveṣī syāt ca tādṛśaḥ yad avasthaḥ śleṣma prakṛti sthaḥ puruṣaḥ rāgī mataḥ tad apasthaḥ na dveṣī syāt 
[65,xvi_66,iii]	kutas iti āha tayoḥ asama rūpa tvāt niyamaḥ ca atra na īkṣyate tayoḥ rāga dveṣayoḥ asama rūpa tvāt viruddha tvāt tad utpādikayoḥ avasthayoḥ api virodhaḥ syāt etat rāga utpādikāyām avasthāyām dveṣaḥ na bhavati eva iti āha niyamaḥ ca atra na īkṣyate śleṣma avasthaḥ rāgī na dveṣi iti na atra niyamaḥ tava api kasmāt amī sama rāga prasaṅga ādayaḥ doṣāḥ na bhavanti iti āha 
[66,iv_66,v]	sa jāti vāsanā bheda pratibaddha pravṛttayaḥ yasya rāga ādayaḥ tasya na ete doṣāḥ prasaṅginaḥ sa jāti vāsanā ātma ātmīya graha mūlasya sa jāteḥ pūrva pūrva abhyaḥ tasya rāga ādeḥ vāsanā apara apara rāga ādi janikāḥ śaktayaḥ tāsām bhedaḥ parasparataḥ tatra pratibaddhā pravṛttiḥ janma yeṣām te tathā rāga ādayaḥ yasya bauddhasya mate tasya na ete anantara muktāḥ doṣāḥ prasaṅginaḥ 
[66,vi_66,ix]	etena bhūta dharma tvam niṣiddham etena vāta ādi dharma tva niṣedhena bhūta dharma tvam niṣiddham rāgāt eḥ bboṃddhavyam doṣāṇām marut tejaḥ ambhaḥ svabhāva tvāt bhavantu sa bhāga hetukāḥ pṛthivī ādi āśritāḥ tu syuḥ ddhavala ādi vat iti āha niścayasya ca niṣedhāt na pṛthivī ādi niḥśritāḥ dhavala ādayaḥ 
[66,x_67,i]	niśrayasya āśrayasya niṣedhāt anāśrayāt sat asatoḥ ityādinā na pṛthivī ādi niḥśritā dhavalādayopi kutas eva rāga ādayaḥ kathantarhi bhūtāni āśritya upādāya rūpam utpadyate iti iṣṭam iti āha tad upādāya śabdaḥ ca hetu arthaḥ sva āśrayeṇa ca avinirbhāga varti tvāt rūpa ādeḥ āśrayaḥ api vā tad upādāya śabdaḥ ca tāni bhūtāni upādāya śabdaḥ ca hetu arthaḥ bhūtāni hetūkṛtya upādāya rūpam utpadyate iti arthaḥ sva āśrayeṇa bhūta catuṣkeṇa rūpa ādeḥ eka sāmagrī adhīna tvena avinirbhāga vartti tvāt vibhāgena anavasthiteḥ āśrayopi vā bhūta catuṣkam 
[67,ii_67,v]	mad ādi śakteḥ iva ced vinirbhāgaḥ syāt etat surāyāḥ mada śakteḥ ādi śabdāt kanaka ādeḥ unmāda śakteḥ iva āśrita tvepi vinirbhāgaḥ bhūtaiḥ saha caitanyasya syāt yathā mada śakti rahitā vyāpannā surā dṛśyate evam caitanya rahitāni bhūtāni api syuḥ iti ced na vastunaḥ śaktiḥ artha antaram vastu naśyet na āśritam āśraye tiṣṭhati avikale yāti tad tulyam ced na bhedataḥ bhūta caitanayoḥ 
[67,vi]	na vastunaḥ sura ādeḥ śaktiḥ artha antaram kintu vastu eva artha kriyāśaktam śukti ādi avasthāyām naśyet asamarthasya ca utpatti rna āśritam śakti ādi avikalaḥ āśraye tiṣṭhati yāti apati tat tulyañcet bhūta cetanayoḥ api aikātmyam tad bhūta caitanye bhūte naṣṭe niścetanam bhūta antaram utpadyate iti ced na yuktam etat bhedataḥ bhūta caitanyayoḥ 
[67,vii_67,ix]	katham iti āha bhinna pratibhāsā avabodhataḥ avikārañca kāyasya tulya rūpam bhavet manaḥ rūpa ādi vat bhinna pratibhāsā avabodhataḥ bhinna ākāra jñāna viṣaya tayā bhinne bhūta caitanye na anyathā kvacid api bheda siddhiḥ yadi ca deha citayoḥ aikyam tadā avikārañca kāyasya yāvat na vikriyate dehantāvat tulyam ekākārambhavet manaḥ rūpa ādi vat 
[68,i_68,iv]	syāt etat eka rūpa tva īpi dehasya arthānām nānā rūpa tvāt jñānam api tathā iti āha vikalpasya kā eva artha paratantra tā vikalpasya kā eva artha paratantra tā yena artha nānā tvāt kalpanā api tathā syāt anapekṣita sannidhayaḥ upādāna vaśena vikalpāḥ pravartante iti vāsanā bhedāt eṣām bhedaḥ anapekṣya yadā kāyam vāsanā bodha kāraṇam jñānam syāt kasyacid kiñcid kutaścid tena kiñcana avijñānasya vijñāna anupādānāt ca sidhyati 
[68,v]	evañcā napekṣya yadā kāyam kiñcid jñānam vāsanā bodhasya prabodhasya kāraṇam syāt kasyacid utpadyamānasya jñānasya tadā tena prabodhaka anurodhena kutaścid jñānāt anantaram kiñcana jñānam syāt iti sustham asya pakṣe avijñānasya vijñāna śūnyasya loṣṭa ādeḥ vijñāna anupādānāt ca sidhyati vijñānāt eva vijñānam 
[68,vi_68,vii]	vijñāna śakti sambandha āt iṣṭañcet sarva vastunaḥ etat śāṃkhya paśoḥ kaḥ anyaḥ sa lajjaḥ vaktum īhate adṛṣṭa pūrvam asti iti tṛṇa agre kariṇām śatam sarvasya vastunaḥ vijñāna śakti sambandhāt avijñānāt vijñāna anutpādanam iṣṭam ced e tad vijñānasya śakti rūpatayā avasthānam sāṃkhya paśoḥ kaḥ anyaḥ sa lajjaḥ vaktum īhate yaḥ brūyāt adṛṣṭam api tṛṇa agre kariṇām śatam asti iti 
[69,i_69,iii]	tathā hi yadi śaktiḥ abhivyakti rūpāt vijñānāt anyā tadā avijñāna tvam siddham atha anyathā tadā yat rūpam dṛśyatām yātam tat rūpam prāk na dṛśyate śatadhā viprakīrṇe api hetau tat vidyate katham yat rūpam khyāna ākhyam dṛśyatām yātam abhivyakta avasthāyām tad rūpam prāk śakti avasthāyām śatadhā api viprakīrṇṇe hetau na dṛśyate kathantat vidyate iti na avijñāna tvam asiddham 
[69,iv_69,vi]	kiñca rāga ādi aniyamaḥ apūrva prādurbhāve prasajyate na ced para lokāt āgacchati citta santānaḥ tadā apūrva sattva prādurbhāve rāga ādi aniyamaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi aniyama vat prasajyate yathā cakṣuḥ kara caraṇa śyāma tā niyamaḥ puruṣe na īkṣyate kadācid kasyacid abhāva darśanāt tathā rāgī rāgitaraḥ nīrāgaḥ ca kaścid syāt 
[69,vii_69,viii]	bhūtātma tā anatikrāntaḥ sarvaḥ rāga ādimān yadi sarvaḥ samāna rāgaḥ syāt bhūta atiśayataḥ na ced bhūtānām prāṇitā abhede api ayam bhedaḥ yad āśrayaḥ tad nirhrāsa atiśaya vat tad bhāvāt tāni hāpayet bhūtātma tāyāḥ anatikrānteḥ sarvaḥ pumān rāga ādimān yadi tadā sarvaḥ samāna rāgaḥ syāt bhūtātma tāyāḥ aviśeṣāt bhūtānām avāntarāt atiśayataḥ sa māna ra āgatā prasaṅgaḥ na ced bhūtānām prāṇitāyāḥ abheda ipyayam bhedaḥ utkaṭa manda rāga tva ādikaḥ yad āśrayaḥ yat avāntara viśeṣa vat kāraṇam āśritya tad kāraṇam nirhrāsa atiśaya vat apacaya tāratamya vat tad bhāvāt rāga ādimattvāt tāni bhūtāni hāpayet bhraṃśayet iti nīrāgopi kaścid sattvaḥ syāt 
[70,i_70,ii]	na ced bhede api rāga ādi hetu tulya ātma tā kṣayaḥ sarvatra rāgaḥ sadṛśaḥ syāt hetoḥ sadṛśa ātmanaḥ bhede manda utkaṭa rāga ādi janake avāntara bhūta viśeṣa īpi rāga ādi hetu tvena yā tulya ātma tā sadṛśa tā tasyāḥ kṣayaḥ na ced sarvatra puṃsi sadṛśaḥ rāga ādiḥ syāt sadṛśa ātmanaḥ hetoḥ bhāvāt 
[70,iii_70,iv]	na hi go pratyayasya asti samāna ātma bhuvaḥ kvacid tāratamyam pṛthivī ādau prāṇita ādeḥ iha api vā na hi go pratyayasya asti samāna ātma bhuvaḥ sadṛśa kāraṇa utpatteḥ kvacid śābaleya ādau tāra tamyam api tu sarvatra samāna tā eva pṛthivī ādau sadṛśe hetau prāṇita ādeḥ iha cārvākamatepi vā viśeṣaḥ na vidyate 
[70,v_70,vi]	auṣṇayasya tāratamye api na anuṣṇaḥ agniḥ kadācana tathā iha api iti ced na agneḥ auṣṇyāt bheda niṣedhataḥ auṣṇyasya tāratamya īpi khādira agni ādaunān uṣṇaḥ agniḥ kadācana tathā iha rāga ādi tāratamyepi na vīta rāgaḥ kaścid iti ced kadācana na etat yuktam agneḥ auṣṇyāt bhedasya niṣedhataḥ na etat yuktam bhāsvara rūpa uṣṇa sparśa ādiḥ agniḥ ucyate tena auṣṇya abhāve agniḥ eva na syāt rāga ādiḥ tu bhūtebhyaḥ anyaḥ tad abhāvepi teṣām bhāvāt 
[70,vii_70,ix]	atas sa viśeṣaṇam hetun darśayati tāratamya anubhavinaḥ yasya anyasya sataḥ guṇāḥ te kvacid pratihanyante tad bhede dhavala ādi vat guṇebhyaḥ anyasya yasya sataḥ dharmiṇaḥ ye tāratamya anubhāvinaḥ guṇāḥ te kvacid dharmiṇi pratihanyante tad bhede bhūta bhede dhavala ādi vat na hi sarvaḥ bhūta pariṇāmaḥ śuklaḥ 
[71,i_71,iii]	syāt etat bhūta dharmaḥ rūpa ādiḥ yathā avaśyam abhūtvā bhavati tathā rāgopi dehinaḥ syāt iti āha rūpa ādi vat na niyamaḥ teṣām bhūta avibhāgataḥ tat tulyañcet na rāga ādeḥ saha utpatti prasaṅgataḥ rūpāḥ divan na niyamaḥ rāga ādeḥ teṣām rūpa ādīnām bhūta avibhāgataḥ na hi rūpa ādi sāmānyam vinā bhūtāḥ ni vartate rāga ādeḥ api tad bhūta avinirbhāga vartti tvam tulyañcet na etat asti rāgāḥ deḥ bhūtaiḥ saha utpatti prasaṅgataḥ viṣayaiḥ kādācid ka sannidhānaiḥ niyamita tvāt 
[71,iv_71,vi]	na saha utpāda prasaṅgaḥ iti ced āha vikalpya viṣaya tvāt ca viṣayāḥ na niyāmakāḥ sa bhāga hetu virahāt rāga ādeḥ niyamaḥ na vā vikalpyaḥ kalpitaḥ tad viṣaya tvāt ca rāga ādeḥ viṣayāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ agrāhyātvān na niyāmakāḥ kiñca avijñānasya vijñāna hetu tvāt na iti uktam tvad mate sa bhāgasya ca hetoḥ virahāt rāga ādeḥ niyamaḥ deśa kāla svabhāva viṣayaḥ na vā syāt ahetutvāt 
[71,vii_71,ix]	bhūtāni eva hi hetuḥ iti ced sarvadā sarva buddhīnām janma vā hetu sannidheḥ tarhi sarvadā sarva buddhīnām sukha duḥkha icchā dveṣa rāga kṛpā ādīnām janma vā syāt hetoḥ bhūta saṃghātasyam sannidheḥ tat evam rāga ādeḥ pāṭava īkṣaṇāt itya ādinā caturṇṇā ām arūpiṇām skandhānām sa bhāga hetuka tve sādhite sādhitam saṃsāri tvam upādāna skandhānām te eva duḥkham iti uktāḥ 
[72,i_72,vi]	duḥkha satyañca aniti ataḥ duḥkhataḥ śūnyataḥ anātmataḥ ca iti catur ākāram ākhyātum āha kadācid upalambhāt tat adhruvam doṣa niśrayāt duḥkham hetu vaśa tvāt ca na ca ātmā na api adhiṣṭhitam kadācid upalambhāt duḥkham adhruvam anityam doṣa niśrayāt rāga ādi doṣa āśrayeṇa utpatteḥ hetu vaśa tvāt ca sarvam para vaśaṃduḥkham iti nyāyāt duḥkham tat na ca ātma āśrayam anātmanaḥ ātma vilakṣaṇa tvāt na api adhiṣṭhitam adhiṣṭhātuḥ ātmanaḥ abhāvāt anena śūnyate iti ākhyātam kasmāt punar ātmā na adhiṣṭhāta iti āha na akāraṇam adhiṣṭhātā nityam vā kāraṇam katham na akāraṇam adhiṣṭhātā ati prasaṅgāt nityam vā dravyam kāraṇam katham tasya krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā virahāt 
[72,vii_72,x]	tasmāt anekam ekasmāt bhinna kālam na jāyate tasmāt anekam bhinna kāla dṛśyamānam sukha duḥkha ādi kāryam na ekasmāt jāyate ekasya aneka karaṇe samarthasya sakṛt eva tad kriyā prasaṅgāt kārya anutpādataḥ anyeṣu saṅgateṣu api hetuṣu hetu antara anumānam syāt na etat nityeṣu vidyate kiñca anekeṣu hetuṣu saṅgateṣu mithas militeṣu api kārya anutpādataḥ hetu antara anumānam syāt yathā rūpa āloka manaskāreṣu satsu api cakṣuḥ vijñānam anutpadyamānam cakṣuḥ anumāpayati na etat kārya anutpattyā anumānam nityeṣu vidyate teṣām avyatireki tvāt 
[72,xi_73,ii]	catur ākāram duḥkham vyākhyāya samudayataḥ hetutaḥ pratyayataḥ prabhavataḥ ca iti catur ākāram samudāyam vyākhyātum āha kādācid ka tayā siddhā duḥkhasya asya sa hetu tā nityam satvam asatvam vā ahetoḥ bāhya anapekṣaṇāt kādācid ka tayā duḥkhasya sa hetu tā siddhā nityam sattvam asat tvaṃmvā hetoḥ bhavati yathā aakāśasya śaśa viṣāṇasya bāhya anapekṣaṇāt yaḥ eva ca duḥkha hetuḥ saḥ eva samudāyaḥ 
[73,iii_73,vi]	taikṣṇya ādīnām yathā na asti kāraṇam kaṇṭaka ādiṣu tathā akāraṇam etat syāt iti kecid pracakṣate nanu yathā kaṇṭaka ādiṣu taikṣṇya ādīnām kāraṇam na asti tathā akāraṇam etat duḥkham syāt tat kutas samudayaḥ iti kecid svabhāva vādinaḥ pracakṣate te evam vaktavyāḥ sati eva yasmin yat janma vikāre vā api vikriyā tat tasya kāraṇam prāhuḥ tat teṣām api vidyate 
[73,vii_73,x]	sati eva yasmin vastuni yasya janma yasya vikāre sati eva vā yasya vikriyā tat tasya janminaḥ vikāriṇaḥ ca kāraṇam prāhuḥ vidvāṃsaḥ tad janma sati eva bīja udaka pṛthivī ādiṣu tad utkarṣa apakarṣa ādi vikāre ca vikṛta tvam teṣām kaṇṭaka ādīnām api asti iti tepi sa hetukāḥ eva evam skandhāḥ api nanu sparśe sati bhavati cakṣuḥ vijñānam asati ca na bhavati na ca tat kāraṇam atas ativyāptiḥ iti āha sparśasya rūpa hetu tvāt darśane asti nimitta tā sparśasya rūpa ādi avinirbhāginaḥ saha kāri bhāvena rūpa hetu tvāt darśane cakṣuḥ vijñāne asti nimitta tā pāramparyeṇa iti na ati vyāptiḥ 
[73,xi_74,iv]	etat ca vyatirekam abhyupagamya uktam na tu rūpam upadarśya sparśa abhāve netra buddheḥ abhāvaḥ śakya darśanaḥ rūpa sparśayoḥ avinirbhāga vartti tvāt tasya ca duḥkhasya nityānām pratiṣedhena na īśvara ādeḥ ca sambhavaḥ asāmarthyāt atas hetuḥ bhava vāñchā nityānām krama ākramābhyām artha kriyā āyām asāmarthyāt pratiṣedhena ca na īśvara ādeḥ ādi grahaṇāt pradhāna puruṣa ādeḥ kāraṇāt sambhavaḥ utpādaḥ atas nityāt anutpatteḥ duḥkhasya hetuḥ bhava vāñchā janma tṛṣṇā janma sthāna avasthā sattva ādi abhilāṣa ātmikā parigrahaḥ yasmāt deśa viśeṣasya tad prāpti āśā kṛtaḥ tṛṇām yasmāt deśa viśeṣasya parigrahaḥ tad prāpti tṛṣṇā kṛtaḥ nṛṇām nṛ śabdaḥ prāṇi upalakṣaṇaḥ tatas garbha sthāna ādānam api tat tṛṣṇā kṛtam eva 
[74,v_74,vi]	nanu uktam bhagavatā tatra katamassamudaya ārya satyam paunarbhāvikī nandī rāga sahagatā tatra tatra abhināndinī yat uta kāma tṛṣṇā bhava tṛṣṇā vibhava tṛṣṇā ce ti tat katham ekā bhava tṛṣṇā ucyate samudaya satyam iti atra āha sā bhava it śā apti anāpti icchoḥ pravṛttiḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ yatas api prāṇinaḥ kāma vibhava icche ca te mate 
[74,vii_74,viii]	yatas kāraṇāt prāṇinaḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ krameṇa āpti anāpti icchoḥ pravṛttiḥ garbha sthāna parigraha āyātaḥ sā bhavet chā api kāma vibhava icche ca te mate sukha prāpti icchā kāma tṛṣṇā duḥkha viyoga icchā vibhava tṛṣṇā bhava tṛṣṇāyām sukha duḥkha prāpti parihāra icchā pūrvikāyām garbha sthāna upādāna icchā ātmikāyām dvayoḥ api saṃgrahāt avirodhaḥ sarvatra ca ātma snehasya hetu tvāt saṃpravartate asukhe sukha saṃjñasya 
[74,ix]	samudayasya ca samudaya ātmaka tvāt sarvatra viṣaye asukhe sukha rahite sukha saṃjñasya duḥkha viparyayaḥ tasya anena aśucau śuci viparyāsa upi kathitaḥ na hi aśucau tathā manyamāna kasyacid sukha saṃjñā aatma snehena iti ātma snehasya hetu tvāt iti ahaṅkāram amakāra utthāpitasya anena ātmani ātma sneha viparyāse uktaḥ saṃpravartate iti anena anitya viparyāsaḥ sūcitaḥ na hi nitya viparyāsamvinā phala arthī pravartate 
[75,i_75,iii]	tasmāt tṛṣṇā bhava āśrayaḥ tat evam catur viparyāsa vāsita mānasaḥ eva ātma snehāt sukha duḥkha prāpti parijihīrṣayā pravartate tathā garbha sthānepi sukha duḥkha prāpti parihāra icchā eva tṛṣṇā tasmāt tṛṣṇā bhavasya āśrayaḥ hetuḥ anena hetutaḥ ākhyātam virakta janma adṛṣṭeḥ iti ācāryāḥ saṃpracakṣate adeha rāga at ṛṣṭeḥ ca dehāt rāga samudbhavaḥ 
[75,iv_75,vii]	nanu viraktasya janma adṛṣṭeḥ iti ācāryā gautamādayopi saṃpracakṣate adehasya rāga adṛṣṭeḥ ca dehāt rāga samudbhavaḥ sthitaḥ taṃtaḥ na dehī vīta rāgaḥ atra āha nimitta upagamāt iṣṭam upādānam tu vāryate nimittasya sahakāri kāraṇasya upagamāt dehosya rāgasya saha ākāri kāraṇam iṣṭam tatas na aniṣṭam āpadyate upādānantu dehaḥ rāgasya vāryate rāgaḥ eva tu upādāna kāraṇam na ca rāgaḥ janma hetuḥ viraktasya karuṇayā janma sambhavāt raktasya api tṛṣṇayā eva janma grahaḥ anena pratyayate iti vyākhyātam 
[75,viii_75,ix]	imām tu yuktim anvicchan bādhate sva matam svayam janmanā sahabhāvaḥ ced jātānām rāga darśanāt virakta janma adṛṣṭeḥ iti imām yuktim anvicchan cā rvā kaḥ sva matam svayaṃbādhate rāga hetukaḥ dehaḥ tad hetukaḥ ca rāgaḥ iti anyonya hetu tvāt janma prabandha siddheḥ vīta rāga abhyupagamāt ca sva mata bādhāsya janmanā sahabhāvaḥ rāga ādīnām na pūrvam rāgosti jātānām rāga darśanāt atas na rāgaḥ deha hetuḥ iti ced 
[75,x_76,iii]	sa bhāga jāteḥ prāk siddhiḥ nanu evam deha upi na syāt rāga hetuḥ sahabhāvāt na ca ahetuka tā tatas sabhāgāt sajātīyāt rāgajjāteḥ utpādāt prāc rāgasya siddhiḥ iti āyātam nanu avidyā tṛṣṇā karma ca janma kāraṇam tat katham tṛṣṇā eva kevalā samudayaḥ uktaḥ iti āha kāraṇa tve api na uditam ajñānam uktā tṛṣṇā eva santāna preraṇāt bhave ānantaryāt ca karma api sati tasmin asaṃbhavāt 
[76,iv]	kāraṇa tvepi na uditam ajñānam avidyā moha apara saṃjñakam uktā tṛṣṇā eva tayā eva santānasya pañca skandha santateḥ preraṇāt kim artham bhave janma nimittam karma api hetu tve api na uktam samudaya tvena sati tasmin ajñāne karmaṇi ca tṛṣṇā asaṃmukhībhāve abhāvāt janmanaḥ ānantaryāt ca tṛṣṇāyāḥ satoḥ api moha karmaṇoḥ tṛṣṇāyāḥ asaṃmukhībhāve janmanaḥ ākṣepakatva asaṃbhavāt yathā vimuktiḥ cittasya iti uktaḥ samudayaḥ 
[76,v_76,vii]	tad anānyantikam hetoḥ pratibandha ādi sambhavāt tat etat yathā ukta kāraṇa samudaya svabhāvam duḥkham anātyantikam saṃbhavat ucchedam duḥkha hetoḥ tṛṣṇāyāḥ pratibandhasya saṃbhāvyamāna tvāt ādi śabdāt avidyā ādeḥ sahakāriṇaḥ vaikalya sambhavāt anena nirodhaḥ eva na asti iti vādinaḥ pratinirodhate iti kathitam 
[76,viii_76,ix]	saṃsāri tvāt aniḥ mokṣaḥ na iṣṭa tvāt aprasiddhitaḥ nanu saṃsāri tvāt aniḥ mmokṣaḥ muktiḥ na asti kasyacid tat katham nirodha sambhāvanā na eṣa doṣaḥ iṣṭa tvāt kaḥ nāma muktim saṃsāriṇaḥ icchati aprasiddhitaḥ tasya na hi saṃsārīm kaścid asti kintu duḥkham kevalam hetu balāt pravartate tad abhāvāt ca na bhavati iti brūmaḥ 
[77,i_77,iii]	yadi saṃsārī kaścid na asti kaḥ mukti arthī kim artham pravartate iti āha yāvat ca ātmani na premṇaḥ hāniḥ sa paritasyati tāvat duḥkhitam āropya na ca svasthaḥ avatiṣṭhate yāvat ca ātmani ekatva ahaṃkāra viṣayeṣu skandheṣu premṇaḥ snehasya na hāniḥ tāvat duḥkhitam ātmānam āropya sa prāṇi abhimataḥ duḥkha santānaḥ paritasyati duḥkham āste na ca duḥkha hetu apagama upāyābhyām sa kleśamvinā svasthaḥ avatiṣṭhate 
[77,iv_77,vi]	kintu mithyā dhyāra upahāna artham yatnaḥ asati api moktari mithyā adhya āropasya saṃsāritva adhyavasāyasya hāna artham yatnaḥ asati api kasmiṃścid ātma ādau moktari na hi yathāvasttu eva vyavahāraḥ kintu yathā avasāyañca tathā hi rajjuḥ api sarpa adhyavasāya viṣaya tvāt parihāra viṣayaḥ evam aham eva baddhaḥ aham eva mokṣyāmi iti adhyāropāt mukti artham vyāyāmaḥ 
[77,vii_77,ix]	bhavatu ātma graha viparyastānām sukha ādi abhilāṣāt pravṛtti lakṣaṇā saṃsāre sthitiḥ unmīlita ātma graha yoni sakala doṣa rāśayaḥ tu kasmāt āsate iti āha avasthā vīta rāgāṇām dayayā karmaṇā api vā avasthā vīta rāgāṇām dayayā api karmaṇā api vā vīta mohānām api duḥkhāt duḥkha hetoḥ ca lokam uddhartu kāma tayā sthitiḥ tāvat kāla anubandhi śarīra ākṣepakena karmaṇā vā sthitiḥ 
[77,x_78,i]	tat eva āha ākṣipte avinivṛtti iṣṭeḥ ākṣipte karmaṇā kāye avinivṛtteḥ nivṛtya bhāvasya iṣṭeḥ yadi evam janma antara ākṣepakasya karmaṇaḥ sadbhāvāt bhavāḥ ntarañca syāt iti āha sahakāri kṣayāt alam na akṣeptum aparam karma bhava tṛṣṇā vilaṃghinām sahakāriṇaḥ ātma ātmīya ādi viparyāsi jñānasya tṛṣṇāyāḥ ca kṣayāt nālam na śaktam karma ākṣeptum aparam bhavam bhava tṛṣṇā vilaṃdhinām tṛṣṇā laṃghanā nairātmya dṛṣṭiḥ iti ātma ātmīya ādi moha nivṛttiḥ ca uktā anena saha akāri vaikalyam uktam 
[78,ii_78,vii]	nanu dayā sattva darśanāt tat ca kṣīṇam muktānām tad kathandayayā sthitiḥ iti āha duḥkha jñāne aviruddhasya pūrva saṃskāra vāhinī vastu dharmaḥ dayā utpattiḥ na sā satva anurodhinī duḥkhasya anitya duḥkha śūnyān ātmaka ākārasya jñāne satya viruddhasya dveṣa abhāvāt sarvatra apratiha tasya pūrva saṃskāra vāhinī pūrva abhyāsa pravṛttā yā dayā utpattiḥ sā na sattva anurodhinī sattva dṛṣṭi vaśā kintu vastunaḥ duḥkhasya kṛpā viṣaya tayā abhyastasya dharmaḥ unmūlita ātma dṛṣṭīnām api duḥkhasya kṛpā viṣaya tayā abhyastasya saṃmukhībhāva mātreṇa dayā utpadyate iti arthaḥ evantarhi rāgopi muktānām syāt iti āha ātma antara samāropāt rāgaḥ dharme atad ātmake ātma antarasya sthira sukha ātma ātmīya rūpasya āropāt dharme skandha mātra rūpe atad ātmake vastunaḥ asthira ādi svabhāve rāgaḥ abhiṣvaṅga rūpaḥ bhavati 
[78,viii_78,xii]	duḥkha santāna saṃsparśa mātreṇa eva dayā udayaḥ dayā udayaḥ tu duḥkha santānasya saṃsparśaḥ darśanam tanmātreṇa evam bhavati na tatra sattva darśana apekṣā yathā duḥkha darśanāt dayā utpattiḥ tathā apakāriṇi dveṣopi syāt iti āha mohaḥ ca mūlam doṣāṇām sa ca satva grahaḥ mohaḥ ca mūlam ādi kāraṇam doṣāṇām sa ca mohaḥ sattva grahaḥ unmūlita sattva dṛṣṭeḥ ca 
[78,xiii_79,iii]	vinā tena udya hetau na dveṣaḥ na doṣaḥ atas kṛpā matā tena sattva graheṇa vinā adya hetau apakāriṇi na dveṣa usti ātmanaḥ adarśanāt tad apakāra bhrānti abhāvāt atas doṣa mūlasya ātma grahasya abhāvāt utpadyamānā kṛpā na doṣaḥ matā yadi pūrva karmmā vedhataḥ tadā eva na nirvāṇam tadā sāṃsārika tā eva syāt iti āha na amuktiḥ pūrva saṃskāra kṣaye anya apratisandhitaḥ akṣīṇa śaktiḥ saṃskāraḥ yeṣām tiṣṭhanti te anadhāḥ manda tvāt karuṇāyāḥ ca na yatnaḥ sthāpane mahān 
[79,iv]	na amuktiḥ kintu muktiḥ eva pūrva saṃskāra kṣaye pūrva karma āvedha kṣaye sati anyasya duḥkhasya hetu vaikalyāt apratisandhitaḥ yeṣām punar mahā kṛpāṇām prāṇi dhāna paripuṣṭasya janma ākṣepaka karmaṇaḥ saṃskāraḥ akṣīṇa śaktiḥ te anadhāḥ samyaksambuddhāḥ yāvat ākāśan tiṣṭhanti eva śrāvakāṇa an tu karmaṇaḥ niyata kāla sthitika deha ākṣepaka tvāt manda tvāt karuṇāyāḥ yatnaḥ ca mahān sthāpane na asti iti na sadā sthitiḥ 
[79,v_79,viii]	tiṣṭhanti eva para adhīnā yeṣām tu mahatī kṛpā tiṣṭhanti eva sarvadā te para adhīnāḥ pareṣām upakaraṇīkṛta ātmānaḥ mahā munayaḥ yeṣām akāraṇa vatsalānām mahatī kṛpā satkāya dṛṣṭeḥ vigamāt ādyaḥ eva abhavaḥ bhavet mārge ced sahajā hāneḥ na hānau vā bhavaḥ kutas nanu ādyaḥ eva mārgge darśana mārgge satkāya dṛṣṭeḥ vigamāt srotaḥ āpannasya bhavaḥ janma antara bandhaḥ na bhavet iti ced sahajā hāneḥ na dvidhā hi sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ ābhisāṃskārikī yā skandha vyatirikta ātmā adhyavasāyinī sahajā ca tatra prathamā darśana mārgge hīyate na dvitīyā bhāvanā mārga heyā sā ca mohaḥ tṛṣṇāyāḥ ca hetuḥ iti bhavati janma prabandhaḥ yadi tu paṭutara prajñasya ādya eva mārggaḥ mārgga antara svabhāvaḥ tadā hānau vā sahajāyāḥ ātma dṛṣṭeḥ punarbhavaḥ kutas 
[79,ix_80,ii]	kīdṛśam punar tad sahaja sattva darśanam iti āha sukhī bhaveyam duḥkhī vā mā bhūvam iti tṛṣyataḥ yā evā aham iti dhīḥ sā eva sahajam sattva darśanam sukhī bhaveyam duḥkhī vā mā abhūvam iti tṛṣyataḥ kāṃkṣamāṇasya yā eva aham iti dhīḥ sā eva sahajam sattva darśanam ucyate tad aprahīṇam srotāpannasya iti katham jñāyate iti āha 
[80,iii_80,v]	na hi apaśyan aham iti kaścid ātmani snihyati na ca ātmani vinā premṇā sukha kāmaḥ abhidhāvati na hi apaśyan aham iti kaścid ātmani snihyati kintu paśyan eva na ca ātmani vinā premṇā sukha kāmaḥ kaścid garbha sthāna ādim abhidhāvati abhidhāvati ca garbha sthānam prahīṇa abhisaṃskārika sattva dṛṣṭiḥ api srotaḥ āpannam tasya aprahīṇam sahajam sattva darśanam 
[80,vi_80,viii]	nanu satya ātmani bandha mokṣau eka adhikaraṇau yuktau na iti āha duḥkhasya utpāda hetu tvam bandhaḥ nityasya tat kutas aduḥkha utpāda hetu tvam mokṣaḥ nityasya tat kutas duḥkhasya upādāna skandhānām utpāda hetu tvam bandhaḥ tad kutas nityasya krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyāḥ virahān aduḥkha utpāda hetu tvam duḥkham pratyaya hetu tā mokṣaḥ tat ca nitya sya kutas na hi pūrva apara ekasya bhāvasya duḥkha hetoḥ paścāt ahetu tvam yuktam 
[80,ix_80,xi]	syāt etat na nityasya hetu tvam bandha mokṣau ca yuktau iti nitya tva anitya tvābhyām avācyasya pudgalasya tau bhaviṣyate iti manvānam vaibhāṣikamprati āha anitya tvena yaḥ avācyaḥ sa hetuḥ na hi kasyacid anitya tvena yaḥ avācyaḥ anitya tvam upalakṣaṇam nitya tvena api avācyaḥ sa hetuḥ na hi kasyacid tasma eva abhāvāt tathā hi yadi asau anityaḥ na bhavati syāt nityaḥ 
[80,xii_81,iii]	atha nityaḥ na bhavati syāt anityaḥ anyonya abhāva lakṣaṇa tvāt anayoḥ eka vidhi pratiṣedhasya apara pratiṣadha vidhinā antarīyaka tvāt na kvacid vastuni dvaya pratiṣedha sambhavaḥ iti pudgalasya abhāvāt ahetu tvam atas bandha mokṣau api avācye pudgale na yujyete kathañcana atha nitya tvena avācya tvāt na doṣaḥ iti ced nanu evam anityaḥ eva uktaḥ syāt tathā hi nityam tam āhuḥ vidvāṃsaḥ yaḥ svabhāvaḥ na naśyati nityam tam āhuḥ vidvāṃsaḥ yaḥ svabhāvaḥ sarvadā na naśyati sa ced īdṛśaḥ na bhavati anityaḥ eva syāt 
[81,iv_81,vi]	tyaktvā imām hrepaṇīm dṛṣṭim ataḥ anityaḥ saḥ ucyatām akṣa imām pudgala dṛṣṭim pudgala nairātmya vādinaḥ saṃskāra aniti a tāvādinaḥ ca śāstuḥ śiṣyāṇām hrepaṇīm lajjā varddhanīm tyaktvā anityaḥ sa pudgalaḥ ucyatām yena bandha mokṣau yujyete eka ākāraḥ nirodhaḥ vyākhyātaḥ trayaḥ ākārāḥ vakṣyante 
[81,vii_81,ix]	uktaḥ mārgaḥ tad abhyāsāt āśrayaḥ parivartate mārga satyam catur ākāram vaktum āha uktaḥ mārgaḥ śāstṛ pada vyākhyā avasare nairātmya darśana lakṣaṇaḥ tasya abhyāsāt āśrayaḥ kleśa vāsanā bhūtayā ālaya vijñānam parivartate kliṣṭa daśā nirodhāt kleśa visaṃyukta citta prabandha ātmanā pariṇamati 
[81,x_81,xiii]	anena mārgataḥ iti mārga ākāraḥ darśitaḥ kleśa visaṃyoga hetutvāt sātmye api doṣa bhāvaḥ ced mārga vat mārgasya abhyāsa prakarṣāt sātmya īpi prakṛti tve ca prāpte punar doṣāṇām moha ādīnām bhāvaḥ prāpnoti ced mārga vat yathā bandha avasthāyām doṣa sātmya īpi mārgaḥ abhyāsa vaśāt āvirbhavati atra āha 
[81,xiv_82,iv]	na avibhu tvataḥ na avibhu tvataḥ asāmarthyāt mārga sātmye api sthitasya cetasi na doṣāṇām utpattum sāmarthyam asti tad nidāna bhūtasya satva darśanasya unmūlita tvāt anena śāntate iti nirodha ākāraḥ uktaḥ doṣāṇām sarvathā śānta tvāt satva darśanam eva punar kasmāt na bhavati iti āha viṣaya grahaṇam dharmom vijñānasya yathā asti saḥ gṛhyate saḥ asya janakaḥ vidyamāna ātmanā iti ca 
[82,v_82,vi]	viṣaya grahaṇam vijñānasya tāvat sati grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ dharmaḥ yathā ca asti sa sa viṣayaḥ tathā gṛhyate vijñānena viṣayiṇā sa ca viṣayosya vijñānasya janakaḥ vidyamānena ātmanā yathā avasthitena rūpeṇa eṣā prakṛtiḥ asyāḥ tad nimitta antarataḥ skhalat vyāvṛttau pratyaya apekṣam adṛḍham sarpa buddhi vat 
[82,vii_82,x]	yathā avasthita vastu grahaṇañca na ātmā eṣā prakṛtiḥ svabhāvaḥ jñānasya viṣayiṇaḥ yathā svabhāvam sva grāhi jñān a jananañca viṣayasya prakṛtiḥ asyāḥ prakṛteḥ tat jñānam nimitta antarataḥ āntarāt avidyā rūpāt āgantukāt ca viṣaya doṣa ādeḥ skhalat viṣaya grahaṇa viparīta ākāram bhavati tat ca vyāvṛttau viṣaya viparīta grahaṇa ākāra tāyāḥ nivṛtti artha pratyaya apekṣam bhrānti nivartaka kāraṇam apekṣyamāṇam adṛḍham asthāṣṇu sarpa buddhi vat yathā sarpabuddhiḥ rajvā bhrānti nimittā jātāḥ rajju svarūpa grāhiṇaḥ pratyayāt nivṛttā na punar udbhavati iti tathā bhrānti nimitta nirāsāt dṛṣṭe nairātmye vastuni sati na asti sattve dṛṣṭi sambhavaḥ jñānasya viṣaya svarūpa grahaṇa pravaṇa tvāt viṣayasya ca su a ākāra arpaṇa pravṛtta tvāt kiñca prabhāsvaram idañcittam prakṛti āgantavaḥ malāḥ prabhāsvaram anātma bhūta doṣa sañcayam idam cittam prakṛtyā svabhāvena ye tu manaḥ doṣāḥ dṛśyante te bhrānti nimitta upanīta tvāt āgantavaḥ asvabhāva bhūtāḥ cetasaḥ tamaḥ tuhina ādayaḥ iva nabhasaḥ 
[83,i_83,iv]	tad prāk api asamarthānām paścāt śaktiḥ kaḥ tad maye tad prāk api tasmāt nairātmya darśanāt pūrvam api tatas śruta cintā adhyavasā nepya āpāta viṣkambhanāt utpattum asamarthānām malānām paścāt mārga niṣpattau śaktiḥ utpattum kva tad maye mārga sātmye svarūpe etat eva āha na alam praroḍhum atyantam syandinyām agni vat bhuvi bādhaka utpatti sāmarthya garbhe śaktaḥ api vastuni 
[83,v]	śaktaḥ api addhatopi manaḥ malaḥ na alam atyantam praroḍhum vastuni citta santāne kīdṛśe bādhaka utpatti sāmarthya garbhe sarva dṛṣṭi bādhakasya nairātmya darśanasya mārga satya utpattiḥ tasyām sāmarthyam prabhaviṣṇu tvam tad garbhe ānantaryasya garbhe tasmin syandinyām bhuvi agni vat yathā hi vahneḥ hetu balāt utpannopi syandinyām bhuvi bādhakavatyām na atyantam prarohati tathā mārga utpatti sāmarthya garbhe cetasi utpannāḥ api malāḥ na atyantam virohanti sa ātmībhūta mārgge tu hetu vaikalyāt na utpadyante eva 
[83,vi_83,vii]	kathañca nairātmya darśinaḥ mala utpattiḥ āśaṃkyate na tāvat hetu sākalyāt satva dṛṣṭeḥ hetu bhūtāyāḥ abhāvāt nairātmya darśana vat sattva darśanañca bhāvanayā utpannam hetuḥ iti ced kutas tasya bhāvanā kinnairātmyasya sa upadrava tvāt kiñcābhūta tvena bhrama hetu tvāt asvabhāvena upahantum śakya tvāt vā etat trayam asaṅgatam iti āha 
[83,viii_83,ix]	nirupadrava bhūta artha svabhāvasya viparyayaiḥ na bādhā yatnava tve api buddheḥ tad pakṣapātataḥ doṣa rāśeḥ udvejakasya prahāṇena nirupadravasya pramāṇa samvādi tvena bhūta arthasya satya arthasya anāropita tvena svabhāvasya prakṛteḥ nairātmyasya abhirucita viṣayasya viparyayeṣu ātma ādi a ākāreṣu abhyāse sa upadrava tva ādinā prayatnaḥ eva tāvat na sambhavati prekṣasya sambhavepi vā viparyayaiḥ 
[84,i_84,iv]	na bādhā nairātmyasya sā ātmībhūtasya svabhāvasya asti buddheḥ tatra doṣa pratipakṣe guṇavati mārgge pakṣapātāt na hi svabhāvaḥ sākṣātkṛtaḥ anyathā kartu śakyaḥ anena praṇītaḥ iti nirodha ākāraḥ darśitaḥ nanu yadi nairātmya sa ātma tva darśanayoḥ paraspara bhedāt bādhā tadā rāga pratighayoḥ api syāt iti āha ātma graha eka yoni tvāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvataḥ rāga pratidhayoḥ bādhāḥ bhede api na parasparam 
[84,v]	ātma grahaḥ ekaḥ yoniṣkāraṇam yayoḥ tau tayoḥ bhāvaḥ tasmāt eka kāraṇa tvāt rāga pratidhayoḥ bhet api na parasparam bādhā rūpa rasayoḥ iva tathā kārya kāraṇa bhāva topi na anyonyam bādhā tathā hi yadā ekasmin rāgaḥ tadā tad apakāriṇi dveṣaḥ yadā ca kvacid dveṣaḥ tadā tad apakāriṇi rāga upīti paraspara kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt na asti virodhaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi buddhīnām iva 
[84,vi_84,viii]	nanu dveṣa ādi pratipakṣāḥ maitrī ādayaḥ na ca tān ucchindanti iti āha moha avirodhāt maitrī a ādeḥ nna atyantam doṣa nigrahaḥ tad mūlāḥ ca malāḥ sarve moha avirodhāt maitrī a ādeḥ maitrī karuṇa ādayaḥ moha avirodhinaḥ atas ca doṣa kāraṇā vaikalyāt na atyantam dveṣa ādi doṣāṇām nigrahaḥ maitrī ādeḥ āpāta viṣkambhana m ātrantu bhavati mohasya anapāyāt tad mūlāḥ ca malāḥ sarve prasūyante 
[84,ix_85,ii]	nanu sattva darśanam doṣa mūlam na mohaḥ iti āha sa ca sat kāya darśanam sa ca mohaḥ sat kāya darśanam nanu mohaḥ asaṃprakhyāna rūpaḥ sattva dṛṣṭiḥ tu viparīta artha pratipatti rūpā tat katham mohaḥ eva sattva darśanam iti āha vidyāyāḥ pratipakṣa tvāt caittattvena upalabdhitaḥ mithyā upalabdhiḥ ajñānam yukteḥ ca anyat yuktimat 
[85,iii]	vidyāyāḥ pratipakṣa tvāt vidyāyāḥ nairātmya dṛṣṭeḥ vipakṣaḥ avidyā sa ca aprakhyāna mātram vā rūpa ādi vā na bhavati nirvāṇepi tayoḥ bhāvāt kintu mithyā upalabdhiḥ ajñānam avidyā adharma anṛta vat vidyāyāḥ sat artha tvāt caittatvena upalabdhitaḥ ca caittatvena karaṇena upalabdhi rūpa tvāt ca āśraya ālambana ākāra kāla dravya samatā ādibhiḥ samam prayuktāḥ saṃprayuktāḥ iti saṃprayukta lakṣaṇam na ca asaṃprakhyānasya nīrūpasya ālambana ākāra yogaḥ iti mithyājñānam avidyā ukte arthe virodhāt bha gavatā pyuktam yāḥ kāścana loka vyavahāra upapattayaḥ sarvāḥ tāḥ ātma abhiniveśatobhavanti ātma abhiniveśa vigamataḥ na bhavanti iti anena sattva dṛṣṭiḥ eva janma hetuḥ uktā ātma abhiniveśa lakṣaṇa tvāt tasyāḥ atas anyat asaṃprakhyāna lakṣaṇam ajñānam ayuktam nirvāṇepi tat sattvāt 
[85,iv_85,vi]	nanu yadi avidyā dṛṣṭiḥ eva tathā ca dṛṣṭi saṃprayuktā avidyā iti saṃprayukta arthaḥ na syāt na sā tena eva samprayuktā kintu sakala kleśa anugatā avidyā sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ tu tat eka deśaḥ tatas cagama avirodhaḥ iti āha vyākhyeyaḥ atra virodhaḥ yaḥ atra vidyā nirdeśe āgama virodha yaḥ prasajati sa sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvena bheda kalpanayā vyākhyeyaḥ samarthanīyaḥ yathā palāśa yuktam vanam iti dṛṣṭi svabhāvā avidyā prādhānyena kleśa hetuḥ iti upadarśanañca prayojanam 
[85,vii_86,ii]	prakṛtam āha yatas ca evam ātma darśana prabhūtāḥ sarva kleśāḥ tad virodhāt ca tad mayaiḥ virodhaḥ śūnyatā dṛṣṭeḥ sarva doṣaiḥ prasidhyati tayā sattva dṛṣṭyā virodhāt ca śūnyatā dṛṣṭeḥ nairātmya dṛṣṭeḥ tad mayaiḥ sattva dṛṣṭi hetukaiḥ sarva doṣaiḥ virodhaḥ sidhyati śīta viruddhasya agneḥ iva tad kārye roma harṣa ādibhiḥ atas sa ātmībhūta nairātmyānām na punar doṣa leśa utpattiḥ anena niḥśaraṇate iti nirodha ākāraḥ nirddiṣṭaḥ doṣebhyaḥ sarvathā niḥśaraṇāt 
[86,iii_86,iv]	na akṣayaḥ prāṇi dharma tvāt rūpa ādi vat asiddhitaḥ sambandhe pratipakṣasya tyāgasya adarśanāt api syāt etat akṣayaḥ rāga ādiḥ prāṇi dharma tvāt rūpa ādi vat na yuktam etat asiddhitaḥ na hi prāṇī kaścid asti yat dharmāḥ rāga ādayaḥ siddhyanti sattve dṛṣṭau tu satyām kevalam upalabhyante iti pratītyasamutpāda mātram etat teṣām pratipakṣasya nairātmya darśanasya sambandhe saṃmukhībhāve tyāgasya āpāta viṣkambhaṇasya adarśanāt api sambhavat pratipakṣa tvena uccheda sambhavāt na akṣayi tvam 
[86,v_86,vii]	syāt etat tāmra ādīnām agni yogāt drava avasthāyām naṣṭam api kāṭhinyam punar śīta samparkāt utpadyate tadvat naṣṭānām api doṣāṇām mārga sātmye punar kutaścid hetoḥ utpattiḥ syāt atra āha na kāṭhinya vat utpattiḥ punar doṣa virodhinaḥ sa ātma tvena anapāya tvāt anekāntāt ca bhasma vat na kāṭhinya vat utpattiḥ punar doṣāṇām doṣa virodhinaḥ nairātmyasya sa ātma tvena prakṛti tvena anapāyāt na hi avyāhate virodhini tad viruddhasya utpatti ragnau iva śīta kāṭhinyam kādācitka tvāt agni nivṛttau tad virodhinyāḥ drava tāyāḥ svarasa nirodhāt utpadyate anaikāntāt ca bhasma vat yathā bhasmani bhūte punar na kāṣṭhotpattiḥ tathā nairātmya sa ātma tāyām na punar naṣṭānām doṣāṇām utpattiḥ iti anaikāntika tā naṣṭa utpatteḥ 
[86,viii_87,i]	nanu ātma bhāvanayā api mokṣa usti tat kim nairātmya bhāvanayā yat āhuḥ ātmā mantavyaḥ nididhyāsitavyaḥ ityādi atra āha yaḥ paśyati ātmānam tatra asya aham iti śāśvataḥ snehaḥ snehāt sukheṣu tṛṣyati tṛṣṇāḥ doṣān tiraskurute yaḥ paśyati ātmānam tatra ātmani asya draṣṭuḥ aham iti śāśvataḥ anupāyi snehaḥ bhavati 
[87,ii_87,iv]	snehāt ātma snehāt sukheṣu tṛṣyati tṛṣṇāvān bhavati iti tṛṣṇā ca sukha sādhana tvena adhyavasitānām vastūnām doṣān aśuci tva ādīn tiraskurute pracchādayati doṣa tiraskaraṇāt guṇa darśī paritṛṣyan mama iti tad sādhanāni upādatte tena ātma abhiniveśaḥ yāvat tāvat sa saṃsāre guṇa darśī śuci tveṣṭa tva guṇān paśyan paritṛṣyan mama iti mama idam sukham iti garddhamānaḥ tasya sukhasya sādhanāni garbha gamana ādīni upādatte 
[87,v_87,viii]	tena ātma darśana mūla tvena janma ādeḥ ātma abhiniveśaḥ yāvat tāvat saḥ ātma darśī saṃsāraḥ eva na kevalam janma prabandhaḥ tasya doṣāḥ api samastāḥ santi iti āha atmani sati para saṃjñā sva para vibhāgāt parigraha dveṣau anayoḥ saṃpratibaddhāḥ sarve doṣāḥ prajāyante ātmani sati tatas anyasmin para saṃjñā para buddhiḥ bhavati sva para vibhāgāt ca kāraṇāt sva parayoḥ yathākramam parigrahaḥ abhiṣvaṅgaḥ dveṣaḥ parityāgaḥ tau bhavataḥ anayoḥ anunaya pratiṣedhayoḥ saṃpratibaddhāḥ sarve doṣāḥ rāga mātsarya īrṣyā ādayaḥ prajāyante 
[87,ix_87,xi]	yadi api ātmani snehavān tathā api atmīye sukha sādhane vairāgyāt na saṃsarati iti ced na etat yuktam yatas niyamena ātmani snihyan tadīye na virajyate ātmani snihyan prīyamāṇaḥ tadīyaḥ ātmīye sukha sādhane niyamena na virajyate abhiṣvajati eva tat katham ātmīya virāgāt muktiḥ ātma snehasya ātmīya vairāgya virodhi tvāt 
[87,xii_88,i]	tam eva tyajati iti ced āha ne ca asti ātmani nirdoṣe sneha apagama kāraṇam snehaḥ sa doṣaḥ iti ced tatas kim tasya varjanam yadi api ātmā nirdoṣaḥ tathā api snehaḥ sa doṣaḥ iti ced tatas sa doṣa tvāt kim kartavyam tasya snehasya varjanam 
[88,ii_88,v]	aduṣite asya viṣaye na śakyam tasya varjanam adūṣitesya viṣayaḥ ātmani na śakyam tasya varjanam na hi snehaḥ sva guṇa doṣābhyām upādīyate tyajyate vā kintu viṣayasya viṣayaḥ ca nirdoṣaḥ iti katham asya varjanam kiñca prahāṇiḥ icchā dveṣa ādeḥ guṇa doṣa anubandhinaḥ tayoḥ adṛṣṭiḥ viṣaye 
[88,vi_88,vii]	icchā dveṣa ādeḥ guṇa doṣa anubandhinaḥ yathākramam viṣayasya guṇa doṣa anuvartinaḥ prahāṇiḥ prahāṇi upāyaḥ tayoḥ guṇa doṣayoḥ adṛṣṭiḥ viṣaye ananya upāya tā darśana artham upacāraḥ viṣaya guṇa doṣa adarśane eva icchā dveṣa ādi prahāṇi upāyaḥ iti arthaḥ nanu adṛṣṭopi iti ādiḥ anicchā mātrāt tyajyamānaḥ dṛśyate iti āha 
[88,viii_88,xi]	na tu bāhyeṣu yaḥ kramaḥ na tu bāhyeṣu vastuṣu yaḥ kramaḥ anicchā mātra kṛta tyāga rūpaḥ saḥ āntareṣu api sneha ādiṣu yuktaḥ bāhya adhīnam bāhyam anicchayā tyaktum śakyam ātma darśana adhīnantu na śakya parihāram avikala hetu tvena utpatteḥ kiñca na hi sneha guṇāt snehaḥ kintu artha guṇa darśanāt kāraṇe avikale tasmin kāryam kena nivāryate 
[88,xii_89,i]	na hi sneha guṇāt snehaḥ kriyate kintu arthasya viṣayasya guṇa doṣa darśanāt jāyate kāraṇe avikale tasmin viṣaya guṇe kāryam snehaḥ kena nivāryate na kenacid kā vā sa doṣa tā dṛṣṭā snehe duḥkha samāśrayaḥ kā vā sa doṣa tā dṛṣṭā snehe yena ayam varjayitavyaḥ duḥkhasya samāśrayaḥ ced doṣaḥ tathā hi ātmani snihyan tad sukha sādhaneṣu tṛṣṇāvān duḥkha bhūtam saṃsāram upādatte 
[89,ii_89,vi]	tathā api na virāgaḥ atra sva tva dṛṣṭeḥ yatha ātmani tathā api duḥkha hetu tvepi na virogaḥ atra snehe yathā ātmani sva tva dṛṣṭeḥ duḥkha nidāna bhūtāyāḥ hetau ātmani na virāgaḥ yadi duḥkha hetau virāgaḥ tathā sva tve dṛṣṭi dvāreṇa sarvam duḥkham iti tasya hetau ātmani eva sa yuktaḥ na ca asti etat na taiḥ vinā duḥkha hetuḥ ātmā ced te api tādṛśāḥ na taiḥ sneha buddhīndriya ādibhiḥ ātmīyaiḥ vinā duḥkha hetuḥ ātmā ced tepi sneha ādayaḥ tādṛśāḥ ātmānam antareṇa na duḥkha hetavaḥ 
[89,vii_89,viii]	nirdoṣam dvayam api evam vairāgyāt na dvayoḥ tatas duḥkha bhāvanayā syāt ced ahidaṣṭa aṅga hāni vat evam paraspara sāpekṣa tve nirdoṣam dvayam api sneha ādiḥ ātmā ca vairāgyan na dvayoḥ api tatas kāryam tathā ca saṃsāraḥ doṣāḥ ca durvārāḥ hetu sākalyāt pravṛttiḥ yadi sneha ādiṣu duḥkha bhāvanayā hāniḥ syāt ahidaṣṭasya aṅgasya hāni vat yathā ātmīyam api ahidaṣṭam aṅgam duḥkha vaśāt virajya tyajyate anupabhoga āśraya tvāt 
[89,ix_89,x]	ātmīya buddhi hānyā atra tyāgaḥ na tu viyaryaye upabhoga āśraya tvena gṛhīteṣu indriya ādiṣu sva tvadhīḥ kena vāryeta vairāgyam tatra tat kutas ātmīya buddhi hānyā tatra ahi daṣṭa aṅge tyāgaḥ na tu viparyaye ātmīya buddhi sattāyām yasmāt upabhogasya āśraya tvena kāraṇa tvena gṛhīteṣu indriya ādiṣu sva tve dhīra ātmīya tva buddhiḥ kena hetunā vāryeta na kenacid tad kutas tatra upabhoga sādhane svīya avayave vairāgyam yena tyajyate tatas yat tyajyate ātmīya buddhi hānyāḥ eva na ca evam sneha ādiṣu ātmīya buddhi hāniḥ asti yena eṣām tyāgaḥ syāt 
[90,i_90,iii]	pratyakṣam eva sarvasya keśa ādiṣu kalevarāt cyuteṣu sadhṛṇā buddhiḥ jāyate anyeṣu sa spṛhā etat ca pratyakṣam eva sarvasya keśa ādiṣu kalevarāt cyuteṣu ātmīya buddhi viṣayeṣu sadhṛṇā buddhiḥ jāyate janasya anyatra acyuteṣu ātmīya buddhi viṣayeṣu sa spṛhā duḥkha bhāvanayā ātmīya buddhiḥ eva hīyate iti ced na yuktam idam 
[90,iv_90,v]	samavāya ādi sambandha janitā tatra hi svadhīḥ samavāya ādi sambandha janitāḥ hi yasmāt tatra buddhi ādau svadhīḥ tathā ca ātmanaḥ sukha ādīnā samavāyaḥ sambandhaḥ śarīreṇa saṃyogaḥ śarīra āśritaiḥ rūpa ādibhiḥ saṃyukta samavāyaḥ śrotra indriyeṇa saṃyogaḥ cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ saṃyogi saṃyogaḥ ātma sambandhaḥ 
[90,vi_90,vii]	sa tathā eva iti sā doṣa dṛṣṭau api na hīyate samavāya ādi abhāve api sarvatra asti upakāritā sa duḥkha bhāvanāyām api tathā eva iti sā sva dhīḥ doṣa dṛṣṭau api na hīyate nimittasya avaikalyāt atha samavāya ādiḥ na asti eva tadā samavāya ādi abhāve api sarvatra buddhi ādau asti upakāritā tad kṛtā 
[90,viii_90,ix]	duḥkha upakārāt na bhavet aṅgulyām iva ced svadhīḥ na hi ekāntena tat dukham bhūyasā sa viṣān na vat tatra sva dhīra śakya dhāraṇā duḥkha upakārāt duḥkha upanidhānāt na bhavet ahi daṣṭāyām aṅgulyām iva sneha buddhi ādau svadhīḥ iti ced na hi ekāntena tad sneha ādi duḥkham duḥkha hetuḥ paryāyeṇa sukha hetu tvāt api kintu bhūyasā tad duḥkham sa viṣān na vat pariṇati duḥkha hetuḥ api viṣa annam āpāta sukham ca 
[90,x_91,ii]	nanu sa viṣam annam sukha miśrañca vairāgya viṣayaḥ sva hita kāmānām evam sneha ādiḥ api syāt iti āha viśiṣṭa sukha saṅgāt syāt tad viruddhe virāgi tā viśiṣṭe sukhe sukha sādhane tadātva pariṇābhayoḥ anugrahi itari viṣa ādi doṣa rahita bhojana ādau saṅgāt abhiṣvaṅgāt syāt tat viruddhe saviṣa anna ādau virāgi tā vairāgyāt ca kiñcid parityajet saukhyam viśiṣṭa sukha tṛṣṇayā 
[91,iii]	kiñcid saukhyam pariṇati duḥkha bahulam parityajet ātma kāmaḥ viśiṣṭasya sukhasya pariṇāma aviruddhasya tṛṣṇayā abhilāṣeṇa yadā tu ātmani sati na kiñcid sukha eka rūpam sarvam sukham duḥkha saṃbhiśram tadā kva parihāraḥ kasmin anurāgaḥ svīkāraḥ na ca icchayā aśakya parihārāḥ sneha ādayaḥ tad kāraṇasya ātmanaḥ avaikalyāt iti uktam 
[91,iv_91,vi]	nanu anairātmya pakṣepi duḥkham sakalam tad nirodhaḥ para sukham tad kvacid tṛṣṇayā pravṛttiḥ na syāt iti āha nairātmye tu yathālābham ātma snehāt pravartate alābhe mattakāsinyā dṛṣṭā tiryakṣu kāmitā nairātmya tattve adhāya upāda ātma snehāt sukha viparyāsāt duḥkheṣu api sukha tayā adhyavasiteṣu viṣayeṣu yathālābham prāpti anukrameṇa pravṛttiḥ bhavati nirvāṇa sukha vyutpatti abhāvāt vyutpattau api tad mārga sa ātma tva abhāvāt sā ātmīkṛta mārggāḥ tu kvacid na pravartante eva tathā ca alābhe mattakāsinyā matta gaja gāminyā kāmukasya tiryakṣu kāmitā dṛṣṭā balavān ātma snehaḥ viśiṣṭa sukha sādhanasya alābhe sukha ābhāsa hetau ca pravartayati 
[91,vii_91,ix]	kiñca yadi buddhīndriya śarīra ādīnām duḥkha hetu tvāt teṣu vairāgyāt tad tyāgāt kaivalyam ātmanaḥ iṣṭam mukti daśa āyān tad ātma bhoga ādi sakala pariccheda abhāvāt nāśā viśeṣāt nāśaḥ eva iṣṭaḥ syāt tat ca idam ayuktam iti āha yasya ātmā vallabhaḥ tasya sa nāśam katham icchati yasya ātmā vallabhaḥ tasya sa katham nāśam icchati na nāśam kaivalyam apratīti viṣaya tvāt icchati 
[91,x_92,v]	katham punar kevalam ātmānam icchat nāśam icchati iti āha nivṛtta sarva anubhava vyavahāra guṇa śrayam icchet prema katham nivṛttaḥ sarvasya a anubhava vyavahārasya samāśrayaḥ āśrayaṇam yasmāt tam nāśa lakṣaṇa aviśiṣṭam iti arthaḥ nāśā viśiṣṭañcā ātmānam katham prema sneha atiśayaḥ icchet yasmāt premṇaḥ prakṛtiḥ na hi tādṛśī premṇaḥ prakṛtiḥ tādṛśī sva viṣaya nāśa eṣaṇa svabhāvā na bhavati tasmāt sarvathā ātma grahaḥ sneham ātmani draḍhayati alam sarvathā ātma grahaḥ ātmani sneha malam atyartha draḍhayati 
[92,vi_92,x]	saḥ ātma grahaḥ ca ātma upakāriṣu ātmīyasneha bījantu tad avastham vyavasthitam ātmīya sneha bījam tad avastham vyavasthitam iti tad pratibaddhānām doṣa aṇāñcā nivṛttiḥ syāt etat ātmīye doṣa darśanāt vairāgyam utpadyate iti āha yatne api ātmīya vairāgyam guṇa leśa samāśrayāt vṛttimān pratibadhnāti tad doṣān saṃvṛṇoti ca 
[92,xi_92,xiii]	doṣa darśanāt yatna īpi sati tāvat kālam ātmīyeṣu vairāgyam yat utpannam tad ātma snehaḥ vṛtti mān ātmīyeṣu guṇa leśasya sukha sādhana tvasya samāśrayaṇāt pratibadhnāti tad doṣān ca duḥkha sādhana ādīn saṃvṛṇoti tat kutas ātma snehavataḥ ātmīye vairāgya yogaḥ ātma snehasya sarva doṣa mūla tvāt ātmani api virāgaḥ ced idānīm yaḥ virajyate ātmani api virāgaḥ ced vādhyate nanu uktam atra na ca ātmani nirdoṣe sneha apagama kāraṇam asti bhavatu tāvat tathā api idānīm atra api pakṣe yaḥ tatra virajyate 
[92,xiv_92,xv]	tyajati asau yathā ātmānam vyarthā atas duḥkha bhāvanā duḥkha bhāvanayā api eṣa duḥkham eva vibhāvayet tena sa tam tyajati yathā ātmānam na hi ātmani viraktopi tam tyajati tathā ātmīya ipi viraktaḥ tam na tyakṣyati iti vyarthātas duḥkha bhāvanā atmanaḥ atyāgāt duḥkha bhāvanayā api eṣa bhāvakaḥ duḥkham eva bhāvyamānam vibhāvayet prakāśayet 
[93,i_93,ii]	pratyakṣam pūrvam api tat tathā api na virāgavān yadi api ekatra doṣeṇa tad kṣaṇam calitā matiḥ tat ca bhāvanātaḥ pūrvam api pratyakṣam eva duḥkham ātma sneha ādi śastra prahāra ādi anubhava kāle tathā api pratyakṣīkṛtātma sneha ādi duḥkha tvepi na virāgavān teṣu kaśrcit tadā tatas bhāvanā prakarṣa ipi evam syāt sākṣātkaraṇa tvāt tasya tat ca na virāga hetuḥ prāk iva yadi api ekatra aparādha kāriṇi doṣa darśanāt tad kṣaṇam niyata kālam anurāgāt calitā matiḥ virāga bhajanāt 
[93,iii_93,v]	viraktaḥ na eva tatra api kāmī iva vanitā antare tyājya upādeya bhede hi saktiḥ yā eva eka bhāvinī tathā api asau tatra viraktaḥ sarvathā paryāyeṇa rāga utpatteḥ kim punar anyatra kāmī iva kvacid kāminyām rāga kāriṇyām viraktā upi na vanitā antare viraktaḥ tasyām api vā krameṇa kiñca pratidhā anunaya viṣaya tvāt tyājya upādeya bhede hi sati saktiḥ āsaktiḥ yā evekasmin bhāvinī dveṣa viṣaya tayā anurāga viṣaya tayā vā 
[93,vi_93,vii]	sā bījam sarva saktīnām paryāyeṇa samudbhave nirdoṣa viṣayaḥ snehaḥ nirdoṣaḥ sādhanāni ca sā saktiḥ bījam kāraṇam sarva saktīnām paryāyeṇa paripāṭyā samudbhava nimittam tathā hi kvacid dveṣa āsaktyā tad anukūla pratikūlayoḥ pratidhā anunayau bhavataḥ tathā anurāga āsaktyā api kvacid tayoḥ eva anunaya t veṣau bhavataḥ tat evam amātnaḥ nirdoṣa tvāt nirdoṣa viṣayaḥ snehaḥ nirdoṣaḥ svayam upabhoga sādhanāni ca indriya śarīra ādini śabda rasa rūpa ādīni nirdoṣāṇi ātma ādīnām sarveṣām pratyekam duḥkha hetu tva abhāvāt 
[93,viii_94,i]	etāvat eva ca jagat kva idānīm sa virajyate sa doṣa tā api ced tasya tatra ātmani api sā samā etāvat eva ca jagat tribhiḥ jagataḥ saṃgrahāt kva idānīm sa moktu kāmaḥ virajyate samudāyāt doṣa darśanāt tatas eva virajyate ced nanu evam ātmani api vairāgyam prāptam na kevalam guṇavattā sa doṣa tā api ced tasya sneha indriya ādeḥ tatra ātmani api kaivalyena iṣṭe sā sa doṣa tā samā tasyāḥ api sneha ādi doṣavat tvāt 
[94,ii_94,vi]	evantarhi ātma doṣam eva vairāgya bhāvanāyāḥ jahyāt iti ced tatra aviraktaḥ tad doṣe kva idānīm sa virajyate tatra ātmani aviraktaḥ tad doṣe kva idānīm ātma darśana kāle sa mumukṣuḥ virajyate yathā sa doṣa īpya ātmani ātma darśanāt aviraktaḥ tathā tad doṣepi snehāt ātmīya tva darśanāt na virajyeta api ca guṇa darśana sambhūtam sneham bādhita doṣa dṛś guṇa darśana sambhūtam sneham bārdhita doṣasya dṛś dṛṣṭiḥ
[94,vii_94,viii]	sa ca indriya ādau na tu evam bāla ādeḥ api sambhavāt doṣavatī api sadbhāvāt svabhāvāt guṇavatī api anyatra sa ca sneha ja indriya ādau evam guṇa darśanāt na dṛṣṭaḥ bāla ādeḥ api guṇa parīkṣā abhyupagamya cakṣuḥ ādau ātmīya tva mātreṇa snehasya sambhavāt guṇa doṣa darśanāt na sneha bhāva abhāvī kintvā ātmīya tva darśana adarśanāt tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt iti darśayati ca svakīye cakṣuḥ ādau guṇa vikale kāṇa tva ādi doṣavatī api ātmīya tva parāmarśāt snehasya sadbhāvāt anyatra parakīye netra ādau doṣa rahite guṇavatī api 
[94,ix_94,x]	ātmīyatāyām vā vyatīta ādau vihānitaḥ tatas eva ca na ātmīya buddheḥ api guṇa īkṣaṇam kāraṇam ātmīyatāyām api vā atīta ādau keśa nakha ādau ādi śabdāt lūna aṅgulī ādau vartamānena snehaḥ ātmīya tvena adṛṣṭeḥ vihānitaḥ parityāgāt sva tvasya tatas eva ca bāla ādeḥ api bhāvāt ātmīya buddheḥ api na guṇa īkṣaṇam kāraṇam kintvā ātma darśanam eva 
[95,i_95,iii]	hīyate sā api tasmāt na aguṇa darśanāt tasmāt guṇa darśana hetuka tva abhāvāt sā ātmīya buddhiḥ api aguṇasya doṣasya darśanāt na hīyate kāraṇa viruddhaḥ hi dharmī nivartakaḥ kasyacid yathā agniḥ romāñca viśeṣasya ātma darśanam hi sneha ātmīya dṛśa ādeḥ kāraṇam na ca tad virodhinī doṣa dṛś api ca asat guṇa āropaḥ snehāt tatra hi dṛśyate tasmāt tad kāraṇa bādhī vidhiḥ tam bādhate katham 
[95,iv_95,vii]	api ca asatām guṇānām āropaḥ tatra ātmīye snehāt hi yasmāt dṛśyate tasmāt tasya sneha ādeḥ kāraṇasya ātma darśanasya ābādhī abādhakaḥ vidhiḥ dīkṣā duḥkha bhāvanā ādi rūpaḥ tam sneha ādim bādhate katham kāraṇa anivṛttyā kārya niṣedhasya kartum aśakyatvāt sāṃkhyāḥ tu manyaṃte cetana acetanayoḥ puruṣa pradhānayoḥ yāvat aikyam manyate puruṣaḥ tāvat sa snehavān ayuktaḥ ca bheda pratītau na snehaḥ viyuktaḥ ca iti atra āha parāpara prārthanātaḥ vināśa utpāda buddhitaḥ kāṇa tva ādi doṣa yuktā parāparasya viśiṣṭa viśiṣṭasya cakṣuḥ śarīra ādikasya prārthanātaḥ ātmanaḥ ca anyasya anabhilāṣataḥ tasmāt pṛthak bhūtam ātmānam ayam amuktā upi janaḥ vetti tathā vināśa utpāda buddhitaḥ 
[95,viii_95,ix]	indriya ādau pṛthak bhūtam ātmānam vetti ayam janaḥ tasmāt na eka tva dṛṣṭyā api snehaḥ snihyan saḥ ātmani śarīra indriya ādau viparyayāt ca ātmani bhinnam ātmānam tebhyaḥ vetti tasmāt na eka tva dṛṣṭyā api snehaḥ kintvā ātma darśanāt saḥ ātma darśī snihyan ātmani 
[95,x_95,xi]	upalambha antaraṅgeṣu prakṛtyā eva anurajyate pratyutpannāt tu yaḥ duḥkhāt nirvedaḥ dveṣaḥ īdṛśaḥ na vairāgyam upalambha antaraṅgeṣu upabhoga sādhaneṣu indriya ādiṣu prakṛtyā svabhāvena eva anurajyate pratyutpannāt tu vartamānāt punar duḥkhāt nirvedaḥ yaḥ sa na vairāgyam kintu dveṣaḥ īdṛśaḥ 
[96,i_96,ii]	tat api asya snehaḥ avasthā antareṣaṇāt dveṣasya duḥkha yoni tvāt sa tāvat mātra saṃsthitiḥ yasmāt tadā api nirveda avasthāyām sneha usya asti na ca viraktasya sneha sambhavaḥ tat astitvam eva kutas iti ced avasthā antarasya duḥkha hetoḥ nirveda kāriṇyām avasthāyām vilakṣaṇasya eṣaṇāt na hi sneham antareṇa eka tyāgāt apara vāñchā dveṣasya duḥkhasya yoni tvāt sa nirveda ākhyaḥ dveṣaḥ yāvat duḥkham anuvartate tāvat mātram tāvat kāla parimāṇam saṃsthitiḥ asya iti 
[96,iii_96,vi]	tasmin nivṛtta īprakṛtim svām eva bhajate punar tathā tasmin duḥkhe kāraṇa nirodhāt nivṛtte punar svām eva prakṛtim viṣayeṣu avirāga lakṣaṇām bhajate sattva darśī kīdṛśam tarhi vairāgyam yuktam audāsīnyam tu sarvatra tyāga upādāna hānitaḥ vāsī candana kalpānām vairāgyam nāma kathyate 
[96,vii_96,x]	sattva dṛṣṭi abhāvāt sarvatra viṣaye pratikūla tva anukūla tvābhyām anadhyavasite tyāga upadānayoḥ hānitaḥ vāsī candrana kalpanām vāsī candanayoḥ kalpāḥ sadṛśāḥ ye vāsī candana kalpāḥ vā ye teṣām sākṣātkṛta nairātmya tattvānām audāsīnyam anunaya pratigha rahita tvam punar vairāgyam nāma āgama prasiddham kathyate nanu yadi duḥkha bhāvanayā snehāt iha anyāḥ na muktiḥ tat katham bhagavatā uktāḥ duḥkha bhāvanā iti āha saṃskāra duḥkha tām matvā kathitā duḥkha bhāvanā saṃskāra duḥkha tām mattvā kathitā duḥkha bhāvanā na hi duḥkha duḥkha tām abhisandhāya tad bhāvanā uktā kintarhi saṃskāra duḥkha tām 
[96,xi_97,iv]	sā eva kim ucyate iti āha sā ca naḥ pratyaya utpattiḥ sā nairātmya dṛś āśrayaḥ sā ca saṃskāra duḥkha tā naḥ asmākam saugatānām pratyaya utpattiḥ hetu pāratantryam sā pratyaya utpattiḥ nairātmyasya dṛśaḥ darśanasya āśrayaḥ kāraṇam tathā hi hetu phala bhūtāḥ kṣaṇa kṣayiṇaḥ bhāvāḥ pravṛttayaḥ na ātma rūpā na api ātma adhiṣṭhitā iti saṃskāra duḥkha tā bhāvanā nairātmya darśana anukūlā sā eva ca mukti hetuḥ iti āha muktiḥ tu śūnyatā dṛṣṭeḥ tad arthāḥ śeṣa bhāvanāḥ muktiḥ tu śūnyatāyāḥ nirātmatāyāḥ dṛṣṭeḥ śeṣasya nitya duḥkha ādeḥ bhāvanāḥ tad arthāḥ nirātma darśana arthāḥ 
[97,v_97,ix]	anityāt prāha tena eva duḥkham duḥkhāt nirātma tām tena eva anitya duḥkha bhāvanāyāḥ śūnyatā bhāvanā anukūla tvena bhagavān anityāt anitya tvāt duḥkham saṃsāri skandhānām hānāt duḥkhāt duḥkha tvāt nirātma tām āha tat yathā rūpam bhikṣavaḥ nityam anityam vā anityam bhadanta yat anityam tat duḥkham sukham vā duḥkhambhadanta yat anityam duḥkham vipariṇāma dharmakam kalpyannu tat evam draṣṭuḥ etat mama eṣoham asmi eṣa me ātmā iti no hi idam bhadanta iti evam hetu phala bhāvanena ātma darśanam eva mukteḥ upāyaḥ iti kathitam tat eva ācāryeṇa uktam uktaḥ mārgaḥ tad abhyāsāt āśrayaḥ parivartate iti na asti virodhaḥ yaḥ punar ātma darśī saḥ aviraktaḥ eva aviraktaḥ ca tṛṣṇāvān sarva ārambha samāśritaḥ aviraktaḥ ca tṛṣṇāvān hāni upādāna lakṣaṇān karma prasava hetūn samāśritaḥ 
[97,x_97,xi]	saḥ amuktaḥ kleśa karmabhyām saṃsārī nāma tādṛśaḥ ātmīyam eva yaḥ na icchet bhoktā api asya na vidyate saḥ amuktaḥ kleśa karmabhyām ātma darśana pravṛtti kāraṇakābhyām saṃsārī nāma prasiddhaḥ tādṛśaḥ tat evam ātmani sati na ātmīya tyāgaḥ tathā amuktiḥ iti uktam bhavatu vā atmīya tyāgaḥ tathā āpi ātmīyam eva yaḥ na icchet tat mate asi a ātmīyasya bhoktā na vidyate bhogya apekṣa tvāt bhoktṛ tvasya 
[98,i_98,ii]	ātmā api na tadā tasya kriyā bhogau hi lakṣaṇam tasmāt anādi santāna tulya jātīya bījikām utkhāta mūlām kuruta satva dṛṣṭim mumukṣavaḥ bhoktṛ a bhāve ātmā api na asti iti prasaṅgāt kutas iti ced hiḥ yasmāt asya ātmanaḥ kriyā bhogau lakṣaṇam karttā bhoktā ca ātmā ucyate yadā ca ātmīyam eva na asti kimartham karma kartavyam kim vā bhoktavyam kartṛ tva bhoktṛ tva abhāvāt ātma abhāvaḥ eva svīkṛtaḥ syāt tasmāt satya ātmani ātmīyam tad sneha ādi sattve anucchedaḥ evam saṃsārasya tasmāt saṃsārāt udvijamānā mumukṣavaḥ utkhāta mūlām uddhṛta kāraṇām sattva dṛṣṭim kuruta 
[98,iii_98,v]	nanu kim asyāḥ mūlam iti āha anādi santānaḥ tulya jātīyaḥ pūrva pūrva sattva darśana svabhāvaḥ avidyā rūpaḥ bījam kāraṇam yasya āḥ tām sattva darśanam avidyā svabhāvam pūrva pūrvam uttarottarasya sattva darśanasya hetuḥ iti arthaḥ nanu uktam īśvareṇa āgame asti ātmā mokṣaḥ ca asya dīkṣā vidhinā iti tat kim atra cintyate tad kāraṇā vā dhī vidhiḥ tam bādhate katham ityādinā ukta tvāt atra āha 
[98,vi_98,ix]	āgamasya tathā abhāva nibandhanam apaśyatām muktim āgama mātreṇa vadan na paritoṣa kṛt āgamasya tathā abhāvasya pratipādita artha samvādi tvasya nibandhanam hetum apaśyatām mumukṣūṇām āgama mātreṇa muktim vadan na paritoṣa kṛt bhavati dīkṣā akiñcitkarī nanu asti prāmāṇya nibandhanam āgamasya dīkṣā vidhi spṛṣṭasya anāroha dharmaka tva darśanam yathā hi bījam dīkṣā vidhi spṛṣṭam na prarohati tathā pumān api dīkṣitaḥ na punar bhavati iti āha 
[99,i_99,iv]	na alam bīja ādi saṃsiddhaḥ vidhiḥ puṃsām ajanmane taila abhyaṅga agni ha ādeḥ api mukti prasaṅgataḥ na alam śaktaḥ bīja ādiṣu saṃsiddhaḥ vidhiḥ dīkṣāyāḥ puṃsām ajanmane taila abhyaṅga agni dāha deḥ api saṃsārat mukti prasaṅgataḥ tailena abhyaktam bījam agninā ca spṛṣṭam na prarohati tathā puruṣopi taila abhyaṅga agni dāhābhyām na punar bhavet syāt etat dīkṣāyāḥ prāk pāpa guroḥ uttaram tulayā lāghavāt pāpa abhāva upalambhaḥ āgama prāmāṇya nibandhanam iti āha prāk guroḥ lāghavāt paścāt na pāpa haraṇam kṛtam mā bhūt gauravam eva asya na pāpam guru amūrttitaḥ 
[99,v]	prāk guroḥ lāghavāt paścāt na pāpa haraṇam kṛtam dīkṣāyāḥ prāk guroḥ paścāt lāghavāt dīkṣayā na pāpa haraṇasya dīkṣitasya kintu gauravam eva asya kṛtam sat mā bhūt iti kasmāt na kalpyate lāghavam hi gaurava virodhi dṛśyamānam tad abhāvam eva gamayet na pāpa bhāvam pāpam eva guru iticed na pāpam guru amūrttitaḥ mūrtta tva abhāvāt bhūrtta dharmaḥ hi gauravam katham pāpasya amūrttasya syāt 
[99,vi_99,xii]	nanu tvad pakṣe api nairātmya darśane bhūtepi kasmāt na janma iti āha mithyājñāna tad udbhūta tarṣa sañcetana avaśāt hīna sthāna gatiḥ janma tatas tacchinna jāyate mithyājñānam duḥkhe viparyāsa matiḥ tad udbhūtaḥ tarṣaḥ mithyājñāna prabhavā tṛṣṇā tābhyām saṃprayukte cetane tad vaśa ādyāḥ hīna sthāna gatiḥ tad janma iti uktam atas tad chit ajñāna tṛṣṇā ācchedakaḥ nairātmya darśī na jātaye kāraṇa abhāvāt tat eva āha tayoḥ eva hi sāmarthyam jātau tanmātra bhāvataḥ tayoḥ eva ajñāna tṛṣṇayoḥ hi sāmarthyam jātau janma nimittam tanmātreṇa bhāvataḥ te ca dīkṣitasya api staḥ iti sa jāyate 
[100,i_100,iii]	nanu karma api janma kāraṇam iṣṭam tat katham ajñāna tṛṣṇe eva ukte iti āha te cetane svayam karma iti akhaṇḍam janma kāraṇam gati pratītyoḥkaraṇāni āśrayaḥ tāni adṛṣṭataḥ adṛṣṭa nāśā āda gatiḥ tad saṃskāraḥ na cetanā te cetane mithyājñāna tad udbhūta ṛṣa saṃcetane svayam ātmanā pūrva śubha aśubha karma saṃskāra sahāye karma karma svabhāve iti akhaṇḍa manyūnam janma kāraṇam uktam iti na virodhaḥ syāt etat gati pratītyoḥ abhimata deśa gamanasya jñānasya ca karaṇāni indriyāṇi āśrayaḥ kāraṇam indriyebhyaḥ utpannena jñānena viṣayam paricchidya pravṛtteḥ tāni indriyāṇi ca adṛṣṭataḥ śubha ādi lakṣaṇāt dīkṣayā ca adṛṣṭa nāśāt tad kāryāṇām kāraṇānām anutpatteḥ viṣayasya pariccheda tṛṣṇayoḥ abhāvāt agatiḥ janma sthānaḥ iti na asti punarbhavaḥ dīkṣitasya tad adṛṣṭañca ātma saṃskāraḥ na cetanā syāt dīkṣitasya api sā asti iti janma api syāta 
[100,iv_100,vi]	atra āha sāmarthyam karaṇa utpatteḥ bhāva abhāva anuvṛttitaḥ dṛṣṭam buddheḥ na ca anyasyāḥ santi tāni nayanti kim buddheḥ bhāva abhāva anuvṛttitaḥ anvaya vyatireka anuvṛttyā karaṇānām ekasmāt deśāt apara deśa sambaddhānām utpatteḥ kāraṇāt sāmārthyam buddheḥ indriya jananam pratidṛṣṭam na anyasya saṃskāra rūpasya adṛṣṭasya tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna anupalambhāt sā buddhiḥ ca asti deśa antara sambaddha karaṇa janikā dīkṣitasyā tad kintāni karaṇāni garbha sthānan na yanti gacchanti hetu avaikalyāt bhavitavyam 
[100,vii_100,ix]	gamanena avaśyam dīkṣayā upahatāḥ buddhiḥ deśa antaram netum indriyāṇi aśaktā ced dhāraṇa preraṇa kṣobha nirodhāḥ cetanā vaśāḥ na syuḥ teṣām asāmarthye tasya dīkṣā ādi anantaram atha buddheḥ tadā abhāvāt na syuḥ sandhīyate malaiḥ nanu evantasya mumukṣoḥ dīkṣa anantaram buddheḥ asāmarthye teṣām indriyāṇām sva viṣaye vyavasthāpanam dhāraṇam tatra ayojanam preraṇam kṣobhaḥ vikāraḥ sva viṣayān nivartanam nirodhaḥ te buddhi nibandhana vṛttayaḥ na syuḥ atha buddheḥ tadā maraṇa kāle abhāvāt na syuḥ dhāraṇa preraṇa ādayaḥ 
[101,i_101,iii]	atra āha sandhīyate janyate malaiḥ mithyā jñānaiḥ mithyājñāna ātma sneha ādibhiḥ buddhiḥ maraṇa samayepī iti kutas buddhi abhāvaḥ buddheḥ teṣām asāmarthye jīvataḥ api syuḥ akṣamāḥ nirhrāsa atiśayāt puṣṭau pratipakṣa sva pakṣayoḥ doṣāḥ sva bīja santānāḥ dīkṣite api anivāritāḥ atha malāḥ api dīkṣayā upahata sāmarthyāḥ na buddhi sandadhati tadā teṣām malānām asāmarthye svīkriyamāṇe jīvatopi dīkṣitasya malāḥ buddhi sandhānam pratyakṣamāḥ syuḥ dīkṣā malānām bādhikā iti api mithyā tathā pratipakṣasya nairātmya bhāvanāyāḥ sva pakṣasya ayoni śoma naskārasya abhyāsāt puṣṭau satyām doṣāṇām yathākramam narhrāsāt apacayāt atiśayāt abhivṛddhe rdoṣāḥ svakīyāt bījāt tulya jātīya kāraṇāt santānaḥ yeṣām te dīkṣitepi doṣa bīje paripoṣavati anivāritāḥ 
[101,iv_101,vi]	syāt etat ātmanā upi garbha gata karaṇa ādi janane vyāpāraḥ saḥ eva dīkṣayā niruddhaḥ iti na punar janma iti āha nityasya nirapekṣa tvāt krama utpattiḥ virudhyate kriyā āyām akriyā yāñca kriyayoḥ sadṛśa ātmanaḥ aikyañca hetu phalayoḥ vyatirekaḥ tatas tayoḥ nityasya anupakārya tayā nirapekṣa tvāt karaṇa ādīnām krameṇa utpattiḥ virudhyate sama tva hetu sadbhāvāt sakṛt utpāda prasakteḥ indriya ādeḥ kriyā āyām akriyā yāñca sadṛśa ātmanaḥ tulya rūpasya ātmanaḥ tayoḥ kālayoḥ te te virudhyete 
[101,vii]	yadi asau kārya karaṇa svabhāvaḥ tadā kāryāt eva kriyā virāmosya virudhyate evam akriyāyām api vācyam kiñca ātmanaḥ karma kartṛ tā hetu tvam bhoktṛ tvañca phalam te ca ātmanaḥ eka rūpasya rūpe iti hetu phalā bheda prasaṅgaḥ vyatirekaḥ bhedaḥ tatas ātmanaḥ tayoḥ kartṛ tu abhoktṛ tvayoḥ dharmayoḥ tatas na aikya prasaṅgaḥ iti ced 
[102,i_102,iv]	kartṛ bhoktṛ tva hāniḥ syāt sāmarthyañca na sidhyati evam kartṛ tu abhoktṛ tvā hāniḥ syāt ātmanaḥ atad svabhāva tvāt tad sambandhāt kartā bhoktā ca anupakṛtasya sambandhi tve ati prasaṅgāt upakṛta tvam veditavyam tat ca aśakya sādhanam yasmāt nityasya avyatireki tvāt sāmarthyañca na sidhyati nanu yadi ātmā na asti tadā anyena anubhūtam karma ca kṛtam anyaḥ smarati bhuḍatkte phalam iti syāt tathā ca atiprasaṅgaḥ iti āha anya smaraṇa bhoga ādi prasaṅgaḥ ca na bādhakāḥ asmṛteḥ kasya cit tena hi anubhūteḥ smṛta udbhavaḥ 
[102,v]	anyasya smaraṇa bhoga ādi prasaṅgāḥ ca na bādhakāḥ bhavanti asmṛteḥ kasyacid smarttuḥ abhāvāt evam bhoga upi na asti bhoktṛ a bhāvāt tena hi tasmāt smartra bhāvāt kāraṇāt viṣayāṇām anubhūteḥ sakāśāt smṛtiḥ eva smṛtam tasya udbhavaḥ vastu dharmaḥ hi eṣa yat anubhavaḥ paṭīyān smaraṇa bīja ādhāna dvāreṇa smaraṇam janayati śubha aśubha cetanāḥ ca saṃskārāḥ bhoga ākāram samvidam pravartayanti tat kim smartṛ bhoktṛ durgraheṇa tad tad ākāraḥ pratītyasamutpannaḥ buddhi prabandhaḥ eva kevalaḥ na tu saṃsārī nāma kaścid 
[102,vi_102,viii]	yadi na asti ātmā katham sa kopa dṛṣṭiḥ saṃsāra pravṛttiḥ vā iti āha sthiram sukham mama ahañcā ityādi satya catuṣṭaye abhūtān ṣoḍaśa ākārān āropya paritṛṣyati sthira makṣaṇikam sukham tri duḥkha tā viparītam mama iti ātmīyam aham iti ātma ahaṃkāraḥ ca iti duḥkha satyasya viparītāḥ ākārāḥ iti ādyān prati satyam caturaḥ kṛtvā ṣoḍaśa ākārān bhūtān prāk yathā ukta bhūta ākāra viparītān satya catuṣṭaye aropayati iti bhrāntiḥ eva sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ sva bīja prabhavā āropya ca kiñcid sva sūkha sādhanañca manyamānaḥ tad artham paritṛṣyati tṛṣṇayā ca janma sthāna upāṃdānam iti saṃsāra pravṛttiḥ 
[103,i_103,iii]	mārga viparyayam saṃsāra hetum uktvā mārgam āha tatra eva tad viruddha artha tattva ākāra anurodhinī hanti sa anucarām tṛṣṇām samyak dṛṣṭiḥ su bhāvitā tatra satya catuṣṭayaḥ eva myak dṛṣṭiḥ na īrātmya dṛṣṭiḥ tad viruddha artha tattva ākāra anurodhinī teṣām sthira sukha ādi ākārāṇām avidyā āropitānām viruddhaḥ arthaḥ tasya tattvāni bhūtāḥ ākārāḥ anityā sukha ādayaḥ ṣoḍaśa ākārāḥ tān anuroddhum śīlam yasyāḥ sā tathā su bhāvitā sa ādara nirantara dīrgha kāla abhyāsa prāpta vaiśadyā hanti tṛṣṇām janma hetum sa anucarām mātsarya ādi parivārām 
[103,iv_103,vi]	nanu tṛṣṇā kṣayepi karma dehayoḥ janma hetvoḥ bhāvāt janma kim na bhavati iti āha trihetoḥ na udbhavaḥ karma dehayoḥ sthitayoḥ api eka abhāvāt vinā bījam na aṅkurasya iva sambhavaḥ trihetoḥ tṛṣṇā karma deha hetoḥ janmanaḥ tṛṣṇāyāḥ kṣaye karma dehayoḥ sthitayoḥ api na udbhavaḥ utpattiḥ na bhavati eka abhāvāt hetu sāmagrya vaikalyāt vinā bījam kṣiti udaka ādi bhāvepi na aṅkurasya udbhavaḥ 
[103,vii_103,ix]	nanu tri hetoḥ janmanaḥ eka abhāvepi ced anutpattiḥ tat kim karmmaṇaḥ dehasya vā kṣayaḥ na abhyasyate pare ca āhuḥ karma kṣayāt muktiḥ iti atra āha asambhavāt vipakṣasya na hāniḥ karma dehayoḥ aśakya tvāt ca tṛṣṇāyām sthitāyām punar udbhavāt asambhavāt vipakṣasya na hāniḥ karma dehayoḥ asti aśakya tvāt ca sati api vā vipakṣe tad abhyāsāt deha karma nivṛttiḥ aśakya kriyā tṛṣṇāyām sthitāyām tad pracitasya ātma grahavataḥ garbha sthāna parigrahe sati punar udbhavāt dehasya śarīriṇaḥ ca tṛṣṇayā eva pravṛttyā sarvatra śubha aśubha pravṛtteḥ ca 
[103,x_104,ii]	evantarhi tṛṣṇā karma ca kṣapayitavyam mumukṣuṇā iti āha dvaya kṣaya artham yatne ca vyarthaḥ karma kṣartha śramaḥ dvaya kṣaya artham yatne kriyamāṇe karma kṣaye vyarthaḥ śramaḥ tṛṣṇā kṣaya mātrāt janma abhāva siddheḥ sat api karma anupayuktam iti alam tad kṣaya prayāsena na ca karma kṣayaḥ pratipakṣa abhāvāt śakyaḥ iti uktam santāpa kleśa upabhogāt pūrva arjita karma kṣayaḥ aparasya ca akāraṇam tatas muktiḥ iti api mohaḥ 
[104,iii_104,v]	tathā hi phala vaicitrya dṛṣṭeḥ ca śakti bhedaḥ anumīyate karmaṇām tāpa saṃkleśāt na eka rūpāt tatas kṣayaḥ karmaṇām phala vaicitryasya nānā gati upabhogyāne kavidhā upakaraṇa sādhya vividha sukha duḥkha upabhoga prakārasya dṛṣṭeḥ ca śakti bhedaḥ sāmarthya nānā tvam anumīyate atas nānā prakāra phala janana sāmarthyāt kāraṇāt eka rūpāt phalāt tāpa saṃkleśāt na karmaṇām kṣayaḥ 
[104,vi_104,viii]	sarveṣām karmaṇām tāpaḥ eva phalam iti ced phalam kathañcid tat janyam alpam syāt na vijātimat athā api tapasaḥ śaktyā śakti saṅkara saṃkṣayaiḥ tasya karmaṇaḥ janyam phalam kathañcid jugupsā ādibhiḥ alpam syāt na tu vijātimat dānam dattvā hiṃsitvā vā jugupsuḥ tayoḥ phalam alpīyaḥ anubhavati kāraṇa tā na vāpādānāt na tu śubhasya duḥkham aśubhasya vā sukham phalam bhavitum arhati atha api tapasaḥ śaktyā śakti saṃkareṇa tāpa kleśa mātra phalena tāni hīyante tapaḥ śaktyā karmaṇām saṃkṣayeṇa vā janma abhāvaḥ 
[105,i_105,iii]	kleśāt kutaścid dhīyeta aśeṣam akleśa leśataḥ yat ca kiñcid avaśiṣṭam tat kleśāt kutaścid keśa ulluñcana ādeḥ kṣīyate karma kṣayāt ca muktiḥ atra āha hīyeta aśeṣam akleśa leśataḥ yadi tapasā karma kṣayaḥ aśeṣam karma hīyeta akleśataḥ vinā eva keśa ulluñcana ādi duḥkhāt karmaṇaḥ kṣīṇa tvāt yathā nāraka ādi duḥkham na bhavati tathā alpīyopi na syāt śakti sāṃkarya ipi leśataḥ santāpa kleśāt kevalāt karma hīyeta na duḥkha antara anubandhī saṃsāra prabandhaḥ tapasvinaḥ syāt 
[105,iv_105,v]	yadi iṣṭam aparam kleśāt tat tapaḥ kleśaḥ eva ced tat karma phalam iti asmāt na śakteḥ saṅkara ādikam tapasaḥ śaktyā śakti saṅkara saṃkṣayaḥ ca tadā vaktum śakyaḥ yadi syāt iṣṭam kleśāt aparam anyat tapaḥ na anyathā kleśaḥ eva ced tat tapaḥ tad kleśa rūpam tapaḥ karma phalam tapaḥ avaśeṣitasya karmaṇaḥ phalam iṣṭa miti asmāt karma phala bhūtāt tapasaḥ śakti saṃkara ādikam na yuktam ādi śabdāt saṃkṣayaḥ ca 
[105,vi_105,viii]	tasya mate tu utpitsu doṣa nirghātāt ye api doṣa virodhinaḥ tad je karmāṇi śaktāḥ syuḥ kṛta hāniḥ katham bhavet utpitsoḥ tṛṣṇā ādeḥ doṣasya nirghātāt yepi doṣa virodhinaḥ nairātmya abhyāsa ādayaḥ upāyāḥ tad je tṛṣṇā ādi doṣa prabhave karmaṇi kāraṇa vāraṇa dvāreṇa vyāhantum śaktāḥ na prāc janite tasya utpanna tvāt atas kṛtasya karmaṇaḥ hāniḥ katham bhavet 
[105,ix_106,i]	nanu yathā doṣebhyaḥ karma tathā karmaṇaḥ doṣāḥ ca bhavanti iti akṣīṇa karmaṇaḥ na syāt muktiḥ iti āha doṣāḥ na karmaṇaḥ duṣṭaḥ karoti na viparyayāt doṣāḥ na karmaṇaḥ bhavanti kintu doṣaiḥ duṣṭaḥ prāṇī karmakaraḥ bhavati na viparyayāt na aduṣṭaḥ karma karoti nairātmya darśinaḥ tṛṣṇā bhāvāt kvacid pravṛtti nivṛtti asambhavāt 
[106,ii_106,iv]	nanu karmaṇaḥ śubhāt sukham sukhāt abhilāṣaḥ abhilāṣāt ca rāgaḥ iti karmaṇaḥ doṣa janma iti āha mithyā vikalpena vinā na abhilāṣaḥ sukhāt api yaḥ ca sukhāt api abhilāṣaḥ rāga hetuḥ dṛśyate sa ca mithyā vikalpena vinā sthira sukha madīya ahaṃkāra vikalpanam antareṇa na bhavati iti āyoni śoma naskāraḥ eva doṣa hetuḥ na karma tatas sati api karmaṇi unmūlita ātma dṛṣṭayaḥ nirdoṣāḥ nirvānti nirvāṇañca duḥkha nirodha lakṣaṇam duḥkham parijñāya tat samudayam mārgabhāvanayā prahāya prāpyate na anyathā iti 
[106,v_106,viii]	catur satya prakāśakaḥ eva mumukṣūṇām upāsyaḥ iti tāyi tvam uktam tat evam anulomataḥ pramāṇa bhūtāye tyādi pañca padāni vyākhyāya pratilomataḥ liṅgalaiṅgika tvam darśayan āha tāyāt tattva sthira aśeṣa viśeṣa jñāna sādhanam tāyāt catur satya prakāśa lakṣaṇāt liṅgāt tattva sthira aśeṣa viśeṣa jñānasya triguṇasya sugata tvasya sādhanam siddhiḥ tattvasya kṣaṇika nairātmyasya jñānāt praśastam 
[106,ix_106,x]	bodha artha tvāt gameḥ apunarāvṛttyā ca sthiram niḥśeṣam viśeṣa jñānam triguṇam sugata tvam bodha artha tvāt gameḥ gata śabdaḥ prakṛtiḥ na hi samvādinaḥ asākṣāt kṛtasya arthasya upadeśaḥ śakya kriyaḥ na ca anumānena jñātasya upadeśaḥ iti yuktam uktam kṣaṇika tva nairātmya ādi viṣayasya anumānasya bhagavat upadeśam antareṇa utpatti bīja abhāvāt agṛhīta upadeśānām abhāvāt na ca nitya parokṣasya arthasya sthairya ādi viparyaya adhyavasāyinaḥ kaścid niścayaḥ asti tasmāt pramāṇa samvādinaḥ parokṣa arthasya upadeśaḥ tad sākṣātkāra pūrvakaḥ eva iti yuktam tāyi tvāt sugata tva anumānam bhagavataḥ sa ca bhagavān tāyaḥ sugata tvāt triguṇāt guṇa anukrameṇa 
[107,i_107,ii]	bāhya śaikṣā śaikṣa adhikaḥ tatas bāhya śaikṣā śaikṣebhyaḥ adhikaḥ ye laukika bhāvanā mārgeṇa vīta rāgāḥ bāhyā atatva darśinaḥ tebhyaḥ tattva darśi tvāt adhikaḥ ye śaikṣāḥ abāhyāḥ parihāṇi dharmāṇaḥ tebhyaḥ apunarāvṛttyā ye ca aśaikṣāḥ śrāvakāḥ aprahīṇa kleśa vāsanā asākṣāt kṛta sarva ākāra vaḥ tavaḥ tebhyaḥ niḥśeṣa pratītyā tasmāt sugata tvāt śāsanam śāstṛ tvam anumīyate 
[107,iii_107,v]	ki punar śāsanam iti āha para artha jñāna ghaṭanam tasmāt tad śāsanam tatas dayā para artha taṃtra tvam tad śāsanam kāraṇe kārya upacārāt para artham yat jñānam sugata tvam tad artham ghaṭanam vyāyāmaḥ buddha tva sādhana mārga abhyāsaḥ iti arthaḥ na hi upāyam antareṇa upeya sambhavaḥ tatas śāsanāt dayā para artha tantra tvam para artha pradhāna tvam jagat hita eṣitvam anumīyate iti arthaḥ 
[107,vi_107,viii]	nanu na avaśyam kāruṇikasya mokṣa mārga abhyāsaḥ sva artha buddhyā api bāhyānām iva sambhavāt tat katham upāya abhyāsāt dayā anumānam iti āha siddhārthasyā avirāmataḥ siddhārthasya niṣpanna mokṣa lakṣaṇa ātma samvādasya api sugatasya khaḍga ādi vat para artha kriyā ataḥ avirāmataḥ anivṛtteḥ phala avasthāyān dayā sadbhāvāt hetu avasthāyām api tasya astitvam anumānañca 
[107,ix_107,xiv]	jagat hita eṣitvasya sugata tva śāstṛ tvatāyi tva sahitasya prāmāṇya sādhana tvam āha dayayā śreyaḥ ācaṣṭe yatas dayayā jagat hita eṣitvena śreyaḥ ācaṣṭe nirdayaḥ tu visamvādana abhiprāya upi brūyāt sadayā upya bhūtam ajñaḥ vakti iti āha jñānāt satyam sa sādhanam jñānāt sugata tvāt bhūtam ācaṣṭe tat ca jñānam sa sādhanam vidyamāna upāya abhyāsam vidyamāna śāstṛ tvam iti arthaḥ 
[107,xv_108,i]	tat ca abhiyogavān vaktum yatas tasmāt pramāṇa tā tat ca satya catuṣṭayam vineyānām vaktum abhiyogaḥ sāda rasa tata pravṛttiḥ tadvān tāyī ca iti arthaḥ tasmāt kāruṇika tvāt sugata tvāt śāstṛ tvāt tāyi tvāt ca bhagavataḥ pramāṇa tā yathā upadarśita artha samvādaka tā anyaiḥ ajñāta catur satya artha prakāśaka tā vā anumīyate iti arthaḥ 
[108,ii_108,v]	evañca anumāna anumeya vyavahāre sthite prāmāṇyāt tāyi tvam hita eṣi tvāt upāya abhyāsāt ca sugata tvambhavati iti uktam kasmāt punar aneka guṇa sambhāra sambhavepi prāmāṇyena eva bhagavataḥ stutiḥ iti āha upadeśa tathā abhāva stutiḥ tad upadeśataḥ pramāṇa tatva sidhi artham upadeśasya tathā abhāvaḥ samvādaka tvam prāmāṇyam tena stutiḥ ācāryeṇa kṛtā tasya bhagavataḥ upadeśataḥ pramāṇasya tattvam lakṣaṇam tat sidhi artham bhagavat deśanāyāḥ pramāṇa viniścayaḥ na utprekṣā mātreṇa iti ākhyātum iti arthaḥ 
[108,vi_108,viii]	nanu nīla samaṅgī puruṣaḥ nīlam jānāti no tu nīlam iti bruvatā bhagavatā pratyakṣam darśitam anumānam na uktam katham āgamāt pratyetavyam iti āha anumāne api avāraṇāt prayoga darśanāt vā asya anumānepya vāraṇa ādiṣṭiḥ darśitā śūnyāḥ para pravādāḥ ityādinā śābda ādeḥ eva niṣedhāt prayogasya para artha anumāna rūpasya darśanāt vāgame asya anumānasya nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ eva bhagavatā 
[108,ix_109,iii]	tam eva prayogam āha yat kiñcid udaya ātmakam nirodha dharmakam sarvam tat iti ādau anekadhā yat kiñcid udaya ātmakam tat sarvam nirodha dharmakam iti ādau āgama vākye anekadhā svabhāva ādi liṅga jam aneka prakāram anumānam duśyate katham punar anena anumānam uktam iti āha anumāna āśrayaḥ liṅgam avinābhāva lakṣaṇam vyāpti pradarśanāt hetoḥ sādhyena uktañca tat sphuṭam
