[109,iv_109,vi]	anumānasya āśrayaḥ kāraṇam liṅgam vaktavyam anumāna nirdeśa artham anyathā aśakyatvāt kim lakṣaṇam iti āha avinābhāvaḥ sādhya avyabhicāri tvam tad lakṣaṇam yasya tat tathā sa ca avinābhāvaḥ liṅgam lakṣaṇam hetoḥ udaya dharmaka tvasya sādhyena nirodha dharmaka tvena vyāpteḥ pradarśanāt yat kiñcit udaya dharmakam tat sarvam nirodha dharmakam ityādinā sphuṭaḥ pravyaktaḥ darśitaḥ iti anumāna prāmāṇya nirdeśa upi bhagavat upajñam eva tat evam bhagavān eva pramāṇa bhūtaḥ tāyī mumukṣubhiḥ upāsyaḥ na itaraḥ iti darśana artham ācāryeṇa tasya stutiḥ uktā iti yuktam 
[110,i_110,iii]	vipratipattayaḥ ca atra saṃkhyā lakṣaṇa gocara phala viṣayāḥ santi tatra saṃkhyā vipratipatti nirākaraṇa artham āha mānam dvividham viṣaya dvaividhyāt mānam dvividham yat tad pramāṇam avisamvādi tvāt ajñāta artha prakāśaka tvāt sāmānya lakṣaṇam uktam tat dvividham pratyakṣa anumāna bhedena kasmāt viṣayasya sva lakṣaṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇa rūpa tayā dvaividhyāt śābda ādikam api hi pramāṇam bha vat sa viṣayam vaktavyam viṣayaḥ ca sva sāmānya lakṣaṇāt atiriktaḥ na asti tatas tad viṣaya tve pratyakṣa anumāna tā eva na api sāmānya viśeṣa ātmakaḥ ekosti viṣayaḥ paraspara viruddhayoḥ aikātmya ayogāt 
[110,iv_110,v]	nanu katham viṣaya dvaividhya siddhiḥ na pratyakṣān na api anumānataḥ yathākramam sva lakṣaṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇa tvāt anayoḥ dvābhyām dvaya siddhiḥ iti ced nanu pratyakṣasya sāmānya aviṣaya tve sādhya sādhana sambandha āgrahaṇāt anumānam eva na syāt sāmānya viṣaya tve ca pratyakṣa tvāt eva tad siddheḥ viphalam anumānasya prāmāṇya kalpanam 
[110,vi]	atra ucyate pratyakṣam api sva lakṣaṇam viṣayīkurvat tad sambhavi vijātīya vyāvṛtti upakalpitam sāmānyam pṛṣṭha vikalpena niścinvat tat viṣayam api niścaya viṣayeṇa ca pratyakṣa viṣaya vyavasthā evantarhi sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tā na syāt iti ced na sajātīya vyāvṛtta tvena api tatas niścayāt dve ca vyāvṛttī sva lakṣaṇe staḥ niścite ca pratyakṣa balāt na ca evam api anumānasya vaiyarthya na hi sāmānyam iti eva pratyakṣa viṣayaḥ parokṣe tasya apravṛtteḥ na ca yat ekadā aparokṣam tat sarvadā tathā sva lakṣaṇam kadācid aparokṣam api anyadā parokṣam evam sāmānyam api tatas aparokṣe sāmānye gṛhītāyām vyāptau parokṣe tasmin anumāna vṛttiḥ iti na kaścid virodhaḥ tasmāt pratyakṣa tvāt vā viṣaya dvaividhya siddhiḥ pratyakṣa anumānābhyām vā iti ubhayathā api upapannam 
[111,i_111,iii]	viṣaya dvaividhyam eva kasmāt iti āha śakti aśaktitaḥ artha kriyāyām śakti aśaktitaḥ artha kriyāyām sva lakṣaṇasya artha kriyā śakta tvāt vijātīya vyāvṛtti upakalpitasya ca sāmānyasya aśakta tvāt viṣaya dvaividhyam na hi ekasya viruddhau imau dharmau yujyete yadi anartha kriyā kāri sāmānyam keśoṇḍuka jñāna pratibhāsi keśa ādī api sāmānyam syāt 
[111,iv_112,i]	keśa ādiḥ nna arthaḥ nartha adhimokṣataḥ na keśādiḥ arthaḥ sāmānya rūpaḥ anartha adhimokṣataḥ yatra hi vyavahartṝṇām artha adhyavasāyaḥ saḥ arthaḥ sva lakṣaṇam sāmānyam vā syāt yatra punar artha buddhiḥ eva na asti sa katham sāmānyam ucyatām sadṛśā sadṛśa tvāt ca viṣaya aviṣaya tvataḥ śabdasya anya nimittānām bhāve dhīḥ sat asatvatas 
[112,ii]	tathā tadṛśā sadṛśa tvāt ca viṣaya dvaividhyam sadṛśam sāmānyam sarva vyakti sādhāraṇa tvāt asadṛśam sva lakṣaṇam sarvatas vyāvṛtta tvāt anayoḥ ca anyonya vyavaccheda rūpa tvāt na rāśi antaram tatas yadi kalpyamānam sadṛśam tadā sāmānyam eva tat atha asadṛśam sva lakṣaṇam eva iti dvaividhyam eva viṣayasya tathā śabdasya viṣaya aviṣaya tvataḥ ca dvaividhyam śabdasya viṣayaḥ sāmānyam aviṣayaḥ sva lakṣaṇam na ca śabda viṣaya aviṣayābhyām anyosti sarvasya saṃgrahāt dvaividhyam eva tathā viṣayāt anyaṣān nimittānām manaskāra vat sādguṇya saṃketa grahaṇānām bhāve grāhikāyāḥ dhiyaḥ sāmānye sattvāt sva lakṣaṇe ca abhāvāt viṣaya dvaividhyam yatra viṣaya vyatirikta nimitta sadbhāve bhavati buddhiḥ tad sāmānyam yatratu na bhavati tat sva lakṣaṇam prakāra antarañca na sambhavati iti buddhi viṣaya aviṣaya tve sāmānya sva lakṣaṇa tā eva iti dvaividhyam eva viṣayasya 
[112,iii_112,v]	tat eva artha kriyā sāmarthya ādikam sva lakṣaṇa ādau yojayan āha artha kriyā samartha yat tat atra paramārtha sat anyat saṃvṛtisat proktam te sva sāmānya lakṣaṇaḥ artha kriyāyām jñāna ādikāyām svarūpa upadhānena samartham yat tat atra vastu vicāraḥ paramārtha sat evam yat asadṛśam śabda aviṣayaḥ anya nimitta bhāve jñāna abhāvaḥ ca tat paramārtha sat atas anyat aśaktam sadṛśam śabda viṣayaḥ anya nimitta bhāve buddheḥ viṣayaḥ ca tat saṃvṛtisat proktam kalpanā mātra vyavahārya tvāt te parama artha saṃvṛtī sva sāmānya lakṣaṇe 
[112,vi_112,vii]	aśaktam sarvam iti ced bīja ādeḥ aṅkura ādiṣu dṛṣṭā śaktiḥ sva lakṣaṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇe iṣṭe sarvam artha kāri tvena iṣṭam aśaktam na kiñcid karttum samartham iti ced bīja ādeḥ kāraṇa abhimatasya aṅkura ādau kārya saṃmate dṛṣṭā śaktiḥ janana lakṣaṇā bīja anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyī aṅkuraḥ dṛśyate idam eva kāraṇasya śakta tvam yat prāc adṛṣṭasya tad bhāvaḥ eva bhāvaḥ 
[113,i_113,ii]	matā sā ced saṃvṛtyā sā śaktiḥ saṃvṛtyā matā ced kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ hi vyavahāra mātrataḥ siddhaḥ na paramārthataḥ na tāvat pratyakṣam tad grahaṇa samartham bīja aṅkura grāhiṇoḥ pratyakṣayoḥ sva viṣaya mātra vyavasthāpanāt kena anvaya vyatireka grahaṇam krameṇa dvayoḥ gṛhītayoḥ tad bala bhāvinā smaraṇena grahaṇam iti ced 
[113,iii]	nanu kena anvaya vyatirekau gṛhītau na pratyekam bīja aṅkura jñānābhyām sva sva viṣaya grahaṇāt na api dvābhyām jñānayoḥ jñeyayoḥ ca sāhitya abhāvāt asāhitye bīja aṅkura mātrasya grahaṇam na anvaya vyatirekayoḥ krama grahaṇam eva kārya kāraṇa bhāva grahaṇam tat tu ghaṭa kulālayoḥ api asti iti ced na ca kramopi kenacid śakya grahaṇaḥ pratiyogya vedanāt pūrva apara grahaṇam atas eva na asti sva jñānena vartamāna tā grahaṇāt ca kārya kāle ca kāraṇam pūrvam ucyate tadā ca tat eva na asti tat etat mṛtasya ārogyam atha yadā eva bījam tadā eva aṅkurāt pūrvam na tu paścāt asya pūrva tvam sambhavati 
[113,iv]	nanu evam pūrva tayā pratibhāsosya prāptaḥ na ca etat asti aṅkura sāhityam pūrva tvam tat ca gṛhyate eva iti ced tādṛśam pūrva tvam anyeṣām api asti iti tepi kāraṇāni syuḥ kiñca pūrva tvam vartamāna kālāt prāc bhāvi tvam ucyate tat yadi vastunaḥ rūpam tadā vartamānam kadāpi na syāt vartam āna tā tad prāgbhāvi tvayoḥ virodhāt syāt etat aṅkura vartam āna tāyāḥ prāc bhāvi tvam pūrva tvam tat ca bījasya vartamāna tvena aviruddham iti na tasya abhāvaḥ evantarhi bīja grahaṇe pūrva tā grahaṇam prāptam na ca bīja svarūpam iva pūrva tām api tad grāhiṇi jñāne kaścid upalabhate 
[113,v_114,ii]	nanu āpekṣikam idam pūrva tvam pratiyoginaḥ apratītau katham pratīyatām yadi evam vastunaḥ na idam kevalam bhāva antara apekṣayā vyavahriyate iti āyātam na hi vastu rūpam sati vastu ninā asti yat ca asti tena vastu rūpa avabhāsini jñāne pratibhāsitavyam eva anyathā jñāna jñeyayoḥ viṣaya viṣayitā eva na syāt tasmāt na adhyakṣāt kārya kāraṇa tā grahaḥ atas ca na anumānāt api na hi sarvadā parokṣe anye anumāna vṛttiḥ vyāpti grahaṇa pūrvaka tvāt tasya na api pratyakṣa bala bhāvi smaraṇam tad grahaṇa pravaṇam na hi tat svatantram pramāṇam kintu pramāṇa vyāpāra vyavasthāpakam yadi yathā anubhavam pravartate na anyathā na ca kārya kāraṇa bhāva anubhavaḥ bhūtaḥ iti uktam atas smaraṇa tvam api asya na asti anūbhūta vikalpanasya smaraṇa tvāt tatas vikalpa mātram etat na tatas vastu vyavasthā iti saṃvṛttyā eva avicārita ramaṇīyayā kārya kāraṇa bhāva vyavahāraḥ na paramārthataḥ astu yathā tathā astu yathā tathā sāṃvṛtam api kārya kāraṇa bhāvam āśritya sādhya sādhana ādi vyavahāra samvāda sampratyayāt samāptaḥ loka vyavahāraḥ sāṃvyavahāri kañca pramāṇam tāvatā eva sustham 
[114,iii_114,iv]	sā asti sarvatra ced buddheḥ na anvayavyatirekayoḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇe adṛṣṭeḥ cakṣu ūru upādi buddhi vat sārtha kriyā sarvatra sva lakṣaṇe sāmānyepi asti ced na sāmānya lakṣaṇe astu tāvat anyasya kāryasya buddheḥ api anvaya vyatirekayoḥ adṛṣṭeḥ antyam hi bhāvānām kāryam buddhiḥ sā api yat anvaya vyatirekau na anuvidhatte tasya kutas artha kriyā pratyakṣam tāvat na sāmānya viṣayam sva lakṣaṇa mātrasya pratibhāsanāt ghaṭaḥ ityādi vikalpa buddhiḥ tu sāmānya avasāyāt tad viṣayā sā api samayā bhoga ādi mātrāt utpatteḥ na sāmānya anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyinī cakṣu ūrūpādi buddhi vat cakṣu ūrūpa ādi ja buddheḥ cakṣuḥ ādi anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam iva sāmarthye sati bhāvāt eka apāyepya bhāvāt ca na evam sāmānya buddhiḥ ābhoga mātrāt utpatteḥ 
[114,v_114,vi]	etena samaya ābhoga ādi antaraṅga anurodhataḥ ghaṭa utkṣepaṇa sāmānya saṃkhyā ādiṣu dhiyaḥ gatāḥ etena sāmānyasya jñāna mātra kārya īpi a sāmarthya kathanena samaya ābhoga ādeḥ antaraṅgasya anurodhataḥ ghaṭaḥ avayavi dravyam utkṣepaṇam karma sāmānyam saṃkhyā guṇaḥ samavāyaḥ ādi śabdāt saṃyoga vibhāga ādayaḥ teṣu yāḥ dhiyaḥ vikalpikāḥ bhavanti tāḥ gatāḥ vyākhyātāḥ na hi rūpa ādi vyatiriktam dravyam apara apara deśi janya hasta ādi kṣaṇāt bhinnam karma vyakti vyatireki sāmānyam pratyakṣa buddha a abhāsate vikalpabuddhiḥ astu kalpikā sā ca saṃketa saṃskāra prabodha mātra bhāvinī na artha adhīnā iti na teṣām sāmarthyam samarthayati 
[115,i_115,iii]	nanu yadi artha nirapekṣāṇām anya nimittānām bhāve yatra buddhiḥ tad sāmānyam tadā taimirika buddhi pratibhāsinaḥ keśādayopi sāmānyam stuḥ teṣu api dhiyaḥ artha nirapekṣa cakṣuḥ ādi mātra nimitta tvāt iti āha keśa ādayaḥ na sāmānyam anartha abhiniveśataḥ keśa ādayaḥ taimirika pratibhāsinaḥ na sāmānyam anartha abhiniveśataḥ na hi teṣu viṣaya buddhiḥ vyavahāriṇām viṣaye ca sāmānya cintā iyam yadi jñeya tvena adhyavasāya abhāvāt na sāmānyam tadā abhāva upyanupalabdhi viṣayaḥ sāmānyam na syāt 
[115,iv_115,vi]	tatas ca anupalabdhiḥ anumānam na bhavet iti āha jñeya tvena grahāt doṣaḥ na abhāveṣu prasajyate na abhāveṣu sāmānya rūpa tva abhāva doṣaḥ prasajyate jñeya tvena grahāt yadi api abhāve artha rūpa tāyāḥ adhyavasāyaḥ na asti jñeya tayā tu asti lokasya tat ca jñeyam yad artha kāri tat sāmānyam eva 
[115,vii_115,x]	yadi tu teṣām api tathā abhāve apratiṣedhāt teṣām taimirika gamyānām keśa ādīnām api tathā abhāve jñāna antareṇa jñeya tve samāna rūpatā iṣyate tadā apratiṣedha ādiṣṭam eva asmākam taimirika jñāna gamyāḥ keśa ādayaḥ iti yadā buddhi antareṇa parāmṛśyante tadā keśa ādayaḥ jñeya tvena sāmānyam iṣṭāḥ eva yadi taimirika dṛṣṭāḥ keśa ādayaḥ na vastu tadā sphuṭa ābhatā na syāt iti āha 
[115,xi_116,ii]	sphuṭa ābhatā jñāna rūpa tayā artha tvāt jñāna rūpa tayā jñāna ākāra tayā keśa ādīnām artha tvāt sva lakṣaṇa tvāt sphuṭa ābhatā yadi jñāna ākāra tayā keśa ādayaḥ sva lakṣaṇantadā sāmānyam katham iti āha keśa ādi iti matiḥ punar sāmānya viṣayā keśādi iti punar vikalpikā matiḥ taimirika upalabdha keśa ādi adhyavasāyinī sāmānya viṣayā ayam arthaḥ taimirika dṛṣṭam keśa ādi sāmānya rūpeṇa vyavasyantī vikalpikā buddhiḥ adhyavasāyena viṣayeṇa sāmānya viṣayā taimirika dhīḥ tu sva lakṣaṇa viṣayāḥ buddhi ākārasya sva lakṣaṇa tvāt 
[116,iii_116,vii]	kintarhi nirviṣayam iti āha keśa pratibhāsam anarthakam taimirika keśa pratibhāsam jñānam anartha kamba āhya keśa abhāvāt jñāna rūpa tayā artha tve sāmānye ced prasajyate nanu jñāna rūpa tayā artha tve keśa ādi iti vikalpa buddhi pratibhāsini sāmānye sva lakṣaṇa tā prasajyate ced 
[116,viii_116,xiii]	tathā iṣṭa tvāt adoṣaḥ tathā jñāna ākāra tayā sāmānyasya api sva lakṣaṇa tāyāḥ iṣṭa tvāt adoṣaḥ kathantarhi sāmānya rūpa tā iti āha artha rūpa tvena samāna tā artha rūpa tvena adhyavasīyamāna jñeya rūpa tvena samāna tā na tu buddhi ākāra tvena katham punar artha rūpa tvena api samāna ta iti āha 
[116,xiv_116,xv]	sarvatra sama rūpa tvāt tad vyāvṛtti samāśrayāt sarvatra vyaktiṣu tad vyāvṛtti samāśrayāt vijātīya vyāvṛtti āśrayeṇa dṛśya vikalpya ekatva adhyavasāyāt upakalpitasya sāmānyasya sama rūpa tvāt sādhāraṇa rūpa tvāt artha tvena sāmānyam ucyate jñāna ākārasya sāmānyasya saṃprati vyatiriktasya ca pūrvam pratiṣedhāt 
[117,i_117,iii]	rūpa ādi svabhāvam eva aviśeṣeṇa sāmānyam kinneṣyate iti āha na tat vastu abhidheya tvāt sāphalyāt akṣa saṃhateḥ tad sāmānyam na vastu rūpa ādi svabhāvam abhidheya tvāt śabda dharma vat sāmānyam śabda jñāna gocaraḥ na ca śabda viṣayaḥ vastu kasmāt iti āha sāphalyāt akṣa saṃhateḥ yadi śabda viṣayaḥ vastu bhavet tadā rūpa ādi śabdāt eva artha ādeḥ api rūpa ādi pratītau na kiñci d akṣaiḥ na ca evam tatas vastu viṣayeṇa indriya jñānena śabdasya na tulya viṣaya tā tathā ca avastu tā eva śābda jñāna avabhāsinaḥ sāmānyasya na rūpa ādi tā 
[117,iv_117,vi]	nanu rūpa ādayaḥ na śabdasya viṣayaḥ kintarhi nāma nimitte viprayukta saṃskāra saṃjñe te vijñānāt vyatirikte vaibhāṣikasya īṣṭe tadā api nāma ādi vacane vaktṛ śrotṛ vācya anubandhini nāma ādi vacanaḥ iṣyamāṇe kintad nāma ādikam vaktari śrotari arthe vā sambaddham asambaddham eva vā kvacid sarvathā vaktṛ śrotṛ vācya anubandhini 
[117,vii_117,x]	asambandhini nāma ādau arthe syāt apravarttanam asambandhini vā nāma ādau śabdena codite arthe apravartanam syāt acodita tvāt bhavatu tāvat anya sambandhini asambandhini vā nāma ādau arthe apravartanam artha sambandhini tu katham apravṛttiḥ acodita tvāt sārūpyāt bhrāntitaḥ vṛttiḥ arthe ced syāt na sarvadā deśa bhrāntiḥ ca 
[117,xi]	na hi devadatte pratipādite tat pitari pravṛttiḥ nimittasya artha sārūpyāt tat bhrāntitaḥ arthe pravṛttiḥ ced sambhāvyate etat kintu na syāt sarvadā na hi yama lakayoḥ niyamena bhrāntyā a nyatra pravṛttiḥ kadācid tatra api darśanāt tathā ādeśa bhrāntiḥ ca na syāt vaktṛ śrotra ādi sambandhini niyata deśe nāma ādau pratipādite tad anya deśe ghaṭa ādau sārūpyāt api na yuktā pravṛttiḥ 
[118,i_118,v]	nanu tvad mate api jñāna ākārasya abhidheya tvāt katham bāhye pravṛttiḥ iti āha na jñāne tulyam utpattitaḥ dhiyaḥ tathāvidhāyāḥ na jñāne jñāna ākāre vācye arthe apravartanam tulyam dhiyaḥ tathāvidhāyāḥ bahis tvena adhya vasita ākārāyāḥ utpattitaḥ śabda janitā hi buddhiḥ vastutas sva aṃśa ālambanā api anādya vidyā vaśāt bahis viṣayā vyavasīyate itiyuktam arthe pravartanam anyatra tatra anupagamāt dhiyaḥ anyatra nāma ādi viṣayiṇi jñāne tad artha adhyavasāyāt arthe pravartanam na yuktam nirākāra buddhi vādi vaibhāṣika mate bāhya artha pratibhāsāyāḥ jñāna ākārāyāḥ dhiyaḥ anupagamataḥ 
[118,vi_118,x]	bāhya artha pratibhāsāyāḥ upāye vā apramāṇātā vijñāna vyatiriktasya yadi jñeya ākārā buddhiḥ syāt syāt tad pratītyā abhimānāt pravṛttiḥ api apravṛtti doṣa darśanāt bāhya artha pratibhāsāyāḥ buddheḥ upāye svīkāre vā apramāṇa tā nāma ādeḥ viprayukta saṃskārasya vijñāna vyatiriktasya katham iti āha vyatireka aprasiddhitaḥ vyatireka aprasiddhitaḥ pratibhāsamānasya ākārasya jñāna tvāt na ca indriya ādiṣu satsu api vijñāna kāryān utpattitaḥ arthaḥ iva nāma ādiḥ api śakya vyavasthānaḥ na hi gṛhīta saṃketasya śabda śrutau kvacid artha apratipattiḥ 
[118,xi_119,iii]	sarva jñāna arthava tvāt ced svapna ādau anyathā īkṣaṇāt ayuktam nanu asti pramāṇam sarvasya jñānasya arthavat tvāt śābdam api jñānam arthavat eva na ca rūpa ādayaḥ viṣayaḥ iti pāriśeṣyān nāma ādikam eva iti ced svapna ādau ādi śabdāt taimirika jñāna ādiṣu anyathā artha śūnyasya īkṣaṇāt sarva jñāna artha vat śābdasya nāma ādi viṣaya tva anumānam ayuktam svapna vijñānam api nimitta viṣayam eva iti ced āha na ca saṃskārān nīla ādi pratibhāsataḥ na ca saṃskārāt nimitta ākhyāt svapna jñānam nīla ādeḥ varṇa saṃsthāna viśeṣataḥ pratibhāsataḥ na ca viprayukta saṃsakāraḥ varṇṇa saṃsthāna viśeṣavān 
[119,iv_119,viii]	nīla ādiḥ eva asau arthaḥ iti ced nīla ādi apratighātāt na svapna pratibhāsi na nīla ādi vastu apratighātāt nīla ādayaḥ hi arthāḥ sva deśe padārtha antarasya vyāghātakāḥ svapna upalabdhāḥ tu na evam pihita dvārāvavaraka udara supta sthāna antara gamanāt hasti yūtha ādi darśanāt kintarhi tat iti āha jñānam tad yogya deśakaiḥ ajñātasya svayam jñānāt 
[119,ix_119,xi]	jñānam tat nīla ādi yogya deśakaiḥ svapnāyamānena samāna deśaiḥ puruṣa antaraiḥ ajñātasya svayam jñānāt svayam vedyam asāmānyam iti jñāna lakṣaṇam tat ca svapna dṛṣṭa nīla ādiṣu vyaktam nāma ādi etena varṇitam etena svapna dṛṣṭasya jñāna tva sādhanena nāma ādi varṇṇitam nāma ādikam api tat na bhavati yogya deśakaiḥ ajñātasya svayam jñānāt jñānam tat tasmāt na asti arthaḥ sāmānya buddhiḥ iti 
[119,xii_119,xiv]	api ca sā eva iṣṭā arthavatī kena cakṣuḥ ādi matiḥ smṛtā artha sāmarthya dṛṣṭeḥ ced anyat prāptam anarthakam yā eva rūpa ādi viṣaya tvena iṣṭā sā eva cakṣuḥ ādi matiḥ arthavatī kena hetunā matā arthasya rūpa ādeḥ cakṣuḥ ādi m ati janane sāmarthya dṛṣṭeḥ ced anya sāmānya viṣayam vikalpa jñānam anarthakam prāptam na hi yathā cakṣuḥ ādi buddheḥ artha vyatirekāt vyatirekaḥ tathā sāmānya buddheḥ vyatirekaḥ ābhoga mātreṇa bhāvāt 
[120,i_120,v]	apravṛttiḥ asambandha ipi artha sambandha vat yadi na kevalam vaktṛ śrotṛ sambandhi niasambandhepi nāma ādau arthe apravṛttiḥ syāt artha sambandha vat nāma ādi arthe pravṛtti artham yat i iṣyate tadā atīta anāgatam nāma ādi tad abhidhāyinām śabdānām vācyam na syāt abhūt māndhātā bhaviṣyati śam kha ścakravartti iti kasmāt iti āha atīta anāgatam vācyam na syāt arthena tad kṣayāt arthena atīta anāgatena saha tasya nāma ādeḥ sambandhinaḥ syāt svarūpa abhāvāt 
[120,vi_120,viii]	atha sāmānya grahaṇāt śabdāt aprasaṃgaḥ mataḥ yadi tat na kevala sāmānya agrahaṇāt grahaṇepi vā śabdāt sāmānya grahaṇāt tad pratītyā phalavanti akṣāṇi iti teṣām vaiphalyasya aprasaṅgaḥ mataḥ yadi tat etat na yuktam kevalasya vyakti śūnyasya sāmānyasya agrahaṇāt vyakti vyaṃgyam hi sāmānyam vyañjaka agrahaṇe katham gṛhyate kevalasya grahaṇepi vā 
[120,ix_120,x]	atad samāna tā vyaktī tena nitya upalambhanam nitya tvāt ca yadi vyaktiḥ vyakteḥ pratyakṣatām prati atad samāna tā vyaktī yat pratītyā yat pratīyate tat tasya sāmānyam vyaṃgyañca svatantra pratītiḥ tu na sāmānyam vyaṅgyam vā tena apara adhīna pratīti tvena nitya upalambhanam sāmānyam prāptam vyakti sadasat tvayoḥ api upalabdhiḥ syāt sva pratītau vyakti nirapekṣa tvāt tathā upalabhya svabhāvasya sāmānyasya nitya tvāt ca nityam upalambhanam bhavet yadi vyakteḥ viśeṣāt vyaktiḥ abhivyaktiḥ sāmānyasya pratyakṣatām prati pratyakṣa bhāva nimittam iṣṭā pratyakṣa bhūta sāmānya viṣayā pratītiḥ vyañjikāyāḥ vyakteḥ bhavati anyā tu sāmānya buddhiḥ vyañjakam antareṇa api 
[121,i_121,iii]	nanu ātmani jñāna janane yat śaktam śaktam eva tat atha aśaktam kadācid ced aśaktam sarvadā eva tat yat sāmānyam ātmani pratyakṣa ātmaka jñāna janane vyañjaka vyāpāra kāle śaktam anyadā api śaktam eva tat nitya eka svabhāvatayā anupakārya tvāt tatas ca kevalasya sāmānyasya pratyakṣa jananāt akṣa vaikalya prasaṅgaḥ atha aśaktam tat kadācid kevala ādi avasthāyāḥ ced tadā sarva dā eva aśaktam tad upeyam ekasya svabhāva dvaya ayogāt svabhāva bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt vastu bhedasya 
[121,iv_121,vi]	etat eva sphuṭayati tasya śaktiḥ aśaktiḥ vā yā svabhāvena saṃsthitā nitya tvāt api kim tasya kaḥ tām kṣapayitum kṣamaḥ tasya sāmānyasya śaktiḥ aśaktiḥ vā sva viṣaya jñāna janana ādau yā svabhāvena saṃsthitā tām śaktim aśaktim vā nitya tvāt acikitsyasya anapaneya prācīna svabhāvasya kaḥ anyaḥ kṣapayitum kṣamaḥ 
[121,vii_121,viii]	tat ca sāmānya vijñānam anurundhan vibhāvyate nīla ādi ākāra leśaḥ yaḥ sa tasmin kena nirmitaḥ kintu yat tat vyakti nirapekṣam iṣṭaṃtat ca sāmānya vijñānam anurundhan viṣaya bhāvena anuvartamānaḥ yaḥ vibhāvyate nīla ādi ākāra leśaḥ asaṃpūrṇṇa sphuṭībhāvaḥ sa tasmin sāmānya jñāne kena arthena nirmitaḥ na tāvat jātyā tasyāḥ tad asambhavāt na api vyakti ātatra tasyāḥ apratibhāsanāt tatas ca kevala sāmānya grāhi tat jñānam iti na yuktam viśeṣa grahaṇe ca akṣa vaiphalyam tad avastham 
[121,ix_122,iv]	syāt etat dvividhaḥ bhāvānām pratyayaḥ pratyakṣaḥ apratyakṣaḥ ca tatra pratyakṣa pratyaya artha tvāt na akṣāṇām vyarthatā iti ced śabda ādi bhāveṣu pratyayaḥ apratyakṣaḥ pratyakṣaḥ tu akṣebhyaḥ iti na tat vaiphalyam atra āha sā eva eka rūpāt śabda ādeḥ bhinna ābhāsā matiḥ kutas sā eva pratyakṣa apratyakṣa ābhāsā bhinna ābhāsā matiḥ eka rūpāt śabda ādeḥ ādi śabdāt gandha rasa ādeḥ kutas eka rūpa viṣayā ca bhinna pratibhāsā ca iti viruddham 
[122,v_122,vii]	kiñca jātiḥ jātimataḥ rūpāt bhinnā abhinnā vā na jātiḥ jātimat vyakti rūpam yena apara āśrayam siddham pṛthak ced kārya tvam hi apekṣā iti abhidhīyate tatra na tāvat jātiḥ jātimat eva vyakti rūpam yena kāraṇena apara āśrayam ananyā anuyāyi siddham na hi ekasyāḥ vyakte rūpam anyatra asti sarva anuyāyi ca sāmānyam iṣṭam vyakteḥ sakāśāt pṛthak ced sāmānyam asya idam sāmānyam iti bhāvika sambandha anupapattiḥ apekṣā lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ ced nanu apekṣā iti kāryatvam ucyate tad sāmānyasya nityasya asambhavi 
[122,viii_122,ix]	niṣpatteḥ apara adhīnam api kāryam sva hetutaḥ sambadhyate kalpanayā kim akāryam kathañcana kāryam api niṣyatteḥ nitya tvāt apara adhīnam sarvatra nirāśaṃsam vastutas na kvacid sambadhyate kevalam kalpanayā kāraṇa ātmani sambadhyate yat tu kathañcana sāmānyam akārya tat kim kvacid sambhatsyate 
[122,x_122,xii]	anya tve tad asambaddham siddhā atas niḥsvabhāva tā jāti prasaṃgaḥ abhāvasya na tasmāt vyakteḥ sakāśāt anya tve tat sāmānyam asambaddham atas asya niḥsvabhāva tā siddhāḥ vyaktibhyaḥ tattva anya tvābhyām vyavasthāpayitum aśakyatvāt yadi api niḥ svabhāvā jātiḥ tathā api na abhāvasya śaśaviṣāṇa ādeḥ api jāteḥ jāti rūpa tāyāḥ prasaṅgaḥ na hi yaḥ yaḥ abhāvaḥ sa jātiḥ ucyate kintu sāmānyam yat tat niḥsvabhāvam 
[123,i_123,iii]	nanu niḥsvabhāva tve katham sāmānyam iti āha apekṣā bhāvataḥ tayoḥ apekṣā bhāvataḥ tayoḥ śābaleyāgo vyāvṛttyoḥ parasparam apekṣā bhāvataḥ tad vyāvṛttiḥ eva sāmānyam na śaśa viṣāṇa ādiḥ na hi tad apekṣā kvacid asti atad vyāvṛttiḥ tu niḥsvabhāva api anugāmi pratyaya hetuḥ sāmānyam abhāva tvam iva prāc abhāva ādiṣu padārtha tvam iva dravya ādiṣu 
[123,iv_123,v]	tasmāt arūpā rūpāṇām mā āśrayeṇa upakalpitā tad viśeṣa avagāha arthaiḥ jātiḥ śabdaiḥ prakāśyate tasmāt vastutas jātiḥ arūpā niḥsvabhāvāḥ rūpāṇām śābaleya ādīnām na āśrayeṇa upakalpitā jātiḥ śabdaiḥ tad viśeṣa avagāha arthaiḥ te ca te viśeṣāḥ ca tad viśeṣāḥ teṣām avagāhaḥ pravṛtti viṣaya tvena vyāpanam saḥ arthaḥ prayojanam yeṣām taiḥ sakṛt eka kārya aneka pratipatti artham tad āśrayeṇa upakalpitā jātiḥ atad vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇā śabdaiḥ abhidheyā 
[123,vi_123,ix]	yadi jātiḥ niḥsvabhāvā katham svabhāva viśiṣṭā vyavasīyate iti āha tasyām rūpa avabhāsoyam tatvena arthasya vā grahaḥ bhrāntiḥ sā tasyām jātau rūpasya svabhāvasya avabhāsaḥ yaḥ ta tvena jāti svabhāvena vā arthasya yaḥ gragraḥ bhrāntiḥ sā jāteniḥsvabhāva tvāt viśeṣa ātmaka tva abhāvāt kintarhi bhrānteḥ bbījam iti āha 
[123,x_123,xiv]	anādika ālīna darśana abhyāsa nirmitā anādi kālī nānām anādi kālikānām tathābhūta adhyavasāya jñānānām abhyāsena nirmitā yadi anya vyāvṛttiḥ sāmānyam kintasya rūpam iti āha arthānām yat ca sāmānya manya vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇam yat niṣṭhāḥ te ime śabdāḥ na rūpam tasya kiñcana arthānām viśeṣāṇām yat ca sāmānya m anya vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇam yad niṣṭhāḥ yat viṣayāḥ te ime sāṃketikāḥ śabdāḥ tasya rūpam svabhāvaḥ na kiñcana vastutas kalpita tvāt 
[123,xv_124,ii]	nanu buddhi ākāraḥ sa svabhāvaḥ saḥ eva tarhi sāmānyambhaviṣyati iti āha sāmānya buddhau sāmānyena arūpāyām avīkṣaṇāt artha bhrāntiḥ apīṣyeta sāmānyam sā apiḥ sāmānya buddha avarūpāyām grāhya rūpa rahitāyām api sāmānyena vijātīya vyāvṛtti upakalpita abhedena ākāreṇa bhedeṣu artheṣu īkṣaṇāt sāmānyam api yat vyavasthāpyate sā api artha bhrāntiḥ iṣyeta vivecakaiḥ na hi buddhi ākāraḥ sāmānyam uktam sva lakṣaṇa tvāt 
[124,iii_124,iv]	abhiplavāt artha rūpa tayā tatvena abhāvāt ca na rūpiṇī niḥsvabhāva tayā avācyam kutaścid vacanāt matam artha niṣṭhatayā tu sāmānye gṛhyamāṇe artha bhramaḥ tathā buddhi ākārasya artha rūpa tvena vyaktiṣu abhiplavāt abhisambandhāt tattvena artha rūpa tvena abhāvāt ca na rūpiṇī tathābhūta bāhya viṣayavatī sāmānya buddhiḥ atas ca tatas ca niḥsvabhāva tayā sāmānyam bheda abhedābhyām avācyam vyaktibhyaḥ svabhāvam hi bhinnam abhinnam vā syāt kutaścid sāmānyāt bhedena vacanāt yadi vastu sāmānyam matam 
[124,v_124,vi]	yadi vastuni vastūnām avācya tvam kathañcana na eva vācyam upādāna bhedāt bheda upacārataḥ yadi evam vyakteḥ api bheda abhedābhyām vācyam syāt yasmāt na vastūnām avācya tvam kathañcana yathā hi sāmānyam svarūpavat tvāt sāmānya antarāt bhedena ucyate tathā vyakteḥ api tattva anya tvābhyām yathāsambhavamucyeta tasmāt yat kutaścid api vastunaḥ tatva anya tvābhyām avācyam tat avastu iti sa viśeṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ athavā nirviśeṣaṇe hetau na asiddhiḥ yata sā amānyā antarāt api sāmānyam bhedena na eva vācyam upādānasya karkaśā baleya ādeḥ bhedāt tad āśraya utpanna buddhi ālambanā aśva tvagotva ādīnām bhedasya upacārāt 
[125,i_125,iii]	kiñca atīta anāgatepi arthe sāmānya vinibandhanāḥ śrutayaḥ niviśante sat asat dharmaḥ katham bhavet atīta anāgatepi arthe sāmānya nibandhanā sāmānya āśrayāḥ śrutayaḥ niviśante vyavatiṣṭhante āsīt ghaṭaḥ bhaviṣyati ityādayaḥ tathā ca asataḥ ghaṭasya sāmānyam dharmaḥ iti uktam syāt tat ca sāmānyam sat asataḥ atīta ādeḥ dharmaḥ katham bhavet na hi taikṣṇyam śaśa viṣāṇasya bhavati 
[125,iv_125,vi]	upacārāt tat iṣṭam ced varttamāna ghaṭasya kā pratyāsattiḥ abhāvena yā paṭa ādau na vidyate atha upacārāt tat asat dharma tvam iṣṭam sāmānyasya na vastutas iti ced sati ghaṭe tad dharmatā dṛṣṭeḥ asati api tasmin sā kalpyate iti arthaḥ nanu sāmānya sambandhinaḥ api ghaṭasya abhāvena atīta ādi ghaṭa lakṣaṇena kā pratyāsattiḥ upacāra nibandhanam asti yā paṭa ādau na vidyate yat abhāvāt ghaṭa sambandhitā sāmānyasya paṭe na upacaryate sādṛśyam pratyāsattiḥ ita ced tat na sat asataḥ sādṛśya abhāvāt prāk tādṛś āsīt iti ced yadā āsīt na tadā tad upacāraḥ sambandhasya sattvāt yadā yana asti tadā api na sādṛśyam sati ca kiñcid upacaryeta na asati 
[125,vii_125,ix]	kiñca buddheḥ askhalitā vṛttiḥ mukhya āropitayoḥ sadā siṃhe māṇavake tadvat ghoṣaṇā api asti laukikī mukhya āropitayoḥ arthayoḥ buddheḥ grāṃhikāyāḥ askhalitā dṛḍhā vṛttiḥ tantrāt avṛttiḥ ca sadā yathā siṃhe māṇavake ca siṃha buddheḥ askhalitā skhalitā ca vṛttiḥ iti laukikī api ghoṣaṇā asti na kevalam prāmāṇikī na ca atīta anāgata ghaṭa ādi buddhiḥ skhalantī jāyate yena atīta anāgata vyakti dharma tā sāmānyasya āropitā syāt 
[126,i_126,ii]	yatra rūḍhyā asat arthopi janaiḥ śabdaḥ niveśitaḥ sa mukhyaḥ tatra tad sāmyāt gauṇonyatra skhalat gatiḥ tasmāt yatra viṣaye asat arthaḥ vācya rahitopi śabdaḥ rūḍhyā vācaka tvena janaiḥ niveśitaḥ saṃketitaḥ sa mṛkhyaḥ tatra arthe tad sāmyāt tad viṣaya sādṛśyāt anyatra sa śabdaḥ skhalat vattiḥ adṛḍha tayā pratyaya haituḥ gauṇaḥ tatas ca sat artha viṣaya tvam mukhya tvam asat artha viṣaya tvañcāmukhya tvam iti mukhyā gauṇa lakṣaṇam apāstam saṃketa vaśena niyama abhāvāt 
[126,iii_126,iv]	yathā bhāvepya bhāva ākhyām yathākalpanam eva vā kuryāt aśakte śakte vā pradhāna ādi śrutim janaḥ yathā bhāvepi putra ādau tad kārya asamartha tvāt asat kalpe abhāva ākhyām śaśa viṣāṇam bandhyā sutaḥ iti ādikām janaḥ kuryyāt tatra bhāvepya mukhyaḥ abhāva śabdaḥ abhāve tu mukhyaḥ tathā yathā kalpanam eva sāṃkhya ādi abhimate vastutas aśakte pradhāna ādau śakte vā puruṣa ādau aneka kārya samarthe tad sāmyāt pradhāna ādi śrutim janaḥ kuryyāt sa pradhāna śabdaḥ abhāṃvaḥ eva mukhyaḥ bhāve ca amukhyaḥ tasmāt sat asat artha viṣaya tā mukhya gauṇa viṣaya tā iti vyabhicāri lakṣaṇam 
[126,v_127,i]	yathā saṃketam eva tu śabda vṛttiḥ iti yukttam na ca etat vastu viṣaya tve nyāyyam tathā hi śabdebhyaḥ yādṛśī buddhiḥ naṣṭe anaṣṭepi dṛśyate tādṛśi eva śabdebhyaḥ yādṛśī yādṛśa ākārā buddhiḥ naṣṭe viṣaye tādṛśī eva anaṣṭepi viṣaye avyāpta tā indriyasya dṛśyate na hi śabda janitā ghaṭa buddhiḥ nimīlita nayanasya naṣṭe anaṣṭe vā ghaṭe viśiṣyate tulya ākāra tvāt vyāpta indriyasya tu śabdam śrṛṇvataḥ yā spaṣṭā buddhiḥ sā pratyakṣā eva na śabda kṛtā tasmāt avastu viṣayā eva śābdī buddhiḥ sat arthānām na etat śotrādi cetasām sat arthānām vastu viṣayāṇām tu śrotra ādi indriya jātānām cetasām na etat viṣaya sada sattā kālayoḥ sāmyam śabda buddheḥ iva artha abhāve indriya buddheḥ anutpatteḥ 
[127,ii_127,vi]	nanu naṣṭe anaṣṭepi vastuni ye śābdaḥ cetasī jāyete sāmānya mātra grahaṇāt sāmānyam cetasoḥ dvayoḥ tābhyām samānya mātrasya grahaṇāt tayoḥ dvayoḥ cetasoḥ sāmānyam sāmyam grāhya pratibhāsa kṛtam asti etat ca ayuktam yasmāt tasya api kevalasya prāk grahaṇam vinivāritam tasya api sāmānyasya kevalasya vyakti śūnyasya grahaṇam prāgnivāritam atad samāna tā avyaktī ityādinā
[127,vii_127,ix]	bhinnam sāmānyam niṣidhya abhinnam api niṣeddhum āha paraspara viśiṣṭānām aviśiṣṭam katham bhavet tathā dvi rūpa tāyām vā tat vastu ekam katham bhavet paraspara viśiṣṭānām viśeṣāṇām aviśiṣṭam abhinnam rūpam katham bhavet avaśyam hi vyaktīnām bhedaḥ kathañci t aṅgīkarttavyaḥ sattva rajaḥ tamasām iva prakṛti caitanyayoḥ iva vā anyathā sāmānyam eva na syāt bhinnānām abhinnasya rūpasya tattvāt ye ca bhinna svabhāvāḥ te na abhinnā bhavitum arhanti viruddha tvāt atha ekasya api samānam asamānañca dve rūpe tathā dvi rūpa tāyām tat vastu ekam katham bhavet anyaḥ hi samānāt asamānaḥ svabhāvaḥ atas ca dve vastunī syātām na tu ekam dvi rūpam 
[127,x_128,i]	atha dvayoḥ ekam tat rūpam sāmānyam tābhyām tat anyat eva syāt yadi rūpam samam tayoḥ yadi tayoḥ dvayoḥ samam samānam rūpam tadā tābhyām eva anyat eva tat syāt pṛthak bhūtam eva sāmānyam bhaviṣyati kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced āha tayoḥ iti na sambandhaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ tu na duṣyati tayoḥ tad sāmānyam iti na sambandhaḥ upakārya upakāraka tva abhāvāt tathā asambandhe ati prasaṅgāt asmad mate tu vyāvṛttiḥ sāmānyam na duṣyati atad kārya vyāvṛtteḥ avastu tvāt anyathā anyān anya tva pakṣa uktaḥ doṣaḥ 
[128,ii_128,vi]	tasmāt samāna tā eva asmin sāmānye avastu lakṣaṇam yatas samāna tvena avastu tā tasmāt samāna tā eva asmin sāmānye avastu lakṣaṇam yat sāmānyam tad avasthiti vyāpti siddheḥ bhede abhede ca vastu tva ayogāt prakāra antarasya ca abhāvāt kiñca kāryañcet tat anekam syāt naśvarañca na tat matam sāmānyam kāryam akāryam vā syāt sambandhinīnām vyaktīnām kāryañcet prativyakti sāmānya uktau anekam syāt ekañca sāmā nyam iṣṭam aneka tve sāmānya rūpa tā nāśaḥ naśvarañca na tad sāmānyam matam kāryatvāt naśvarañca tat prāpnoti kāryatvasya nāśi tvena svabhāvasya vyāpteḥ 
[128,vii_128,xii]	kiñca vastu mātra anubandhi tvāt vināśasya na nityatā vastu mātra anubandhi tvāt nāśasya vastunona nityatā syāt anitya tā virahe tu vastu virahopi vyāpya abhāvasya vyāpaka abhāva niyata tvāt atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā asambandhaḥ ca jātīnām akārya tvāt arūpa tā akārya tvāt jātīnām sva vyaktibhiḥ saha sambandhaḥ ca na syāt kārya kāraṇa bhāva abhāve tasya idam iti sambandhasya anutpattiḥ iti uktam kārya tvam hi apekṣā iti abhidhīyate iti atra antare akārya tvāt jātīnām a rūpatā niḥsvabhāva tā utpadyamānam hi sa svabhāvam bhavet na itarat niyāmaka abhāvena svabhāva abhāva prasaṅgāt 
[128,xiii_129,ii]	śābda pratyayasya avastu viṣaya tāyām upapatti antaram āha yat ca vastu balāt jñānam jāyate tat apekṣate na saṅketam na sāmānya buddhiṣu etat vibhāvyate yat ca jñānam indriya jam vastunaḥ rūpa ādeḥ bbalāt jāyate tat na saṃketam apekṣate bāla badhira ādeḥ api bhāvāt sāmānya buddhiṣu tu etat saṃketa anapekṣa tvam na vibhāvyate saṃketa grahaṇa smaraṇa apekṣa tvāt tasmāt na vastu bala bhāvinyastāḥ tathā tve sati indriya artha sannipāte kṣepā yogāt 
[129,iii_129,iv]	yāpya bheda anugā buddhiḥ kācid vastu dvaya īkṣaṇe saṅketena vinā sārtha pratyāsatti nibandhanā yā api saṃketena vinā vastu dvaya īkṣaṇe śāvaleyam dṛṣṭvā bāhuleyam paśyataḥ abheda anugamāt saḥ eva ayam iti abhedam adhyavasyantī buddhiḥ utpadyate śāvaleya karka darśane tu na utpadyate sā arthānām śāvaleya ādīnām asati api sāmānye yā pratyāsattiḥ ekabuddhi ādi kārya tvam tat nibandhanā 
[129,v_129,vii]	sāmānyam vinā eka kārya tā eva na syāt iti āha pratyāsattiḥ vinā jātyā yatheṣṭā cakṣuḥ ādiṣu jñāna kāryeṣu jātiḥ vā yayā anvā iti vibhāgataḥ pratyāsattiḥ vinā jānyā cakṣuḥ ādiḥ yeṣām viṣaya āloka manaskārāṇām teṣu jñāna kāryeṣu jñāna hetuṣu jāti ādi vinā rūpa jñāna eka kārya janaka tvam pratyāsattiḥ yathā iṣṭā yathā vā śāvaleyāt bāhuleya ādīnām karkā ādīnāñca tulye bhede yathā pratyāsatyā jāti antaram vinā eva vibhāgataḥ jātiḥ anveti śāvaleya bāhuleya ādiṣu eva go tvam samavetam na karkā ādiṣu sā eva anugāmi pratyaya nibandhanam āḥ tām alam jātyā 
[129,viii_130,iii]	itas ca na vastu sāmānyam kathañcid api vijñāne tad rūpa anava bhāsataḥ dṛśya tvena abhimatasya tad rūpasya su agrāhiṇi vijñāne kathañcid api anavabhāsataḥ nanu santi api indriyāṇi na upalabhyante tatas atra anupalambhāt asatvam na na hi indriyāṇi sva grāhiṇi jñāne pratyavabhāsamāna tvāt santīṣyante kintarhi satsu api viṣaya manaskāra ādiṣu kadācid pravartate jñānam kadācid na iti vyabhicāra balāt ati indriyāṇi kānicid indriya vyapadeśyāni vyavasthāpyante yadi nāma indriyāṇām syāt draṣṭā bhāseta tad vapuḥ rūpava tvāt yadi tu ati indriyāṇām atīndriya darśī draṣṭā nāma syāt bhāseta rūpava tvāt teṣām indriyāṇām vapuḥ 
[130,iv_130,v]	na jātīnām kevalānām adarśanāt vyakti grahe ca tat śrabda rūpāt anyat na dṛśyate jātīnāntu duśya abhimatānām kevalānām vyakti svarūpa vyatiriktānām adarśanāt abhāvaḥ eva vyakti grahe tasyāḥ vyakteḥ śabdasya gauḥ ityasya rūpāt anyat sāmānyam na dṛśyate 
[130,vi_130,vii]	jñāna mātra artha karaṇepi a yogyamat eva tat tad ayogya tayā arūpam tat hi avastuṣu lakṣaṇam atas eva adṛśyamāna tvāt jñāna mātrasya arthasya artha kriyāyāḥ karaṇepyayogyam eva tat antyā hi iyam bhāvānām artha kriyā yat uta sva jñāna jananam tatra api ayogya tayā tad sāmānyam arūpam niḥsvabhāvam hiḥ yasmāt sarva artha kriyāyām aśakta tvam avastuṣu lakṣaṇam sarva sāmarthya rahitam hi avastu iṣyate 
[130,viii_130,x]	tathā ca sāmānyam iti na vastu yathā ukta viparītam yat tat sva lakṣaṇam iṣyate yathā uktāt sāmānyāt viparītam yat tat sva lakṣaṇam ucyate idañca vaiparītyam anabhidheya tvam tatvā anya tvābhyām vācya tvam asat artha pratyaya aviśiṣṭa pratibhāsa viṣaya tvam asādhāraṇa tvam saṃketa smaraṇa anapekṣa pratipattika tvam anya rūpa vivikta svarūpa pratibhāsavat tvam artha kriyā akṣamatvañca etat yuktam sva lakṣaṇam iṣyate etad viparyayasya avastu tva sādhanasya sāmānya lakṣaṇa tvāt 
[130,xi_131,ii]	yat ca atad kārya vyavaccheda lakṣaṇa m uktam sāmānyam trividham tat ca bhāva abhāva ubhayāśrayāt sāmānyam tat ca trividham boddhavyam bhāva abhāva ubhayāśrayāt kiñcid bhāva upādānam sāmānyam yathā rūpa ādīn bhāvān āśritya kṛtaka tva ādi śabda vācyam liṅgam abhāva upādānam yathā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya asataḥ anupalabdhiḥ anutpattimat tva ādi ca tad hi abhāva āśrayam sāmānyam liṅgam ubhaya āśrayam anupalabdhi mātraṃjñeya tva ādi ca bhāva abhāva sādharaṇa tvāt 
[131,iii_131,iv]	yadi bhāva āśrayam jñānam bhāve bhāva anubandhataḥ na ukta uttara tvāt dṛṣṭa tvāt atīta ādiṣu ca anyathā yadi kiñcid sāmānyam bhāva āśrayam tat jñānam tad bhāve bhāva viṣayam prāpnoti bhāva anubandhataḥ bhāva anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt na etat yuktam na tat vastu abhidheya tva ādinā ukta uttara tvāt niṣiddham hi sāmānyasya vastu tvam anantaram eva prapañcena iti anumāna bādhita tvam pratijñāyāḥ dṛṣṭa tvāt atīta ādiṣu ca anyathā vastu vyatirekeṇa eva āsīt ghaṭaḥ bhaviṣyati ca iti sāmānya buddhiḥ utpadyate iti asiddha tā api bhāva anubandhate iti hetoḥ 
[131,v_132,ii]	bhāva dharma tvahāniḥ ced bhāva grahaṇa pūrvakam tat jñānam iti adoṣa uyam vastu vinā sāmānya buddhi utpāde bhāva dharma tva hāniḥ sāmānyasya prasajyate ced bhāvasya rūpa ādeḥ grahaṇa pūrvakam tasya sāmānyasya sādhāraṇa bāhya rūpa tayā adhyavasita buddhi ākāra lakṣaṇasya adhyavasāyena jñānam iti ayam avastu dharma tva lakṣaṇaḥ adoṣaḥ doṣaḥ na bhavati na hi sāmānyam rūpa ādiḥ iva bhāva rūpa tayā jñāna viṣayaḥ iti bhāva dharmaḥ iṣṭam meyam tu ekam sva lakṣaṇām kintu bhāva vāsanā prabodha prasūta vikalpa kalpita tvāt paramārthataḥ meyam tu ekam sva lakṣaṇam tasya eva rūpa buddhi utpādaka tvāt 
[132,iii_132,vii]	tasmāt artha kriyā siddheḥ sat asat tā vicāraṇāt sāmānyasya tu kalpita tvāt sāmarthya abhāvāt svalakṣaṇam ekam prameyam tasmāt artha kriyā siddheḥ artha kriyā arthibhiḥ sat asat tābhyām tasya eva vicāraṇāt asattvam api sva lakṣaṇasya eva vicintyate yadi ekam eva prameyam tad ācāryeṇa prameya dvaividhyam yat uktam na sva sāmānya lakṣaṇābhyām anyat prameyam asti iti tat virudhyate iti āha tasya sva para rūpābhyām gateḥ meya dvayam matam tasya sva lakṣaṇasya pratyakṣatas sva rūpeṇa anumānataḥ para rūpeṇa sāmānya ākāreṇa gateḥ meya dvayam matam na tu bhūta sāmānyasya sattvāt 
[132,viii_132,xi]	ayathā abhiniveśena dvitīyā bhrāntiḥ iṣyate yā ca dvitīyā para rūpeṇa gatiḥ ayatha abhiniveśena bhrāntiḥ iṣyate sā anumānam yathā arthosti yathā vā su a ākāraḥ tathā na abhiniviśate kintu su a ākāram bāhyam sādhāraṇa tayā manyate gatiḥ ced para rūpeṇa na ca bhrānteḥ pramāṇa tā nanu anumānam para rūpeṇa gatiḥ ced tadā bhrāntiḥ eva na ca bhrānteḥ pramāṇatā iṣyate mṛgatṛṣṇā ādeḥ iva 
[133,i_133,vi]	atra ucyate abhiprāya avi saṃvādāt api bhrānteḥ pramāṇa tā gatiḥ api anyathā dṛṣṭā bhrānteḥ api pramāṇa tā abhiprāyasya artha kriyā arthibhiḥ jñāna gocara tayā abhiprāya viṣayīkṛtasya artha kriyā samarthasya arthasya saṃvādāt artha kriyā arthinaḥ hi tad sādhana samartha artha prāpakam pramāṇam icchanti anyathā para rūpeṇa gatiḥ api kācid abhipreta artha samvādikā dṛṣṭā iti pramāṇam eva nanu anumānam vastu eva gṛhṇat pramāṇam astu kim bhrāntiḥ iṣyate iti āha pakṣaḥ ca ayam kṛta uttaraḥ pakṣaḥ ca ayam prāk eva na tat vastu abhidheya tvāt ityādinā kṛta uttaraḥ 
[133,vii_133,ix]	nanu bhrāntam api yadi anumānam pramāṇam tadā sarvā eva bhrāntiḥ pramāṇam syāt iti āha maṇi pradīpa prabhayoḥ maṇi buddhyā abhidhāvatoḥ mithyājñāna aviśeṣepi viśeṣa urtha kriyām prāti maṇi pradīpayoḥ ye prabhe tayoḥ maṇi buddhyā maṇiḥ eva ayam iti adhyavasāyena tad grahaṇa artham dhāvataḥ mithyājñānasya bhrānta tvasya aviśeṣepi viśeṣaḥ artha kriyām prati maṇi prabhāyāṃm api adhyavasāyī maṇi sādhyām artha kriyām prāpnoti 
[133,x_133,xi]	yathā tathā ayathārtha tvepi anumāna tad ābhayoḥ artha kriyā anurodhena pramāṇa tvam vyavasthitam dīpa prabhā āyāntu maṇi vyavasāyī tat na prāpnoti iti yathā tathā trirūpa liṅga jam anumānam tadābhañca tat na na tathā tayoḥ su a ākāre bāhyadhyavasāya pravṛtta tvāt ayathārtha tvepi pramāṇa tvam vyavasthitam viśeṣeṇa avasthitam artha kriyā anurodhena anumānam eva pramāṇam paramparayā arthāt utpatteḥ tad prāpaka tvāt na itara dvi paryayāt tasmāt prameya dvi tvam gati bhedāt 
[133,xii_134,i]	tayoḥ lakṣaṇam grahaṇañca ākhyātum āha buddhiḥ yatra artha sāmarthyāt anvaya vi atirekiṇī tasya sva tatram grahaṇam atas anyat vastu atīndriyam artha sāmarthyāt jāyamānā buddhiḥ yatra anvaya vyatirekiṇī tad sva lakṣaṇantasya grahaṇam apara āśrayam svarūpa grahaṇam sva janyayā artha svarūpayā buddhyā sākṣāt tasya grahaṇāt atas sva lakṣaṇa tvāt anyat vastu yat anvaya vyatirekau na anukaroti buddhiḥ sākṣāt apratibhāsamānam kevala madhyavasāya viṣayaḥ tad sāmānya lakṣaṇam atīndriyam buddhiṣu aprati bhāsanāt 
[134,ii_134,iv]	kathantat pratyetavyam iti āha tasya adṛṣṭa ātma rūpasya gateḥ anyorthaḥ āśrayaḥ tad āśrayeṇa sambandhī yadi syāt gamakaḥ tadā tasya sāmānyasya sva lakṣaṇa viśeṣeṇa sva lakṣaṇa vivekena adṛṣṭa ātma rūpasya gateḥ pratīteḥ tasmāt anyaḥ arthaḥ liṅga bhūtaḥ āśrayaḥ siddhi nimittam yadi tatas pratyetavyena anagni vyavaccheda ādinā tad āśrayeṇa ca dharmiṇā sambandhī sambandhavān syāt tadā gamakaḥ na anyathā anane sādhya pratibandhaḥ anvaya vyatireka rūpaḥ pakṣa dharma tā ca liṅgasya uktā 
[134,v_134,vii]	nanu anya āśrayeṇa ca svarūpa pratītiḥ bhaviṣyati tathā api parokṣa tā katham iti āha gamaka anuga sāmānya rūpeṇa eva tadā gatiḥ tasmāt sarvaḥ parokṣa ūrthaḥ viśeṣeṇa na gamyate tadā artha antarāt pratīti kāle gamakam pakṣa sa pakṣa anuyāyi liṅgam tad anuyāyinā tad vyāpakena sāmānya rūpeṇa eva parokṣa ūrthaḥ gamyate na tu sarvatas vyāvṛttena viśiṣṭena rūpeṇa tasmāt sarvaḥ parokṣaḥ arthaḥ pratīyamānaḥ na viśeṣeṇa kathañcid gamyate yena parokṣatā hāniḥ syāt 
[134,viii_134,ix]	yā ca sambandhinaḥ dharmāt bhūtiḥ dharmiṇi jñāyate sa anumānam parokṣāṇām ekāntena eva sādhanam yā ca sambandhinaḥ dharmāt anvaya vi atirekataḥ liṅgāt tad āśraye dharmiṇi jñāyate parokṣa artha pratītiḥ sa anumānam trirūpa liṅga prabhavat tvāt tat eva anumānam parokṣāṇām ekāntena eva sādhanam pratyakṣasya tatra āvṛtteḥ 
[134,x_134,xi]	na pratyakṣa parokṣābhyām meyasya anyasya sambhavaḥ tasmāt prameya dvi tvena pramāṇa dvi tvam iṣyate na ca pratyakṣa parokṣābhyām anyasya prameyasya sambhavaḥ iti darśitam prāk tasmāt prameyasya dvi tvena pramāṇa dvi tvam iṣyate prameyam adhigacchat pramāṇam ucyate 
[135,i_135,iv]	tri eka saṃkhyā nirāsaḥ vā prameya dvaya darśanāt tat ca dvidham iti tad grāhakam dvayam api pramāṇam eva prameya dvayasya darśanāt tri eka saṃkhyā nirāsaḥ vā boddhavyaḥ tṛtīya ādikam na pramāṇam tṛtīya ādi prameya abhāvāt na api ekam dvitīyasya prameyasya tena anadhigateḥ na hi pratyakṣam sva lakṣaṇa sāmarthyāt tad ākāra grāhi jātam sāmānyam pratyeti kalpanā gamya tvāt tasya ekam eva aprameya tvāt asataḥ ced matam ca naḥ nanu pratyakṣam ekam eva pramāṇam asataḥ aprameya tvāt asat ca sāmānyam atra āha asataḥ aprameya tvam matañca naḥ 
[135,v_135,vi]	anekāntaḥ aprameya tve asadbhāvasya viniścayaḥ tad niścaya pramāṇām vā dvitīyam kim aniṣṭam āpadyate sva lakṣaṇam eva tu para rūpeṇa gateḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇam iṣṭam tat ca sat eva iti katham aprameyam tatas tad sādhanam api pramāṇam eva tathā asataḥ aprameya tve sādhye asattvāt iti hetuḥ anekānta upi tathā hi para loka ādeḥ asat tayā cārvākeṇa āpi iṣyate eva kena api pramāṇena niścayaḥ athavā prameya tva abhāvasya api asattva hetunā eva niścayaḥ iti vyaktam anaikāntika tvam atas ca yatas eva pramāṇāt tasya abhāvasya niścayaḥ tat eva dvitīyam pramāṇam anumānam na adhyakṣam 
[135,vii_135,ix]	kasmāt evam iti āha na akṣajā matiḥ abhāve artha balāt jāteḥ artha śakti anapekṣaṇaḥ vyavadhāna ādi bhāvepi jāyeta indriya jā matiḥ na akṣa jā matiḥ abhāve viṣaye pravartate arthasya grāhyasya balāt jāteḥ yat balena pratyakṣam pravartate tat eva pratipadyate na ca abhāvasya sāmarthya nāma yadi punar artha sāmarthya anapekṣaṇam asya tadā grāhyasya arthasya śakti anapekṣaṇe tad vyavadhāna ādi bhāvepi indriya jā matiḥ jāyeta na ca etat asti tatas artha sāmarthya apekṣi na abhāva viṣayam bhavitum arhati 
[135,x_136,ii]	syāt etat abhāve vinivṛttiḥ ced pratyakṣasya eva niścayaḥ viruddham sā eva vā liṅgam anvaya vyatirekiṇī pratyakṣasya eva pravṛttiḥ bhāve sattva niścayaḥ vinivṛttiḥ ca abhāve niścayaḥ na tu pramāṇa antara vṛttiḥ iti ced viruddham idam yaḥ pratyakṣa abhāvāt niścayaḥ sa pratyakṣāt iti na hi pratyakṣata nivṛttyoḥ aikātmyam tathā hi abhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ eva syāt bhāvopi ca abhāvaḥ na ca pratyakṣata nivṛttau api avaśyam abhāvaḥ vyavadhāna ādiṣu artha sattva ipi tasya abhāvāt atha artha anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyinī pratyakṣa nivṛttiḥ eka jñāna saṃsargi padārtha antara upalabdhi rūpā abhāva niścaya hetuḥ tadā sā eva pratyakṣa nivṛttiḥ anupalabdhi ākhya anvaya vyatirekiṇī liṅgam iti tad jā pratītiḥ anumānam eva iti katham na apratyakṣam pramāṇam 
[136,iii_136,vii]	kiñca siddham ca para caitanya pratipatteḥ pramā dvayam para caitanya pratipatteḥ pramāṇa dvayam siddham na hi pratyakṣāt arvāk darśanaḥ para caitanyam avaiti kintu sva santāne buddhi pūrvaka tvena upalabdha ceṣṭā ādi darśanāt tad anumānam para citta niścayaḥ kim asti iti āha vyavahāra ādau pravṛtteḥ ca siddhaḥ tad bhāva niścayaḥ paraspara preṣaṇa adhyeṣaṇa vyavahāra ādau pravṛtteḥ ca siddhaḥ ca tasyāḥ para caitanya pratipatteḥ bhāva niścayaḥ 
[136,viii_136,x]	nanu anumāna abhimatā pratītiḥ na asti eva iti na brūmaḥ kintu prāmāṇye tasyāḥ vipratipadyāmahe iti āha pramāṇam avisaṃvādāt tat kvacid vyabhicārataḥ na āśvāsaḥ iti ced liṅgam durdṛṣṭiḥ atad īdṛśam pramāṇantad anu mānam avisamvādāt pratyakṣam api hi samvādaka tvāt pramāṇam tat ca anumānasya api samānam kvacid śyāmatā ādi sādhana artham upātte tad putra ādau liṅge vyabhicārataḥ samvāde anāśvāsaḥ iti ced liṅgasya durvṛṣṭiḥ bhrāntiḥ aliṅgaḥ eva liṅga buddhiḥ tasyāḥ etat liṅgam īdṛśam vyabhicāri bhavataḥ pratibhāti na khalu trividham liṅgam sādhya vyabhicāri yat ca vyabhicāri tat trividham eva na bhavati 
[137,i_137,iii]	etat eva āha yatas kadācid siddhā asya pratītiḥ vastunaḥ kvacid tat avaśyam tatas jātam tad svabhāvopi vā bhavet yatas vastunaḥ dhūma śiṃśapa ādeḥ liṅgāt asya sādhyasya vahri vṛkṣa ādeḥ kvacid dharmiṇi kadācid anumāna kāle pratītiḥ siddhā tat dhūma ādikam tatas vahni ādeḥ avaśyam jātam tat śiṃśapa ādikam tasya vṛkṣasya svabhāvopi vā avaśyam bhavet 
[137,iv_137,vi]	na ca kārya svabhāvayoḥ kāraṇa vyāpaka vyabhicāraḥ yasmāt sva nimittāt svabhāvāt vā vinā na arthasya sambhavaḥ yat ca rūpam tayoḥ dṛṣṭam tedavān yatra lakṣaṇam svasya nimittāt kāraṇāt vinā svabhāvāt vyāpakāt vā vinā arthasya kāryasya vyāpyasya ca na sambhavaḥ tad utpādya tvāt tad rūpa tvāt ca tatas tad āśrayeṇa utpannā anumāna pratītiḥ avyabhicāriṇī eva yat ca tayoḥ dhūma śiṃśapayaḥ rūpam sādhya kārya svabhāva tvasya avyabhicāra nimittam dṛṣṭam tat eva anyatra api hetau lakṣaṇam boddhavyam na ca tad putra tvam śyāma tvasya kāryam svabhāvaḥ vā tatas yat vyabhicāri tad aliṅgam eva 
[137,vii_137,ix]	anupalabdheḥ avyabhicāram darśayitum āha svabhāve sva nimitte vā dṛśye darśana hetuṣu anyeṣu satsu adṛśye ca sattā vā tadvataḥ katham pratiṣedhasya svabhāve svasya niṣedhya ātmanaḥ nimitte kāraṇe dṛśye darśana yogye darśanasya hetuṣu indriya manaskāra ādiṣu anyeṣu satsu vidyamāna iṣu dṛśye anupalabhyamāne ca tadvataḥ dṛśya anupalambhavataḥ bhāvasya sattā vā katham yujyate na hi satsu anyeṣu upalambha pratyayeṣu dṛśyasya sataḥ kadācid anupalambha sambhavaḥ tasmāt dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ artha abhāvaḥ eva bhavati iti tad prabhavā abhāva pratīti ravi samvādinī tasmāt sādhya pratibaddha liṅga prasūta tvāt trividha liṅga jepi anumāne na asti anāśvāsaḥ 
[138,i_138,v]	aprāmāṇye ca sāmānya buddheḥ tat lopaḥ āgataḥ pretyabhāvavat evam api tu aprāmāṇye sāmānya buddheḥ iṣyamāṇe tasya parokṣasya arthasya anumāna vyavasthāpyamānasya lopaḥ abhāvaḥ āgataḥ pretyabhāva vat para lokasya iva yadi hi pratyakṣam ekam pramāṇam tadā yatra tat na pravartate tasya api abhāvaḥ eva syāt na ca etat asti na hi cārvākaḥ deśa antara stham sva pitaram anupalabha māna stabhāvam vyavasthāpayitum arhati syāt etat akṣaiḥ tat paryāyeṇa pratīyate na upalabhyamānam eva asti kintu paryyāyeṇa paripāṭyā akṣaiḥ yat pratīyate tat api asti ced pitṛ ādayaḥ ca upalabdhāḥ upalapsyante ca iti santi eva 
[138,vi_138,vii]	tat ca na indriya śakti ādau akṣa buddheḥ asambhavāt abhāva pratipattau syāt buddheḥ janma animittakam tat ca na yuktam indriya ākhyāyām śaktau ādi grahaṇāt āhāra ādeḥ kṣudh upaghāta ādi sāmarthye ca paryyāyeṇa api indriya buddheḥ asambha vāt abhāva pratītau satyām pratyakṣāyāḥ buddheḥ janma animittakam syāt na hi dṛṣṭa mātrebhyaḥ viṣaya āloka manaskāra cakṣuḥ golakebhyaḥ adhyakṣa janma satsu api teṣu abhāvāt vyatirekāt atiriktam kiñcid adṛśyam kāraṇam iṣyate yasya indriyam iti vyapadeśaḥ tasya paryyāyeṇa api na adhyakṣam grāhakam asti iti abhāvaḥ syāt tatas ca akāraṇakam pratyakṣa janma prāptam ahetoḥ ca nityam satvam asat tvam vā syādi tyuktam 
[138,viii_139,ii]	syāt etat pratyakṣāt eva sāmānya pratītiḥ bhaviṣyati kim anumānena iti āha sva lakṣaṇe ca pratyakṣam avikalpa tayā vinā vikalpena na sāmānya grahaḥ tasmiḥ tatas anumā sva lakṣaṇe ca pratyakṣam avikalpa tayā pravartate sāmānyasya tu grahaḥ vikalpena vinā na bhavati tatas kāraṇāt tasmin sāmānye anumā eva vikalpikā na adhyakṣam avikalpa kam 
[139,iii_139,v]	nanu prameya niyame varṇa anitya tā na pratīyate pramāṇam anyat tad buddhiḥ vinā liṅgena saṃbhavāt pratyakṣam sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam anumānam sāmānya viṣayam iti prameyasya niyame svīkriyamāṇe varṇṇasya nīla ādeḥ viṣayasya anitya tā anitya tā sāmānya ātma tā na pratīyate iti prāptam na hi sāmānya viśeṣa ātmakam prameyam viśeṣa mātra viṣayeṇa adhyakṣeṇa sāmānya mātra viṣayeṇa anumānena vā pratyetum śakyam pratīyate ca atas tat buddhiḥ pramāṇam anyat syāt na pratyakṣam sāmānyasya grahaṇāt na api anumānam vinā liṅgena sambhavāt viśeṣasya api grahaṇāt ca 
[139,vi_139,viii]	tathā viśeṣa dṛṣṭe liṅgasya sambandhasya aprasiddhitaḥ tad pramāṇa antaram meya bahu tvāt bahu tā api vā viśeṣa dṛṣṭe pratyakṣeṇa agnim dṛṣṭvā kramāt tam eva dhūmāt liṅgāt saḥ eva ayam vahniḥ iti niścinoti anumānena liṅgasya sambandha asiddhitaḥ tad pramāṇa antaraṃsyāt na hi tat pratyakṣam liṅgam balāt utpatteḥ na api anumānam dahana dhūma viśeṣayoḥ sambandha agrahaṇāt tasmāt meyānām pratyakṣam lakṣaṇam sāmānyam sāmānya viśeṣāṇām bahu tvāt bahutā api vā
[139,ix_139,x]	pramāṇānām anekasya vṛtteḥ ekatra vā yathā viśeṣa dṛṣṭeḥ eka tri saṃkhyā apohaḥ na vā bhavet pramāṇānām syāt anekasya vā pramāṇasya ekatra viṣaye vṛtteḥ pramāṇa bahutā syāt yathā ekam eva sva lakṣaṇam pratyakṣeṇa viśeṣa dṛṣṭena ca anumānena pratīyate prameyasya dvi tva grahaṇayoḥ niyame pramādvi tvam syāt na anyathā tri eka saṃkhyāyāḥ apohaḥ yaḥ uktaḥ prameya dvi tvāt sa na vā bhavet 
[140,i_140,v]	viṣayān iyamāt anya prameyasya ca sambhavāt viṣayasya grahaṇa aniyamāt yadā hi ekena api pramāṇena anekam gṛhyate tadā prameya dvi tvepi ekam eva pramāṇam syāt prameya dvayāt anyasya ca sāmānya viśeṣasya meyasya sambhavāt tri ādikam vā tad grāhakam mānam bhavet atra ucyate yojanāt varṇa sāmānye na ayam doṣaḥ prasajyate vikalpakena jñānena anitya tāyāḥ varṇṇa sāmānye yojana āt ayam sāmānya viśeṣa ātmaka prameya grāhaka pramāṇa antara abhyupagama lakṣaṇaḥ doṣaḥ na prasaṃjyate na hi viśeṣaḥ anitya tayā yojyate vikalpānām atad viṣaya tvasya ukteḥ vakṣyamāṇa tvāt ca 
[140,vi_141,i]	nanu varṇṇa sāmānyasya avastu tvāt tad yojitā anitya tā ādayaḥ avastu dharmāḥ syuḥ iti āha na avastu rūpam tasya eva tathā siddhe prasādhanāt anyatra na anya siddhiḥ ced na tasya eva prasiddhitaḥ na avastunaḥ rūpam anitya tva ādi tasya eva vastunaḥ tathā anitya tva ādibhiḥ ākāraiḥ siddhe rniścayasya prāk prasādhanāt adhyavasāya anurodhena hi vikalpānām viṣaya vyavasthā yadi api ca ete su a ākāra grāhiṇaḥ tathā api bāhyam eva viṣaya tayā vyavasthāpyante anādi abhyāsa viśeṣāt anumānantu vastu pratibaddha liṅga prabhava tvāt yatha avasthitam eva vastu vyavasyati iti vastu eva kṣaṇa sthiti dharmakam asmāt siddham tatas na avastu rūpam anitya tva ādi syāt etat anye trāvastuni sāmānye anitya tā ādi sambandhini sidhyati anyasya vastunaḥ anitya rūpasya na siddhiḥ iti ced na etat yuktam tasya eva vastunaḥ tasya eva anitya rūpasya adhyavasāya vaśena anumānāt prasiddhitaḥ 
[141,ii_141,iv]	katham punar vastu adhyavasāye api tad samvādaka tā iti āha yaḥ hi bhāvaḥ yathābhūtaḥ sa tādṛś liṅga cetasaḥ hetuḥ tad jā tathābhūte tasmāt vastuni liṅgi dhīḥ yaḥ hi sādhya dharmaḥ yathābhūtaḥ kāraṇa vyāpaka svabhāvaḥ sa tādṛśaḥ kāraṇa kārya tayā vyāpaka vyāpya tayā gṛhīta vyāptikasya liṅgasya cetasaḥ paraṃparā hetuḥ tad jā tasmāt liṅga cetasaḥ jātā tathābhūte vastuni kāraṇa vyāpaka rūpe sādhya dharme liṅgi dhīḥ tasmāt paraṃparayā sādhya pratibandhāt liṅgi dhīḥ sati eva vastuni bhavantī tad samvādāt pramāṇam eva 
[141,v_141,vii]	nanu liṅgam api liṅgi vat sāmānyam eva tathā dhūmaḥ kṛtakam vā iti eva na liṅgam kintarhi vahni kārya tayā anitya tva vyāpya tayā ca gṛhītam na ca viśeṣe vyāpti grahaḥ sāmānyañca na adhyakṣa gamyam vikalpa mātreṇa tad pratītau anāśvāsaḥ na eṣa doṣaḥ pratyakṣeṇa kāraṇa kāryayoḥ vyāvṛtti dvaya viśiṣṭayoḥ gṛ hītayoḥ vijātīya vyāvṛtti āśrayeṇa utpanna vikalpena kvacid anumānena vyāptim gṛhītavataḥ paścāt dhūma kṛtaka tva ādi darśanāt tādrūpye kārya vyāpya buddhiḥ liṅga buddhiḥ sā ca tad pratibandhāt anumānam eva iti na asti anāśvāsaḥ etat eva āha liṅga liṅgi dhiyoḥ evam pāramparyeṇa vastuni pratibandhāt tad ābhāsa śūnyayoḥ api avaṃcanam liṅga liṅgi dhiyoḥ evam ukta kramāt pāramparyeṇa vastuni pratibandhāt tayoḥ liṅga liṅginoḥ ābhāsaḥ sākṣāt svarūpa pratibhāsaḥ tat śūnyayoḥ api liṅga liṅgi vastuni avañcanam samvādanam 
[142,i_142,ii]	nanu liṅga buddheḥ api liṅgi buddhi tvāt pṛthak upādānam anarthakam na anarthakam pratyakṣam udbhūta vikalpaḥ vā tad buddhiḥ iti vipratipatti nirāsa artha tvāt yadi pramāṇe liṅga liṅgi dhiyau tadā pratyakṣa vat abhrānte syātām iti āha tad rūpa adhyavasāyāt ca tayoḥ tad rūpa śūnyayoḥ tad rūpā vañcaka tvepi kṛtā bhrānti vyavasthitiḥ 
[142,iii]	tayoḥ dvayoḥ tad rūpasya liṅga liṅgi rūpasya adhyavasāyāt pravartane sati vastuni paramparayā tad pratibaddha tayā ca tad rūpasya avañcaka tve samvādaka tvepi bhrānti vyavasthitiḥ kṛtā kasmāditi āha tat rūpa śūnyayoḥ na hi liṅga liṅgi svarūpa pratibhāsinyau dhiyau ime sva pratibhāse anarthe artha adhyāvasāyena pravṛtta tvāt 
[142,iv_142,v]	tasmāt vastuni boddhavye vyāpakam vyāpya cetasaḥ nimittam tad svabhāvaḥ vā kāraṇam tat ca tat dhiyaḥ tasmāt vastuni vidhinā boddhavye vyāpakam sādhyam vyāpya cetasaḥ liṅga buddheḥ nimitte paramparayā yasmāt svabhāvaḥ vā tat vyāpakam vyāpyasya yathā nitya tvam kṛtaka tvasya kāraṇam vā dahanaḥ dhūmasya tat ca vyāpya cetasaḥ tat dhiyaḥ svabhāva kāraṇa dhiyaḥ nimittam iti tayā adhyavasitasya samvāda niyamaḥ samvādi tvam evam pratyakṣasya api prāmāṇya lakṣaṇam 
[142,vi_143,i]	pratiṣedhaḥ tu sarvatra sādhyate anupalambhataḥ siddhim pramāṇaiḥ vadatām arthāt eva viparyayāt pratiṣedhaḥ tu yatra sākṣāt niṣedhya anupalabdhiḥ viruddhā hi upalabdhiḥ vā darśyate tatra sarvatra anupalambhataḥ sādhyate yasmāt pramāṇaiḥ arthasya siddhim vadatām arthāt sāmārthyāt eva viparyayāt pramāṇa abhāvāt artha abhāvaḥ sidhyati 
[143,ii_143,iv]	nanu viruddha ādi upalabdhau anupalambhaḥ katham niṣedha sādhakaḥ iti āha dṛṣṭā viruddha dharma uktiḥ tasya tad kāraṇasya vā niṣedhe yā api tasya eva sā apramāṇa tva sūcanā dṛṣṭā viruddha dharmasya uktiḥ yā tasya niṣedhyasya tad kāraṇasya vā niṣedhe kartavye yathā na atra śīta sparśaḥ na vā roma harṣa yukta puruṣa vān ayam pradeśaḥ vahneḥ iti sā api tasya eva niṣedhyasya eva apramāṇa tvasya pramāṇa rahita tvasya sūcanā viruddhasya kāraṇa viruddha tvasya ca upalambhena niṣedhya anupalambhaḥ eva khyāpyate 
[143,v_143,vi]	anyathā ekasya dharmasya svabhāva uktyā parasya tat nāstitvam kena gamyeta anyathā ekasya viruddha ādeḥ dharmasya svabhāva uktyā sattā pratipādanena parasya niṣedhyasya tat na astitvam sisā dhayiṣitam kena kāraṇena gamyeta na hi anya sattve aparasya satva abhāva uti prasaṅgāt aniṣiddha upalabdheḥ abhāvā siddheḥ 
[143,vii_143,x]	virodhāt ced asau api siddhaḥ kena atha yat niṣidhyate yat ca upadarśyate tayoḥ virodhāt saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇāt eka bhāve anya abhāvaḥ iti ced nanu asau api virodhaḥ kena prakāreṇa siddhaḥ asaha sthānāt iti ced tat kutas matam dṛśyasya darśana abhāvāt iti ced sā apramāṇa tā dvayoḥ saha anavasthānāt virodhaḥ siddhaḥ iti ced tad sahānavasthānam kutas hetoḥ matam yena virodha vyavasthā avikala kāraṇasya pravartamānasya dṛśyasya anya bhāve adarśanāt saha anavasthāna gatiḥ iti ced nanu yat eva adarśanam sā apramāṇa tā pramāṇa rahita tā anupalabdhiḥ iti arthaḥ 
[143,xi_144,i]	tasmāt sva śabdena uktā api sā abhāvasya prasādhikā yasya apramāṇam sā avācyaḥ niṣedhaḥ tena sarvathā yasmāt avaśyam paramparayā anupalabdheḥ eva pratiṣedhaḥ tasmāt sva śabdena anupalambha svarūpa vācaka śabdena uktā svabhāva anupalambha ādau api śabdāt anuktā api viruddha upalabdhi ādau sa anupalabdhiḥ abhāva sādhikā tasyāḥ eva pratipādya tvāt yasya tu cārvākasya sā anupalabdhiḥ apramāṇam pratiṣedhe sādhye tena sarvathā niṣedhaḥ avācyaḥ pratyakṣasya bhāva mātra viṣaya tvāt pramāṇa antarasya ca abhāvāt 
[144,ii_144,iii]	etena tad viruddha artha kārya uktiḥ upavarṇitā prayogaḥ kevalam bhinnaḥ sarvatra arthaḥ na bhidyate etena svabhāva tad kāraṇa viruddha upalabdhyoḥ anupalabdhi tva pratipādanena tayoḥ svabhāva tad kāraṇayoḥ viruddha arthasya kārya uktiḥ upavarṇṇitā boddhavyā yathā na atra śīta sparśaḥ roma harṣavān vā puruṣaḥ dhūmāt iti atra api niṣedhya anupalambhasya paraṃparayā pratipādanāt upalakṣaṇañca etat vyāpaka viruddha tad kārya upalabdhī api boddhavye yathā na atra tuṣāra sparśaḥ vahneḥ dhūmāt iti etāsu svabhāva anupalabdhi viruddha upalabdhi ādiṣu prayogaḥ śabda abhidhā vyāpāraḥ param anupalambha upalambha pratipādaka tvena bhidyate sarvatra arthaḥ niṣedhya anupalambha lakṣaṇaḥ na bhidyate tasya eva sarvatra pratipādya tvāt 
[144,iv_144,v]	viruddham tat ca sa upāyam avidhāya apidhāya ca pramāṇa uktiḥ niṣedhe yā na sāmnāya anusāriṇī yā punar dvividhena api virodhena viruddham artham abhidhā yaḥ yam kañcid artham upadarśyate tat niṣedhyañca saha abhāva niścaya upāyena kāraṇa vyāpaka kārya anupalambhe vartamānam avidhāyātaḥ eva apidhāya ca pidhānam iva pidhānam sva rūpa pratīti virodhi tvāt anupalambhaḥ tam akṛtvā kāraṇa ādi anupalambha apradarśanāt tad upalambha saṃbhāvanā na vyāhata eva evam niṣedhya upalambha sambhāvanām anivārya anya vidhinā niṣedhe kartavye pramāṇa uktiḥ yā na sāmnāya anusāriṇī 
[145,i_145,v]	ukti ādeḥ sarva vid pretya bhāva ādi pratiṣedha vat ukti ādeḥ hetoḥ sarva vidaḥ pretyabhāvasya para lokasya niṣedha vat yathā na sarvajña tvam asya puruṣasya vaktṛ tvāt pretyabhāvaḥ puruṣa tvāt ityādi kasmāt punar iyam viruddha uktiḥ eva na iti āha atīndriyāṇām arthānām virodhasya aprasiddhitaḥ atīndriyāṇām sārvajña para loka ādīnām arthānām kenacid vaktṛ tva ādinā virodhasya aprasiddhitaḥ jñāna utkarṣa apakarṣayoḥ vacana apakarṣa utkarṣa adarśanāt viparyaya darśanāt ca 
[145,vi_145,vii]	bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ kaḥ syātām yat yukti saṃvidau tādṛśaḥ anupalabdheḥ ced ucyatām sā eva sādhanam yadi ca ukti samvidau saha syātām kaḥ tayoḥ parasparam bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ na hi jñāna vacanayoḥ virodhaḥ siddhaḥ yena eka satve aparasya abhāvaḥ avirodhopi na siddhaḥ iti ced satyam kintu saṃśayepi na vaktṛ tvam anaikāntikam tādṛśaḥ sarvajñasya vaktuḥ anupalabdheḥ abhāvaḥ ced ucyatām niṣedhe sādhye sā eva anupalabdhiḥ sādhanam na atra anyasya śaktiḥ 
[145,viii_145,ix]	aniścaya karam proktam īdṛś kva anupalambhanam tat na atyanta parokṣeṣu sat asat tā viniścayau kintvī dṛś ati indriya artha viṣayam anupalambha namaniścaya karam proktam sati api arthe sambhavāt tat tasmā atyanta parokṣeṣu sat asat tā niścayau na sataḥ sati api pramāṇa āvṛtteḥ pramāṇa nivṛttau api artha abhāva asiddheḥ tasmāt na anupalabdheḥ kutaścid anya smāt abhāva siddhiḥ kintu viruddhāt eva 
[145,x_145,xi]	bhinnaḥ abhinna upi vā dharmaḥ sa viruddhaḥ prayujyate yathā agniḥ ahime sādhye sattā vā janma bādhanī sa ca viruddhaḥ dharmaḥ kvacid bhinnaḥ vā prayujyate yathā agniḥ ahime hima abhāve sādhye kvacid abhinnaḥ vā yathā sattā janmanaḥ bādhanī mahat ādīnām janma abhāva prasaṅgaḥ sattvāt iti sattā janmanoḥ ca abhedaḥ sāṃkhya abhyupagamāt ucyate na tu paramārthataḥ tādātmyam viruddhayoḥ asti viruddhe ca sattā janmanī prāk asattayā hi abhivyakti rūpa tāya lābhaḥ janma ucyate sattā tu vidyamāna tā tatas yena rūpeṇa sattvam na tena janma yena ca janma tena na sattvam iti vyaktaḥ paraspara parihāra sthitiḥ virodhaḥ 
[146,i_146,ii]	yathā vastu eva vastūnām sādhane sādhanam matam tathā vastu eva vastūnām sva nivṛttau nivarttakam yathā ca vastūnām sādhyānām sādhane sādhanam vastu eva matam na avastu tathā vastu eva svasya nivṛttau vastūnām nivarttakam na avastu 
[146,iii_146,iv]	etena kalpanā nyastaḥ yatra kvacana sambhavāt dharmaḥ pakṣa sapakṣa anyatara tva ādiḥ apa uditaḥ etena vastunaḥ sādhana tva pratipādanena vikalpanā nyastaḥ dharmaḥ pakṣa sa pakṣa anyatara tva ādi ādi śabdāt mad upagama ādiḥ ca apoditaḥ pratikṣiptaḥ boddhavyaḥ tādṛśasya sādhanasya yatra kvacana sādhye sambhavāt na hi pakṣa tvam sa pakṣa tvam vā jāti niyatam kintu vāñcha adhīnam avastu atas samīhita siddhau sarva sarvasya sidhyet 
[146,v_146,vi]	tatra api vyāpakaḥ dharmaḥ nivṛtteḥ gamakaḥ mataḥ vyāpyasya sva nivṛttiḥ ced paricchinnā kathañcana tatra vastuni api vyāpakaḥ dharmaḥ kāraṇam svabhāvaḥ vā vyāpyasya kāryasya svabhāvasya nivṛtteḥ gamakaḥ mataḥ vyāpakasya kāraṇa svabhāvasya sva nivṛttiḥ kathañcana sākṣāt paramparayā vā paricchinnā ced syāt 
[146,vii_147,iii]	yat apramāṇa tā bhāve liṅgam tasya eva kathyate tad atyanta vimūḍha artham tathā yasya arthasya eka jñāna saṃsarggiṇaḥ apramāṇa tā pramāṇa nivṛttiḥ tasya eva abhāve abhāva vyavahāre ca sādhye sā pramāṇa nivṛttiḥ svabhāva anupalambha ākhyā liṅgam kathyate tad svabhāva anupalabdhi liṅgam atyanta vimūḍha artha ye hi anupalabhyamānam api dṛśyam asat tayā mohāt na vyavaharanti tān prati vyavahāra sādhakam tat liṅgam kasmāt punar amūḍha artham api tat na iti āha āgopālam asaṃvṛtteḥ āgopālam asya arthasya asaṃvṛtteḥ agūḍha tvāt prasiddheḥ iti arthaḥ 
[147,iv_147,vi]	etāvat niścaya phalam abhāvenupalambhanam tat ca hetau svabhāve vā adṛśye dṛśya tayā mate etāvat trividham kāraṇa vyāpaka svabhāva anupalambhanam abhāve abhāva vyavahāre ca niścaya phalam kāraṇa viruddha upalambha ādayaḥ tu kāraṇa ādi anupalambha upalakṣaṇa tvāt trividhaḥ eva antarbhūtāḥ tat ca abhāva niścaya phala tvam anupalambhasya hetau svabhāve ca vyāpake niṣedhya rūpe ca dṛśya tayā darśana yogya tayā mate adṛśye anupalabhyamāne sati na anyathā tat evam trividha liṅga jam anumānam pramāṇam vastu samvādāt tatas tad prasiddhasya anitya tā ādeḥ na vastu dharma tā iti sthitam 
[147,vii_147,ix]	nanu anityaḥ ayam varṇṇaḥ iti sva lakṣaṇe yojanā tat katham yojanāt varṇṇa sāmānyaḥ iti uktam atra āha anumānāt anitya ādeḥ grahaṇe ayam kramaḥ mataḥ prāmāṇyam eva na anyatra gṛhīta grahaṇāt matam anumānāt parokṣasya anityādeḥ dharmasya grahaṇe vastu sāmānyam anitya tvena gṛhyate iti ayam kramaḥ mataḥ varṇṇa sāmānyañca pratyakṣataḥ siddham tad bala bhāvinā vikalpena vijātīya vyāvṛtti āśrayeṇa vyavasthāpanāt yaḥ tu vinaśvaram varṇṇam dṛṣṭvā anityaḥ ayam iti viśeṣa viṣayaḥ anumānāt anyatra tatra prāmāṇyam eva na matam gṛhīta grahaṇāt 
[147,x_148,iv]	katham gṛhīta grāhi tvam iti āha na anyāsya anitya tā bhāvāt pūrva siddhaḥ sa ca aindriyāt na aneka rūpaḥ vācyaḥ asau na anyā bhāvāt varṇṇa ādeḥ anitya tā tasya eva kṣaṇa kṣayi svabhāva tvāt sa ca bhāvaḥ aindriyāt pratyakṣat siddhaḥ pūrva vikalpāt tatas tam eva yathāgṛhītam vikalpayan vikalpaḥ gṛhīta grāhī yatas eva na anya abhāvāt anitya tā atas eva abhāvaḥ asau dharmi dharma rūpa tayā na aneka rūpaḥ tathā na vācyaḥ asau śabdānām dharmi dharma abhāvasya taiḥ vacanāt tasya ca vastuni asambhavāt kaḥ tarhi vācyaḥ iti āha vācyaḥ dharmaḥ vikalpa jaḥ vikalpa jaḥ vijātīya āśrayeṇa vikalpa kalpitaḥ dharmaḥ parasparam yathā saṃketam asaṃkīrṇṇaḥ śabdānām vācyaḥ 
[148,v_148,vi]	sāmānya āśraya saṃsiddhau sāmānyam siddham eva tat tad asiddhau tathā asya eva hi anumānam pravartate tasmāt sāmānyasya anitya ādeḥ āśrayasya varṇṇa ādeḥ pratyakṣāt saṃsiddhau siddham eva tad sāmānyam yadi tu abhyāsa ādi abhāvāt anurūpa niścaya abhāvāt ajñānam tadā pratyakṣāt tat asiddhau asya eva hi varṇṇa ādeḥ tathā nitya tvena tat avyabhicāri liṅgadanu mānam pravartate 
[148,vii_148,ix]	kasmāt punar gṛhītepya parijñānam iti āha kvacid tad aparijñānam sadṛśa apara sambhavāt bhrānteḥ apaśyataḥ bhedam māyā golaka bheda vat kvacid anitya tā ādau gṛhītā ipi anurūpa niścaya abhāvāt aparijñānam pūrvakṣaṇa vināśa kāle tad sadṛśasya aparasya sambhavāt bhāva śūnya antarā lakṣaṇa abhāvāt saḥ eva ayam iti bhrānteḥ sthairya grāhiṇyāḥ kṣaṇānām bhedam apaśyataḥ aniścicanvataḥ puṃsaḥ dṛṣṭāntam āha māyā golaka bheda vat māyākāra darśitau golakau bhinnau adhyakṣeṇa gṛhītvā api sādṛśyāt lāghavāt ca vipralabdha buddhiḥ eka tvena adhyavasyati yathā tathā sthira adhyavasāyaḥ 
[148,x_149,i]	nanu yadi kvacid nāśaḥ dṛśyeta tadā asya ahetukasya svabhāva tvāt kṣaṇa kṣayiṣu bhāveṣu ekatā buddheḥ bhrānta tvam bhavet iti āha tathā hi aliṅgam ābālam asaṃśliṣṭa uttara udayam paśyan paricchinatti eva dīpa ādim nāśinam janaḥ tathā hi dīpa ādi ādi śabdāt turaṅga disantāna viccheda kāle asaṃśliṣṭa uttara udayam aghaṭitaḥ uttarasya udayaḥ janma yasmin tam ekasya svarasa nirodhi tve aparasya kāraṇa abhāvāt anutpattau nāśinam adhyakṣataḥ paśyan aliṅgaṅgama kaliṅga rahitam ābālam bāla paryantam janaḥ paricchinatti eva tatas prāk api sataḥ svarasa nirodhāt sadṛśa apara aparakṣaṇa pracaye saḥ eva ayam iti buddhi bhrāntiḥ eva 
[149,ii_149,iv]	yathā bhāva svabhāva bhūtāyām api śaktau phale adṛśaḥ anānantaryatas mohaḥ viniścetuḥ apāṭavāt bhāvasya bīja ādeḥ svabhāva bhūtāyām api aṅkura ādi janikāyām śaktau phale aṅkura ādau anānantarī ataḥ adṛśaḥ adarśanāt viniścetuḥ punsaḥ apāṭavāt mohaḥ aśakta bhramaḥ tathā kṣaṇikeṣu bhāveṣu sadṛśa apara apara utpatteḥ bhāva śūni akṣaṇā darśanāt ca sthira bhramaḥ 
[149,v_149,vi]	tasya eva vinivṛti artham anumāna upavarṇanam vyavasyanti īkṣaṇāt eva sarva ākārān mahā dhiyaḥ tasya ekatva bhramasya eva nivṛtti artha samvādi liṅga jasya kṣaṇika tā viṣayasya anumānasya upavarṇṇanam niścaya āropa manasā urbbādhya bādhaka bhāvataḥ iti nyāyāt ye tumahā ādhiyaḥ viparīta vyavasāya anākrānta pratyakṣāḥ yoginaḥ te padārthasya īkṣaṇāt eva sarvān ākāran vyavasyanti niścinvanti 
[149,vii_149,ix]	evañca vyāvṛtte sarvatas tasmin vyāvṛtti vinibandhanāḥ buddhayaḥ arthe pravarttante abhinne bhinna āśrayāḥ iva tasmin arthe vastutas abhinne niraṃśe sarvatas sajātīyāt vijātīyāt ca vyāvṛtte yāvattyaḥ vyāvṛttayaḥ santi tāvat vyāvṛtti vinibandhanāḥ niścaya ātmikāḥ buddhayaḥ bhinna āśrayāḥ iva tad tad vyāvṛtti mātra viṣaya tvena bhinna dharmi dharmma ādi gocarāḥ iva pravartante 
[149,x_149,xi]	yathā codanam ākhyāḥ ca saḥ asati bhrānti kāraṇe pratibhāḥ pratisandhatte sva anurūpāḥ svabhāvataḥ yathā codanam yathā saṃketam ākhyāḥ śabdāḥ ca pravartante yatra vyāvṛttau yaḥ śabdaḥ viniveśitaḥ sa ca tasyām niścitāyām pravartate sa bhāvaḥ asati bhrānti kāraṇe yathā abhyāsam sva anurūpāḥ sva vyāvṛtti samucitāḥ pratibhā niścaya buddhīḥ svabhāvataḥ pratisaṃdhatte utpādayati tasmāt abhyāsavatām īkṣaṇā devān ityādi niścayaḥ anyeṣāntu sthira āropaṇa artham anumānam iti sthitam etat 
[150,i_150,vi]	anye tu ācāryāḥ prāhuḥ siddhaḥ atra api athavā dhvaṃsaḥ liṅgāt anupalambhanāt atra varṇṇa santāna viccheda kālepi santāna viccheda lakṣaṇaḥ dhvaṃsaḥ anitya tā na bhāva svabhāva ātmikā sa ca anupalambhanāt liṅgat siddhaḥ na adhyakṣāt bhāva viṣaya tvāt tasya kasmāt punar dhvaṃsaḥ anitya tā iti āha prāk bhūtvā hi abhavat bhāvaḥ nityaḥ iti abhidhīyate prāk bhūtvā hi bhāvaḥ paścāt abhavan anityaḥ iti abhidhīyate na tu bhāvaḥ iti eva tathā dhvaṃsaḥ eva anitya tā sā ca anupalabdhi liṅga jā anumāna gamyā 
[150,vii_150,ix]	nanu prāk paścāt abhāvayoḥ vyavadhāyakaḥ sattā sambandhaḥ anitya tā na pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ iti āha yasya ubhayānta vyavadhi sattā sambandha vācinī anitya tā śrutiḥ tena tāvantau iti kau smṛtau yasya naiyāyika ādeḥ ubhayasya prāk paścāt abhāvasya antarasya yaḥ vyavadhāyakaḥ sattā sambandhaḥ tad vācinī anityatā śrutiḥ iṣṭā tena vādinā tāvantau iti kausmṛtau 
[150,x_150,xi]	prāk paścāt api abhāvaḥ ced saḥ eva anitya tā na kim ṣaṣṭhī ādyayogāt iti ced antayoḥ sa katham bhavet prāgbhāvaḥ paścāt abhāvopi ced saḥ eva prāc abhāvaḥ paścāt abhāvaḥ anitya tā kinneṣyate sattā viśeṣaṇa tvena api tad abhyupagamasya iṣṭa tvāt paṭasya ghaṭe ca abhāvaḥ iti ṣaṣṭi ādi vibhakti ayogāt pradhvaṃsa abhāvaḥ na anitya tā na hi bhāva abhāvayoḥ saṃyoga ādiḥ kaścid sambandha usti yaḥ ucyeta ṣaṣṭi ādibhiḥ iti ced evantarhi antayoḥ sa ṣaṣṭi ādi yogaḥ katham bhavet abhāvayoḥ vyavadhi bhūtā sattā ityādi 
[151,i_151,v]	kiñca sattā sambandhayoḥ dhrauvyāt antābhyām na viśeṣaṇam sattā tad sambandhe para mate dhrauvyādantābhyām prāc pradhvaṃsa abhāvābhyām na viśeṣaṇam syāt anta dvaya viśiṣṭā sattā tad sambandhaḥ vā iti na hi niṃtyasya sarva kāla vyāpinaḥ anta sambhavaḥ aviśeṣaṇam eva syāt antau ced kārya kāraṇe kārya kāraṇe antau abhimate iti ced tadā tābhyām sattā sambandhayoḥ aviśeṣaṇam eva syāt 
[151,vi_151,vii]	asambandhāt na bhāvasya prāgabhāvam sa vā aṃchati tad upādhi samākhyāne tepyasya ca na sidhyataḥ yasmāt sa naiyāyika ādiḥ bhāvasya asambandhāt prāgabhāvam sambandhinam na vāñchati tathā ca tad upādhi samākhyāne prāc abhāva viśeṣaṇam kārya kāraṇam iti samākhyānam vyapadeśaḥ yayoḥ te tathā te kārya kāraṇepyasya na sidhyataḥ yasya hi prāc abhāvaḥ sa bhavan kāryam syāt na ca tad sambandhaḥ bhāvasya iti kārya abhāvaḥ kārya abhāvāt ca kāraṇa abhāvaḥ tad utpādakasya kāraṇa tvāt 
[151,viii_151,x]	kiñca sattā sva kāraṇa śleṣa karaṇāt kāraṇam kila sā sattā sa ca sambandhaḥ nityau kāryam atha iha kim janma sattā āśleṣaḥ sattā samavāyaḥ sva kāraṇena samavāyinā saha nityaḥ tayoḥ karaṇāt kila tvayā iṣṭam kāraṇam sā ca sattā sa ca sambandhaḥ nityau dvau api kāryam atha iha dvayoḥ madhye kim yuktam 
[151,xi_152,ii]	api ca yasya abhāvaḥ kriyeta asau na bhāvaḥ prāgabhāvavān sambandha anabhyupagamāt nityam viśvam idam tatas yasya abhāvasya utpatteḥ prāc abhāvaḥ kāraṇaiḥ asau kriyate na ca kaścid bhāvaḥ prāgbhāvavān sambandhavān anabhyupagamāt tatas kārya abhāvāt nityam viśvam idam prāptam 
[152,iii_152,v]	kathantarhi abhāvena sambandhaḥ na kathañcid kintu buddhi parikalpitaḥ eva asau iti āha tasmāt anarthā skandinyaḥ abhinna artha abhimateṣu api śabdeṣu vācya bhedinyaḥ vyatireka āspadam dhiyaḥ yasmāt vāstava sambandha abhyupagame doṣaḥ tasmāt bhāvasya prāc abhāvaḥ iti abhinna artha tvena abhimateṣu api śabdāt bhinna artha abhimateṣu ca bījasya aṅkuraḥ ityādiṣu śabdeṣu dhiyaḥ anartha askandinyaḥ kalpita sambandha viṣayāḥ vācya bhedinyaḥ saṃketa anurodhāt upakalpita sambandhi sambandha lakṣaṇa vācya bhedavatyaḥ vyatirekasya sambandhi sambandhasya āspadam nimittaṃbhavanti alam vāstava sambandha anubandhena doṣa āśrayeṇa 
[152,vi_152,xi]	tat evam meya bahu tvāt bahu tā api ca iti atra sa anuṣaṅgam prativihitam anekasya vṛtteḥ ekatra vā yathā viśeṣa dṛṣṭena iti atra āha viśeṣa pratyabhijñānam na pratikṣaṇa bhedataḥ agnim dṛṣṭvā krameṇa dhūmāt liṅgāt tasya eva viśeṣasya saḥ eva ayam vahniḥ iti yat pratyabhijñānam na tad pramāṇam pratikṣaṇam bhāvasya bhedataḥ eka artha sādhya artha kriyāyāḥ samvāda abhāvāt syāt etat na yathā dṛṣṭaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ gṛhyate kintu tad sāmānyam iti āha na vā viśeṣa viṣayam dṛṣṭa sāmyena tad grahāt na vā viśeṣa viṣayam tad viśeṣa dṛṣṭam anumānam vaktavyam prāk dṛṣṭasya viśeṣasya sāmyena tasya uttarasya grahaṇāt 
[153,i_153,iii]	syāt etat atra yatra dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antikayoḥ bhedaḥ tatra sāmānyatas dṛṣṭam anumānam iha tu nidarśanam tat eva iti sāmānya agrahaṇam yadi nidarśana tvāt siddhasya pramāṇena asya kim punar tat eva dārṣṭa antikam nidarśanam iti sāmānya agrahaṇam yadi ucyate tadā nidarśana tvāt siddhasya niścitasya asya dārṣṭa antikasya pramāṇena kim kartavyam 
[153,iv_153,vii]	vismṛta tvāt adoṣaḥ ced tatas eva anidarśanam dṛṣṭe tad bhāva siddhiḥ ced pramāṇāt na aprasiddhaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ sa ced siddhaḥ kim anumānena gṛhītasya apivismṛta tvāt punar anumāna pratīta avadoṣaḥ ced tatas vismṛta tvāt eva anidarśanam na hi gṛhīta vismṛtasya dṛṣṭānta tā pūrva pratyayena dṛṣṭe artha pramāṇāt viśeṣa dṛṣṭa anumāna ādyaḥ eva prāk dṛṣṭaḥ saḥ eva ayam iti tad bhāvasya pūrvasya siddhiḥ ced iṣyate nanu ayam tad bhāvaḥ kim anya vastuni sādhyate uta tatra eva anya vastuni tattva ārope viparyāsaḥ tad siddha repramāṇa tā pratyakṣa itarayoḥ aikyāt eka siddhiḥ dvayoḥ api 
[153,viii]	tatra anya vastuni vartamāne tattvasya atīta vastu ātmakasya ārope svīkriyamāṇe viparyāsaḥ ayathārtha tvam syāt na hi anyasya ani ātma tvam asti tad aśakya prāpaṇam upadarśayat apramāṇam syāt atha tatra eva tad bhāva siddhiḥ iti dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā tad siddheḥ eka siddheḥ viśeṣa dṛṣṭasya anumānasya apramāṇa tā gṛhīta grāhi tvāt na hi ekasya nirbhāgasya kiñcid agṛhītam nāma tathā hi pratyakṣa itarayoḥ adhyakṣa anumāna viṣaya yauḥ aikyāt dvayoḥ api pratyakṣe anumāne ca ekasya arthasya siddhiḥ 
[153,ix_153,xi]	tatas ca dṛṣṭānta grāhiṇā eva abhraṣṭa smṛti saṃskāreṇa pratyakṣeṇa siddha tvāt viphalam anumānam pratyakṣa saṃskāra bhraṃśe tu na adṛṣṭāntam anumānam asti tasmāt sandhīyamānam ca anyena vyavasāyam smṛtim viduḥ tad liṅga apekṣaṇāt no ced smṛtiḥ na vyabhicārataḥ anyena atīta darśanena eka viṣaya tayā sandhīya mānam ghaṭyamānam param vyavasāyaṃsmṛtim viduḥ vidvāṃsaḥ gṛhīta artha vikalpena smṛti tvam tat ceha avikalam tasya pratipattavyasya cihnam avyabhicāri liṅgam ntad apekṣaṇāt nocet viśeṣa dṛṣṭam anumānam smṛtiḥ sā tu liṅga nirapekṣyā na etat yuktaṃvyabhicāra taḥ tathā hi yadi liṅgantri rūpanta dā vyāpti grahaṇa viṣaya tvena eva tad siddheḥ vyartham anumānam atha na trirūpanta dāḥ nāvya bhicāra niścayaḥ tasmāt viśeṣa dṛṣṭasya apramāṇa tvāt ekatra aneka vṛtteḥ api tri eka saṃkhyā apohana abhāvaḥ nirastaḥ tasmāt sthitam etat mānam dvividham meya dvaividhyāt iti 
[154,i_154,iii]	idānīm avasara prāptām pratyakṣasya lakṣaṇa vipratipattim nirākarttum āha pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham pratyakṣeṇa eva sidhyati pratyātma vedyaḥ sarveṣām vikalpaḥ nāma saṃśrayaḥ yat tat pratyakṣam iti prasiddhaṃtat kalpanāyāḥ apoḍham draṣṭavyam kalpanā artha rahitam iti arthaḥ tat ca etat īdṛśam pratyakṣeṇa eva sva samvedanena eva sidhyati kalpanā rahitasya arthasya rūpasya samvedanasya aparokṣa tvāt yadi tu kalpanā svabhāva tvam asya syāt tathā eva prakāśeta vikalpasya aparokṣa tvāt tathā hi pratyātma vedyaḥ sarveṣām prāṇinām vikalpaḥ nāma saṃśrayaḥ śabda saṃsargavān sa yadi syāt upalabhya eva bhavet 
[154,iv_154,vi]	tasmāt saṃhṛtya sarvatas cintām stimitena antarātmanā sthitopi cakṣuṣā rūpam īkṣate sākṣa jā matiḥ saṃhṛtya ākṛṣya sarvatas vikalpanīyāt cintām stimitena sarva avikalpa vigamāt adhikṣiptena antarātmanā cetasā sthitaḥ api puruṣaḥ cakṣuḥ vijñānena rūpam īkṣate sākṣa jā nirvikalpā matiḥ sarva samviditā eva 
[155,i_155,iii]	santi eva indriya dhiyaḥ kalpanāḥ tāḥ tu na upalabhyante iti api asat tathā hi punar vikalpayan kiñcid āsīt me kalpanā īdṛśī vetti ca iti na pūrva ukta avasthāyām indriyāt gatau vikalpa avasthāyāḥ ūrdhvam punar vikalpayan pumān āsīt me kalpanedṛśī iti vā iti na indriyāt utpannāyām gatau buddhau saṃhṛtya ityādinā pūrva m ukta avasthāḥ yasyāḥ tasyāḥ kalpanām vā iti yadi sā tatra syāt atad saṃskārasya smṛtiḥ jāyate tasmāt na asti iti niścīyate 
[155,iv_155,vi]	kiñca vācya vācaka ākāra saṃsargavatī pratītiḥ kalpanā na ca indriya viṣaye ananvayāt saṃketā asambhavāt ca śabda yojana asti tathā hi ekatra dṛṣṭaḥ bhedaḥ hi kvacid na anyatra dṛśyate na tasmāt bhinnam asti anyat sāmānyam buddhaya bhedataḥ ekatra deśa ādau na dṛśyate na ca ananuyāyini śabda saṃketaḥ sāmānyam anuyāyi iti ced tasmāt bhedāt anyat bhinnam sāmānyam na asti buddheḥ abhedataḥ 
[155,vii_155,ix]	yadi hi sāmānyam sāmānyam syāt dvi ākārā buddhiḥ bhavet viśeṣa mātra ākāra eva tu pratyakṣa buddhiḥ upalabhyate tasmāt viśeṣa viṣayā sarvā eva indriya jā matiḥ na viśeṣeṣu śabdānām pravṛttau asti sambhavaḥ tasmāt sarvā eva indriya jāḥ matiḥ viśeṣa mātra viṣayā anyasya anupalabdheḥ na ca viśeṣeṣu śabdānām pravṛttau saṃbhava usti
[155,x_155,xi]	ananvayāt viśeṣāṇām saṅketasya apravṛttitaḥ viṣayaḥ yaḥ ca śabdānām saṃyojyeta saḥ eva taiḥ viśeṣāṇām ananvayāt tatra saṃketasya apravṛttitaḥ uttarakālam śabda artha pratipatti artham saṃketa kriyā na ca viśeṣāḥ kāla antaram anuvartante tasmāt yaḥ eva śabdānām viṣayaḥ vyavacchedaḥ saḥ eva taiḥ saṃyojyeta na sva lakṣaṇam 
[155,xii_155,xiii]	asya idam iti sambandhe yau arthau pratibhāsinau tayoḥ eva hi sambandhaḥ na tadā indriya gocaraḥ tasmāt asya arthasya idam vācakam iti sambandhe vācya vācaka bhāva lakṣaṇe yau arthau pratibhāsinau tayoḥ eva hi sambandhaḥ vaktavyaḥ yadā ca arthan dṛṣṭvā saketam tatra pravartayati tadā indriya gocaraḥ arthaḥ na asti 
[156,i_156,ii]	viśada pratibhāsasya tadā arthasya avibhāvanāt vijñāna ābhāsa bhedaḥ ca padārthānām viśeṣakaḥ saṃhṛta indriya vyāpārasya tadā saṃketa saṃkalpa kāle viśada pratibhāsasya arthasya avibhāvanāt yadi tatra arthaḥ pratibhāti tadā indriya jñāna vat sphuṭaḥ pratīyate na ca pratibhāsa bhedepi śabda indriya jñānayoḥ eka viṣaya tvam yasmāt vijñānasya ābhāsa bhedaḥ ākāra bhedaḥ padārthānām grāhyāṇām viśeṣakaḥ bhedakaḥ yadi tu pratibhāsa bheda īpi artha abhedaḥ tadā viśvam ekam dravyam syāt 
[156,iii_156,v]	syāt etat yadā sva lakṣaṇam upadarśya śabdaḥ niveśyate tadā sva lakṣaṇam eva vācya vācakam iti āha cakṣuṣā artha avabhāse api yam paraḥ asya iti śaṃsati saḥ eva yojyate śabdaiḥ na khalu indriya gocaraḥ cakṣuṣā artha vabhāsepi jāte tathā śrotra acśābda avabhāsepi yam artham anya vyavacchedam buddhi parivarttinam paraḥ pratipādakaḥ asya arthasya ayam vācakaḥ iti śaṃsati kathayati saḥ eva anya vyavacchedaḥ śabdaiḥ yojyate na khalu indriya gocaraḥ sva lakṣaṇam ananvayāt tasya tad darśana antaram saṃketa saṃkalpe ca vināśāt ca 
[156,vi_156,x]	avyāpṛta indriyasya anyavāṅga mātreṇa avibhāvanāt tathā avyāpṛta indriyasya anya vāc mātreṇa sva lakṣaṇa avibhāvanāt pratyakṣaḥ iva syāt etat saṃketa aviṣaya tvepi śabda saṃsṛṣṭam eva sva lakṣaṇam adhyakṣam prakṛtyā pratyeṣyati iti āha na ca anudita saṃbandhaḥ svayam jñāna prasaṅgataḥ na ca anudita sambandhaḥ vācya vācaka bhāvaḥ yasya sa śabdaḥ pratyāyakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti śeṣaḥ tathā abhyupagame tu svayam saṃketam anapekṣya eva śrutāt śabdāt arthasya jñāna prasaṅgataḥ 
[156,xi_156,xii]	nanu indriya vyāpāra sama kālam ahirahiḥ iti dhārāvāhi sa vikalpakam adhyakṣam pravartate yadi tu tatra vikalpakam avikalpa kañca dvayam iṣyate tadā vikalpena nirvikalpasya vyavadhānāt darśanam vicchinnam syāt na ca etat asti na yugapad jñāna sambhavaḥ atra āha manasaḥ yugapad vṛtteḥ sa vikalpa avikalpayoḥ vimūḍhaḥ laghu vṛtteḥ vā tayoḥ aikyam vyavasyati 
[157,i]	manasoḥ sa vikalpa avikalpayoḥ ekasmāt samanantarāt yugapad vṛtteḥ kāraṇāt tayoḥ aikyam vimūḍhaḥ pratipattā vyavasyati nirvikalpakam hi sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam vikalpaḥ ca vastutas atat viṣaya tvepi avasāya anurodhāt tad viṣayaḥ saha utpattiḥ ca anubhava siddha tvāt durapahnavā tatas saha utpannayoḥ eka viṣayayoḥ aikya bhramaḥ eṣaḥ para abhimatāyām yugapad anutpattau api sa vikalpa avikalpayoḥ laghu vṛtteḥ śīghra vṛtteḥ vā kāraṇāt tayoḥ mūḍha matiḥ pratipattā aikyam vyavasyati alāta bhrāntau cakram iva 
[157,ii_157,iv]	yadi darśanam avikalpam tat anantarantu vikalpaḥ punar tad anantaram darśanam tadā vikalpa vyavadhānena vicchinnam darśanam bhavet iti ced bhinna jātīya vikalpenyasya vā katham vikalpena vyavadhānāt vicchinnam darśanam bhavet na dhārāvāhi iti ced nanu asya parasya api gām paśyataḥ nirvikalpena pratyakṣeṇa bhinna jātīyasya aśvādeḥ vikalpe jāyamāne darśanam katham avicchinnam na hi aśva vācaka śabdena saṃyojya gauḥ gṛhyate yena ekam eva sa vikalpam tat adhyakṣam bhavet eka tve vā aśu apratītiḥ na syāt go viṣaya tvāt tasya 
[157,v_157,vii]	syāt etat alāta dṛṣṭi vat bhāva pakṣaḥ ced balavān mataḥ anyatra api samānam tat varṇayoḥ vā sakṛt śṛ tiḥ alātasya bhramyamānasya nānā deśeṣu lāghavāt bhāva pakṣa balava tvāt ca darśana pratisandhānena cakra dṛṣṭi vat vijātīya vyavakīryamāṇasya darśanasya antarā abhāvepi bhāva pakṣaḥ balavān mataḥ iti darśana āviccheda buddhiḥ ati ced anyatra abhāva pakṣepi tad balavat tve lāghava sāmarthyāt samānam tatas darśana viccheda lāghavāt viccheda dhīrā iva astu saraḥ rasaḥ ityādau varṇṇayoḥ vā lāghavāt sakṛt śrutiḥ prāptā 
[157,viii_158,i]	kiñca sakṛt saṅgata śabda artheṣu indriyeṣu iha satsu api pañcabhiḥ vyavadhānepi bhāti avyavahitā iva yā sakṛt yugapad saṃgatāḥ sva sva gocarībhūtāḥ sarve arthāḥ yeṣu teṣu indriyeṣu cakṣuḥ ādiṣu manaḥ paryanteṣu satsu api iha saṅkrānta kāntā vadana pratibimbasya sahakāra sugandhinaḥ śītasya bhramat bhramara upagītasya svādrunaḥ madhunaḥ sārvaguṇa anubhava kāle prasarat saṃkalpa janmanām yūnām yā matiḥ pañcabhiḥ indriya buddhibhiḥ vyavadhānepi tvad pakṣe avyavahitā iva sama kālā iva bhāti 
[158,ii_158,iii]	sā matiḥ nāma paryanta kṣaṇika jñāna miśraṇāt vicchinna abha iti tat citram tasmāt santu sakṛt dhiyaḥ sa indriya matiḥ nāmnaḥ śabdasya paryantaḥ varṇṇaḥ tasya kṣaṇikam jñānam tena miśraṇāt saraḥ rasaḥ iti ādiṣu avicchinnā prāpnoti vijātīya vijñāna antara avyavadhānāt tathā api vicchinna ābhā kramavatī yat tu citram āścaryam yadi lāghava kṛtaḥ sakṛt graha abhimānaḥ tadā varṇṇa jñāne sa nitarām yuktaḥ vijātīya avyavadhānāt indriya jñāneṣu tu na yuktaḥ pañcabhiḥ vyavadhānāt tasmāt sakṛt hiyaḥ santu yathoktam manasaḥ yugapad vṛtteri ti 
[158,iv_158,vi]	anyathā pratibhāsā viśeṣaḥ ca sāntara anantare katham śuddhe manaḥ vikalpe ca na krama grahaṇam bhavet sa antare pañcabhiḥ indriya jñānaiḥ vyavahita tvāt anantare saraḥ rasaḥ iti ādike jñāne vijātīya avyavadhānāt pratibhāsasya aviśeṣaḥ ca aprasaktaḥ sa ca anubhava bādhita tvāt katham abhyupagamaḥ iti śeṣaḥ yadi laghu vṛtti tvāt sakṛt grahaḥ tadā śuddhe vijātīya avyavakīrṇṇe manaḥ vikalpe ca prābandhike krama grahaṇam anubhava siddham na bhavet 
[158,vii_158,x]	yaḥ agrahaḥ saṅgatepi arthe kvacid āsakta cetasaḥ nanu yadi yugapad jñāna utpattiḥ tad aikatra āsaktam punar utpatti dharmakam cetaḥ yasya tasya āsakta cetasaḥ kvacid arthe sva indriyeṇa saṅgatepi yaḥ agrahaḥ vijñāna anutpattiḥ sa katham āha saktyā na utpatti vaiguṇyāt ca udyam vai tad dvayoḥ api 
[159,i]	ekatra saktyā viṣaya āsañcāra lakṣaṇayā anyasya bhinna viṣayasya jñānasya utpatti vaiguṇyāt aviguṇaḥ hi samanantara pratyayaḥ sva kāryam ārabhate na tu āsakti viguṇaḥ yat ca etat ca udyam parihṛtam asmābhiḥ tat dvayoḥ api samānam yugapad vijñāna anutpatti vādinā upi mate sarvatra iva aindriya saṃgame samāne kvacid eva jñānam kvacid na iti kutas 
[159,ii_159,iv]	tatra āsakti vaiguṇyam eva manasaḥ uttaram tat ca samānam asmākam alāta dṛṣṭi vat iti dṛṣṭāntasya asiddhim āha śīghra vṛtteḥ alāta ādeḥ anvaya pratidhātinī cakra bhrāntim dṛś ādhatte na dṛśām ghaṭanena sā śīghrā pravṛttiḥ bhramaṇam yasya alāta ādeḥ tasya anvayena anugamena pratighātaḥ upahata tvam tadvatī dṛś dṛṣṭiḥ cakra ākārām bhrāntim indriya jām dhatte na dṛśām bhinna bhinna deśa alāta darśanānām ghaṭanena yojanayā sā mānasī bhrāntiḥ sphuṭa pratibhāsa tvāt mānasasya na viparyayāt tasmāt ahirahiḥ iti vikalpa sama kālam adhyakṣam vastu sphuṭam avaiti na tu vikalpaḥ iti sthitam
