[159,v_159,vi]	kecid indriya ja tvādeḥ bāla dhī vat akalpanām āhuḥ bāla avikalpe ca hetum saṅketa manda tām kecid ācāryīyāḥ śaṅkarasvāmi prabhṛtayaḥ indriya ja tvāt ādi śabda ādamāna satva anubhava ākāra pravṛt tattva ādeḥ hetoḥ pratyakṣa buddhim akalpanām bāladhīvadāhuḥ dṛṣṭānta siddhayartham bālasya avikalpe vikalpa abhāve ca saṃketam aṃdatām hetum āhuḥ vācya vācaka yojanāḥ hi vikalpaḥ sā ca saṃketa pūrvikā tad abhāvāt bālasya kalpanā bhāvaḥ 
[159,vii_159,viii]	teṣām pratyakṣam eva syāt bālānām avikalpanāt saṅketa upāya vigamāt paścāt api bhavet na saḥ teṣām evam vādinām mate bālānām pratyakṣam eva jñānam syāt na vicārakam kim kāraṇam avikalpanāt bhavatu kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced āha saṃketa upāyasya vicārasya vigamāt bālānām paścāt api sa saṅketaḥ na bhavet tad abhāvāt vikalpa abhāvaḥ ca 
[159,ix_160,i]	manaḥ vyutpanna saṅketam asti tena sa ced mataḥ evam indriya jepi syāt śeṣavat ca idam īdṛśam janma antara āgatam vyutpannam saṃketam manosti bālānām tena saṃketaḥ teṣām mataḥ ced evam sati indriya jepi jñāne syāt kalpanā tad nivartaka hetu abhidhānāt tatas dṛṣṭa asiddhiḥ eva idam indriya ja tu ā ādi īdṛśam niṣedhyena saha asiddha virodham śeṣavat ca uktam 
[160,ii_160,iv]	atha anyena liṅgena avyabhicāriṇā bāla jñānam avikalpanam prasādhya dṛṣṭāntīkriyate tadā yat eva sādhanam bāle tat eva atra api kathyatām sāmyāt akṣa dhiyām uktam anena anubhava ādikam yat eva avyabhicāri bāle bālasya indriya jñāne sādhanam tat eva atra vyutpanna saṃketānām indriya jñānepi kathyatām kim indrija tva ādinā upanyastena vyutpanna avyutpannayoḥ akṣadhi yāma śabda saṃsṛṣṭa tva mātra anukaraṇena sāmyāt anena indriya ja tu at ūṣaṇena anubhavaḥ ādiḥ yasya māna sattva ādeḥ tat uktam doṣavat tayā boddhavyam 
[160,v_160,vii]	avikalpa siddhau para matam dūṣayitvā svayam upapatti antaram āha viśeṣaṇam viśeṣyañca sambandham laukikīm sthitim gṛhītvā saṅkalayya etat tathā pratyeti na anyathā viśeṣaṇam vyavacchedakam viśeṣyam vyavacchedyam tayoḥ sambandham yathāsambhavam samavāya ādikam laukikīm loka prasiddhām sthitim vyavasthāñca jāti ādikam viśeṣaṇam viśeṣyam dravya ādi viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya śabdayoḥ ca pūrva apara niyamaḥ iti pṛthak pratyekam svarūpeṇa gṛhītvā tad anantaram etat sarve saṅkalayya saṃyojya tathā viśeṣaṇa viśiṣṭa tvena pratyeti viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ na anyathā viśeṣaṇa ādi agrahaṇe 
[161,i_161,ii]	yathā daṇḍini jāti ādeḥ vivekena anirūpaṇāt tadvatā yojanā na asti kalpanā api atra na asti atas yathā daṇḍini daṇḍī iti viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ daṇḍa puruṣa tad sambandha ādi grahaṇa pūrvikā tad agrahe ca na bhavati jātiḥ ādiḥ yasya guṇa karma ādeḥ svarūpasya jāti ādimataḥ vivekena anirūpaṇāt tadvatā jātimatā yojanāḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ na asti atas yojanā virahāt atra jāti mat ādau kalpanā api na asti iti tasmāt jāti ādi yojana ātmikā kalpanā na asti śabda yojana ātmikā tu sambhāvyeta sā api sva lakṣaṇe saṃketa abhāvāt nirastā prāk 
[161,iii_161,viii]	nanu yadi sāmānya abhāvaḥ tadā vibhinnāsu vyaktiṣu katham anvayi pratyayaḥ iti āha yat api anvayi vijñānam śabda vyakti avabhāsi tat yat api anvayi vijñānam utpadyate tat ca śabdasya gauḥ iti ādeḥ vyakteḥ ca varṇṇa saṃsthāna viśeṣasya ābhāsaḥ ākāraḥ tadvat pratīyate na jātyābhāsa vat kim punar sāmānya ābhāsam eva na iti āha varṇṇa ākṛti akṣara ākāra śūnyam go tvam hi varṇṇyate varṇṇaḥ nīla ādiḥ ākṛtiḥ saṃsthānam akṣaram gavā ādi śabdaḥ teṣām ākāraḥ yathā pratītaḥ tena śūnyam go tvam hi sāmānya vādibhiḥ varṇyate
[161,ix_161,xi]	atas anvayi vijñāne yat varṇṇa saṃsthāna ādi pratibhāsate na tad sāmānyam samāna tvepi tasya eva na īkṣaṇam netra gocare pratibhāsa dvaya abhāvāt buddhe rbhedaḥ ca durlabhaḥ tasya eva samāna tve vā svīkriyamāṇe netra gocare arthe na aṅgīkartavyam īkṣaṇam vikalpa pratibhāsinaḥ pratibhāsa dvayasya sphuṭa asphuṭa varṇṇa saṃsthānavataḥ abhāvāt eka ākāram eva jñānam yadi ubhaya ābhāsam aṅgīkriyate tadā buddheḥ bhedaḥ pratyakṣatva apratyakṣa tva ādinā durlabhaḥ yat api spaṣṭa pratibhāsam adhyakṣam tat api anakṣa jam syāt aspaṣṭa pratibhāsa tvāt evam anakṣajam adhyakṣam syāt spaṣṭa pratibhāsa tvāt tasmāt adṛṣṭena sāmānya ādinā na yojayati iti akalpanam adhyakṣam 
[162,i_162,vi]	kiñca samavāya āgrahā dakṣaiḥ sambandha adarśanam sthitam samavāyasya atīndriyasya agrahāt akṣaiḥ akṣa bhavaiḥ vijñānaiḥ jāti tadvatoḥ sambandhasya aviśiṣṭa pratītyā adarśanam sthitam niścitam yat balena yat pratītiḥ tad agrahe na yuktā sā yadi na asti samavāyaḥ tadā iha tantuṣu paṭaḥ ityādayaḥ buddhayaḥ na syuḥ iti āha paṭaḥ tantuḥ u iha iti ādi śabdāḥ ca ime svayam kṛtāḥ iha tantuṣu paṭaḥ ityādi śabdāḥ ime svayam samaya anulocanaiḥ kṛtāḥ na vastu para adhīnāḥ 
[162,vii_162,xii]	tathā hi śṛṅgam gavīti loke syāt śṛṅge gauriti alaukikam śṛṅgam gavi tiṣṭati iti loke syāt pramāṇa prasiddhyoḥ anurodhāt śṛṅge gauḥ iti tu tad upakalpitam alaukikam pramāṇa prasiddhi bahirbhāvāt yadi avayavebhyaḥ na gauḥ bhinnaḥ tadā gavi śṛṅgam iti api na syāt iti āha gavā ākhya pariśiṣṭa aṅga viccheda anupalambhanāt śṛṅgasya gavā ākhyaiḥ pariśiṣṭa aṅgaiḥ vicchedesya viyogasya anupalambhanāt śṛṅgam gavīti ucyate na tu avayava atirikta go sadbhāvāt 
[162,xiii_162,xv]	nanu tantuṣu paṭaḥ iti bhavati eva pratītiḥ iti ced āha taiḥ tantubhiḥ iyam śāṭī iti uttaram kāryam ucyate tantu saṃskāra sambhūtam na eka kālam kathañcana taiḥ tantubhiḥ paṭa avasthā prāc bhāvibhiḥ iyam śāṭī iti kāraṇa bhūta tantu uttara kāla bhāvi tantūnām saṃskāraḥ turī vema kuvinda kara ādi sahakārī prabhava avasthā viśeṣa lābhaḥ tasmāt svarasena nirudhyamānāt saṃbhūtaṃkāryam ucyate na tu tantubhiḥ saha eka kālam kāryam tantu paṭaḥ iti kathañcana kathyate kārya kāraṇayoḥ sama kāla tva abhāvāt 
[163,i_163,iii]	yadi na asti tantu paṭayoḥ bhedaḥ tadā katham ete tantavaḥ paṭaḥ ca ayam iti vyapadeśaḥ iti āha kāraṇa āropataḥ kaścid ekāpa uddhāratopi vā tantu ākhyām varttayet kārye darśayan na āśrayam śruteḥ kāraṇānān tantūnām āropataḥ ekasya tantoḥ apa uddhārataḥ buddhyā niḥkarṣaṇāt vā kaścid vyavaharttā kārye paṭe tantu ākhyām tantu śrutim vartayet paṭa śruteḥ āśrayam kāraṇam darśayet na tantubhyaḥ vyatiriktaḥ paṭosti evam ākāra pariṇatāḥ tantavaḥ paṭaḥ iti arthaḥ 
[163,iv_163,ix]	yadi tantavaḥ kevalāḥ na tebhyaḥ paṭaḥ anyaḥ tadā paṭa vyapadeśaḥ nirnibandhanaḥ syāt iti āha upakārya upakāri tvam vicchedāt dṛṣṭiḥ eva vā tantūnām parasparam śīta ādi apanoda kṣamam sāhityam upakārya upakāri tvam anyonyasya vicchedāt dṛṣṭiḥ eva vā paṭa vyapadeśa nibandhanam iti śeṣaḥ yadi vyatiriktam vyapadeśa nibandhanam na asti tadā paṭaḥ iti vyapadeśaḥ na mukhyaḥ syāt bāhīke go vyapadeśa vat iti āha mukhyam yat askhalat jñānam ādi saṃketa gocaraḥ mukhyantat ucyate yat ādi saṃketasya gocaraḥ na vyatiriktaḥ iti eva paraspara aviccheda avastheṣu ca paṭa śruteḥ saṃketāt askhalat gati gocara tvāt mukhya tvam tasmāt pratyakṣataḥ jāteḥ anupalambhāt yojana āvirahaḥ 
[163,x_164,iv]	syāt etat viśiṣṭa pratītiḥ viśeṣaṇa pratīti pūrvikā yathā daṇḍi pratītiḥ viśiṣṭa pratītiḥ ca śāvaleya ādiṣu gauḥ iti viśeṣaṇañca śāvaleya ādiṣu go tvam eva iti anumānataḥ jāti siddhiḥ iti āha anumānañca jāti ādau vastunaḥ na asti bhedini anumānam vastunaḥ śābaleya ādeḥ bhedini jāti ādau na asti na hi vyakti vyatiriktam viśeṣaṇam upalabhyate śṛṅga ādi ava yava sanniveśaḥ eva tu abhinnaḥ viśeṣaṇam astu tathā ca nābhimata siddhiḥ dṛṣṭānta asiddhim api āha sarvatra vyapadeśaḥ hi daṇḍa ādeḥ api sāṃvṛtāt 
[164,v]	sarvatra puruṣa ādau daṇḍī ityādi vyapadeśa upi hi na daṇḍa ādeḥ vastunaḥ kintu sāṃvṛtāt daṇḍa sva lakṣaṇasya vyupadeśe hetu tve sarvatra puruṣe syāt sambandhini eva anyatra iti ced tarhi sambandhaḥ daṇḍaḥ kāraṇam daṇḍi vyapadeśasya sambandhaḥ ca saṃyoga ādiḥ na asti iti param kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ pariśiṣyate tasya nimitta tve yathā daṇḍī puruṣaḥ tathā puruṣī daṇḍaḥ iti api syāt samāna tvāt nimittasya tasmāt kalpita viśeṣaṇa bhāva niyamaḥ daṇḍaḥ sambandhī sāṃvṛtaḥ eva viśeṣaṇam 
[164,vi_164,viii]	kiñca vastu prāsāda mālā ādi śabdāḥ ca anya anapekṣiṇaḥ gehaḥ yadi api saṃyogaḥ tad mālā kintu tat bhavet ṣaṭsu padārtheṣu vastu vastu iti sarva anuyāyī śabdaḥ prāsādeṣu prāsāda mālā iti śabdaḥ gṛheṣu bahuṣu nagaram ityādi śabdāḥ ca anya an apekṣiṇaḥ artha antara bhūta viśeṣaṇa rahitāḥ iti vyabhicāritā hetoḥ na hi padārtheṣu vyatiriktam sāmānyam vastu tā tvam abhyupagamyate vaiśeṣikaiḥ na ca prāsādaḥ dravyam vijātīyānām dravya anārambhāt tatas ca mālāguṇopi gehaḥ yadi api saṃyogaḥ tasya mālā kintu tat bhavet na bhāva guṇaḥ nirguṇa tvāt guṇānām 
[165,i_165,ii]	jātiḥ ced gehaḥ ekopi mālā iti ucyeta vṛkṣa vat mālā bahutve tad śabdaḥ katham jāteḥ ajātitaḥ jātiḥ ced abhyupagamyate ekaḥ gehaḥ mālā iti ucyeta vṛkṣa vat yathā vṛkṣa tva jāti yogāt ekaḥ vṛkṣaḥ vṛkṣaḥ iti ucyate evam ekopi gehaḥ mālā syāt tathā geha mālānām bahu tve tad śabdaḥ mālā iti anugāmi śabdaḥ katham jāte rmālāyām ajātitas jāti antara virahāt 
[165,iii_165,vi]	kiñca mālā ādau ca mahatva ādiḥ iṣṭaḥ yaḥ ca aupacārikaḥ mukhyā viśiṣṭa vijñāna grāhya tvāt na aupacārikaḥ mahatī prāsāda mālā iti katham vyapadeśaḥ mahatvam parimāṇam guṇaḥ tasya mālāyām na sattvam na hi prāsāda mālā kiñcid iti uktam na api saṃyoga lakṣaṇe prāsāde mahat tvam nirguṇa tvāt guṇānām kāṣṭha ādiṣu dravyeṣu prāsāda ārambhakeṣu mahattva sattvāt vṛkṣeṣu kusuma sambhavāt vana saṃkhyā lakṣaṇam kusumitam iti yathā ucyate tathā prāsāda mālā ādau mahatva ādiḥ aupacārikaḥ yaḥ ca iṣṭaḥ sa ca ayuktaḥ kāṣṭha ādiṣu api tādṛśasya mahat tvasya abhāvāt kiñca mahān parvataḥ iti mukhya mahat tva grāhaka jñānena askhalat vṛtti tvāt aviśiṣṭena jñānena grāhya tvāt prāsāda mālā maha tva ādiḥ aupacārikaḥ na yuktaḥ na hi māṇavakaḥ iva siṃha buddhiḥ mahat tva buddhiḥ ca mālāyām skhalati 
[165,vii_165,ix]	kiñca bhinna viśeṣaṇam mukhyam abhinna viśeṣaṇañcāmukhyam iti yat ucyate tat api ayuktam iti āha ananya hetu tā tulyā sā mukhya abhimateṣu api padārtha śabdaḥ kam hetum anyam ṣaṭkam samīkṣate mukhya abhimateṣu api daṇḍya ādiṣu ananya hetu tā bhinna viśeṣaṇa nimitta rahita tā tulyā gauṇena sarvatra vyapadeśaḥ hi daṇḍa ādeḥ api sāṃvṛtāt iti ukteḥ kiñca anuyāyī padārtha śabdaḥ ṣaṣṭhyā padārtheṣu kam anyam hetum nimittam pravṛttau samīkṣate na hi ṣaṣ padārtha atiriktam kiñcid asti 
[166,i_166,v]	yaḥ yathā rūḍhitaḥ siddhaḥ tad sāmyādyaḥ tathā ucyate tasmāt yaḥ arthaḥ yena prakāreṇa rūḍhitaḥ ādi saṃketa anusāreṇa siddhaḥ sa mukhyaḥ yaḥ ca tasya mukhyasya sāmyāt tathāmukhya vācaka śabdena ucyate sa gauṇaḥ kutas etat iti āha yatra gauṇaḥ ca bhāveṣi api abhāvasya upacārataḥ bhāveṣu api ku putra ādiṣu putra ādiḥ iti abhāva upacārataḥ para mate tu bhāve vṛtta tvāt mukhya tvam bhavet 
[166,vi_166,viii]	syāt etat rūḍhyā eva mukhya tā kintu sā api bhinne viśeṣaṇe sati iti āha na saṃketā anvayinī rūḍhiḥ vaktuḥ icchā anvayī ca saḥ kriyate vyavahāra artha chandaḥ śabda aṃśanā bhavat saṃketa anvayinī yathā saṃketam rūḍhiḥ sa ca saṃketaḥ vaktuḥ saṃketayituḥ icchā anvayī vyavahāra artham kriyate chandasaḥ gāyatrī ādeḥ śabda aṃśasya prakṛti pratyaya ādeḥ nāma vat na hi viśiṣṭa ānupūrvīkeṣu varṇṇeṣu pṛthak bhūtam gāyatrī ādi śūbda nimittam kiñcid asti śabda aṃśeṣu vā api tu saṃketayituḥ icchā anurodhāt eva tathā vyapadeśaḥ 
[166,ix_167,i]	yadi vyaktibhyaḥ na bhinnam sāmānyam tadā katham anugāmī pratyayaḥ iti āha vastu dharma tayā eva arthāḥ tādṛś vijñāna kāraṇam bhedepi yatra tad jñāna an tān tathā pratipadyate vastu dharma tayā prakṛtyā eva kecid arthāḥ parasparam bhedepi tādṛśasya anugāminaḥ atad kāryaṃvyāvṛtti viṣayasya vijñānasya kāraṇam yatra yeṣu artheṣu anugāmi jñānam tān abhedinaḥ arthān tathā ekatvena pratipadyate na tu eka sāmānya balāt tathā jñānam 
[167,ii_167,iv]	syāt etat prativyakti jñānāni api bhinnāni iti katham anugāmi jñānam iti āha jñānāni api tathā bhede abheda pratyavamarśane iti atad kārya viśleṣasya anvayaḥ na eka vastunaḥ jñānāni api para sparataḥ bhede tathā arthavat vastu dharmitayā abheda pratyavamarśane nimittam tatas jñānāni api tad eka parāmarśa gocara tayā anugāmi pratyayaḥ ucyante iti anena prakāreṇa bhediṣu artheṣu atad kāryāt arthasya viśleṣaḥ vyavacchedaḥ tasya anvayaḥ vidyate na tu ekasya vastunaḥ sāmānyasya 
[167,v_167,ix]	vastūnām vidyate tasmāt tad niṣṭhā vastuni śrutiḥ vastūnām viśeṣāṇām anvayaḥ vidyate anupalambha bādhita tvāt tasya tasmāt tad niṣṭhā vyāvṛtti viṣayā vastuni śrutiḥ pravartate nanu atad kārya vyāvṛttiḥ vastunaḥ svabhāva bhūtā tatas vyāvṛtti viṣaya tve vastu viṣaya tā eva śabdasya syāt iti āha bāhya śakti vyavaccheda niṣṭhā abhāvepi tad śrutiḥ bāhyasya vastunaḥ śakteḥ atad kāryāt yaḥ vyavacchedaḥ tatra niṣṭhā viṣayi tvam tasya abhāvepi tad śrutiḥ vyavaccheda vācinī śrutiḥ 
[167,x_167,xi]	vikalpa pratibimbeṣu tad niṣṭheṣu nibadhyate tatonya apoha niṣṭha tvāt uktā anyāpoha kṛt śrutiḥ vikalpānām pratibimbeṣu ākāreṣu tad niṣṭheṣu tad vyāvṛtti vastu tvena vyavasthā viṣaya tayā tad vyavahāra vyavasthitiṣu saṃketa kāle nibadhyate tatas vikalpa pratibimbānām bāhya vyāvṛtta ātma tvena vyavahāra viṣaya tvāt anya apoha niṣṭha tvāt kāraṇāt uktā śrutiḥ anyā apoha kṛt anya vyāvṛtta ākāra vikalpa jananāt anya vyāvṛtteṣu pravartanāt ca śabdaḥ anya apoha kṛt uktaḥ 
[168,i_168,iii]	nanu śābde jñāne grāhyam bāhya tayā eva pratīyate na jñāna ākāratayā iti āha vyatirekī iva yat jñāne bhāti artha pratibimbakam śabdāt tat api na artha ātmā bhrāntiḥ sā vāsanodbhavā śabdāt utpanna jñāne artha pratibimbakam vyatirekī iva bhinnam bāhyam iva yat ābhāti tat api na artha ātmā bahis artha svarūpam kintu bhrāntiḥ sā vāsanā nirmitā yathā taimirika dṛṣṭeṣu keśa ādiṣu bāhya bhramaḥ evam vikalpa ākārepi bāhya vyavahāraḥ avidyā vaśāt iti arthaḥ 
[168,iv_168,vi]	jñāna ākāraḥ tarhi vastu bhūtaḥ vācyaḥ syāt iti āha tasya abhidhāne śrutibhiḥ arthe koṃśaḥ vagamyate tasya āgatau ca saṃketa kriyā vyarthā tad arthikā tasya jñāna ākārasya śrutibhiḥ abhidhāne arthe atad kārya vyāvṛtte śabdena ācodite koṃśaḥ vagamyate na kaścid tad akārya vyāvṛttasya arthasya śabdāt agatau ca satyām saṃketa kriyā vyarthā yasmāt tad arthikā atad kārya vyāvṛtta artha pratīti phalā sa iṣyate 
[168,vii_168,ix]	evantar hi anya apoha īpi saṃkete kṛte pravṛttiḥ artheṣu na syāt tasya artha ātma tva abhāvāt iti āha śabda urtha aṃśaṃkamāha iti tatra anya apohaḥ ucyate ākāraḥ sa ca na artha isti tam vadan artha bhāj katham śabdaḥ artha aṃśaṃkamāha iti praśne tatra anya apohaḥ atad kārya vyāvṛttiḥ sarva viśeṣa saṃbhavinī vācyatayā ucyate atas artha aṃśa ātmani anyā apohe gṛhīta saṃketaḥ śabdāt uccarita artham pratītya tatra pravarttitaḥ iti yuktam yaḥ tatra akṣa ākāraḥ sa ca arthe na asti tam buddhi ākāram vadan śabdaḥ artha bhāj bāhya artha abhidhāyī katham astu 
[169,i_169,iii]	kiñca śabdasya anvayinaḥ kāryam arthena anvayinā sa ca ananvayī dhiyaḥ abhedāt darśana abhyāsa nirmmataḥ śabdasya anvayinaḥ anvayina arthena kāryam vyavahāra kāle pratīti lakṣaṇam prayojanam sa ca buddhi ākāraḥ sva lakṣaṇa darśana abhyāsena vāsanānirmmitaḥ ananvayī dhiyaḥ ananvayinyāḥ abhedāt 
[169,iv_169,vi]	nanu yadi arthaḥ śabdasya na viṣayaḥ tadā tadam śarūpa upyanya apohaḥ katham vācyaḥ iti āha tad rūpāra upagatyāni avyāvṛtta adhigateḥ punar śabda artha arthaḥ saḥ eva iti vacane na virudhyate buddhi ākāre tad rūpasya apartha aṃśa apohasya āropa gatyā eka tva adhyavasāyena anya vyāvṛttasya arthasya adhigateḥ śabda artha aṃśa apohaḥ śabda arthaḥ ucyate na tu sāmānyāt śabdāt artha pratīteḥ yadi punar buddhi ākārasya vyāvṛtta artha tvena pratīteḥ sa buddhi ākāraḥ eva śabda arthaḥ iti upacārāt ucyate buddhi ākāra śabda artha vādinā tadā evam vacane kiñcid api na virudhyate buddhi ākārasya anvayinaḥ śabda artha tva aniṣṭeḥ 
[169,vii_169,viii]	mithyā ava bhāsinaḥ vā ete pratyayāḥ śabda nirmmitāḥ mithyā ava bhāsinaḥ vā śabda nirmitāḥ ete pratyayāḥ tathā hi na tāvat arthaḥ śabda buddheḥ viṣayaḥ tad svarūpa anavabhāsataḥ tatra śabda saṃketa abhāvāt ca na api buddhi ākāraḥ tasya vedanepi viṣaya tvena anadhyavasāyāt sva lakṣaṇa tvāt saṃketa abhāvāt ca na hi buddhi ākārasya bahiṣṭvam bāhyasya vā buddhyākara tvam asti yena tathā iti bhāsaḥ satya pratibhāsaḥ syāt tasmāt vastutas avastu pratibhāsinaḥ śābdāḥ pratyayāḥ 
[169,ix_170,i]	kathantarhi idānīm artha aṃśa apoha kṛt śrutiḥ uktā iti āha anuyānti imam artha aṃśam iti vā apoha kṛt śrutiḥ imam anya apoham artha aṃśam śabdāḥ atad pratibhāsi tvā ipi anuyānti vṛtti viṣaya tvena vyavasthāpayanti artha darśana āyāta tvena parasparam yā tad pratibandhanāt iti ca anya apoha kṛt śrutiḥ uktā 
[170,ii_170,vi]	tasmāt saṃketakālepi yasmāt vyavahāra kāle anya vyavaccheda pratītiḥ śabdāt tasmāt saṃketa kālepī anyāpohaḥ śrutau vācya tayā sambadhyate na anyat nanu artham upadarśya saṃketaḥ kriyate tat katham apohaḥ ucyate iti āha nirdiṣṭa arthena saṃyutaḥ sva pratīti phalena anya apohaḥ saṃbadhyate śrutau nirdiṣṭena arthena anya vyāvṛttena vyavahāra kāle svasya pratītiḥ phalam prayojanam yasya tena saṃyutaḥ abheda adhyavasāyāt eka tvam upanītaḥ anya apohaḥ buddhi ākāra svabhāvaḥ śrutau sambadhyate na tu arthaḥ eva 
[170,vii_170,ix]	tathā hi anyātra adṛṣṭi apekṣa tvāt kvacid tad dṛṣṭi apekṣaṇāt śrutau saṃbadhyata īpohaḥ na etat vastuni yujyate saṃketasya anyatra vyavacchedye avṛkṣe adarśana apekṣa tvāt kvacid avyavacchedye vṛkṣa eka deśe dṛṣṭi apekṣaṇāt śrutau apohaḥ sambadhyate iti niścīyate vastu nisāmānya ādau saṃketa viṣaye etat vyavacchedya avi avacchedyayoḥ darśana adarśana apekṣaṇam na yujyate vastuni vidhi mukhena pratipādye kim anyatra adarśana apekṣayā apekṣyate ca tatas anya vyavacchedaḥ eva pratipādyate iti gamyate anya vyavacchedaḥ sāmānya ādikam ca apekṣyate vipakṣa parihāreṇa pratipatti artham iti ced alam tadā sāmānyena anya vyavacchedena eva vyavahāra parisamāpteḥ 
[170,x_170,xii]	yatas ca jāti guṇa kriyā ādīni viśeṣaṇāni vastu grāhiṇi jñāne na ābhāsante tasmāt jāti ādi tad yogāḥ na arthe teṣu ca na śrutiḥ saṃyojyatenyavyāvṛttau śabdānām eva yojanāt tasmāt jāti ādayaḥ teṣām yogāḥ ca arthe na santi atas teṣu śrutiḥ ca na upayujyate anya vyāvṛttau eva pratīti siddhāyām śabdānām yojanāt 
[171,i_171,iii]	tat evam jāti ādi kalpanā tad sambandha kalpanā ca na asti iti uktam śabda kalpanā api na sambhavati iti āha saṃketa smaraṇa upāyam dṛṣṭa saṃkalana ātmakam pūrva apara parāmarśa śūnye tat cākṣuṣe katham śabda kalpanam hi pūrva gṛhītasya saṃketasya smaraṇam upāyaḥ yasya saṃketa smaraṇa upāyam vācaka tvena dṛṣṭasya śabdasya saṃkalanam tathā ayojanam ātmā yasya tat dṛṣṭa saṃkalana ātmakam prasiddham tat ca pūrvasya saṃketa kāla dṛṣṭa vācaka śabdasya aparasya dṛśyamāna arthasya parāmarśaḥ vāci avācaka tā yojanantena śūnyā śabda āmiśra vastu svarūpa grāhiṇi cākṣuṣe jñāne katham saṃbhāvyate cākṣuṣam ca akṣaja mātra upalakṣaṇam indriya jñānam iti arthaḥ 
[171,iv_171,vi]	kiñca anyatra gata citta upi cakṣuṣā rūpam īkṣate tad saṃketā grahaḥ tatra spaṣṭaḥ tad jā ca kalpanā dṛśyamānāt arthāt anyatra atīta ādau vikalpanīye gata cittaḥ pravṛtta vikalpā upi draṣṭā cakṣuṣā cakṣuḥ vijñānena rūpam īkṣate tasya dṛśyamāna arthasya saṃketaḥ saṃketa viṣayaḥ vācakam nāma tasya āgrahaḥ asmaraṇam tatra cākṣuṣe jñāne spaṣṭaḥ tatas tad jāḥ vācakanāma smaraṇa prabhavā kalpanā ca cākṣuṣe jñāne na asti iti śeṣaḥ 
[171,vii_171,ix]	kiñca jāyante kalpanāḥ tatra yatra śabdaḥ niveśitaḥ tena icchātaḥ pravartteran na īkṣeran bāhya m akṣa jāḥ tatra viṣaye śabda yojana ātmikāḥ kalpanāḥ jāyante yatra saṃketa kāle śabdaḥ niveśitaḥ na ca indriya viṣaye śabda saṃketaḥ iti na tat jñānam śabda yojana ātmakam atha indriya viṣayaḥ eva śabda niveśaḥ tadā tena śabda viṣaya tvena kāraṇena icchātaḥ pravartterannakṣa jāḥ pratyayā vikalpavat na ca etat asti icchā prabhava tve vā bāhya artha saṃnidhāna anapekṣa tvāt bāhyam artham na īkṣerannakṣa jāḥ pratyaya vikalpavat 
[171,x_172,i]	api ca rūpam rūpam iti īkṣeta tat hiyam kim iti īkṣate asti ca anubhavaḥ tasyāḥ saḥ vikalpaḥ katham bhavet sarva vikalpa vādinaḥ mate rūpam iti pravṛtta vikalpa buddhiḥ rūpam īkṣeta tat hiyam rūpa dhiyam api kalpyamānām kim iti īkṣate jñātā rūpa buddhi anubhavaḥ na asti iti na yuktam yasmāt asti ca anubhavaḥ tasyāḥ sarveṣām pratipad tṛṇām na ca rūpaḥ iva tat buddhau api kalpanā anubhūyate tatas ca rūpa buddheḥ anubhavaḥ avikalpaḥ katham bhavet 
[172,ii_172,iii]	tayā eva anubhave dṛṣṭam na vikalpa dvayam sakṛt etena tulya kāla ani avijñāna anubhavaḥ gataḥ tayā eva rūpa buddhyā rūpasya sva ātmanaḥ cā anubhavebhyupagamyamāne rūpam iti rūpa anubhavaḥ iti ca vikalpa dvayam sakṛt syāt tat ca na asti anubhava vādhita tvāt etena sakṛt kalpanā dvaya niṣedhena tulya kālena anyena nirvikalpa jñānena anubhavaḥ rūpa buddheḥ gataḥ nirṇṇīta uttaraḥ boddhavyaḥ 
[172,iv_172,vi]	uttara kāla bhāvinā vikalpa jñānena anubhavaḥ iti ced āha smṛtiḥ bhavet atīte ca sā agṛhīte katham bhavet syāt ca anya dhī pari cheda abhinna rūpā sva buddhi dhīḥ atīte ca rūpa anubhave smṛtiḥ paścāt tanena vikalpena na bhavet na anubhavaḥ sā smṛtiḥ agṛhīte anubhave katham bhavet yadi ca atīta buddhiḥ vikalpyate tadā anyasya puṃsaḥ dhiyaḥ paricchedena parokṣa buddhi vikalpa ātmakena abhinna rūpā tathā tvena sva buddhi dhīḥ syāt asti ca para buddhi pratīti vilakṣaṇa sva buddhi anubhavaḥ tasmāt avikalpaḥ eva asau 
[172,vii_172,ix]	kiñca atītam apadṛṣṭāntam aliṅgañca artha vedanam siddham tat kena tasmin hi na pratyakṣam na laiṅgikam sa vikalpaka pratyakṣa vādinā nirvikalpasya api asva saṃvedana vādinaḥ mate atītam artha vedanam na kevalam adhyakṣataḥ vartamāna viṣaya tvāt na sidhyati kintu anumānāt api yasmāt aliṅgam liṅga rahitam tathā hi dharmiṇaḥ jñānasya asiddha tvāt liṅgam āśraya asiddham anumānāt jñāna siddhi vādinaḥ kasyacid jñānasya adhyakṣa asiddha tvāt anumāna siddhau anavasthānāt apadṛṣṭāntam dṛṣṭānta asiddhau navya āpti siddhiḥ iti liṅga rahitam eva atītam rūpa ādi darśanam tat tasmāt kena pramāṇena siddham tasmin hi rūpa ādi darśane na pratyakṣam abhimata tvāt asti na ca laiṅgikam anumānam ukta kramāt iti sakalam apratipattikam andha mūkam jagat prāptam iti 
[173,i_173,iv]	atha tad svarūpa avabhāsinyā buddhyā anantarayā yadi rūpa ādiḥ iva gṛhyeta tad svarūpa avabhāsinyā atīta rūpa ādi buddhi rūpa pratibhāsinyā tad janyayā anantayā dhiyā atīta buddhiḥ yadi gṛhyate sautra antika mate rūpa ādiḥ iva tad anukāriṇyā tad anantarayā dhiyā tadā kaḥ doṣaḥ iti āha yadā ciram bahuṣu viṣayeṣu jñānāni pravartante tadā 
[173,v]	na syāt tad pūrvadhī grahaḥ saḥ vikalpaḥ sva viṣayaḥ vijñāna anubhavaḥ yathā aśakya samayam tadvat anyat api avikalpakam sāmānya vācinaḥ śabdāḥ tad eka arthā ca kalpanā abhāve nirvikalpasya viśeṣa adhigamaḥ katham asti ced nirvikalpañca kiñcid tad tulya hetukam sarvam tathā eva hetoḥ hi bhedāt bhedaḥ phala ātmanām 
[173,vi^1]	tasmāt antyāt jñānāt yāḥ pūrvāḥ dhiyaḥ tāsām grahaḥ na syāt iti doṣaḥ antya buddhi janitayā hi dhiyā sā eva gṛhyate na tu anyāḥ iti syāt asti ca anubhavaḥ tāsām yat valena ciram aham adrākṣam iti bhavati draṣṭuḥ tasmāt sva viṣayaḥ svarūpa ālambanaḥ vijñānānām pūrva bhāvinām anubhavaḥ avikalpaḥ sa yathā tadvat anyat api jñānam antyam apratibaddha vṛtti ca avikalpakam boddhavyam yasmāt sakalam eva sva rūpam aśakya samayam śabda saṃketā viṣayaḥ tatas ca na vikalpa grāhyam kiñca viśeṣa saṃketa abhāvāt vyavahāra kāla anuyāyi tvāt ca sāmānya vācinaḥ śabdāḥ taiḥ śabdaiḥ eka arthāḥ eka viṣayā
[173,vi^2]	ca kalpanā śabda yojanayā śabda arthaḥ eva kalpanā para mate ca nirvikalapasya jñānasya abhāve viśeṣasya vikalpā viṣayasya adhigamaḥ katham na kathañcid iti arthaḥ viśeṣa anubhava darśanāt asti kiñcid nirvikalpam ca jñānam yathā āhuḥ mī mām sa ka ādayaḥ iti ced evantarhi tena nirvikalpena tulya hetukam cakṣū rūpamanaskāra ādi samāna hetukam viśeṣa viṣayam sarvam jñānam tathā eva avikalpakamaḥ tu na tu sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam api kiñcid savikalpakam hiḥ yasmāt hatoḥ bhedāt phala ātmanām bhedaḥ bhavati hetu abhede tu phala abhedaḥ eva yuktaḥ na anyathā kvacid api eka jātīya tā syāt 
[174,i_174,iii]	kiñca anapekṣita bāhya arthāḥ yojanā samaya smṛteḥ tathā anapekṣya samayam vastu śaktyā eva netra dhīḥ yojanā kalpanā anapekṣita bāhya arthāḥ bahis artha saṃketa viṣayam anapekṣya eva samayasya prāk gṛhītasya smṛteḥ sakāśāt bhavati tāvat tathā samayam anapekṣya vastunaḥ sva lakṣaṇasya śaktyā su a ākāra anukāri vijñāna janana sāmarthyena eva netradhīḥ jāyate yadi tadā kaḥ virodhaḥ 
[174,iv_174,vi]	syāt etat saṃketa smaraṇa apekṣa rūpam yadi akṣa cetasi anapekṣya na ced śaktam syāt smṛtau eva liṅga vat rūpam akṣa cetasi kartavye saṃketa smaraṇa apekṣam tad anapekṣam punar na aśaktam iti evam tarhi śrutau eva rūpam śaktam iti syāt na tu indriya buddhau liṅga vat yathā hi liṃgam na liṃga buddhau sākṣāt śaktam kintu liṅga liṅginoḥ sammbandhi smṛtau eva tathā saṃketa smaraṇe rūpam nimittam syāt na ca agṛhītam smṛti pratibodhakam iti nirvikalpa kam asya grahaṇam prāk tatas smṛtiḥ tatas ca yojana iti kramaḥ 
[174,vii_174,ix]	katham punar artha sammukhībhāvāt smṛti janma iti āha tasyāḥ tad saṅgama utpatteḥ akṣadhīḥ syāt smṛteḥ nna vā tatas kāla antarepi syāt kvacid vyākṣepa sambhavāt tasyāḥ smṛteḥ tasya arthasya saṃgamena sammukhībhāvena utpatteḥ na tu akṣa dhīḥ arthāt syāt sā tu smṛteḥ artha janitāyāḥ syāt na vā smṛteḥ api bhavet smṛti adhīna tāyām na artha adhīna tā yat ca smaraṇam bhāvi tat na avaśyam bhavati iti kadācid na bhavet api tatas smṛteḥ kāla antareṇa api syāt adhyakṣadhīḥ smṛti anantaram kvacid viṣaya antare vyākṣepasya aśakti lakṣaṇasya saṃbhavāt tad nivṛttau satyām krameṇa bhavet 
[175,i_175,iii]	syāt etat prathama mubhi mukhī bhavan arthaḥ smṛteḥ hetuḥ tatas indriya jñānasya iti krameṇa ubhaya hetuḥ ced prāk eva syāt abhedataḥ anyokṣa buddhi hetuḥ ced smṛtiḥ tatra api anarthikā krameṇa ubhaya hetuḥ abhimataḥ ced yadi evam pūrva apara eka svabhāva sāmarthyasya bhāvasya abhedataḥ tat janyam dvayam api prāk eva syāt na kramatas syāt etat bhāvānām kṣaṇika tvāt ca anyaḥ smṛti prabodhakaḥ kṣaṇaḥ anyaḥ ca akṣa buddheḥ hetuḥ ced tatra ādyepi kṣaṇe vācaka śabda smṛtiḥ anarthikā 
[175,iv_175,vi]	yasmāt yathā samita sidhi artham iṣyate samaya smṛtiḥ bhedaḥ ca asamitaḥ grāhyaḥ smṛtiḥ tatra kimarthikā yathā samitasya śabda vācya tayā arthasya siddhi artham samaya smṛtiḥ iṣyate bhedaḥ viśeṣaḥ asamitaḥ saṃketā viṣayaḥ ca akṣa dhiyā grāhyaḥ tatra smṛtiḥ samayasya kimarthikā niṣprayojanā 
[175,vii_175,ix]	sāmānye kāla antara anuvarttini saṃketaḥ saḥ eva smaryate iti ced āha na sāmānya mātra grahaṇe bheda apekṣā na yujyate tasmāt cakṣuḥ ca rūpañca pratītya udeti netra dhīḥ sāmānya mātrasya grahaṇe abhyupagamyamāne bhedasya viśeṣasya saṃketa viṣayasya apekṣā na yujyate yathā gauḥ iti ukte kīdṛśaḥ gauḥ iti tasmāt sāmānyavati viśeṣe saṃketaḥ tena eva arthi tvāt vyavahāriṇām tathā ca bhedaḥ ca asamitaḥ grāhyaḥ iti uktam tasmāt cakṣuḥ ca rūpañca prati iti āsādya udā iti netra dhīḥ iti abhyupagantavyam 
[175,x_175,xii]	vyavadhānena api rūpa kāraṇa tā syāt iti ced āha sākṣāt ced jñāna janane samarthaḥ viṣa yokṣa vat sākṣāt ca viṣayaḥ rūpa ādiḥ sva grāhaka jñāna janane samarthaḥ akṣa vat na vyavadhānena smṛti adhīnatāyām doṣasya ukta tvāt tasmāt aśabda saṃsṛṣṭa artha bala bhāvitad rūpa anukāri pratyakṣam anāviṣṭa abhilāpam avikalpakam eva yuktam 
[176,i_176,ii]	atha kasmāt dvaya adhīna janma tat tena na ucyate atha dvaya adhīna janma viṣaya indriya utpatti tad indriya jñānam indriyeṇa ucyate vyapadiśyate pratyakṣam iti pratigatam akṣampratyakṣam indriya āśritam iti arthaḥ kasmāt punar viṣayeṇa na ucyate prativiṣayam iti 
[176,iii_176,v]	na khalu vyasani tayā vyapadeśaḥ niyujyate api tu samīkṣya gamaka tvam hi vyapadeśaḥ na gṛhyate tat ca akṣa vyapadeśa isti tad dharmaḥ ca niyojyatām gamaka tvam samīkṣya paribhāvya tat ca gamaka tvam akṣeṇa vyapadeśe pratyakṣam iti atra asti tasya gamaka tvasya vyāpakasya dharmmaḥ vyāpya bhūtaḥ niyojyatām 
[176,vi_176,vii]	tatas liṅga svabhāvotra vyapadeśe niyojyatām nivarttate vyāpakasya svabhāvasya nivṛttitaḥ tatas vyāpaka abhāvāt vyapadeśe dharmmiṇi atra gamaka tve sādhye niyojyatām liṅgam prativiṣayam iti vyapadeśāt vyāpakasya gamaka tvasya nivṛttitaḥ nivartate niyojyata iti vyāpaka anupalabdhyā tatra niyojya tva abhāvaḥ siddhaḥ 
[176,viii_176,ix]	sañcitaḥ samudāyaḥ sa sāmānyam tatra ca akṣadhīḥ sāmānya buddhiḥ ca avaśyam vikalpena anubadhyate nanu sañcita ālambanāḥ pañca vijñāna kāyāḥ iti siddhāntaḥ tatra aneka artha janya tvāt sva arthe sāmānyagotara miti ca uktam tathā ca paramāṇūnām samudāyaḥ sañcitaḥ iti ucyate saḥ eva ca sāmānye mataḥ tatra ca sāmānye akṣadhīḥ jjāyate sāmānya buddhiḥ ca avaśyam vikalpena anubadhyate anusīvyate 
[177,i_177,iv]	tat katham avikalpam pratyakṣam ucyate atra āha artha antara abhisambandhāt jāyante ye aṇavaḥ apare uktāḥ te sañcitāḥ te hi nimittam jñāna janmanaḥ artha antarāṇām paramāṇu antarāṇām abhisambandhāt sannidhāna viśeṣeṇa upasarpaṇa pratyayebhyaḥ pūrvakebhyaḥ parama sannihitebhyaḥ aparenyeye aṇavaḥ jāyante te sañcitāḥ uktāḥ sañcita ālambanāḥ vijñāna kāyaḥ iti ādau jñāna janmanaḥ te eva hi nimitta muktāḥ tatra aneka artha janya tvāt ityādinā 
[177,v_177,vi]	aṇūnām sa viśeṣaḥ ca na antareṇa aparān aṇūna tad eka aniyamāt jñānam uktam sāmānya gocaram aṇūnām sa ca jñāna janana sāmarthya lakṣaṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ aparān aṇūn a vyavadhāna varttinaḥ antareṇa vinā na bhavati na hi pratyekam aṇavaḥ dṛśyāḥ kim tu sahitāḥ eva tat tasmāt ekasmin arthe paramāṇau jñānasya aniyamāt sāmānya gocaram saṃcita paramāṇu saṃghāta viṣayam jñānam uktam tattva vādinā na tu paramāṇu atirikta sāmānya viṣayam tat katham sāmānya viṣaya tvāt sa vikalpa tva prasaṅgaḥ 
[177,vii_177,viii]	atha eka āyatana tvepi na anekam dṛśyate sakṛt sakṛt graha avabhāsaḥ kim viyukteṣu tila ādiṣu atha eka indriya jñāna janaka tvāt nīla pīta ādīnām eka āyatana tve rūpa āyatana tva saṃgrahepi na anekam nīla ādi sakṛt dṛśyate kintu krameṇa tad katham aṇūnā bahūnām ekadā grahaṇam atra ucyate yadi na anekam ekadā gṛhyate tadā tila ādiṣu viyukteṣu vibhinna deśeṣu sakṛt graha avabhāsaḥ yugapad grahaṇa anubhavaḥ kim kasmāt he toḥ 
[178,i_178,iii]	jñānānām laghu vṛtti tvāt sakṛt grahaṇa bhramaḥ ced āha pratyuktam lāghavañca atra teṣu eva krama pātiṣu kim na ākrama grahaḥ tulya kālāḥ sarvāḥ ca buddhayaḥ pratyuktam pratikṣiptam ca atra sakṛt graha avabhāse lāghavam buddhīnām anyatra api samānam tat varṇṇayoḥ vā sakṛt śrutiḥ ityādinā tathā api ucyate teṣu eva tila ādiṣu hasta ādibhyaḥ krama pātiṣu kim kasmāt na ākrama grahaṇam bhavati sarvāḥ ca buddhayaḥ saha avasthiteṣu sambhavantyaḥ tulya kālāḥ 
[178,iv_178,vi]	tatas kāścid tā su akrama ābhāsāḥ kramavatyā uparāḥ ca kim sarva artha grahaṇe tasmāt akramoyam prasajyate tāsu kāścid akrama ābhāsāyāḥ saha sthita vastu viṣayāyāḥ aparāḥ ca buddhayaḥ kramavatyaḥ ayugapad pratibhāsāḥ kim bhavanti yāḥ krama pāti vastu viṣayāḥ asti ca ayam bhedaḥ tasmāt sarvasya arthasya kramiṇaḥ akramiṇaḥ ca grahaṇe akramaḥ ayam lāghava aviśeṣāt prasajyate 
[178,vii_178,ix]	kiñca na ekam citra pataṅga ādi rūpam vā dṛśyate katham citram tat ekam iti ced idam citra tarantataḥ citra pataṅga ādi na ekam anekam nīla ādi rūpam vā dṛśyate katham yadi na anekam ekena gṛhyate citram nīla pīta ādi ātmakam tad pataṅga ādikam ekam iti ced idañcitram ekam yat ucyate tat tatas citra pataṅgāt api citrataram āścaryataram citram iti nānā rūpāṇi tat eva punar ekam ucyate iti upahasati 
[178,x_179,i]	tathā ca na ekam svabhāvam citram hi maṇi rūpam yathā eva tat nīla ādi pratibhāsaḥ ca tulyaḥ citra paṭa ādiṣu citram aneka rūpam hi yasmāt tasmāt na ekam pataṅga ādi yathā eva saṃsthāna viśeṣeṇa sanniviṣṭānām bahūnām maṇīnām rūpam tat citram anekam na ekam avayavi dravyam vijātīyānām dravya anārambhāt citra buddhiḥ eka tvāt mukhyā pataṅgemaṇi rūpa ādiṣu punar upacaritā iti ced āha nīla ādi pratibhāsaḥ citra pratibhāsaḥ sa citra paṭaḥ ādiḥ yeṣām maṇi rūpa ādīnām teṣu citra pataṅge ca tulyaḥ na tu agnimāṇavakayoḥ dahana buddhiḥ iva skhalat a skhalat vṛttiḥ lakṣyate 
[179,ii_179,iii]	tatra avayava rūpañcait kevalam dṛśyate tathā nīla ādīni nirasya anyat citram citram yat īkṣase tatra citra paṭa ādiṣu kevalam avayava rūpam tathā citra tayā dṛśyate na avayavī vijātīyānām dravya anārambhāt iti ced citra pataṅga ādau api nīla ādīni nirasya pṛthakkṛtya tebhyaḥ anyat citram avayavi rūpam yat īkṣase tvam tat citram āścaryam sva siddhānta anurāga bheṣaja viśodhita cakṣuḥ īkṣase tvam eva yadi īdṛśam avayavinam param na atra ani eṣām adhikāraḥ 
[179,iv_179,vi]	api ca tulya artha ākāra kāla tvena upalakṣitayoḥ dvayoḥ nānā arthā kramavatī ekā kim eka artha akramā aparā tulya artha ākāra tvena tulya kālattvena ca upalakṣitayoḥ kṛtrimā kṛtrima pataṅga viśeṣaṇayoḥ dvayoḥ mmadhye ekā kṛtrima pataṅga viṣayā dhīḥ nāna arthāḥ vijātīya ātmaka dravya anārambhāt kramavatī ca nīlānām bahūnām krameṇa grahaṇāt aparā akṛtrima pataṅga viṣayāḥ eka arthauviya viviṣayā atas eva akramā ca kim kasmāt iṣyate dvayoḥ api samāna tā yuktāḥ nimittasya sāmyāt 
[179,vii_179,ix]	kiñca vaiśvarūpyāt hiyām eva bhāvānām viśva rūpa tā tat ced anaṅgam kena iyam siddhā bheda vyavasthitiḥ dhiyām eva vaiśvarūpya anna anākāra tvāt bhāvānām grāhyāṇām viśva rūpa tā vyavasthāpyate citrasya avayavinaḥ ekatā svīkāre tad buddhiṣu pratibhāsa nānātvam bheda vyavasthitau anaṅgam ced tadā bhāvānām bheda vyavasthitiḥ apahanūyeta eva kena anyena nibandhena siddhā bhaviṣyati 
[180,i_180,iv]	api ca vijātīnām anārambhāt ālekhya ādau na citra dhīḥ arūpa tvāt na saṃyogaḥ citraḥ bhakteḥ ca na āśrayaḥ vijātīnām bhinna jātīnām rāga dravyāṇām kārya dravya anārambhāt ālekhya ādau citra dhīḥ na syāt ālekhyam saṃyogaḥ tasya citram rūpam iti ced na saṃyoga upi citraḥ tasya arūpa tvāt saṃyogaḥ guṇaḥ tathā rūpañca na ca guṇe guṇa antaram asti syāt etat yathā taruṣu saṃkhyā lakṣaṇam vanam kusumita tvam ca atas eka artha samavāyāt vane kusumita buddhiḥ tathā avayaveṣu citra saṃyogayoḥ samavāyāt citram citram iti buddhiḥ upacārāt ityādi bhakteḥ upacārasya ca saṃyogaḥ āśrayaḥ na yuktaḥ 
[180,v_180,vi]	pratyekam avicitra tvāt gṛhīteṣu krameṇa ca na citra dhī saṅkalanam anekasya ekayā agrahāt pratyekam avayavaānām avicitra tvāt nīla ādiṣu krameṇa sva buddhibhiḥ gṛhīta iṣu buddhi antareṇa citra saṃkalanam saṃkṣipya grahaṇañca na yuktam ekayā dhiyā anekasya agrahāt 
[180,vii_180,viii]	nānā artha ekā bhavet tasmāt siddhātopya vikalpikā vikalpayat nāyeka artha yatonyat api paśyati katham nīlānām ekabuddhyā saṃkalanam iṣṭau vā tasmāt saṃkalana svīkārāt eva ekā buddhiḥ nānā arthā aneka viṣayā bhavet atas aneka artha vedanāt api buddhiḥ avikalpikā siddhā yatas śabda yojitam ekam artham vikalpayat nānyat asaṃyojitam artha antaram api paśyati draṣṭā na hi ekadā aneka śabda yojanā tasmāt artha sañcaya viṣaya tvāt sāmānya viṣaya tvam tathā api tu avikalpite tena virodhaḥ 
[180,ix_181,i]	nanu citra avabhāseṣu artheṣu yadi a eka tvam na yujyate sā eva tāvat katham buddhiḥ ekā citra avabhāsinī citram nānā kāraḥ avabhāsaḥ yeṣām pataṅga ādīnām teṣu artheṣu ekatvam na yujyate yadi sā eva citra artha grāhiṇī buddhiḥ citra avabhāsinī citra ākārā katham ekā saṃmatā yathā citra tvepi buddhiḥ ekā tathā kārya dravyañca ekam syāt 
[181,ii_181,vii]	atra āha idam vastu bala āyātam yat vadanti vipaścitaḥ idam vastunaḥ avyabhicāri liṅgasya balāt āyātam yat vadanti vipaścitaḥ bu ddhāḥ bhagavantaḥ kim tat iti āha yathā yathārthāḥ cintyante viśīryante tathā tathā yathā yathā yena prakāreṇa eka tvena aneka tvena vā arthāḥ nīla ādayaḥ bāhya jñāna ātmānaḥ vā vicintyante tathā viśīryante kvacid api na vyavatiṣṭhante iti yāvat na hi jñānam ekam nānā ākāra tvāt tad lakṣaṇa tvāt ca bhedasya na api anekam citra pratibhāsa anupapatteḥ parasparam avedanāt anyasya ca grāhakasya abhāvāt 
[181,viii_181,xii]	kim syāt sā citra tā ekasyām nanu yadi sā citra tā buddhau ekasyām syāt tayā ca citram ekam dravyam vyavasthāpyeta tadā ki dūṣaṇam syāt āha na syāt tasyām matau api na kevalam dravye tasyām matau api ekasyām na syā ccitra tā ākāra nānātva lakṣaṇa tvāt bhedasya nānā tvepi citra tā katham aneka puruṣa pratīti vat 
[181,xiii_181,xv]	kathantarhi pratītiḥ iti āha yadi idam svayam arthānām rocate tatra ke vayam yadi idamatāt rūpyepi tādrūpya prathanam arthānām bhāsamānānām nīla ādīnām svayam apara preraṇayā rocate tatra tathā pratibhāse ke vayam asahamānāḥ api niṣeddhum avastu ca pratibhāsate ca iti vyaktam ālīkyam 
[182,i_182,ii]	tasmāt na artheṣu na jñāne sthūla ābhāsaḥ tad ātmanaḥ ekatra pratiṣiddha tvāt bahuṣu api na sambhavaḥ tasmāt na artheṣu bāhyeṣu na jñāne tad grāhake sthūla ābhāsaḥ sthūlaḥ ākāraḥ saṃgacchate tad ātmanaḥ sthūla svarūpasya ekatra avayave paramāṇau vā pratiṣiddha tvāt bahuṣu api teṣu sambhavaḥ na asti militāḥ api hi taeva te ca pratyekam sthaulya vikalāḥ iti samuditāḥ api tathā eva syuḥ tathā nīla ādi ākāreṣu pratyekam citrasya sthaulyasya abhāvāt samudāyepi abhāvaḥ 
[182,iii_182,v]	nanu sukha ādi ātmakam sva prakāśam vijñānam ekam idam itiyoga ācāra matam avyāhatam iti āha pariccheda untaranyaḥ ayam bhāgaḥ bahis iva sthitaḥ jñānasya abhedinau bhinnau pratibhāsaḥ hi upaplavaḥ paricchedaḥ grāhaka ākāraḥ sukha ādeḥ antara bahis deśe paricchedāt anyoyam bhāgaḥ grāhyaḥ nīla ādiḥ bbahis sthitaḥ iva ābhāti sarveṣām hiḥ yasmāt jñānasya abhedinau bhinnau ākārau tattvataḥ na yuktau tasmāt antar bbahis deśa sambandha tayā pratibhāsaḥ upaplavaḥ na satyaḥ 
[182,vi_182,vii]	tatra ekasya api abhāvena dvayam api avahīyate tasmāt tat eva tasya api tattvam yā dvaya śūnyatā tatra eka jñāna ātmani viruddham dvayam na yuktam iti ekasya grāhya tvasya grāhaka tvasya vā avaśya abhyupaganta vyena abhāvena dvayam api avahīyate anyonya sāpekṣayoḥ eka abhāve aparābhāvasya nyāya prāpta tvāt tasmāt tasya jñānasya api tattvam tat eva yā dvayena grāhya grāhaka ākāreṇa śūnyatā nāma 
[182,viii_182,ix]	tat bheda āśrayiṇī ca iyam bhāvānām bheda saṃsthitiḥ tad upaplava bhāve ca teṣām bheda upyupaplavaḥ iyam ca bhāvānām rūpa vedanā ādīnām bheda saṃsthitiḥ tasya grāhya grāhakasya bhedaḥ saḥ āśrayaḥ yasyāḥ sā tathā tasya grāhya grāhaka bhāvasya bheda vyavasthā nibandhanasya upaplava bhāve mithyātve ca teṣām rūpa ādīnām bhedaḥ api tad vyavasthāpitaḥ upaplavaḥ na kevalam rūpa ādīnām bheda abhedau upaplavaḥ 
[183,i_183,iii]	lakṣaṇa śūnya tvāt niḥsvabhāva tvam api iti āha na grāhya grāhaka ākāra bāhyam asti ca lakṣaṇam atas lakṣaṇa śūnya tvāt niḥsvabhāvāḥ prakāśitāḥ rūpa ādīnām grāhya grāhaka ākārābhyām bāhyam bhinnam lakṣaṇam na ca asti tathā hi viṣaya tayā kiñcid nirddiśyate yathā rūpyate iti kṛtvā rūpam kiñcid viṣayi tayā vijānāti ityādi vyutpattyā yathā rūpiṇaḥ skandhāḥ na tu etat vyatiriktam kiñcid lakṣaṇam asti atas lakṣaṇena grāhya grāhaka tvena śūnya tvāt niḥsvabhāvāḥ sarva dharmmāḥ prakāśitā bhagavadbhiḥ bu ddhaiḥ 
[183,iv_183,vi]	kiñca bahis arthavādepi lakṣaṇa śūnya tvāt niḥsvabhāva tām dharmmāṇām ākhyātum āha vyāpāra upādhikam sarvam skandha ādīnām viśeṣataḥ lakṣaṇam sa ca tat tvan na tena api ete vilakṣaṇāḥ skandhaḥ ādiḥ yeṣām dhātu āyatanānām teṣām yat lakṣaṇam rāśībhavanti iti rāśi arthaḥ skandhānām kārya utpādaka tvena ākāra arthaḥ dhātūnām āyantan vanti iti āya dvāra arthaḥ āyatanānām tat sarvam lakṣaṇam vyāpāra upādhikam vyāpāra viśeṣaṇam sa ca vyāpāraḥ apratīteḥ bheda pakṣe na tattvam abheda īpi prāc abhāvī bhāvaḥ eva syāt sa ca tattvam na bhavati aśaktam sarvam iti cedi tyatra ukta kramāt tena vyāpāra upādhika lakṣaṇā yogena api vilakṣaṇāḥ niḥsvabhāvāḥ ete skandha ādayaḥ 
[183,vii_183,ix]	katham tarhi bāhya skandha ādi deśanā bhagavatām iti āha yathā svaṃpratyaya apekṣādavidyā upapluta ātmanām vijñaptiḥ vitatha ākārā jāyate timira ādi vat anādya vidyā upapluta ātma nām aprahīṇa akliṣṭa jñānānām puṃsām yathāsvam yasya bhramasya yaḥ atmīyaḥ pratyayaḥ yathāsvaṃpratyayaḥ tasya apekṣaṇam apekṣaḥ tasmāt vitathau grāhya grāhaka ākārau yasyāḥ sā tādṛśī vijñaptiḥ jāyate timira ādi vat timira ādau iva vitatha ākāra candra dvaya ādi vijñāptiḥ 
[184,i_184,v]	asaṃvidita tattvā ca sā sarva apara darśanaiḥ sā ca vijñaptiḥ sarvaiḥ apara darśanaiḥ anutkṛṣṭa darśanaiḥ asam viditāḥ dvaya śūnyatā tattvam yasyāḥ sā asaṃvidita tatvā kasmāt iti āha asaṃbhavāt vinā teṣām grāhya grāhaka viplavaiḥ grāhya grāhaka viplavaiḥ vinā teṣām apara darśanānām vijñapteḥ asambhavāt grāhya grāha kopa pluta darśana tvam eva ca anutkṛṣṭa darśana tvam 
[184,vi_184,vii]	tad upekṣita tattva arthaiḥ kṛtvā gaja nimīlanam kevalam loka budhyā eva bāhya cintā prayanyate tat bhrānta darśana anurodhāt upekṣita tatva arthaiḥ avadhārita tadadvaya vivekaiḥ bhagavadbhiḥ buddhaiḥ ggaja nimīlanam kṛtvā gajasya iva pārśva dvayam paśyatā upi nayana nimīlana kalayā tattvam apaśyantam iva ātmānam darśayadbhiḥ lokasya avidyā upahatasya buddhyā dvaya grāhiṇyā bāhyasya cintā skandha āyatana ādi tvena pratanyate skandha ādi deśanayā hi loka buddhi anurodha pravartita pāṣaṇḍa grāha nivṛttau mukhyayā yeṣu mumukṣavaḥ avatāryante iti deśanā kramaḥ 
[184,viii_184,x]	athavā citra tvepi bāhyam ekam na yuktam buddhiḥ tu citrā api ekā eva iti darśayitum āha nīla ādiḥ citra vijñāne jñāna upādhiḥ ananya bhāj aśakya darśanaḥ nīla ādiḥ citre jñāne jñāna upādhiḥ anubhavasya ātma bhūtaḥ ananya bhāj ākāra antara asahacaraḥ kevalaḥ iti arthaḥ tādṛśaḥ aśakya darśanaḥ saha eva ākāra antara vedana niyamāt na hi citre vijñāne samutpanne nīlam nirasya pītam śakya darśanam tasmāt aśakya vivecana tvam tulya yogakṣema tvam saha pratibhāsa niyata tvam jñāna ātmanām nīla ādīnām eka tvam bāhya ātmanām tu na etat saṃbhavati ekam pidhāya api draṣṭum anyasya śakya tvāt 
[184,xi_185,i]	nanu jñāna ākāra upi nīlaḥ pīta anubhava kāle tadā na anubhūyate tadā śakya vivecanaḥ eva iti āha tam hi patati arthe vivecayan tam anubhūyamānāt pītāt vivecayan bhedena vyavasthāpayan pramātā arthaḥ eva nīle patati vivecaka tvena parokṣam tadā nīlam arthaḥ eva aparokṣatā eva tu jñāna svabhāvaḥ atas yat vivicyate tad ajñānam yat jñānam tat na vivecyatas eva 
[185,ii_185,iv]	tasmāt yat yathā bhāsate jñānam tat tathā eva prakāśate iti nāma eka bhāvaḥ syāt citra ākārasya cetasi yat jñānam yathā nīla ādi ātma tayā jātam sat tathā bhāsate prakāśate bhāsamāna svabhāva tvāt jñānam tathā tena eva svarūpeṇa anubhūyate sarveḥ pratipattṛbhiḥ na ca utpannasya api jñānasya sva prakāśakasya aviditaḥ kaścid ākārosti iti aśakya vivecana tvāt tulya yogakṣema tvāt saha pratibhāsa niyamāt citrasya nīla pīta ādi ākārasya cetasi buddhau eka bhāvaḥ nāma bhavet tadā kaḥ doṣaḥ 
[185,v_185,ix]	paṭa ādi rūpasya ekatve tathā syāt aviveki tā jñāna vat paṭa ādi rūpasya ekatve abhyupagamyamāne tathā jñānasya iva avivekitā aśakya vivecana tvam syāt na ca asti nīla ādīnām grahaṇa agrahaṇa bhedasya darśanāt syāt etat avayavāḥ nīla ādyāḥ parasparataḥ avayavinaḥ ca bhinnāḥ teṣām bhedāt vivekena grahaṇam yaḥ tu abhinnaḥ avayavī na tasya vivekena grahaṇam iti āha vivekīni nirasya anyadā viveki ca na īkṣate vivekīni nīla ādi avayava rūpāṇi nirasya pṛthak kṛtvā anyadā viveki ḥ ūpañca na īkṣate dṛśya sammatam anupalabhyamānam katham abhyupagama arha 
[185,x_186,i]	yat ca ucyate paramāṇavaḥ pratyekam atīndriya tvāt sañcitāḥ api na jñāna gocaraḥ iti tatra āha kaḥ vā virodhaḥ bahavaḥ saṃjāta atiśayāḥ pṛthak bhaveyuḥ kāraṇam buddheḥ yadi na ātma indriya ādi vat yadi bahavaḥ paramāṇavaḥ upasarpaṇa pratyayāt saṃjā tātiśayāḥ vijñāna janana yogyāḥ saṃhatāḥ utpannā sva grāhi kāryañca buddheḥ kāraṇam bhaveyuḥ tadā kaḥ virodhaḥ indriyāḥ divat indriya ādayaḥ pratyekam na buddheḥ hetuḥ militāḥ tu bhavanti tadvat aṇavopi syuḥ na hi pareṣām iva asmākañca nitya eka svabhāvāḥ aṇavaḥ te hi yathāpratyayam atīndriyāḥ santaḥ aindriyāḥ api syuḥ 
[186,ii_186,vii]	nanu hetu tva īpi katham aṇavaḥ grāhyāḥ iti āha hetu bhāvāt ṛte na anyā grāhyatā nāma kācana hetu bhāvat ṛte vinā grāhyatā nāma yā prasiddha sā na anyā kācid api tu hetutaina grāhyatā evantarhi indriya ādikam api hetu tvāt grāhyam syāt iti āha tatra buddhiḥ yat ākārā tasyāḥ tat grāhyam ucyate tatra teṣu hetuṣu buddhiḥ yat ākārā bhavati tasyāḥ buddheḥ tat grāhyam ucyate aṇu sañcayaḥ sā eva ca buddhiḥ ākāram anukaroti na indriya ādeḥ 
[186,viii_186,ix]	katham vā avayavī grāhyaḥ sakṛt sva avayavaiḥ saha na hi go pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sāsna ādīnām adarśane tat katham tat grāhyam yopya āha na anekam sakṛt gṛhyate iti tad mate avayavī sva avayavaiḥ sa āsnāka kullāṅgūla ādibhiḥ saha katham vā grāhyaḥ yuktaḥ na gṛhyate eva iti ced na hi gorava yavinaḥ pratyayaḥ sāsna ādīnām avayavānām adarśane kvāpi dṛṣṭaḥ 
[186,x_186,xi]	guṇa pradhāna adhigamaḥ saha api abhimataḥ yadi sampūrṇa aṅgaḥ na gṛhyeta sakṛt na api guṇa ādimān yadi saha api abhimataḥ guṇa pradhānayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ adhigamaḥ na upādhīnām anyonyam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhūtānām dravyāṇām vā tādṛśāṇām evantarhi viṣāṇī sāsnādi mān iti vā yadā gṛhyate tadā tena eva avayavena sambandha vyavasāyāt itara avayava sambandha anavasāyāt saṃpūrṇa aṅgaḥ avayavī na gṛhyeta sakṛt gṛhyate ca na api guṇa ādimān gṛhyeta viṣāṇī gauḥ iti buddhyā viṣāṇa viśiṣṭaḥ gauḥ viṣayīkṛtaḥ na tu anye guṇa karma sāmānya ādayaḥ tatas ca nīla ādi rūpam guṇaḥ parispanda ādi ca karmma vastu tva ādi ca sāmānyam na gṛhyeta dṛṣṭa viruddhañca etat 
[187,i_187,iii]	sarveṣām guṇa karmma sāmānya avayava ādīnām vastutas viśeṣaṇa tvāt sarva grahaṇam iti ced āha vivakṣā paratantra tvāt viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ yad aṅga bhāvena upāttantattena eva hi gṛhyate viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ vivakṣā paratantra tvān puruṣa icchā anurodhāt na pāramārthika tvam tathā viṣāṇī gauḥ iti goḥ viṣāṇam ityādau viparyayaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ prayoktuḥ icchā vaśena dṛśyate tasmāt yat eva hi aṅga bhāvena viśeṣaṇa bhāvena sva manīṣikayā pratipādayitra upāttam tena eva viśeṣaṇena viśiṣṭam tad vivakṣitam gṛhyate na tad itaraiḥ teṣām avivakṣita tvena avivakṣita tvāt tatas ca na saṃpūrṇṇa aṅgaḥ na api guṇa ādimān gṛhyeta 
[187,iv_187,vi^1]	kiñca svatas vastu antarā bhedāt guṇa ādeḥ bhedakasya ca agrahāt eka buddhiḥ syāt paśyatā upi para aparam guṇa ādi bheda grahaṇāt nānātva pratipad yadi astu nāma tathā api eṣām bhavet sambandhi saṃkaraḥ vastunaḥ svatas vastu antarāt bheda abhāvāt vadanti hi svatas hi na gauḥ nāgaurggo tva yogāt gauḥ tathā svatas hi śuklaḥ na aśuklaḥ śukla tva yogāt śuklaḥ ityādi bhedakasya ca guṇa ādeḥ agrahāt padārthaiḥ saha tatas ca parāparam artha jātam paśyatā upi eka padārtha tva buddhiḥ syāt na hi dravyāṇām anyonyasya bhedakāḥ guṇa jāti ādayaḥ taiḥ saha gṛhyante yena bheda buddhiḥ syāt dravye gṛhīte paścāt guṇa ādīnām bhedānām viśeṣāṇām nānā tva grahaṇam dravyāṇām yadi iṣyate astu nāma paścāt guṇa ādi grahaṇam tathā api eṣām guṇa karmma sāmāni ādīnām sambandhinaḥ sāṃkaryam syāt svatas hi dravyam bhedāt na upalabhyate
[187,vi^2]	 paścāt upalabhyamānaiḥ tu guṇa ādibhiḥ saṃbandhi tayā avagataiḥ bhedena tat vyavasthāpanīyam tatas ca ekatra eka dravye guṇa ādayaḥ sambandhi tayā pratīyeran bhinna deśānām guṇānām bhinna deśeṣu yojanāt na sambandhi sāṃkaryam iti ced na deśa bhedasya api viśeṣaṇa tvāt sa upyekasya iti syāt ekasya viruddha dharma ayogāt pratīyamāna arthāḥ paścāt pratīyamānairūpa ādhibhiḥ bhinnāḥ vyavasthāpyante iti ced nanu evam api svatas arthānām bheda abhāvāt bheda nibandhanaiḥ ca upādhibhiḥ saha vedanā bhāvāt na adhyakṣa siddhā bheda vyavasthitiḥ syāt kintu viruddha upādhi sambandhāni atha anupapattyā kalpanīyā tathā ca pratyakṣa virodhaḥ 
[188,i]	atha dṛṣṭerthe paścāttanam adhyakṣam upādhi grāhakam tān yojayet bheda grāhakam katham adṛśyamāne yojana upādhīnām pratyakṣa kṛtā vikalpa kṛtā eva tu syāt tathā ca vyaktam na bheda darśanam syāt vikalpa viṣayasya asphuṭa tvāt ṛṣṭe arthe paścāt upādhiḥ pratīyamānaḥ tasya eva dṛṣṭaḥ iti ced tasya iti kim ucyate na tāvat anekāsu upādhi grahaṇāt pūrvam aneka tvasya apratīteḥ ekam ced katham upādhibhiḥ bhedanīyam anavadhṛta eka aneka bhāvam vastu mātram tat iti ced tatra tarhi deśa bhedāt aya upi upādhayaḥ paścāt upalabhyamānāḥ yojyante tad anantaram dṛṣṭa tvāt tatas ca anivāryaḥ sambandhi saṃkara prasaṅgaḥ 
[188,ii_188,iv]	sāṃkhyamatepi śabda ādīnām aneka tvāt siddhoneka grahaḥ sakṛt sanniveśa graha ayogāt agrahe sanniveśinām śabda ādīnām sukha duḥkha moha ātmaka tayā aneka tvāt śabda ādi grahe sakṛt aneka grahaḥ siddhaḥ saṃnniveśinām agrahe sanniveśasya graha ayogāt na hi aṅguli agrahaṇe muṣṭi grahaṇam 
[188,v_189,i]	yadi pratyakṣam avikalpam tadā katham dharmma dharmmyādi grahaṇam iti āha sarvatas vinivṛttasya vinivṛttiḥ yatas yatas tat bheda unnīta bhedā sā dharmmiṇaḥ aneka rūpa tā sarvatas parasmāt vinivṛttasya arthasya yatas yatas parasmāt vinivṛttaḥ taiḥ bhedaiḥ vyāvṛttibhiḥ unnītā sā aneka rūpa tā dharmmi dharmma ātmaka tayā dharmmiṇaḥ arthasya sarvaṃtas vyāvṛtte pratyakṣeṇa gṛhīte vastuni tad vyāvṛtti anukāriṇaḥ vikalpāḥ pratyakṣa dṛṣṭa tvena dharmmi dharmma bhāvam vyavasthāpayanti iti pratyakṣa kṛtaḥ saḥ ucyate na tu pratyakṣa pratibhāsamāna tvāt 
[189,ii_189,iv]	tathā hi te kalpitāḥ rūpa bhedāt nirvikalpasya cetasaḥ na vicitrasya citra ābhāḥ kādācid kasya gocaraḥ te dharmi dharma ādayaḥ rūpa bhedāt buddhi ākāra viśeṣā vijātīya vyāvṛtti āśrayeṇa kalpitā vicitra ābhāḥ vastu bala bhāvi tvāt kādācid kasya vicitrasya dharmmi dharmma bheda pratibhāsa rahitasya nirvikalpasya cetasaḥ pratyakṣasya na gocaraḥ pratyakṣam hi vastu sāmarthya utpannam tat ākāram anukuryāt na vikalpitam 
[189,v_189,vii]	bhavatu vā vastu eva sāmānyam tathā api na asau śabda vikalpa viṣayaḥ iti āha yadi api asti sita tva ādi yādṛś indriya gocaraḥ na sobhidhīyate śabdaiḥ jñānayoḥ rūpa bhedataḥ yadi api sita tva ādi sāmānyam asti paṭa ādau dharmmiṇi yādṛś sita tva ādi viśat ākāraḥ indriyasya gocaraḥ saḥ indriya jñāna gocaraḥ arthaḥ abhidhīyate na śabdaiḥ jñānayoḥ indriya śabda janitayaḥ rūpasya ākārasya sphuṭa asphuṭa tvena bhedataḥ
[189,viii_189,ix]	eka artha tvepi buddhīnām nānā āśrayatayā sa ced śrotra ādi cittāni idānīm bhinna arthāni iti tad kutas buddhīnām indriya śabda janitānām ekārtha tve eka viṣaya tvepi nānā āśrayatayā kāraṇa bheda ātmakasya ākāra bhedaḥ ced idānīm evam sthitau śrotra ādi indriya cittā nibhinna arthāni śabda rūpa gandha ādi bhinna viṣayāṇi iti vyapadiśyake tat kutas pramāṇāt avadhāritam tāni api citā anyabhinna viṣaya tvepi indriyāṇām āśraya bhūtānām bhedāt bhinna ākārāṇi iti kin na kalpyate 
[190,i_190,iii]	kiñca jātaḥ nāma āśrayonyonyaḥ cetasām tasya vastunaḥ ekasya eva kutas rūpam bhinna ākāra avabhāsi tat sāmānya ādi cetasām āśrayaḥ kāraṇam indriyam śabdaḥ ca iti anyonyaḥ nāma jātaḥ tathā pi sāmānya ādeḥ vastunaḥ ekasya eva rūpam tat kutas bhinna ākāra avabhāsi sphuṭa asphuṭa avabhāsi sphuṭa asphuṭa pratibhāsam na hi svarūpeṇa bhāsamānam ekam bhinna pratibhāsam yuktam 
[190,iv_190,v]	yat api ucyate paraiḥ śābda indriya jñānayoḥ yādi na eka viṣaya tvam tadā viṣāṇa ādimantam artham gauḥ iti śabdāt pratītya kāla antare vyakti viśeṣam dṛṣṭavataḥ ayam asau śabdāt prāk mayā pratītaḥ gauḥ iti pratyabhijñānam ekatā adhya vasāyi yat utpadyate tat na syāt iti tatra āha vṛtteḥ dṛśya aparāmarśena abhidhāna vikalpayoḥ darśanāt pratyabhijñānam gavā ādīnām nivāritam 
[190,vi]	abhidhāna vikalpayoḥ dṛ śyasya adhyakṣa viṣayasya aparāmarśena viṣayīkaraṇena vṛtteḥ paścāt darśanāt saḥ eva ayam śabda nirdiṣṭaḥ gauḥ iti pratya bhijñānam gavā ādīnām yat iṣyate tat nivāritam boddhavyam indriya śabda jñānayoḥ bhinna ākāra tvena eva viṣayat tva abhāvāt katham tad eka tā vyavasāyi vastu viṣayam syāt 
[190,vii_190,viii]	anvayāt ca anumānam yat abhidhāna vikalpayoḥ dṛśye gavā ādau jāti ādeḥ tat api etena dūṣitam yat ca dṛśye gavā ādau aneka tra abhinna ākārayoḥ abhidhāna vikalpayoḥ anvayāt anuvṛtteḥ jāti ādeḥ anumānam paraiḥ ucyate tat api etena abhidhāna vikalpayoḥ dṛśya tva aparāmarśena hetunā dūṣitam boddhavyam na hi anvayinau api śabda vikalpau vastu spṛśataḥ tat katham tābhyām vastunaḥ sāmānyasya siddhiḥ 
[190,ix_191,iii]	yadi na asti sāmānyam tathā katham astu pratyabhijñānam iti āha darśanāni eva bhinnāni api ekām kurvanti kalpanām pratyabhijñāna saṃkhyātām svabhāvena iti varṇitam darśanāni indriya jñānāni eva bhinnāni nānā kṣaṇa viṣayāṇi anekāni api svabhāvena pratyabhijñāna kāraṇa svarūpeṇa sva kāraṇa prasūtena kalpanā ātmeka tva adhyavasāyinīm pratyabhijñāna saṃkhyātām pratyabhijñāna nāmnā prasiddhām kurvanti iti varṇṇitam prāk tasmāt sthitam etat pratyakṣam anirdeśya tvāt avikalpam iti uktam indriya pratyakṣam 
[191,iv_191,vi]	mānasam ākhyātum āha tat ca indriya jñāna anantaram iṣṭam tena saha eka viṣayam bhinna viṣayam vā syāt ubhayathā api tu doṣaḥ iti āha pūrva anubhūta grahaṇe mānasasya apramāṇa tā adṛṣṭa grahaṇa indha ādeḥ api syāt artha darśanam pūrva anubhūtasya indriya jñāna gṛhītasya grahaṇe mānasasya svīkriyamāṇe apramāṇa tā syāt ajñāta artha prakāśasya pramāṇa tvāt indriya jñāna adṛṣṭasya grahaṇe punar iṣyamāṇe andha ādeḥ api syāt arthasya rūpa ādeḥ darśanam 
[191,vii_191,ix]	indriya jñāna anubhūta viṣaya tvepi dvau vikalpau saḥ arthaḥ kṣaṇikaḥ na vā kṣaṇika tvāt atītasya darśane ca na sambhavaḥ vācya makṣaṇika tve syāt lakṣaṇam sa viśeṣaṇam prathama pakṣaḥ indriya jñāna viṣayasya arthasya pūrva kālasya sahabhuvaḥ vā kṣaṇika tvāt atītasya naṣṭasya mānasena darśane darśanasya ca na sambhavosti akṣaṇika tve vai adhigata artha adhigantṛ tvādapramāṇam syāt atha mānasam adhigata artha adhigantṛ pramāṇam iṣyate tadā api mānasasya sa viśeṣaṇam lakṣaṇam vācyam syāt yathā adhigata viṣaya tvepi kalpanā apoḍham abhrānta mānasam pratyakṣam iti 
[192,i_192,iii]	kiñca niṣpādita kriye kiñcid viśeṣam asamādadhat karmmaṇi aindriyam anyat vā sādhanam kim iti iṣyate niṣpāditā kriyā yasmin tatra karmaṇi viśeṣam kañcid asamādadhat aindriyam indriya jñānam anyat vā paraśu ādi sādhanam kim iti iṣyate kriyā nirvartanam hi sādhana vyāpāraḥ tat ced niṣpannam kim anyat kurvat tat sādhanam syāt 
[192,iv_192,vi]	api ca sakṛt bhāvaḥ ca sarvāsām dhiyām tad bhāva janmanām anyaiḥ akārya bhedasya tad apekṣā virodhataḥ tasmāt sthirāt bhāvāt janma yāsāntāsām sarvāsām dhiyām sakṛt bhāvaḥ ca syāt na krama bhāvaḥ krami sahakārī apekṣayā krameṇa sthira upyarthaḥ karoti buddhīḥ iti ced atas anyaiḥ saha kāribhiḥ akāryaḥ bhedaḥ viśeṣaḥ yasya sthira eka rūpasya tasya tad apekṣāyāḥ virodhataḥ 
[192,vii_192,ix]	yatas evam tasmāt indriya vijñāna antara pratyaya udbhavaḥ manonyam eva gṛhṇāti viṣayam na andhadṛś tatas tasmāt indriya vijñānam eva anantara pratyayaḥ tasmāt udbhavaḥ yasya tad manaḥ mānasam pratyakṣam indriya pratyakṣa grāhyāt viṣayāt anyam eva viṣayam gṛhṇāti tatas indriya jñāna janya tvāt mānasasya andhānām cakṣuḥ vijñāna vikalānām dṛś darśanam rūpasya na bhavati gṛhīta grāhi tvam ca viṣaya antara grahaṇāt apāstam 
[192,x_192,xii]	yadi anya viṣaya grāhakam mānasam tadā bhūta bhaviṣyat grāhakam api syāt iti āha sva artha anvaya artha apekṣā eva hetuḥ indriya jā matiḥ tatonya grahaṇepyasya niyata grāhyatā matā sva arthaḥ svakīyaḥ viṣayaḥ tasmāt anvaye utpādaḥ yasya arthasya tad apekṣā eva indriya jā matiḥ manaḥ vijñānasya hetuḥ iṣyate tatas anyasya viṣayasya grahaṇepi manaḥ vijñānasya iṣyamāṇe niyata indriya jñāna grāhya upādeya kṣaṇaḥ eva grāhyaḥ yasya tad bhāvaḥ niyata grāhya tā sā matā 
[193,i_193,iii]	nanu sva jñānena sva ālambana jñānena ekakālikaḥ tulya kālikorthaḥ tad atulya kriyā kālaḥ katham sva jñāna kālikaḥ sahakārī bhavet arthaḥ iti ced akṣa cetasaḥ tena sahakāri sammata indriya jñānena atulyaḥ kriyā kālaḥ yasya bhinna kāla tvāt saḥ arthaḥ sahakārī katham akṣa cetasaḥ bhavet iti ced 
[193,iv_193,vi]	atra āha asataḥ prāc asāmarthyāt paścāt ca anupayogataḥ prāgbhāvaḥ sarva hetūnām na atorthaḥ sva dhiyā saha kārya utpatteḥ prāc asataḥ tatra asāmarthyāt sat adhiṣṭhānam hi sāmarthyam asataḥ katham syāt kārya utpatteḥ paścāt sataḥ kāraṇa vyāpārāt vā paścāt kārya sama kālasya sataḥ vā tatra anupayogataḥ vyāpāra abhāvāt kāryāt prāgbhāvaḥ sarva hetūnām iti sthitam viṣayaḥ ca jñānānām na akāraṇa m ati prasaṅgāt atas viṣayaḥ kāraṇa ātmakaḥ sva dhiyā sva ālambana dhiyā saha na bhavati pūrva bhāvi tve ca viṣayasya tad kāla indriya jñāna sahakāritā yuktimatī 
[193,vii_193,ix]	nanu bhinna kālam katham grāhyam iti ced grāhyatām viduḥ hetu tvam eva yukti jñāḥ jñāna ākāra arpaṇa kṣamam prāgbhāva bhāvi tvāt bhinna kālam vastu katham grāhyam iti ced hetu tvam eva jñāne akārasya sva anurūpasya arpaṇakṣaṇam grāhyatām yukti jñāḥ viduḥ na hi saṃdaṃśa ayogolayoḥ iva jñāna padārthayoḥ grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ kathantarhi yat ākāram anukaroti tat grāhyasya grāhakam iti ucyate 
[193,x_193,xii]	nanu yadi kāraṇam grāhyaṃtadā samanantara pratyaya ādikam ca tathā syāt iti āham kāryam hi aneka hetu tve api anukurvat udeti yat tat tena api atra tad rūpam gṛhītam iti ca ucyate kāryam hi jñānam aneka hetu tve api yad kāraṇam ākāra dvāreṇa anukurvat udeti tad kāraṇam arpi tad rūpam uparopita sva ākāram tena kāraṇa ākāreṇa gṛhītam iti ca ucyate yathā pitṛ rūpam putreṇa gṛhītam iti kathyate uktam mānasam 
[194,i_194,iv]	sva samvedanam ākhyātum āha aśakya samayaḥ hi ātmā rāga ādīnām ananya bhāj teṣām atas sva saṃvittiḥ nnābhi jalpa anuṣaṅgiṇī rāga dveṣa sukha duḥkha ādīnām sarva citta caittānām ātma saṃvedanam pratyakṣam avikalpa tvāt tathā hi rāga ādīnām ātmā sva rūpam ananya bhāj na anyam bhajate sva rūpa mātra avasthiteḥ tasmāt aśakyaḥ samayaḥ saṃketaḥ asmin atas saṃketa aviṣaya tvāt teṣām rāga ādīnām svasya ātmanaḥ samvittiḥ prakāśaḥ abhijalpaḥ vācaka śabda ullekhaḥ tad anuṣaṅgaḥ yasya asti sā tathā na bhavati vācyam hi vācakena saṃyojyeta na ca rāga ādi ātmā vācyaḥ tatas tad prakāśaḥ na śabda saṃgataḥ 
[194,v_194,ix]	avedakāḥ parasya api te svarūpam katham viduḥ nanu rāga sukha ādayaḥ ātma guṇāḥ parasya bāhyasya api avedana aṅga jñāta tvāt te svarūpam katham viduḥ vedakasya kadācid sva vedanam saṃbhāvyeta avedakam ca na kvacid upayogi yadi na sva vedanā rāga ādayaḥ tadā katham vedayantaḥ iti āha eka artha āśrayiṇā vedyā vijñānena iti kecana ekorthaḥ ātmā āśrayaḥ rāga ādibhiḥ saha yasya asti tena eka artha āśrayiṇā jñānena vedyā rāga ādayaḥ iti kecana naiyāyika ādayaḥ 
[194,x_195,ii]	atra āha tat atad rūpiṇaḥ bhāvaḥ tad atad rūpa hetu jāḥ tad sukha ādi kim ajñānam vijñāna abhinna hetu jam tad rūpiṇaḥ vivakṣita eka rūpavantaḥ atad rūpiṇaḥ itara rūpavantaḥ bhāvāḥ yathākramam tad rūpāt dṛṣṭa eka rūpāt hetoḥ sāmagrī lakṣaṇāt jātāḥ atad rūpa hetu jātāḥ vilakṣaṇa sāmagrī jātāḥ bhavanti iti tāvat sthitam tat tasmāt imam nyāyam ullaṅghya vijñānena saha abhinnaḥ ekaḥ hetuḥ indriya viṣaya manaskāra ādi sāmagrī lakṣaṇaḥ tasmāt jātam sukha ādikam kasmāt ajñānam samāna sāmagrī prasūta tvāt dvayam api jñānam syāt na vā kiñcid 
[195,iii_195,v]	abhinna hetuka tām eva samarthayitum āha sārthe sati indriye yogye yathāsvam api cetasi dṛṣṭam janma sukha ādīnām tad tulyam manasām api yasya yat ā ātmīyam janakam tasmin indriye sārthe sa viṣaye yogye kārya utpādanam prati cetasi samanantara pratyaye sati sukha ādīnām api janma dṛṣṭam tat yathāsvam indriya ādiṣu yogyeṣu satsu janma darśanam manasām jñānānām api tulyam atas tulya hetuka tvāt tulya jātīya tā eva yuktā na anyathā kvacid ekatā syāt 
[195,vi_195,viii]	tulya hetuka tvepi saṃskāra ādeḥ niyāmaka tvāt sukha ādikam ajñānam syāt iti āha asatsu satsu ca eteṣu na janma ajanma vā kvacid dṛṣṭam sukha ādeḥ buddheḥ vā tat tatas na anyatas ca te asatsu indriya ādiṣu duḥkha ādeḥ buddheḥ vā janma na kvacid iṣṭam satsu ca eteṣu indriya ādiṣu ajanma vā sukha ādeḥ bbuddheḥ vā na kvacid dṛṣṭam tat tasmāt tatas indriya ādeḥ dṛṣṭa sāmarthyāt kāraṇāt te sukha buddhī jāyete anyatas saṃskāra ādeḥ na te tasya sāmarthya adarśanāt 
[195,ix_195,xi]	nanu abhinna hetuka tve sukha duḥkha ādi bhedaḥ ca na syāt iti āha sukha duḥkha ādi bhedaḥ ca teṣām eva viśeṣataḥ tasyāḥ eva yathā buddheḥ mmāndya pāṭava saṃśrayāḥ sukha duḥkha ādi bhedaḥ ca avāntaraḥ teṣām indriya ādīnām eva hetūnām viśeṣataḥ avāntarāt yathā tasyāḥ buddheḥ eva antara hetu viśeṣāt māndya pāṭava saṃśrayāḥ paraspara saṃbhavinaḥ bhavanti tasmāt sukha ādayaḥ vijñānena abhinna hetuka tvāt vijñāna svabhāvāḥ eva iti sthitam 
[196,i_196,iii]	idānīm para vedya tām eṣām niṣeddhum āha yasya arthasya nipātena te jātāḥ dhī sukha ādayaḥ muktvā tam pratipadyeta sukha ādīn eva sā katham yasya arthasya strī ādeḥ nipātena sannidhānena te dhī sukha ādayaḥ jātāḥ tam kāraṇa bhūtam ākāra arpaṇa kṣamam muktvā sukha ādīn eva saha bhāvinaḥ viṣaya lakṣaṇa rahitān sā buddhiḥ katham pratipadyeta akāraṇasya viṣaya tva iti prasaṅgāt 
[196,iv_196,v]	avichinnā atha bhāseta tad saṃvittiḥ krama grahe tad lāghava āt ced tad tuli abhitya saṃvedanam na kim atha indriya jñānena viṣaya grahaḥ tad anantaram mānasādhyakṣeṇa sukha ādi grahaḥ iti krama grahe svīkriyamāṇe tayoḥ viṣaya sukhayoḥ saṃvittiḥ avicchinnā yaugapadyena na bhāseta asti ca yugapad pratibhāsaḥ parisphuṭaḥ tayoḥ bbāhya sukha grāhi manasoḥ lāghavāt yaugapadya pratibhāsaḥ ced tad lāghavam pratikṣaṇam ekaika tva saṃvedana abhāvasya api tulyam iti asamvedanam eva sāhityasya kim na bhavati 
[196,vi_196,xi]	indriya buddhyā eva ekayā bāhya sukhayoḥ sakṛt grahaṇam iti ced āha na ca ekayā dvaya jñānam niyamāt akṣa cetasaḥ na ca ekayā dvayasya jñānam saṃbhavati akṣa cetasoḥ bbāhya rūpa ādi grahaṇaḥ eva niyamā nniyata tvāt sukhā dyātma guṇa grahaṇa abhāvāt kiñca sukha ādi abhāva ipi arthāt ca jāteḥ tad śakti asiddhitaḥ na akāraṇam viṣayaḥ sukha ādi abhāvepi kevalāt arthāt indriya buddheḥ jāteḥ utpādāt tasya sukha ādeḥ indriya buddhi jananam prati śakti asiddheḥ aviṣaya tvam 
[196,xii_197,iii]	pṛthak pṛthak ca sāmarthye dvayoḥ nīla ādi vat sukham gṛhyeta kevalam dvayoḥ rūpi sukha ādyoḥ pṛthak pṛthak jñāna upapattau sāmarthye vā abhyupagamyamāne nīla ādi vat kevalam sukham gṛhyeta ayuktam ca etat tasya tad hetu artham agṛhṇataḥ na hi tasya sukha ādeḥ hetum artham strī ādim agṛhṇataḥ 
[197,iv_197,vii]	na hi saṃvedanam yuktam arthena eva saha grahe sukhasya saṃvedanam yuktam arthena eva saha sukhasya indriya dhiyā grahe na asti doṣaḥ iti ced na kim sāmarthyam sukha ādīnām na iṣṭā dhīryat tat udbhavā sukha ādeḥ indriya buddhi janane kim asti sāmarthyam yena tasyāḥ sa viṣayaḥ san saha gṛhyeta yadi asmāt tat udbhavā sukhāt udbhavā na indriya dhīriṣṭā tasmāt na tad grāhikā 
[197,viii_197,ix]	vinā arthena sukha ādīnām vedane cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ rūpa ādiḥ strī ādi bhedaḥ akṣṇā na gṛhyeta kadācana tatas ca katham artha sukhayoḥ saha vedanam arthena vinā eva cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ cakṣuḥ ādi jñānaiḥ sukha ādīnām vedane ca abhyupagamyamāne strī ādeḥ bhedaḥ viśeṣaḥ rūpa ādiḥ sukha hetuḥ akṣṇā cakṣuḥ jñānena na kadācana gṛhyeta 
[197,x_197,xii]	kasmāt evam iti āha na hi sati antaraṅgerthe śakte dhīḥ bāhya darśanaḥ artha grahe sukha ādīnām tad jānām syāt avedanam antaraṅge sannihite arthe kṣetrajña samavete sukha ādau śakte sva grāhi jñāna utpādana kṣame sati na hi bāhya darśanī dhīḥ artha grāhiṇī yuktā bahiraṅgaḥ bāhyorthaḥ indriya āloka ādi sahakāryapekṣaṇāt sukha ādiḥ tu na tad sāpekṣaḥ iti tasmāt jātāḥ dhīḥ tam eva gṛhṇīyāt indriya dhiyā artha grahe svīkriyamāṇe sukha ādīnām tad jānām artha darśana prasūtānām artham avedanam syāt indriya buddhiḥ artha grahaḥ eva upayuktā tad kālam anyā ca dhīḥ na asti paścāt jñāna antara kāle viṣaya bala bhāvinaḥ sukha ādeḥ abhāvaḥ iti katham vedanam 
[197,xiii_198,i]	dhiyoḥ yugapad utpattau tad tad viṣaya sambhavāt sukha duḥkha vidau syātām sakṛt arthasya sambhave viṣaya sukha grāhiṇyoḥ dvayoḥ indriya buddhi manaḥ buddhi ātmikayoḥ tasya sukha hetoḥ duḥkha hetoḥ ca viṣayasya sambhavāt yugapad utpattau abhimatāyām sakṛt arthasya sukha duḥkha hetoḥ sambhave sati sukha duḥkha vidau syātām 
[198,ii_198,iv]	syāt etat satya antarepi upādāne jñāne duḥkha ādi sambhavaḥ na upādānam viruddhasya tat ca ekam iti ced matam na kevalam arthe sati kintarhya antare samanantara pratyaye jñānaḥ upādāne sati duḥkha ādi saṃbhavaḥ tat ca upādāna apekṣam jñānam viruddhasya sukha duḥkha ādeḥ na kāraṇam bhavitum arhati iti matam ced 
[198,v_198,vii]	atra āha tad ajñānasya vijñānam kena upādāna kāraṇam ādhipatyam tu kurvīta tad viruddhepi dṛśyate tat vijñānam ajñānasya sukha duḥkha ādeḥ upādāna kāraṇam kena hetunā sammatam samāna jātīyam kāraṇam upādānam na anyat na ca sukha ādi jñānām iṣṭam jñānam ajñāna kārye ādhipatyam sahakāri tvam kurvīta tad ādhipatyam viruddhepi kārye dṛśyate 
[198,viii_198,ix]	akṣṇoḥ yathā ekaḥ ālokaḥ naktañcara tadanyayoḥ rūpa darśana vaiguṇya avaiguṇye kurute sakṛt yathā ekaḥ ālokaḥ naktaṃcarasya manuṣya ādeḥ akṣṇaḥ rūpa darśanasya vaiguṇya avaiguṇye yathākramam sakṛt kurute 
[198,x_198,xi]	tasmāt sukha ādayorthānām sva saṃkrānta avabhāsinām vedakāḥ sva ātmanaḥ ca eṣām arthebhyaḥ janma kevalam yasmāt anyena sukha ādīnām vedanam na ghaṭate tasmāt sukha ādayaḥ jñāna ātmānaḥ svasmin svarūpe pratibandha dvāreṇa saṃkrānta avabhāsana śīlāḥ ca ye arthānām teṣām vedakāḥ ātmanaḥ ca aparokṣa tvāt vedakāḥ artha sarūpasya ātmanaḥ aparokṣatā eva artha vedanam sva vedanañca na tu anyaḥ kaścid grahaṇa prakāraḥ tatas ca eṣām sukha ādīnām artha sarūpāṇām arthebhyaḥ janma eva kevalam grahītṛ tvam na aparaḥ kaścid vyāpāraḥ 
[199,i_199,ii]	artha ātmā sva ātma bhūtaḥ hi teṣām taiḥ anubhūyate tena artha anubhava khyātiḥ ālambaḥ tu tad ābhatā atas eva artha anubhavaḥ katham sva vedanam artha jñānayoḥ bhedāt tad vedanayoḥ ca bhedasya nyāya prāpta tvāt iti bruvāṇaḥ pratikṣiptaḥ tathā hi teṣām sukha ādīnām artha ātmā artha ākāraḥ pratibimba saṃkrāntyā sva ātma bhūtaḥ svabhāva bhūtaḥ taiḥ sukha ādibhiḥ anubhūyate aparokṣa tvāt tena upacāreṇa arthasya para bhūtasya pratibimba hetoḥ anubhavasya khyātiḥ prasiddhiḥ tatas ca jñānasya ālambaḥ artha ālambanam tad ābhatā artha ākāra tvam vicāryamāṇam avaśiṣyate na tu pāramārthika mālam vyālambaka tvam nāma 
[199,iii_199,v]	idānīm sāṃkhya matam utthāpayan āha kaścid bahis sthitān eva sukha ādīn apracetanān grāhyān āha na tasya api sakṛt yuktaḥ dvaya grahaḥ kaścid bahis sthitān eva na tu ātma samavāyinaḥ pradhāna pariṇāma ja tvena sukha duḥkha moha svabhāva tvāt arthān apracetanāt ātmanaḥ eva cetana tvāt buddhi darpaṇe jaḍa ātmani svacche artha cetanayoḥ pratibimba saṃkrānti dvāreṇa cchāyā āpattyā cetanasya grāhyān āha tasya api mate dvayasya sukhasya nīla ādeḥ ca sakṛt grahaḥ niyamena na yuktaḥ kadācid rūpa nirapekṣam api rūpa sukham anubhūyeta 
[199,vi_199,vii]	sukha ādya bhinna rūpa tvāt na ulādeḥ ced sakṛt grahaḥ bhinna avabhāsinoḥ grāhyam cetasoḥ tad abhedi kim sukha ādeḥ abhinna rūpa tvāt nīla ādeḥ sakṛt niyamena grahaḥ ced bhinna avabhāsinoḥ bhinna ākārayoḥ sukha nīla cetasoḥ grāhyam tat kim abhedi iṣyate sukha duḥkha ādīnām nīla pīta ādīn āñca bhinna manaḥ grāhyānām eka tvam evam syāt 
[199,viii_199,x]	kiñca tasya aviśeṣe bāhyasya bhāvanā tāratamyataḥ tāratamyañca buddhau syāt na prīti paritāpayoḥ yadi nīla ādi eva sukha ādi ātmakam tadā tasya bāhyasya sukha duḥkha ādi ātma tayā aviśeṣe viśeṣa abhāve ruci aruci viṣaya tayā bhāvanāyāḥ tāratamyataḥ tāratamyañca buddhau prīti paritāpayoḥ na syāt na hi grāhyā viśeṣe tat jñānam viśiṣyate 
[199,xi_200,i]	sukha ādi ātma tayā buddheḥ api yadi avirodhitā saḥ idānīm katham bāhyaḥ sukha ādi ātmā iti gamyate buddheḥ api pradhāna pariṇāma rūpāyāḥ bhāvanā tāratamyāt sukha ādi ātma tā viśeṣāt bāhya aviśeṣepi prīti paritāpa tāratamyasya avirodhitā iṣyate yadi idānīm anya abhyupagame bāhyaḥ arthaḥ sa sukha ādi ātmā iti katham gamyate anubhūyamānam sukham anyatra asaṃbhavat bāhye vyavasthāpanīyam 
[200,ii_200,iii]	agrāhya grāhaka tvāt ced bhinna jātīyayoḥ pumān agrāhakaḥ syāt sarvasya tatas hīyeta bhoktṛtā yadā tu buddhiḥ api sukha ātmikā tadā kim bāhya sukha kalpanayā bāhya mahatoḥ asukha rūpa tvāt ca bhinna jātīyayoḥ grāhya grāhaka tva abhāvāt sukha ādi ātma tā bāhyasya gamyate iti ced pumān cetanaḥ nirguṇa tvāt asukha ādi rūpaḥ grāhyasya acetanasya sukha ādi ātmakasya sarvasya bhinna jātīya tvāt agrāhakaḥ syāt tatas agrāhaka tvāt bhoktṛtā asya hīyate anubhavitā hi bhoktā ucyate anubhava abhāve katham bhoktā 
[200,iv_200,v]	kārya kāraṇa tānena pratyuktā akārya kāraṇe grāhya grāhaka tā bhāvāt bhāvenyatra api sā bhavet buddhi sukhayoḥ grāhya grāhaka abhāvāt na akāraṇam viṣayaḥ iti kārya kāraṇa tā tatas grāhyasya sukha ādi ātmaka tvāt tad kāryayā buddhyā api sukha ādi ātmikayā bhavitavyam iti paraiḥ uktā kārya kāraṇa tā sā anena atiprasaṅgena pratyuktā tathā hi bhoktā api grāhakaḥ iti sa ca kārya sukha ādi ātmakaḥ katham syāt api ca akārya kāraṇe buddhi sukhe grāhya grāhaka tāyāḥ kārya kāraṇa tā nibandhanāyāḥ abhāvāt grāhya grāhaka tva bhāvāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya ca bhāve abhyupagamyamāne anyatra ātma viṣayayoḥ api sā kārya kāraṇa tā syāt grāhya grāhaka tāyāḥ bhāvāt 
[201,i_201,vi]	yasmāt sukha ādeḥ bbāhyasya bhāvanātaḥ tāratamya anuyoga yogaḥ tasmāt te āntarāḥ eva tasmāt asukha ādayaḥ āntarāḥ jñāna svabhāvāḥ abāhyāḥ abhyupagantavyāḥ kiñca samvedya tvāt ca cetanāḥ saṃvedanam na yat rūpam na hi tat tasya vedanam samvedya tvāt ca hetoḥ te cetanāḥ tathā hi samvedanam tad rūpam yat viṣaya svarūpam na bhavati tad saṃvedanam tasya viṣayasya vedanam yasmāt na bhavati na hi aviṣaya svarūpam prativiṣayam bheda vyavasthām karttum arhati iti sa ākāram grāhakam tathā ca sa ākāram jñānam eva sukham astu tad upadhāyakam tu bāhyam ayuktam bhāvanā viśeṣeṇa sukha ādi vedanasya aviśeṣa darśanāt bāhya adhīna tve ca tad ayogāt 
[201,vii_201,ix]	syāt etat atad svabhāvaḥ anubhavaḥ bauddhān tān san ava eti ced muktvā adhyakṣa smṛta ākārām saṃvittim buddhiḥ atra kā bhāvanātaḥ tāratamya yoginaḥ tān buddhi ātmaka sukha ādīn atad svabhāvaḥ asukhya ādi ākāraḥ anubhavaḥ san ava eti pratyeti iticet saṃvitti madhyakṣākārām harṣa viṣāda ākārām smṛta ākārām atīta sukha ādi kalpanā rūpām saumanasya lakṣaṇām muktvā atra saṃvedana avasare kā parā buddhiḥ anubhūyate yasyāḥ sukha ādi ātmaka tva madhyavasāya ātmaka tvañcā iṣyate 
[201,x_201,xi]	tān tān arthān upādāya sukha duḥkha ādi vedanam ekam āvirbhavat dṛṣṭam na dṛṣṭam tu anyat antarā tān tān artha aniṣṭān aniṣṭān upādāya aśritya ekam sukha duḥkha ādi vedanam āvirbhavat dṛṣṭam anyat buddhi rūpam antarā viṣaya saṃvedanayoḥ antarāle na dṛṣṭam 
[201,xii_201,xiii]	saṃsargāt avibhāgaḥ ced ayaḥ golaka vahni vat bheda abheda vyavasthā evam ucchinnā sarva vastuṣu buddhi cetanayoḥ saṃsarggāt ayaḥ golaka vahnyoḥ iva avibhāgaḥ bhedān upalabdhiḥ iti ced evam bhinna ākāra anubhavepya bheda kalpanāyāṃsarva vastuṣu bheda abheda vyavasthā ucchinnā syāt 
[202,i_202,iii]	tathā hi abhinna vedanasya aikyam yat na evam tat vibheda vat sidhyet asādhana tvesya na siddham bheda sādhanam abhinnam eka ākāram vedanam yasya tasya aikyam yat na evam bhinna vedanam tat vibheda vat sidhyet asya eka ākāra jñānasya abhedam prati asādhana tve tad viparīta bhinna ākāra vedanam bheda sādhanam asiddham 
[202,iv_202,v]	bhinna ābhaḥ sita duḥkha ādiḥ abhinnaḥ buddhi vedane abhinna ābhe vibhinne ced bheda abhedau kim āśrayau sāṃkhyasya tu sita duḥkha ādiḥ bhinna ākāraḥ abhinnaḥ iṣṭaḥ buddhi vedane tu abhinna ābhe vibhinne iṣṭe ced bheda abhedau kim āśrayau kim nimittau te vyavasthāpanīyau 
[202,vi_202,viii]	nanu vedanā cetanā saṃjñā ādīnām caittānām mahā bhūmikā ādīnām sakṛt utpannānām bhedaḥ parasparam pratīyate atha ca asti tadvat buddhi sukhayoḥ api syāt iti āha tiraskṛtānām paṭunā api ekadā abheda darśanāt pravāhe vitti bhedānām siddhā bheda vyavasthitiḥ paṭunā sukha duḥkha ādīnām vedanā skandha saṃgṛhītena caittena tiraskṛtānām abhibhūtānām saṃjñā ādīnām ekadā abheda darśanāt pravāhe citta santāne sukha ādya bhāva kāle sva rūpeṇa upalakṣitānām bheda vyavasthitiḥ siddhā raveḥ udaye tārakāḥ anupalakṣitāḥ api niśāyām upalakṣyamāṇāḥ bhedena vyavasthā apyante eva tasmāt jñāna ātmānaḥ sva vedanāḥ ca sukha ādayaḥ iti ākhyātam sva vedanam 
[202,ix_203,i]	yogi jñānam ākhyātum āha prāk uktam yoginām jñānam teṣām tat bhāvanā mayam vidhūta kalpanā jālam spaṣṭam eva avabhāsate prāk prathama paricchedeyoginām jñānam sattya viṣayam uktam teṣām yoginām bhāvanā mayam bhāvanā hetu niṣpattikam tat jñānam sattya svarūpa viṣaya tvena vidhūta kalpanā jālam avikalpa tvāt ca spaṣṭam viśada jñeya ākāram eva avabhāsate 
[203,ii_203,iv]	bhāvanā bhavam katham spaṣṭam iti āha kāma śoka bhaya unmāda caura sva prādi upaplutāḥ abhūtān api paśyanti pura tova sthitān iva kāmaḥ ca śokaḥ ca bhayañca taiḥ unmādāḥ caura svapna ādayaḥ ca iti kāma śoka bhaya unmāda caura svapna ādibhiḥ upaplutāḥ bhrāntāḥ te abhūtān api arthān bhāvanā vaśāt puratas avasthitān iva paśyanti yasmāt tad anurūpām pravṛttim ceṣṭante 
[203,v_203,x]	bhavatu bhāvanā jam spaṣṭam avikalpam tu katham iti āha na vikalpa anubaddhasya asti sphuṭa artha avabhāsitā na vikalpena anubaddhasya saṃstutasya jñānasya sphuṭa artha avabhāsitā asti nanu viplava vaśāt vikalpakam api svapne spaṣṭa ābham jñānam bhavati iti āha svapnepi smaryate smārttam na ca tat tādṛś arthavat svapnepi smārttam smaraṇam kiñcid utpadyate na ca tad prabodha avasthāyām tādṛś arthavat yādṛśaḥ nirvikalpena anubhūtaḥ arthaḥ tādṛśa arthena yuktam smaryate kintarhi aspaṣṭa artham eva svapna smaraṇam smaryate 
[203,xi_203,xiii]	nanu abhūta artha bhāvanā bala jam bhavatā api spaṣṭa ābham avikalpañca siddhānte na iṣyate iti tena saha virodhaḥ ityāḥ ha aśubhā pṛthivīkṛtsnā ādi abhūtam api varṇyate spaṣṭa ābham nirvikalpañca bhāvanā bala nirmitam aśubhā vinīlaka vipūyaka asthi saṃkala ādikā pṛthvīkṛtsnā ādi bhūmaya tva ādi abhūtam asatyam api bhāvanā balena nirmitam spaṣṭa ābham nirvikalpa kañcā asmābhiḥ varṇṇi ate iti na asti siddhānta virodhaḥ 
[204,i_204,ii]	tasmāt bhūtam abhūtam vā yat yat eva abhibhāvyate bhāvanā pariniṣpattau tat sphuṭa ākalpa dhī phalam yatas bhāvanāyāḥ bhāvya spaṣṭa tāyām ādhipatyam tasmāt bhūtam ārya satya ādi abhūtam aśubha ādi yat yat eva atyantam bhāvyate tat bhāvyamānam bhāvanāyāḥ sa ādara nirantara dīrgha kāla pravarttitāyāḥ pariniṣpattau sphuṭā kalpa dhīḥ sā phalam yasya tat tathā 
[204,iii_204,vi]	tatra pramāṇām samvādi yat prāk nirṇīta vastu vat tat bhāvanā jam pratyakṣam iṣṭam śeṣāḥ upaplavāḥ tatra bhāvanā bala bhāviṣu spaṣṭa aniḥ vikalpeṣu yat saṃvādi upadarśita artha prāpakam tat bhāvanā jam pratyakṣam pramāṇam iṣṭam kim iva iti āha prāk prathama paricchede nirṇṇītam vastu satya catuṣṭayam tasmin iva yathā ārya sattya viṣayam bhāvanā bala jam saṃvādi tvāt pratyakṣam pramāṇam evam anyat api īdṛśam śeṣāḥ ayathārthāḥ upaplavāḥ bhramāḥ yathā aśubhā pṛthvīkṛtsnā ādi pratyayāḥ 
[204,vii_204,ix]	kalpanā api sva saṃvitta āviṣṭā na arthe vikalpanāt iti vyākhyātum āha śabda artha grāhi yat yatra tat jñānam tatra kalpanā svarūpañca na śabda arthaḥ tatra adhyakṣam atas akhilam śabda artha grāhi anya vyavacchedasya grāhakam yat jñānam yatra viṣaye tat jñānam tatra kalpanā ucyate jñānānām svarūpañca sva lakṣaṇa ātmakam na śabdasya arthaḥ viṣayaḥ atas vācya tvāt tatra svarūpe akhilam jñānam avikalpa tvāt adhyakṣam uktam caturvidham pratyakṣam 
[204,x_205,i]	pratyakṣa ābhāsam idānīm vaktavyam trividham kalpanā jñānam āśraya upaplava udbhavam avikalpakam ekañca pratyajña ābham caturvidham trividham kalpanā jñānam pratyakṣa ābham marīcikāyām jalādhyavasāyi bhrānti jñānam saṃvṛtau vi saṃvādi vyavasāya sāṃvṛta jñānam pūrva dṛṣṭa eka tva kalpanā pravṛttam liṅga anumeya ādi jñānam avikalpa kañcaḥ ekam pratyakṣa ābham kīdṛśam āśrayasya indriyasya upaplavaḥ timirā dyupaghātaḥ tasmāt bhavaḥ yasya tat tathā evañca caturvidhañca pratyakṣa ābhāsam 
[205,ii_205,iii]	nanu avikalpakam pratyakṣam tatas trayam api idam sa vikalpaka tvāt ekaḥ pratyakṣa ābhāsaḥ tat kim bhrānti jñānam mṛgatṛṣṇikāyām jalāvasāyi saṃvṛti satas dravya ādeḥ jñānam anumānam liṅga jñānam ānumānikam liṅgi jñānam smārtta smṛtiḥ ābhilāpikam ca iti vikalpa prabhedaḥ ācārya dignāgena uktaḥ iti āha anakṣaja tu asiddhi artham ukte dve bhrānti daśanāt siddha anumādi vacanam sādhanāya eva pūrvayoḥ 
[205,iv]	dve sāṃvṛta āropitayoḥ kalpanā jñāne anakṣaja tvasya anindriya tvasya siddhi artham bhedena ukte pareṣām tayoḥ akṣa ja tva bhrānti darśanāt ghaṭoyam dvau kampate ityādi jalam idam iti ca vyavasāya ātmakam indriya pratyakṣam eva pratipadyate iti paraḥ manyate tad nirāḥ sārtham dvayoḥ upādānam anindriya tvena smṛti bala bhāvi tvena siddham ca tad anumā ādi ca tasya vacanam pūrvayoḥ saṃvṛta āropita kalpanayoḥ eva anakṣaja tu a sādhanāya tathā hi yat pūrva anubhūta samaya smṛti bhāvi na tat pratyakṣam yathā anumāna ādi anubhūta samaya smṛti sāpekṣā ca avayavi jala ādi kalpanā iti viruddha upalabdhiḥ uktā 
[205,v_205,vii]	nanu sāṃvṛta āropita kalpanāyāḥ katham pratyakṣatā āśaṅkā iti āha saṃketa saṃśraya anyārtha samāropa vikalpane na pratyakṣa anuvṛtti tvāt kadācid bhrānti kāraṇam bahūnām rūpa ādīnām ekārtha kāri tva khyāpana artham ghaṭaḥ ityādi śabda niveśaḥ sa saṃśrayaḥ hetuḥ yasyāḥ sā saṃketa saṃśraya ākalpanā dṛśyamānāt marīci nicaya ādeḥ anyasya jala ādeḥ āropitasya kalpanā anya artha kalpanā te ete kalpane pratyakṣa anantara bhāvi tvena pratyakṣa anuvṛtti tvāt ātmani api kadācid avimarśakānām pratyakṣatā bhrānti kāraṇam bhavataḥ 
[206,i_206,ii]	yathā eva iyam parokṣa artha kalpanā smaraṇa ātmikā samayā apekṣiṇī na artham pratyakṣam adhyavasyati atas yathā eva iyam anumāna anumānika ādi parokṣa artha kalpanā pūrvam gṛhīta samaya apekṣiṇī satī smaraṇa ādi rūpā pratyakṣam pratyakṣa viṣayam artham na adhyavasyati kintu kalpitam eva gṛhṇāti 
[206,iii_206,iv]	tathā anubhūta smaraṇam antareṇa ghaṭa ādiṣu na pratyayonuyan tat ca pratyakṣāt parihīyate tathā saṃketa kāle vyavahāra laghava artham kalpitasya dravya ādeḥ anumāna bhūtasya paścāt smaraṇam antareṇa ghaṭa ādiṣu ghaṭaḥ ayam ityādi eka vastu avasāyī pratyayaḥ na bhavati tat ca saṃketitam āropitam ca artham anuyan ghaṭaḥ ayam jalam iti ca pratyayaḥ pratyakṣāt pratyakṣa tvāt parihīyate tasya vastu viṣaya tvāt saṃketa apekṣasya ca viparyayāt 
[206,v_206,vi]	apavādaḥ caturthotra tena uktam upaghāta jam kevalantatra timiram upaghāta upalakṣaṇam sa taimiram iti caturthaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ kalpanā rahita tvena atiprasaktāyāḥ pratyakṣatāyāḥ apavādaḥ abhrānta tvasya lakṣaṇa eka deśa tva upalakṣaṇa tvam ca na tu kalpanā apoḍha tva nirākṛtasya udāharaṇam idam kevalam sa taimiram iti atra timiram sa bāhya upaghātasya jñāna vikṛti hetoḥ upalakṣaṇam tena anya indriya vikāra jam indriya jañca nirvikalpam pratyakṣa ābhāsam sidhyati 
[206,vii_206,viii]	mānasam tat api iti eke teṣām granthaḥ virudhyate nīla dvi candra ādi dhiyām hetu rakṣāṇi api iti ayam tat dvi candra ādi jñānam api mānasam manaḥ bhramaḥ iti eke ā cā ryāḥ teṣām evam vādinām nīla dvi candra ādidhiyām akṣāṇi api hetuḥ iti etad artha vācakaḥ granthaḥ virudhyate granthaḥ punar ayam yāvat cakṣuḥ ādīnām api ālambana tva prasaṅgaḥ tepi hi paramārthataḥ anyathā vidyamānāḥ nīla ādi ābhāsasya dvi candra ādi ābhāsasya ca jñānasya kāraṇībhavanti iti 
[207,i_207,iii]	syāt etat pāramparyeṇa hetuḥ ced indriya jñāna gocare vicāryamāṇe prastāvaḥ mānasasya iha kīdṛśaḥ mānasasya pratyakṣasya indriyam pāramparyeṇa hetuḥ tena virodha abhāvaḥ ced vāda vidhi prakaraṇe indriya jñānasya pratyakṣasya gocarevicāryamāṇe mānasasya vikalpasya iha avasare kīdṛśaḥ prastāvaḥ yena paramparayā tad hetuḥ indriyam ucyate 
[207,iv_207,v]	kim vaindriyam yat akṣāṇām bhāva abhāva anurodhi ced tad tulyam vikriyāvat ced sā eva iyam kim niṣidhyate timira jñānam bhramam anicchatā upi kim kīdṛśam aindriya jñānam iṣyate yadakṣāṇām bhāva abhāvayoḥ anurodhi svabhāvābhyām anuvartakam tat aindriyam iti ced tat indriya bhāva abhāva anurodhi tvam taimirika jñānasya api tulyam na hi indriya vyāpāram antareṇa taimirika jñānam utpadyate indriya vikāreṇa vikriyāvat jñānam aindriyam ced dvi candra ādi jñānānām timira ādi indriya vikāreṇa vikriyā sā eva iyam abhūta artha upadarśanānmikā bhrānta tva nimitta muktā asmābhiḥ kim niṣidhyate 
[207,vi_207,vii]	sarppa ādi bhrānti vat ca asyāḥ syāt akṣa vikṛtau api nivṛttiḥ na nivartteta nivṛtta īpi akṣa viplave yadi ca dvi candra ādi dhīḥ mānasī bhrāntiḥ tadā sarpa ucita deśe manda mandāloke rajū ādau saṃsthāna sāmya grahāt utpannāyāḥ sarpa ādi bhrānteḥ iva marīciṣu jala bhrānteḥ iva yathā pratyakṣam vicārāt asyāt vicandra ādi bhrānteḥ akṣa vikṛtau api sā nivṛttiḥ syāt akṣa viplavaḥ hi na tasyāḥ hetuḥ tatas ca sati api tasmin vimarśāt nivartate sarpa buddhiḥ iva tathā hi akṣa viplavepi timira ādau nivṛttepi tattvam avicārayataḥ na nivartate tad dvi candra buddhiḥ akṣa viplavasya tad kāraṇa tva abhāvāt akāraṇa nivṛttau ca nivṛttyayogāt 
[207,viii_208,i]	kiñca kadācid anya santāne tathā eva arpyeta vācakaiḥ dṛṣṭa smṛtim apekṣeta na bhāseta parisphuṭam yathā anubhavam sama deśa kālasya anyasya citta santāne yathā ahirahiḥ iti upadarśanena sarpa bhrāntiḥ arpyate tathā dvi candra ādi bhrāntiḥ api tasyāḥ vācakaiḥ śabdaiḥ arpyeta sāmagrī tulya tvāt timirasya ca ahetuka tvāt api ca yathā marīciṣu taraṅga jala samāsu pūrva dṛṣṭa jala smaraṇa sāpekṣā jala bhrāntiḥ tatra dvi candra ādi bhrāntiḥ api mānasī tvāt dṛṣṭa candra dvaya smṛtim apekṣeta na ca iyam smaraṇa sāpekṣā cakṣuḥ visphāraṇa mātreṇa spharaṇāt tathā mānasī tvāt parisphuṭam su vyakta grāhya ākārā na bhāseta jala ādi bhrāntiḥ iva 
[208,ii_208,iii]	suptasya jāgrataḥ vā api yā eva dhīḥ sphuṭa bhāsinī sā nirvikalpa ubhayathā api anyathā eva vikalpikā tasmāt suptasya jāgratā upi vā yā eva dhīḥ sphuṭa avabhāsinī vyakta grāhya ākārā sā nirvikalpā abhyupaganta vyāanyathā eva hi asphuṭa avabhāsinī dhīḥ ubhayathā suptasya jāgrataḥ pi vā kalpikā yuktā 
[208,iv_208,vi]	yatas evam tasmāt tasya avikalpepi prāmāṇyam pratiṣidhyate visaṃvādāt tad artham ca pratyakṣa ābham dvidhā uditam tasmāt kalpanā apoḍham iti ukte timira jñānasya avikalpe nirvikalpa tvepi sati prāmāṇyam pratyakṣa ātmakam prāptam sa taimiram iti apavādena visamvādāt pratiṣidhyate saṃvāda lakṣaṇa tvāt prāmāṇyasya tad artham upapluta jñāna nivṛtti artha ca ācārya diṅnāgena pratya kṣābham saṃkṣepataḥ dvidhā uktam sa vikalpam avikalpañca uktam pratyakṣa ābham
