[208,vii_208,ix]	pramāṇa phala vyavasthām kartum āha kriyā sādhanam iti eva sarvam sarvasya karmmaṇaḥ sādhanam na hi tat tasya sādhanam yā kriyā yatas kriyāyāḥ sādhanam hetuḥ iti eva na hi sarvam kāraṇam sarvasya karmmaṇaḥ kriyāyāḥ sādhanam karaṇam kintarhi tat vastu tasya karmaṇaḥ sādhanam karaṇam yā kriyā yatas padārthāt avyavadhānena bhavati sa tasyāḥ kāraṇam ucyate tatas ca indriya ādeḥ pramitim pratyavyavahita sādhaka tva abhāvāt na pramāṇam 
[209,i_209,iii]	kintarhi pramāṇam asti iti āha tatra anubhava mātreṇa jñānasya sadṛśa ātmanaḥ bhāvi antena ātmanā yena pratikarmma vibhajyate tatra rūpa ādau karmaṇi jñānasya anubhava mātreṇa anubhava ātmanaḥ sadṛśa ātmanaḥ tulya rūpasyatena ātmanā sva rūpeṇa prativiṣayam vyatirekiṇā bhāvyam yena pratikarmma prativiṣaya jñānam vibhajyate nīlasya idam pītasya idam iti anyathā anubhava mātra tayā sarvatra viṣaye sadṛśam jñānam prativiṣayam katham bhedena vyavasthāpayitum śakyeta 
[209,iv_209,vi]	syāt etat indriya ādeḥ hetoḥ savya apāḥ rata ādi lakṣaṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ jñānānām bhedena niyāmakam iti āha anātma bhūtaḥ bhedaḥ sya vidyamānopi hetuṣu bhinne karmaṇi abhinnasya na bhedena niyāmakaḥ hetuṣu indriya ādiṣu bhedaḥ viśeṣaḥ sa vya apāra tā ādi lakṣaṇaḥ vidyamāna upyasya jñānasya anubhava mātra ātma tayā bhinnasya bhinne karmmaṇi nīla ādau grāhye bhedena niyāmakaḥ na yuktaḥ kasmāt iti āha anātma bhūtaḥ jñāna asvarūpa tvāt indriyasya viśeṣaḥ pratikarmma na bhettum arhati 
[209,vii_209,viii]	tasmāt yatosya ātma bhedāt asya adhigatiḥ iti ayam kriyāyāḥ karma niyamaḥ siddhā sā tad prasādhanā tasmāt asya jñānasya ātma bhedāt yatas asya arthasya iyam adhigatiḥ iti kriyāyāḥ adhigateḥ karmaṇi vedye niyamaḥ sā kriyā tad prasādhanā tad karaṇā abhyupagantavyā 
[209,ix_210,i^1]	syāt etat indriya ādiḥ eva sva bhedāt bhedakaḥ jñānasya prativiṣayam adhigateḥ niyāmakaḥ tatas ca anubhava ātma tvāt aviṣayaḥ eva asiddhaḥ iti āha arthena ghaṭayati enām na hi muktvā artha rūpa tām anyaḥ sva bhedāt jñānasya bheda kopi kathañcana enām adhigatim artha rūpa tām artha sarū patām muktvā na hi anyaḥ kaścindriyā ādiḥ sva bhedāt kathañcana kena api prakāreṇa jñānasya bheda kopi arthā iva jñeyena ghaṭayati yojayati nīlasya iyam adhigatiḥ pītasya ca iyam ityādi tathā hi yadi api pratyartham pratīndriyañca jñānānām asti bhedaḥ tathā api viṣaya sārūpya abhāve saḥ eva viśeṣaḥ aśakya nirdeśaḥ atha viśeṣa upyadhi gateḥ eva vyavasthāpyate iti ced nanu tasyāḥ eva vyavasthāpakam iṣyate na cāvyasthite vyavasthāpake vyavasthāpya siddhiḥ nanu na sarvatra paraśu vyāpāra dṛṣṭi pūrvikā a chidā siddhiḥ
[210,i^2]	 chidā darśanāt api paraśu vyāpāra vyavasthiteḥ evam iha api adhi gati pūrvikāyām pramāṇa sthitau na doṣaḥ asamānam etat tathā hi para śu chidayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva viśeṣaḥ kriyā karaṇa bhāvaḥ adhigati jñāna ātma bhūta viśeṣayoḥ tu vyavasthāpya vyavasthāka bhāvaḥ eṣitavyaḥ ubhayoḥ api jñāna svarūpa ātma tvāt tatra kāraṇam ajñātam api sva kāryam nirvartayati iti kārya darśanāt ca tad vyavasthā yuktā eva vyavasthāpakaḥ tu na anupalakṣitaḥ vyavasthāpya vyavasthāyām kṣamate na hi apratītam kalpyamānam āśvastyaṃvyavasthāpayati 
[210,ii_210,iii]	tasmāt prameya adhigateḥ sādhanam meya rūpa tā sādhane anyatra tad karma sambandhaḥ na prasidhyati tasmāt prameya adhigateḥ phala bhūtāyāḥ vyavasthāpyāyāḥ sādhanam pramāṇam meya rūpa tā atha na sārūpyam tasya prativiṣayam bhinnasya sūpa lakṣaṇa tvāt sārūpyāt punar anyatra sādhane tasyāḥ kriyāyāḥ karmma sambandhaḥ nīlasya iyam adhigatiḥ pītasya ca ityādi na sidhyati indriya adhigati viśeṣasya sambhavepi anubhava mātra ātmaka jñānasya aviśeṣaka tva ayogāt jñāna gatasya apara viśeṣasya lakṣaṇa bhedena anupalakṣaṇāt 
[210,iv_211,i]	sā ca tasya ātma bhūtā eva tena na artha antaram phalam sā ca adhigatiḥ anubhava svabhāvāḥ jñānasya ātma bhūtā eva tena pramāṇān na artha antaram phalam prameyam eva phalam iti arthaḥ grāhya grāhaka bhāvopi bhāktaḥ eva iti darśayitum āha dadhānam tat ca tām ātmani artha adhigamana ātmanā tat ca jñānam ātmani tām artha sarūpa tām dadhānam bibhrat arthasya adhiga mana ātmanā adhigama lakṣaṇena
[211,ii_211,iii]	sa vyāpāram iva ābhāti vyāpāreṇa sva karmaṇi tad vaśāt tad vyavasthānāt akārakam api svayam vyāpāreṇa sa vyāpāram iva sva karmmaṇi grāhye ābhāti vyāpāram api vastutas akārakam api svayam tad vaśāt meya sārūpi avaśāt tasya adhigamasya vyavasthānāt 
[211,iv_211,v]	yathā phalasya hetūnām sadṛśa ātma tayā udbhavāt hetu rūpa grahaḥ loke akriyāvatvepi kathyate yathā lokepi hetūnām sadṛśa ātma tayā sadṛśa rūpatayā udbhavāt phalasya akriyāvat tva ipi hetu rūpa grahaṇa vyāpāra abhāvepi hetu rūpa grahaḥ kathyate pituḥ rūpam gṛhītam sutena ityādi atas artha rūpa tām muktvā adhigati sādhana manyat ayuktam 
[211,vi_211,vii]	ālocana akṣa sambandha viśeṣaṇa dhiyāmataḥ na īṣṭamprāmāṇyam eteṣām vyavadhānāt kriyām prati atas ālocanasya artha ālocana mātrasya jāti ādi viśiṣṭa niścaya phalam prati akṣa sambandhasya indriya artha sannikarṣasya ālocana phalam prati viśeṣaṇasya vedya viśeṣya buddhi phalam prati prāmāṇyam sādhana tvam na iṣṭam eteṣām ālocana artha sambandha viśeṣaṇa jñānānām kriyāyām adhigati viṣaya sārūpyeṇa vyavadhānāt 
[211,viii_212,i]	vyavasthānepi sādhakatama tvam syāt iti ced āha sarveṣām upayoga ipi kārakāṇām kriyām prati yat antyam bhedakam tasyāḥ tat sādhakatamam matam sarveṣām kārakāṇām sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa kriyām pratyupayogepi teṣu madhye yatkārakam antyam kāraka antareṇa avyavahita vyāpya aram sat kriyā bhedakam tat tasyāḥ sādhakatamam matam na anyat 
[212,ii_212,iv]	tathā hi sarva sāmānya hetutvāt akṣāṇām asti na īdṛśam tat bhedepi hi atat rūpasya asya idam iti tad kutas akṣāṇām tāvat īdṛśam sādhakatama tvam na asti sarvam sāmānya hetutvāt sarva jñāna sādhāraṇa hetu tvāt avāntara adhi gati bhedaka tva anupapatteḥ teṣām indriyāṇām pramāda āvila tva ādi bhedepi jñānasya atad rūpasya viṣaya sārūpya rahitasya idam asya grāhakam iti grāhaka tvam yat iṣyate tad kutas 
[212,v_212,vi]	etena śeṣam vyākhyātam viśeṣaṇa dhiyām punar atā drupye na bhedopi tadvat anya dhiyopi vā etena akṣāṇām asādhana tva darśanena śeṣam ālocana artha sambandha ādi vyākhyātam tat api artha sārūpya rahitam asādhanam sārūpye ca svīkartavye tat eva avyavahita tvāt sādhanam astu viśeṣaṇa dhiyām punar ayam adhikaḥ doṣaḥ atādrūpye viśeṣaṇa sārūpya abhāve viśeṣya dhiyaḥ sakāśāt bheda upi na syāt dvayoḥ api ākāra rahita tvena bheda sthiti anupapatteḥ tatas ca ekā pramāṇam anyā ca phalam iti kutas atha sārūpyam viśeṣaṇa dhiyaḥ bhedakam iṣyate evam ca sati tat eva pramāṇam phalam ca syāt artha sarūpa tvāt adhigati rūpa tvāt ca tadvat viśeṣaṇa buddheḥ iva anyaḥ buddheḥ viṣaya sārūpyam phala ātma kañca iṣyatām 
[212,vii_212,ix]	kiñca na iṣṭaḥ viṣaya bheda upi kriyā sādhanayoḥ dvayoḥ eka artha tve dvayam vyartham na ca syāt krama bhāvitā kriyā sādhanayoḥ viṣaya bheda upi na iṣṭaḥ sarvasya na hi anyatra paraśu vyāpāraḥ chidā ca anyatra iha tu viśeṣaṇe pramāṇa vyāpāraḥ kriyā ca viśeṣyaḥ iti bhinna viṣaya tā katham iṣṭā 
[213,i]	atha etad doṣa tayā dvayoḥ kriyā sādhanayoḥ krama bhāvinoḥ eka artha tve eka viṣaya tve ca svīkriyamāṇe dvayam bhinnam pramāṇam phalam ca vyartham viśeṣaṇa jñānam pramāṇam phalam ca astu viṣaya svarūpa tvāt adhigama svabhāvāt ca tatas param tu viśeṣya jñānam adhigata adhigantṛ tvāt anupayuktam na ca eka viṣayayoḥ jñānayoḥ krama bhāvitā asti viṣayasya tad janana śaktasya krameṇa sva kārya janana virodhāt 
[213,ii_213,vii]	sakṛt utpattau eva viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya dhiyoḥ pramāṇaphala tā bhaviṣyati iti ced āha sādhya sādhana tā bhāvaḥ sakṛt bhāve sakṛt bhāve sādhya sādhana tāyāḥ abhāvaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva viśeṣa tvena tasyāḥ iṣṭa tvāt nanu evam ākāra adhigamayoḥ eka jñāna ātma tvepi pramāṇa phala tā anupapannā iti āha dhiyoṃśayoḥ tad vyavasthā āśraya tvena sādhya sādhana saṃsthitiḥ dhiyaḥ aśaṃyoḥ ākāra adhigama lakṣaṇayoḥ sādhya sādhana saṃsthitiḥ kriyā karaṇa vyavasthā tad vyavasthā āśraya tvena ākāra vaśena adhigati viśeṣa vyavasthānāt na asti atra kārya kāraṇa ātmakaḥ kriyā karaṇa bhāvaḥ kim tu vyavasthāpya vyavasthāpaka bhāvaḥ sa ca tādātmyepi aviruddhaḥ 
[213,viii_213,x]	artha sannikarṣa upi na pramāṇam iti āha sarva ātmanā api sambaddham kaiścid eva avagamyate dharmaiḥ sa niyamaḥ na syāt sambandhasya aviśeṣataḥ bāhyam sarva ātmanā sarvaiḥ ākāraiḥ indriya ādibhiḥ sambaddham api kaiścid eya dharmmaiḥ nīla tva ādibhiḥ ggamyate na tpaṇu puñja tva ādibhiḥ saḥ eṣa grahaṇasya niyamaḥ na syāt sambandhasya api gati sthiti hetoḥ aviśeṣataḥ 
[214,i_214,ii]	tad abheda ipi bhedoyam yasmāt tasya pramāṇa tā saṃskārāt ced atādrūpye na tasya api avyavasthiteḥ yasmāt indriya sannikarṣa ādeḥ prāmāṇyam ayuktam tat tasmāt abhedepi sannikarṣa ādyaviśeṣepi yasmāt niyāmakāt tad jñānasya ayam bhedaḥ nīlasya idam jñānam pītasya ca idam ityādi tasya pramāṇatā yuktā sa ca ākāraḥ eva iti saḥ eva pramāṇam jñāna jāta jñāna hetoḥ saṃskārāt jñānasya kaiścid eva dharmaiḥ grahaṇa niyamaḥ iti ced na tasya saṃskārasya api atādrūpye viṣayāsa rūpa tve avyavasthiteḥ 
[214,iii_214,v]	yat ākāram jñānam syāt tasya anubhavaḥ saṃskāraḥ ca bhavet tasmāt ca grahaṇa pratiniyamaḥ anubhava sthiti abhāve tu sarvam avyavasthitam kriyā karaṇayoḥ aikya virodhaḥ iti ced asat dharma bheda abhyupagamāt kriyā karaṇayoḥ adhigama ākārayoḥ aikātmye virodhaḥ iti ced asat etat dharma bhedasya vyāvṛtti upakalpitasya abhyupagamāt anākāra vyāvṛttiḥ pramāṇam anadhigati vyāvṛttiḥ ca phalam iti na anayoḥ aikyam 
[214,vi_214,ix]	kathantarhi uktam sā ca tasya ātma bhūtā eva tena na artha antaram phalam iti āha vastu abhinnam iti iṣyate paramārthataḥ jñāna ātmakam vastu abhinnam iti iṣyate na tu kalpita dharma dvāreṇapi kim punar tattvataḥ eva sādhanāt bhinnā adhigatiḥ chi dādi vat neṣyatas iti āha evam prakārā sarvā eva kriyā kāraka saṃsthitiḥ bhāvasya bhinna abhimateṣu api āropeṇa vṛttitaḥ 
[214,x]	sarvā eva kriyā kārakayoḥ saṃsthitiḥ vyavasthā evaṃprakārā kalpitā eva bhinna abhimateṣu api dāru paraśu ādiṣu kriyā karaṇa bhāvasya āropeṇa vṛttitaḥ na hi tatra api kārya kāraṇa vastu dvaya vyatiriktā kriyā asti dvidhā bhūtam kāṣṭham eva ātad vyāvṛttyā bheda antara pratikṣepeṇa chidā iti ucyate tad kāraṇeṣu ca puruṣa kara paraśu ādiṣu sāmagryantara varttinaḥ karācchidāyāḥ anutpatteḥ paraśorasādhāraṇam sahakāri tvam upadarśayitum atat vyāvṛttyā karaṇa vyapadeśaḥ na tu kriyā karaṇa tvam anyat eva kārya karaṇābhyām adhigama ākārayoḥ tu vyavasthāpya vyavasthāpaka bhāvaḥ kriyā karaṇa bhāvaḥ yathā yaḥ kampate saḥ aśvaḥ iti uktā pramāṇa phala vyavasthā 
[215,i_215,vi]	idānīm yoga ācāraḥ vedya vedaka bhāvam apaśyan sautra antikam pṛcchati kārtha saṃvid kā arthasya saṃvid jñānam ucyate atas āha yat eva idam pratyakṣam prativedanam yat eva idam pratyakṣam anubhava siddham prativedanam nīla ādi ākāreṇa pratiniyatam vedanam pratisantāna niyatam vā sā eva artha saṃvid ucyate 
[215,vii_215,viii]	tad artha vedanam kena tādrūpyāt vyabhicāri tat nanu tat pratiniyatam vedanam anubhūyamānam arthaṃsya vedanam kena hetunā ucyate sva prakāśa ātmaka tvāt sva vedanam eva tat yuktam na artha vedanam tasya sarvadā parokṣa tvāt tādrūpyāt artha sarūpa tvāt jñānam artha vedanam iti ced tad artha sārūpi aṃvyabhi ca ari dvi candra keśoṇḍūka jñāna ādi ākārasya artham antareṇa api bhāvāt 
[215,ix_215,xiii]	atha sonubhavaḥ kva asya atha anubhāvya abhāve saḥ anubhavaḥ pratyātma vedyaḥ asya jñānasya na karmmaṇi vyavasthāpanīyaḥ na hi karma rahitā kriyā kvacid asti atra āha tat eva idam vicāryate yat ucyate vyavahartṛ bhiḥ idam anena anubhūyate iti tat eva idam asmābhiḥ vicāryate jñānam sva prakāśam upalabhyate prakāśaḥ ca ucyate iti ayuktam 
[216,i_216,iii]	yat ca artha sārūpyam anubhava nibandhanam uktam tat api asambhavī iti darśayan āha sarūpayanti tat kena sthūla ābhāsañca te aṇavaḥ te parasparam bhinnāḥ aṇavaḥ tat jñānam sthūla ābhāsam sthūla ākāram kena rūpeṇa sarūpayanti yat aṇu svarūpam asthūlam asti na tat jñāna ārūḍham yat ca jñāna ārūḍham sthaulyam na aṇuṣu tat asti 
[216,iv_216,v]	tat na artha rūpa tā tasya satyāṃrtha avyabhicāriṇī tad samvedana bhāvasya na samarthā prasādhane tasmāt tulya jñānasya na artha rūpa tā asti satyām vā artha rūpa tāyām vyabhicāriṇī sā dvi candra jñāna ādiṣu tatas ca tad saṃvedana bhāvasya artha saṃvedana tvasya prasādhaneṣu sā artha rūpa tā na samarthā na kevalāt artha sārūpyāt artha saṃvedana tvam yena vyabhicāraḥ syāt kintarhi sārūpya tad utpattibhyām te ca dvi candra jñāna ādīnām na staḥ candra dvayasya abhāvāt tad utpatteḥ ayogāt 
[216,vi_216,viii]	etat eva āha tat sārūpya tad utpattī yadi samvedya lakṣaṇam samvedyam syāt samāna artham vijñānam samanantaram tena grāhyeṇa sārūpyam tasmāt utpattiḥ sva samvedyasya lakṣaṇam yadi saṃmatam tadā api samanantaram jñānam uttara jñānena samāna artham samāna grāhyam saṃvedyam syāt tad sarūpa tad utpattyoḥ saṃbhavāt 
[216,ix_217,i]	syāt etat idam dṛṣṭam śrutam vedam iti yatra avasāya dhīḥ sa tasya anubhavaḥ sārūpya tad utpattimat tva ipi idam dṛṣṭam śrutam vedam iti yatra avasāya dhīḥ utpadyate tasya saḥ anubhavaḥ na anyasya na ca samanantara pratyaye dṛṣṭa śrutādi avasāyaḥ bhavati tat na grāhyaḥ asau atra āha sā eva pratyāsattiḥ vicāryate dṛśya darśanayoḥ sā eva pratyāsattiḥ vicāryate asmābhiḥ 
[217,ii_217,iii]	dṛśya darśanayoḥ yena tasya tat darśanam matam tayoḥ sambandham āśritya draṣṭuḥ eṣa viniścayaḥ yena pratyāsatti sambhavena tasya bāhyasya tat jñānam darśanam matam tayoḥ dṛ śyadarśanayoḥ sambandham pratyāsattim āśritya draṣṭuḥ puruṣasya idam dṛṣṭam śrutam vedam iti artha niścayaḥ tad sārūpya tad utpatti lakṣaṇā ca pratyāsattiḥ samanantara pratyayepi samānā iti tad nibandhanaḥ dṛṣṭa śruta adhyavasāyaḥ pi tatra syāt iti arthaḥ 
[217,iv_217,v]	ātmā sa tasya anubhavaḥ sa ca na anyasya kasyacid pratyakṣa prativedya tvam api tasya tad ātma tā tasmāt vedya rahitaḥ tasya jñānasya sa nīla ādi rūpaḥ ātma anubhavaḥ sa ca anubhavaḥ na anyasya kasyacid bāhyasya tasya jñānasya pratyakṣa prativedya tvam api yat ucyate sā tad ātma tā aparokṣa anubhava ātma tā 
[217,vi_217,vii]	na anyonubhāvyaḥ tena asti tasya na anubhava uparaḥ tasya api tulya codya tvāt svayam sā eva prakāśate yathā ca svarūpāt anyaḥ buddhyā anubhāvyaḥ na asti tathā tasya jñānasya ca aparaḥ anubhavaḥ na asti tasya jñāna grahaṇa sya api tulya artha codya tvāt sa hi anya tva nibandhanaḥ grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ tat ca anupapannam iti uktam tat tasmāt tat jñānam aparokṣatayā utpannam svayam prakāśate na anyena prakāśyate 
[217,viii_218,i]	katham tarhi nīla ādi anubhava prasiddhiḥ iti āha nīla ādi rūpaḥ tasya asau svabhāva unubhavaḥ ca saḥ nīla ādi anubhavāt khyātaḥ svarūpa anubhavopi san tasya jñānasya nīla ādi rūpaḥ asau svabhāvaḥ anubhavaḥ prakāśa ātmakaḥ ca saḥ tena svarūpa anubhavopi sannīla ādi anubhavot tathā saṃprasiddhiḥ 
[218,ii_218,iii]	prakāśamānaḥ tādātmyāt svarūpasya prakāśakaḥ yathā prakāśa ubhimataḥ tathā dhīḥ a ātma vedinī yathā prakāśaḥ tādātmyāt prakāśa ātmaka tvāt para nirapekṣaḥ prakāśamānaḥ svarūpasya prakāśakaḥ abhimataḥ tathā dhīḥ para nirapekṣā prakāśa ātmanā utpannā prakāśamānā atma vedinī iti upacārāt ucyate 
[218,iv_218,v]	tasyāḥ ca artha antare vedye durghaṭau vedya vedakau avedya vedaka ākārā yathā bhrāntaiḥ nirīkṣyate vibhakta lakṣaṇa grāhya grāhaka ākāra viplavā cakāraḥ hetau yasmāt tasyāḥ dhiyaḥ artha antare vedye vedya vedaka ākārau durghaṭau tasmāt vastutas avedya vedaka ākārā sā buddhiḥ nīla prakāśa ātmanā utpannā tathā prakāśate na tu tatra kaścid grāhyasya grāhakasya ca ākāraḥ samasti katham tarhi grāhya grāhaka pratibhāsa vyavasāyau iti āha bhrāntaiḥ aprahīṇa dvaya vāsanā viplavaiḥ yathā vibhakta lakṣaṇau grāhya grāhaka ākārau eva viplavau yasyāḥ sā tādṛśī nirīkṣyate vibhāvyate bhrānta darśana anurodhena 
[218,vi_218,vii]	tathā kṛta vyavasthā iyam keśa ādi jñāna bheda vat tathā grāhya grāhaka bhedena kṛta vyavasthā sa nīla ādi bahis deśam grāhyam āntarañca saṃvedanam grāhakam iti viplavaḥ eṣa keśa ādi jñāna bheda vat na hi keśoṇḍūka jñāna viśeṣasya grāhaka vat grāhyaḥ keśa avayavosti kim tarhi keśa ābhāsaḥ prakāśaḥ eva kevalaḥ 
[218,viii_218,ix]	yadā tadā na saṃcodya grāhya grāhaka lakṣaṇī tadā anya samvidobhāvāt sva samvid phalam iṣyate viplava vaśāt ca grāhya grāhaka bhedena buddhiḥ yadā vyavasthāpyate tadā na sam ca udya grāhya grāhaka lakṣaṇā sā na hi vastutas grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ sambhavati na ca viplava vaśāt vastu vyavasthā keśa dvi candra ādeḥ api tattva prasaṅgāt yadā ca na grāhya grāhaka tā vijñaptimātra tāyām tadā anyasya grāhyasya saṃvidaḥ jñānasya abhāvāt sva saṃvid phalam iṣyate 
[219,i_219,iii]	yadi bāhyonubhūyeta kaḥ doṣaḥ na eva kaścana idam eva kim uktam syāt sa bāhyorthonubhūyate nanu yadi bāhyaḥ arthaḥ jñānena anubhūyate tadā kaḥ doṣaḥ yena sva saṃvid phalam iṣyate āha yadi anubhūyate tadā na eva kaścana doṣaḥ anubhavaḥ eva tu bāhyasya na asti iti ucyate tathā idam eva kim uktam syāt bāhyaḥ arthaḥ jñānena anubhūyate iti
[219,iv_219,v]	yadi buddhiḥ tad ākārā sā asti ākāra viśeṣiṇī sā bāhyāt anyatas vā iti vicāram idam arhati yadi buddhiḥ tad ākārā vā bāhya sarūpā iti ucyate satyam asti sā buddhiḥ ākāra viśeṣiṇī nīla ānīla ādi ākāra viśeṣa yuktā kiṃtu sā buddhiḥ bbāhyāt arthāt jāyeta anyatas vāsanā pratiniyamāt vā iti vicāram idam arhati na tāvat buddhi vyatirekiṇā arthaḥ kaścid hetutayā upalabhyate buddhi svarūpa mātra vedanāt kādācid ka tayā tu kāraṇam tasyāḥ kiñcid vyavasthāpanīyam tat ca bāhyam vāsanā vā syāt ubhayathā api upapatteḥ 
[219,vi_220,iii]	darśana upādhi rahitasya agrahāt tad grahe grahāt darśanam nīla nirbhāsam tatra darśanena jñānena upādhinā viśeṣaṇena rahitasya nīla ādeḥ agrahāt tasya grahe ca nīlasya grahāt saha eva nīla dhiyoḥ vedanāt darśanam nīla ādi nirbhāsam nīla ākāram vyavasthitam yat tāvat nīla ādikam bāhyam iti ucyate tad jñānena saha upalambha niyamāt tad abhinna svabhāvam dvi ca ndra ādi vat kaḥ tarhi na asti iti āha na arthaḥ bāhyosti kevalam bāhyaḥ nīlādiḥ arthaḥ kevalam na asti tad sādhaka tvena abhimatasya adhyakṣasya asāmarthyāt 
[220,iv_220,vi]	evantarhi jñānasya gaja ādi ākārasya āloka ādi nimitta antara sadbhāvepi deśa kāla ādi pratiniyama darśanāt arthaḥ vyavasyati iti āha kasyacid kiñcid eva antar vāsanāyāḥ prabodhakam tatas dhiyām viniyamaḥ na bāhya artha vyapekṣayā kasyacid jñānasya gaja ādi ākārasya kiñcid eva jñānam antar vāsanāyāḥ samanantara pratyaya antara varttinyāḥ niyata jñāna janana yogya tā lakṣaṇāyāḥ prabodhakam kārya utpāda nābhi mukhya kārakam tatas prabodhaka vaśāt dhiyām niyata ākāra tayā viniyamaḥ na bāhya artha vyapekṣayā kaḥ hi viśeṣaḥ bāhyaḥ vā niyāmakaḥ pratibhāsasya prabuddha vāsanā viśeṣaḥ samanantara pratyayaḥ vā tatra vāsanāyāḥ sāmarthyam svapna ādau upalabdham na tu bāhyasya nitya parokṣa tvāt na tathā api parokṣasya bāhyasya sādhakasya abhāvepi na abhāvasthitiḥ iti ced pratibhāsamānam jñānam bāhyam tu na pratibhāsate eva iti tāvatā eva abhimata siddheḥ sādhaka pramāṇa rahita piśācāyamāna bahis artha niṣedhena asmākam ādaraḥ yadi tu tad niṣedha nirbbandhaḥ garīyān sa aṃśatvānaṃśa tva kalpanayā paramāṇu pratiṣedhe ācāryīyaḥ paryāṣitavyaḥ 
[220,vii_220,viii]	tasmāt dvi rūpam asti ekam yat evam anubhūyate smaryate ca ubhaya ākārasya asya samvedanam phalam yasmāt bāhyaḥ arthaḥ na anubhūyate tasmāt ekam vijñānam avidyā upapluta tvāt dvi rūpam bodha rūpam nīla ādi rūpañcā asti yat yasmāt jñānam evam dvi ākāra tayā anubhūyate sva vedanena yathā anubhavam kāla antare smaryate ca yathā ca anyasya saṃvedana abhāvāt ubhaya ādi ākārasya nīla ādi anubhava rūpasya saṃvedanam phalam tat evam prameyaḥ grāhya ākāraḥ pramāṇam grāhaka ākāraḥ phalam sva saṃvid iti darśitam bhavati 
[221,i_221,ii]	yadā niṣpanna tad bhāvaḥ iṣṭa uniṣṭopi vā paraḥ vijñapti hetuḥ viṣayaḥ tasyāḥ ca anubhavaḥ tathā yadā bahis arthavādepi paraḥ vāhyaḥ arthaḥ iṣṭaḥ aniṣṭaḥ api vā niṣyanna tat bhāvaḥ bhāvanā vaśāt vyavasthita iṣṭā an iṣṭa bhāvaḥ sarūpāyāḥ vijñapteḥ hetuḥ san viṣayaḥ bhavati tadā tasyāḥ vijñapteḥ tathā iṣṭa aniṣṭa ākāreṇa anubhavaḥ viṣayasya ca anubhavaḥ ucyate tena viṣaya sārūpyam pramāṇam artha saṃvid phalam uktam 
[221,iii_221,v]	athavā vijñāna vādepyaviruddham iti āha yadā sa viṣayam jñānam jñāna aṃśa irtha vyavasthiteḥ tadā yaḥ ātma anubhavaḥ saḥ eva artha viniścayaḥ yadā jñānasya aṃśe ākāre viplava vaśāt arthasya vyavasthiteḥ jñānam sa viṣayam iṣṭam tadā yaḥ ātmanaḥ jñāna ākārasya anubhavaḥ saḥ eva arthasya niścayaḥ saṃvedanam iṣyate tatas ca vijñāna vāde pi artha ākāraḥ pramāṇam artha saṃvid phalam aviruddham 
[221,vi_222,i]	yadi iṣṭa ākāraḥ ātmā syāt anyathā vā anubhūyate iṣṭoniṣṭopi vā tena bhavati arthaḥ praveditaḥ bahis arthanayepi buddhi vedanasya eva artha vedana tvāt tathā yadi iṣṭa ākāraḥ asyāḥ buddheḥ ātmā anubhūyate anyathā aniṣṭa ākāraḥ vā tadā tena jñānena iṣṭaḥ aniṣṭaḥ vā arthaḥ praveditaḥ bhavati na anyathā 
[222,ii_222,iii]	vidyamānepi bāhyerthe yathā anubhavam eva saḥ niścita ātmā sva rūpeṇa na aneka ātma tva doṣataḥ yasmāt vidyamānepi bāhye arthe yathā anubhavam anubhava ākāra anatikrameṇa sa bāhyaḥ arthaḥ niścita ātmā vyavasthāpyate na artha svarūpeṇa yathā sambhavinā niścita ātmā vyavatiṣṭhate iṣṭa aniṣṭa tvena puruṣābhyām ekasya arthasya grahaṇāt aneka ātma tva doṣaḥ prasajyate 
[222,iv_222,v]	yadi bāhyam na vidyeta kasya saṃvedanam bhavet yadi agatyā svarūpasya bāhyasya eva na kim matam abhyupāyepi bhedena na syāt anubhavaḥ dvayoḥ adṛṣṭa āvaraṇāt syāt ced na nāma artha vaśā gatiḥ aneka ātmaka tvasya abhyupāye svīkāra īpi dvayoḥ puruṣayoḥ bhedena iṣṭa tvena ekasya anyasya ca aniṣṭa tvena anubhavaḥ na syāt dvi ākāra tvāt vastunaḥ tathā eva pratīti prasaktiḥ adṛṣṭena sukha duḥkha vedanīyena karmaṇā āvaraṇāt dvitīyasya ākārasya eka ātma tvena pratibhāsaḥ syāt iti ced evam satyartha vaśā gatiḥ jñānam iti nāma prasiddham na syāt adṛṣṭa vaśena iṣṭa aniṣṭa ākārayoḥ pratīteḥ upadarśanāt 
[222,vi_222,viii]	kiñca tam aneka ātmakam bhāvam eka ātma tvena darśayat tat adṛṣṭam katham nāma bhavet arthasya darśakam bhāvam aneka ātmakam eka ātmaka tvena eka ākāra tayā darśayat adṛṣṭam tat katham arthasya darśakam nāma bhavet tat eva hi darśakam asya yat tad svarūpam pratibhāsayati na ca eka ākāraḥ arthaḥ tatas tad pratītiḥ na artha pratītiḥ 
[223,i_223,ii]	iṣṭa aniṣṭa avabhāsinyaḥ kalpanā na akṣa dhīḥ yadi aniṣṭa ādā asandhānam dṛṣṭam tatra api cetasām yathā avasthita vastu grāhiṇī akṣa dhīḥ tad anantaram iṣṭa aniṣṭa avabhāsinyaḥ kalpanā ayathārthā tena aneka ātmaka tva doṣa prasaṅgaḥ iti yadi iṣyate tatra aindriya tvepya niṣṭa ādau ādi śabdāt kāmalā ādau cetasām indriya jñānānām asandhānam artha ākārān anuvidhānam dṛṣṭam tasmāt indriya buddhiḥ ayatha artha ākārā na bhavati iti na asti 
[223,iii_223,iv]	tasmāt prameye bāhyepi yuktam sva anubhavaḥ phalam yatas svabhāvosya yathā tathā eva artha viniścayaḥ tasmāt na kevalam svarūpe bāhyepi prameye sva anubhavaḥ phalam yuktam yatas kāraṇāt svabhāvosya jñānasya yathā pratibhāti tathā eva na arthasya viniścayaḥ sidhyati 
[223,v_223,vi]	tad artha ābhāsa tā eva asya pramāṇam na tu san api grāhakā atmā apara artha tvāt bāhyeṣu artheṣu apekṣate tat tasmāt bāhyeṣu artheṣu grāhyeṣu asya jñānasya artha ābhāsa tā artha ākāra tā eva pramāṇam apekṣate na tu anvayi grāhaka ātmā grāhaka ākāraḥ apara artha tvāta ātma viṣaya tvāt tasya 
[223,vii_223,viii]	yasmāt yathā niviṣṭa usau artha ātmā pratyaye tathā niścīyate niviṣṭa ūsau evam iti ātma saṃvidaḥ yasmāt kāraṇat yathā iṣṭa tvena aniṣṭa tvena vā arthasya ātma ākāraḥ pratyaye niviṣṭaḥ tathā arthom niścīyate tasmāt artha ākāraḥ pramāṇam asau artha ākāraḥ evam iṣṭa aniṣṭa tvena buddhau niviṣṭaḥ iti ātma saṃvidaḥ sva saṃvedanāt niścīyate 
[223,ix_223,x]	iti artha saṃvid sā eva iṣṭā yata ūrtha ātmā na dṛśyate tasmāt buddhi niveśya arthaḥ sādhanam tasya sā kriyā iti tasmāt sā eva ātma saṃvid artha saṃvidiṣṭā yatas svarūpāt bahis bhūtaḥ artha ātmā na dṛśyate buddhi ākāraḥ eva tu vedyate atas tad vedana darśanam eva artha vedanam yasmāt ca artha sārūpya vaśena artha adhigati vyavasthā tasmāt buddhi niveśya arthaḥ artha pratibimbam sādhanam pramāṇam tasya pramāṇasya sādhigatiḥ kriyā phalam iṣyate 
[224,i_224,ii]	yathā niviśate sorthaḥ yatas sā prathate tathā artha sthiteḥ tad ātma tvāt sva vid api artha vinmatā yatas kāraṇāt yathārthaḥ jñāna ātmani niviśate tathā sā sva saṃvittiḥ prathate khyāti tasmāt arthasya sthiteḥ adhigateḥ tad ātma tvāt paramārthataḥsu avid api satī artha vid matā sva saṃvedanam eva artha vedanam upacārāt ucyate iti tādātmyam anayoḥ 
[224,iii_224,vii]	tasmāt viṣaya bheda upi na yasmāt artha ākāraḥ eva pramāṇam pratīti sādhana tvāt phalañca pratīyamānam tasmāt pramāṇa phalayoḥ viṣaya bheda upi na asti yathā para mate ālocana viśeṣaṇa jñāna ādīnām ekārtha apekṣiṇyau eva hi sārūpya pratipattī pramāṇa phala tvam pratilabhete yadi artha saṃvedanam phalam tadā sva vid phalam katham uktam iti āha sva saṃvedanam phalam uktam svabhāva cintāyām tādātmyāt artha saṃvidaḥ artha saṃvedaṃnasya vastutas svabhāva cintāyām sva saṃvedanam phalam uktam artha saṃvidaḥ tādātmyāt sva saṃvedana ātma tvāt na su a ākāra pratīteḥ anyā asti artha pratītiḥ sva rūpeṇa tasyāḥ pratīteḥ 
[224,viii_224,x]	nanu yadi yathārtham na anubhavaḥ tadā sva vāsanā prabodhakam anuvartamānasya jñānasya arthoṃbāhya usti iti etat eva kutas iti āha tathā avabhāsamānasya tādṛśaḥ anyādṛśopi vā jñānasya hetuḥ artha upi iti arthasya iṣṭā prameya tā tathā iṣṭa aniṣṭa ākāreṇa avabhāsamānasya jñānasya arthopi tādṛśonyādṛśaḥ vā hetuḥ iti arthasya prameya teṣṭā sautra antika mate sārūpyasya paramārthataḥ sarūpayanti tat kena sthūla ābhāsañca teṇavaḥ iti pratiṣedhāt 
[225,i_225,v]	yathā kathañcittasya artha rūpam muktvā avabhāsinaḥ artha grahaḥ katham yadi sārūpya abhāvaḥ tadā tasya jñānasya avabhāsinaḥ yathā kathañcid iṣṭa aniṣṭa ādinā bhāsamānam artha rūpam artha ākāram muktvā katham kena prakāreṇa arthasya grahaḥ syāt na hi arthaḥ sva rūpeṇa dṛśyate tat sva rūpa buddhi vedanāt artha graha vyavasthā sārūpyam eva ced na saṃbhavati katham artha grahaḥ iti manyate sautra antikaḥ yoga ācāraḥ tu tasya sāhāyyakam manyamānaḥ āha satyam na jāneham apodṛśam satyam na jāne aham api īdṛśam artha grahaḥ katham iti 
[225,vi_225,viii]	katham tarhi asati arthe grāhya grāhaka phala bhedaḥ iti āha avibhāga upi buddhi ātma viparyāsita darśanaiḥ grāhya grāhaka saṃvitti bhedavān iva lakṣyate paramārthataḥ avibhāgaḥ bheda rahitā upi buddhi ātma dvaya vāsanayā viparyāsitam vibhāgena upadarśitam darśanam yeṣām taiḥ atattva darśi puruṣaiḥ grāhya grāhaka saṃvittīnām parasparam bhedaḥ tadvān iva lakṣyate 
[225,ix_225,xi]	atra dṛṣṭāntam āha mantra ādi upapluta akṣāṇām yathā mṛd śakala ādayaḥ anyathā eva avabhāsante tad rūpa rahitāḥ api yathā mūcchakala ādayaḥ mantra ādibhiḥ upapluta yathārtha jñāna hetu kṛtam akṣam yeṣām teṣām anyathā suvarṇṇa ādi tvena eva avabhāsante tena suvarṇṇa ādinā rūpeṇa rahitāḥ api vastutas 
[226,i_226,iii]	kasmāt punar mmantra ādi sāmarthyāt suvarṇṇādi tām eva yātam mṛd khaṇḍam iti na abhyupagamyate iti āha tathā eva adarśanāt teṣām anupapluta cakṣuṣām dūre yathā vā maruṣu mahān alpopi dṛśyate mantra ādinā anupapluta cakṣuṣā anyena puṃsā teṣām mṛd śakala ādīnām yathā upahata akṣeṇa te dṛśyante tathā eva darśanāt mṛdātma tvena eva darśanāt suvarṇṇa ādi tvena niṣpatti kalpanam a yuktam yathā maruṣu dūre alpopi mahān dṛśyate tad deśa sthaiḥ alpa tvena eva bhātasya darśanāt 
[226,iv_226,v]	yathā anudarśanañcā iyam meyamāna phala sthitiḥ kriyate avidyamānā api grāhya grāhaka saṃvidām tasmāt grāhya grāhaka saṃvidām paramārthataḥ avidyamānā api meyamāna phala sthitiḥ yathādarśanam kriyate grāhya ākāraḥ meyaḥ grāhaka ākāraḥ mānam saṃvittiḥ phalam iti vyavasthāpyate 
[226,vi_226,vii]	anyathā ekasya bhāvasya nānā rūpa avabhāsinaḥ satyam katham syuḥ ākārāḥ tad eka tvasya hānitaḥ anyathā yadi vastutas grāhaka ādi vibhāgaḥ iṣyate tadā ekasya bhāvasya jñāna ātmanaḥ nānā rūpa avabhāsinaḥ aneka ākāra pratibhāsavantaḥ ākārāḥ grāhya ādikāḥ katham satyam syuḥ tasya eka jñāna ātmanaḥ eka tvasya hānitaḥ na hi ekam pratibhāsamāna aneka ākāra ātmakam bhavitum arhati pratibhāsena sarveṣām bhedena vyavasthāpanāt 
[226,viii_226,x]	anekam eva tarhi jñānam pariccheda ādi tvena syāt iti āha anyasya anya tva hāneḥ ca na ca anekam jñānam ekam eva iṣṭavyam vastutas bhinnasya abhede iṣyamāṇe grāhya ādeḥ para sparataḥ anyasya anyatva hāneḥ yadā hi bheda pratibhāsepi eka tvam iṣṭam tadā bhedaḥ eva na vyavasthitaḥ tatas ca sukha duḥkha ādayaḥ nīla pīta ādayaḥ ca parasparam na bhidyeran pratibhāsa bhedasya tad sādhana tvāt anyasya ca tad sādhanasya abhāvāt 
[227,i_227,iii]	evantar hi ekam tāvat jñānam nānā ākāram syāt iti śaṅkāyām nakāram kāka akṣi vat saṃbandhayan āha nābhedaḥ rūpa darśanāt rūpa abhedepi paśyantī dhīra bhedam vyavasyati na abhedaḥ jñānasya abhibuddhasya rūpasya adarśanāt rūpa abhedañca adraya ādau paśyantī dhīra bhedam vyavasyati na ca grāhya grāhaka ādiṣu bhinna ābhāseṣu abheda pratibhāsaḥ 
[227,iv_227,vi]	tasya āt bhāvāḥ yena nirūpyante tad rūpam na asti tattvataḥ yasmāt ekam anekam ca rūpam teṣām na vidyate bhāvāḥ grāhya ādayaḥ yena rūpeṇa grāhya tva ādinā nirūpyante anubhūyante tad rūpam tattvataḥ teṣām na asti yasmāt ekam rūpam anekañca rūpam teṣām na vidyate vastu bhavat ekam anekam vā syāt na ca grāhya ādi a ābhāḥ ekaḥ anekaḥ vā yuktaḥ tasmāt uppalavaḥ eva ayam 
[227,vii_227,xi]	nanu sādharmya darśanāt loke bhrāntiḥ nāma upajāyate atadātmani tādātmya vyavasāyenā na iha tat adarśanāt jagati asmin ekasya api tad ātmanaḥ loke sādharmya darśanāt atad ātmani tādātmya vyavasāyena bhrāntiḥ vitatha ākārā buddhiḥ jāyate iti nāma prasiddham iha vijñapti naye tat sādharmya darśanam na asti ekasya api tad ātmanaḥ abhūta ākārasya jagati adarśanāt atra āha asti iyam api yā tu antar upaplava samudbhavā doṣa udbhavā prakṛtyā sā vitatha pratibhāsinī anapekṣita sādharmya dṛś ādiḥ taimira ādi vat 
[227,xii]	sādharmya darśana ādyāḥ mānasī bhrāntiḥ iyam api asti yā punar antar upaplava samudbhavā avidyā prabhavā sā prakṛtyā doṣa udbhavā avidyā timira ādi hetukā vitatha pratibhāsinya bhūta ākārāḥ anapekṣita sādharmya dṛś ādiḥ taimira ādi vat yathā timira jñānam indriya doṣāt anapekṣita sādharmyam eva jāyate tathā grāhya ādi bhrāntiḥ api iti arthaḥ jāyamānam eva hi jñānam vāsanā sāmarthyāt anubhavān anubhava tvena antar bbahis deśa tvena sukha ādi nīla ādi darśayati evam tarhi bahis artha upadarśana śaktam eva sva darśana hetu balāt kasmāt na iṣyata jñānam iti ced na svapna ādau avidyāyāḥ asat grāhya ākāra upadarśana sāmarthya upalabdheḥ ākāra atirikta bahis arthasya adarśanāt na jñānasya tad upadarśana sāmarthya kalpanā nyāyyā iti āstām tāvat idam 
[228,i_228,iii]	vijñaptimātra tāyām pramāṇa phala vyavasthāpana artham āha tatra buddheḥ paricchedaḥ grāhaka ākāra sammataḥ tad ā ātmyāt ātma vittasya sa tasya sādhanam tatas tatra vijñaptimātra tāyām buddheḥ sa grāhaka ākāraḥ saṃmataḥ paricchedaḥ ākāraḥ ātma vid tasya grāhaka ākārasya phalam tādātmyāt pariccheda svabhāva tvāt sva saṃvittiḥ phalam vā iti sūtre su ābhāsam viṣaya ābhāsañca jñānam utpadyate tatra yat sva saṃvedanantat phalam viṣayaḥ pariccheda ātmakaḥ eva hi grāhaka ākāraḥ saḥ eva ca ātma vedanam tatas pariccheda vaśena ātma vedana vyavasthānāt sa paricchedaḥ tasya ātma vidaḥ phala bhūtāyāḥ sādhanam pramāṇam 
[228,iv_228,v]	tatra ātma viṣaye māne yathā rāga ādi vedanam iyam sarvatra saṃyojyā māna meya phala sthitiḥ tatra evam satya ātma viṣaye māne sva saṃvedane pramāṇe yathā rāga ādi vedanam māna meya phala ātmakam iyam māna meya phala sthitiḥ sarvatra vijñaptinayepi saṃyojyā 
[228,vi_228,viii]	tathā hi tatra api anubhava ātma tvāt te yogyā sva ātma saṃvidi iti sā yogyatā mānam ātmā meyaḥ phalam sva vid tatra api rāga ādi vedanepi te rāga ādayaḥ anubhava ātma tvāt sva ātmanaḥ saṃvidi yogyāḥ iti tasmāt sā sva vedana yogya tā rāga ādīnām mānam ātmā meyaḥ phalam sva vid 
[229,i_229,iii]	nanu rāga ādiṣṭa ātma saṃvedanam phala bhūtam māna yuktam iha tu grāhaka ākāraḥ yogya tā lakṣaṇam pramāṇam ucyate iti vyāhatam iti śaṅkāyām uttaram grāhaka ākāra saṃkhyātā pariccheda ātma tā ātmani sā yogyatā iti ca proktam pramāṇam sva ātma vedanam yā grāhaka ākāra saṃkhyātā pariccheda ātma tā sā atmani saṃvedane yogyatā ca iti tasmāt rāga ādiṣu sva ātma saṃvedanam pramāṇam proktam na hi sva vedanam phala bhūtam iha vivakṣitam kintu yogya tā tasmāt abhinna artha tā eva 
[229,iv_229,vi]	nanu su ābhāsam tāvat astu jñānam pariccheda svabhāva tvāt viṣaya ābhāsam tu katham yathā viṣayam kāraṇam tathā cakṣuḥ ādiḥ api iti tat ākāra tā api syāt iti āha sarvam eva hi vijñānam viṣayebhyaḥ samudbhavat tad anyasya api hetu tve kathañcid viṣaya ākṛti sarvam eva hi jñānam viṣayebhyaḥ samudbhavat utpadyamānam tebhyaḥ viṣayebhyaḥ anyasya indriya ādeḥ api hetu tve kathañcid sva kāraṇa āyāta viṣaya gata śakti bhedāt viṣaya ākṛti bhavati na indriya ādi ākāram 
[229,vii_229,viii]	yathā eva āhāra kāla ādeḥ hetu tve apatya janmani pitroḥ tat ekasya ākāram dhatte na anyasya kasyacid yathā eva apatya janmani pitroḥ mātā pitroḥ āhāra kāla ādeḥ ca hetu tvepi tat ekasya pitroḥ mmadhye ekasya pituḥ mmātuḥ vākāram apatyam dhatte anyasya āhāra kāla ādeḥ ca kasyacid na 
[229,ix_229,x]	tad hetu tvena tulyepi tad anyaiḥ viṣaye matam viṣaya tvam tad aṃśena tad abhāve na tat bhavet yatas evam tat tasmāt tatas viṣayāt anyaiḥ indriya ādibhiḥ hetu tvena tulye sadṛśepi viṣaye rūpa ādau viṣaya tvam grāhya tvam tena su a ākāra arpaka tvena aṃśena viśeṣaṇam matam yasmāt ākāra arpaka tvam viṣaya lakṣaṇam avasthitam tasmāt tasya akāra arpakatvasya abhāve tad viṣaya tvam indriya ādiṣu na bhavet 
[230,i_230,iii]	kiñca anartha ākāra śaṅkā syāt api arthavati cetasi atīta artha grahe siddhe dvi rūpa tva ātma vedane arthavati cetasi anartha ākāra tā artha ākāra rahita tā śaṅkā syāt api dṛśyamānasya ākārasya artha tvena eva sambhāvyamāna tvāt atītasya arthasya grahe vikalpa ātmake tu arthasya ābhā vāt artha ābhāsa tayā ca dvi rūpa tvam tathā ca aparokṣa tvāt ātma saṃvedanam ca iti dve api astu siddhe na hi asan eva arthaḥ dṛśyate tatas artha ākāra tā sā jñānasya eva tathā arthena ca parokṣa tva abhāvāt svābhāsañca tat na ca anyena jñānena tat vedyate vedya vedaka bhāvasya niṣiddha tvāt atas sva vedanam eva tat 
[230,iv_230,vi]	syāt etat atītāḥ vyaktiḥ asattvāt na vikalpa viṣayaḥ jātisyu sattvāt syāt iti āha nīla ādi ābhāsa bheditvāt na arthaḥ jātiḥ atadvatī sā vā anityā na jātiḥ syāt nityāḥ vā janikā katham atīta vikalpasya nīla ādi ābhāsa bhedi tvāt varṇṇa saṃsthāna ādi ākāra viśeṣavat tvāt na jātiḥ atadvatī varṇṇa ādi ākāra rahita artheḥ viṣayaḥ kiñca jātiḥ viṣayī bhavantī anityā vā bhavet nityā vā sā ca anityāḥ jātiḥ na syāt nitya lakṣaṇa tvāt tasyāḥ nityāḥ vā buddheḥ janikā katham syāt 
[230,vii_231,i]	nityasya krama yaugapadyābhyām virahāt nāma nimitte viprayuktaḥ saṃskāraḥ viṣayaḥ ced iti āha nāma ādikam niṣiddham prāk na ayam arthavatām kramaḥ icchā mātra anurodhi tvāt artha śaktiḥ na sidhyati nāma ādikam viṣaya tvena niṣiddham prāknāma ādi vacane vaktṛ śrotṛ vācyā anubandhinī tyādinā kiñca arthavatām sa viṣayāṇām cakṣuḥ vijñāna ādīn ām ayam kramaḥ artha sāmarthyena vinā utpādaḥ iti na asti manaḥ vijñānānām tu artha sannidhāna anapekṣāṇām icchā mātra anurodhi tvāt janikā artha śaktiḥ na sidhyati na ca ahetuḥ arthī grāhyaḥ ati prasaṅgāt 
[231,ii_231,iv]	bhavatu atīta artha lambanam vijñānam viṣaya ākāram anubhavaḥ tu mā bhūt iti āha smṛtiḥ ca īdṛgvidham jñānam tasyāḥ ca anubhavāt bhavaḥ sa ca artha ākāra rahitaḥ sā idānīm tadvatī katham īdṛgvidham atīta vikalpana ātmakam jñānañca smṛtiḥ tasyāḥ ca anubhavāt bhavaḥ utpādaḥ na hi anubhavam antareṇa smṛtiḥ sa ca anubhavaḥ bhavat mate artha ākāra rahitaḥ idānīm asmin abhyupagame sā smṛtiḥ tadvatyartha ākāravatī katham astu yadi anubhava ārūḍhaḥ na artha ākāraḥ katham asau viditaḥ aviditasya kā smṛtiḥ 
[231,v_231,vii]	arthāt smṛtiḥ utpadyate iti ced āha na arthāt bhāvaḥ tadā abhāvāt syāt tathā anubhavepi saḥ ākāraḥ sa ca na arthasya spaṣṭa ākāra vivekataḥ na arthāt bhāvaḥ tasyāḥ tadā smṛti kāle abhāvāt atīta arthasya yathā ca arthāt utpadyamānāyāḥ smṛteḥ artha ākāraḥ bhavati tathā anubhavepi arthāt utpadyamāne saḥ artha ākāraḥ syāt api ca smṛti ārūḍhaḥ saḥ aspaṣṭaḥ ca ākāraḥ na arthasya anubhava ārūḍhāt spaṣṭāt artha ākārāt vivekataḥ bhedāt 
[231,viii_231,ix]	vyatiriktam tat ākāram pratīyāt aparaḥ tathā nityam ātmani sambandhe pratīyāt kathi tañca na yadi ca buddhi vyatiriktaḥ arthaḥ eva manaḥ vijñāna grāhyaḥ tadā buddheḥ vyatiriktam ekena vikalpyamānantat ākāram aparopi yogya deśa sthaḥ pramā na pratīyāt para upalabhyatām niṣeddhum nityam ātmani asya vikalpyasya arthasya sambandhe vā svīkriyamāṇe yadā svayam anucintayitum parasmai kathyate tadā kathañcid paraḥ na pratīyāt pratyeti ca kathitam
[232,i_232,ii]	ekaikena abhisambandhe pratisandhiḥ na yujyate eka artha abhiniveśa ātmā pravaktṛ śrotṛ cetasoḥ prati iti artham ekena ekena vaktrā śrotrā ca bhinnasya bhinnasya arthasya abhisambandhe atra api svīkrimāṇe pravaktṛ śrotṛ cetasoḥ pratisandhiḥ eka artha abhiniveśāt yat eva anena kathitam tat eva mayā pratītam yat eva mayā kathitam tat eva anena jñātam iti abhinna artha adhyavasāya rūpaḥ na yujyate 
[232,iii_232,iv]	tat eka vyavahāraḥ ced sādṛśyāt atad ābhayoḥ bhinna ātmā arthaḥ katham grāhyaḥ tadā syāt dhīra narthikā vaktṛ śrotṛ sambandhinoḥ tayoḥ arthayoḥ eka vyavahāraḥ eka tva avasāyaḥ sādṛśyāt ced tad ubhaya darśane sādṛśyam na ca atra darśanam bhavatu vā tathā api atada abhayoḥ bhinna ātma sambandha artha apratibhāsinoḥ vaktṛ śrotṛ cetasoḥ bhinna ātmā arthaḥ katham grāhyaḥ yadā ca artha abhedaḥ na asti tadā abhinna artha adhyavasāyinī dhīḥ vaktṛ śrotroḥ anarthikā syāt yathārtham buddheḥ abhāvāt yathābuddhi ca artha abhāvāt 
[232,v_232,ix]	bhavatu tāvat evam smṛtiḥ viṣaya ākārā anubhava jñānam tu anākṛti syāt iti āha tat ca anubhava vijñānena ubhaya aṃśauvalaṃbinā eka ākāra viśeṣeṇa tat jñānena anubudhyate tat ca anubha viṣayeṇa smaraṇena anuba dhyate anugamyate smaryate iti yāvat kīdṛśena ubhaya aṃśa avalambinā jñeya prācīna jñāna gata viṣaya ākāra anubhava rūpa dharma dvaya viṣayeṇa katham anubadhyate iti āha ekasmāt avivāda siddhāt anubhava ākārāt viśeṣaḥ viṣaya ākāraḥ tena smaraṇa jñānena hi vijñāna maryākāra anubhava ākāra viśiṣṭam eva smaryate tatas tādṛśam eva tat 
[233,i_233,ii]	anyathā hi atathārūpam katham jñānedhirohati eka ākāra uttaram jñānam tathā hi uttaram uttaram anyathā atathā rūpam ākāra dvaya rahitam anubhava jñānam sva grāhiṇi smaraṇa jñāne katham dvi ākāram adhirohati adhirūḍham ca tatas dvi ākāram tat tathā jñānam uttaram uttaram buddhi pūrva jñāna ālambanam eka ākāra uttaram ekena ekena ākāreṇa adhikam pratīyate arthejñānena tad ālambakaḥ ekaḥ artha ākāraḥ pratīyate tad ālambanena tu viṣaya bhūta jñāna ākāraḥ tad ālambakaḥ ca su a ākāraḥ 
[233,iii_233,iv]	tasya artha rūpeṇa ākārau ātma ākāraḥ ca kaścana dvitīyasya tṛtīyena jñānena hi vivicyate yasmāt tasya dvitīyasya jñānasya tau dvau ākārau artha rūpeṇa viṣaya bhāvena tad ālambakaḥ ātma ākāraḥ ca kaścana tṛtīyena dvitīya jñāna ālambakena hi yasmāt vivecyate avadhāryate tasmāt artha ākāram sva vedanañca jñānam abhyupagantavyam 
[233,v_233,ix]	artha kārya tayā jñāna smṛtau artha smṛteḥ yadi bhrāntyā saṅkalanam atha nirākāram eva jñānam arthasya kāryam anubhava rūpam artha kārya tayā jñāta smṛtau viśeṣaṇa tvena arthasya smṛteḥ smaryamāṇasya arthasya bhrāntyā jñāna ātmani saṃkalanam sambandhanam yadi syāt tadā kaḥ doṣaḥ āha jyotiḥ manaskāre ca sā bhavet arthavat jyotiṣaḥ ālokasya manaskārasya ca jñāna hetu tvāt tad kārya jñāne smaryamāṇe sā smṛtiḥ jyotiḥ manaskāre āloka samanantara pratyayoḥ api syāt tatra bhrāntyā artha ākāram iva āloka manaskāra ākāram api saṃkalanīyam na tu artha ākāram eva niyamena saṃkalayitum yuktam 
[233,x_234,i]	sarveṣām api kāryyāṇām kāraṇaiḥ syāt tathā grahaḥ kulāla ādi vivekena na smaryeta ghaṭaḥ tatas yadi ca artha kāryam bhrāntyā smaryate tadā sarveṣām api kāryyāṇām kāraṇaiḥ saha tathā grahaḥ kāraṇa ātma tvena grahaṇam syāt tatas ca dhaṭa kulāla ādi kāryam kulāla ādeḥ vivekena bhedena na smaryeta 
[234,ii_234,iv]	atha asti eva kaścid āloka ādibhyaḥ viṣayasya jñāna ātmani āropaṇīyaḥ viśeṣaḥ tatas tad ākāra avagraheṇa smaryate na anyathā iti āha yasmāt atiśayāt jñānam artha saṃsarga bhājanam sārūpyāt tat kim anyat syāt dṛṣṭeḥ ca yamala ādiṣu yasmāt artha āropitāt atiśayāt jñānam artha saṃsargasya artha saṃśleṣasya bhājanam pātram bhavati arthena sārūpyāt anyat kintat syāt sārūpyāt anyasya atiśayasya upalakṣaṇa tva ayogāt yamala ādiṣu sārūpyāt bhrāntyā tathā artha niścayasya dṛṣṭeḥ ca 
[234,v_234,vii]	kiñca ādya anubhaya rūpa tve hi eka rūpam vyavasthitam dvitīyam vyatiricyeta na parāmarśa cetasā ādyasya artha jñānasya anubhaya rūpa tve artha ākāra rahita tvāt anubhava eka rūpa tve tad ālambakam dvitīyam jñānam ekasmin rūpe anubhava ātmani vyavasthitam parāmarśa cetasā jñāna jñāna ālambakena tṛtīya jñānena na vyatiricyeta na viṣaya jñāna grāhaka tayā bhedena gṛhyeta sva ābhāsa mātra tvena sarvasya aviśeṣāt 
[234,viii_234,ix]	artha saṃkalana āśleṣā dhīḥ dvitīya avalambate nīla ādi rūpeṇa dhiyam bhāsamānām puras tatas yatas buddheḥ anākāra tve doṣaḥ ayam tatas puras arthasya dhiyam nīla ādi rūpeṇa bhāsamānām dvitīyā dhīḥ artha saṃkalanasya artha ākāra avagrahasya āśleṣaḥ saṃsarggaḥ yasyāḥ sā tām avalambate 
[234,x_235,i]	anyathā hi ādyam eva ekam saṃyojyeta artha sambhavāt jñānam na adṛṣṭa sambandham pūrva arthena uttarottaram anyathā yadi anākāram jñānam artha kārya tayā bhrāntyā artha ākāram smaryate iti āśrīyate tad ādyam eva ekam artha jñānam smṛtyā arthena saṃyojyeta arthāt saṃbhavāt tasya na uttarottaram jñānam pūrvasya jñānasya arthena akāraṇa bhūtena adṛṣṭa sambandham saṃyojyeta tasmāt sthitam etat jñānānām viṣaya sārūpya anubhava rūpa tvābhyām dvi ākāra tvam tatas ca saha upalambha niyamaḥ artha vijñānayoḥ artha ākāra tāyāḥ artha upalambhāt anubhava rūpa tāyāḥ svave dana tvāt 
[235,ii_235,iv]	tathā ca sakṛt samvedyamānasya niyamena dhiyā saha viṣayasya tatas anya tvam kena ākāreṇa sidhyati dhiyā saha niyamena sakṛt saṃvedyamānasya viṣayasya tatas dhiyaḥ anya tvam bhedaḥ kena ākāreṇa prakāreṇa sidhyati bhinnayoḥ saha upalambha niyama ayogāt 
[235,v_235,x]	yadi viṣaya jñānayoḥ abhedaḥ tadā grāhya grāhaka tayā bhedaḥ katham pratibhāti iti āha bhedaḥ ca bhrānta vijñānaiḥ dṛśyeta indau iva advaye bhedaḥ ca vāsanā vaśāt bhrāntam upapluta ākāram jñānam yeṣām taiḥ arvāk darśibhiḥ dṛśyeta indau iva advaye eka rūpe dvaitam timira upahata buddhibhiḥ bhedepi kasmāt na saha upalambha niyamaḥ iti āha saṃvitti niyamaḥ na asti bhinnayoḥ nīla pītayoḥ bhinnayoḥ nīla pītayoḥ saṃvitti niyamaḥ na asti tatas yatra asti tatra abhedaḥ eva 
[235,xi_236,i]	tathā hi na arthaḥ asamvedanaḥ kaścid anartham vā api vedanam dṛṣṭam samvedyam ānantat tayoḥ na asti viveki tā tasmāt arthasya durvāram jñāna kāla avabhāsinaḥ jñānāt avyatireki tvam na artha unubhavam antareṇa kaścid dṛṣṭaḥ vedanañcā artha ākāramvinā na dṛṣṭam samvedyamānam tat tasmāt tayoḥ artha tad upalambhayoḥ na asti vivedhitā tasmāt jñāna kāla avabhāsinorthasya artha jñānayoḥ api saha saṃvitti jñā nāt avyatireki tvam abhinna tvam durvāram iti upasaṃhāraḥ syāt etat hetu bheda anumā bhavet abhāvāt akṣa buddhīnām satsu api anyeṣu hetuṣu niyamam yadi na brūyāda pratyayāt samanantarāt 
[236,ii]	satsu api anyeṣu indriya ādiṣu hetuṣu akṣa buddhīnām abhāvāt hetu bhedasya tad atiriktasya kāraṇa viśeṣasya anumā bhavet kāraṇa sākalye sati tanmātra sādhyasya kāryasya anutpāda ayogāt yaḥ ca asau kāraṇa bhedaḥ sa bāhyaḥ arthaḥ bhaviṣyayi iti manyate paraḥ evam api anumāna gamyaḥ bahis arthaḥ bhavet na pratyakṣaḥ yathā iṣyate kintu vyatireka sāmarthyāt api tadā arthaḥ sidhyeta yadi yoga ācāraḥ nānā artha pratibhāsinīnām dhiyām utpāda kramasya niyamaṃyathā pratyayam prabuddha vāsanā garbhāt samanantara pratyayāt na brūyāt 
[236,iii_236,iv]	bījāt aṃkura janma anneḥ dhūmāt siddhiḥ iti īdṛśī bāhya artha āśrayiṇī yā api kāraka jñāpaka sthitiḥ nanu bāhya arthāḥ bhāve bījāt aṅkurasya janma iti īdṛśī evaṃjātīyā yā api pratīti siddhā kāraka sthitiḥ dhūmāt kāryāt kāraṇasya agneḥ siddhiḥ iti īdṛśī yā api jñāpaka hetu sthitiḥ tad ucchedaḥ syāt hetu phala bhāva āśrayasya bāhyasya eva abhāvāt 
[236,v_236,vii]	atra āha sā api tad rūpa nirbhāsā tathā niyata saṅgamāḥ buddhīḥ āśritya kalpyeta yadi kim vā virudhyate sā kāraka jñāpaka sthitiḥ api tad rūpa nirbhāsā bīja aṅkura dhūma agni pratibhāsavāsanā pratiniyamāt tathā krama viśeṣeṇa niyataḥ saṅgamaḥ utpādaḥ yāsām tāḥ buddhīḥ āśritya yadi kalpyate tadā kim vā virudhyeta na kiñcid hi bīja pratibhāsam jñānam sva hetoḥ prabuddha aṅkura jñāna vāsanā pāṭavam aṅkura jñānam janayati evam dhūma jñānam agni jñānam utpādayati tāvatā eva ca jñāpaka vyavasthāyāḥ avirodhaḥ 
[237,i_237,iii]	nanu asti virodhaḥ tathā hi anagni janyaḥ dhūmaḥ syāt tad kāryāt kāraṇe agatiḥ na syāt kāraṇa tāyām vā kutas ekāntataḥ gatiḥ dhūma jñānāt agni jñāna utpāde anagni janyaḥ dhūmaḥ syāt agni pratibhāsasya prāk avidyamāna tvāt viparyayaḥ syāt tat tasmāt kāryāt kāraṇe gatiḥ na syāt agni jñānam prati dhūma jñānasya kāraṇa tāyām vā kāraṇāt kāryaekāntataḥ asaṃdigdhā kutas gatiḥ iti
[237,iv_237,vi]	atra āha tatra api dhūma ābhāsā dhīḥ prabodha paṭu vāsanām gamayet agni nirbhāsān dhiyam eva na pāvakam tatra dhūmāt agni anumānepi dhūma ābhāsā dhīḥ agni vāsanā pratibaddhāḥ eka sāma gagrayadhīna tayā agni nirbhāsān dhiyam eva dhūma jñānāt eva prabodhena paṭu janana unmukhāḥ vāsanā śaktiḥ yasya aḥ tāṅgamayet na pāvakam bāhya rūpam sarvadā adarśanāt 
[237,vii_237,ix]	agni vāsanā dhūma jñānayoḥ hetu phala tām ākhyātum āha tad yogya vāsanā garbhaḥ eva dhūma avabhāsinīm vyanakti citta santānaḥ dhiyam dhūma ugnitaḥ tatas tasya agni pratibhāsasya yogyā janana samarthāḥ vāsanā garbhe svabhāva bhūtāḥ yasya citta santānasya sa cittaṃsantānaḥ dhūma avabhāsinīm dhiyam vyanakti utpādayati tatas agnitaḥ eva dhūmaḥ bhavati iti na kārya kāraṇa tā viparyayaḥ na ca kāraṇāt kārya anumānam agni vāsanā prabhava tvāt dhūma agni jñānayoḥ dhūma jñānāt prabuddha agni vāsanā t vāreṇa agni jñāna anumitiḥ eka sāmagrayadhīnā 
[237,x_238,ii]	evantarhi vijñāna nayaḥ eva sarva vyavasthā nama virodhāt katham ācāryeṇa bahis artha apekṣayā jñāna dvi rūpa tā uktā iti āha asti eṣa viduṣām vādaḥ bāhyantu āśritya varṇyate dvairūpyam saha saṃvitti niyamāt tat ca sidhyati asti eṣa sarva vyavasthāsu vijñaptimātra tā pratipādakaḥ viduṣām nyāya darśinām yaḥ gā cā rā ṇām vādaḥ sautra antikaiḥ iṣṭam bāhyam artham āśritya jñānasya dvairūpyam ācāryeṇa varṇyate tat ca dvairūpyam saha samvedana niyamāt saha upalambha niyamāt sidhyati bhedepi sati tad abhāvāt 
[238,iii_238,v]	dvairūpya siddhau upapatti antaram vaktum āha jñānam indriya bhedena paṭu manda āvila ādikām pratibhāsa bhidām arthe vibhradekatra dṛśyate indriyasya bhedena prasāda upaghāta ādinā viśeṣeṇa puruṣa arthe jñānam paṭu manda āvila ādikām pratibhāsa bhidām vibhrat dadhat dṛśyate 
[238,vi_238,vii]	arthasya abhinna rūpa tvāt eka rūpam bhavet manaḥ sarvam tad artham arthāt ced tasya na asti tad ābhatā tasya jñānasya arthāt ced na asti tad ābhatā a rtha ākāra tā tadā arthasya abhinna rūpa tvāt tad artha tad viṣayam sarvam manaḥ vedanam eka rūpam bhavet na paṭu mandā vilatā ādi bhinnam jñānasya sva gata ākāra bheda anabhyupagamāt arthasya eka rūpa tvāt pratibhāsa bheda virodhāt asti ca ayam tasmāt artha rūpa tā anubhava rūpa tā ca iti dvairūpya siddhiḥ 
[238,viii_238,x]	nanu artha rūpa tāyām api arthasya eka rūpa tvāt tat sarūpam jñānam eka ākāram syāt na prasanna āvila ādi rūpam iti āha artha āśrayeṇa udbhavataḥ tad rūpam anukurvataḥ tasya kenacid aṃśena paratopi bhidā bhavet arthasya sarūpasya āśrayeṇa udbhavataḥ tasya jñānasya tad rūpam artha ākāram anukurvataḥ kenacid aṃśena ākāreṇa paṭu manda tva ādinā paratas vāsanā ādeḥ api kāraṇāt bhidā bhavet 
[239,i_239,ii]	tathā hi āśritya pitaram tad rūpaḥ hi sutaḥ pituḥ bhedam kenacid aṃśena kutaścid avalambate tathā hi pitaram āśritya tad rūpaḥ pitṛ ākāra upi sutaḥ utpannaḥ kenacid aṃśena ākāreṇa kutaścid karmma ādeḥ hetoḥ pituḥ sakāśāt bheda m anyādṛśa tvam avalamvate pitāputrayoḥ sarvathā sāmya abhāvāt 
[239,iii_239,v]	dvairūpya siddhau upapatti antaram āha mayūra candraka ākāram nīlalohita bhāsvaram sampaśyanti pradīpa ādeḥ mmaṇḍalam manda cakṣuṣaḥ mayūra candraka ākāram antarā antarā nīlalohita bhāsvaram dīptam pradīpa ādeḥ maṇḍalam avidyamānam eva manda cakṣuṣaḥ saṃpaśyanti dīpasya tādṛśa svarūpa abhāvāt jñānasya anubhava ātmanaḥ saḥ ākāraḥ iti dvairūpya siddhiḥ 
[239,vi_239,viii]	atha tādṛśam vastu eva utpannam dṛśyate iti na jñāna ākāraḥ iti āha tasya tad bāhya rūpa tve kā prasanna īkṣaṇe akṣamā bhūtam paśyan ca tad darśī kathañca upahata indriyaḥ śodhitam timireṇa asya vyaktam cakṣuḥ atīndriyam paśyataḥ anyākṣa dṛśya irthe tat avyaktam katham punar tasya maṇḍalasya tad bāhya rūpa tve abhyupagamyamāne prasanna īkṣaṇe draṣṭari kā akṣamā dveṣaḥ yena asmai na ātmānam upadarśayet yat vastupahata indriyeṇa dṛśyate tad anupahata indriyeṇa sutarām dṛśyate bhūtam satyam ca paśyan tad darśī maṇḍaladarśī katham upahata indriyaiḥ aparaiḥ adṛśyam maṇḍalam paśyataḥ asya manda cakṣuṣṭvena naṣṭasya timireṇa vyaktam cakṣuḥ śodhitam iti upahasati kintu taimirikasya atīndriya artha darśana kṣamam tat cakṣuḥ anyasya ataimirikasya akṣa dṛśye arthe pradīpe katham punar avyaktam asphuṭam yat atīndriyam paśyati tat sarvam dṛśyam sutarām paśyati 
[239,ix_240,i]	kiñca āloka akṣamanaskārāt anyasya ekasya gamyate śaktiḥ hetuḥ tatas na anyaḥ ahetuḥ ca viṣayaḥ katham āloka akṣamanaskārāt anyasya dīpasya ekasya maṇḍala jñāna janane śaktiḥ ggamyate tanmātra bhāvena bhāvāt tatas dīpāt anyaḥ maṇḍalaḥ na hetuḥ ahetuḥ ca asau maṇḍala jñānasya katham viṣayoti prasaṅgāt 
[240,ii_240,vi]	saḥ eva yadi dhī hetuḥ kimpradīpam apekṣate sa maṇḍalaḥ eva maṇḍala grāhiṇyāḥ dhiyaḥ hetuḥ na dīpaḥ yadi iṣyate tadā maṇḍalam kim kasmāt pradīpam apekṣate na hi ahetoḥ apekṣā ati prasaṅgāt dīpaḥ maṇḍalañca maṇḍala buddhi hetuḥ iti āha dīpa mātreṇa dhībhāvāt ubhayat na api kāraṇam ubhayam na kāraṇam dīpa mātreṇa maṇḍala dhiyaḥ bhāvāt 
[240,vii_240,viii]	dūra āsanna ādi bhedena vyakta avyaktam na yujyate tat syāt āloka bhedāt ced tad pidhāna apidhānayoḥ yadi ca arthaḥ eva sa ākāraḥ grāhyaḥ jñānantu anākāram tadā arthasya dūra āsanna ādinā bhedena viśeṣeṇa vyakta avyaktam na yujyate eka ātmanaḥ padārthasya svarūpeṇa dṛśyamāna tvāt dūra āsanna sthābhyām samānaḥ pratīyeta jñāna svagata ākāra bheda anabhyupagamāt vyavaghāna avyavadhānayoḥ ālokasya māndyāmāndya bhedāt tat vyakta avyaktam vastu syāt iti ced dūra sthitau tasya ālokasya pidhānam apidhānañcā abhyupagantavyam tayoḥ tulyayoḥ 
[240,ix_240,x]	tulyā dṛṣṭiḥ adṛṣṭiḥ vā sūkṣma ūṃśaḥ tasya kaścana ālokena ca mandena dṛśyatetas bhidā yadi sarvasya pratipattuḥ dṛṣṭiḥ adṛṣṭiḥ vā tulya arthasya syāt dūra sthasya rajaḥ nīhāra ādibhiḥ upahata tvāt mandena ālokena tasya dṛśya arthasya sūkṣmaḥ aśaḥ avayavaḥ kaścana na dṛśyate atas sannikṛṣṭāt vyaktam dṛśyamānāt arthāt avyakta tvena bhidā yadi ucyate tadā api dvayī kalpanā 
[241,i_241,iii]	yosau sthavīyān dṛśyate saḥ ekaḥ anekaḥ vā ekatverthasya bāhyasya dṛśya adṛśya bhidā kutas aneka tve aṇuśas bhinne dṛśya adṛśya bhidā kutas tatra ekatve arthasya bāhyasya abhyupagamyamāne dṛśya adṛśya bhidā kutas śaṅkitā evam dṛśyam adṛśyam eva vā syāt ekāntena aneka tve dṛśyasya arthasya abhyupagamyamāne aṇuśas bhinne asmin dṛśya adṛśya bhidā kutas na hi aṇuṣu api sthūla sūkṣma bhedaḥ yena kiñcid upalabhyeta kiñcid nā iti vibhāgaḥ 
[241,iv_241,v]	māndya pāṭava bhedena bhāsaḥ buddhi bhidā yadi bhinne anyasmin abhinnasya kutas bhedena bhāsanam atha eka rūpepi arthe bhāsaḥ ālokasya māndya pāṭava bhedena spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa tayā bhedaḥ buddheḥ yadi iṣyate tadā api anyasmin āloke paṭu manda tayā bhinne abhinnasya arthasya svarūpeṇa dṛśyamānasya kutas bhedena spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa tayā bhāsanam yuktam 
[241,vi_241,viii]	kiñca mandantat api tejaḥ kim āvṛtteḥ iha sā na kim tanu tvan tejasā upyetat asti anyatra api atānavam vyavahita vastu antarāla vartti tejaḥ mandam kim kasmāt hetaḥ rajaḥ nīhāra ādibhiḥ tad deśa varttibhiḥ āvṛtteḥ ālokaḥ mandaḥ iti ced iha sannihitavastu antarāla varttini āloke sā rajaḥ nīhāra ādibhiḥ āvṛttiḥ kinna bhavati tanu tvāt ā ārakasya nīhāra ādeḥ nna āvṛttiḥ ced tad tanu tvam tejasā upi sannihita vastu antarāla varttinaḥ asti iti sannihitañca vastu na sphuṭam pratīyate tathā anyatra dūra stham vastu sphuṭam pratīyet dūra sthe vastuni āvāraka ālokayoḥ samānam ata anavam samīpa sthe ca samam tānavam iti na syāt pratīti bhedaḥ 
[241,ix_241,xi]	kiñca ati āsanne ca su vyaktam tejaḥ tat syāt ati sphuṭam tatra api adṛṣṭam āśritya bhavet rūpa antaram yadi locanasya ati āsanne śalākā ādau su vyaktam tejaḥ āvārakasya tanu tvāt iti tad ati āsannam śalākā ādikam ati sphuṭam syāt na ca manāga vyavahitam iva ati āsannam vastu sphuṭam īkṣyate tatra dūrātyāsatti bhedena vyakta avyakta darśana īpi adṛṣṭam dharma adharmam āśritya apekṣya rūpa antaram vyakta avyaktam jāyate iti yadi ucyate 
[242,i_242,ii]	anyonya āvaraṇāt teṣām syāt tejaḥ vihatiḥ tatas tatra ekam eva dṛśyeta tasya anāvaraṇe sakṛt tadā teṣām vyakta avyaktānām rūpāṇām anyonyasya āvaraṇāt kadācid kasyacid upalambhaḥ bhavati iti vaktavyam tatas eka upalambha kāle apara upalambha hetoḥ tejasaḥ vihatiḥ āvṛtiḥ iti ca syāt anyathā na avṛtte tasmin aparasya api upalabdhiḥ syāt avaikalyāt sāmagryāḥ tatra apara upalambha hetoḥ ālokasya āvaraṇe sati ekam eva vyaktam avyakta svarūpam dūra āsannādi deśa sthitaiḥ pratipattṛbhiḥ sarvaiḥ dṛśyeta na tu ekena vyaktam itareṇa ca avyaktam iti syāt tasya adṛṣṭa utpanna rūpasya parasparam anāvaraṇe tejasaḥ ca anāvaraṇe sakṛt 
[242,iii_242,iv]	paśyet sphuṭa asphuṭam rūpam ekaḥ adṛṣṭena vāraṇe artha anarthau na yena staḥ tat adṛṣṭam karoti kim sphuṭa asphuṭam rūpam paśyet ekaḥ pratipattā dṛśya rūpa dvayasya darśana hetoḥ ca ālokasya anāvaraṇāt adṛṣṭena dvitīyasya rūpasya varaṇe vyaktam avyaktam eva vā rūpam ekam dṛśyate iti ced yena dvitīya rūpa āvaraṇena kṛtena puṃsaḥ artha anarthau adṛṣṭa kāryau na staḥ sambhavataḥ tad āvaraṇam adṛṣṭam karttṛ kim kasmāt karoti śubha aśubha lakṣaṇam hi adṛṣṭam artha anartha phalam yat punar anubhava svabhāvam tat dṛṣṭa phalam eva bhavati 
[242,v_242,vii]	yasmāt sarvam anantara uktam asaṃgatam tasmāt saṃvid yathā hetu jāyamāna artha saṃśrayāt pratibhāsa bhidām dhatte śeṣāḥ kumati durnnayāḥ tasmāt artha saṃśrayāt jāyamānā saṃvid buddhiḥ yathā hetu vāsanā prabodha hetu anatikrameṇa pratibhāsasi a ākārasya vyakta avyakta ādeḥ bhidām dhatte vibhartti iti nyāyyam tad itare punar āloka bheda upanyāsa ādyāḥ śeṣāḥ kumatiḥ durnayāḥ para vādinām kumatīnām durvimarśāḥ 
[243,i_243,iii]	kiñca anākāreṇa jñānena arthaḥ kṣaṇikaḥ akṣaṇikaḥ vā vyajyeta tatra jñāna śabda pradīpānām pratyakṣasya itarasya vā janakatvena pūrveṣām kṣaṇikānām vināśataḥ kṣaṇikānām jñāna śabda pradīpa ādīnām sva viṣayasya pratyakṣasya apratyakṣasya vā jñānasya janakatvena hetūnām pūrveṣām jñāna kāle vināśataḥ
[243,iv_243,vii]	vyaktiḥ kutas asatām jñānāt asatām jñānāt kutas vyaktiḥ yadā arthaḥ tadā na jñānam yadā jñānam tadā na arthaḥ iti kutas vyaṅgya vyañjaka bhāvaḥ tayoḥ atha śabda ādayaḥ jñānena saha dvitīyam sva upādeya kṣaṇam janayanti saḥ eva tena jñānena vyajyate na itarat iti āha anyasya anupakāriṇaḥ vyaktau vyajyeta sarva urthaḥ tad hetoḥ niyamaḥ yadi sva kāraṇāt anyasya saha utpannasya anupakāriṇaḥ vyakti vivakṣāyām sarvaḥ arthaḥ samāna kālena jñānena vyajyatām anupakāraka tva aviśeṣāt tasmāt saha utpādakāt hetoḥ anupakāraka tva viśeṣeṣu api saha utpannaḥ eva arthaḥ jñānena vyajyate iti niyamaḥ yadi kalpyate
[243,viii_243,ix]	na eṣā api kalpanāḥ jñāne jñānantu artha avabhāsataḥ tam vyanakti itim kathyeta tad abhāvepi tad kṛtam tadā eṣā api kalpanā na yuktāḥ jñāne vyañjaka tvasya saha utpanna indriya ādi vyañjaka tva prasaṅgāt asmākam mate tu sa ākāram tena arthena kṛtam jñānam iti jñānasya kāle tasya arthasya abhāva ipi artha avabhāsatortha ākārāt saṃvedyamānāt tam artham vyanakti iti kathyate anyasya artha vyakti prakārasya ayogāt 
[243,x_243,xii]	saha utpannasya api tarhi su a ākāra jñānena vyaktiḥ syāt iti āha na ākārayati ca anya ūrthaḥ anupakārāt saha uditaḥ vyaktonākārayat jñānam su a ākāreṇa katham bhavet kāraṇāt anyasya anyaḥ ca arthaḥ saha utpannaḥ jñānam na ākārayati su a ākāreṇa viśeṣayati anupakārāt na hi anupakāraka ākāreṇa viśiṣyate ati prasaṅgāt yaḥ ca arthaḥ jñānam na akārayati sa katham vyaktaḥ bhavet 
[244,i_244,iii]	akṣaṇikasya api arthasya vyaktim niṣeddhum āha vajra upalādiḥ api arthaḥ sthiraḥ sonya anapekṣaṇāt sakṛt sarvasya janayet jñānāni jagataḥ samam yaḥ vajra upalādiḥ sthiraḥ arthaḥ saḥ api jñāna utpādana svabhāva tvena anyasya sahakāriṇaḥ anupakārakasya anapekṣaṇāt sakṛt sarvasya jagataḥ sva grāhakāṇi jñānāni samam eka kālam janayet 
[244,iv_244,vi]	na ca etat asti kramāt bhavanti tāni asya saha kāri upakāryataḥ āhuḥ pratikṣaṇam bhedam sa doṣaḥ atra api pūrvavat krameṇa utpādāt kramāt bhavanti jāyamāna anitāni vajra ādi jñānāni asya vajra upala ādeḥ sahakāriṇām upakārāt svabhāva antara lakṣaṇāt pratikṣaṇam bheda manya svabhāva tām āhuḥ yathā ca pūrvavat śabda ādiṣu iva atra vajra ādiṣu api kṣaṇikeṣu vijñānāt pūrva kāla bhāviṣu saḥ avyakti doṣa prasaṅgaḥ tad avasthaḥ 
[244,vii_244,ix]	punar buddheḥ artha ākāra siddhi artham āha saṃvedanasya tādātmye na vivāda usti kasyacid tasya artha rūpa tā asiddhā sā api sidhyate saṃsmṛteḥ samvedanasya tādātmye anubhava rūpa tve kasyacid viduṣaḥ vādaḥ na asti tasya saṃvedanasya artha rūpa tā vivādāt asiddhā sā artha ākāra tā api saṃsmṛteḥ artha ābhāsa anubhavasya samyak smaraṇāt sidhyati 
[245,i_245,ii]	bhedena ananubhūtesmin avibhakte sva gocaraiḥ evam etat na khalu evam iti sā syāt na bhedini asmin artha saṃvedanena bhedena anubhūte sva sya gocaraiḥ artheḥ su a ākāra samarpaṇa dvāreṇa avibhakte para sparataḥ bhedena vyavasthāpite etat jñānam evam ghaṭa grāhakam na khalu evam na eva ghaṭagrāhakam iti sā samvedana smṛtiḥ bhedinī vibhāgavatī na syāt jñānena saha 
[245,iii_245,iv]	na ca anubhava mātreṇa kaścid bhedaḥ vivecakaḥ vivekinī na ca aspaṣṭa bhede dhīrī a mala ādi vat na ca anubhava mātreṇa avāntara bhinnena pratijñānam kaścid bhedaḥ vidyamānopi parasparam vivecakaḥ bheda vyavasthāpana hetuḥ tathāvidhā aspaṣṭe bhede sati api dhīḥ smṛti rūpā vivekinī na bhavati kintu eka bodha adhyavasāyinī pratyabhijñā eva sya ādi amala ādi vat yamalayoḥ artha antara bheda sadbhāvā ipi ekaḥ dṛśyamānaḥ na aparasmāt bhedena avasīyate kintu eka tvena eva pratyabhijñāyate 
[245,v_245,vii]	tasmāt artha ākāra anubhava ākāra tayā buddhiḥ dvi rūpā eva dvairūpya sādhanena api prāyas siddham sva vedanam sva rūpa bhūta ābhāsasya tadā saṃvedana īkṣaṇāt jñānānām dvairūpya sādhanena api prāyas bāhulyena sva vedanam jñānam siddham tathā ajñānasya svarūpa bhūtasya ābhāsasya ākārasya tadā dvi rūpa jñāna utpatti kāle saṃvedanāt anubhūteḥ īkṣaṇāt 
[245,viii_245,x]	jñāna antareṇa sarūpeṇa jñānam arthavat vedyate iti ced tadā dhiyā atad rūpayā jñāne niruddhe anubhavaḥ katham svañca rūpam na sā vetti iti utsanna unubhavaḥ akhilaḥ dhiyā atad rūpayā agrāhya jñāna svarūpayā niruddhe grāhye jñāne katham anubhavaḥ sva kāla ijñānam na vedyate grāhaka kāle grāhyasya eva abhāvaḥ iti katham buddhi vedanam svañca rūpam tvad mate sā buddhiḥ na vetti iti anubhavaḥ akhilaḥ arthasya jñānasya ca utsannaḥ syāt jñāna prakāśaḥ hi artha prakāśaḥ sa ca sva para kālayoḥ na asti iti prakāśaḥ na syāt sarvasya 
[246,i_246,iii]	kiñca bahirmukhañca tat jñānam bhāti artha pratibhāsa vat buddheḥ ca grāhikā vittiḥ nnityam antar mukha ātmani asya arthasya grāhyasya pratibhāsa vat ākāra vat tat bāhya grāhakam jñānam bahirmukham bāhya tayā pratibhāti yathā nīla ādi jñānam buddheḥ ca ātmani grāhikā vittiḥ nityam sarvakālam antar mukhā abāhya tayā grāhaka tvena pratibhāti tat etat sva vedana tāyām eva upapannam 
[246,iv_246,vi]	yadi tu buddhi antara grāhikā buddhiḥ syāt tadā nīla ādi vat smaryamāṇā atīta sva buddhi vat ca grāhaka ākāra tvāt bahiṣṭvena avabhāseta tathā sva vedana tā abhāve yaḥ yasya viṣaya ābhāsaḥ tam vetti na tat iti api prāptām kā saṃvid anyā asti tādrūpyāt iti ced matam yaḥ viṣayasya ābhāse ākāraḥ yasya jñānasya tam su a ākāra arpakam viṣayam tat ākāra vat jñānam na vetti iti prāptam viṣaya svarūpasya ātmanaḥ vedane hi viṣaya vedanam tad parokṣa tayā arthopi parokṣaḥ syāt yatas artha svarūpa dhī vedanādanyā kā saṃvid arthasya asti tādrūpyāt viṣaya sārūpyāt asva saṃvedanāt arthasya saṃvid iti ced matam 
[246,vii_246,ix]	evam sati prāptam saṃvedanam sarva sadṛśānām parasparam buddhiḥ sarūpā tat vicced na idānīm vid sa rūpikā sarveṣām yamalaka ādīnām sadṛśānām parasparam samvedanam prāptam na sadṛśaḥ iti eva anubhavaḥ sarūpā tad vid arthasya saṃvedanañced idānīm asmin abhyupagame sarūpekā vinna bhavati sārūpyam vedana lakṣaṇam na bhavati kintu anubhava rūpa tā sati api sārūpye yamalaka ādīnām anubhava tvāt na api sārūpyavāhita anubhava mātram vedanam kintu sva saṃvedanam sārūpyam 
[247,i_247,v]	yadi sārūpya vaśāt vedanam tadā buddhi ātmanā api sārūpyāt vedanam syāt tathā grāhya grāhakayoḥ bhedaḥ eva prāptaḥ iti āha svayam sonubhavaḥ tasyāḥ na sa sārūpya kāraṇaḥ tasyāḥ buddheḥ saḥ anubhavaḥ aparokṣa tvam svayam svarūpeṇa tathā utpatteḥ na sārūpya kāraṇaḥ saḥ anubhavaḥ buddheḥ evam tarhi bāhyepi arthe buddhi sārūpyam niṣphalam iti āha kriyā karmma vyavasthāyāḥ tat loke syāt nibandhanam tad artha sārūpyam kriyāyāḥ arthāt anubhūteḥ karmaṇaḥ bāhyasya vyavasthāyāḥ nibandhanam loke bahis adhyavasāyini syāt 
[247,vi_247,viii]	na hi asya sārūpyam antareṇa iyam asya saṃvittiḥ iti śakyam vyavasthāpayitum svabhāva bhūta tad rūpa saṃvidārā upaviplavāt nīla ādeḥ anubhūta ākhyā na anubhūteḥ para ātmanaḥ yasyāḥ buddheḥ svabhāva bhūtasya rūpasya viṣaya ākārasya saṃvidaḥ bahis artheṣu āropaḥ saḥ eva viplavaḥ bhrānti upanīta tvāt tasmāt nīla ādeḥ vastutaḥ adṛśyamānasya api anubhūta ākhyā anubhava vyavahāraḥ lokasya na punar jñānāt para ātmanā urthasya sākṣāt anubhūteḥ artha anubhava vyavahāraḥ 
[247,ix_247,xiii]	dhiyaḥ nīla ādi rūpa tve bāhyorthaḥ kim pramāṇakaḥ paramārthataḥ tu dhiyaḥ nīla ādi rūpa tve sva samvedye tad ākāra arppakaḥ bāhyaḥ arthaḥ sva rūpeṇa adṛśyamānaḥ kim pramāṇakaḥ na hi ākāra dvayam vedyate yena ekaḥ bāhyasya aparaḥ jñānasya iti syāt bāhyaḥ eva ākāravān dhīḥ tu nirākāra iti pratyakṣa siddhaḥ arthaḥ syāt iti āha dhiyaḥ anīla ādi rūpa tve sa tasya anubhavaḥ katham dhiyaḥ anīla ādi rūpa tve saḥ artha ākāra rahita unubhavaḥ tasya nīlasya grāhakaḥ iti katham śakya vyavasthāpanaḥ 
[247,xiv_248,i]	yadā saṃvedana ātma tvam na sārūpya nibandhanam siddham tat svatas eva asya kimarthena upanīyate anubhava mātra ātma tayā sarvatra jñāne aviśeṣāt viśeṣa vyavasthāna śaktayā yadā samvedana ātmaka tvam aparokṣa tvam na sārūpya nibandhanam tadā svatas eva prakāśa ātmatayā utpatteḥ tad saṃvedana ātma tvam siddham tatas ca arthena asya jñānasya kim unnīyate yena tasya tat vedanam iti ucyate na hi jñānasya sva prakāśe artha apekṣā na ca svasmāt vyatiriktam tena vedyate tat katham artha vedanam anena iti ucyate 
[248,ii_248,iv]	kiñca na ca sarva ātmanā sāmyam ajñāna tva prasaṅgataḥ na ca kenacid aṃśena sarvam sarvasya vedanam jñānam sarva ātmanā vai eka deśena vā arthasya sarūpam yat tat grāhakam syāt tatra na tāvat sarveṇa jaḍa tva ādinā sāmyam ajñāna tva prasaṅgataḥ na ca jaḍayoḥ grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ kenacid aṃśena vastu tva nīla tva ādīnā sarvam jñānam sarvasya arthasya saṃvedanam syāt sarvam vā nīla jñānam sarvasya nīlasya vedanam syāt 
[248,v_248,vi]	yathā nīla ādi rūpa tvāt nīla ādi anubhavaḥ mataḥ tathā anubhava rūpa tvāt tasya api anubhavaḥ bhavet yathā nīla ādi rūpa tvāt jñānam nīla ādīnām anubhavaḥ mataḥ tathā kim anubhava rūpa tvāt tasya anubhavasya artha viṣayasya api pūrvakasya uttaram jñānam anubhavaḥ na bhavet 
[248,vii_248,viii]	na anubhūta unubhavaḥ iti arthavat hi viniścayaḥ tasmāt adoṣaḥ iti ced na arthepi asti eṣa sarvadā na anubhave anubhūtaḥ anubhavaḥ iti arthavat arthaḥ iva gṛhīte viniścayaḥ bhavati tasmāt anubhavasya api anubhavaḥ grāhyaḥ kaḥ syāt iti ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced na kevalam anubhave arthe api eṣonubhūta tva niścayaḥ sarvadā na asti na hi dhārā vāhinī artha jñāne artheṣu pratikṣaṇam anubhūta niścayaḥ tatas ca arthopi na anubhūtaḥ syāt 
[248,ix_249,ii]	kasmāt vā anubhave na asti sati sattā nibandhane api ca idam yat ābhāti dṛśyamāne sitā ādike puṃsaḥ sita ādi abhivyakti rūpam saṃvedanam sphuṭam tat kim sita ādi abhivyakteḥ para rūpam atha ātmanaḥ kasmāt vā anubhave anubhūta niścayasya sattā nibandhane sārūpye tad utpāde ca sati na asti sattā niścayaḥ arthepi anubhūta nibandhane sārūpya tad utpattī eva te tad jñāna ipi samāne api ca sva saṃvedana anabhyupagame sitā ādike dṛśyamāne yat idam sita ādi abhivyakti rūpam antar prakāśamānam saṃvedanam sphuṭam puṃsaḥ pratipattuḥ ābhāti tat kim sita ādi abhivyakteḥ para rūpam atha ātma bhūtam iti vikalpau sataḥ tattva anya tva avyatikramāt 
[249,iii_249,iv]	para rūpe aprakāśāyām vyaktau vyaktam katham sitam jñānam vyaktiḥ na sā vyakta iti avyaktam akhilam jagat para rūpe abhyupagamyamāne samvedanam yat prakāśate tat na sita ādi vyakti rūpam iti aprakāśāyām śukla ādi vyaktau sitam katham vyaktam jñānam hi vyaktiḥ na ca sā vyaktā sitā ādike dṛśyamāne iṣyate iti avyaktam akhilam jagat prāptam sita ādi abhivyaktiḥ eṣitavyā 
[249,v_249,x]	tathā hi vyakteḥ vyakti antara vyaktau api doṣa prasaṅgataḥ artha vyakteḥ vyaktiḥ āpadyamānā na vyaktā syāt atha vyaktiḥ eva na sidhyet tasyāḥ sva prakāśa tve artha vyaktiḥ api tathā astu atha artha vyaktiḥ vyakteḥ vyakti antarāt uttara kāla bhāvi vedanāt vyaktiḥ evam tasyāḥ ca anyatas iti anavasthā durvārā kiñca dṛṣṭyā vā ajñāta sambandham viśinaṣṭi tayā katham dṛṣṭyā dhi yā asamviditayā saha ajñāta sambandham artham katham viśinaṣṭi pratipattā dṛṣṭoyam iti 
[249,xi_250,i]	katham arthaḥ dṛṣṭyā ajñāta sambandhaḥ iti āha yasmāt dvayoḥ eka gatau na dvitīyasya darśanam dvayoḥ saṃsṛṣṭayoḥ dṛṣṭau syāt dṛṣṭam iti niścayaḥ yasmāt dvayoḥ artha jñānayoḥ madhye ekasya gatau darśana kāle na dvitīyasya darśanam asti tathā hi na padārthaḥ dṛśyate na tadā buddhiḥ upalabhyate tad upalambhasya bhāvi tvāt yadā ca buddhiḥ upalabhyate na tadā anyaḥ atīta tvāt tasmāt dvayoḥ artha jñānayoḥ saṃsṛṣṭayoḥ eka upalambhāt dṛṣṭau satyām dṛṣṭam idam iti niścayaḥ tatas anya upalabdhiḥ sva upalabdhi rūpā iva syāt etat 
[250,ii_250,vi]	sarūpam darśanam yasya dṛśyatenyena cetasā dṛṣṭa ākhyā iti na ced yasya arthasya sarūpam samāna ākāram darśanam jñānam anyena cetasā dṛśyate tatra arthe dṛṣṭa ākhyā dṛṣṭa vyavahāraḥ iti ced atra āha siddham sārūpye asya sva vedanam asya jñānasya arthena saha sārūpye siddhe sva saṃvedanam jñānam siddham tathā hi artha ākāraḥ tāvat jñāna kāle parisphuṭam vedyamānaḥ jñānasya ātmā ced jñānam api artha ākāra vat aparokṣam eva svabhāvataḥ iti na anya vedyam 
[250,vii_250,xi]	atha ātma rūpam naḥ vetti para rūpasya vid katham atha jñānam ātma rūpam na vetti para rūpasya bāhya rūpasya vid katham na hi artha ākāra jñāna vedanam antareṇa artha vedanam iti uktam sārūpya mātreṇa artha vittiḥ bhaviṣyati iti ced sārūpyāt vedanā ākhyā ca prāk eva prativarṇṇitā sārūpyāt anubhava ātma tā rahitāt vedanā ākhyā vedana vyavahṛtiḥ ca prāk eva prāptam saṃvedanam sarva sadṛśānām paraspara bhiti anena prativarṇṇitā pratyuktā 
[250,xii_250,xiv]	kiñca dṛṣṭayoḥ eva sārūpya graha urthañca na dṛṣṭavān prāk katham darśanena asya sārūpyam sodhyavasyati dṛṣṭayoḥ eva kayoḥ cit sārūpya grahaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā yama lakayoḥ na ca kaścid draṣṭā jñānāt prāc artham dṛṣṭavān tad kathan darśanena saha āsya adṛṣṭasya arthasya sa draṣṭā sārūpyam adhyavasyati niścinoti 
[250,xv_251,ii]	kiñca sārūpi abhapi na icchedyaḥ tasya na ubhaya darśanam tadā arthaḥ jñānam iti ca jñāte ca iti gatā kathā sārūpyam api śabdāt sva samvedanam yaḥ vādī na icchet na tasya ubhayasya arthasya jñānasya ca darśanam saṃgacchate sārūpya abhāve artha vedanā ayogāt sva vedana abhāve ca na jñāna samvedanam anyena tad grahasya niṣiddha tvāt yadā ca evam tadā arthaḥ jñānam iti bhedaḥ te ca jñāte ca uti kathā api gatā iti kṛtsnam jagat andhamūkam bhavet pratīti nibandhana tvāt asya vyavahārasya 
[251,iii_251,iv]	atha svarūpam sā tarhi svayam eva prakāśate yat tasyām aprakāśāyām arthaḥ syāt aprakāśitaḥ atha yat etat sitā ādi abhivyakti rūpam sphṛṭa samvedanam ābhāti tat buddheḥ svarūpam sā buddhiḥ tarhi svayam eva aparokṣa tayā prakāśate yadi asmāt asyām buddhau aprakāśāyām parokṣāyām arthaḥ aprakāśitaḥ syāt prakāśate ca arthaḥ iti buddhiḥ api aparokṣa svabhāva iti sva samvedana siddhiḥ 
[251,v_251,vi]	etena anātma vid pakṣe sarva artha adarśanena ye apratyakṣām dhiyam prāhuḥ tepi nirvarṇita uttarāḥ anātma vid pakṣe sva saṃvedana abhāve etena anantaram upadarśitena sarvasya arthasya adarśanena darśana abhāva prasaṅgena ye jaiminīyāḥ apratyakṣām dhiyam arthāpatti gamyām āhuḥ tepi nirvarṇṇita uttarāḥ datta uttarāḥ boddhavyāḥ tathā hi artha darśanāni atha anupapattyā buddhiḥ vyavasthāpanīyā artha darśanam eva tu buddhi parokṣatāyām a saṅgatam iti na tat anyathā anupapadyamānam bṛddhim kalpayitum alam 
[251,vii_251,ix]	api ca āśraya ālambana abhyāsa bhedāt bhinna pravṛttayaḥ sukha duḥkha abhilāṣa ādi bhedāḥ buddhyaḥ eva tāḥ āśrayasya indriyasya ālambanasya sukha ādi vedanīyasya abhyāsasya ca yathā vṛttasya bhedāt viśeṣāt sukha duḥkha bhilāṣa ādi bhedāḥ bhinna pravṛttayaḥ nānā ākārāḥ samvi dita rūpāḥ jāyante buddhyaḥ eva ca tāḥ bodha svabhāva tvāt jñānena abhinna hetuka tvāt ca 
[252,i_252,ii]	pratyakṣāḥ tad viviktañca na anyat kiñcid vibhāvyate yat tat jñānam para upyetān bhuñcītāṃnyena vidyadi tatas pratyakṣāḥ na ca sāmānyena vedanam iti sva vedana tā eva na ca tebhyaḥ sukha ādibhyaḥ viviktam bhinnam anyat kiñcid bṛddhi svarūpam vibhāvyate upalabhyate yat tat pratyakṣam jñānam syāt kiñca anyena jñānena anyasya jñānasya vid vedanam yadi iṣyate tadā bhoktṛ santāna varttinaḥ etān sukha ādīn paraḥ pratipattā ala bhyamānaḥ bhuñjīta sukha ādi upabhogavān bhavet bhoktṛ puruṣa vat 
[252,iii_252,iv]	tad jā tad pratibhāsā vā yadi dhīḥ vetti na aparā ālambamānasya anyasya api asti avaśyam idam dvayam tasmāt sukha ādeḥ jātā tad pratibhāsā sukha ādi pratibhāsā vā tān sukha ādīn vetti bhoktṛ tvena na aparāyāḥ kāśi cad buddhiḥ iti yat i iṣyate tadā bhoktṛ santāna varttinaḥ sukha ādīn ālambamānasya anyasya puruṣa antara jñānasya idam tad ja tvam tad pratibhāsi tvam dvayam ālambanīya sukha ādi apekṣayā api adaśyam asti tatas sā upi bhoktā syāt 
[252,v_252,vii]	atha na utpadyate tasmāt na ca tad pratibhāsinī sā dhoḥ niḥ viṣayā prāptā atha anyasya dhīḥ bhoktṛ sukha ādeḥ sakāśāt na utpadyate na api tad pratibhāsinīṣyate tadā sā dhīḥ nirviṣayā prāptā grāhyasya para rūpasya abhāvepi prakāśamānā sva prakāśa eva syāt syāt etat bhoktuḥ sukham yadi api svarūpeṇa para buddhyā na gṛhyate tad sāmānya mātram tu gṛhyate iti bhoktṛ tva nirālambana tvayoḥ abhāvaḥ iti āha 
[252,viii_253,iv]	sāmānyam ca tad agrahe na gṛhyate iti proktam tasya bhoktṛ sukha viśeṣasya agrahe tad samavāyi sāmānyam na gṛhyate iti proktam atad samāna tā vyaktī tena nitya upalambha nami tyādinā na ca tat vastu kiñcana tasmāt artha avabhāsa ūsau na anyaḥ tasyāḥ dhiyaḥ tatas na ca tad sāmānyam kiñcana vastu yathā hi upagatasya anupalambha bādhita tvāt tasmāt anantara uktāt yukti kalāpāt artha avabhāsa ūsau sphṛṭam prakāśamānaḥ tasyāḥ parokṣa tvena iṣṭāyāḥ dhiyaḥ na anyaḥ kintu tad rūpaḥ eva 
[253,v_253,viii]	siddhe pratyakṣa bhāva ātma vidau gṛhṇāti tat punar na adhyakṣam iti ced eṣa kutas bhedaḥ sama arthayoḥ tatas artha ābhāsa jñānayoḥ tādātmyāt pratyakṣa bhāva ātma vidau pratyakṣa tva svasaṃvittī siddhe jñānasya aparokṣa tayā para nirapekṣa prakāśa tvāt ca syāt etat sva santāna varttinaḥ sukha ādīn adhyakṣam ālambate tatas prīti paritāpa ādi yogāt bhoktṛtā anyasya punar tān sukha ādīn na adhyakṣam gṛhṇāti kintu buddhi mātram tatas prīti paritāpa ādi abhāvāt na bhoktṛttvam iti ced sama arthayoḥ eka viṣayayoḥ sva para santāna varttinoḥ jñānayoḥ eṣa pratyakṣa apratyakṣa lakṣaṇaḥ kutas bhedaḥ sukha svarūpa viṣaya tvāt dvayam api pratyakṣam apratyakṣam vā syāt 
[253,ix_253,x]	adṛṣṭa eka artha yoga ādeḥ samvidaḥ niyamaḥ yadi sarvathā anyaḥ na gṛhṇīyāt samvid bheda upyapoditaḥ adṛṣṭāt śubha aśubha ādi lakṣaṇāt ekārtha samavāya ādeḥ vā nimittāt sva santāna vartti sukha grāhikāyāḥ samvidaḥ niyamaḥ bhoga rūpa tva avadhāraṇam tena anyasya na bhoktṛtā iti yat i iṣyate tadā adṛṣṭena eka artha samavāyena vā niyamitam sukha ādi anyaḥ na gṛhṇīyāt eva ityaḥ tu svarūpa pratibhāse bhoktṛ tvasya apratiṣedhāt na hi ātma samavāyitā mātreṇa sukha ādeḥ bhogaḥ kintarhi upalambhena sa ca parasya api asti iti bhoktā syāt ekasya viṣayasya samvidbhedaḥ grahaṇa bhedepi vyakta avyakta tayā uditaḥ nirākṛtaḥ tatas sva rūpa pratibhāsasya eka prakāra tvāt 
[254,i_254,ii]	yeṣāñca yoginonyasya pratyakṣeṇa sukha ādikam vidanti tulya anubhavāḥ tadvat tepi syuḥ āturāḥ yeṣāñca pareṣām kāraṇa ādīnām yoginoni asya sukha ādikam pratyakṣeṇa yoga bala utpannena vidanti iti matam teṣām mate pareṇa sukhinā duḥkhinā ca saha tulya anubhavāḥ yoginaḥ iti tadvat duḥkhi puruṣa vat yoginā upyāturāḥ duḥkha pīḍitāḥ syuḥ 
[254,iii_254,iv]	viṣaya indriya sampāta abhāvāt teṣām tad udbhavam na udeti duḥkham iti ced na vai duḥkha samudbhavaḥ viṣaya indriyayoḥ sampātasya saṃsargasya abhāvāt tad udbhavam viṣaya indriya saṃsarga jam duḥkham teṣām yoginām na udeti iti ced na vai na eva duḥkhasya samudbhavaḥ utpattiḥ
[254,v_254,vi]	duḥkhasya vedanam kintu duḥkha jñāna samudbhavaḥ na hi duḥkha ādi asaṃvedyam pīḍā anugraha kāraṇam duḥkhasya vedanam duḥkhi tvam kintu duḥkha viṣaya jñāna samudbhavaḥ duḥkhitā na hi duḥkham ādi śabdāt sukham asamvedyam ajñāyamānam pīḍā anugrahayoḥ kāraṇam bhavati yena duḥkha sukhayā uru utpattī duḥkhitā sukhite syātām 
[254,vii_254,ix]	nanu bauddhasya api mate yoginaḥ sukha ādi ākāreṇa jñānena para duḥkham ālambamānāḥ kasmāt āturāḥ na bhavanti duḥkhinaḥ iva yoginopi duḥkha ākāram sva samvedanañca jñānam iti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti āha bhāsamānam svarūpeṇa pīḍā duḥkham svayam yadā na tad ālambanam jñānam na tadā evam prayujyate duḥkham svayam para nirapekṣa prakāśam svarūpeṇa prakāśa svabhāvena bhāsamānam pīḍā tat tasmāt utpannam tat sarūpam tad ālambanam yoginaḥ jñānan na pīḍā iti yadā bauddhaiḥ iṣyate tadā evam yoginopi para duḥkha ālambakāḥ duḥkhinaḥ syuḥ iti na yujyate yena ayam bhedaḥ
[255,i_255,ii]	bhinne jñānasya sarvasya tena ālambana vedane artha sārūpyam ālambaḥ ātmā vittiḥ svayam sphuṭā tena sarvasya jñānasya ālambana vedane bhinne bhinna lakṣaṇe tathā hi artha sārūpyam ālambaḥ ālambana arthaḥ ātmā svayam para nirapekṣaḥ sphuṭāḥ vittiḥ vedana arthaḥ 
[255,iii_255,iv]	api ca adhyakṣatā abhāve dhiyaḥ syāt liṅgataḥ gatiḥ tat ca akṣam arthaḥ dhīḥ pūrvaḥ manaskāra upi vā bhavet api ca dhiyaḥ adhyakṣatā abhāve liṅgataḥ gatiḥ syāt tat ca liṅgambhavat akṣam indriyam arthaḥ viṣayaḥ dhīḥ anantarā pūrvakaḥ manaskāraḥ vā bhavet 
[255,v_255,vi]	kārya kāraṇa sāmagrayāmasyām sambandhi na aparām sāmarthya adarśanāt tatra na indriyam vyabhicārataḥ tathā arthaḥ dhīmanaskārau jñānam tau ca na sidhyataḥ na aprasiddhasya liṅga tvam vyaktiḥ arthasya ced matā liṅgam yasmāt kārya kāraṇa sāmagra yāmasya āmebhyaḥ aparam ātmanaḥ saṃyoga ādi sambandhi na asti sāmarthya adarśanāt tatra teṣu indriyam tāvat na liṅgam vyabhicārataḥ sati api tasmin jñāna abhāvāt tathā artha upi jñāna vyabhicārāt na liṅgam dhīmanaskārau bodha svabhāva tvāt jñānam tau ca līṅga jñānāt prāk na sidhyataḥ jñānasya anumeya tvāt na ca aprasiddhasya niścitasya liṅga tvam sattā mātreṇa liṅga tve ati prasaṅgāt arthasya vyaktiḥ sphuṭa tā burddharliṅgam matā ced 
[255,vii_255,viii]	sā eva nanu jñānam vyakta ūrtha ūnena varṇṇitaḥ vyaktau ananubhūtāyām tad vyakta tva aviniścayāt nanu sā eva vyaktiḥ jñānam artha prakāśa lakṣaṇa tvāt na ca tat eva liṅgi ca iti yuktam anena vyakteḥ liṅga tva kathanena vyaktaḥ arthaḥ varṇṇitaḥ pratikṣiptaḥ tathā hi vyaktau bṛddhi rūpāyām ananubhūtāyām artha sambandhinaḥ tad byakta tvasya vyakti vyakta tvasya aviniścayāt na liṅga tvam sattā mātreṇa liṅga tve ati prasaṅgāt 
[256,i_256,iv]	atha arthasya eva kaścid sa viśeṣaḥ vyaktiḥ iṣyate atha arthasya eva svabhāva bhūtaḥ sa kaścid svabhāva viśeṣaḥ vyaktiḥ iṣyate na jñānam na anutpāda vyayavataḥ viśeṣaḥ arthasya kaścana tat api arthasya sthira eka rūpa tvāt anutpāda vyayavataḥ viśeṣaḥ vyakti rūpaḥ kaścana na saṅgataḥ 
[256,v_256,vi]	tat iṣṭau vā pratijñānam kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ prasajyate sa ca jñātaḥ athavā ajñātaḥ bhavet jñātasya liṅgatā tasya viśeṣasya iṣṭau vā pratijñānam arthasya pūrva svabhāva nāśe sati svabhāva antara utpādāt kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ prasajyate sa ca artha svabhāva viśeṣaḥ jñātaḥ ajñātaḥ vā bhavet liṅgam jñānasya tatra jñātasya yadi līṅgatā iṣyate 
[256,vii_256,ix]	tadā yadi jñāne aparicchinne jñātosau iti tad kutas jñāta tvena aparicchinnam api tat gamakam katham jñāne aparicchinne tad upādhiḥ jñāta usāvarthom liṅgam iti yat iṣṭam tat kutas upapadyate atha ajñātasya liṅgatā tadā jñāta tvena aparicchinnam api tat vastu katham gamakam liṅgam sattā mātreṇa gamaka tve ati prasaṅgāt iti uktam na ca jñāna adarśane dṛṣṭa tā yuktā 
[256,x_256,xiii]	adṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa yonyena draṣṭrā dṛṣṭā na hi kvacid hiḥ yasmāt adṛṣṭā dṛṣṭiḥ jñānam yeṣām te arthāḥ kvacid anyena draṣṭrā dṛṣṭāḥ iti na dṛṣṭāḥ niścaya viṣayāḥ syuḥ atha arthasya eva viśeṣaḥ kaścid buddhi kṛtaḥ āste tena buddhi anumānam iti āha viśeṣaḥ sonya dṛṣṭau api asti iti syāt svadhī gatiḥ 
[257,i_257,iv]	sa viśeṣaḥ arthasya anyena puruṣeṇa dṛṣṭau api asti iti puruṣa antarasya ātad vyāpṛta indriyasya tasmāt artha gata viśeṣāt svadhī gatiḥ syāt atha dharmasya sādhāraṇa tvāt tasya buddhi avyabhicārāt tasmāt anumitiḥ buddheḥ svadharma nirapekṣiṇaḥ kevalāt na artha dharmāt kaḥ svadharmaḥ svadhiyaḥ paraḥ tasmāt kevalāt artha dharmāt svadharma nirapekṣiṇaḥ anumātṛ puruṣa ātma bhūta jñāna nirapekṣāt vuddheḥ anumitiḥ na sambhavati sarvasya eva tasmāt sva buddhi anumāna prasaṅgāt atha ātma dharmaḥ eva sa kaścid buddheḥ gamakaḥ iti ced āha svasya ātmanaḥ dharmaḥ sva buddheḥ ātma sambandhinyāḥ buddheḥ aparonyaḥ kaḥ 
[257,v_257,vi]	pratyakṣa adhigataḥ hetuḥ tulya kāraṇa janmanaḥ tasya bhedaḥ kutas buddheḥ vyabhicāryan yajaḥ ca saḥ pratyakṣa adhigataḥ hetuḥ syāt na hi apratītasya hetu tā na ca buddheḥ pratyakṣata iṣyate tad vyatiriktiḥ ca kaścid ātma dharmaḥ na pratyakṣaḥ iti na syāt buddhi anumānam kiñca ātma dharma ūsau buddhyā samam eka kāraṇaḥ vā syāt bhinna kāraṇaḥ vā tatra buddhyā saha tulyāt kāraṇāt janma yasya tasya ātma dharmasya buddheḥ sakāśāt kutas bhedaḥ abhinna hetuka tve abhinnatā eva yuktā atha anya hetu kosau tadā anyajaḥ ca sa vyabhicārī syāt eka sāma graya dhīnayoḥ eka darśanāt apara anumānam avyabhicāri na anyathā 
[257,vii_257,ix]	uktam eva artham saṃgṛhṇan āha rūpa ādīn pañca viṣayān indriyāṇi upalambhanam mukttvā na kāryam aparam tasyāḥ samupalabhyate rūpam ādiḥ yeṣām tān śabda gandha rasa sparśan pañca viṣayān pañca indriyāṇi cakṣuḥ śrotra ādīni upalambhanam jñānam muktvā tasyāḥ buddheḥ na kāryam aparam samupalabhyate iyatā eva sarvasya saṃgrahāt 
[258,i_258,ii]	tatra atyakṣam dvayam pañca su artheṣu ekopi na īkṣyate rūpa darśanataḥ jātaḥ yoni atha avyasta sambhavaḥ tatra teṣu madhye dvayam indriyam jñānañcātyakṣam atīndriyam indriyasya jñānāni atha anupapattyā vyavasthāpanāt jñānasya tvad mate apratyakṣa tvāt rūpa ādiṣu pañca su artheṣu ekopi na īkṣyate buddheḥ apratyakṣa tvāt yaḥ yāvat dṛśyamānaḥ anyathā jñānam antareṇa vyasta sambhavaḥ pratikṣipta sattvaḥ viṣayasya rūpa darśanataḥ buddheḥ jātaḥ abhyupagamyate 
[258,iii_258,iv]	yat evam apratītam tat liṅgam iti ati laukikam vidyamānepi liṅge tāntena sārddham apaśyataḥ yat ca evam buddhinā antarayīkatayā apratītam tat buddheḥ liṅgam iti atilaukikam lo kātikrāntam kiñca abhyupagamya ucyate vidyamānepi kasmiṃścid liṅge kadācid buddhim tām tena liṅgena sārdham apaśyataḥ apratipatteḥ 
[258,v_258,vi]	katham pratītiḥ liṅgam hi na adṛṣṭasya prakāśakam tatas eva asya liṅgāt prāk prasiddheḥ upavarṇṇane tasmāt liṅgāt katham buddhi pratītiḥ liṅgam hi anvaya rahitam adṛṣṭasya arthasya na prakāśakam yuktam tatas eva liṅgāt asya jñānasya anvaya siddhi artham ātmani anumānāt prāk siddheḥ niścayasya upavarṇṇane vā abhidhīyamāne
[258,vii_258,ix]	dṛṣṭānta antara sādhya tvam tasya api iti anavasthitiḥ iti arthasya dhiyaḥ siddhiḥ na arthāt tasyāḥ kathañcana tasya anvaya sādhakasya api anumānasya dṛṣṭānta antareṇa anumāna sādhyena sādhya tvam iti anavasthitiḥ syāt tathā ca ekasya asiddhau sarvasya asiddhiḥ prasajyate iti tasmāt arthasya dhiyaḥ sakāśāt siddhiḥ na arthāt tasyāḥ dhiyaḥ katham ca na siddhiḥ iti nyāyyam 
[258,x_259,ii]	tad aprasiddhau arthasya svayam eva aprasiddhitaḥ pratyakṣāñca dhiyam dṛṣṭvā tasyāḥ ca iṣṭā abhidha ādikam yasmāt tasyāḥ dhiyaḥ asiddhau arthasya svayam eva aprasiddhitaḥ katham liṅga tā sva prakāśa tvāt pratyakṣām dhiyam tasyāḥ ca ceṣṭā abhidhā adiḥ yasya sukha prasāda vaivarṇṇya ādeḥ tam dṛṣṭvā gṛhīta vyāptikasya anya sambandhi ceṣṭā ādi darśanāt 
[259,iii_259,iv]	para citta anumānañca na syāt ātmani adarśanāt sa bandhasya manaḥ buddhau artha liṅga aprasiddhitaḥ para citta anumānañca iṣṭam na syāt buddheḥ ātmani sva santatau ceṣṭā ādibhiḥ saha sambandhasya adarśanāt api ca vāsanā mātra bala bhāvinyā manaḥ bṛddhau vikalpa buddhau viṣaya bhūtasya arthasya abhāvātarthasya liṅgasya asidhitaḥ buddhi antarāt liṅgāt anumānam syāt
