[259,v_259,vi]	prakāśitā katham vā syāt buddhiḥ buddhi antareṇa vaḥ aprakāśa ātmanoḥ sāmyāt vyaṅgya vyañjaka tā kutas katham vā buddhi antareṇa apratyakṣeṇa buddhiḥ prakāśitā syāt vaḥ yuṣmākam darśane yasmāt aprakāśa ātmanorlliṅga liṅginoḥ asiddha tvena sāmyāt vyaṅgya vyañjaka tā kutas yadi aprakāśa ātmanoḥ na vyaṅgya vyañjaka tā tadā artha jñānayoḥ api katham vyaṅgya vyañjaka tā bhāvaḥ iti 
[259,vii_259,xi]	viṣayasya katham vyaktiḥ viṣayasya katham vyaktiḥ iti uttaram āha prakāśe rūpa saṃkramāt sa ca prakāśaḥ tad rūpaḥ svayam eva prakāśate prakāśe sva samvidite jñāne viṣayasya rūpa saṃkramāt sārūpya saṃbhavāt jñānena artha prakāśitaḥ iti ucyate sa ca prakāśaḥ tad rūpaḥ viṣaya svarupaḥ svayam eva aparokṣa prakāśa ātmanā utpannaḥ prakāśate na tu anyena prakāśyate 
[260,i_260,iii]	syāt etat buddhiḥ api buddhi antara sa rūpa utpannā prakāśamānā buddheḥ vyañjikā matā iti ced āha tathā abhyupagame buddheḥ buddhau buddhiḥ sva vedikā siddhānyathā tulya dharmā viṣayopi dhiyā saha buddheḥ prakāśyāyāḥ buddhau vyañjikāyām tathā saṃkrānta sārūpya prakāśa dvāreṇa vedanā abhyupagame vyañjikā buddhiḥ sva saṃvedikā siddhā dhī sarūpāyāḥ buddheḥ sva prakāśa tve pūrva buddhiḥ prakāśitā syāt anyathā sva prakāśa tva anabhyupagame viṣaya upya prakāśa svabhāvatayā dhiyā saha tulya dharmā iti sā upi buddheḥ vyañjakaḥ syāt sarūpayoḥ dhī viṣayayoḥ anyonyam vyañjaka tā bhavet 
[260,iv_260,v]	iti prakāśa rūpāḥ naḥ svayam dhīḥ saṃprakāśate anyosyām rūpa saṃkrāntyā prakāśaḥ san prakāśate iti tasmāt naḥ asmākam mate dhīḥ svayam ātmanā prakāśa rūpa utpannā satī prakāśate na tu anyena prakāśyate iti yuktam anyaḥ punar anyosyām buddhau prakāśāyām rūpa saṃkrāntyā prakāśaḥ san prakāśate tatas artha vedana vyavahāraḥ 
[260,vi_260,x]	sādṛśyepi hi dhīḥ anyā prakāśyā na tayā matā svayam prakāśamānā sādṛśye sārūpyepi sati tayā sarūpayā dhiyā anyā pūrvikā dhīḥ na prakāśyā matā prakāśa svabhāvasya pareṇa prakāśa ayogāt kintu svayam prakāśa svabhāvatayā prakāśamānā prakāśate iti abhyupeyam evantarhi arthasya aprakāśa ātmanaḥ katham prakāśate iti āha arthaḥ tad rūpeṇa prakāśate arthaḥ sārūpya saṃkrānteḥ tad rūpeṇa jñāna rūpeṇa prakāśate na tu sākṣāt sva rūpeṇa 
[260,xi_261,i]	dṛṣṭāntam āha yathā pradīpayoḥ ddīpa ghaṭayoḥ ca tad āśrayaḥ vyaṅgya vyañjaka bhedena vyavahāraḥ pratanyate yathā pradīpayoḥ prakāśa ātmanoḥ na prakaśya prakāśaka bhāvaḥ tathā buddhyoḥ api yathā dīpa ghaṭayoḥ prakāśa aprakāśa svabhāvayoḥ ekaḥ prakāśakaḥ anyaḥ prakāśyaḥ tathā jñāna arthayoḥ api tad āśrayaḥ aprakāśa prakāśa ātma niṣṭhaḥ vyaṅgya vyañjaka bhedena vyavahāraḥ loke pratanyate 
[261,ii_261,iii]	viṣaya indriya mātreṇa na dṛṣṭam iti niścayaḥ tasmāt yatoyam tasya api vācyam anyasya darśanam yatas ca viṣaya mātreṇa indriya mātreṇa ve dam dṛṣṭam iti na niśi asta smāt yatas tad vyatiriktāt jñānāt idam dṛṣṭam iti niścayaḥ tasya api viṣaya indriyābhyām anyasya jñānasya darśanam aparokṣa tvam vācyam iti buddhi parokṣa tā ādaḥ na yuktaḥ 
[261,iv_261,viii]	sva saṃvitti siddhi artham upapatti antaram āha smṛteḥ api ātma vid siddhāḥ jñānasya jñānasya atītasya smṛteḥ api ātma vid su saṃvittiḥ siddhā pratītam eva hi smaryate yathārthaḥ syāt etat jñānam pratītam anyena cetasā na sva saṃvedanena iti āha anyena vedane dīrgha ādi grahaṇan na syāt bahu mātra anavasthiteḥ 
[261,ix]	anyena jñānena pūrvakasya jñānasya vedane abhidhīyamāne dīrgha deḥ svarasya grahaṇam na syāt kṣaṇikasya jñānasya ekāṇu atyaya kāla mātra sthāyinaḥ aneka kṣaṇa nirvarttyāsu bahvīṣu mātrāsu dīrgha ādi nirvarttanikāsu grāhaka tvena anavasthiteḥ na hi ekakṣaṇa mātra sthā api jñānam aneka kṣaṇa kalāpa nirvartanīya mātrā sañcaya ātmakam dīrgha ādikam śaknoti grahītum kintvakāra ādi eka eka mātra avayava leśam gṛhṇāti tad grāhaka tvena dvitīya jñānena tat pratīyate evam apara aparaiḥ jñānaiḥ avayava leśa grāhakaiḥ sva sva grāhaka jñāna antaritaiḥ grahaṇa krame kena mātrā grahaṇam mātrā pracaya dīrgha ādi grahaṇam vā syāt 
[262,i_262,ii]	avasthita avakramāyām sakṛt ābhāsanāt matau varṇṇāḥ syāt akramaḥ adīrghaḥ atha aneka mātrā kālam ekā eva buddhiḥ asti iti ucyate tadā aneka kālam avasthitau satya amakra māyām matau sarva mātrāṇām sakṛt ābhāsanāt dīrgha ādiḥ varṇṇaḥ akramaḥ syāt pratīti nibandhana tvāt vastu vyavasthāyāḥ tathā ca adīrghaḥ bhavet na hi eka kālam uccais uccāryamāṇā upi eka mātrikaḥ dīrghaḥ 
[262,iii_263,i]	nanu kramavantaḥ varṇṇāḥ avayava krameṇa utpadyamānāḥ dīrgha ādi buddhim utpādayiṣyanti iti āha kramavān akramām katham upakuryāt asaṃśliṣyan varṇṇa bhāgaḥ parasparam kramavān varṇṇa bhāgaḥ svasva kāla sthāyī parasparam asaṃśliṣyan asambadhyamānaḥ dīrgha buddhim akramām katham upakuryyāt utpādayet kramavati jñeye jñānam api tathā eva yuktam 
[263,ii_263,iv]	atha utpannāḥ varṇṇa avayavāḥ antya avayava utpatti paryantam anuvartante tatas krama grahaṇam sarva grahaṇañcā asti iti yuktam dīrgha ādi grahaṇam iti āha āntyam pūrva sthitāt ūrdhvam vardhamānaḥ dhvaniḥ bhavet ā antyam antyam varṇṇa avayavam yāvat pūrva pūrveṣām varṇṇa avayavānām krama utpannānām sthitau satyām prathama varṇṇa avayavāt ūrdhva pūrva utpannasya anuvṛttau apūrvasya ca aparasya utpattau varddhamānaḥ dhvaniḥ bhavet na ca etat asti avayava krama grahaṇena dīrgha buddheḥ utpāḥ dāt 
[263,v_263,vii]	syāt etat krameṇa utpannānām avayavān ām antya avayava kāle grahaṇam iti na varddhamāna dhvaniḥ bhavati pūrvam kasyacid grahaṇa abhāvāt iti āha akrameṇa grahāt ante krama vat hīḥ ca naḥ bhavet akrameṇa grahaṇādantya varṇa niṣpatti kāle ca tad grāhikā kramavatī dhīḥ naḥ bhavet tatas ca na dīrgha grahaṇam na hi eka kālam anekaiḥ uccāryamāṇe anekasmin akāra ādau dīrgha buddhiḥ bhavet 
[263,viii_264,i]	ekaika buddhiḥ sakṛt utpannā krameṇa avayavān gṛhṇāti antya avayava grahaṇa kāle dīrghagrāhikā iti ced āha dhiyaḥ sva yañca na sthānam tad ūrdhva viṣaya āsthiteḥ dhiyaḥ avayava grāhikāyāḥ tasmāt ekāyavagrahaṇāt ūrdhvam pūrva gṛhītasya viṣayasya āsthiteḥ hetoḥ na sthānam sthitiḥ yuktā 
[264,ii_264,iii]	sthāne svayat na naśyet sā paścāt api aviśeṣatas doṣoyam sakṛt utpanna ākrama varṇṇa sthitau api atha viṣayān avasthānepi svayam avinaśvara svabhāva tayā buddheḥ sthāne vā svīkriyamāṇe paścāt anta avayava grahaṇa anantaram api avinaśvara svabhāvatayā aviśeṣatas na naśyet buddheḥ sakṛt utpannāyāḥ cira avasthāne yaḥ doṣaḥ sarva dā avināśa prasaṅgaḥ uktaḥ ayam sakṛt utpannānām akramāṇām varṇṇānām kramagrāhi vijñāna utpatti kālam yāvat avasthitau api ucyamānāyām boddhavyaḥ yadi sakṛt utpannā api avinaśvara svabhāva tayā kañcid kālam anuvartate tadā ciram api tad svabhāva apracyavāt anuvarteran 
[264,iv_265,i]	kiñca sakṛt yatna udbhavāt vyarthaḥ syāt yatnaḥ ca uttara uttaraḥ sakṛt kṛtāt yatnāt tālu ādi vyāpārāt varṇṇānām utpanna tvāt uttarottaraḥ yatnaḥ ca vyarthaḥ syāt yopi manyate prayatna preritena vāyunā stimitasya vāyoḥ ākāśa saṃyuktasya saṃyoga vibhāga kṛtā śabdasya abhivyaktiḥ bhavati iti tam pratyāha vyaktau api eṣa varṇṇānām doṣaḥ samanuṣajyate varṇṇānām vāyavīya saṃyoga vibhāga dvāreṇa abhivyakta avapīṣyamāṇāya āmayam anantara uktaḥ akramāṇām sakṛt abhivyakteḥ uttaraḥ yatnaḥ prāṇa preraṇa ādikaḥ vyarthaḥ syāt iti doṣaḥ samanuṣajyate 
[265,ii_265,iv]	syāt etat anekayā tad grahaṇe yāntyā dhīḥ sā anubhūyate na dīrghagrāhikā sā ca tat na syāt dīrgha dhī smṛtiḥ anekayā dhiyā tasya aneka āśraya ātmakasya varṇṇasya grahaṇe kṛte paścāt yāntyā dhīrantyāvayava grāhikā sā buddhi antareṇa anubhūyate tayā dīrgha ādi buṃddhiḥ bhaviṣyati iti ced nanu evam pūrvāsām buddhīnām aneka avayava grāhikāṇām na buddhi antareṇa grahaḥ na api sva samvedanena vittiḥ yā ca anubhūyate sā antya avayava grāhikā dhīḥ sā api hi na dīrgha ādi varṇṇa grāhikā tat tasmāt dīrgha dhī smṛtiḥ na syāt 
[265,v_265,vi]	pṛthak pṛthak ca buddhīnām samvittau tat dhvaniḥ śruteḥ avicchinna ābhatā na syāt ghaṭanañca nirākṛtam na hi agṛhītam eva smaryate varṇṇa avayava grāhikāṇām buddhīnām pṛthak pṛthak sva sva grāhiṇībhiḥ buddhibhiḥ saṃvitta āviṣyamāṇāyāñca tat dhvani śruteḥ dīrgha ādi varṇṇabuddheḥ avicchinna ābhatā nirantara pratibhāsa tā na syāt antarā antarā buddhi grāhiṇībhiḥ buddhibhiḥ avayava grāhi buddhīnām vyavadhānāt sva grāhikābhiḥ buddhibhiḥ vyavadhānepi buddhīnām laghu vṛtti tvāt ghaṭanam avyavadhāna adhyavasānam nirākṛtam anyatra api samānam tat ityādinā yathāvayava grāhikāḥ buddhayaḥ laghu vṛttayaḥ tathā tad grāhi buddhi kāle tad abhāva uṃpi laghu vṛttiḥ iti buddhi avaccheda varṇṇa vicchedaḥ api manyeta iti uktam prāk 
[265,vii_265,ix]	kiñca vicchinnam śrṛṇvatā upyasya yadi avicchinna vibhramaḥ hrasva dvaya uccāraṇepi syāt avicchinna vibhramaḥ vicchinnam śṛṇvatopi laghu vṛtteḥ yadi avicchinna bhramaḥ tadā hrasva dvaya uccāraṇepi laghu vṛtteḥ avicchinna vibhramaḥ syāt iti dīrgha buddhiḥ bhavet 
[266,i_266,ii]	vicchinne darśane ca akṣāt avicchanna adhiropaṇam na akṣāt sarva akṣa buddhīnām vitatha tva prasaṅgataḥ varṇṇa avayavānāmakṣāt indriyāt vicchinne sva buddhibhiḥ vyavahite ca vastu tas darśane akṣāt avicchinnasya darśanasya adhiropaṇam āropaḥ iti na yuktam eva sarvāsām akṣa buddhīnām rūpa ādi grāhiṇīnām vitatha tva prasaṅgataḥ na kiñcid abhra antam syāt 
[266,iii_266,v]	buddheḥ buddhi antareṇa gṛhītau aviccheda pratibhāsaḥ na asti iti sa upapattikam ākhyātum āha sarva antya upi hi varṇṇa ātmā nimeṣa tulita sthitiḥ sa ca kramāt aneka aṇu sambandhena nitiṣṭhati sarveṣām dīrgha ādīnām eka mātrika tva āt antyaḥ varṇṇa ātmā akāra ādiḥ nimeṣeṇa nayana nimīlanena tulita aparimitā sthitiḥ yasya sa tathā sa ca akṣi nimeṣa kāla sthāyi akāra ādiḥ aneka iṣām ākāśa tamaḥ saṃjñitānām pakṣma mālā dvaya varttinām aṇūnām sambandhena ākramaṇena nimeṣa kāla saṃjñitena kramāt bhūyas kṣaṇa vyavadhānāt nitiṣṭhati parisamāpyate etena antya upi varṇṇaḥ aneka kṣaṇa sthāyi iti uktam 
[266,vi_266,vii]	ekāṇu atyaya kālaḥ ca kālolpoyān kṣaṇaḥ mataḥ buddhiḥ ca kṣaṇikā tasmāt kramāt varṇṇān prapadyate ekasya aṇoḥ atyayaḥ ākramaṇam sa kālaḥ parimāṇam yasya tādṛśaḥ ca kālolpīyān laghutamaḥ bhettum aśakyaḥ kṣaṇaḥ bhavet tāvat kāla mātra sthāṣṇu tayā buddhiḥ ca kṣaṇikā tasmāt kṣaṇika tvāt buddhiḥ kramāt puna rdhīḥ vyavahitā bhūyasī bhavantī varṇṇān pratipadyate tad katham avicchinna varṇṇa grahaḥ saṅgataḥ 
[267,i_267,ii]	iti varṇṇepi rūpa ādau avicchinna avabhāsinī vicchinnā api anyayā buddhiḥ sarvā syāt vitathā arthikā iti tasmāt varṇṇepi rūpa ādau api buddhiḥ tad grāhikayā anyayā dhiyā antaritā vastutas vicchinnā api avicchinna avabhāsinī kutaścid nimitāt bhavantī sarva avitathā arthikā śūnyā bhrāntiḥ syāt 
[267,iii_267,iv]	ghaṭanam yat ca bhāvānām anyatra indriya vibhramāt bheda alakṣaṇa vibhrāntam smaraṇanta dvi kalpakam yat ca bhāvānām sadṛśa apara apareṣām utpadyamānānām saḥ eva ayam iti eka tva ghaṭanam tat bhāvānām para sparataḥ bheda alakṣaṇena vibhrāntam vikalpakam jñānam smaraṇam anyatra indriya vibhramāt atas punar alātā ādiṣu bhrāmyamāṇeṣu cakra ādi ākāram jñānam utpadyate asau indriya kramaḥ nirvikalpakaḥ eva 
[267,v_267,vi]	tasya spaṣṭa avabhāsi tvam jalpa saṃsargiṇaḥ kutas na akṣa grāhyesti śabdānām yojana iti vivecitam tasya vikalpasya jalpa saṃsargiṇaḥ śabda saṃsargavataḥ spaṣṭa avabhāsi tvam jñeya ākāra vaiśadyam kutas yasmāt akṣa grāhye sva lakṣaṇe śabdānām saṃketa agrahaṇāt vācaka tvena yojanā na asti iti vivecitam prāk 
[267,vii_268,iii]	vicchinnam paśyata upyakṣaiḥ ghaṭayet yadi kalpanā atha akṣaiḥ indriya jñānaiḥ sva jñāna vyavahitaiḥ apara aparam artham vicchinnam paśyatā upi jñāna anucarī kalpanā tat eva idam iti eka tvena ghaṭayet iti yadi ucyate tadā vicchinna darśanam eva na asti iti vaktum āha arthasya tad saṃvitteḥ ca satatam bhāsamānayoḥ arthasya grāhyasya tad saṃvitteḥ ca vijātīya avyavakīrṇṇa tvāt satatam bhāsa mānayoḥ anayoḥ avi cheda bhāsanasya 
[268,iv_268,v]	bādhake asati sannyāye vicchinne iti tad kutas buddhīnām śakti niyamāt iti ced sa kutas mataḥ bādhake san ca asau nyāyaḥ ca tasmin pramāṇa bhūte bādhake asati iti arthaḥ te artha saṃvittī jñāna jñānena vicchinne iti yat ucyate tad kutas buddhīnām ekaika buddhi janana śakti niyamāt na grāhya buddhyā saha tad grāhikā buddhiḥ bhavati tatas vicchinna tayā artha darśanam iti ced sa yugapad jñāna anutpādaḥ kutas hetoḥ mataḥ 
[268,vi_268,vii]	yugapad buddhi adṛṣṭeḥ ced tat eva idam vicāryate yugapad buddhyoḥ utpannayoḥ adṛṣṭeḥ ced yadi adarśanam pramāṇam vicchedasya api tat asti iti sa upya yukta abhyupagamaḥ atha viccheda adarśanepi vicārāt sā sidhyati tadā tat eva idam yugapad buddhi adarśanam api bādhya tayā na yugapad buddhi utpāda bādhana asamartham iti vicāryate tat kim asya upanyāsena 
[268,viii_268,x]	nanu uktam bhagavatā asthānam etat yat dve citte yugapad saṃpratipadyeya ātāmi ti tat katham iti āha tāsām samāna jātīye sāmarthya niyamaḥ bhavet tāsām buddhīnām vikalpikānām indriya jānāñca samāna jātīyaḥ ekasmin jñāne karttavye sāmarthya niyamaḥ tathā bhagavatā pratipāditaḥ bhavet tatas grāhya grāhakam asamāna jātīyam buddhi dvayam api saha jāyeta samāna jātīyantu na saha jāyate 
[269,i_269,iii]	tathā hi samyak lakṣyante vikalpāḥ krama bhāvinaḥ tathā hi vikalpāḥ krama bhāvinaḥ samyak lakṣyante indriya jñānāni ca samāna jātīyāni kramavanti ca dṛśyante vikalpa indriya jñāne cakṣuḥ śrotra ādi jñāne ca saha utpadyante etena yaḥ samakṣerthe pratyabhijñāna kalpanām spaṣṭa avabhāsām pratyakṣām kalpayet sā upi vāritaḥ 
[269,iv_269,vii]	etena vikalpa avikalpayoḥ saha utpādena yaḥ mīmāṃsakaḥ samakṣe pratyakṣe arthe saḥ eva ayam iti eka tva viṣayām pratyabhijñāna ākhyām kalpanām spaṣṭa pratibhāsām pratyakṣām pramāṇam kalpayet sa upi nivāritaḥ vikalpaḥ hi vikalpita artha gocara tvāt aspaṣṭa pratibhāsaḥ eva viśada pratibhāsana indriya jñānena sahabhāvi tvāt spaṣṭa grāhyā ropaḥ adhyavasīyate kiñca eka tvam antareṇa api pratyabhijñānam dṛśyate iti darśayan āha keśa gola ka dīpa ādau api su aṣṭa avabhāsanāt lūna punar jāte keśa ādau māyā kāra darśite golaka ādau kṣaṇa vināśi dīpa ādau spaṣṭa avabhāsanāt 
[269,viii_269,ix]	pratīta bheda īpi adhyakṣā dhīḥ kathantādṛśī bhavet tasmāt na pratyabhijñānāt varṇṇa ādi eka tva niścayaḥ pratyakṣāt pratīte bhede sā pratyabhijñā tādṛśī eka tva adhyavasāyinī dṛśyamāna adhyakṣāḥ dhīḥ katham bhavet prāpnoti ca pratyabhijñā pratyakṣa vādinaḥ mate tasmāt na asti pratyabhijñānāt varṇṇa ādye katva niścayaḥ 
[270,i_270,ii]	pūrva anubhūta smaraṇāt tad dharma āropaṇāt vinā saḥ eva ayam iti jñānam na asti tat ca akṣa je kutas yasamāt pūrva anubhūtasya arthasya smaraṇāt tad dharmasya vidyamāna tvena āropaṇāt vinā saḥ eva ayam iti jñānam eka tva viṣayam na asti tat ca pūrva anubhūta smaraṇam tad dharmāra upaṇañca akṣa je vartamāna vastu bala bhāvini kutas sambhavati 
[270,iii_270,v]	syāt etat artha jñānayoḥ yugapad sambhave satya vicchinnam varṇṇa ādi darśanam syāt iti āha na ca artha jñāna samvityoḥ yugapad sambhavaḥ yatas lakṣyete pratibhāsau dvau na artha artha jñānayoḥ pṛthak na hi artha ābhāsi ca jñānam arthaḥ bāhyaḥ ca kevalaḥ na ca artha jñānayoḥ ye samvittī tayoḥ yugapad sambhava usti yata ūrthasya artha jñānasya dvau pratibhāsau pṛthak na bhedana lakṣyate na hi artha ābhāsi tat jñānam arthaḥ bāhyaḥ ca kevelaḥ buddhi vyatiriktaḥ iti dvau pratibhāsau sambhavataḥ 
[270,vi_270,viii]	syāt etat artha jñāna jñānayoḥ bhinnau eva pratibhāsau kevalam tad uttarayā vikalpa buddhyā ekatvena gṛhyete atra āha eka ākāram atigrāhye bheda abhāva prasaṅgataḥ eka ākārayā matyā vikalpikayā grāhye artha jñānayoḥ jñāne yadi tadā tayoḥ bhedasya abhāva prasaṅgataḥ eka tvam eva abhyupagantavyam artha jñāna jñānayoḥ pratibhāsa bheda abhāvāt 
[270,ix_271,i]	su upa lakṣeṇa bhedena yau samvittau na lakṣitau artha artha pratyayau paścāt smaryete tau pṛthak katham arthaḥ ca artha pratyayaḥ ca artha artha pratyayau sūpa lakṣeṇa bhedena saṃvittau anubhave na lakṣitau tau paścāt kāla antare pṛthak bhedena ayam arthaḥ artha jñāḥ nañcā idam iti katham smaryete yugapad arthaṃjñāna tad jñānayoḥ utpāde pratibhāsana ānātva prasaṅgāt 
[271,ii_271,iii]	krameṇa anubhava utpādepi artha artha manasoḥ ayam pratibhāsasya nānā tva codya doṣaḥ duruddharaḥ artha artha manasoḥ krameṇa anubhava utpādepīṣyamāṇe ayam pratibhāsasya nānā tva codya lakṣaṇaḥ doṣaḥ duruddharaḥ dvaya pratibhāsasya krameṇa abhyupagamāt 
[271,iv_271,v]	artha saṃvedanam tāvat tata ūrtha ābhāsa vedanam na hi saṃvedanam śuddham bhavet arthasya vedanam tathā hi nīla ādi ākāraḥ ekaḥ ekam ca vedanam lakṣyate na tu nīla ābhe vedane vedanam param na ca artha jñānam jñānañca kadācid bhedena pratīyate tathā hi nīla ādi ākāraḥ ekaḥ grāhya tayā ekañca tad grāhakam vedanam lakṣyate na tu nīla ābhe vedane pṛthak grāhakam aparam vedanam lakṣyate tasmāt jñānasya viditasya anyena anubhava asambhave sva vedanam eva tat iti vyavatiṣṭhate 
[271,vi_271,viii]	kiñca jñāna antareṇa anubhavaḥ bhavet tatra api ca smṛtiḥ dṛṣṭā tad vedanam kena tasya api anyena ced nīla ādi viṣayasya jñānasya jñāna antareṇa anubhavaḥ bhavet tatra api jñāna jñānepi hismṛtiḥ dṛṣṭa yadā jñāna antara ālambakam jñānam krameṇa smaryate na ca aguhītam smaryate iti tasya jñāna jñānasya vedanam vaktavyam tat kena astu vedanam yadi sva samvedanena tadā pūrvakasya api tathā sthitiḥ vyartham anyena vedanā aṅgīkaraṇam tasya api anyena ced vedanam tadā 
[272,i_272,ii]	imām mālām jñāna vidām koyam janayati anubandhinīm pūrvā dhīḥ sā eva ced na syāt sañcāraḥ viṣaya antare jñāna vṛttīnām imām mālām anubandhinīm prabandha pravṛttām kaḥ janayati na tāvat artha indriya ādi sāmagrī tasyāḥ artha jñāna mātra janana vyāpāra tvāt sā eva grāhyā dhīḥ pūrvikā sva grāhikām dhiyam janayati sā ca sva grāhikām iti prabandha pravṛttiḥ iti ced evam sati sva kāraṇa grahaṇa pravaṇa tvāt viṣaya antare jñānāt anyasmin arthe sañcāraḥ grāhaka tvena pravṛttiḥ na syāt 
[272,iii_272,v]	tathā hi tām grāhya lakṣaṇa prāptām āsannām janikām dhiyam agṛhītvā uttaram jñānam gṛhṇīyāt aparam katham janikām dhiyam āsannām grāhya lakṣaṇa prāptām agṛhītvā uttaram jñānam aparam viṣayaṃkatham gṛhṇīyāt 
[272,vi_272,viii]	pratyāsannena arthena pratibaddha śakti tvāt pūrvā dhīḥ artha grāhakam eva jñānam janayati na sva grāhakam iti ced āha ātmani jñāna janane svabhāve niyatān ca tām kaḥ nāmānyaḥ vibadhnīyāt bahis aṅge antaraṅgikām ātmani vijñāna janane sva grāhaka jñāna utpādake svabhāvaḥ niyatām vyavasthitām ca tām imām antaraṅgikām anya nirapekṣa tvāt kaḥ nāmānyoḥ thaḥ bahis aṅgaḥ sva jñāna janane cakṣuḥ manaskāra ādi apekṣi tvāt vibadhnīyāt sva grāhaka jñāna janana pravṛttām tiraskuryyāt yena viṣaya antara sañcāraḥ dhiyaḥ syāt 
[272,ix_273,i]	bāhyaḥ sannihita upyarthaḥ tām vibadhnan hi na prabhuḥ dhiyam na anubhavet kaścid anyathā arthasya sannidhau tasmāt vāhyaḥ sannihita upyarthaḥ tām sva grāhaka jñāna janane śaktām dhiyam vibadhnan pratihātum na prabhuḥ śaktaḥ anyathā yadi evam na abhyupagamyate tadā arthasya sannidhau tat jñānasya eva utpādanāt jñāna jñānasya anutpādāt hiyam kaścid na anubhavet 
[273,ii_273,iii]	na ca asat nihita artha asti daśā kācid atas dhiyaḥ utkhāta mūlā smṛtiḥ api utsannā iti ujjvalam matam na ca kācid daśā sannihita arthā sti yatra jñāna jñānam utpadyeta na artha jñānam iti na syāt anubhavaḥ buddheḥ tasmāt dhiyaḥ smṛtiḥ apyu tkhāta mūlāḥ utsannā buddhi smaraṇasya hi mūlam buddhi anubhavaḥ iti jñānān anubhave kutas smaraṇam iti jñāna antareṇa jñāna anubhava vādinām ujjvalam matam iti upahasati kiñca 
[273,iv_273,v]	atīta ādi vikalpānām yeṣām na arthasya sannidhiḥ sañcāra karaṇa abhāvāt utsīdet artha cintanam yeṣām atīta ādi arthaṃviṣayāṇām vikalpānām arthasya sannidhiḥ na asti yaḥ pūrvakasya jñānasya sva grāhaka jñāna janana śaktim pratibadhnīyāt yena viṣaya antara grāhiṇaḥ vikalpāḥ syuḥ tatra sañcāra kāraṇasya arthasya vikalpa viṣayasya abhāvāt kasyacid atīta ādeḥ arthasya cintanam vikalpanam utsīdet 
[273,vi_273,ix]	syāt etat ātma vijñāna janane śakti saṃkṣayataḥ śanais viṣaya antara sañcāraḥ yadi tad jñānānām ātmani grāhaka jñāna janane śanais krameṇa sva grāhaka jñāna janikāyāḥ śakteḥ saṃkṣayataḥ tathābhūta jñāna anutpattau viṣaya antare sañcāraḥ jñāna pravṛttiḥ yadi kathyate sā eva artha dhīḥ kutas śakti kṣaye pūrva dhiyaḥ na hi dhīḥ prāk dhiyām vinā 
[273,x_274,i]	tadā pūrva dhiyaḥ śakti kṣaye sati sā eva artha grāhikā dhīḥ kutas jāyate na hi prāk dhiyā pūrvikām dhiyam samarthām vinā uttaram artha jñānam utpadyate anya artha aśakti viguṇe jñāne jñāna udaya āgateḥ yadi ca sa aśakta tvāt sva grāhikām dhiyam karttum asamartha artha dhiyam api na kuryyāt tathā hi anyasmin arthe āsaktiḥ abhiṣvaṅgaḥ tayā viguṇe pūrve vijñāne tad uttarasya jñānasya udaya āgateḥ janma apratīteḥ pūrva buddheḥ sāmarthyāt uttara buddheḥ janma iti niścīyate tatas samarthā pūrva buddhiḥ sva grāhiṇīm eva dhiyam janayet tatra para apekṣā virahāt 
[274,ii_274,iv]	nanu ālaya vijñānāt sakṛt ṣaḍ pravṛtti vijñānāni jāyante iti iṣyate tatat sāni arthā śakti vaiguṇyepi pūrva cetasaḥ ālaya jñāna antaram jāyeran ālaya jñānasya avyāhata śakti tvāt iti āha sakṛt vijātīya jātau api ekena paṭīyasā cittena ahita vaiguṇyāt ālayāt na anya sambhavaḥ sakṛt vijātīyānām pravṛti jñānānām jātau api ālaya jñānādiṣṭāyām ekena cittena sva viṣaya āsaktena paṭīyasā viṣaya antara jñāna jananam pratyāhitam āropitam vaiguṇyam yasya tasmāt ālayāt anyasya viṣaya antara grāhi jñānasya sambhavaḥ na bhavati 
[274,v_274,vii]	na hi ālaya jñānam iti eva pravṛtti jñānāni bhavanti kintu manaskā rasāt guṇyam apekṣante anyathā yadi evam na iṣyate tadā na apekṣeta anyathā sāmyam manaḥ vṛtteḥ manontaram manaḥ jñāna krama utpattiḥ api apekṣā prasādhanī manasaḥ samanantara pratyayasya vṛtteḥ sāmyam artha antarāna āsakta tvena ānukūlyam utpitsu manaḥ antaram na apekṣeta apekṣate ca tatas manaskāra anukūla tāsa apekṣāt ālayāt jñāna utpattiḥ tathā manaḥ jñānānām vikalpānām krameṇa utpattiḥ yugapad anutpāda upyuttara jñānānām pūrva jñāna apekṣā prasādhanī 
[274,viii_275,i]	eka tvāt manasoni asmin saktasya anya āgateḥ yadi jñāna antarasya anudayaḥ na kadācid sahodayāt aviguṇa pūrva jñāna anapekṣāyām ālayāt indriya jñānāni iva vikalpa jñānāni api saha jāyeran aṇu parimāṇasya nityasya ekasya manasaḥ anyasmin indriye saktasya anyatra indriya antare agateḥ agamanāt indriya antara jasya jñāna antarasya anudayaḥ yadi sammataḥ saḥ pi na yuktaḥ kadācid nartakī dṛṣṭi avasthā ādiṣu aneka viṣaya sannipāte cakṣuḥ ādi jñānānām sahodayāt 
[275,ii_275,iv]	yadā ca na paṭīyān kaścid viṣayaḥ pratyupatiṣṭhate puruṣasya ca na kvacid viśeṣeṇa icchā bhavati tadā sama vṛttau ca tulyat tvāt sarva dānya āgatiḥ bhavet janma ca ātma manaḥ yoga mātra jānām sakṛt bhavet artha puruṣa icchāyāḥ samāyām sādhāraṇāyām vṛttau ca manasaḥ eka indriya sambaddhasya tulya tvāt viṣaya antare preraka abhāvāt udāsīna tvāt sarvadā tad indriya jñāna utpattau satyām anyasya indriya antara jñāna jñeyasya āgatiḥ bhavet pratītiḥ na syāt asti ca kvacid anāsaktasya viṣaya antareṣu ekasya api aneka artha darśanam ātma manaḥ yoga mātra jānām viṣaya anirapekṣāṇām sukha ādi jñānānām indriya manaḥ yoga viśeṣasya niyāmakasya abhāvāt sakṛt vā janma syā t 
[275,v_275,vi]	ekā eva caitkriyā ekaḥ syāt kindīpaḥ aneka darśanaḥ krameṇa api na śaktam syāt paścāt api aviśeṣatas na hi rūpa ādi buddhīnām eva sukha ādi buddhīnām indriya manaḥ yoga viśeṣāt pratiniyamaḥ śakyaḥ vaktum ekasmāt manasaḥ ekā eva sukha ādi buddhi lakṣaṇā kriyā jāyate na ca dve iti ced yadi evam kim kasmāt dīpaḥ ekaḥ aneka darśanaḥ aneka draṣṭṛ jñāna janakaḥ draṣṭuḥ aneka tvāt ekopyaneka jñāna janakaḥ iti ced jñeyasya aneka tvāt tad grāhaka an eka jñāna jana kopi syāt iti samānam kiñca manaḥ nityam ekadā api sarva jñāna janana śaktam na vā śaktañcet sarva jñānāni sakṛt kuryāt aśak tañcet krameṇa api tat janane na śaktam syāt pūrva avasthitasya aśaktasya rūpasya paścāt api aviśeṣatas viśeṣa abhāvāt 
[276,i_276,ii]	anena deha puruṣau uktau saṃskārataḥ yadi niyamaḥ sa kutas paścāt buddheḥ ca id aḥ tu sammatam anena manasaḥ śakta tva aśaktatva vikalpāt doṣa dvayena deha puruṣau śarīra ātmānau uktau ukta uttarau tayoḥ api tathā avikalpe tathā doṣa sadbhāvāt jñāna jāta jñāna hetoḥ saṃskārataḥ buddhīnām asakṛt bhāva niyamaḥ yadi iṣṭaḥ tadā saṃskārasya kutas paścā dutpannaḥ buddhīḥ niyamayet buddheḥ pūrvikāyāḥ upapadyate iti ced astu pūrvasyāḥ buddheḥ vāsanā saṃjñakasya saṃskāraḥ sa buddhi ātmanaḥ janma sammatam asmākam tathā ca yat uktam na hi dhīḥ prāk dhiyā vinā iti tat eva prasādhitam syāt tatas ca buddheḥ buddhi antara janmanaḥ sāmarthyāt uttarayā dhiyā pūrva buddhiḥ gṛhyeta iti na syāt viṣaya antarasañca ārosyāḥ 
[276,iii_276,v]	syāt etat buddheḥ upādāna tā mātram buddhi antaram prati na tat grāhya tā tatas viṣaya antara sañcāraḥ bhavet iti āha na grāhyatā anyā jananāt jananam grāhya lakṣaṇam agrāhyam na hi tejosti na buddhi antara jana nāt anyā tat grāhya tā kintarhi jananam eva grāhyasya lakṣaṇam tat ced asti kutas grāhyatāyāḥ abhāvaḥ na hi tejaḥ jyotiḥ buddheḥ janakatayā agrāhyam asti tasmāt idam eva buddhim prati grāhya tvam grāhyasya yat tat jñānam nāma 
[277,i_277,iii]	nanu ca tejasaḥ buddhi janakasya sūkṣmaḥ vyavahitaḥ sannihitataraḥ ca kaścid avayavaḥ yathā na gṛhyate tathā janikā api buddhiḥ na gṛhyeta iti āha na ca saukṣmya ādi anaṃśake anaṃśake niravayave jñāne saukṣmyam sūkṣma tvam na asti ādi śabdāt sva santāna varti tva avyavadhānātya asatti ādayaḥ ca anupalambha hetavaḥ na santi 
[277,iv_277,vi]	syāt etat jñānasya dve śaktī jñāna janana śaktiḥ grāhyatā śaktiḥ catatra krameṇa grāhyatā śakti hānau janana śakti mātram avatiṣṭhate iti āha grāhyatā śakti hāniḥ syāt na anyasya janana ātmanaḥ grāhyatāyāḥ na khalu anyat jananam grāhya lakṣaṇe anyasya jñāna kārya bhūta janana ātmanaḥ janaka svabhāvasya pūrva jñānasya grāhyatā śakti hāniḥ na syāt jananasya grāhya lakṣaṇa tvāt tasya ca sattvāt tathā hi grāhya lakṣaṇe akṣa vidyu palabhyamānena khalu grāhyatāyāḥ anyat sākṣāt jjananam yat eva uttarottara jñānasya sākṣāt jananam tat eva tad grāhya tvam tatas janana sattve na asti grāhya tva hāniḥ 
[277,vii_277,viii]	sākṣāt na hi anyathā buddhe rūpa ādiḥ upakārakaḥ grāhyatā lakṣaṇāt anyaḥ tad bhāva niyamosya kaḥ na hi anyathā sākṣāt jana nāt anyena prakāreṇa rūpa ādiḥ dṛśyamānaḥ buddheḥ grāhikāyāḥ upakārakaḥ paraspara upakāriṇā upi grāhya tve rūpa kāraṇa grahaṇam api syāt anupakārakasya grāhya tve sarva grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt asya rūpa ādeḥ grāhya tā lakṣaṇāt deśa ādi aviprakarṣiṇaḥ sākṣāt janaka tvāt anyaḥ kaḥ tad bhāva niyamaḥ grāhya tva niyamaḥ 
[277,ix_278,i]	buddheḥ api tat asti iti sā api sattve vyavasthitā grāhya upādāna saṃvittī cetasaḥ grāhya lakṣaṇam tad sākṣāt janakatva lakṣaṇam grāhya tvam buddheḥ api asti iti sā api uttarabuddhi janikā tathā eva tad grāhya tve vyavasthitā rūpa ādiṣu kāraṇa tvepi deśa ādi aviprakarṣaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi upayogañca apekṣya tat grāhyatā iṣyate cetasaḥ tu deśa ādi viprakarṣa abhāvāt caśruḥ ādi upayoga abhāvāt ca grāhiṇaḥ jñānasya upādānam upādāna kāraṇa tā samvittiḥ anubhava ātma tā te grāhya lakṣaṇam sva samvedana svabhāvatāyām satyām upādāna kāraṇa tā uttara buddhi grāhyatā iti arthaḥ 
[278,ii_278,iv]	nanu sūkṣma vyavahita āsanna rūpa ādi anupādānañca jñānañced na grāhyam tadā katham yoginām teṣām grahaṇam iti āha rūpa ādeḥ cetasaḥ ca evam aviśuddha dhiyam prati grāhya lakṣaṇa cintā iyam acintyā yoginām gatiḥ rūpa ādeḥ a sūkṣmasya avyavadhāna ādi viśiṣṭasya buddhi kāraṇa tvam cetasaḥ ca anubhava ātma tve sati upādāna tā grāhya tvam iti evam anena prakāreṇa grāhya lakṣaṇa cintā iyam prakrāntāḥ aśuddha dhiyam vāsanā upapluta buddhimat arvāk darśinam janam prati na tu viśiṣṭa buddhīn yoginaḥ prati yasmāt yoginām sūkṣma vyavahita para citta digatiḥ acintyā bhāva sattā mātram yogi jñāna apekṣyam grāhya lakṣaṇam iti arthaḥ 
[278,v_278,vi]	tatra sūkṣma ādi bhāvena grāhyam agrāhya tām vrajet rūpa ādi buddheḥ ki jātam paścāt yat prāk na vidyate tatra etādṛśe grāhya lakṣaṇa dvaye sthite sati rūpam sthūlam avyavadhāna ādi bhāve sati grāhyam sat paścāt sūkṣma ādi bhāvena agrāhya tām vrajet iti yujyate eva etat buddheḥ ekadā grāhyāyāḥ paścāt agrahaṇa kāle kim sūkṣma tva ādi agrāhyatā kāraṇam jātam yat prāk upalambha kāle na vidyate na hi sva santāna vartitanaḥ ca isaḥ niravayavasya sarvadā kiñcid upalambha kāraṇam asti tāduśasya yadi anupalambhaḥ kadācid na upalabhyeta upalabhyate ca iha kadācid sarvadā upalambha prasaṅgaḥ 
[279,i_279,ii]	sati svadhī grahe tasmāt sā eva anantara hetu tā cetasaḥ grāhyatā sā eva tatas na artha antare gatiḥ tasmāt citta antareṇa svadhī grahe sati cetasaḥ yā eva anantara hetu tā buddhi antaram prati sā eva grāhyatā sā ca na apaiti tatas uttarottara buddheḥ pūrva pūrva buddhi grahaṇam eva vyāpāra eti artha antare na syāt gatiḥ 
[279,iii_279,vi]	nanu bhāvāḥ aneka śakti yogāt aneka kārya kāriṇaḥ eka śakti yogāt eka kārya kāriṇaḥ tat jñānasya grāhyatā śaktiḥ api anyā anyā ca janana śaktiḥ tatas grāhyatā śaktihānāt api janana śaktiḥ bhaviṣyati iti āha nānā eka śakti abhāvepi bhāvaḥ nānā eka kārya kṛt prakṛtyā eva iti gaditam nānā ekasmāt na ced bhavet nānā eka śakti abhāvepi bhāva vyatiriktā anekāsām śaktīnām ekasyāḥ ca śakteḥ abhāvepi bhāvaḥ sva hetoḥ nāna eka kārya kāraṇa svabhāvatayā utpannaḥ nānā eka kārya kṛt prakṛtyā eva bhavati iti gadi tam nanu nānā ekam kāryam ekasmāt kāraṇāt na bhavet siddhānta virodhāt iti ced 
[279,vii_280,i]	na kiñcid ekam ekasmāt sāmagrayāḥ sarva sambhavaḥ sattyam etat na kiñcid kāryam ekasmāt kāraṇāt jāyate kintu sāmagryā janma aneka upādāna sahakāri bhāva sañcaya ātmikāyāḥ sarvasya ekasya anekasya ca kāryasya sambhavaḥ kathantarhi ekam anekasyam hetuḥ ucyate iti āha ekam syāt api sāmagryoḥ iti uktam tad aneka kṛt cakṣu rūpa āloka manaskāra ādiṣu jāyamāna rūpa kṣaṇa indriya jñāna kārya dvaya apekṣayā avāntara bhinta sāmagryoḥ ekasya rūpasya upādāna sahakāri bhāvena upayogāt ekasmāt api anekam kāryam jāyate iti tatas ekam aneka kārya kṛt iti ucyate na tu ekasmāt asahāyāt anekam kāryam jāyate iti abhiprāyāt
[280,ii_280,viii]	syāt etat artham pūrvañca vijñānam gṛhṇīyāt yadi dhīḥ parā dhīḥ jāyamānā pūrvañca vijñānam arthañca tad kāla sannipatitam yadi gṛhṇīyāt tadā viṣaya antara sañcāraḥ sambhavet atra āha abhilāpa dvayam nityam syāt dṛṣṭa kramam akramam pūrva gṛhītasya varṇṇasya cintā dā ādi śabdāt pratyakṣepi ekasmin cetasi dṛṣṭaḥ kramaḥ yasya tat dṛṣṭa kramam abhilāpa dvayam varṇṇa dvayam nityam akramam syāt yugapad pratīyeta iti arthaḥ kim kāraṇam iti āha pūrva apara artha bhāsi tvāt cintā ādi jñānena hi pūrva varṇṇa grāhaka jñānam gṛhyeta iti tad pratibhāsī varṇṇaḥ gṛhyeta tad kāla upanipatitaḥ ca anyaḥ varṇṇaḥ iti krama upalabhyayoḥ yugapad grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ dvis dvirekam ca bhāseta bhāsanāt ātma tad dhiyoḥ ekañca varṇṇa ādiḥ dvis dvis bhāseta ātma tad dhiyoḥ bhāsanāt tad darśane tat jñāna darśane tu tat ṛṣṭam iti dvidhā darśana prasaṅgaḥ 
[280,ix_280,x]	viṣaya antara sañcāre yadyanti at na anubhūyate para anubhūta vat sarvān anubhūtiḥ prasajyate atha viṣaya jñāne vṛtte tad jñāne ca utpanne viṣaya darśanasya niṣpanna tvāt jñāna antaram viṣaya antara grāhakam iti syāt viṣaya antara sañcāraḥ iti abhimate yat yantyam jñānam jñāna anubhavitṛ na anubhūyate tadā sarvasya arthasya tat jñānasya ca ananubhūtiḥ prasajyate para anubhūta vat puruṣa antara anubhūta artha tad jñānayoḥ iva 
[281,i_281,iii]	nanu ātmanā anubhūtam artham tat jñānam pratyakṣam na paraiḥ anubhūtam iti yadi ucyate ātma anubhūtam pratyakṣam na anubhūtam paraiḥ yadi ātmā anubhūtiḥ sā siddhā kutas yena evam ucyate nanu antya jñānān anubhave artha jñānasya ananubhavāt tad anubhava abhāve ca artha anubhava asiddheḥ ātmā anubhūtiḥ sā kutas siddhā yena evam ucyate ātma anubhūtam pratyakṣam na para anubhūtam iti 
[281,iv_281,vi]	nanu cakṣuḥ ādau anartha bhūte cakṣuḥ ādinā rūpa ādi anubhūtam iti yathā tathā jñānān anubhavepi arthaḥ jñātaḥ iti bhaviṣyati iti āha vyakti hetu aprasiddhiḥ syāt na vyakteḥ vyaktam icchataḥ vyakti asiddhau api vyaktam yadi vyaktam idam jagat artha vyakti hetoḥ cakṣuḥ ādeḥ artha darśanepya prasiddhiḥ avyaktiḥ syāt yatas na kāraṇa darśana pūrvakam kārya darśanam na tu vyakterūpa labdheḥ vyaktam artham icchataḥ vyakti asiddhiḥ yuktā yadi punar vyakteḥ asiddhau api vyaktam vastu ucyate tadā sarvam idam jagat vyaktam syāt avyakta vyaktika tvena viśeṣa abhāvāt tathā hi arthaḥ na sattā mātreṇa pratītaḥ ucyate pratipatti saṃyogāt na api jñāna sattā mātreṇa para citta jñānena api saṃvedana prasaṅgāt kintu jñāna anubhavena artha pratītiḥ vācyā na ca anyena samvedanam jñānasya upapapadyate iti sva prakāśam eva svabhāvataḥ tat vaktavyam iti sva samvedana siddhiḥ iti 
[282,i]	pratyakṣam ākhyāya avasara prāptam anumānam idānīm vaktavyam tat ca dvividham sva artham parārthañca tatra sva artham idānīm vaktavyam etat pūrvaka tvāt para arthasya 
[282,ii_282,iv]	tad liṅge vipratipattayaḥ santi iti tāsām nirākaraṇena tad vyavasthāpana artham āha pakṣa dharmaḥ tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ pakṣaḥ dharmi dharma samudāya unumeyaḥ tad eka deśa tvāt upacāreṇa dharmī pakṣaḥ uktaḥ tasya dharmaḥ anena pakṣa dharma tvam uktam dharmi dharmaḥ hetuḥ iti anumāne sarvasya dharmmi dharmmaḥ hetuḥ syāt iti upacāra āśrayaṇam tathā cākṣuṣa tva ādiḥ śabde dharmiṇi na hetuḥ tad aṃśena pakṣasya dharmeṇa sisā dhayiṣitena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ boddhavyaḥ dvividhā ca iyam vyāptiḥ vyāpaka vyāpya dharma tayā tatra vyāpye sati vyāpakasya avaśyambhāvaḥ tasya vyāptiḥ vyāpyasya ca vyāpakaḥ eva sati bhāvaḥ nāma tasya vyāptiḥ ābhyām yathākramam anvaya vyatirekau uktau vyāpya sadbhāve vyāpakasya satva niyamasya anvaya rūpa tvāt vyāpaka abhāve vyāpya abhāvasya ca vyatireka rūpa tvāt 
[283,i_283,iv]	etena tri rūpa tvam hetoḥ lakṣaṇa muktam tridhā eva saḥ tridhā eva tri prakāraḥ eva kārya svabhāva anupalambha bhedena sa hetuḥ yathā agniḥ atra dhamāt vṛkṣa vyavahāra yogyoyam śiṃśapā tvāt na iha pradeśe ghaṭaḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdheḥ iti saṃkhyā niyamaḥ uktaḥ kasmāt punar trividhaḥ eva hetuḥ iti āha 
[283,v_283,ix]	avinā abhau a niyamāt avinā abhā asya sādhya avyabhicāri tvasya trividhaḥ eva hetau niyamāt niyata tvāt saṃyogi ādiṣu ca abhāvāt sati eva avinā abhāve hetu tvam sa ca vyāptyā kathitaḥ anena saṃkhyā niyama kāraṇam uktam hetavaḥ uktāḥ ke punar hetvābhāsāḥ iti āha hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare hetu vat ābhāsantaḥ iti hetvābhāsāḥ hetu pratirūpakāḥ tatas trividhāt hetoḥ apare anye saṃyogi ādayaḥ avinā abhāve sati hetu tvam sa ca tādātmyāt tad utpatteḥ ca ye tu tad vikalāḥ te avinā abhāva virahāt hetvābhāsāḥ iti arthaḥ 
[283,x_284,i]	yadi tad utpattyā gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ tadā dhūma tva viśeṣa vat sāmānya dharmāḥ pārthiva tvādayopi gamakāḥ syuḥ tathā agneḥ sāmānya dharma vat cāndana tvāt ayopi viśeṣa dharmma agamyāḥ syuḥ sarvathā kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt iti āha kāryam svabhāvaiḥ yāvadbhiḥ avinābhāvi kārya vat kārya svabhāvaiḥ yāvadbhiḥ viśiṣṭaiḥ ddhūmavatva ādibhiḥ avinābhāvi vinā na bhavati iti kāraṇe kāraṇa viṣaye avadhāritam taiḥ eva viśiṣṭaiḥ svabhāvaiḥ hetuḥ na sādhāraṇaiḥ pārthiva tva ādibhiḥ agnim antareṇa api teṣām bhāvāt tathā kāraṇe adhikaraṇe yāvadbhiḥ svabhāvaiḥ agni tva ādibhiḥ sāmānya dharmaiḥ avinābhāvi kārya dhūma ādi niścitam teṣām sāmanya dharmāṇām hetuḥ na viśeṣa dharmāṇām ca andana tva ādīnām tāni antareṇa api dhūma ādeḥ darśanāt yadi dhūma tva viśeṣitam pārthiva tvam hetuḥ kriyate tadā iṣṭam eva vyabhicāra abhāvāt yadi ca kāraṇa gata cāndana tva ādi viśeṣa janitaḥ dhūmasya viśeṣaḥ śakyaḥ niścetum tadā ca andana tva ādayaḥ gamyāḥ iṣyante na hi kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ sattā mātreṇa gabhya gamaka bhāva nimittam kintu niścaya apekṣaḥ sa ca yāvat niścīyate tathā agamya gamaka bhāvaḥ 
[284,ii]	bhāvopi svabhāvopi hetuḥ svabhāve sādhye kīdṛśe hetoḥ bhāvaḥ kevalaḥ bhāva mātram tat anuroddhum anuvarttitum śīlam asya iti bhāva mātra anurodha tasmin yasya sattā mātreṇa yaḥ dharmaḥ avaśyam bhavati na hetu antaram apekṣate tasmin sādhye svabhāva ākhyaḥ hetuḥ na anyatra yathā vastra tvam rāge evañca vidhi sādhana tvam kārya svabhāvayoḥ darśitam 
[284,iii_285,iv]	idānīm tṛtīya hetoḥ pratiṣedha phala tvam āha apravṛttiḥ pramāṇānām pramāṇa nivṛtti rūpā anupalabdhiḥ asati sat vyavahāra atikrānta tvāt asat aviśiṣṭe deśa kāla svabhāva viprakṛṣṭe sumeru ādau sat jñāna śabda vyavahārāṇām pravṛtti pratiṣedhaḥ apravṛttiḥ tad phalā etat ca apravṛtti phala tvam dṛśya adṛśya anupalabdhyoḥ sādhāraṇaṃjñāna pūrvaka tvāt sat jñāna śabda vyavahārasya jñāna abhāve tad abhāvasya nyāya prāpta tvāt dṛśya anupalabdheḥ phala antaram āha kācid pramāṇa nivṛttiḥ asat jñānam abhāva jñānam tad phalā katham iti āha hetu bheda vyapekṣayā hetuḥ anupalambhaḥ tasya bhedaḥ viśeṣaṇam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta viṣaya tvam tasya vyapekṣayā kāṃkṣayā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anupalabdhiḥ iti arthaḥ 
[285,v]	nanu yadi anupalabdhyā abhāvaḥ sādhyate tadā upalabdhi abhāvopi tatas eva iti anavasthānāt abhāva apratipattiḥ syāt dṛṣṭāntaḥ ca na syāt anyasya abhāva sādhanasya abhāvāt anupalabdheḥ ca anavasthā prāpta tvāt atha padārtha antara upalabdhiḥ eva anupalabdhiḥ tayā adhyakṣa siddhyā abhāvaḥ sādhyate tasmāt na doṣaḥ yadi evam artha antarāt api kinnābhāvaḥ sādhyate tat api hi anupalabdhi rūpam pratyakṣa siddhañca kaḥ vā anya upalambha abhāvena sambandhaḥ 
[285,vi_286,i]	ucyate eka jñāna saṃsarggi vastu antaram tad upalabdhiḥ ca anupalabdhiḥ vivakṣita upalabdheḥ anya tvāt abhakṣā sparśanīya vat saḥ eva abhāvaḥ tad atiriktasya vigrahavataḥ abhāvasya abhāvāt tasmāt tādātmyam abhāva anupalambhayoḥ sambandhaḥ evam tarhi anupalabdhi siddhiḥ eva abhāva siddhiḥ kim sādhyate satyam na abhāvaḥ sādhyaḥ siddha tvāt asya kintarhi viṣaya upadarśanena viṣayī vyavahāraḥ sādhyate yathā go vyavahāra viṣayaḥ ayam sāsna ādi samudāya ātmaka tvāt 
[286,ii_286,iv]	sā ca prayoga bhedāt anupalabdhiḥ caturvidhā katham iti āha viruddha kāryayoḥ siddhiraḥ hetu bhāyoḥ dṛśya ātmanā urabhāva artha anupalabdhiḥ caturvidhā viruddhañca kāryañca viruddha kārye kāryañca pratyāsatteḥ viruddhasya eva boddhavyam tayoḥ dṛśya ātmanoḥ hetu bhāvayoḥ kāraṇa svabhāvayoḥ ca dṛśya ātmanoḥ yathākramam siddhiḥ upalabdhiḥ asiddhiḥ anupalabdhiḥ ca 
[286,v_286,vi]	viruddha upalabdhiḥ yathā na atra śīta sparśaḥ agneḥ vyāpya vyāpakayoḥ vastutaḥ tādātmyāt vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhiḥ api anena eva uktā bhavati yathā na atra tuṣāra spararśaḥ agneḥ viruddha kārya upalabdhiḥ yathā na atra śīta sparśaḥ dhūmāt kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ yathā na atra dhūmaḥ anagneḥ svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ yathā na atra dhūma unupalabdheḥ anena vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ api uktāḥ yathā na atra śiṃśapā vṛkṣa abhāvāt caturvidhā api anupalabdhiḥ abhāva arthā pratiṣedha phalā tatra svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ svayam eva pratiṣedhya abhāva rūpa tayā siddhā abhāva vyavahāra sādhanī itarāḥ tu niṣedhya abhāva avyabhicāriṇyaḥ tad abhāvam abhāva vyavahārañca sādhayanti tasya asiddha tvāt 
[286,vii_287,i]	yadi viruddha kārya upalabdhyā abhāva siddhiḥ tadā viruddha kāraṇa upalabdhyā api kim na sādhyate iti āha tad viruddha nimittasya yā upalabdhiḥ prayujyate nimittayoḥ viruddha tva abhāvaḥ hi vyabhicāravān tad viruddha nimittasya niṣedhya viruddha kāraṇasya yā upalabdhiḥ prayujyate yathā na śīta sparśaḥ tra kāṣṭhāt iti sā niṣedhyasya viruddhasya ca ye nimitte tayoḥ viruddha tva abhāve vyabhicāriṇī anaikāntikī virodhe tu nimittayoḥ iṣyate eva yathā na asya roma harṣa ādi viśeṣāḥ santi sannihita dahana viśeṣa tvāt romaharṣa tada bhāvayoḥ virodhaḥ tad kāraṇayoḥ ca śīta dahanayoḥ iti yuktā iyam anupalabdhiḥ tathā niṣedhya viruddha kāraṇa kāya palabdhiḥ yathā na roma harṣa yukta puruṣa vān ayam pradeśa udhūmāt iti ukta aṣṭavidhā anupalabdhiḥ 
[287,ii_287,iv]	anayā diśā aparāḥ api boddhavyāḥ iṣṭam viruddha kāryepi deśa kāla ādi apekṣaṇām anyathā vyabhicārī syāt bhasma iva aśīta sādhane virupaddha kārye viruddha kārya upalabdhau api viṣaye nirdeśāt deśasya sannihitasya kālasya varttamānasya kvacid atīta apekṣaṇam iṣṭam anyathā vyabhicāri syāt liṅgam udāharaṇam āha bhasma iva aśītasya śīta abhāvasya sādhane yathā na āsīt kvacid śīta sparśaḥ na asti vā atra bhasmanaḥ iti bhasma anaikāntikam deśa viśeṣye atīta kāla apekṣayā tu syāt hetuḥ na āsīt atra śīta sparśaḥ bhasmanaḥ iti 
[287,v_288,ii]	nanu hetunā yaḥ samagreṇa kārya utpāda unumīyate artha antara anapekṣa tvāt sa svabhāva unuvarṇṇitaḥ hetunā samagreṇa yaḥ kārya utpāda unumīyate sa kasmin hetau antarbhavati iti āha sa svabhāva hetuḥ anuvarṇṇitaḥ na hi samagrāt hetoḥ kārya sambhava unumīyate kintarhi kārya arjana yogya tvam tat ca artha antara anapekṣa tvāt hetu sākalya mātrā anubandhyā iva iti tasmin sādhye hetu sākalyam svabhāva hetuḥ eva 
[288,iii_288,v]	kasmāt punar kāryam eva na anumīyate iti āha sāmagrophala śaktīnām pariṇāma anubandhini anaikāntika tā kārye pratibandhasya sambhavāt kārye anumeye anaikāntika tā hetu sākalyasya kīdṛśe sāmagryāḥ phalañca tāḥ uttarakṣaṇam śaktayaḥ ca tāsām pariṇāmaḥ kārya utpāda anuguṇaḥ tāratamya yogī kṣaṇa prabandhaḥ tad anubandhini tad apekṣiṇi atas eva pratibandhasya sambhavāt iti uktam 
[288,vi_288,viii]	na khalu kāryam hetavaḥ militāḥ iti eva bhavati kim tu eṣām viśeṣam apekṣate atra antare ca śakti vyāghātaḥ mantra tantra ādinā vaikalyañca sambhavati iti kāryasya avaśya bhāvāt na tad anumānam eka sāmagrī adhīnasya rūpa āde rasataḥ gatiḥ hetu dharma anumānena dhūma indhana vikāra vat yā ca rasataḥ madhura ādikāt rūpa ādeḥ ādi śabdāt gandhasya sparśasya ca eka sāmagrī adhīnasya rasa ādinā saha ekasāmagraya āyattasya gatiḥ sā katham iti āha hetu dharma anumānena rasa kāraṇasya dharmaḥ rasa ādi sahacara rūpa janaka tvam tad anumānena rasāt rūpa ādi gatiḥ na hi kāryam rasaḥ kāraṇam antareṇa kāraṇañca asya rasa sahakāri rūpa janakam puñjāt puñja utpatteḥ atas tasmin anumite anumitam eva rūpam dhūma indhana vikāra vat dhūmāt hetu dharma anumānena indhana vikārasya aṅgārādeḥ ddhūma sahacarasyaḥ vā anumānam 
[289,i_289,iv]	etat eva sphuṭayannā śakti pravṛttyā na vinā rasaḥ sā eva anya kāraṇam iti atīta eka kālānām jāyate kārya liṅgataḥ rasa hetoḥ śakti pravṛttyā śakti ābhimukhyena vinā na rasaḥ utpadyate sā eva rasa hetoḥ śakti pravṛttiḥ anyasya rūpa ādeḥ kāraṇam itara samāna kāla rūpa ādi janaka tvena rasa hetoḥ atītasya hetoḥ eka kālānām rasa sahacarāṇām ca rūpa ādīnām gatiḥ tasya rasa rūpa hetoḥ kāryāt rasāt liṅgāt jātā evam pipīlika utsaraṇa ādi darśanāt varṣā pipīlikā ādi kṣobha hetoḥ bhūta pariṇāma viśeṣasya anumānāt varṣa anumānam kārya liṅga jam veditavyam nadī pūra ādeḥ varṣa kārya tvam vyaktam eva 
[289,v_289,vi]	hetunā yaḥ asamagreṇa kārya utpādaḥ anumīyate tat śeṣa vat asāmarthyāt dehāt rāga anumāna vat yaḥ punar hetunā asamagreṇa kārya utpādaḥ kārya utpādana yogya tvam anumīyate tad śeṣa vat ana ekānti kam asāmarthyāt samartham hi kārya utpādana yogyam na ca vyagrāṇām samartha tā dehāt buddhīndriya ādeḥ ca hetoḥ rāga anumāna vat deha ādīnām kathañcid rāga hetu tva ipi na ayoni śomanaskāra rahitānām kāraṇa tvam sahitānām eva hetu tvāt tatas kevalāt dehāt rāga anumānam anaikāntikam 
[290,i_290,iii]	tathā vipakṣe adṛṣṭi mātreṇa kārya sāmānya darśanāt hetu jñāna pramāṇa āmam vacanāt rāgita ādi vat vipakṣe adṛṣṭi mātreṇa kārya sāmānyasya kvacid dharmiṇi darśanāt hetu jñān aṃyat pramāṇa ābham sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttikam tat vacanāt rāgita ādi vat yathā vacanasya vīta rāge adarśanāt kvacid darśanāt rāga anumānam anaikāntikam na hi rāga vacanayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ siddhaḥ vaktu kāma tā hetu tvāt tasya sā ca vīta rāgasya karuṇayā saṃbhavati yadi api vaktari rāgaḥ dṛśyate tathā api kvacid vaktu kāma tāsa tvepi rāga abhāve vacana abhāva asiddheḥ na tad kāryatā siddhiḥ upala khaṇḍāt vaktu kāma tā nivṛtteḥ eva vacana abhāvaḥ na tu rāga abhāvāt tatas vīta rāgāt sandigdhosya vyatirekaḥ 
[290,iv_290,v]	na ca adarśana mātreṇa vipakṣe avyabhicāritā saṃbhāvya vyabhicāri tvāt sthālī taṃḍula pāka vat na ca vipakṣe hetoḥ adarśana mātreṇa sādhya abhāva prayukta sādhana abhāva niścaya rahitena sādhya avyabhicāritā sādhyate sambhāvya vyabhicāri tvāt yadi vipakṣāt hetu nivṛtti niścayaḥ evam vyabhicāra śaṅkā nirāsaḥ sa tu na asti iti tasya api abhāvaḥ sthālī taṇḍula pāka vat sthālī antargatānām taṇḍulānāṃpākasya iva anumānam tad itareṣām pāka adarśanāt śeṣavat 
[291,i_291,iii]	kim punar śeṣavat iti ucyate iti āha yasya adarśana mātreṇa vyatirekaḥ pradarśyate tasya saṃśaya hetu tvāt śeṣavat tat udāhṛtam yasya liṅgasya adarśana mātreṇa vipakṣevī atirekaḥ pradarśyate na tu kāraṇa vyāpaka nivṛttyā tasya saṃśaya hetu tvāt sādhya aniścāyaka tvāt śeṣavat tat udāhṛtam sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvam śeṣavat ucyate pratibandha abhāvāt iti arthaḥ 
[291,iv_291,v]	hetoḥ triṣu api rūpeṣu niścayaḥ tena varṇitaḥ asiddha viparīta artha vyabhicāri vipakṣataḥ sūtram uktam asya ayam arthaḥ yaḥ guṇaḥ sa dravya āśrayī tat yathā rūpa ādiḥ apākaja anuṣṇa aśīta sparśasya guṇaḥ tasmāt tasya āśraya bhūtena dravyeṇa bhavitavyam na ca ayam dṛṣṭānām pṛthivī ādīnām guṇaḥ teṣām pāka ja an uṣṇa aśīta sparśa ādi guṇa tvāt tatas yasya ayam guṇaḥ sa vāyuḥ bhaviṣyati iti ukte vaiśeṣikeṇa tatra ācārya dignāgena uktam yadi adarśana mātreṇa dṛṣṭebhyaḥ sparśasya pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate na ca sā upi yuktaḥ iti dṛśya adṛśya samudāyasya sāmānyena niṣedhāt yat etat uktam tat virudhyate iti vārtikakāraḥ darśayan āha dṛṣṭa ityādi yadi adṛṣṭyā nivṛtiḥ syāt tadā adṛṣṭena darśanāt kāraṇāt apāka jasya anuṣṇa aśīta sparśasya dṛṣṭā ayuktiḥ dṛṣṭeṣu pṛthivī ādiṣu asaṅga tiryām varṇitā vaiśeṣikaiḥ yasyāḥ ācāryeṇa ayukta tvam uktam sā syāt avirodhinī yuktā eva syāt iti arthaḥ vāyu prakaraṇe pṛthivī ādibhyaḥ yadi sparśa ādeḥ guṇa tvam siddham syāt tatas vāyu dravya anumānam syāt sā eva tu asiddhā svātantryeṇa pratīteḥ sparśa aviśeṣa usmākam vāyuḥ ācāryeṇa tu sparśa vyatiriktam vāyum abhyupagamya ayukta tvam uktam pare 
[292,i]	tena pratibandhasya avaśya abhyupagantavya tvena hetoḥ triṣu api pakṣa dharma anvaya vyatirekeṣu niścayaḥ ācārya dignāgena vārṇṇitaḥ katham uktaḥ iti āha asiddhasya viparīta arthasya viruddhasya vyabhicāriṇaḥ anaikāntikasya vipakṣeṇa tatra asiddhatva vipakṣeṇa pakṣa dharma tvasya niścayaḥ uktaḥ viruddha vipakṣeṇa anvayasya anaikāntika vipakṣeṇa vyatirekasya 
[292,ii_292,iv]	na hya sati pratibandhe vipakṣāt vyatirekaḥ śakya niścayaḥ uktaḥ ca niścayaḥ tatas pratibandha upya ācāryeṇa iṣṭaḥ iti pratīyate anyathā vyabhicāri vipakṣeṇa vaidharmya vacanam ca yat yadi adṛṣṭi phalam tat ca tad anuktepi gamyate pratibandha aniṣṭau vyabhicāriṇaḥ anaikāntikasya vipakṣeṇa vaidharmyasya vyatirekasya vacanam yat ācāryasya eṣa tāvat nyāyaḥ yat u bhayam vaktavyam viruddha anaikāntika pratipakṣeṇa iti ubhayam anvaya vyatirekau tat ca yadi adṛṣṭi phalam adarśana mātra phalam tad adarśana mātram anuktepi vyabhicāri vipakṣeṇa vyatirekaḥ gamyate hetu trairūpya nirddeśāt eva vipakṣe adarśana mātrasya gata tvāt tasmāt vaidharmya vacanena vipakṣe hetu abhāvaḥ kathyate sa ca adarśana mātreṇa na sidhyati 
[292,v_293,i]	na asti iti vacanāt eva sidhyati iti ced na ca na asti iti vacanāt tat na asti eva yathā yadi na asti sa khyāpyate ca ayam uktau na iti gatiḥ tadā na ca na asti iti vacanāt eva tad sādhanam vipakṣe na asti eva iti yuktam tat api hi anupalambham eva khyāpayati sa ca sarvasmāt vipakṣāt hetvabhāva pratītau aśaktaḥ kathantarhi iti āha yathā yena prakāreṇa sādhya sādhanayoḥ pratibandhaḥ sati sādhya abhāvena sādhanam vipakṣe na asti sa nyāyaḥ yadi khyāpyate vyabhicāri vipakṣeṇa vaidharmya uktyā tadā na asti iti gamyate na anyathā 
[293,ii_293,v]	kiñca yadi adṛṣṭau nivṛttiḥ syāt śeṣavat vyabhicāri kim vyatireki api hetuḥ syāt na vācyā asiddhi yojanā yadi adṛṣṭau vipakṣāt hetoḥ nivṛttiḥ syāt śeṣavat sandigdha vipakṣa vyatirekaṃvyabhicāri kim iṣṭam ācāryeṇa evañca sarasāni etāni phalāni rūpa aviśeṣāt iti sarvasya tādṛś rūpasya pakṣīkṛta tvāt na vyabhicāra darśanam vipakṣe ca adarśanam asti iti prāptam adarśana mātrat vyatireka vādinaḥ hetu tvam asya vyatireki api hetuḥ syāt na idam nirātmakam jīvat śarīram aprāṇa ādimatva prasaṅga ādi ti bau ddham prati sā ātmakasya kasyacid asiddheḥ anvaya abhāvāt nirātmakebhyaḥ ca paṭa ādibhyaḥ nivṛtteḥ prāṇādiḥ vyatirekī sa hetuḥ syāt adarśanāt vyatireka siddheḥ aniṣṭaḥ ca ācāryeṇa 
[293,vi]	kiñca vādi prativādinoḥ asiddhasya anyatara asiddhasya sandigdhasya āśraya asiddhasya sandigdha āśraya asiddhasya asiddhasya ca nirāsam pakṣa dharma tva niścayena pratipādyāṃnvayavyatireka niścaya vacanena sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ hetoḥ anvayasya vyatirekasya ca viparītāyāḥ asiddheḥ caturvidhāyāḥ yojanāḥ ācāryeṇa sa pakṣe sannasan iti evamādiṣu api yathāyogam udāhāryyam ityādinā nirdiṣṭā sā api na vācyā adarśanasya vyatireka niścaya hetu tve sandigdha vyatirekasya hetu tvāt 
[293,vii_294,ii]	api ca viśeṣasya vyavaccheda hetu tā syāt adarśanāt pramāṇa antara vādhā ced na idānīt nāstitādṛśaḥ viśeṣasya asādhāraṇasya śrāvaṇa tva ādeḥ nitye anitye ca adarśanāt ubhayatas vyāvṛtteḥ śabde dharmiṇi dvaya vyavacchedana hetu tā syāt pramāṇa antara bādhā ced anyonya vyavaccheda rūpayoḥ eka pratiṣedhasya apara vidhinā antarīyaka tvāt ubhaya vyavaccheda unumāna bādhitaḥ na idānīm bādha saṃbhave na asti tādṛśaḥ evam tarhi adṛṣṭeḥ abhāva niścayaḥ na asti iti vaktavyam yathā śrāvaṇa tvena ubhaya vyāvṛtta tayā niścitena prasādhyamānasya ubhaya vyavacchedasya pramāṇa antareṇa bādhā 
[294,iii_294,iv]	tathā anyatra api saṃbhāvyam pramāṇa antara bādhanam dṛṣṭā ayuktiḥ adṛṣṭeḥ ca syāt sparśasya avirodhanī tathā anyatra api vipakṣāt hetoḥ vyatirikepi saṃbhāvyam pramāṇa antara bādhanam adarśana mātrasya nimittasya samāna tvāt tathā dṛṣṭā ayuktiḥ adṛṣṭeḥ ca syāt sparśasya avirodhinī dṛṣṭeṣu pṛthivī ādiṣu apākajasya anuṣṇa aśīta sparśasya ayuktiḥ yoga abhāvaḥ adṛṣṭeḥ adarśanāt vaiśeṣikasya iṣṭā anupalambhāt vyāptyā nivṛttyā niścaya ādā cāryeṇa pratikṣiptā ca yadi adarśana mātraṇe dṛṣṭebhyaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate na ca sā upi yuktaḥ ityādinā avirodhīnaḥ virodha rahitā syāt evam ācāryīyaḥ kaścana pratibandham anabhyupagacchan virodhāt upālabdhaḥ 
[295,i_295,iii]	saṃprati parān pratyāha deśa ādi bhedāt dṛśyante bhinnāḥ dravyeṣu śaktayaḥ tatra eka dṛṣṭyā na anyatra yuktaḥ tad bhāva niścayaḥ deśa ādi bhedāt deśa kāla sahakāri bhedāt dṛśyante bhinnāḥ nānā prakārāḥ dravyeṣu śaktayaḥ tatra ekasmin deśa ādau ekasya dravyasya śakti viśeṣavataḥ dṛṣṭyā anyatra deśa ādautasya śakti viśeṣavataḥ dravyasya bhāva niścayaḥ na yuktaḥ pratibandham antareṇa na hi ekatra yathā oṣadhayaḥ dṛṣṭāḥ tathā eva anyatra api tāḥ śakyante vyavasthāpayitum kṣetra ādi viśeṣāt viśiṣṭatara rasa vīrya ādi darśanāt 
[295,iv_295,vi]	kiñca ātma mṛd cetana ādīnām yaḥ abhāvasya aprasādhakaḥ saḥ eva anupalambhaḥ ki hetu abhāvasya sādhakaḥ ātma mṛd cetana ādīnām yaḥ abhāvasya aprasādhakaḥ ātmanā unupalabhyamānasya ca yaḥ anupalambhaḥ abhāvasya aprasādhakaḥ vaiśeṣikasya iṣṭaḥ tathā mudaḥ cetanāyāḥ svabhāva bhūtāyāḥ yaḥ anupalambhaḥ abhāva aprasādhakaḥ cārvākasya iṣṭaḥ tathā kṣīra ādau dadhi ādi abhāvasya yonupalambhaḥ aprasādhakaḥ iṣṭaḥ sāṃkhyasya saḥ eva anupalambhaḥ kim kasmāt vipakṣe hetu abhāvasya iṣṭaḥ vaiśeṣika ādibhiḥ yathā ghaṭa ādau prāṇa ādi matva abhāvaḥ vaiśeṣikasya vaktṛ tva abhāvaḥ vipakṣe cārvākasya saṃghāta tvā abhāvaḥ vā vipakṣe sāṃkhyasya anupalambha ādiṣṭaḥ uktaḥ pareṣān ca nyāya vyāghātaḥ paraspara virodhaḥ ca 
[296,i_296,iii]	yasmāt adarśana mātrat na vyatireka siddhiḥ tasmāt tanmātra sambandhaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhāvam eva vā nivartayet kāraṇam vā kāryam avyabhicārataḥ tasmāt tanmātra sambandhaḥ tad sādhanam kevalam tanmātram tena sambaddhaḥ hetu sattā mātreṇa kāraṇa antara apekṣā rahitena sambandhaḥ yasya iti arthaḥ svabhāvaḥ vyāpakaḥ dharmaḥ nivarttamānaḥ bhāvam vyāpyam eva vā nivarttayet yathā vṛkṣa tvam śiṃśapām vṛkṣa viśeṣa tvāt śiṃśapāyāḥ kāraṇam vā nivarttamānam kāryam nivarttayati avyabhicārataḥ na hi vyāpyam kāryam ca vyāpakena kāraṇena vinā bhavataḥ tad svabhāva tvāt tad adhīna tvāt ca iti 
[296,iv_296,vi]	tādātmya tad utpattī avaśya āśrayaṇīye anyathā eka nivṛtya anya vinivṛttiḥ katham bhavet na aśvavān iti saṃdehe kim na vā paśu saṃśayaḥ anyathā ekasya sādhyasya nivṛtyā anyasya sādhanasya vinivṛttiḥ katham bhavet svatantra tvāt na hi martyaḥ aśva rahitaḥ iti gorahitā upi bhavati 
[296,vii_296,ix]	tathā sannidhānāt tathā ekasya katham anyasya sannidhiḥ gomān iti eva martyena bhāvyam aśvavatā api kim tathā sannidhānāt ekasya hetoḥ katham anyasya sādhyasya sannidhiḥ gomān iti eva martyena bhāvyam aśvavatā api kim gavāśvasya parasparam apratibaddha tvāt eka bhāve na anya bhāvaḥ tathā śiṃśapā avṛkṣa ādau api syāt yasmāt kāraṇa vyāpaka nivṛttyā kārya vyāpaka nivṛttiḥ darśanīyāḥ vipakṣe 
[297,i_297,ii]	tasmāt vaidharmya dṛṣṭānte na iṣṭā uvaśyam iha āśrayaḥ tad abhāve ca tat na iti vacanāt api tad gatiḥ tasmāt vaidharmya dṛṣṭānte na iṣṭaḥ avaśyam iha āśrayaḥ vastu bhūtaḥ dharmī tasya kāraṇa vyāpakasya sādhyasya abhāve ca tad kārya vāyapyam sādhanam na iti vacanāt api tasya sādhya abhāve sādhana abhāvasya gatiḥ vastuni vastu nivṛttiḥ sandigdhā vastu sambandha avirodhāt avastuni tu vastu sattā virudhyate nivṛttiḥ tu yuktā atas sa dharmiṇam antareṇa api voṅmātra topi gamyate eva 
[297,iii_297,v]	yatas tad bhāva hetu bhāvau hi dṛṣṭānte tad avedinaḥ khyāpyete viduṣām vācyaḥ hetuḥ eva hi kevalaḥ tad bhāva hetu bhāvau dṛṣṭānte khyāpyete tasya sādhanasya bhāvaḥ tādātmyam sādhyasya hetu bhāvaḥ ca khyāpyate vaidharmya dṛṣṭānte sādhya nivṛttyā sādhana nivṛtti kathanena tayoḥ tādātmya tad utpatti bandham ajānataḥ yāhi anya nivṛttyā itara nivṛttiḥ sā vastu bhūtam āśrayam antareṇa api śakyate nirdeṣṭum ye tu pratibandham vidanti teṣām viduṣām hetuḥ eva kevalaḥ vācyaḥ na dṛṣṭāntaḥ tatra darśanīyasya pratibandhasya siddha tvāt yasmāt dṛṣṭānte pratibandhaḥ kathyate 
[297,vi_298,i]	tena eva jñāta sambandhe dvayoḥ anyatara uktitaḥ artha apatyā dvitīyepi smṛtiḥ samupajāyate tena eva kāraṇena jñāta sambandhe hetau sādharmya vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ anyatarasya uktitaḥ artha āpattyā sāmarthyena dvitīyepi smṛtiḥ samupajāyate iti na tasya nirdeśaḥ karttavyaḥ tathā hi yat kṛtakam tat anityam yathā ghaṭaḥ iti tādātmye nirjñāte nitya tva abhāve kṛtaka tva abhāvaḥ sāmarthyāt ākāśa ādau gamyate tathā vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntena tādātmye kathite sāmarthyāt anvayaḥ ghaṭa ādau gamyate evam sādhana bhāve sādhyasya avaśyam bhāvaḥ yadi sādhya abhāve hetu abhāvaḥ tathā sādhya abhāve hetu abhāvaḥ tadā bhavati 
[298,ii_298,iv]	yadi sādhana bhāve avaśyam sādhya bhāvaḥ evam kārya anupalambhayoḥ api yojyam hetu svabhāva abhāvotaḥ pratiṣedhe ca kasyacid hetuḥ yukta upalambhasya tasya ca anupalambhanam yatas kāraṇa vyāpaka nivṛttibhyām kārya vyāpya nivṛttiḥ atas hetoḥ svabhāvasya vyāpakasya abhāvaḥ kasyacid kāryasya vyāpyasya ca pratiṣedhe abhāve abhāva vyavahāre ca hetuḥ tathā tasya pratiṣedhyasya yukta upalambhasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalambhanam pratiṣedhe pratiṣedha vyavahāre hetuḥ tasya svayam eva abhāva rūpa tvāt 
[298,v_298,vi]	itīyan trividha uktā api anupalabdhiḥ anekadhā tad tad viruddha ādi agati gati bheda prayogataḥ iti nirdiṣṭa krameṇa iyam anupalabdhiḥ kāraṇa vyāpaka svabhāva anupalabdhi bhedena trividhā api anekadhā bahu prakārā tad tad viruddha ādi agati gati bheda prayogataḥ te ca kāraṇa vyāpaka svabhāvāḥ teṣām viruddha ādayaḥ ca tad tad viruddha ādayaḥ ādi śabdāt viruddha kārya ādayaḥ ca teṣām yathākramam agati gatayaḥ kāraṇa vyāpaka svabhāvānām anupalabdhayaḥ teṣām viruddha ādīnām upalabdhayaḥ ca tāsām anyonyam bhedaḥ nānātvam tasya prayogataḥ śabdasya abhidhā vyāpārāt yathā uktaṃprāk sā eṣā aneka prakārā api trividha anupalabdhiḥ saṃgṛhīta iti arthaḥ 
[298,vii_299,i]	uktam artha ślokābhyām saṃgṛhṇan āha kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt vā svabhāvāt vā niyāmakāt avinā abhauva niyamaḥ adarśanāt na na darśanāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt tat utpatteḥ vā niyāmakāt sādhanasya sādhya avyabhicāra kāraṇāt svabhāvāt tādātmyāt vā niyāmakāt avinā abhāva niyamaḥ sādhya avyabhicāri tva niyamaḥ sādhanasya vipakṣe hetoḥ adarśanāt na sa pakṣe darśanāt darśana adarśanayoḥ vyabhicāriṇī api hetau sambhavāt niyama hetu abhāvāt ca 
[299,ii_299,iii]	avaśyaṃbhāva niyamaḥ anyathā parasya kaḥ paraiḥ artha antara nimitte vā dharme vāsasi rāga vat anyathā tādātmya tad utpattyoḥ avyabhicāra nibandhanayoḥ asvīkāre parasya sādhyasya paraiḥ sādhanaiḥ kaḥ avaśyaṃbhāva niyamaḥ na kaścid utpādakāt anyorthaḥ artha antaram tad nimitte vā dharme asvabhāva bhūte kaḥ avaśyambhāva niyamaḥ vāsasi rāga vat yathā artha antara nimittasya rāgasya vastre na avaśyaṃbhāva niyamaḥ 
[299,iv_299,v]	artha antara nimittaḥ he dharmaḥ syāt anyaḥ eva saḥ paścāt bhāvāt na hetu tvam phalepi ekānta tā kutas vastra utpādakāt artha antara nimittaḥ rāga dravya kāraṇaḥ hi dharmaḥ rāgaḥ prāc utpannād vastrāt anyaḥ eva syāt bhinna kāla tvāt bhinna hetuka tvāt ca ittham api yadi eka tvaṃviśvam ekam bhavet tatas ca saha utpatti nāśau syātām sarvatra sarvam ca upayujyate ekatva abhimānaḥ tu sadṛśa apara apara utpatteḥ bhrāntyā tasya ca artha antara nimittasya dharmasya vastra utpādāt paścāt bhāvāt na hetu tvam vastram prati atas kāraṇa tayā api na asya anumānam rāga utpattau vastram sahakāri kāraṇam atas kārya tayā rāga anumānam ced phalepi kāraṇāt anumīyamāne ekānta tā kutas na hi avaśyam kāraṇāni kāryavanti bhavanti 
[300,i_300,iii]	yadi darśana adarśane na anvaya vyatirekabuddhi hetuḥ ddhūma ugnit na vyabhicarati iti na syāta pratipattiḥ iti āha kāryam dhūmaḥ hutabhujaḥ kārya dharma anuvuttitaḥ tasya abhāve tu sa bhavan hetumat tām vilaṃghayet kāryam dhūmaḥ hutabhujaḥ kārya dharmasya kāraṇa anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi tvasya trividha darśana adarśana niścitasya anuvṛttitaḥ sa dhūmaḥ tasya agneḥ abhāve tu bhavan hetumat tām vilaṃghayet atikrāmayet 
[300,iv_300,v]	nityam sattvam asat tvam vā ahetoḥ anya anapekṣaṇāt apekṣātaḥ ca bhāvānām kādācid kasya sambhavaḥ ahetu tve ca dhūmasya nityam sattvam ākāśasya iva syāt asattvam śaśa viṣāṇa ādeḥ iva ahetoḥ anya apekṣaṇa abhāvāt apekṣātaḥ ca bhāvānām kādācid kasya sambhavaḥ tatas yadi ahetuḥ bhāvaḥ tadā nityam syāt asat eva vā syāt hetu abhāvāt tasmāt dhūmasyakādācitka tva darśanāt hetumatvam agni anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna darśanāt tad kāryatvañca yaḥ ca yasya kāryam sa tam na vyabhicarati tad adhīna svarūpa tvāt 
[300,vi_300,viii]	atas ca agni svabhāvaḥ śakrasya mūrdhā yadi agniḥ eva saḥ atha anagni svabhāva ūsau dhūmaḥ tatra katham bhavet agni svabhāvaḥ śakrasya mūrddhā valmīkaḥ yadi agniḥ eva sa tadā na hi vahni svarūpa tām vihāya anyat vahne rūpam atha anyathā pratīyamāna tvāt anagni svabhāva ūsau tadā dhūmaḥ vahneḥ janya svabhāvaḥ tatra śakra mūrdhni katham bhavet na hi vahni janyonyasmāt bhavitum arhati tad adhīna tvāt tatas śakra mūrdhnaḥ dhūma utpattiḥ iti bhrāntiḥ eṣā vahneḥ eva tad deśa vartinaḥ anupalakṣitāt utpattiḥ 
[301,i_301,iii]	kiñca dhūma hetu svabhāvaḥ hi vahniḥ tad śakti bhedavān adhūma hetoḥ dhūmasya bhāve sa syāt ahetukaḥ dhūma hetu svabhāvaḥ tad śakti bhedavān dhūma janana śakti viśeṣa yuktaḥ vahniḥ pratītaḥ adhūma hetoḥ adahanāt dhūmasya bhāve sa dhūmaḥ ahetukaḥ syāt hetum pramāṇa niścitam antareṇa eva utpādāt ahetu tve ca nityam sattvam asat tvam vām syāt iti uktam 
[301,iv_301,vi]	syāt etat śālūka ādi sva bījāt vijātīyāt ca gomaya ādeḥ dṛśyate tat katham avahneḥ ddhūma utpāde ahetu tu a prasaṅgaḥ iti āha anvaya vyatireka ādyaḥ yasya dṛṣṭā unuvartakaḥ svabhāvaḥ tasya tad hetuḥ atas bhinnāt na sambhavaḥ anvaya vyatirekāt yaḥ svabhāvaḥ yasya anuvarttakaḥ apekṣakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ taṃsya svabhāvasya tat anuvarttyamānam hetuḥ atas bhinnāt vijātīyāt na saṃbhavaḥ kasyacid yat hi śālūka ādi sva bīja prabhavam yat ca vijātīya prabhavam tayoḥ sadṛśa tva pratītau api na tādṛśa tvam rasa vīrya vipāka bhedāt yadi tu hetu bhedepya bhedaḥ viśva ātmakam dravyam syāt iti ādi uktaṃprasajyeta 
[301,vii_302,i]	svabhāvepya vinābhāvaḥ bhāva mātra anurodhini tad abhāve svayambhauvasya abhāvaḥ syāt abhedataḥ svabhāvepi hetau a vinā bhāvaḥ kva sādhye bhāva mātra anurodhini sādhana svarūpa mātra anuvarttini vyāpake yathā kṛtaka tvasya anitya tve yatas tasya vyāpakasya abhāve bhāvasya vyāpyasya kṛtaka tva ādeḥ svayam abhāvaḥ syāt abhedate aikātmyāt vastutas 
[302,ii_302,iv]	yadi yaḥ eva kṛtakaḥ saḥ eva anityaḥ bheda abhāvāt tadā pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ hetuḥ syāt iti āha sarve bhāvāḥ svabhāvena sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ svabhāva para bhāvābhyām vyāvṛtti bhāginaḥ yatas sarve bhāvāḥ svabhāvena sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ ātma ātmīya rūpa vasthita tvāt svabhāva para bhāvābhyām sajātīyāt vijātīyāt ca vyāvṛtti bhāginaḥ yasmāt na kenacid miśrāḥ 
[302,v_303,i]	tasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ arthānām yatas ca tad nibandhanāḥ jāti bhedāḥ prakalpyante tad viśeṣa avagāhinaḥ tasmāt yatas yatas asvarūpāt arthāt vyāvṛttiḥ arthānām tad nibandhanāḥ tad tat vyāḥ vṛtti nimittāḥ jāti bhedāḥ tad viśeṣa avagāhinaḥ tad sva lakṣaṇa āśrayāḥ kalpyante śabdaiḥ svavācya tayā 
[303,ii_303,iv]	yatas śabdaḥ kāścid artha kriyāḥ kurvan atad kāriṇaḥ aśabdāt akṛtakāt nityādeḥ ca vyāvṛttaḥ iti tad tadvayava cheda pratipādana artham śabda kṛtaka anitya tva ādyāḥ jātayaḥ ananya śabda vācya tayā kalpyante tasmāt viśeṣaḥ yaḥ yena dharmeṇa saṃpratīyate na sa śakyaḥ tatonyena tena bhinnā vyavasthitiḥ tasmāt svabhāva abhedepi kṛtaka tva anitya tva ādīnām yena dharmeṇa nāmnā anityaḥ iti anena yaḥ viśeṣaḥ nityāt vyāvṛttiḥ saṃpratīyate na sa viśeṣaḥ śakyaḥ tatas anitya śabdāt anyena kṛtaka śabdena pratyetum tena kāraṇena sādhya sādhanayoḥ bhinnā vyavasthitiḥ yadi api śabdaḥ eva kṛtakaḥ anityaḥ ca tathā api aśabda vyāvṛtta tayā niścitaḥ dharmī kṛtaka tayā ca hetuḥ anitya tayā ca asiddhaḥ sādhyaḥ tatas dharmi sādhya sādhanānām bhedaḥ kalpitaḥ na tu tāni eva kalpitāni teṣām sattvāt tatas kalpita dharmiṇi kalpitāt sādhanāt kalpitasya sādhyasya siddhim ācakṣāṇaḥ pratyākhyātaḥ tasmāt na pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ hetuḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ bhinna vyavaccheda rūpa tvāt 
[303,v_303,vii]	kasmāt punar vyavacchedaḥ śabda liṅgābhyām pratipādyate iti iṣyate na tu vastu eva vidhi rūpeṇa iti āha ekasya artha svabhāvasya pratyakṣasya sataḥ svayam konyaḥ bhāgaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ syāt yaḥ pramāṇaiḥ parīkṣyate ekastha artha svabhāvasya svayam ātmanā pratyakṣasya sataḥ konyaḥ bhāgaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ syāt yaḥ pramāṇaiḥ parīkṣyate nirṇṇīyate yadi pramāṇa antaraiḥ śabda antaraiḥ ca vastu eva viṣayīkarttavyaṃtadā tat pratyakṣeṇa śabda antareṇa ca dṛṣṭam eva iti vyarthāni pramāṇāni syuḥ 
[304,i_304,iii]	tvad matepi pratyakṣeṇa dṛṣṭe dharmiṇi pramāṇa antara vaiphalyam syāt na iti āha no ced bhrānti nimittena saṃyojyeta guṇa antaram śuktau vā rajata ākāraḥ rūpa sādharmya darśanāt dṛṣṭe sarvathā vastuni no ced bhrānti nimittena sādṛśya ādinā saṃyojyeta āropyeta guṇa antaram dharmma antaram asat eva śuktau vā śuktau iva rūpa sādharmya darśanāt bhrānti nimittāt rajata ākāraḥ tadā sarvathā vastu niścayāt pramāṇa antara śabda antara vaiphalyam syāt 
[304,iv_304,vi]	etat eva āha tasmāt dṛṣṭasya bhāvasya dṛṣṭaḥ eva akhilaḥ guṇaḥ bhrānteḥ na niścayaḥ iti sādhanam saṃpravarttate tasmāt dṛṣṭasya bhāvasya dṛṣṭaḥ eva akhilaḥ guṇaḥ dharmaḥ tathā api bhrānteḥ viparīta ākāra āropikāyāḥ na niścīyate iti āropita vyavaccheda artham sādhanam śabda antarañca saṃpravarttate 
[304,vii_304,ix]	na kevalam pratyakṣāt vastu grahe sādhana antara śabda antara vaiphalyam kintu anumānāt api iti āha vastu grahenumānāt ca dharmasya ekasya niścaye sarva grahaḥ hi apohe tu na ayam doṣaḥ prasajyate vastu grahenumānāt ca dharmasya ekasya kṛtaka tva ādeḥ pratyaya bheda abheditva ādi kṛte niścaye sarvasya anitya tva ādeḥ grahaḥ syāt eka rūpa tvāt kṛtaka tva ādi sādhana antara vaiyarthyam apohe tu anya vyavacchede śabda liṅga viṣaye svīkriyamāṇe na ayam pramāṇa antara ādi vaiphalyaṣaḥ prasajyate na khalu pratyagra dṛṣṭam vastu antaram śabda liṅgābhyām viṣayīkriyate kintu anya vyavacchedaḥ ekasmin ca vyavacchede siddhepya siddham vyavaccheda antaram liṅga antarataḥ śabda antarataḥ ca sādhyate iti na kaścid doṣaḥ 
[305,i_305,ii]	tasmāt apoha viṣayam liṅgam iti prakīrtitam anyathā dharmiṇaḥ siddhau kim atas sādhakam param tasmāt ācāryeṇa apoha viṣayam liṅgam iti prakīrtitam liṅgam upalakṣaṇam śabdaḥ ca anyathā yadi vastu viṣayam liṅgam tadā dharmmiṇaḥ sarva ātmanā pratyakṣataḥ siddhau kim atas dharmiṇaḥ parama siddham asti yat prasādhakam liṅgampramāṇam syāt 
[305,iii_305,iv]	kvacid sāmānya viṣayam dṛṣṭe jñānam aliṅga jam katham anya apoha viṣayam tanmātra apoha gocaraḥ nanu kvacid nīlā dau asamāropitaḥ anyaḥ viparīta aṃśaḥ yasmin tasmin pratyakṣeṇa dṛṣṭe yat jñānam aliṅga jam vikalpakam sāmānya viṣayam bhavati tad āropa abhāvāt katham anya apoha viṣayam āha tanmātrasya ānīla mātrasya apohaḥ vijātīyāt vyāvṛttiḥ vyavacchedaḥ sa gocaraḥ yasya tat tathā nīla vikalpasya ānīla vyavacchedaḥ eva viṣayaḥ iti arthaḥ 
[305,v_306,i]	kasmāt evam iti āha niścaya āropa manasoḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāvataḥ samāropa viveke asya pravṛttiḥ iti gamyate niścaya āropamanasoḥ bāṣya bādhaka bhāvataḥ samāropasya viveke vyavacchede asya niścayasya pravṛttiḥ iti gamyate 
[306,ii_306,iv]	tasmāt yāvantoṃ aśasamāropāḥ niścayāḥ tad nirāsataḥ tāvantaḥ eva śabdāḥ bhinna vyavaccheda gocarāḥ yāvantaḥ aśasya dharmasya samāropāḥ tasya nirāsa nimittam viniścayāḥ śabdāḥ ca tāvantaḥ eva tena te niścayāḥ śabdāḥ ca bhinna vyavaccheda gocarāḥ 
[306,v_306,vi]	anyathā vastu viṣayīkurutaḥ ekena vā dhiyā ekatra na anyaḥ viṣaya uḥ ti iti syāt paryāyatā anyathā yadi śabda niścayau sarva ātmanā vastu viṣayīkurutaḥ tat ekena śabdena buddhyā vā vikalpikayā vyāpte sarva ātmanā viṣayīkṛte vastuni ekatra na anyaḥ apratipannaḥ viṣaya uḥ ti iti paryāyatā śabdānām syāt vikalpā nāñca eka viṣaya tā bhavet 
[306,vii_306,ix]	nanu dravyāt upādhayaḥ parasparañca bhinnāḥ tad nimittāḥ vikalpāḥ śabdāḥ ca teṣu tad ādhāre vā dravye varttante iti āha nānā upādhi viśiṣṭasya bhedinorthasya grāhikā upakāra aṅga śaktibhyaḥ abhinna ātma niścaya grahe yasya api naiyāyika ādeḥ mate nānā upādheḥ dravya tva ādi aneka dharma viśiṣṭha syātas eva upāghi bhedāt bhedinorthasya grāhikāḥ vidhi rūpeṇa dhīḥ tasya api matena nānā prakārāṇām upādhīnām upakārasya aṅgam yāḥ śaktayaḥ tābhyaḥ abhinna ātmanaḥ upādhimataḥ dravyasya niścaya jñānena grahe 
[307,i_307,iii]	sarva ātmanā kṛte grāhe kaḥ bhedaḥ syāt aniścitaḥ tayoḥ ātmani sambandhāt eka jñāne dvaya grahaḥ sarva ātmanā kṛte sati upakāryasya upādhi ka lāpasya madhye kaḥ bhedaḥ upādhi viśeṣaḥ syāt aniścitaḥ yathā dravyam ekam upādhim upakaroti tathā parān api tatas eka upādhi upakāraka tve vidhi rūpeṇa gṛhyamāṇe sarva upādhi upakāraka tvam gṛhyeta tathā ca sarva upādhi grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ na hi yat sa apekṣam yat rūpam tad agrahaṇe tat gṛhītum śakyam nanu dhūma apekṣam vahneḥ kāraṇa tvam na ca tad grahe dhūma grahaḥ na etat yuktam tathā hi 
[307,iv_307,v]	kim punar kāraṇa tvam iṣṭam vahneḥ yadi avidyamāna tvāt dhūmāt pūrva kāla bhāvitā dhūmāsāhityam varttamāna kāla sattā na tat dhūma apekṣam sva kāraṇāt tathā utpatteḥ dhūmam antareṇa eva ca bhāvāt na ca tad grahe dhūma grahaḥ viruddha tvāt na hi dhūma grahaṇe tasmāt prāk bhāvi tvasya tat asā ahityasya ca grahaṇam atha dhūmasya ayam hetuḥ iti niścaya viṣaya tvam kāraṇa tvam iṣṭantadā asti eva īdṛśa kāraṇa tvasya grahe dhūma pratītiḥ ubhaya prati iti ākāra tvāt asya niścayasya dvaya anvaya vyatireka grahaṇa sāpekṣa tvāt ca nanu ca gṛhīta tad utpatteḥ agni mātra darśanāt kāraṇa tva pratītiḥ na ca tadā dhūma pratītiḥ 
[307,vi^1]	na ca tatra pratyakṣāt kāraṇa tvasya pratītiḥ kintu agni rūpa mātrasya anyathā sarvasya tad darśinaḥ kāraṇa tva pratīti prasaṅgaḥ kintu vyāpti graha sāpekṣā ānumānikī tad pratītiḥ tathā hi gṛhīta tad utpatteḥ eva iyam bhavati na anyasya tad utpatti grahe ca yat evam rūpam tat etat kāraṇam iti gṛhītā vyāptiḥ anumāna pratītau ca dhūma kāraṇam vahniḥ iti vyavaccheda dvayam anyonya sāpekṣam pratīyate eva iti alam tad prasaṅgena na hi anutkhātita kāryaḥ kāraṇa tva niścayaḥ atyantam abhyāsāt ca vyāpti graha saṃskārasya prabuddha tvāt apekṣā
[307,vi^2]	na asti iti atatva vivekinām na anumāna tva prabodhaḥ na hi anumānam aham iti utpannam anumānam ucyate kintu trirūpa liṅga jam anumeya viṣayam kāraṇa tva jñānañca tādṛśam eva dravyantu yena eva rūpeṇa ekam upādhim upakaroti tena eva aparān api iti ekopodhi upakāraka tve gṛhyamāṇe na aneka upādhi upakāraka tvasya grahaṇāt sarva upādhi grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ paraspara sāpekṣa tvāt tatas ca tayoḥ upādhi kalāpa tad upakāraka tvayoḥ ātmani sambandhāt dravyasya sambandhāt ekasya upādhi upakāraka tvasya jñāne dvayasya grahaḥ syāt eka niyatā pratītiḥ na bhavet iti arthaḥ 
[308,i_308,iv]	atha dravyāt upādhi upakārikāḥ śaktayaḥ bhinnāḥ eva dravya grahaṇe tāsām agrahaṇāt na sarva upādhi grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ iti āha dharma upakāra śaktīnām bhede tāḥ tasya kim yadi na upakāraḥ tatas tāsām tathā syāt anavasthitiḥ dharmāṇām upādhīnāu pakārasya nimitta bhūtānām śaktīnām dravyāt bhede svīkriyamāṇe tāḥ śaktayaḥ tasya dravyasya kim kasmāt yadi na upakāraḥ tatas dravyāt tāsām śaktīnām upakāram antareṇa sambandhe ati prasaṅgāt atha tāsām śaktīnām dravyeṇa upakāraḥ kriyate svarūpeṇa tadā śakti upakāra tvasya grahaṇāt śaktīnām grahaḥ tad grahāt ca sarva upādhi graha prasaṅgaḥ tad avasthaḥ syāt etat śaktīḥ api bhinnābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ upakaroti tathā syāt anavasthitiḥ tathā hi yāḥ tāḥ śakti upakārikāḥ śakti apaḥ tāḥ dravyasya upakāra dvārāt yadi iṣṭāḥ tadā asvarūpeṇa upakāraka tve sarva upādhi graha prasaṅga bhayāt anyāḥ śaktaye eṣṭavyāḥ tathā ca anavasthā vyaktā 
[308,v_308,vii]	uktam artham saṃgṛhṇan āha eka upakārake grāhye adṛṣṭāḥ tasmin na santi te sarva upakārakam hi ekam tad grahe sakala grahaḥ ekasya upādheḥ upakārake dravye grāhye abhimate tatas eka upādhi upakāraka dravya svabhāvāt apare upādhi antarāṇām upakārakāḥ upakāra śakti bhedāḥ dṛṣṭe tasmin eka upādhi upakārake dravye adṛṣṭāḥ ye te na santi ekam eva hi rūpam sarva upādhi upakārakamatas tasya eka upādhimatas grahe sakala upādhi grahaḥ syāt 
[309,i_309,ii]	yadi bhrānti nivṛtti artham gṛhītepi anyat iṣyate tad vyavaccheda viṣayam siddhantadvat tatas aparam sarva ātmanā vikalpena gṛhītepi vastuni bhrāntyā tathā na niścayaḥ iti yadi bhrānti nivṛtti artham anyat pramāṇa antaram iṣyate tad bhrānti nivarttakam pramāṇa antaram vyavaccheda viṣayam siddham bhrama āropita tva apoha viṣaya tvāt tatas bhrānti nivarttakāt aparam yat pūrvam utpannam vastu viṣayam iṣṭam tadvat apoha viṣayam siddham 
[309,iii_309,vi]	kasmāt iti āha tad vipakṣa samāropa viṣaye yadi niścayaiḥ niścīyate na yat rūpam tat teṣām viṣayaḥ katham avidyamāna ani asamārope viṣaye vṛtteḥ vikalpaḥ hi vyavaccheda viṣayam niścinvan tad vipakṣa samāropa viṣaye na bhavati kintu tad vyavaccheda niścaya āropa manasā urbbādhya bādhaka bhāvataḥ iti uktam api ca niścayaiḥ eka ākāra pravṛttaiḥ yat rūpam na niścīyate tad teṣām viṣayaḥ katham ucyate niścitañcā pratipannam ca iti vipratiṣiddham yadi kṛtaka tva niścaye anitya tva ādi api niścitam katham tasya apratipattiḥ kṛtaka tvasya api vā mā abhūt 
[309,vii_309,ix]	evantarhi pratyakṣa gṛhīte vastuni niścaya aniścayau na syātām iti āha pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītepi viśeṣa īśa vivarjite yad viśeṣa avasāya isti pratyayaḥ sa pratīyate pratyakṣeṇa gṛhītepi viśeṣe sva lakṣaṇe sarvatas vyāvṛtte aśaiḥ bhāgaiḥ vivarjite yasya viśeṣasya vyavacchedasya avasāya isti pratyayaḥ sahakārī prakaraṇa abhyāsa pāṭava ādiḥ sa pratīyate na itaraḥ na khalu asmad mate pratyakṣam niścaya ātmakam na api anubhava mātra adhīnaḥ niścayaḥ yena sarvathā niścaya prasaṅgaḥ kintu yatra vyavacchede abhyāsāt ayaḥ sahakāriṇaḥ pratyakṣasya santi sa niścīyate na anyaḥ iti yuktaḥ vibhāgaḥ 
[310,i_310,ii]	tatra api ca anya vyāvṛttiḥ anya vyāvṛttaḥ iti api śabdāḥ ca niścayāḥ ca eva nimittam anurundhate tatra api ca anya apohepi śabda vikalpa viṣaye anya vyāvṛttiḥ anya vyāvṛttaḥ iti api ye śabdāḥ ca niścayāḥ ca eva bhinna viṣayāḥ iva pravartante na te vyāvṛtti vyāvṛttayoḥ vāstava bheda nibandhanāḥ kintarhi saṃketam eva bheda vyavahāra vyasthāpakam vakṣyamāṇa nimittam anurundhate anuvarttante yadi goranyā ago vyāvṛttiḥ tadā yathā gaura goḥ aśvādeḥ vyāvṛttaḥ tathā ago vyāvṛtteḥ api vyāvṛttaḥ tatas ca aśva ādi vat goragauḥ eva syāt yaḥ hi ago vyāvṛtteḥ vyāvṛttaḥ saḥ agauryatha āśvādiḥ gauḥ ca tathā iti syāt tathā ago vyāvṛttiḥ api na prāpnoti sarvasya eva ago tvāt goragoḥ anya tve hi tasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ syāt yadā tu gauḥ eva na asti tadā kasya kasmāt vyāvṛttiḥ tasmāt na vyāvṛtti vyāvṛttayoḥ vastutas bhedaḥ 
[310,iii_310,v]	tatas ca dvayoḥ eka abhidhānā ipi vibhaktiḥ vyatirekiṇī bhinnam artham iva anveti vācyate sa viśeṣataḥ dvayoḥ vyāvṛtti vyāvṛttayoḥ ekasya arthasya abhidhāna ipi vastutas vibhaktiḥ ṣaṣṭhī ādiḥ vyatirekaḥ vācya bhedaḥ tadvatī vyāvṛttasya vyāvṛttiḥ iti bhinnam iva artham anveti anugacchati vācaka tvena vācyasya leśa viśeṣataḥ alpa bhedāt sa aṅketikāt abhinne pi arthe 
[311,i_311,iii]	kimartham saṃketa bhedaḥ kaḥ ca vācya viśeṣaḥ iti āha bheda antara pratikṣepa apratikṣepau tayoḥ dvayoḥ padam saṅketa bhedasya jñātṛ vāñcha anurodhinaḥ bheda antarasya pratipādyamānāt vyavacchedāt anyasya vyavacchedasya pratikṣepaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyasya svabhāvaḥ apratikṣepaḥ tad sambhavaḥ tau tayoḥ dvayoḥ vyāvṛtti vyāvṛtta śabdayoḥ saṃketa bhedasya jñātṛ vāñchā anurodhinaḥ padam kāraṇam jñātā hi kadācid gauḥ a naśva tvam niṣkṛṣṭa dharma antara sambandha yogya tvam jijñāsate tadā go tvam asya iti ucyate na tu go tvam asya śuklam iti yadā tu vyāvṛttiḥ eva aniṣkṛṣṭa dharma antara sambandha yogyā jijñāsitā bhavati tadā vyāvṛtta śabda saṃketaḥ yathā gaurayam iti dharmma antara sāmānādhikaraṇyañca gauḥ śuklaḥ ityādi 
[311,iv_311,v]	bhedoyam a iva sarvatra dravya bhāva abhidhāyinoḥ śabdayoḥ na tayoḥ vācye viśeṣaḥ tena kaścana bhedoyam a iva saṃketa kṛtaḥ dharma antara pratikṣepa apratikṣepa pratipatti phalaḥ dravya bhāva abhidhāyinā ūrddharmi dharma vācinoḥ śabdayoḥ na vāstavaḥ tena tayoḥ vācye niścaya viṣaye na kaścid viśeṣaḥ bheda antara pratikṣepa apratikṣepābhyām ekasya eva pratyāyanāt 
[312,i_312,ii]	jijñāpayiṣuḥ artham tam tat hitena kṛtā api vā anyena vā yadi brūyāt bhedaḥ na asti tatas paraḥ tathā vyavaharttā jijñāpayiṣuḥ artham tam sa aṅketikam bhedam tat hitena kṛtā api vā pācaka tvam asya pācakoyampākaḥ pākyaḥ vā ityādi anyena vā svayaṃkṛtena samayena yadi brūyāt tathā api tatas bheda pratipādakāt tad hita ādeḥ bhedaḥ paraḥ vāstavaḥ na asti 
[312,iii_312,iv]	tena anya apoha viṣaye tad doṣa upavarṇṇanam pratyākhyātam pṛthaktve hi syāt doṣaḥ jāti tadvatoḥ tena vyāvṛtti vyāvṛttayoḥ abhedena anya apoha viṣaye jātimān śabda vācyaḥ iti pakṣaḥ tadvat pakṣa bhūḥ doṣaḥ anya apoha īpi syāt iti tad doṣa upavarṇṇanam pratyākhyātam tadvat pakṣaḥ hi jātim abhidhāya śabdaḥ tadvati varttate iti tad vacane svātantryam asya na syāt sāmānādhikaraṇyañca na bhavet gauḥ śuklaḥ iti jāteḥ aśukla tvāt na ca upacāra āśrayeṇa svātantryam sāmānya ādhikaraṇyañca askhalat gati yuktam ityādi jāti tadvatoḥ pṛthaktve hi syāt doṣaḥ eṣaḥ na tu vyāvṛtti vyāvṛttimatoḥ bhedaḥ iti na atra tad pakṣa ukta doṣaḥ 
[312,v_312,vii]	yadi vyāvṛtti tadvatoḥ na bhaveḥ tadā goḥ go tvam śukla tva sāsna ādi matva ādayaḥ ca iti ṣaṣṭhī vacana bheda ādi na prāpnoti iti āha yeṣām vastu vaśāḥ vācaḥ na vivakṣā para āśrayāḥ ṣaṣṭhī vacana bheda ādi codyam tān prati yuktimat yeṣām bāhyānām mate vastu vaśāḥ vastu āyattāḥ vācaḥ na vivakṣā paraḥ āśrayaḥ kāraṇam yāsām tāḥ tathā ṣaṣṭhī vacana bheda ādi codyam tān prati yuktimat 
[312,viii_313,i]	yat yathā vācaka tvena vaktṛbhiḥ viniyamyate anapekṣita bāhya artham tat tathā vācakam vacaḥ asmākam yat vacaḥ yathā dharma antarasya pratikṣepeṇa aprativācaka tvena vaktṛbhiḥ niyamyate viśeṣeṇa vyavasthāpyate anapekṣita vāhya artha saṃketa mātra anurodhi tvāt tad vacaḥ tathā vācakam iṣṭam iti na codya avakāśaḥ 
[313,ii_313,iii]	dārāḥ ṣaṇṇagarīti ādau bheda abheda vyavasthiteḥ khasya svabhāvaḥ kha tvam vā iti atra vā kim nibandhanam yasya tu vāstavaḥ eva śābdaḥ vyavahāraḥ tasya dārāḥ ṣaṇṇa garīti ādau ādi śabdāt gṛhāḥ viṃśatiḥ iti ādau ca yathākramam abhinne bhinne ca vastutas bheda abhedayoḥ bahuvacana eka vacana nimittayoḥ vyavasthiteḥ khasya svabhāvaḥ kha tvam vā iti atra dharmi dharma bhedasya kim vā nimittam na kiñcana na hi ekasyāḥ striyāḥ bahu tvam ṣaṇṇām nagarāṇām vai eka tvam ākāśasya svabhāvaḥ bhinnaḥ sāmānyam vā asti atha ca asti śabda vṛttiḥ tatas kalpitaḥ eva tad viṣayaḥ vaktavyaḥ 
[313,iv_313,vi]	yadi sarvatas vyāvṛtta svabhāvāḥ bhāvāḥ na teṣu sāmānyam asti katham go tvam ityādi sāmānya pratītiḥ iti āha eka artha pratibhāsinyāḥ bhāvān āśritya bhedinaḥ rūpam pareṣām vyāvṛttam sā dhīḥ saṃvṛtiḥ ucyate bhedinaḥ sarvatas vyāvṛttān bhāvān āśritya paramparā pātebhyaḥ utpadya yayā dhiyā eka artha pratibhāsinyā eka artha adhyavasāyasva ākārayā svarūpeṇa sva pratibhāsena pareṣām sva lakṣaṇānām rūpam sarvatas vyāvṛttam saṃvriyate pracchādyate sā buddhiḥ saṃvṛtiḥ ucyate 
[314,i_314,ii]	tayā saṃvṛta nānātvāḥ saṃvṛtyā bhedinaḥ svayam abhedinaḥ iva ābhānti bheda arūpeṇa kenacid tayā saṃvṛttyā svayam ātmanā bhedinaḥ sva svabhāva vyavasthitāḥ bhāvāḥ saṃvṛta nānātvāḥ sthagita bhedāḥ kenacid rūpeṇa vijātīya vyāvṛtti upakalpitena go tva ādinā abhedinaḥ iva ābhānti 
[314,iii_314,iv]	tasyāḥ abhiprāya vaśāt sāmānyam sat prakīrtitam yathā tayā upakalpitam tat asata paramārthataḥ tasyāḥ buddheḥ sāmānya rūpa tayā adhyavasita ākārāyāḥ abhiprāya vaśāt sāmānyam sat prakīrttitam vijātīya vyāvṛtteḥ vastuṣu abhāvāt tad upakalpitam go tva ādi sāmānya rūpeṇa buddhi ākāra madhyavasyanti vyavaharttāraḥ adhyavasāya anurodhena ca sāmānyam sat iti ucyate yathā vastu tvena tat sāmānyam tayā saṃvṛtti buddhyā kalpitam tathā asat paramārthataḥ 
[314,v_314,vii]	tat eva asattvam āha vyaktayaḥ na anuyanti anyat anuyāyi na bhāsate jñānāt avyatiriktam vā katham artha antaram vrajet vyaktayaḥ tāvat na parasparam anuyanti bhedāt tāsu anuyāyi ca kiñcid na bhāsate vyakti mātra vedanāt yat ca jñānāt avyatiriktam ākāra svarūpam tat katham artha antaram jñāna antaraṃvā vrajet sva lakṣaṇa rūpa tvāt asya 
[314,viii_314,ix]	tasmāt mithyā vikalpa uyam artheṣu eka ātma tā grahaḥ itaretara bhedaḥ sya bījam saṃjñā yad arthikā tasmāt artha rūpasya jñāna rūpasya ca sāmānyasya yogāt mithyā vikalpa uyam artha śūnya eṣa vikalpa uyam artheṣu eka ātma tāyāḥ sāmānya rūpa tāyāḥ grahaḥ asya ca eka ātma tayā pratibhāsinaḥ mithyā vikalpasya bījam hetuḥ itarasmāt atat kārya kāriṇaḥ bhedaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ yad arthikā saṃjñā śabdopi vijātīya vyāvṛttau saṃketyate tad viṣayaḥ ca 
[315,i_315,iii]	katham punar bhinnānām abhinnam kāryam iti āha eka pratyavamarśa artha jñāna ādi eka artha sādhane kecid bhedepi niyatāḥ svabhāvena indriya ādi vat eka pratyavamarśaḥ eka ākāra adhyavasāyaḥ artha jñānam rūpa ādi jñānam ca tad ādiḥ yasya jvara haraṇa ādeḥ tasya eka arthasya sādhane karaṇe svabhāvena prakṛtyā sva hetu dattayā bhedepi bheda aviśeṣepi kecid bāhuleya ādayaḥ niyatā na karkā ādayaḥ indriya ādi vat yathā cakṣu ūru upāloka manaskāra ādayaḥ eva bheda aviśeṣepi rūpa vijñānam janayanti na śrotra śabda ādayaḥ 
[315,iv_315,vi]	etat eva dṛṣṭa antareṇa dṛḍhayan āha jvara ādi śamane kāścid saha pratyekam eva vā dṛṣṭāḥ yathā vā oṣadhayaḥ nānā tvepi na ca aparāḥ jvara ādi śamane karttavi ekāścit gūḍūcī ādayaḥ saha parasparam pratyekam vā dṛṣṭā nānā tvepi na ca aparāḥ yathā gūḍūcī musta ādayaḥ bhinnāḥ tathā trapuṣādayopi tathā api kāścid jvaram śamayanti na sarvāḥ evam śābaleya ādayaḥ eka pratyavamarśam kurvanti na karkā ādayaḥ 
[315,vii_315,ix]	syāt etat tāsu oṣadhīṣu sāmānyam kiñcid asti tat jvara ādi śamanam karoti tat na eṣa dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti āha aviśeṣāt na sāmānyam aviśeṣa prasaṅgataḥ tāsām kṣetra ādi bhedepi dhrauvyāt ca anupakārataḥ aviśeṣāt sāmānyasya akriyā avasthātaḥ kriyā avasthāyām na sāmānyam kāñcid artha kriyām upakalpayati tāsām gūḍūcī ādi vyaktīnām kṣetra ādi bhedepi sāmānyasya kāryiṇaḥ aviśiṣṭa tvāt jvara śamana ādeḥ kāryasya aviśeṣa prasaṅgataḥ cira kṣipra praśamana ādya bhāva āsakteḥ dhrauvyāt ca anupakārataḥ sāmānyasya nitya tvāt anyebhyaḥ sahakāribhyaḥ upakāra abhāvāt sakṛt tad kāryāṇi syuḥ 
[316,i_316,iii]	apoha viṣaya tve śabda vikalpayoḥ sāmānyam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvam dharmi dharma bhāvan ca vyavasthāpayitum āha tad svabhāva vikalpā dhīḥ tad arthe vā api anarthikā vikalpikā atad kārya artha bheda niṣṭhā prajāyate tasya utpala ādeḥ śabda ādeḥ ca sva lakṣaṇasya svabhāva grahāt ūrdhvam yā vikalpikā dhīḥ prajāyate vastutas anarthikā api tad arthā iva sva lakṣaṇa viṣayevā adhyavasāya anurodhāt paramārtha tā atad kāryebhyaḥ arthebhyaḥ bhedaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ tatra niṣṭhā avasthānam yasyāḥ sā tathā vijātīya vyāvṛtti viṣayā iti arthaḥ 
[316,iv_317,i]	tasyām yat rūpam ābhāti bāhyam ekam iva anyatas vyāvṛttam iva nista tvam parīkṣā anaṅga bhāvataḥ arthāḥ jñāna niviṣṭāḥ te evam vyāvṛtta rūpakāḥ abhinnāḥ iva ca ābhānti vyāvṛttāḥ punar anyatas tasyām vikalpa buddhau yat rūpam yaḥ ākāraḥ dṛśya vikalpayoḥ eka tva adhyavasāya abhyāsa dāḍhryāda bāhyam api bāhyam iva asādhāraṇam api ekam iva sarva vyaktiṣu sadṛśa vṛtteḥ yathā yathā vyaktayaḥ dṛśyante tathā tathā eva adhyavasāyāt vyāvṛttam iva vijātīya vyāvṛtta vastu abhedena niścayāt na ca tad vyāvṛttam go rūpatva prasaṅgāt atas eva nista tvam niḥsvarūpam yathā bhūta rūpa tirodhānena anyathā adhyavasāyāt tathā ca aparīkṣāyāḥ vicārasya anaṅga bhāvāt anāśrayān nista tvam tat dvividham tu arthaḥ jñānam vā na ca etat tathā yatas kāraṇāt tena kalpitena sāmānya rūpeṇa te arthāḥ eka artha kriyā kāriṇaḥ atad kāryebhyaḥ vyāvṛtta svabhāvāḥ jñāna niviṣṭāḥ vikalpa buddhi ārūḍhāḥ abhinnāḥ ivā bhānti utpala tva ādinā śabda tva ādinā ca etena sāmānya vyavasthā uktā te eva eka jāti avasitā anyatas anīlāt nityāt ca nīlam ityādi vikalpa ākāreṇa ekena tad kāritā vyāvṛtta rūpa tā adhyavasāya viṣayeṇa viśeṣitāḥ vyāvṛttāḥ ābhānti nīlotpalam iti śabdasya anitya tvam iti
