[317,ii_317,iii]	te eva teṣām sāmānya samāna ādhāra gocaraiḥ jñāna abhidhānaiḥ vyavahāraḥ mithyā arthaḥ pratanyate teṣām ubhaya vyāvṛtti viśeṣitānām vikalpa ārūḍhānām arthānām sāmānyayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhūtayoḥ ddharma dharmi rūpayoḥ ca sāmānādhikaraṇyam samāna ādhāraḥ bhāva pradhāna tvāt nirdeśasya sa gocaraḥ yeṣāntaiḥ jñāna abhidhānaiḥ vikalpa śabdaiḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvasya dharmi dharma bhāvasya vyavahāraḥ mithyā arthaḥ pratanyate vistāryate 
[317,iv_317,vi]	sa ca sarvaḥ padārthānām anyonya abhāva saṃśrayaḥ tena anya apoha viṣayaḥ tad atad kārya kāriṇām vastu lābha āśrayaḥ sa ca jñāna abhidhāna lakṣaṇaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva ādi vyavahāraḥ sarvaḥ padārthānām tad atad kārya kāriṇā m anyotyasya itaretarasya abhāvaḥ vyavacchedaḥ saṃśrayaḥ viṣayaḥ yasya sa tathā tena vyavaccheda viṣaya tvena apoha viṣayaḥ vyavasthāpyate vastunaḥ lābhasya prāpteḥ ca āśrayaḥ nimittam sa vyavahāraḥ bhavati yatra yathā ukta anumittau yathā na anyatra bhrānti sāmya īpi dīpa tejaḥ maṇau yathā 
[317,vii]	yatra vyavahāre vastunaḥ sambandhaḥ paraṃparayā tad utpatteḥ astiyathā ukta anumitau yādṛśī sādhya pratibaddha kārya svabhāva anupalambha liṅga jānu mitiḥ uktā tatra yathā paraṃparayā vastu sambandhāt vastu prāptiḥ na anyatra bhrānti sāmya īpi dīpa tejaḥ maṇau yathā kuñcikā vivara deśa sthe dīpa tejasi bhrāntyā samāropite maṇā auparamparayā api vastu sambandha abhāvāt na prāptiḥ evam yadi api sarvasya vikalpasya sva pratibhāse anarthertha adhyavasāyena vṛtteḥ bhrānta tvam tathā api yaḥ vastu sambandhavān sa tad prāpakaḥ na itaraḥ iti yuktaḥ vibhāgaḥ 
[318,i_318,iii]	nanu yadi jñāna niviṣṭānām arthānām sāmarthya ādi vyavahāraḥ tadā bāhyeṣu sa na syāt iti āha tatra anekopi kāryā ekā na tad kārya para āśrayaiḥ jñāna abhidhānaiḥ eka tvāt vyavahāraḥ pratāryate tatra gavāśvādi vyaktiṣu madhye anekopi śāvaleya bāhuleya ādiḥ ekam abheda avasāya ādi kāryam yasya jñāna abhidhānaiḥ kīdṛśaiḥ tad vāha ādya kāryam kāryam na bhavati yeṣām karkā ādīnām tebhyaḥ anya tā tad vyavacchedaḥ saḥ āśrayaḥ viṣayaḥ yeṣām taiḥ eka tvena vyavahāram pratāryate prāpyate śāvaleya ādiḥ vijātīya vyāvṛtau vyāvṛtti āśrayaiḥ śabda jñānaiḥ ekatvena vyavahniyate iti arthaḥ 
[318,iv_318,v]	tatas ca ekopi aneka kṛt tad bhāva paridīpanāt atad kārya artha bhedena nānā dharmaḥ pratīyate tatas ca ekopi dīpa ādiḥ āloka andhakāra apanayana varti dāha ādi aneka kārya kṛt tad bhāvasya aneka kārya kāri tvasya paridīpana nimittam atad kārya arthebhya ekaika kārya samarthebhyaḥ bhedena vyavacchedena nānā dharmaḥ pratīyate śabda vikalpaiḥ yathā anāloka kāribhyaḥ bhedāt āloka kṛt anandhakāra hantṛbhyaḥ bhedāt andhakāra hantā dīpaḥ ucyate ityādi 
[318,vi_319,i]	yathāprati iti kathitaḥ śabda artha usā vasan api sāmānādhikaraṇyam ca vastuni asya na sambhavaḥ tat evam yathāprati iti saṃvyavahāra an atikrameṇa śabda arthaḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇaḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ ca ca śabdāt kathitaḥ asan api paramārthataḥ yatas vastuni asya śabda arthasya sāmānya ādeḥ pāramārthikasya asaṃbhavaḥ sarvatas vyāvṛttasya vastu mātrasya adhyakṣeṇa upalambhāt tad vyāvutti āśrayeṇa kalpyamānam sāmānyam tad sāmānādhikaraṇyam ca avastu eva 
[319,ii_319,iii]	dharmma dharmmi vyavasthānam bhedaḥ abhedaḥ ca yādṛśaḥ asamīkṣita tatva ūrthaḥ yathā loke pratīyate tathā dharma dharmmiṇoḥ vyavasthā niyamaḥ śabdaḥ dharmyā iva kṛtaka tvam dharmaḥ eva tayoḥ bhedaḥ śabdaḥ dharmī kṛtaka tvam dharmaḥ iti abhedaḥ ca kṛtakaḥ anityaḥ ca śabdaḥ ityādi yādṛśaḥ dharma antara pratikṣepa apratikṣepa abhyām uktaḥ asamīkṣita tatva ūrthaḥ alakṣita tatvaḥ yathā loke pratīyate 
[319,iv_319,v]	tam tathā eva samāśritya sādhya sādhana saṃsthitiḥ parama artha avatārāya vidvadbhiḥ avakalpyate tam dharmmi dharmma ādi vibhāgam tathā eva samāśritya sādhya sādhana saṃsthitiḥ vidvadbhiḥ avakalpyate parama arthe vastu svabhāva bhūte kṣaṇika tva ādau avatārāya lokasya vastu tva kṣaṇika tvayoḥ bhedaḥ paraḥ kalpitaḥ vastu tu kṣaṇikam eva tat ca sādhya sādhana kalpanayā śakyam pratyetum 
[319,vi_319,viii]	kasmāt punar vastuni sāmānya dharmi dharma ādi na asti iti āha saṃsṛjyante na bhidyante svatorthāḥ pāramārthikāḥ rūpam ekam anekañca teṣu buddheḥ upaplavaḥ pāramārthikāḥ arthāḥ svatas sva rūpeṇa na saṃsṛjyante yatas sāmānyam vastu syāt na api bhidyante kṛtaka tva śabda tva ādinā yatas dharmi dharma bhedaḥ bhavet yat tu teṣu rūpam ekam go tva ādi anuyāyi anekañca śabda kṛtaka tva ādi vyavahriyate asau buddheḥ anādi vāsanā upahatāyāḥ upalpavaḥ mithyā upadarśanam 
[320,i_320,ii]	bhedaḥ tata upi bauddhe arthe sāmānyam bhedaḥ iti api tasya eva ca anya vyāvṛttyā dharma bhedaḥ prakalpyate tatoyam viśeṣaḥ idam sāmānyam iti bhedaḥ idam sādhyam idam sādhanam iti api bhedaḥ bauddhe buddhi parikalpite arthe na vastuni kathantarhi sva lakṣaṇe kṛtaka tva ādi bhedaḥ iti āha tasya eva sva lakṣaṇasya anyasmāt akṛtaka ādeḥ vyāvṛtyā tad āśrayeṇa dharma bhedaḥ prakalpyate 
[320,iii_320,vi]	kasmāt kalpita bheda dvāreṇa sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ iṣṭaḥ na vastu bhedena iti āha sādhya sādhana saṃkalpe vastu darśana hānitaḥ bhedaḥ sāmānya saṃsṛṣṭaḥ grāhyaḥ na atra sva lakṣaṇam sādhya sādhana saṃkalpe idam sādhyam idam sādhanam iti vikalpe kriyamāṇe vastu darśanasya hānitaḥ kalpitaḥ eva bhedaḥ na khalu vikalpe vastu darśanam asti kalpita gocara tvāt tasya ālocana ajñānam vastu viṣayam na kiñcid tat vibhajati nanu ācārya ādigna asya bhedaḥ sāmānya saṃsṛṣṭaḥ grāhyaḥ iṣṭaḥ atra bhedaḥ sāmānya saṃsṛṣṭaḥ pratīyate iti asmin vacane na sva lakṣaṇam grāhya tayā nirdiṣṭam kintu adhyavaseya tayā 
[320,vii_320,ix]	kasmāt evam iti āha samāna bhinna ādi ākāraiḥ na tat grāhyam kathañcana bhedānām bahu bhedānām tatra ekasmin ayogataḥ samāna bhinna ādi ākāraiḥ sāmānya ākāra dharmi dharma bheda ākāra sāmānādhikaraṇyā ādi ākāraiḥ ca tat sva lakṣaṇam kathañcana grāhyam na bhavati kim kāraṇam iti āha bhedānāṃdharmāṇām kṛtaka tva ādīnām bahu bhedānām aneka prakārāṇām tatra sva lakṣaṇaḥ ekasmin ayogataḥ 
[321,i_321,ii]	tad rūpam sarvatas bhinnam tathā tad pratipādikā na śrutiḥ kalpanā vā asti sāmānyena eva vṛttitaḥ tasmāt tasya sva lakṣaṇasya rūpam sarvatas sajātīya vijātīyāt bhinnam tathā tena sarvatas bhinnena rūpeṇa tad pratipādikā śrutiḥ kalpanā vā na asti sāmānyena eva kalpitena rūpeṇa śabda vikalpayoḥ vṛttitaḥ 
[321,iii_321,v]	kim punar sva lakṣaṇam eva śabdaiḥ na ucyate iti āha śabdāḥ saṃketitam prāhuḥ vyavahārāya sa smṛtaḥ tadā sva lakṣaṇam na asti saṅketaḥ tena tatra na śabdāḥ saṃketitam artham āhuḥ na yam kañcid sa saṃketaḥ vyavahārāya smṛtaḥ saṃketitam artham śabdāt uccaritāt pratipadyeyam iti saṃketa grahaṇam tadā vyavahāra kāle ca sva lakṣaṇam saṃketa viṣayaḥ na asti tena tatra sva lakṣaṇe saṃketaḥ na yuktaḥ 
[321,vi_321,viii]	evantarhi sāmānye vyavahāra kāla anuyāyini saṃketaḥ syāt iti āha api pravartteta pumān vijñāya artha kriyā kṣamān tad sādhanāya iti artheṣu saṃyojyante abhidhā kriyāḥ apipravartteta pumān śabdāt vijñāya artha kriyā kṣamān tasyāḥ artha kriyāyāḥ sādhanāya iti etad artham artheṣu saṃyojyante saṃketyante śabdāḥ na vyasani tayā 
[321,ix_321,x]	atra anartha kriyā yogyaḥ na asti tat vā analam sa ca sākṣāt na yojyate kasmāt ānantyāt ced idam samam tatra evam sati anartha kriyāyām yogyaḥ artha kriyāyām śaktā jātiḥ iti na tatra saṅketaḥ yuktaḥ tadvān jātimān viśeṣaḥ alam śakta urtha kriyāyām iti tatra saṃketaḥ iti ced sa viśeṣaḥ ca sākṣāt saṅkete kasmāt na yojyate kim jāti vyavadhi svīkāreṇa anartha kriyā kāri tvāt asyāḥ sva lakṣaṇasya ca viparyayāt vyaktīnām ānantyāt na tatra śakyaḥ iti ced idam ānantyam samam jātimat vyaktiṣu api 
[322,i_322,ii]	tad kāriṇām a tad kāri bheda sāmye na kim kṛtaḥ tadvat doṣasya sāmyāt ced aḥ tu jātiḥ alam parā kiñca yām artha kriyām uddiśya śabda niyogaḥ tad kāriṇām arthānām atad kāribhyaḥ yaḥ bhedaḥ vyavacchedaḥ tat eva sāmyam sāmānyam anya apohaḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt tatra kim saṃketaḥ na kṛtaḥ sāmānya vat apohopi sādhāraṇaḥ anartha kriyā kārī sva lakṣaṇa sambandhāt tad upalabhya rūpaḥ caḥ tadvat doṣasya jātimati saṃketa viṣaye ānantyāt saṃketa akaraṇasya sāmyāt ced aḥ tu doṣaḥ samāna tvāt dvayoḥ asta jātiḥ parā alam anupayuktā jātim abhyupetya api vijātīya vyavacchedaḥ a vaśya āśrayaṇīyaḥ yadi gauḥ aśva ādibhyaḥ na vyavacchinnaḥ tadā aśvaḥ eva syāt yaḥ ca ekasya vyavacchedaḥ sa sarvasya saḥ eva saṅketa viṣayaḥ astu kim pramāṇa bādhita jāti svīkāreṇa atas eva tadvat doṣa upi na sambhavati abhyupagamya tu sāṃpratam āpāditam kiñca 
[322,iii_322,iv]	tad anya parihāreṇa pravartteta iti ca dhvaniḥ tena tebhyaḥ avyavacchede pravartteta kathañca saḥ tasmāt ekārtha kriyā kāriṇaḥ anyasya parihāreṇa śabdāt pravarttata iti dhvaniḥ ucyate tena dhvaninā tebhyaḥ atad kāribhyaḥ asya tad kāriṇaḥ avyavacchede vyavacchede akriyamāṇe katham sa śrotā pratiniyata padārtha arthī pravartteta viṣayān abhidhānāt 
[323,i_323,iii]	atha śabdaiḥ vyavacchedaḥ kriyate eva pravṛtti viṣayaḥ tu jāti ḥ ucyate iti āha vyavaccheda usti ced asya nanu etāvat prayojanam śabdānām iti kim tatra sāmānyena apareṇa vaḥ asya jātimataḥ vyavacchedaḥ asti ced nanu eta avat anya vyavacchedena pravarttanam śabdānām prayojanam iṣṭam iti sāmānyena apareṇa kim kāryam vaḥ tad antareṇa ca śabdāt anya vyavaccheda abhidhānā ipi pravṛtti saṃbhavāt 
[323,iv_323,vi]	yadi na asti jātiḥ tadā bhinna svabhāveṣu bhāveṣu saḥ eva ayam gauḥ ityādi pratyabhijñānam na syāt iti āha jñāna ādi artha kriyām tān tām dṛṣṭvā bhedena kurvataḥ artha antad anya viśleṣa viṣayaiḥ dhvanibhiḥ saha jñānam ādiḥ yasyāḥ bāha ādi artha kriyāyāḥ tām eka ākāra parāmarśa viṣayām bhedena nānā tvepi kurvata ūrthān dṛṣṭvā tad anyasmāt yaḥ viśleṣaḥ sa viṣayaḥ yeṣām taiḥ ddhvanibhiḥ saha 
[323,vii_323,ix]	saṃyojya pratyabhijñānam pūrva dṛṣṭā anya darśane parasya api na sā buddhiḥ sāmānyāt eva kevalāt saṃyojya saḥ eva ayam gauḥ iti ādi pratyabhijñānam pūrva dṛṣṭāt arthāt vilakṣaṇasya darśanepi kuryāt tad anya viśleṣasya sarvatra sāmyāt kiñca yadi nānātvāt pratyabhijñānam ayuktam tadā parasya api na sā pratyabhijñā buddhiḥ sāmānyāt eva kevala ādiṣṭā kintu sāmānya viśeṣābhyām 
[323,x_324,ii]	kasmāt iti āha nityam tanmātra vijñāne vyakti ajñāna prasaṅgataḥ nitya tayā tasya sāmānya mātrasya vijñāne vyakti ajñāna prasaṅgataḥ tadā kadācid sambaddhasya agṛhītasya tadvataḥ tadvat tā niścayaḥ na syāt vyavahāraḥ tatas katham yadā sāmānya jñānasya na viśeṣaḥ viṣayaḥ tadā kadācid agṛhītasya sambaddhasya sāmānyena tadvataḥ viśeṣasya tadvat tā niścayaḥ idam asya sāmānyam iti jñānam na syāt tatas tadvat tā vyavahāraḥ katham tvad mate 
[324,iii_324,iv]	eka vastu sahāyāḥ ced vyaktayaḥ jñāna kāraṇam tat ekam vastu kim tāsām nānātvam samapohati nānā tvāt ca eka vijñāna hetu tā tāsu na iṣyate ekam vastu sāmānyam tad sahāyāḥ ced vyaktayaḥ jñānasya pratyabhijñānasya kāraṇam iṣyante tat ekam sāmānyam vastu kintāsām vyaktīnām amiśra svabhāvānām nānātvam samapohati yena pratyabhijñāna hetu tve nānā tvāt ca ekasya pratyabhijñā jñānasya hetu tā tāsu tvayā na iṣyate tat ced tathā eva na syāt pratyabhijñānam 
[324,v_324,vi]	anekam api yadi ekam apekṣya abhinna buddhi kṛt tābhiḥ vinā api pratyekam kriyamāṇān dhiyam prati tena ekena api sāmānyāt tāsām na iti agrahe dhiyā anekam api vyakti rūpam yadi ekam sāmānyam apekṣya abhinna buddhi kṛt pratyabhijñāna kārīṣyate tābhiḥ vyaktibhiḥ pratyekaṃvinā eka ekayā preritena sāmānyena ekena kriyamāṇām dhiyam pratyabhijñām pratibhāsām vyaktīnāṃsāmarthyam na iti tayā dhiyā tāsām agrahaḥ kevalam sāmānya grahaṇe ca tadvat tā niścayaḥ na syāt iti duḥpariharam 
[324,vii_325,ii]	nanu yathā nīla ādīnām ekaika apāyepi cakṣuḥ vijñānam dṛṣṭam tad samudāyepi dṛśyate evam yadi api pratyekam vyaktīnām vyabhicāraḥ tathā api yadā satvam tadā viṣaya tvam iti āha nīla ādeḥ netra vijñāne pṛthak sāmarthya darśanāt nīla ādeḥ netra vijñāne kārye pṛthak pratyekam sāmarthya darśanāt 
[325,iii_325,vi]	śakti siddhiḥ samūhepi na evam vyakteḥ kathañcana śakti siddhiḥ samūhepi yuktā evam vyakteḥ nna pratyabhijñāna janane sāmarthyam kathañcana dṛṣṭam yena samudāyepi sāmarthya kalpanā syāt tāsām anyatama apekṣyam tat ced śaktam na kevalam tāsām vyaktīnām anyatama apekṣyam tat sāmānyam pratyabhijñāne śaktam na kevalam iti ced 
[325,vii_325,viii]	tat ekam upakuryuḥ tāḥ katham ekān dhiyañca na kāryaḥ ca tāsām prāpta ūsau jananam yat upakriyā tat sāmānyam ekam kathantā vyaktayaḥ upakuryuḥ na tu ekāndhiyam anupakriyamāṇasya samaveta tve ati prasaṅgāt vyaktibhiḥ sāmānyam upakarttavyam tathā dhīḥ api eka upakarttavyā yat ca sāmānya ādiḥ upakriyate vyaktibhiḥ kāryaḥ ca tāsām prāpta ūsau yadi asmāt upakriyā jananam eva na hi upakriyamāṇāt anyasmin upakāra ākhye vastuni kṛtepi tasya kiñcid tad sambandhāt ced sambandhaḥ bhinnaḥ eva iti kintasya jātam abhinne tu upakāre saḥ eva kṛtaḥ syāt tathā jananam eva upakāraḥ 
[325,ix_325,x]	abhinna pratibhāsā dhīḥ na bhinneṣu iti ced matam pratibhāsaḥ dhiyā bhinnaḥ samānāḥ iti tad grahāt eka sāmānya abhāve abhinna pratibhāsā eka ākārā dhīḥ na bhinneṣu iti ced matam nanu pratibhāsaḥ dhiyā bhinnaḥ na eka ākāraḥ samānāḥ imāḥ iti tāsām vyaktīnām grahāt na hi bhūta kaṇṭha guṇavat ekam sāmānyaṃsarvān upāyāyi vyakti vyatiriktam pratibhāti kintu gauḥ gauḥ iti sāmānyam avasīyate tat ca bheda adhiṣṭhānam eva 
[326,i_326,ii]	kathantāḥ bhinna dhī grāhyāḥ samāḥ ced eka kārya tā sādṛśyam nanu dhīḥ kāryam tāsām sā ca vibhidyate nanu samāḥ ced vyakta yodhyavasīyante katham tāḥ bhinna dhī grāhyāḥ na khalu sama tvam eka tvam kintu eka kārya tā sādṛśyam na hi saḥ eva ayam tat atra vā iti niścayaḥ api tu ayam api gauḥ iti adhyavasāyaḥ tathā ca eka artha kriyā kāri tvam eva sādṛśyam nanu dhīḥ kāryam tāsām vyaktīnām sā ca prativyakti bhidyate tat katham ekārtha kriyā kāri tvam sādṛśyam 
[326,iii_326,v]	atas āha eka pratyavamarśasya hetu tvāt dhīra bhedinī ekadhī hetu bhāvena vyaktīnām api abhinnatā yadi api prativyakti bhinnā tathā api eka pratyavamarśasya hetu tvāt dhīra bhedinī ekā abhidhīyate tathāvidhāyāḥ ca ekasyāḥ dhiyaḥ hetu bhāvena vyaktīnām abhinna tā ucyate 
[326,vi_326,vii]	sā ca atad kārya viśleṣaḥ tad anyasya anuvartinaḥ adṛṣṭeḥ pratiṣedhāt ca saṃketaḥ tad vidarthikaḥ sā ca abhinnatā atad kāryebhyaḥ padārthebhyaḥ viśleṣaḥ vyavacchedaḥ tad kāriṇām vastu bhūta jātiḥ eva kinneṣyate iti āha tatas vyavacchedāt anyasya anuvarttinaḥ sāmānyasya vastu sataḥ adṛṣṭeḥ svabhāva anupalabdhyā pratiṣedhāt ca tatas ca saṃketaḥ tad vidarthikaḥ tasya vyavacchedasya vidarthaḥ yasya asti sa tathā 
[326,viii_327,i]	atatkāri vivekena pravṛti artha tayā śrutiḥ akārya kṛti tad kāri tulya rūpa avabhāsinīm saṃketaḥ ca atatkāri vivekena pravṛtti aryatayā pravṛtti prayojana tvena kṛtaḥ tatas ca śrutiḥ api dhiyam janayanti arthena visaṃvādikā iti sambandhanīyam kīdṛśīm dhiyam su a ākāre akārya kṛti kārya kāraṇā samarthe tad kāri tulya rūpa avabhāsinīm eka artha kriyā kāri sarva vastu sādhāraṇa eka rūpa adhyavasāyinīm 
[327,ii_327,v]	dhiyam vastu pṛthak bhāva mātra bījām anarthikām janayanti api atatkāri parihāra aṅga bhāvātaḥ vastu naḥ tad kāriṇaḥ atad kāribhyaḥ ca pṛthak bhāvaḥ eva kevalaḥ sa bījam kāraṇam yasyāḥ tām anarthikām artha śūnyām paramārthataḥ katham avisamvādikā tarhi sā iti āha atatkāriṇām vijātīyānām parihārasya aṅga bhāvataḥ kāraṇa tvāt tad vyavacchedasya viṣaya tvāt tatra pravṛttiḥ 
[327,vi_327,vii]	vastu bheda āśrayāt ca arthe na visaṃvādikā matā tatonya apoha viṣayā tad kartṛ āśrita bhāvataḥ vastu bheda āśrayāt ca vastu viṣayasya paraṃparayā hetu tvāt tatra pravarttayantī śrutiḥ arthe na visaṃvādikā matā tatas nyāyoha viṣayā tad kartṛ āśrita bhāvataḥ tad kārya kartṛ vastu āśrita tvāt 
[327,viii_327,ix]	avṛkṣa vyatirekeṇa vṛkṣa artha grahaṇe dvayam anyonya āśrayam iti eka graha abhāve dvayāgrahaḥ nanu saṃketa kāle avṛkṣa vyatirekeṇa vṛkṣa arthasya grahaṇe dvayam anyonya āśrayam vṛkṣaḥ avṛkṣaḥ ca anyonya apekṣaḥ iti ekasya vṛkṣasya avṛkṣasya ca avyavasthita tvāt graha abhāve dvaya āgrahaḥ prāptaḥ niścite hi vṛkṣe tad abhāvaḥ śakyaḥ niścetum avṛkṣa tve ca niścite vṛkṣaḥ niśceyaḥ iti ekā niścayāt dvaya aniḥ cayaḥ 
[328,i_328,iv]	saṅketā sambhavaḥ tasmāt iti kecid pracakṣate teṣām avṛkṣā ssaṅkete vyavacchinnā na vā sa iṅketa asambhavaḥ tasmāt iti kecid jaiminīyāḥ pracakṣate teṣām eva vādinām jātau api saṅkete kriyamāṇe avṛkṣāḥ vyavacchinnā na vā yadi vyavacchinnāḥ katham jñātāḥ prāc vṛkṣa grahaṇāt ṛte anirākaraṇe teṣām saṅkete vyavahāriṇām yadi vyavacchinnāḥ iṣyante katham saṃketāt prāk jñātāḥ vṛkṣa grahaṇāt ṛte saṃketāt vṛkṣasya ajñāta tvāt avṛkṣāḥ katham jñātāḥ atha na vyavacchinnāḥ tadā anirākaraṇe teṣām saṃkete vyavahāriṇām vyavahāra kāle 
[328,v_328,vi]	na syāt tad parihāreṇa pravṛttiḥ vṛkṣa bheda vat avidhāya niṣidhya anyat pradarśya ekam puras sthitam vṛkṣoyam iti saṃketaḥ kriyate tat prapadyate byavahārepi tena ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced teṣām avṛkṣāṇām parihāreṇa na syāt pravṛttiḥ vṛkṣa bheda vat yathā vṛkṣa viśeṣāṇām vṛkṣa saṃkete avyavacchinna tvāt pravṛtti viṣaya tvam evam avṛkṣāṇām api syāt nanu ekam śākhādi mantam puras sthitam pradarśya tasmāt anyat avidhāya niṣidhya ca vṛkṣoyam iti ca saṃketaḥ kriyate vastu sāmānya ādibhiḥ tat saṃketa viṣayam sāmāni aṃtad sambandhi bāhya lakṣaṇam vyavahāre prapadyate tena ayam anantara ukta doṣaḥ na bhavati iti ced 
[328,vii_329,ii]	taruḥ ayam api ayam eva iti prasaṅgaḥ na nivarttate eka pratyavamarśa ākhye jñāne atra ca ayam api śākhā ādimān taruḥ ayam eva taruḥ iti pūrvakaḥ avṛkṣa avyavaccheda prasaṅgaḥ na nivarttate atra ca uktaḥ eva doṣaḥ iti dvayoḥ api ekāgrahāt dvaya asambhavāt saṅketāsambhavaḥ samānaḥ idānīm parihartum āha eka pratyavamarśa ākhye jñāne bheda aviśeṣepi kecid eva bhāvāḥ eka ākāra adhyavasāya hetavaḥ na itare ekatra hi sthitaḥ prapattā tad atad dhetūn arthān vibhajate svayam tad buddhi vartinaḥ bhāvān bhātaḥ hetu tayā dhiyaḥ ahetu rūpa vikala aneka rūpān iva svayam bhedena pratipadyeta iti uktiḥ bhede niyujyate 
[329,iii]	tatra ekasmin eka ākāra jñāna adhyavasāye sthitaḥ pratipattā puruṣaḥ tad atad dhetūn arthān vibhajate svayam yā an eka ākāra parāmarśa viṣaya buddhi ādi hetūn adhyavasyati yān ca anyathā tān yathākramam tad hetūnatad hetu uḥ cam bhedena vyavasthāpayati saṃketāt prāk eva tat buddhi varttinaḥ eka ākāra parāmarśa viṣayān bhavān śākhā ādimataḥ dhiyaḥ eka ākārāyāḥ hetu tayā bhātaḥ pratibhā samānā na hetoḥ eka ākāra buddhi akāraṇasya śākhā ādimatva rahitasya rūpeṇa vikalān parama artha bhinnān api eka rūpān iva svayam ātmanā saṃketayitā manyamānaḥ pratipādya upi tāna tad kāribhyaḥ śākhā ādimatvarahitebhyaḥ bhedena asaṃkareṇa pratipadyeta iti uktiḥ śabdaḥ bhede anya apohe niyujyate 
[329,iv_330,i]	tam tasyāḥ dhīḥ vikalpikā bhrāntyā ekam vastu iva īkṣate kvacid niveśanāya arthe vinivartya kutaścana buddheḥ prayujyate śabdaḥ tad arthasya avadhāraṇāt vyarthonyathā prayogaḥ syāt tam bhedam tasyāḥ ukteḥ uccāritāyāḥ vācya tayā pratiyatī dhīḥ vikalpikā prakṛti bhrāntyā ekam iva vastu īkṣate tasmāt kutaścanā kārya kāriṇaḥ arthāt vinivarttya kvacid eka artha kriyā kāriṇī arthe buddheḥ niveśanāya śabdaḥ prayujyate tad arthasya śabda arthasya avadhāraṇāt ghaṭena udakam ānaya ityādau pratipadam avadhāraṇam iṣṭam vyarthaḥ anyathā prayogaḥ syāt yadi yena kenacid ānayanam iṣṭam udakam ānayā iti ucyeta yadi śabdānām vyavacchedaḥ vācyaḥ tadā jñeya ādi padānām sarvasya jñeya tvena vyavacchedya abhāvāt 
[330,ii_330,v]	arthaḥ na syāt iti āha tad jñeya ādi padeṣu api vyavahāra upanīteṣu vyavacchedya usti kaścana yasmāt vyavacchedam antareṇa na śabda prayogaḥ tat tasmāt jñeya ādi padeṣu api kutaścid prakaraṇāt vyavahāra upanīteṣu viśeṣa viṣayeṣu kaścana tat itarosti kalpitaḥ vā niveśanam ca yaḥ yasmāt bhidyate tad nivartanāt tad bhede bhidyamānānām samāna ākāra bhāsini 
[330,vi_331,i]	yaḥ yasmāt atad kāriṇaḥ bhidyate tam atad kāriṇam vinivartya bhidyamānānām tad bhede atad kāri bhede samāna ākāra bhāsini niveśa nañca śabdānām sa ca ayam anya vyāvṛtyā gamyate tasya vastunaḥ sa ca ayam anya vyavacchedaḥ proktaḥ ācāryeṇa anya vyāvṛttyā anya vyāvṛtta tvena gamyate tasya vastunaḥ
[331,ii_331,v]	kaścid bhāgaḥ iti proktaḥ rūpam na asya api kiñcana kaścid bhāgaḥ dharmaḥ iti artha vācakena śabdaḥ artha antara nivṛtti viśiṣṭān eva bhāva ānāha ityādinā granthena na tu anyavyāvṛttiḥ nāma kācid anyā tad viśiṣṭañca vastu vācyam iti kintvā ākṣipta vyāvṛttikaḥ dharmaḥ eva kaścid kalpita bhedaḥ bahis adhyavasāya viṣayaḥ śabda vācyaḥ vastutas rūpam na asya api kiñcana asti tad gatau eva śabdebhyaḥ gamyatenya nivarttanam śabdebhyaḥ tasya dharmasya nīla ādeḥ gatau eva gamyate anyasya nivartta nam asaṃkara pratīti sāmarthyāt 
[331,vi_331,vii]	na tatra gamyate kaścid kenacid bhedavān paraḥ na ca api śabdaḥ dvayakṛt anyonya abhāvaḥ iti asau na tatra śābdyām buddhau kaścid nīla ādiḥ kenacid vyāvṛtti ādinā viśiṣṭaḥ paraḥ gamyate na ca api śabdaḥ dvayasya vyāvṛtti vacanasya tad viśiṣṭa vacanasya mukhyatas kṛt karttā asaṃkīrṇṇa dharma vadan sāmarthyāt vyāvṛttiñca āha tat eva āha anyonya abhāvaḥ iti yasmāt paraspara abhāva rūpaḥ sarvaḥ dharmaḥ tasmāt tad vacane vyāvṛttiḥ api sāmarthyāt uktā 
[331,viii_331,ix]	arūpaḥ rūpavat tvena darśanam buddhi viplavaḥ tena eva aparama artha ūsau anyathā na hi vastunaḥ yaḥ ca ayam bheda usāvarūpaḥ rūpava tvena yat tad darśana masya sa buddhi viplavaḥ tena eva buddhi viplavena aparama aparama arthaḥ asatya ūsau bhedaḥ anyathā paramārtha tve vyāvṛttiḥ vastunaḥ na vastu syāt 
[331,x_332,ii]	tat ca ayuktam vyāvṛtti vastu bhavati bhedosya asmādi ti īraṇāt na hi vastunaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ vastu bhavitum arhati asmāt eva vṛkṣāt asya vṛkṣasya bhedaḥ iti īraṇāt vikalpanāt bhedasya vastu tve bhidyamānā śiṃśapā eva vā bhedaḥ syāt vastu antaram vā na tāvat śiṃśapā dhava ādeḥ avṛkṣāt bheda abhāva prasaṅgāt na hi śiṃśapā svabhāva lakṣaṇaḥ bhedaḥ dhava ādeḥ asti yena tepya vṛkṣasya bhedāḥ syuḥ 
[332,iii]	sarvatra eva hi bhidyamāna abhāvāḥ tad ātmanaḥ iti ced na tarhi ekaḥ bhedaḥ tad kāriṇa ām a tad kāribhyaḥ yaḥ śabda vācyaḥ vyakti svabhāvasya tu bhedasya saṃketā viṣaya tvāt avācya tā eva atha vastu antaram bhedaḥ tadā tasmāt bheda ākhyānāt vastu antarāt bhidyamānasya śiṃśapā ādeḥ bhedaḥ vaktavyaḥ anyathā vastu antaratva ayogāt evañcāvṛkṣa vyāvṛttā idvarya āvṛtta tvāt śiṃśapādiḥ avṛkṣaḥ karkā ādi vat bhedasya ca vṛkṣāt bhinna tvam bheda antara upādhikam eva iti dravya antara varṇṇa bhedaḥ syāt na hi anyonyasya bhedaḥ sambandha abhāvena ati prasaṅgāt sati sambandhe kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ eva asau tatas sarvam kāryam sva kāraṇasya bhedaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ syāt tasmāt yaḥ ayam bhedaḥ śabda vyavahāra viṣayaḥ anuyāyī sa kalpitaḥ aparama arthaḥ sva svabhāva vyavasthitāḥ tu bhāvāḥ pāramārthikaḥ bhedaḥ 
[332,iv_332,vi]	nanu yadi vastu eka rūpam tadā ekena śabdena liṅgena vā vastuni pratipāditeśabda pramāṇa antara vṛttiḥ na syāt eka artha śleṣa vicchedaḥ ekaḥ vyāpriyate dhvaniḥ liṅgam vā tatra vicchinnam vācyam vastu na kiñcana ekasya nitya tva ādeḥ arthasya śleṣaḥ sambandhaḥ tasya vicchede vyāvṛttau ekaḥ dhvaniḥ liṅgam vā vyāpriyate tatra dhvanau liṅgaḥ vā vicchinnam sarvatas vyāvṛttam na kiñcana vācyam asti ekā vyāvṛttiḥ śabdena liṅgena vā pratipādyate na vastu iti arthaḥ 
[333,i_333,ii]	yasya abhidhānataḥ vastu sāmarthyāt akhile gatiḥ bhavet nānā phalaḥ śabdaḥ eka ādhāraḥ bhavati atas yasya vastunaḥ abhidhānataḥ vastu sāmarthyāt akhile kṛtakān iti ādi vastu rūpe gatiḥ bhavet yena śabda pramāṇa antara vaiyarthyam syāt atas śabdaḥ bhūyāt nānā phalaḥ aneka dharma pratīti phalaḥ eka ādhāraḥ eka dharmi niṣṭaḥ bhavati 
[333,iii_333,vii]	sādhya sādhana bhāva ādim ākhyāya sāmānādhikaraṇyan darśayitum āha vicchedam sūcayan ekam apratikṣipya varttate yadā anyat tena sa vyāptaḥ eka tvena na bhāsate vicchedam anīla ādi vyavacchedam ekaikam nīla ādi śabdaḥ sūcayan yadā apratikṣipya anyat anutpala vyavaccheda ādau varttate tad vācaka śabda prayoge sati tena vyāptaḥ śiṣṭaḥ eka tvena ca bhāsate sāmānādhikaraṇyam syāt tadā buddhi anurodhataḥ tadā sāmānādhikaraṇyam syāt nīlotpalam iti ubhaya vyāvṛtti viśiṣṭa eka vastu vyavasāyikāyāḥ buddheḥ anurodhataḥ 
[333,viii_333,x]	kiñca vastu dharmasya saṃsparśaḥ viccheda karaṇe dhvaneḥ syāt satyam sati tattve hi na eka vastu abhidhāyini dhvaneḥ viccheda karaṇe vyāvṛtti pratipādaka tve avasthite vastu dharmasya nīla ādeḥ saṃsparśaḥ pravṛtti viṣaya tvaṃsyāt sa vicchedaḥ hi yasmāt tatra vastuni satyam san tasmāt sūcane tadvatī pravṛttiḥ yuktā ekam sāmānyam vastu tad abhidhāyini tu dhvanau na vastu saṃsparśaḥ 
[333,xi_334,ii]	hetum āha buddha avabhāsamānasya dṛśyasya abhāva niścayāt tena anya apoha viṣayāḥ proktāḥ sāmānya gocarāḥ śabdāḥ ca buddhayaḥ ca eva vastuni eṣām asaṃbhavāt buddha avabhāsamānyasya dṛśyasya sammatasya tasya svabhāva anupalabdheḥ abhāva niścayāt na vastuni sattvam iti katham tad pratipādikāyāḥ śruteḥ vastuni vṛttiḥ tena vyavacchedasya vastuni sattvena sāmānya gocarāḥ śabdāḥ buddhayaḥ ca kalpikāḥ anya apoha viṣayāḥ ācāryeṇa proktāḥ apohaḥ śabda liṅgābhyām pratipādyate iti bruvatā na tu bhūta sāmānya viṣayā vastuni eṣām nīla tva ādīnām anupalabdhi bādhita tvena asambhavāt 
[334,iii_334,iv]	eka tvāt vastu rūpasya bhinna rūpā matiḥ kutas anvaya vyatirekau vā na ekasya eka artha gocarau yadi vācyam tat eka tvāt vastu rūpasya tasmin bhinna rūpā anitya kṛtaka tva ādyāḥ matiḥ kutas eka tvāt viṣayasya eka rūpavat buddhiḥ yuktā viśeṣaḥ ca sarvatas vyāvṛttaḥ iti tad ātma bhūtam sāmānyam api tathā syāt tatas ca ekasya sāmānyasya anvaya vyatireka anuvṛtti ananuvṛttī eka artha gocarau vyakti antara viṣayau na sambhavataḥ tathā hi sāmānyam vyakti antara anuyāyi na vyaktiḥ iti vadatā vyakti abhinna ātmanaḥ sāmānyasya anvaya vyatirekau viruddhau abhyugatau syātām tat ca ayuktam 
[334,v_335,ii]	abheda vyavahārāḥ ca bhede syuḥ anibandhanāḥ athavā vyakti ātmanaḥ vyakti rūpavat bhede ca sāmānyasya abheda vyavahārāḥ anibandhanāḥ syuḥ ekasya anuyāyinaḥ abhāvāt asmad mate tu sarvatra bhāvāt vyāvṛtteḥ na ete doṣāḥ prasaṅginaḥ sarvatra vyaktiṣu bhāvāt vyāvṛtteḥ sajātīyāt vijātīyāt ca ete doṣāḥ bhinna ābhāsa buddhi viṣa tva abhāva anvaya vyatireka ādi viruddha dharma adhyāsāḥ aprasaṅginā ubhavanti śabda vikalpānām bhinna bhinna vyāvṛtti viṣaya tvāt vijātīya vyāvṛtti āśrayeṇa anvaya buddhi viṣaya tvāt sajātīya vyāvṛtti āśrayeṇa vyatirekabuddhi viṣaya tvāt ca iti kasmāt punar anya vyāvṛttau śabda saṅketaḥ na sva lakṣaṇaḥ iti āha 
[335,iii_335,iv]	eka kāryeṣu bhāveṣu tad kārya paricodane gaurava aśakti vaiphalyāt bheda ākhyāyāḥ samā śrutiḥ kṛtā vṛddhaiḥ atad kārya vyāvṛtti vinibandhanā eka kāryeṣu ekatva adhyavasāya viṣaya kārya kāriṣu bhāveṣu tad kārya paricodana nimittam prativyakti bheda ākhyāyāḥ bhinnasya śabdasya yojanena saṃketa kriyāyāḥ vyakti ānantyāt gauravāt aśaktevaiphalyāt ca samā ekā śrutiḥ atad kāryebhyaḥ vā vyāvṛttiḥ tad nivandhanā tad āśrayā vṛddhaiḥ kṛtā saṃketitā 
[335,v_335,vi]	na bhāve sarva bhāvānām sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ yat rūpam śāvaleyasya bāhuleyasya na asti tat na bhāve sva lakṣaṇe kasmāt iti āha sarva bhāvānām sva svabhāva vyavasthiteḥ kāraṇataḥ yat rūpam śāvaleyasya bāhuleyasya na asti tat rūpam 
[335,vii_336,ii]	atad kārya parāvṛttiḥ dvayoḥ api ca vidyate atad kāryebhyaḥ parāvṛttiḥ ca dvayoḥ śāvaleya bāhuleyayoḥ api vidyate tatas tatra eva saṃketaḥ na sva lakṣaṇe sva lakṣaṇāni eva tarhi abhinnasya śabdasya vācyāni syuḥ iti āha artha abhedena ca vinā śabda abhedaḥ na yujyate arthasya abhedena ca vinā śabdasya abhedaḥ na yujyate ati prasaṅgāt 
[336,iii_336,vii]	evantar hi eka kārya tā eva bhinna śabda vācyā syāt iti āha tasmāt tad kāryatā apīṣṭā atad kāryāt eva bhinna tā yasmāt artha abhedāt śabdā bhedaḥ kāryañca prativyakti bhinnam iti tad kārya tā api eka kāryā ucyate sā api atad kāryāt bhinna tā eva sa ca apohaḥ atad kārya vyāvṛttau saṃketa kriyām draḍhayitum dṛṣṭāntam āha cakṣuḥ ādau anekatra rūpa vijñānake kvacid aviśeṣeṇa tad kārya codanā saṃbhave sati sakṛt sarva prati iti artham kaścid sāṅketikīm śrutim kuryāt ṛtepi tad rūpa sāmānyāt vyatirekiṇaḥ 
[336,viii]	yathā cakṣuḥ ādau anekatra kvacid rūpa vijñāna phale viṣaya bhūte aviśeṣeṇa sāmānyenatasya cakṣuḥ ādi kāryasya kāraṇa vācaka eka śabda dvāreṇa codanāyāḥ parebhyaḥ prakāśanāyāḥ cakṣuḥ āloka ādiṣu eka sāmānya bhāvepi saṃbhave sati kaścid sandheya vyavahāra ruciḥ sakṛt sarvasya cakṣuḥ ādeḥ prati iti artham sāṃketikīm śrutim kuryāt kutas rūpaṃvijñānam iti ṛtevinā api tad rūpāt rūpa vijñāna janakāt sāmānyāt cakṣuḥ ādi vyatirekiṇaḥ 
[336,ix_336,x]	eka vṛtteḥ aneka upi yadi eka śrutimān bhavet vṛttiḥ ādheya tā vyaktiḥ iti tasmin na yujyate nityasya anupakārya tvāt na ādhāraḥ atha ekasya sāmānyasya vṛtteḥ aneka upi viṣayaḥ yadi eka śrutimān bhavet tadā kaḥ doṣaḥ nanu kā iyam vṛttiḥ iṣṭā kim ādheya tā uta vyaktiḥ abhivyaktiḥ iti etat dvayam api tasmin sāmānye na yujyate katham iti āha nityasya anādheya atiśayasya aviśiṣṭa rūpasya kenacid anupakārya tvāt na ādhāraḥ kaścid na hi anupakārakaḥ ādhāraḥ ati prasaṅgāt 
[337,i_337,iii]	nanu vadarasya anupakārakam api kuṇḍam ādhāraḥ iti āha pravisarppataḥ śaktiḥ tad deśa jananam kuṇḍādeḥ bbadara ādiṣu na saṃbhavati sā api atra tad abhāvepi avasthiteḥ badara ādiṣu guru tayā pravisarppataḥ visarppaṇāt pratikṣaṇam asamāna deśa utpatteḥ kuṇḍa ādeḥ sahakāriṇaḥ tad deśa jananam badara upādāna deśa jananam śaktiḥ kāraṇa tvam ādhāra tā sā api śakti lakṣaṇa ādhāra tā atra sāmānye na saṃbhavati janya tva abhāvāt sāmānyasya sthitim kurvan viśeṣaḥ ādhāraḥ syāt iti āha tasya viśeṣasya abhāvepi avasthiteḥ 
[337,iv_337,v]	na sthitiḥ sā api ayuktā eva bheda abheda vivecane na sthitiḥ viśeṣāt sāmānyasya svarūpa atiriktāyāḥ sthiteḥ niṣkriya tvena abhāvāt svarūpa sthitiḥ tat ca pratyekam vyakti apāyepi asti iti na asau tatas astu vā sthitiḥ sā api ayuktā eva bheda abheda vivecane kriyamāṇe tathā hi āśraya hetukā sthitiḥ sāmānya abhinnā abhinnā vā syāt bhinnā ced tasyāḥ kāraṇa tvāt āśraya syāt na tu sāmānyasya sthitiḥ asambandhāt sāmānyasya api ced bhede sati kaḥ anayoḥ sambandhaḥ na kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ sthiteḥ āśrayāt utpatteḥ sāmānyāt utpattau vā na vyaktiḥ ādhāraḥ syāt sthiti hetu tva abhāvāt sāmānyañca nitya tvāt akāryam eva na ca anyaḥ sambandha usti nirākaraṇāt 
[337,vi_338,ii]	evam gamana pratibandha ādiṣu api vācyam tat evam na tāvat ādheya tā vṛttiḥ vyaktiḥ api na yuktā vijñānāt patti yogya tvāya ātmani anya anurodhi yat tat vyaṅgyam yogyatāyāḥ ca kāraṇam kārakam matam prāk eva asya ca yogya tve tad apekṣā na yujyate yat sva rūpeṇa sthitam eva sāmānyam sva viṣaya vijñāna utpatti yogya tvāya ātmani anya anurodhi para apekṣam tat vyaṅgyam ucyate yat ca yogyatāyāḥ svarūpa bhūtāyāḥ kārakam tat kāraṇam matam vyatirikta yogya tā karaṇe tu na syāt sāmānya sya upalabdhiḥ upalambhā yogya svabhāva tvāt yogyatā sambandha ipi anupalabhya svabhāvān apāyāt tad avasthaḥ anupalambhaḥ atha vyañjaka abhimataiḥ viśeṣaiḥ na yogya tā kriyate tadā sā prāk eva asti iti syāt tathā ca prāk eva asya yogya tve tad apekṣā vyañjaka apekṣā na yujyate 
[338,iii_338,vii]	sāmānyasya avikāryasya tad sāmānyavataḥ kutas tat tasmāt sāmānyavataḥ viśeṣasya sakāśāt sāmānyasya avikāryasya vyaktiḥ api kutas sambhavati atha na sāmānyasya saṃskārāt vyaktiḥ vyañjikā kintu indriyasya añjana vat iti āha añjana ādeḥ iva vyakteḥ saṃskāraḥ akṣasya na bhavet tad pratipatteḥ abhinna tvāt tad bhāva abhāva kālayoḥ añjana ādeḥ iva indriyasya na saṃskāraḥ vyakteḥ sakāśāt tad pratipatteḥ tasyāḥ vyakteḥ bhāva abhāva kālayoḥ abhinna tvāt na hi yathā indriyasya añjana saṃskāra bhāva abhāvayoḥ artha pratipatteḥ spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa lakṣaṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ tathā vyakti bhāva abhāva kālayoḥ sāmānya pratīteḥ sarvadā tulya ākāra tvāt tasyāḥ 
[338,viii_339,i]	kiñca vyañjakasya ca jātīnām jāti mattā yadi iṣyate prāptaḥ go tva ādinā tadvān pradīpa ādi prakāśakaḥ vyañjakasya viśeṣasya jātīnām jāti mattā yadi iṣyate tadā go tva ādinā sāmānyena pradīpa ādiḥ tasya prakāśakaḥ tadvān sāmānyavān prāptaḥ vyañjaka lakṣaṇa tvāt tadvatas tasmāt na vṛttiḥ abhivyaktiḥ api tat katham eka vṛtteḥ aneka upyeka śabdavān syāt 
[339,ii_339,vi]	kiñca vyakteḥ anyā athavān anyā yeṣām jātiḥ tu vidyate teṣām vyaktiṣu apūrvāsu katham sāmānya buddhayaḥ vyakteḥ anyā athavā ananyāḥ avyatiriktā yeṣām vaiśeṣika sāṃkhya ādīnām jātiḥ vidyate eva iti matam teṣām mate vyaktiṣu apūrvāsu katham sāmānya buddhayaḥ syuḥ tathā hi ekatra tad satoni atra darśana asambhavāt sataḥ ananyatve anvaya abhāvāt anya tvepi anapāśrayāt 
[339,vii_339,viii]	ananya tve ekatra vyaktau tadātmanaḥ sataḥ sāmānyasya anyatra vyakti antare anvaya abhāvāt darśana asambhavāt katham sāmānya buddhiḥ anya tvepi jāteḥ anapāśrayāt ukta yuktyā aśrayatva abhāvāt na vyaktiṣu apūrvāsu tad nibandhanā dhīḥ syāt api ca sāmānyam sva āśraya gatam vā kalpyate sarva gatam vā ākāśa ādi vat tatra prathama pakṣam dūṣayitum āha 
[339,ix]	na yāti na ca tatra āsīt asti paścāt na ca aṃśa vat jahāti pūrvam na ādhāram aho vyasana santatiḥ eka vyakti sthitam sāmānyam vyakti antaram utpadyamānam niṣkriya tvāt na yāti na tatra vyakti utpatti deśe prāk āsīt vyakti mātra niṣṭha tvāt asti ca paścāt utpatteḥ sāmānyam sāmānya śūnyāyāḥ vyakteḥ sthiti anupagamāt na ca aṃśa vat na hi sāmānyam sa avayavam yena kvacid ekena avayavena samavetam sat avayava antaraiḥ utpadyamāna vyaktibhiḥ sambadhyate na ca pūrva utpannam ādhāram jahāti utpitsu vyakti antareṇa sambandha artham anyatra sthitasya apara sambandhaḥ tad deśa āgamanam kila na yujyate iti aho vyasana santatiḥ sva āśraya gata sāmānya vādinām 
[340,i_340,iii]	kiñca anyatra varttamānasya tatonya sthāna janmani sva sthānāt acalatonyatra vṛttiḥ ayuktimat anyatra pūrva sthitāyām vyaktau varttamānasya sāmānyasya svasmāt sthānāt āśrayāt acalataḥ tatas pūrva vyakteḥ anyatra sthāne janma yasya tatra dravye vṛttiḥ iti ayuktimat na hi vyakti antara sthitasya vyakti antaram anāgacchataḥ tena saha anutpadyamānasya ca tad sambandhaḥ yuktaḥ 
[340,iv_340,vi]	tathā yatra asau varttate bhāvaḥ te na saṃbadhyata ipi na tad deśinañca vyāpnoti kim api etat mahā adbhutam yatra deśe asau śāvaleya ādiḥ bhāvaḥ varttate tena deśena sāmānyam na sambadhyate sva vyakti niṣṭha tvāt tasya tad deśinam sāmānya sambandha rahitaḥ deśaḥ yasya tam viśeṣañca vyāpnoti iti kim api mahā adbhutam etat durbuddhi vilapiteṣu 
[341,i_341,ii]	vyakti avaikatra vyaktā atha sarvagā jātiḥ iṣyate sarvatra dṛśyeta abhedāt sā api na vyakti apekṣiṇī atha sarvatragā jātiḥ iṣyate tadā ekatra eva deśe vyaktyā vyaktā sā jātiḥ sarvatra deśe dṛśyeta abhedāt eka vyakti vyaktam rūpam sarvatra vidyamānam abhinnam iti upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ vyaṅgya vyañjaka bhāvaḥ ca ayuktaḥ iti uktam bhavatu vā tathā api na sā jātiḥ vyakti apekṣiṇī 
[341,iii_341,ix]	tathā hi vyañjakasya apratītau na vyaṅgyam samyak pratīyate viparyayaḥ punar kasmāt iṣṭaḥ sāmānya tadvatoḥ vyañjakasya pradīpa ādera pratītau na vyaṅgyam ghaṭa ādiḥ saṃpratīyate iti tāvat sthitam sāmānya tadvatoḥ punar kasmāt viparyayaḥ iṣṭaḥ yadi vyaktiḥ sāmānyasya vyañjikā tadā vyakteḥ grahe sāmānyam na gṛhyeta iha tu sāmānyasya vyaṅgyasya prāk grahaṇam tatas tad viśiṣṭa tvena vyaktiḥ gahyate iti kim iṣyate vyañjaka agrahe vyaṅgya agrahṇāt kiñca pācaka ādiṣu abhinnena vinā api arthena vācakaḥ yadi sāmānyam eva abhinna abhidhāna hetuḥ na vyaktayaḥ tadā pācaka ādiṣu abhinnena arthena pācaka tva ādi sāmānyena vinā eva tvad matepi pācaka ādi śabdaḥ katham vācakaḥ pratyayaḥ ca anuyāyī karma pacana ādi tad hetuḥ iti ced āha 
[341,x_342,iii]	bhedāt na hetuḥ karma asya na jātiḥ karma saṃśrayāt bhedāt na hetuḥ karma ādi karma api prativyakti ekasyām api paurvāparyeṇa bhinnam eva tat katham vyakti vat eka abhidhāna hetuḥ karma sāmānyam hetuḥ ced āha asya karmaṇaḥ jātiḥ nābhinnā abhidhāna hetuḥ tasyāḥ karma saṃśrayāt karmaṇi samaveta tvāt tatra eva abhidhāna hetu tā syāt na dravye atha karma sāmānyam karmaṇi sambaddham tat ca dravyaḥ iti paramparayā tad sambaddham tad nimittaḥ śabdaḥ dravye varttate iti āha śruti antara nimitta tvāt karmaṇaḥ na nimitta tā asaṃbaṃdhāt na sāmānyam na ayuktam śabda kāraṇāt atiprasaṃgāt 
[342,iv]	śruti antarasya pācaka ādi śabdāt anyasya pākaḥ iti ādi śabdasya nimita tvāt karmaṇaḥ dravye pācaka śabda vṛttau na asti nimitta tā paraṃparayā api tathā anitya tvāt sthiti abhāvāt ca karmaṇaḥ tasmin nivṛtte pācaka ādi pratipattiḥ nna syāt apacati apitad vi apadeśaḥ dṛśyate nitya tvāt karma sāmānyam pācaka vyapadeśe hetuḥ ced āha asambandhāt dravyeṇa karma sāmānyasya na sambandhaḥ sākṣāt tatra asamavāyāt na api paraṃparayā karmaṇā tad samavetasya naṣṭa tvāt samavāyinā sāmānyena sambandha abhāvāt nasāmānyam śabdasya pācaka ādeḥ kāraṇa anna ayuktam kiṃtu ayuktam eva atiprasaṅgāt karma tvasya sambandha vyatirekeṇa vyapadeśa hetu tve sarvatra tathā tva prasaṅgaḥ 
[342,v_343,iv]	apacati api puruṣe atīta anāgatam karma tad vyapadeśa nimittam iti ced āha karma api na asat jñāna abhidhānayoḥ anaimittika tā āpatteḥ na karma āsat api jñāna abhidhānayoḥ hetuḥ anaimittika tāyāḥ āpatteḥ hetum vinā bhavataḥ ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt atīta anāga tañca karma avidyamāna tvāt asat eva pāka ādi nirvarttikā śaktiḥ pācaka ādi vyapadeśa hetuḥ iti ced āha na ca śaktiḥ ananvayāt 
[343,v_343,vi]	śaktiḥ hi dravyāt abhinnā bhinnā vā pratipannā abhinnā ced tadā dravya vat ananvayāt na ca anvayinaḥ anvayi śabda hetu tā atha bhinnā tadā anupakārakayoḥ sambandha anupapatteḥ dravyeṇa upakriyamāṇā śaktiḥ tad sambandhinī iti vaktavyam atra api dravyam śakti antareṇa svayam eva asamartha svabhāva tayā śaktim upakaroti iti vācyam ādye anavasthā dvitīye tu kāryam eva kin na karoti iti alam śakti svīkāreṇa sāmānyam pācaka tva ādi yadi prāk eva tat bhavet vyaktam sattā ādi vat no ced na paścāt aviśeṣataḥ kriyā upakāra apekṣasya vyañjaka tve avikāriṇaḥ atiśaye vā hi api asya kṣaṇika tvāt kriyā kutas 
[343,vii]	abhinna abhidhāne nimittam sāmānyam eva pācaka tva ādi yat i iṣyate tadā pāka ādi kriyā ataḥ prāk eva tat pācaka tva ādi sāmānyam dravya utpattau eva vyaktam bhavet no ced prāk avyaktam na paścāt api vyaktam syāt aviśeṣatas viśeṣa abhāvāt nitya eka rūpasya sāmānyasya kriyāyāḥ karmaṇaḥ pāka ādi na upakāraḥ tad apekṣasya dravyasya pācaka tva ādi sāmānya vyañjaka tve ca iṣyamāṇe avikāriṇaḥ sthirasya dravyasya apekṣā na asti atiśaye vā prāk avasthātaḥ svīkriyamāṇe kṣaṇika tvam syāt kṣaṇika tvāt utpatti anantara vināśi tvāt kriyā karma kutas sambhavati utpatti anantaram sthitau hi karma kuryāt sā ca kṣaṇikasya na asti iti na tena upakāra upi 
[344,i_344,ii]	tulye bhede yayā jātiḥ pratyāsattyā prasarpati kvacid na anyatra sā eva astu śabda jñāna nibandhanam vastu bhūta sāmānya vādinā upi vyaktīnām tulye bhede parasparam eka artha karaṇa ādikayā yayā pratyāsattyā kvacid vyaktau śāvaleya bāhuleyayoḥ jātiḥ prasarppati na anyatra karkā ādau sā eva pratyāsattiḥ abhinnasya śabda jñānasya nibandham astu kim pramāṇa antara bādhita jāti svīkāreṇa 
[344,iii_344,v]	sāṃkhyā prāhuḥ na nivṛttim vihāya asti yadi bhāva anvaya uparaḥ ekasya kāryam anyasya na syāt atyanta bhedataḥ yadi nivṛttim vijātīya vyavacchedam vihāya bhāvānām satva rajaḥ tamaḥ sāmya avasthā svabhāva prakṛti ātmanā advayaḥ eka rūpaḥ anvayaḥ aparaḥ na asti tat ekasya kāryam aṅkuraḥ anyasya kṣiti ādeḥ na syāt bīja kṣiti ādīnām atyanta bhedataḥ aṅkura kārakam yat rūpam bījasya tat ced kṣiti ādeḥ nna asti na syāt asau tad kārakaḥ astitve ca eka rūpa anvayaḥ 
[344,vi_344,viii]	siddhāntavādi āha yadi eka ātma tayā anekaḥ kāryasya ekasya kārakaḥ ātmā ekatra api vā asti iti vyarthāḥ syuḥ sahakāriṇaḥ yadi eka ātma tayā anekaḥ bīja salila ādiḥ kāryasya aṅkurasya ekasya kārakaḥ tadā aṅkura kārakaḥ ātmā anuyāyī ekatra api bīje anyatra vā asti iti vyarthāḥ sahakāriṇaḥ syuḥ ekatra vidyamānena eva tena ātmanā kārya utpatteḥ 
[345,i_345,ii]	na apaiti abhinnam tat rūpam viśeṣāḥ khalva pāyinaḥ eka apāye phala abhāvāt viśeṣebhyaḥ tad udbhavaḥ sahakāriṇām abhāvepi bīja satve abhinnam tat pradhānam karttṛ rūpam na apaiti nitya tvāt vyakti satvāt ca viśeṣāḥ khalu nūnam apāyinaḥ na pradhānam ekasya sahakāriṇaḥ viśeṣasya apāyepi phalasya abhāvāt viśeṣebhyaḥ tasya kāryasya udbhavaḥ niścīyate na pradhānāt viśeṣasya anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt sāmānyasya viparyayāt 
[345,iii_345,vi]	sa pāramārthikaḥ bhāvaḥ yaḥ eva artha kriyā kṣamaḥ sa ca na anveti yonvā iti na tasmāt kārya sambhavaḥ saḥ eva pāramārthikaḥ bhāvaḥ yortha kriyā kṣamaḥ sa ca viśeṣa urtha kriyā kṣamaḥ na anveti parasparam bhedāt yaḥ anveti pradhāna ākhyaḥ bhāvaḥ na tasmāt kāryasya sambhavaḥ yadi eka rūpān anugamaḥ tadā viśeṣeṣu api kecid janayanti na aparaḥ iti kutoyaṃvibhāgaḥ iti āha tena ātmanā api bhede hi hetuḥ kaścid na ca aparaḥ svabhāva uyam abhede tu syātām nāśa udbhavau sakṛt 
[345,vii]	yena eka rūpa anvaye sahakāri vaikalya prasaṅgaḥ tena kāraṇena ātmanā sva rūpeṇa bīja jala śilā anala ādīnām bhedepi kaścid kṣiti salila bīja ādiḥ aṅkurasya hetuḥ na ca aparaḥ śilā anala ādiḥ hi yasmāt svabhāva uyam aṅkura janana śaktaḥ tad itaraḥ ca pramāṇa dṛṣṭaḥ bīja ādīnām śilā ādīnān ca na atra paryanuyoga avatāraḥ kutas utpannaḥ iti ced sva sva hetoḥ sā upi kasmāt tad janakaḥ iti ced sva hetoḥ tatra api praśne tat eva uttaram anādiḥ ca hetu phala paraṃpara eka rūpa anugamāt viśeṣāṇām abhedetu svīkriyamāṇe sakṛt ekasya nāśa udbhavau syātām viśeṣa antarayoḥ yathāsaṃbhavam nāśaḥ janmani ca tad aparasya viśeṣasya tad abhinna rūpa tayā nāśa udbhavau syātā 
[346,i_346,ii]	bheda upi tena na evam ced yaḥ ekasmin vinaśyati tiṣṭhati ātmā na tasya atas na syāt sāmānya bheda dhīḥ atha parasparam viśeṣāṇām ekāntena nābhedaḥ kintarhi bhedaḥ viśeṣa rūpa tayā tena bhedena evam sakṛt nāśa udbhava prasaṅgaḥ na ced yadi ekasmin viśeṣe vinaśyati tiṣṭhati ātmā anuyāyī pradhāna ākhyaḥ tadā sa tasya viśeṣasya ātmā na bhavati na hi yasmin vinaśyati yaḥ na naṣṭaḥ sa tasya svabhāvaḥ viruddha dharma adhyāsa lakṣaṇa tvāt abhedasya atas parasparam sarvathā bhedāt na syāt sāmānya bheda dhīḥ anvayi sāmānyam ananvayī bhedaḥ ucyate yadā ca sāmānyam bhedāt bhinnam tadā anugāmi vyakti svarūpam na sāmānyam na ca tad ātmakaḥ bhedaḥ atas tat buddhiḥ api na bhavet 
[346,iii_346,iv]	nanu anya nivṛttau api samānam etat bhāve naśyati anya nivṛttiḥ naśyati na vā yadi naśyati na syāt vyakti antare tad buddhiḥ atha na naśyati tadā atyanta bhedāta sāmānya bheda buddhiḥ na syāt iti āha nivṛtteḥ niḥsvabhāva tvāt na sthāna āsthāna kalpanā upaplavaḥ ca sāmānya dhiyaḥ tena api adūṣaṇā 
[346,v_347,i]	nivṛtteḥ niḥsvabhāva tvāt na sthāna āsthānayoḥ sthiti nivṛttyoḥ kalpanā yuktā kalpitā hi anya nivṛttiḥ niḥsvabhāvā sā kim bhāvāt bhinnā abhinnā vā iti na yuktā kalpanā na hi śaśa viṣāṇam bhinnam abhinnam vā iti yuktam kalpiyitum upaplavaḥ mithyā tvañca sāmānya dhiyaḥ viṣaya abhāvāt tena na api adūṣaṇā yat tasya janakam rūpam tatonyaḥ janakaḥ katham bhinnāḥ viśeṣāḥ janakāḥ 
[347,ii]	nanu uktam yadi bhāvāḥ sarvathā bhinnāḥ tadā yat tasya bījasya janakam rūpam na tad anyasya kṣiti ādeḥ iti tatonyaḥ janakaḥ katham iti atra uttaram api uktam abhinna rūpa anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna abhāvāt bhinna aviśeṣāḥ eva janakāḥ tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt kāryasya sarve eva te tad kāryasya utpādaka tayā utpannāḥ tat utpādayanti 
[347,iii_347,vi]	api abheda upi teṣu ced tena te ajanakāḥ proktāḥ teṣu viśeṣeṣu anvayinā rūpeṇa abheda upyasti tena eva te janakāḥ iti ced tena anvayi rūpeṇa te viśeṣāḥ ajanakāḥ proktāḥ ekatra api viśeṣe tad bhāvāt saha kāri vaiphalya prasakteḥ tad anvaya vyatireka anartha vidhānāt viśeṣasya viparyayāt ca iti kiñca pratibhāsā upi bhedakaḥ ananya bhāj saḥ eva arthaḥ tasya vyāvṛttayā upare 
[347,vii_348,i]	pratibhāsā upi ananya bhāj bhedakaḥ viśeṣāṇām asaṃkīrṇṇa rūpa vyavasthāpanāt api śabdāt utpatti sthiti vināśa ādayaḥ ca samānāḥ tatas ca viśeṣaḥ eva arthaḥ pāramārthikaḥ ye tu apare sāmānya ādayaḥ dharmāḥ te tasya śeṣasya vijātīyāt vyāvṛttayaḥ kalpitāḥ anartha kriyā kāriṇaḥ tat kāryam kāraṇañca uktam tat sva lakṣaṇam iṣyate tad tyāga āpti phalāḥ sarvāḥ puruṣāṇām pravṛttayaḥ 
[348,ii_348,vii]	artha kriyā kāri tu yat rūpam tat kārya kāraṇañca uktam tat sva lakṣaṇam iṣyate tasya tyāga āptiḥ tad phalāḥ puruṣāṇām artha anartha prāpti parihāra eṣiṇām pravṛttayaḥ sarvāḥ kiñca yathā abheda aviśeṣepi na sarvam sarva sādhanam tathā abheda aviśeṣepi na sarvam sarva sādhanam sāṃkhyasya api mate yathā abhedasya pradhāna ātma tayā sarva bhāveṣu aviśeṣepi na sarva vyaktam sarvasya kāryasya sādhanam hetuḥ tathā bheda aviśeṣepi na sarva kṣiti bīja anala śilā ādikam sarvasya tāpa aṅkura ādeḥ sādhanam bhede hi kārakam kiñcid vastu dharma tayā bhavet viśeṣa antarāt bhede hi sati vastu dharma tayā vastu svabhāva tvāt kiñcid vastu kārakam bhavet na sarvam iti yuktam sva hetu bala āyātatvāt bhinna śaktikatvasya 
[348,viii_348,xi]	abhede tu virudhyete tasya ekasya kriyā akriye abhede tu sarva bhavānām virudhyete tasya ekasya aṅkura ādeḥ kriyā kriye bīja rūpa tayā pradhānam aṅkura kāraka m akāra kañca dahana rūpa tayā vipratiṣid dhañca etat katham ekasya yuktam bheda upyastya kriyātaḥ ced na kuryuḥ sahakāriṇaḥ vyaktīnām mithas vyakti rūpa tayā bheda upyasti vyakti antara sādhyasya kāryasya akriyātaḥ ced tadā bhedāt sahakāriṇaḥ kāryam na kuryuḥ ekasya yaḥ kārakaḥ svabhāvaḥ tasya anyatra abhāvāt 
[348,xii_349,iv]	paryāyeṇa atha karttṛ tvam sa kim tasya eva vastunaḥ atha kāraka eka svabhāva anugamāt sahakāriṇām paryāyeṇa karttṛ tvam sa paryāyaḥ tasya anvayinaḥ ekasya vastunaḥ kim kasmāt yuktaḥ na hi ekam vastu kārya kurvata paryāyeṇa na karoti iti yuktam vyapadeṣṭum tena eva kriyamāṇa tvāt sahakāriṇām bahūnām paryāyeṇa kriyā sambhāvyate teṣu ca ekasya kārakam rūpam anyatra na asti iti na te kuryuḥ sarveṣān ca sva hetu vala āyātaḥ eka kārya kārakaḥ svabhāvaḥ asmābhiḥ iva sāṃkhyaiḥ neṣyate kiñca atyanta bheda abhedau tu syātām tadvati vastuni tadvati sāmānya viśeṣavati vastuni svīkriyamāṇe atyantam ekāntena sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ bheda abhedaḥ syātām sāmānya svarūpa tvāt bhedasya sāmānyam eva bhavet na bhedaḥ bheda ātma tvāt sāmānyasya bhedaḥ eva bhavet sāmānyam 
[349,v_349,ix]	atha tayoḥ kathañcana bheda upyasti iti ced āha anyonyam vā tayoḥ bhedaḥ sadṛśā sadṛśa ātmanoḥ tayoḥ sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ sadṛśā sadṛśa ātmanoḥ sādhāraṇā sādhāraṇa svarūpayoḥ anyonyam bhedaḥ eva vā bhavet na kathañcid eka tvam etat eva sphuṭayitum pūrvapakṣayati tayoḥ api bhavet bhedaḥ yadi yena ātmanā tayoḥ bhedaḥ sāmānyam iti etat yadi bhedaḥ tad ātmanā bhedaḥ eva 
[350,i]	na sarva ātmanā abhedaḥ tayoḥ sāmānya viśeṣoḥ api kathañcid bhedaḥ bhavet yadi anyathā sāmānya viśeṣa bhāva anupapattiḥ atra āha yena ātmanā sva rūpeṇa sādhāraṇena ca asādhāraṇena ca tayoḥ sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ bhedaḥ sāmānyam viśeṣaḥ iti etat vyavasthāpyate tena ātmanā sādhāraṇa asādhāraṇena yadi bhedaḥ tadā bhedaḥ eva tayoḥ syāt bhinna lakṣaṇa tvāt 
[350,ii_350,iv]	tathā ca syāt niḥsāmānya viśeṣa tā bheda sāmāni ayoḥ yadvat ghaṭa ādīnām parasparam tathā ca niḥsāmānya viśeṣa tā samānya viśeṣa rūpa tā abhāvaḥ sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ abhitayoḥ syāt yadvat ghaṭa ādīnām viśeṣāṇām parasparam na sāmānya viśeṣa tā viśeṣaḥ sva lakṣaṇa rūpam anugāmi sāmānyam tat eva anugāmi viśeṣaḥ ucyate yadi tu tayoḥ bhedaḥ eva na sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvaḥ syāt yam a ātmānam puraskṛtya puruṣoyam pravartate tad sādhya phala vān chāvān bheda abhedau tad āśrayau cintyate sva ātmanā bhedaḥ 
[350,v]	api ca ayam vyavahārī puruṣaḥ yam arthasya ātmānam svabhāvam puraskṛtya pravṛtti viṣaya tvena āgraham kṛtvā tad sādhya phala vān chāvān artha sādhya phala samīhā yuktaḥ sana pravarttate tad āśrayau tad artha viṣayau bheda abhedau śāstra kāraiḥ cintyete na tu artha kriyā anupayukta sāmānya viṣayau teṣāñca artha kriyā kāriṇām puruṣa pravṛtti viṣayāṇām arthānām sva ātmanā sva rūpeṇa bhedaḥ 
[350,vi_351,i]	katham tarhi ekabuddhi śabda viṣaya tā iti āha vyāvṛttyā ca samāna tā asti eva vastu na anveti pravṛtti ādi prasaṅgataḥ vijātīyāt vyāvṛtyā ca sā samāna tā asti eva sva svabhāva niyatantu sva lakṣaṇam vastu na anveti sarvatra pravṛtti ādi prasaṅgataḥ agniḥ api salila svabhāvaḥ eva iti salila arthī tatra api pravartteta tasmāt sthitam etat na kiñcid kim api anveti iti 
[351,ii_351,iii]	etena eva yadāhrīkāḥ kim api ayuktam ākulam pralapanti pratikṣiptam tat api ekānta sambhavāt etena sāṃkhyam atanirākaraṇena eva āhrīkā digambarā yat syāt uṣṭraḥ dadhi vastu tvāt na vā syāt uṣṭraḥ viśeṣa rūpataye ti kim api ayukta tayā heya upādeya viṣaya apariniṣṭhānāt ākulam pralapanti tat api pratikṣiptam ekāntasya bhedasya sambhavāt 
[351,iv_351,vi]	ākula tvam eva ākhyātum āha sarvaṃsya ubhaya rūpa tve tad viśeṣa nirākṛteḥ coditaḥ dadhi khāde ti kim uṣṭram na abhidhāvati sarvasya vastunaḥ ubhayarupa tve sva para rūpa tve sati tad viśeṣasya dadhyeva dadhinā uṣṭra auṣṭraḥ eva uṣṭraḥ na dadhīti asya bhedasya nirākṛteḥ dadhi khāda iti coditaḥ niyojyaḥ kim uṣṭram prati na abhidhāvati 
[351,vii_351,viii]	atha arasti atiśayaḥ kaśicat yena bhedena varttate saḥ eva viśeṣaḥ anyatra na asti iti anubhayam param atha asti dadhnaḥ sakāśāt uṣṭrasya atiśayaḥ viśeṣaḥ kaścid yena viśeṣeṇa coditena bhedena pratiniyamena dadhi śabdāt dadhnī eva uṣṭra śabdāt uṣṭraḥ eva pravarttate evantarhi sa viśeṣaḥ eva anyatra asambhavī uṣṭraḥ viśeṣaḥ dadhi lakṣaṇaḥ anyatra vastuni na asti iti sarvam vastu anubhayam na sva para rūpam kintu param eva parasmāt 
[352,i_352,iii]	kiñca sarva ātma tve ca sarveṣām bhinnau syātām na dhīdhvanī bheda saṃhāra vādasya tad abhedāt asambhavaḥ sarveṣām bhāvānām sarva ātma tve ca bhinnau dhī dhvanī na syātām eka viṣaya tvāt tayoḥ dhī dhvanyoḥ abhedāt bheda saṃhāra vādasya asambhavaḥ syāt uṣṭrāt bhinnam dadhi iti bheda vyavahāraḥ dadhyeva uṣṭraḥ iti ca tad ātma tā upasaṃhāra vyavahāraḥ ca buddhi śabdayoḥ abhedāt na syāt na hi buddhi śabdayoḥ bheda vyavahāraḥ yuktaḥ tad nibandhana tvāt tasya tad abhāvepi bhāve ca atiprasaṅgāt bheda pratītyoḥ bhāvāt tādātmya upasaṃhāraḥ ca katham tad adhīna tvāt tasya 
[352,iv_352,v]	dravya abhāvāt abhāvasya śabdāḥ rūpa abhidhāyinaḥ na āśaṅkyāḥ eva siddhāḥ te atas vyavat cheda vācakāḥ uktam tāvat bhāva ādi śabdānām vyavaccheda viṣaya tvam yepi abhāva ādi śabdāḥ abhāvasya svarūpa abhāvāt tepi rūpa abhidhāyinaḥ vastu vācakāḥ na aśaṅakyāḥ eva sambhavat vastu vācyam syāt na vā iti cintyeta api yatra tu vastu eva na asti tatra kā cintā atas te abhāva ādi śabdāḥ vyavacchedasya bhāva vyāvṛtteḥ vācakāḥ siddhāḥ tasmāt sthitam etat svabhāva hetoḥ vastutaḥ sādhya ātmaka tvepi na pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ hetuḥ sādhya sādhana dharmi dhvani vikalpānām bhinna vyavaccheda viṣaya tvāt na ca sādhya ādīnām kalpita tvam bhedasya kalpanāt śabda tvena niścitaḥ dharmī sattvena ca hetuḥ kṣaṇika tvena niścitaḥ sādhyaḥ iti akalpitāḥ eva dharmya ādayaḥ iti uktam 
[352,vi_353,i]	sa ca ayam svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ upādhi bheda apekṣaḥ vā svabhāvaḥ kevalaḥ athavā ucyate sādhya sidhi artham nāśe kāryatva sattva vat kvacid upādhi bhedaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣaḥ bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ vā tad apekṣaḥ kevalaḥ viśeṣaṇa rahitaḥ śuddha ūthavā sādhya sidhi artham ucyate nāśe kāryatva sattva vat nāśe sādhye kārya tvam bhinna viśeṣaṇa apekṣaḥ svabhāvaḥ tad janmani apekṣita para vyāpārasya kāryatvāt evam pratyaya bheda bhedi tva ādayaḥ draṣṭavyāḥ utpattimatvam punar abhinna viśeṣaṇam utpattyā svabhāva bhūtayā kalpita bhedayā viśeṣaṇāt sattvantu kevalam nāśaḥ eva sādhye svabhāvaḥ viśeṣaṇa anupādānāt 
[353,ii_353,iii]	sattā svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ ced sā sattā sādhyate katham bhedena ananvayāt soyam vyāhataḥ hetu sādhyayoḥ nanu sattā svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ ced abhimataḥ sāmānya rūpaḥ viśeṣasya ananvayāt tadā sā sattā pradhāna ākhyā sarva vyakti vyāpinī katham sādhyate acetana tva ādi hetoḥ atha bhedānām parasparam atyantam bhedena ananvayāt na sādhyate tadā soyam bhedānām ananvayaḥ hi hetu sādhyayoḥ vyāhitaḥ 
[353,iv_353,vii]	artha ananvayinaḥ sādhya tā na yuktā tathā sādhana tā api tat katham sattvam sādhanam tasmāt sattā sāmānyam sādhyañca sādhanañcān anvayāt syāt atra āha bhāva upādāna mātre tu sādhye sāmānya dharmiṇi na kaścid arthaḥ siddhaḥ syāt aniṣiddhañca tādṛśam bhāvaḥ sattā sā upādānam viśeṣaṇam yasya sa bhāva upādānaḥ saḥ eva kevalaḥ tanmātram tasmin sādhye sāmānya dharmiṇi sāmānya dharmavati na kaścid arthaḥ pradhāna siddhi lakṣaṇaḥ sāṃkhyasya siddhaḥ syāt satva mātra viśeṣaṇasya dharmiṇaḥ sādhanāt aniṣiddhañca tādṛśam sādhyam bhedānām satvasya iṣṭa tvāt 
[354,i_354,ii]	upātta bhede sādhyesmin bhavet hetuḥ ananvayaḥ sattāyām tena sādhyāyām viśeṣaḥ sādhitaḥ bhavet atha eka sukha ādi ātmakam iti apradhāna viśeṣaṇa viśeṣitam sattvam sādhyam tadā upātta bhede sādhye asmin sattve bhavet hetuḥ ananvayaḥ anvaya rahitaḥ pradhānasya kvacid anvayā siddheḥ sāmānyam eva punar kinna sādhyate sāmānye sādhye siddha sādhana doṣāt sattāyām sādhyāya āmiṣṭāyām tena vādinā viśeṣaḥ eva abhimataḥ sādhitaḥ bhavet 
[354,iii_354,vi]	atra ca ananvaya doṣaḥ uktaḥ asmākantu aparāmṛṣṭa tad bhede vastu mātre tu sādhane tanmātra vyāpinaḥ sādhyasya anvayaḥ na vihanyate aparā muṣṭaḥ anadhyavasitaḥ tasya vastunaḥ bhedaḥ yasmin tasmin vastu mātre tu sādhane tanmātra vyāpinaḥ sādhyasya anitya tvasya anvayaḥ na vihanyate atas sādhana tvam sattvasya yuktam 
[354,vii_354,ix]	nanu dhūmāt agni sādhanepi samānam etat tathā hi yadi dhūmāt agni sattā mātram sādhyate tadā siddha sādhya tā atha parvate asti iti sādhyate tadā anvayā siddhiḥ na etat asti na hi pakṣā yoga vyavacchedaḥ tam agnim viśeṣīkaroti anagni vyāvṛttasya sādhanāt sattā sādhane tu tat sattva viśeṣaḥ eva pradhāna ākhyaḥ sādhyaḥ kiñca na asiddhe bhāva dharma usti vyabhicāryu bhaya āśrayaḥ dharmaḥ viruddhaḥ abhāvasya sā sattā sādhyate katham 
[355,i]	sattāyām sādhanam acetana tvādi iṣṭam sadbhāva dharmaḥ abhāva dharmaḥ ubhaya dharmaḥ vā bhavet tatra sādhanāt prāc asiddhe bhāve bhāva dharmaḥ na asti iti asiddhā asau ubhaya āśrayaḥ bhāva abhāva dharmaḥ ca vyabhicārya naukāntikaḥ na hi ubhaya dharmaḥ ekāntena eka sattām gamayati amūrta tvam iva vastu tām abhāvasya tu dharmaḥ viruddhaḥ asattva sādhanāt tatas trividha doṣa duṣṭa tvāt sādhanasyasā sattā katham sādhyate 
[355,ii_355,iv]	sādhana pakṣetu sattā dharmiṇi siddha tvāt na asiddhā anitya tā vyāpti prāpteḥ virodha vyabhicārau ca apāḥ tau tasmāt siddhaḥ svabhāvaḥ gamakaḥ atas gamyaḥ tasya vyāpakaḥ siddhaḥ svabhāva niyataḥ sva nivṛttau nivartakaḥ vyāpya svabhāvaḥ sādhya ātma tayā siddhaḥ niścitaḥ gamakaḥ tasya vyāpyasya vyāpakaḥ svabhāvaḥ siddhaḥ gamyaḥ vyāpakasya tatra bhāvaḥ eva vyāpyasya ca tatra eva bhāvaḥ iti ubhaya dharma rūpāyāḥ vyāpteḥ siddha tvāt 
[355,v_355,viii]	atas ca ayaṃvyāpakaḥ sva nivṛttau tasya vyāpyasya nivarttakaḥ anena sādharmya vaidharmya prayogau uddiṣṭau udāharaṇam āha anitya tve yathā kāryam akāryam vā avināśini ahetu tvāt vināśasya svabhāvāt anubandhitā anitya tve sādhye kārya hetuḥ yathā yat kṛtakam tat anityam tathā ghaṭaḥ kṛtakaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti sādharmya prayogaḥ akāryam akārya svabhāvaḥ vā avināśini nāśābhāvaḥ iti anitya tva nivṛttau kṛtaka tva nivṛttiḥ yathā ākāśe kṛtakaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti vaidharmya prayogaḥ katham punar gamyate sattva mātra anubandhinī naśvaratā iti āha ahetu tvāt ahetu kṛta tvāt vināśasya svabhāvāt vastu sattā mātreṇa anubandhitā 
[356,i_356,iii]	kasmāt evam iti āha sa apekṣāṇām hi bhāvānām na avaśyam bhāvita īkṣyate bāhulyepī iti ced tasya hetoḥ kvacid asambhavaḥ sa apekṣāṇām bhāvānām hi yasmāt avaśyaṃbhāvitāḥ na īkṣyate rāgasya iva vāsasi tatas ca kaścid ghaṭaḥ na vinaśyet api vināśakānām hetūnām bāhulyāt avaśyam iti ced bāhulyepi tasya nāśakasya hetoḥ kvacid ghaṭa ādau asambhavaḥ syāt tad vyāghātakānām api bāhulyāt 
[356,iv_356,vii]	etena vyabhicāri tvam uktam kārya avyavasthiteḥ sarveṣām nāśa hetūnām hetum at nāśa vādinām etena nāśa hetūnām pratirodha sambhavena hetum at nāśa vādinām matena nāśa hetūnām mudgara ādīnām sarveṣām nāśe kārye anumāpayitavye vyabhicāri tvam uktam boddhavyam kārya avyavasthiteḥ vināśa hetoḥ vināśasya utpatti niyama abhāvāt katham punar vināśasya ahetu tā iti āha asāmarthyāt ca tad hetoḥ bhavati eva svabhāvataḥ yatra nāma bhavati asmāt anyatra api svabhāvataḥ 
[356,viii]	asāmarthyāt ca tad hetoḥ vinaśvarasya vā bhāvasya vināśaḥ kriyate nāśa hetunā tatra vinaśvarasya svayam eva vināśāt alam nāśa hetunā avinaśvarasya nāśam karttum na kaścid samarthaḥ ca śabdāt kriyā pratiṣedhaḥ syāt tathā hi abhāvaḥ yadi paryudāsaḥ bhāva antaram kapāla ādikam tadā tasya mudgara ādi hetuteṣyate eva tat utpādepi ghaṭasya na kiñcid iti prāgvat upalabdhi ādi prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt abhāvam karoti bhāvam na karoti iti syāt tathā ca ākarttuḥ ahetu tā eva tasmāt vināśa hetoḥ ayogāt eva vināśaḥ svabhāvataḥ sva hetoḥ bhavati asmāt iti bhāvaḥ hetuḥ yatra nāma vināśaḥ bhavati iti mudgarāt kapāla utpattau loka abhimānaḥ tatra vināśaka ayogāt sva hetoḥ eva vinaśvara svabhāvatayā utpatteḥ dvitīye kṣaṇe na bhavati iti vaktavyam tasmāt ahetu tva vyavasthānāt anyatra api yatra visadṛśa anutpattyā vināśa utpatti abhimānaḥ na asti tatra api svabhāvataḥ sva hetoḥ eva vinaśyati iti vināśaḥ eka kṣaṇa sthāyī bhāvaḥ jāyate 
[357,i_357,iii]	tathāvidhe ca bhāva mātra anurodhini vināśe satvam hetuḥ avyabhicāraḥ kāryasya kāraṇe tad adhīna tvāt iti uktam tat eva āha yā kācid bhāva viṣayā anumitiḥ dvividhā eva sā sva sādhye kārya bhāvābhyām sambandha niyamāt tayoḥ yā kācid bhāva viṣaya anumitiḥ sā dvividhā eva kārya bhāvābhyām hetubhyām kāraṇa vyāpaka viṣayā bhavantī tayoḥ kārya svabhāvayoḥ eva sva sādhye sambandhasya niyamāt anyasya tu sādhye anāpatteḥ atad ātma tvāt ca na avi abhicāra niyamaḥ 
[357,iv_357,vi]	anupalabdheḥ api upalabdhi nivṛtti mātra lakṣaṇāyāḥ prāmāṇyam ākhyātum āha pravṛtteḥ buddhi pūrva tvāt tad bhāva anupalambhane pravarttitavyam na iti uktā anupalabdheḥ pramāṇa tā sat jñāna śabda vyavahārāṇāṃpravṛtteḥ buddhi pūrvaka tvāt tasyāḥ buddheḥ bhāva anupalambhane kāraṇa abhāvāt pravartitavyam na iti sāmarthyāt sidhyati na hi kāraṇa abhāvam kāryam yuktam atas anupalabdheḥ upalabdhi nivṛttiḥ upāyāḥ pravṛtti niṣedhe sādhye pramāṇa tā ukta ācāryeṇa na piśāca ādikam ghaṭa ādikam sat iti vaktavyam anupalabdheḥ iti sat vyavahāra pratiṣedha mātram sādhyate na tu asattva vyavahāraḥ 
[358,i_358,iii]	yatra tarhi pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ śāstrasya nivṛttiḥ tasya abhāvaḥ eva sādhayitum yuktaḥ iti āha śāstra adhikāra asambaddhāḥ bahava ūrthāḥ atīndriyāḥ aliṅgāḥ ca kathanteṣām abhāva unupalabdhitaḥ śāstra adhikāre asambaddhā anena śāstra viṣaya tvam āha bahavaḥ arthāḥ aniyata kāraṇa upanipāta janyāḥ sūkṣmāḥ durllakṣa bhedāḥ manaḥ vṛttayaḥ janminām deśa phala vyavahitāḥ vā anutpannāḥ dravya viśeṣāḥ atīndriyāḥ anena pratyakṣa aviṣaya tām āha liṅgāt ca ananumeya tām āha teṣām arthānām pratyakṣa anumāna śāstra nivṛtti lakṣaṇāyāḥ anupalabdhitaḥ katham abhāvaḥ sādhayitum yuktaḥ sati api anupalambhe teṣām sattva sambhavāt 
[358,iv_358,vi]	atas īdṛśī anupalabdhiḥ sat asat niścaya phalā na iti syāt vā apramāṇa tā pramāṇam api kācid syāt liṅga atiśaya bhāvinī sataḥ asat niścaya phalā na iti apramāṇa tā vā asyāḥ syāt sattva pratiṣedhe sādhye kācid tu anupalabdhiḥ lliṅga jā pratītiḥ asmin eva sādhye pramāṇam api syāt liṅga atiśaya bhāvinī liṅga viśeṣa prabhavā yathā uktam prāk hetu bheda vyapekṣayā iti upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anupalabdhi liṅga jā iti arthaḥ 
[358,vii_358,viii]	svabhāva jñāpaka ajñānasya ayam nyāya udāhṛtaḥ yat punar uktam apramāṇam anupalabdhiḥ iti yasya kasyacid svabhāvasya jñāpakasya liṅgasya ca ajñānasya anupalabdheḥ ayam nyāya udāhṛtaḥ na hi svabhāvaḥ na upalabhyataiti eva na asti deśa kāla svabhāva viprakṛṣṭānām adarśanepi sattva avirodhāt tatas na asti virakta cetaḥ iti ādya yuktam na ca kāraṇam iti eva kāryāṇi avyavadhānataḥ bhavanti tatas na asti dāna hiṃsā virati cetanānām abhyudaya hetu tā phala anantarya abhāva āditya yuktam 
[359,i_359,iv]	kārye tu kāraka ajñānam abhāvasya eva sādhakam kārakājñānantu kārye abhāvasya eva sādhakam na hi asati kāraṇe kārya saṃbhavaḥ svabhāva anupalambhaḥ ca svabhāverthasya liṅgini tad abhāvaḥ pratīyeta hetunā yadi kenacid tathā arthasya vyāpaka tayā niścitasya svabhāvasya anupalambhaḥ ca svabhāve vyāpye liṅginya sat tayā sādhye sādhanaṃtadā ca kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhī gamike yadi kena cit hetunā upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptānupalambhena anyena vā tayoḥ kāraṇa vyāpakayoḥ abhāvaḥ pratīyate na tu upalambha abhāva mātreṇa sandigdha asiddha tvāt 
[359,v_359,vii]	svabhāva anupalambham āha dṛśyasya darśana abhāva kāraṇā asambhave sati bhāvasya anupalambhasya bhāva abhāvaḥ pratīyate dṛśyasya vastunaḥ darśana abhāvasya yat kāraṇam vyavadhāna indriya vaikalya ādi tasya asambhave sati bhāvasya anupalabdhasya bhāvaḥ ābhāvaḥ svabhāva anupalabdheḥ pratīyate 
[359,viii_360,ii]	viruddhasya ca bhāvasya bhāve tad bhāva bādhanāt tad viruddha upalabdhau syāt asattāyāḥ viniścayaḥ viruddhasya nivarttakasya vahnaya ādeḥ bhāvasya bhāve tasya salila ādeḥ nivartti asya bhāva bādhanāt tad viruddha upalabdhau satya ām asattāyāḥ viniścayaḥ syāt nanu anupalabdheḥ abhāva sādhane kaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ vyomakusuma ādiḥ iti ced atra api yadi anupalabdheḥ abhāva siddhiḥ tadā dṛṣṭānta antara apekṣāyām anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ tad anapekṣāyām tad anupalabdhiḥ abhāva ākhyam pramāṇam astu 
[360,iii_360,iv]	asambaddham etat na hi abhāvaḥ anupalabdhyā sādhyate anupalabdhiḥ eva hi abhāvaḥ sa ca siddhaḥ eva tathā api tu mūḍhaḥ tam avyavaharat nimitta upadarśanena vyavahāryate tathā ca bhāvaḥ abhāvasya daṣṭa antaḥ tayoḥ sva naimittika pravarttanasya siddha tvāt nanu yat idaṃna santi pradhāna ādayaḥ anupalabdheḥ iti tatra katham asa dvayavahāra vidhiḥ sat vyavahāra pratiṣedhaḥ vā pradhāna ādi śabda vācyasya pratiṣedhe tad śabda aprayogāt 
[360,v_360,vii]	atra āha anādi vāsanā udbhūta vikalpa pariniṣṭhitaḥ śabda arthaḥ trividhaḥ dharmaḥ bhāva abhāva ubhayāśrayaḥ anādi vikalpa abhyāsa vāsanāyāḥ udbhūta vikalpe pariniṣṭhitaḥ pratibhāsamānaḥ śabda arthaḥ dharmaḥ trividhaḥ katham iti āha bhāva abhāva ubhayāśrayaḥ sat asat ubhaya vikalpa vāsanā prabhava tvāt tad adhyavasāyena tad viṣaya tvāt tatra bhāva upādānaḥ vikalpaḥ paṭa ādiḥ abhāva upādānaḥ śaśaviṣā ṇa ādiḥ ubhaya upādānaḥ pradhāneśvara ādiḥ 
[361,i_361,ii]	tasmin bhāvānupādāne sādhye asya anupalambhanam tathā hetuḥ na tasya eva abhāvaḥ śabda prayogataḥ tasmin śabda arthe pradhāna ādau bhāvānupādāne bhāva bhūta pradhāna āśraye sādhye asya pradhāna ādeḥ tathā bāhya bhāva āśraya tvena anupalambhanam hetuḥ vyavahāra sādhanaḥ na tu tasya śabda arthasya eva abhāvaḥ pradhāna ādi śabdasya tad pratipādakasya prayogataḥ 
[361,iii_361,v]	yadi tu vastu eva śabda viṣayaḥ tadā parama artha eka tāna tve śabdānām anibandhanā na syāt pravṛttiḥ artheṣu darśana antara bhediṣu parama artha eka tāna tve parama artha eka para vṛtti tve śabdānām artheṣu darśana antara bhediṣu pratidarśanam bhinna abhyupagamena nitya tva anitya tva triguṇī maya tva ādi kalpita bhedeṣu anibandhanā parama artha nibandhana rahitā pravṛttiḥ na syāt na hi paraspara viruddhāḥ bahavaḥ dharmāḥ ekatra santi 
[361,vi_361,vii]	atīta ajātayoḥ vā api na ca syāt anṛta artha tā vācaḥ kasyāścid iti eṣā bauddha artha viṣayā matā atīta ajātayoḥ vapi asatoḥ na syāt śabda vṛttiḥ na ca kasyāścid vācaḥ anṛta artha tā syāt artham antareṇa śabda abhāvāt yasmāt ete doṣāḥ vastu viṣaya tve vācaḥ iti tasmāt eṣā bauddha artha viṣayā kalpita artha gocarā matā 
[361,viii_362,i]	yaḥ ca śabda arthaḥ tasya bhāvān upādāna tvam sādhyate na tu saḥ eva niṣidhyate anyathā śabda artha apahnave sādhye dharma ādhāra nirākṛteḥ na sādhyaḥ samudāyaḥ syāt siddhaḥ dharmaḥ ca kevalaḥ śabda arthasya apahnave sādhye dharma ādhārasya dharmiṇā unirākṛteḥ samudāyaḥ sādhyaḥ na syāt dharmi dharma samudāyaḥ ca anumeyaḥ dharmaḥ eva kevalaḥ sādhyate iti ced siddhodharmaḥ ca abhāva ādiḥ kevalaḥ kimartham sādhanīyaḥ pradhāna ādi vikalpasya bhāvān upādāna tvam tu na siddham tat eva sādhyam yuktam 
[362,ii_362,vi]	kiñca sat asat pakṣa bhedena śabda arthānapavādibhiḥ vastu eva cintyate hi atra pratibaddhaḥ phala udayaḥ sat asat pakṣa bhedena vastu eva vyavahāribhiḥ śabda arthānapavādibhiḥ cintyate na avastu hi yasmāt atra vastuni phalasya artha kriyāyāḥ udayaḥ pratibaddhaḥ tatas ca artha kriyā asamarthasya vicāraiḥ kim tad arthinām ṣaṇḍhasya rūpe vairūpye kāminyā kim parīkṣayā 
[362,vii_362,x]	artha kriyā āyām asamarthasya śabda artha ādeḥ vicāraiḥ sat asat pakṣa cintābhiḥ tad arthinām artha kriyā arthinām kim na kiñcid prayojanam ṣaṇḍhasya napunsakasya rūpe vairūpye vā kāminyāḥ vṛṣasyantyāḥ yoṣitaḥ kim parīkṣayā yat punar ācāryeṇa uktam kalpitasya anupalabdhiḥ ddharmmaḥ iti tasya korthaḥ śabda arthaḥ kalpanā jñāna viṣaya tvena kalpitaḥ dharmaḥ vastu āśrayā asiddhiḥ asya uktā nyāya vādinā kalpanā jñānasya viṣaya tvena kalpitaḥ iṣṭaḥ pradhāna ādi śabda arthaḥ asya kalpitasya vastu āśrayā asiddhiḥ vastvā adhiṣṭhāna tva anupalabdhiḥ ddharmaḥ nyāya vādinā ācāryeṇa uktā 
[363,i_363,ii]	nanu yat uktam pramāṇa traya nivṛttau api na artha abhāva niścayaḥ iti tat mā bhūt pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ asarva viṣaya tvāt tad nivṛttyā abhāva niścayaḥ āgamaḥ tu sarva viṣayaḥ iti tad nivṛttau yuktaḥ arthā sattva niścayaḥ iti āha na antarīyaka tā abhāvāt śabdānām vastu bhissaha na artha siddhiḥ tatas te hi vakttṛ abhiprāya sūcakāḥ 
[363,iii_363,vi]	na antarīyaka tāyāḥ avinā abhāvasya abhāvāt vastubhiḥ saha śabdānām tatas śabdebhyaḥ na arthasya siddhiḥ niścayaḥ kintarhi tebhyaḥ gamyate iti āha vaktuḥ abhiprāyasya vivakṣāyāḥ te śabdāḥ sūcakāḥ tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi tvāt na ca vivakṣā yathārtham bhavati yena paraṃparayā tad samvādaḥ syāt visamvāda abhiprāyāt ajñānāt vā anyathā api vivakṣā sambhavāt āpta vāda avisaṃvāda sāmānyāt anumāna tā yadi evam sarvam eva vacanam pravṛtti kāmānām parīkṣā arham syāt kaḥ ca samvāda arthaḥ kathañca āpta vāda sāmānyāt anumāna tā asya ācāryeṇa uktā iti āha sambaddha anuguṇa upāyam puruṣa artha abhidhāyakam parīkṣā adhikṛtam vākyam atas nadhikṛtamparam 
[363,vii_364,i]	sambaddha vākyānām paraspara abhisambaddhānām ekārtha upasaṃhārāt na ca daśa dāḍima ādi vākyam iva eka arthān abhidhāyi anuguṇoṇāyam śakya anuṣṭhāna upeya sādhanam na tu viṣa śamana takṣaka phaṇā ratna alaṅkāra upadeśakam iva puruṣa arthasya svarga apavargasya abhidhāyakam na tu kāka danta parīkṣā upadeśakam iva parīkṣāyām pravṛtti arha viṣayam adhikṛtam vākyam atas aparamanadhikṛtam anavadhāna arha tvāt pratyakṣeṇa anumānena dvividhena api abādhanam dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa arthayoḥ asya avisaṃvādaḥ tad arthayoḥ 
[364,ii]	asya ca parīkṣā arhasya vākyasya avisamvādaḥ tad arthayaḥ rāgama abhidheyayoḥ dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭayoḥ pratyakṣā pratyakṣa yoḥ arthayoḥ pratyakṣeṇa anumānena ca dvividhena iti vastu bala bhāvinā agama āśrayeṇa ca ābādhanam anyeṣān ca bādhanam nāma yathā pratyakṣa tvena sammatānām pañcānām skandhānām pratyakṣeṇa ābādhanam siddhiḥ eva apratyakṣa tvena iṣṭānām śabda ādi triguṇa maya tva dravya karma sāmānya saṃyoga ādīn āñca tena bādhanam anumeya tvena iṣṭānām catur ārya satyānām vastu bala pravṛttena anumānena ābādhanam siddhiḥ eva ananumeya tvena iṣṭānān cātma īśvara ādīnām anumānena bādhaḥ eva atyanta parokṣāṇām rāga ādi hetukā adharma prahāṇa ādīnām āgama āśraya anumānena ābādhanam siddhiḥ evam rāga ādi hetu tvena iṣṭasya hetutva anuparodhinaḥ snonaḥ vāsa agnihotra ādeḥ prahāṇa upāya tayā anupadeśāt hetu vyāghātasya upāya tvena upadeśāt ca evam vidhama bādhanam avisamvādaḥ iṣṭaḥ 
[364,iii_364,iv]	āpta vāda avisaṃvāda sāmānyāt anumāna tā buddheḥ agatyā abhihitāḥ niṣiddhā api asya gocare tasya evam bhūtasya āpta vādasya adṛṣṭa vyabhicārasya avisamvāda sāmānyāt pratyakṣa anumāna āgamyepi arthe utpannāyāḥ buddheḥ avisamvādāt anumāna tā ca ācārya dignāgena abhihita āgatyā atyanta parokṣeṣu artheṣu dāna hiṃsā cetana ādiṣu artha anartha śravaṇāt āgama prāmāṇyam anāśritya sthātum asāmarthyāt etat bhāve virodha abhāvāt ca satyām pravṛttau varam evam pravṛttiḥ iti agatyā anumāna tā uktā na tu vastutas vacanānām artheṣu na antarīyaka tva abhāvāt 
[365,i_365,iii]	kim vā heya upādeya tattvasya sa upāyasya prasiddhitaḥ pradhāna artha avisamvādāt anumānamparatra vā heyasya duḥkha satyasya upādeyasya nirodha satyasyasā upāyasya yathākramam samudaya satyasya sa mārga satyasya ca āgama ukta vastu bala pravṛttena anumāne prasiddhitaḥ niścayāt satya catuṣṭaya adhigamasya nirvāṇa hetu tvena pradhāna arthasya avisamvādāt paratra atyanta parokṣepi arthe bhaga vat vacanāt utpannam jñānam anumānam yuktam iti vā pakṣa antaram 
[365,iv_365,vi]	puruṣa atiśaya apekṣam yathārtham apare viduḥ iṣṭoyam arthaḥ pratyetum śakyaḥ sotiśayaḥ yadi apare naiyāyika ādayaḥ puruṣasya atiśaya apekṣam yathābhūta artha darśi tad ākhyāt puruṣa praṇītam vacanam yathārtham satya artham pratijānīyuḥ siddhāntam āha puruṣa atiśaya praṇītam vacanama pramāṇam iti iṣṭaḥ ayam arthaḥ yadi puruṣāṇām sotiśayaḥ jñātum śakyaḥ syāt 
[365,vii_366,i]	kintu ayam evam na vā iti anya doṣa aniḥ doṣa tā api vā durlabha tvāt pramāṇānām durbodha iti apare viduḥ ayam pumān evaṃdoṣavān na vā nirdoṣaḥ iti anyasya doṣāḥ nirdoṣa tā api vā pramāṇānām durlabha tvāt durbodha iti apare saugatāḥ viduḥ durbbodha iti anya doṣāḥ iti anena liṅga vacana vipariṇāmena sambandhanīyam tat kim aśakya ucchedāḥ doṣāḥ na iti āha sarveṣām sa vipakṣa tvāt nirhnāsā atiśayam śritaḥ sa ātmībhāvāt tad abhyāsāt hīyeranna āsravāḥ kvacid 
[366,ii_366,iv]	sarveṣām āsravāṇām rāga ādīnāṃpratipakṣa saṃmukhībhāva abhāvayoḥ nnirhrāsa atiśayau upacaya apacayau śrayantaḥ iti nirhrāsa atiśayam śritaḥ teṣām sa vipakṣa tvāt pratipakṣa sambhavāt tasya pratipakṣasya abhyāsāt sā ātmībhāvāt āsravā kvacid citta santāne hīyeran iti khalu nirdoṣa puruṣa apalāpaḥ kriyate kintu tad avadhāraṇa upāyaḥ na asti iti ucyate icchā adhīnasya vyāhārasya anyathā api karttum śakya tvāt na tatas tathā artha niścayaḥ atha sātmīya bhūta pratipakṣasya mārga abhyāsāt nirdoṣa tāyām api satyām vipakṣa abhyāsāt punar doṣa utpattiḥ iti āha nirupadrava bhūta artha svabhāvasya viparyayaiḥ na bādhā yatnava tve api buddheḥ tad pakṣapātataḥ 
[366,v]	nirupadravasya doṣa rāśeḥ udvejakasya prahāṇāt bhūta arthasya pramāṇa paridṛṣṭa artha viṣaya tvāt svabhāvasya anāropita tvāt mārga sātmyasya vipakṣeṇa na bādhā yatnavatvepi yatnaḥ eva tāvat na sambhavati vipakṣa abhyāse doṣa darśanāt yatnavatvepi tu buddheḥ tatra mārga sātmye abhiruci viṣaya tvena pakṣapātataḥ na bādhā na hi rajvām nivṛtta sarppa bhramaḥ sarppam bhāvayitum yatate kaścid bhūta arthasya darśanāt 
[366,vi_366,x]	kaḥ punar doṣāṇām hetuḥ yad prahāṇāt amī prahīyante iti āha sarvāsām doṣa jātīnām jātiḥ sat kāya darśanāt sarvāsām doṣa jātīnām doṣa prakārāṇām jātiḥ janma sat kāya darśanāt ātma abhiniveśāt nanu avidyā hetukāḥ kleśāḥ bhagavatā uktaḥ iti āha sā avidyā tatra tad snehaḥ tasmāt dveṣa ādi sambhavaḥ 
[367,i_367,iii]	sā avidyā satkāya darśanam eva avidyā anyatra ucyate iti na asti virodhaḥ tatra sat kāya darśane sati teṣu ātmīyeṣu snehaḥ tasmāt ātmīyeṣu snehāt tad apakāriṣu dveṣa ādīnām sambhavaḥ iti doṣa utpatti kramaḥ atas nairātmya darśanam mārgaḥ yuktaḥ sat kāya dṛṣṭi pratipakṣa tvāt yatas ca sattva dṛṣṭiḥ avidyā mohaḥ nidānam doṣāṇām atra eva abhidhīyate satkāya dṛṣṭiḥ anyatra 
[367,iv_367,vii]	atas eva mohaḥ avidyā doṣāṇām nidānam abhidhīyate bhagavatā avidyāḥ hetukāḥ sarvai kleśāḥ iti punar anyatra pradeśe satkāya dṛṣṭiḥ doṣa nidānam abhidhīyate nanu anyepi indriya viṣayāḥ yoni śoma naskāra ādayaḥ doṣa hetavaḥ tad kim avidyā sat kāya dṛṣṭiḥ eva abhihite iti āha tad prahāṇe prahāṇataḥ tasya mohasya sat kāya dṛṣṭi lakṣaṇasya prahāṇe doṣāṇām prahāṇataḥ prādhānyāt saḥ eva uktaḥ na itaraḥ iti arthaḥ 
[367,viii_367,x]	veda pramāṇyam nirācikīrṣan paramatam utthāpayati girām mithyātva hetūnām doṣāṇām puruṣa āśrayāt apauruṣeyam satya artham iti kecid pracakṣate girām vācām mithyātvaṃsya hetūnām doṣāṇām ajñāna visamvāda abhiprāya ādīnām vā puruṣasya āśrayāt āśrayaṇa tvāt apauruṣeyam vākyam mithyātva hetoḥ puruṣa doṣasya abhāvāt satya artham iti kecid jaiminīyāḥ pracakṣate 
[368,i_368,ii]	girām satya tva hetūnām guṇānām puruṣa āśrayāt apauruṣeyam mithyā artham kim na iti anye pracakṣate tān eva prati girām satya tvasya hetūnām dayā dharma paratva ādīnām guṇānām puruṣasya āśrayāt apauruṣeyam vākyam satya tā hetoḥ puruṣa guṇasya abhāvāt mithyā artham kim na bhavati iti anye sau ga tāḥ pracakṣate 
[368,iii_368,v]	kiñca artha jñāpana hetuḥ hi saṅketaḥ puruṣa āśrayaḥ girā ām apauruṣeya tvepi ataḥ mithyātva sambhavaḥ saṅketam antareṇa apauruṣeyāt api vākyāt artha pratīteḥ abhāvāt artha jñāpana hetuḥ iha saṅketaḥ svīkartavyaḥ sa ca puruṣa kṛta tvāt puruṣa āśrayaḥ atas saṃketasya puruṣa āśraya tvāt girā ām apauruṣeya tvepi mithyātvasya sambhavaḥ saṃketa vaśena vācaḥ artham bruvate sa ca doṣa āśrayeṇa puruṣeṇa kriyate iti tāsām na visaṃvāda śaṅkā nirāsaḥ pauruṣeya vākya vat iti vyartham apauruṣeya tva kalpanam 
[368,vi_368,viii]	atha śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ na pauruṣeyaḥ kintu svābhāvikaḥ tatas na mithyātva sambhavaḥ tadā sambandha apauruṣeya tve syāt pratītira saṃvidaḥ sambandha apauruṣeya tvepīṣyamāṇe syāt arthānām pratītiḥ a saṃvidaḥ avidyamāna saṅketa pratīteḥ puṃsaḥ na ced śabda arthayoḥ sāṃketikaḥ vācya vācaka tā sambandhaḥ kintu svābhāvikaḥ tadā agṛhīta saṅketa upi śrutāt śabdāt artham pratipadyeta iti 
[369,i_369,iii]	atha saṃketāt satopi tasya sambandhasya abhivyaktiḥ pradīpa ādi vat ghaṭa ādeḥ atas na agṛhīta vyañjakasya vyaṅgya pratītiḥ tadā saṃketāt tad abhivyaktau asamarthāni akalpanā saṅketāt tasya sambandhasya abhivyakta aviṣyamāṇāyām saṃketāt anyasya sambandhasya kalpanā asamarthā sambandha vyavasthāpanāya saṃketāt eva vācya vācaka bhāvasya kalpitasya ghaṭamāna tvāt hasta saṃjñā ādeḥ iva artha pratipādanasya 
[369,iv_369,viii]	kiñca vācā kim ekena arthena saha vācya vācaka sambandhaḥ atha anekaiḥ tatra girām eka artha niyame na syāt artha antare gatiḥ girām ekasmin arthe vācakatayā niyame sati saṃketa vaśāt anyatra arthe na syāt gatiḥ dṛśyate ca vivakṣātaḥ aneka artha abhidhānam aneka artha abhisambandhe viruddha vyakti sambhavaḥ anekaiḥ arthaiḥ vācaka tva abhisambandhe viruddhasya arthasya vyakteḥ pratīteḥ sambhavaḥ syāt agniṣṭomaḥ svargasya sādhanam iti viparyaya upyavasīyeta tatas ca apravṛttiḥ eva syāt svargīrthinaḥ 
[369,ix_369,xi]	atha aneka artha abhidhāyī api śabdaḥ puruṣeṇa saṅketāt abhimata artha abhidhāyi tvena niyamyate tadā apauruṣeya tāyāñca vyarthā syāt parikalpanā vācyaḥ ca hetuḥ bhinnānām sambandhasya vyavasthiteḥ apauruṣeya tāyāñca vyarthā parikalpanā syāt tad abhyupagamepi puruṣa svātantrya abhyupagamāt tadā arthebhyaḥ bhinnānām śabdānām taiḥ saha sambandhasya vyavasthiteḥ hetuḥ ca vācyoyena avyabhicāraḥ na hi śabda arthayoḥ tādātmyam bhedāt na api tad utpattiḥ artham antareṇa api vivakṣātaḥ śabda utpatteḥ anyathā ca avyabhicāra abhāvāt 
[370,i_370,iii]	uktam artham saṃgṛhṇāt na āha asaṃskārya tayā puṃbhiḥ sarvathā syāt nirarthatā saṃskāra upagame mukhyam gaja snāna nibham bhavet yadi saṅketa nirapekṣāṇām svatas eva vācaka tvam śabdānām tadā apuṃbhiḥ asaṃskārya tayā saṅketa dvāreṇa niyamya tayā sarvathā nirarthatā syāt puruṣa saṅketa nirapekṣāt śabdāt arthaṃpratīteḥ abhāvāt etad doṣa bhayāt saṃskārasya upagame svīkāre idam apauruṣeya tvam mukhyam anupacaritam gaja snānam bhavet gajaḥ hi snāne paṅkam apanīya punar tena ātmānam limpati tathā apauruṣeya tvam sambandhasya svīkṛtya api punar saṅkete puruṣa apekṣā iti vyaktam sāmyam 
[370,iv_370,viii]	sambandhi nām a nitya tvāt na saṃbandhā isti nityatā tathā sambandhinām arthānām anitya tvāt saṃbandhe nityatā na asti na hi āśraya apāye bhavati āśritam kiñca nityasya anupakārya tvāt akurvāṇaḥ ca na āśrayaḥ arthaiḥ atas sa śabdānām saṃskāryaḥ puruṣaiḥ dhiyā nityasya sambandhasya anupakārya tvāt akurvāṇaḥ anupakurvāṇaḥ śabdaḥ arthaḥ ca āśrayaḥ na yuktaḥ yatas svābhāvika sambandha anupapattiḥ atas sambandhaḥ arthaiḥ saha śabdānām puruṣaiḥ vyavahartṛbhiḥ artha pratipādana abhiprāya anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam āśritya dhiyā kalpikayā saṃskāryaḥ vyavasthāpyaḥ 
[371,i_371,iv]	atha anityaḥ eva sambandhaḥ tadā sambandhinām nāśe sambandhasya naṣṭa tvāt nirarthakaḥ śabdaḥ syāt athavā arthaiḥ eva saha utpāde na svabhāva viparyayaḥ śabdeṣu yuktaḥ vācyaiḥ arthaiḥ eva saha sambandhasya utpādaḥ iṣyate tadā utpādaḥ iṣyamāṇepi pūrvam arthena saha sambandhasya vinaṣṭa tvāt artha sambandha rahita ātmasu śabdeṣu svabhāvasya sambandha vikalasya viparyayaḥ sambandha yogī na yuktaḥ na hi nityasya pūrva apara eka svabhāvasya anyathātvam yuktam anyathā nitya tā hāni prasaṅgāt 
[371,v_371,viii]	asmad mate tu sambandhe na ayam doṣaḥ vikalpite vikalpite kalpanā nirmite sambandhe ayam svabhāva anyatva prasaṅga doṣaḥ na bhavati na hi kalpanāk lṛptaḥ dharmaḥ svabhāvam vastutas spṛśati nitya tvāt āśraya apāyepya nāśaḥ yadi sammataḥ nityeṣu āśraya sāmarthyam kim yena iṣṭaḥ sa ca āśrayaḥ 
[371,ix]	sambandhasya nitya tvāt āśrayasya vācyasya apāyepya nāśaḥ yadi jāteḥ iva sammataḥ tadā nityeṣu jāti sambandha ādiṣu āśrayasya vācyasyāḥ vācakasya ca kim sāmarthyam upakāra viśeṣa ādhāya kaṃyena sāmarthyena sa vācyadira āśrayaḥ iṣṭaḥ na hi anupakāryam āśrita mati prasaṅgāt nityasya ca upakārāsambhavaḥ bheda abheda kalpanāyām ayukta tvāt 
[371,x_372,i]	atha nityasya api jāti sambandha ādeḥ āśrayeṇa abhivyakti lakṣaṇaḥ upakāraḥ kriyate na ca avyakti hetuḥ kārakaḥ dīpa ādi vat ghaṭa ādeḥ iti āha jñāna utpādena hetūnām sambandhāt sahakāriṇām tad utpādana yogya tvena utpattiḥ vyaktiḥ iṣyate ghaṭa ādiṣu api yukti jñaiḥ jñāna utpādena hetūnām dīpa ādīnām sahakāriṇām sambandhāt tad utpādana yogya tvena jñāna utpādana samartha tvena utpattiḥ ghaṭa ādiṣu api bhāveṣu yukti jñaiḥ nyāya vidbhiḥ vyaktiḥ iṣyate anyathā jñāna utpādana yogyasya svabhāvasya anutpattau jñāna utpādanam na syāt 
[372,ii_372,iii]	aviśeṣe avikāriṇām vyañjakaiḥ svaiḥ kutas korthaḥ vyaktāḥ taiḥ te yatas matāḥ nityānām jāti sambandha ādīnām avikāriṇām kutaścid aviśeṣe viśeṣa asambhave svaiḥ vyañjakaiḥ āśraya abhimataiḥ korthaḥ svabhāvānyathātva ādiḥ kutas na kaścid yatas arthāt kṛtāt taiḥ vyañjakaiḥ te jāti ādayaḥ vyaktāḥ matāḥ 
[372,iv_372,vi]	kiñca sambandhasya ca vastu tve syāt bhedāt buddhi citra tā tābhyām abhede tau eva na atonyāḥ vastunaḥ gatiḥ yadi sambandhasya vastu tvanta dā vastu tve sati bhedaḥ abhedaḥ vā abhyupagantavyaḥ tatra bhedāt buddheḥ citra tā syāt vācya vācakau sambandhaḥ ca iti tritayam dṛśyeta na ca īkṣyate atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā tābhyām abhede sambandhasya tau vācya vācakau eva syātām na tu sambandhaḥ nāma kaścid atha sambandhaḥ na bhinnaḥ na api abhinnaḥ atas bheda abhedābhyām anyāḥ vastunaḥ gatiḥ na asti anyonya vaccheda ātmaka tvāt anayaḥ rāśi antara asambhavān na anyaḥ prakāra usti vastunaḥ 
[372,vii_373,iii]	tasmāt bhinna tvāt vastu rūpasya sambandhaḥ kalpanā kṛtaḥ sat dravyam syāt para adhīnam sambandhonyasya vā katham bhinna tvāt vastunoḥ sambandhinoḥ rūpasya sambandhaḥ śleṣa lakṣaṇaḥ kalpanayā kṛtaḥ na vāstavaḥ anyathā sat dravyam sambandha ākhyam para adhīnam sambandha āyattam katham syāt katham vā bhinnayoḥ sambandhinoḥ śleṣa lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ parasparam amiśra svabhāva tvāt sarvasya tathā api sambandha iti prasaṅgāt kiñca varṇṇāḥ nirarthakāḥ santaḥ 
[373,iv]	ayam sambandhaḥ varttamānaḥ varṇṇeṣu pada ādiṣu vā varttata tatra varṇṇāḥ santoniḥ arthakāḥ pratyekam teṣām artha pratipādaka tva abhāvāt nānā prayoktṛ prayuktebhyaḥ artha apratipatteḥ ca vyatikrama prayuktebhyaḥ ca saraḥ rasaḥ ityādibhyaḥ tulyā syāt pratipattiḥ tad samudāyasya ca asambhavaḥ krameṇa upalambhāt na ca samudāyaḥ nāma samudāyibhyaḥ bhinnaḥ anupalambha bādhita tvāt teṣāñca vācaka tvāt ekasmāt api pratītiḥ syāt pratyekam na ced vācakāḥ samuditebhyopi tebhyaḥ na syāt pratītiḥ tadā api anyasya abhāvāt 
[373,v]	atha krameṇa varṇṇeṣu gṛhīteṣu tad saṃskāra sahāyena adhyakṣeṇa gṛhīta ādantya varṇṇāt artha pratītiḥ tat kim antyaḥ eva varṇṇaḥ vācakaḥ na anye tathā tet vyartham teṣām uccāraṇam saveṣu pratīteṣu artha pratītiḥ iti ced kim antya varṇṇa grāhikayā buddhyā sarvatra grahaṇam anya ani abuddhyā eva ced tāḥ kim buddhayaḥ antya varṇṇa buddhi kāle bhavanti yena tadā artha pratītiḥ ucyate anya anya kāle eva iti ced yadi tābhiḥ vācakāḥ varṇṇāḥ gṛhyante ekaika varṇṇa grahaṇepi artha pratītiḥ syāt vācakeṣu sarvaṣu gṛhīteṣu pratītiḥ iti ced tadā tu na pratyekam vācakaḥ tat atiriktaḥ ca samudāyaḥ na asti 
[374,i]	pratyekam samarthāḥ sthiti bīja ādayaḥ aṅkura janane na ca kevala ajanayanti iti ced ye samarthāḥ na teṣām kṣaṇika tvāt pṛthak bhāvaḥ iti asamānam samuditāḥ eva tu samarthāḥ na tu evam varṇṇānām kvāpi samudāyaḥ krama upalabhya tvāt tadā ced pratipādakāḥ avācakāḥ eva pūrva varṇṇa grahaṇa saṃskāra īpi kim antya varṇṇa buddhau sarve pratibhānti na vā na tāvat upalabhyante tatas tat upadarśam api vyartham sarveṣu kramāt pratīteṣu smṛtiḥ samudāya viṣayā bhavati iti ced kimvarṇṇānām samudāya usti pratītaḥ vā yaḥ smaryate kevalam kalpyate kalpitasya vācaka tva abhyupagame na vivādaḥ tasmāt na varṇṇe sambandha vṛttiḥ 
[374,ii_374,v]	pada vākya ādiṣu tarhi syāt iti ced pada ādi parikalpitam avastuni katham vṛttiḥ sambandhasya asya vastunaḥ na hi krama uccāritebhyaḥ varṇṇebhyaḥ vyatiriktam pada ādikam upalabhyate kevalam kalpanā buddhyā krama uccāritānām varṇṇānām samudāyaḥ kalpitaḥ padam padānāñca samudāyaḥ kalpitaḥ vākyam ucyate tat ca kalpita tvāt avastu avastuni sambandhasya vastunaḥ katham vṛttiḥ na hi śaśa viṣāṇasya nīla ādi ḥ ddharmaḥ yuktaḥ tat evam na sambandhaḥ nityaḥ anityaḥ vā yuktaḥ iti sthitam apauruṣeya tā āpi iṣṭā karttṛṇāma smṛteḥ kila santi asya api anuvaktāraḥ iti dhik vyāpakam tamaḥ
