[374,vi]	veda vākyānām apauruṣeya tā api kenaci nmī mām sa kaḥ pravareṇa iṣṭā karttṛṇāma smṛteḥ liṅgāt kila akṣamāyām kila śabdaḥ asya api arthasya nyāyāt dūram āyātasya anuvaktāraḥ paṇḍitaṃmanyāḥ santi tasya eva tāvat īdṛśam prajñā skhalitam katham vṛttam iti sa vismaya anukampat naḥ cetaḥ tat api apare anuvadanti iti nirdaya ākrānta bhuvanam dhik avya apakantamaḥ tathā hi karttuḥ smaraṇam asiddham smaranti saugatāḥ mantrāṇām kartṝn aṣṭaka ādīn kāṇādāḥ ca vidhātāram mithyā tad smaraṇañcet kumāra sambhava ādeḥ api kāli dāsa ādi karttṛ smaraṇam mithyā iti tat api apauruṣeyam tatra ekam smaraṇam apramāṇam anyat ca anyathā iti na atra vibhāga kāraṇam bahūnām saṃpratipatti vipratipattayaḥ ca na pramāṇa itara lakṣaṇe samvāda satvena sidhyataḥ tatas ca asmṛta karttṛkam iti aśakya niścayam sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvāt 
[375,i_375,ii]	yathā ayam anyatas aśrutvā na imam varṇa pada kramam vaktum samarthaḥ puruṣaḥ tathā anyopī iti kaścana yadā api vedān adhīyānaḥ yathā ayam idāni intanaḥ māṇavakaḥ anyatas upādhyāyāt aśrutvā imam ucyamānam varṇṇa padayoḥ kramam ānupūrvī viśiṣṭām veda ākhyām vaktum asamarthaḥ vedaka pāṭhaka tvāt tathā anyaḥ upādhyāyaḥ tat upādhyāya upīti anādiḥ eṣa kramaḥ itikaści nmī mām sa kaḥ sarvasya eva veda pāṭhaḥ para upadeśāt iti nitya tā eva vedānām 
[375,iii_375,v]	tatra api āha anyaḥ vā racitaḥ granthaḥ sampradāyāt ṛte paraiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kaḥ abhihitaḥ yena sopyevam na anumīyate anyaḥ vā veda āditaraḥ kāvya ādiḥ granthaḥ racitaḥ kavi prabhṛtibhiḥ saṃpradāyāt ṛte upadeśāt vinā paraiḥ adhyetṛbhiḥ abhihitaḥ kaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na kaścid yena para upadeśe asati aśakya adhyayana tvena sa upi kāvya ādiḥ evam nityam na anumīyate tatra api hetuḥ ayam siddhaḥ eva atha puruṣeṇa tad karaṇa avirodhāt sandigdha vyatireka tā asya hetoḥ tadā vedepi duṣṭa tvam asyāḥ katham nivāryam 
[375,vi_375,viii]	api ca yat jātīyaḥ yatas siddhaḥ saḥ aviśiṣṭa ugni kāṣṭha vat adṛṣṭa hetuḥ api anyaḥ tad bhavaḥ saṃpratīyate yat jātīyaḥ yad dravya samāna jātīyaḥ yaḥ padārthaḥ yatas hetoḥ siddhaḥ anvaya vyatirekābhyām niścitaḥ sa tad jātīya tvena aviśiṣṭaḥ anyaḥ adṛṣṭa hetuḥ api tad hetuka tvena saṃpratīyate kim iva agni kāṣṭha vat kāṣṭha kārya tvena vahneḥ niścita tvāt vahni darśanāt adṛṣṭam api kāṣṭham anumīyate na ca vaidika pauruṣeya vākyānām kaścid bhedaḥ sarveṣām durbhaṇa tva ādīnām mantra ādi sāma arthya anāñca sādhāraṇa tvāt 
[375,ix_375,xi]	idānīm veda karaṇa samartha puruṣa adarśanam bhās ra tādiṣu api samānam tatas asati avāntara bhede bhedāt hetu upanyāsaḥ na yuktaḥ sati tu vastutas tatra apradarśya ye bhedam kārya sāmānya darśanāt hetavaḥ pravitanyante sarve te vyabhicāriṇaḥ tatra sādhanīkṛte vastuni avāntara bhede bhedam apradarśya kārya sāmānyasya vijātīya vyāvṛtti mātrasya darśanāt ye hetavaḥ yad veda adhyayanam tad veda adhyayana pūrvakam na karaṇa pūrvakam yathā yaḥ pathika agniḥ sa jvālā pūrvakaḥ na vāraṇi nirmathana pūrvakaḥ ityādayaḥ pravitanyante vistāryante sarva te vyabhicāriṇaḥ anaikāntikāḥ na hi veda adhyayanam iti eva adhyayana pūrvakam kṛtvā karaṇa pūrvakasya api adhyayanasya upapatteḥ araṇi nirmathanasya ca vahneḥ bhāva avirodhāt 
[377,i_377,iii]	bhavatu vā sarvathā anāditā siddhyet evam na apuruṣa āśrayaḥ tasmāt apauruṣeya tve syāt anya upya nara āśrayaḥ evam veda adhyayanam adhyayana pūrva tāsā dhanam tathā api sarvathā anāditā veda adhyayanasya sidhyet ḍimbhaka pāṃśu krīḍā ādīnām iva na apuruṣa āśrayaḥ puruṣa āśrayaṇa abhāvaḥ tu na sidhyet ḍimbhaka pāṃśu krīḍā ādayaḥ hi darśana pūrvakāḥ anādayaḥ ca na ca apauruṣeyāḥ ḍimbhakaiḥ eva kriyamāṇa tvāt evam śabdāḥ api adhyetṛbhiḥ eva kriyante na tu svayam ātmānam dhvanayanti yena apauruṣeyāḥ syuḥ anādiḥ tādṛś karaṇa kramaḥ puruṣa paraṃparāyāḥ anādeḥ āgata tvāt atha anādi tvā deva apauruṣeya tā iti āha tasya anādi tvāt apauruṣeya tve sādhye syāt anyaḥ pyapauruṣeyaḥ anara āśrayaḥ iti prasaṅgaḥ 
[377,iv_377,viii]	tam eva āha mleccha ādi vyavahārāṇām nāstikya vacasām api anādi tvāt tathā abhāvaḥ mleccha ādeḥ vyavahārāṇām mātṛ vivāha mukti prāpaṇa māraṇa ādīnām nāstikya vacasām api para loka karma phala ādi apavādi nām anādi tvāt tathā abhāvaḥ apauruṣeya tvam syāt yadi pauruṣeyāḥ katham anādayaḥ iti āha pūrva saṃskāra santateḥ 
[378,i_378,iv]	pūrva saṃskārāt anādeḥ santateḥ santānena pravṛtteḥ atha anādi tvāt mleccha ādi vyavahārāṇāñca apauruṣeya tā astitva āha tādṛśe apauruṣeya tve kaḥ siddhepi guṇaḥ bhavet tādṛśe mleccha ādi vyavahāra sādhāraṇe apauruṣeya tve siddhepi kaḥ guṇaḥ avisamvādaka lakṣaṇaḥ bhavet pauruṣeya vākyānām visamvāda adarśanādapauruṣeya tvam iṣṭam sa ca tasmin api sati mleccha ādi vyavahārāṇām iva duṣpariharaḥ 
[378,v_378,x]	atha veda vākyānām eva anādi tvāt apauruṣeya tvam tadā artha saṃskāra bhedānām darśanāt saṃśayaḥ punar arthasya saṃskāraḥ vyākhyānam tasya bhedānām vikalpānām prakṛti pratyaya aneka artha tvāt rūḍheḥ nirukta ādibhyaḥ ca yathāpratibham puṃsān darśanāt saṃśayaḥ artha niścaya abhāvaḥ kasya ca apauruṣeya tvam iṣṭam kimvarṇṇānām uta pada vākyānām iti āha anya aviśeṣāt varṇṇānām sādhane kim phalam bhavet anyaiḥ lokikaiḥ varṇṇaiḥ vaidikānām aviśeṣāt pratyabhijñāyamāna tvena eka tvāt apauruṣeya tvasya sādhane kim phalam bhavet tathā tve laukikānām artha vyabhicārāt 
[378,xi_378,xii]	vākyam bhinnam na varṇebhyaḥ vidyate anupalambhataḥ aneka avayava ātma tve pṛthak teṣām nirarthatā atad rūpe ca tādrūpyam kalpitam siṃhatā ādi vat vākyam padañca varṇṇebhyaḥ bhinnam na vidyate anupalambhāt tat katham asya apauruṣeya tvam sādhyam abhinnam ced tadā aneka avayava ātma tve vākyasya teṣām avayavānām pṛthak pratyekam nirarthaka tā iti pada ātmakam anarthakam eva syāt tatas ca ātad rūpe avācaka rūpe tādrūpyam vācaka tvam kalpitam kalpanā buddhi nirmitam māṇavaka ādau iva siṃhatā ādi tatas pauruṣeyam eva vācaka tvam syāt iti prastuta kṣatiḥ 
[379,i_379,vi]	atha pratyekam avayavānām sārthaka tvam tadā pratyekam sārthaka tvepi mithyā aneka tva kalpanā eka avayava gatyā ca vākya artha pratipad bhavet pratyekam sārthaka tvepi mithyā aneka tvasya aneka avayava ātmakasya kalpanā ekasmāt artha pratīteḥ tathā ekasya avayavasya gatyā vākya arthasya pratipad pratītiḥ bhavet ekasya api vācaka tvāt tad samudāyaḥ vācakaḥ iti ced sa kintebhyaḥ bhinnaḥ sa ca pratyuktaḥ avayavāḥ militāḥ samudāyaḥ iti ced sa ca na sambhavati eva tat yadi pratyekam vācaka tvam eva tadā eṣām pratyekam vācaka tve ca ekasmāt api syāt artha pratītiḥ atha sakṛt śrutau ca sarveṣām kāla bhedaḥ na yujyate eka avayava gatyā artha pratipatteḥ avayava antara vaiphalya doṣāt sarva avayavānām sakṛt śrutiḥ iṣyate tadā sarveṣām avayavānām sakṛt śrutau ca abhimatāyām avayava śravaṇasya kāla bheda ūna yujyate dṛśyeta ca 
[379,vii_379,viii]	atha anavayavam ekam varṇṇebhyaḥ vyatiriktam sphoṭa rūpam vākyam tat ca kramavadbhiḥ nniyata ānupūrvīkaiḥ dhvanibhiḥ krameṇa vyajyate vyakti anukrameṇa eva ca krama vat pratīyate tad rūpā vibhāgena nāda rūpāṇām varṇṇānām grahaṇāt varṇṇa vibhāga vat ca lakṣyate vastutas tathā rahitam api iti kecid ekatvepi hi abhinnasya kramaśas gati asambhavāt 
[379,ix_380,ii]	tat eka tva ipi hi abhinnasya anavayavasya sphoṭa rūpasya vākyasya prathama dhvaninā api vyakta tvāt kramaśas gateḥ pratīteḥ asambhavāt sakṛt pratīti prasaṅgaḥ yadi prathama vyaktau na pratītiḥ aparāsu api na syāt tad eka vyañcaka tvāt vyaktīnām kiñca vākyantat nityam anityam vā syāt anityam yatna sambhūtam pauruṣeyam kathat na tat nitya upalabdhi nitya tve api anāvaraṇa sambhavāt 
[380,iii]	yadi anityam pauruṣeyam katham na tat yatna sambhavāt ghaṭa ādi vat nitya tvepi upalabdhiḥ nityā bhavet vākyānām anāvaraṇa sambhavāt āvaraṇa ayogāt yadi nityam kadācid upalabhyate tadā tasya anāvṛta svabhāva tā abhyupagantavyā tādṛśam nityam upalabhyeta abhimata kālaḥ iva āvṛta svabhāve tu sarvadā anupalambhaḥ syāt tasmāt kāla bhedena upalabhya anupalabhya svabhāva tvāt ekasya nāśāt anyasya udayaḥ iti syāt tathā ca nitya tva kṣatiḥ 
[380,iv_380,vi]	eka svabhāvaḥ eva śabdaḥ param aśrutiḥ vikala tvāt ced kasyacid sahakāriṇaḥ kāmam anya pratīkṣā uktiḥ niyamaḥ tu virudhyate kasyacid sahakāriṇaḥ jñāna janakasya vaikalyāt aśrutiḥ iti ced kāmam anyasya sahakāriṇaḥ upakārakasya pratīkṣā apekṣaṇam astu niyamaḥ pūrva apara eka svabhāvatā āvaraṇantu śabdānām virudhyate na hi eka svabhāvaḥ param apekṣate ca iti kṣamam upakārakasya apekṣaṇīya tvāt upakāra antarasya ca svabhāva antara lakṣaṇa tvāt 
[380,vii_380,ix]	api ca śabdāḥ avyāpinaḥ vyāpinaḥ vā syuḥ tatra sarvatra anupalambhaḥ syāt teṣām avyāpitā yadi sarveṣām upalambhaḥ syāt yugapad vyāpitā yadi yadi avyāpitā teṣām sarvatra deśe aanupalambhaḥ syāt na hi eka deśa sthitaḥ śailaḥ sarvatra upalabhyate yogyatā atiśaya lābhāt vyañcakebhyaḥ dṛśyate eva iti ced evantarhi sarvaiḥ sarva deśa sthaiḥ upalabhyeta tathā vyāpitā yadi sarveṣām śabdānām yugapad upalambhaḥ syāt vyāpi tvāt sarveṣām sarvatra bhāvāt 
[380,x_381,ii]	atha vyāpi tvā ipi yaḥ eva abhivyaktyā saṃskṛtaḥ saḥ eva upalabhyate na itaraḥ saṃskṛtasya upalambhe ca kaḥ saṃskarttā avikāriṇaḥ indriyasya syāt saṃskāraḥ śṛṇuyāt nikhilañca tat saṃskṛtasya ca upalambhe ca svīkriyamāṇe nitya tvāt avikāriṇaḥ kaḥ saṃskarttā nāma na hi anupakurvan saṃskarttā anupakāryaḥ vā saṃskāryaḥ atha indriyam anitya tvāt saṃskārya tatas saṃskṛtaḥ eva paśyati na anyaḥ iti vibhāgaḥ satyam indriyasya syāt saṃskāraḥ kintu tad indriyam nikhilam ca śabda grāmam śṛṇuyāt na tu eka śabdam 
[381,iii_381,iv]	saṃskāra bheda bhinna tvāt ekārtha niyamaḥ yadi aneka śabda saṃghāte śrutiḥ kalakale katham saṃskārasya śabda viṣayasya bhedāt pratiniyamāt bhinna tvāt indriya saṃskārāṇām ekasmin arthe śabde niyamaḥ śrutiḥ yat īṣyate tadā aneka śabda saṃghāte kalakale śrutiḥ anekeṣām śabdānām kathaṃsaṃskāra pratiniyamāt indriyam na aneka śabda grāhi syāt 
[381,v_381,vii]	atha dhvanayaḥ kevalam tatra śrūyante ced na vācakāḥ dhvanibhyaḥ bhinnam asti iti śraddheyam avivakṣitam tatra kalakale dhvanayaḥ śabda vyañjakāḥ kevalam śrūyante na vācakāḥ śabdāḥ dhvanibhyaḥ śrūyamāṇebhyaḥ bhinnam śabda rūpam asti iti yat kiñjididam atiśraddheyam śraddhā vaśāt yadi etat aṅgīkriyate na tu pramāṇa balāt 
[381,viii_381,x]	kiñja sthiteṣu anyeṣu śabdeṣu śrūyate vācakaḥ katham kalakale dhvani mātram yadi śrūyate na śabdaḥ tadā bahūnām vyāharttṝṇām tūṣṇīmbhāvāt anyeṣu api eṣu śabdeṣu sthiteṣu ekasmin puruṣe vyāharati katham vācakaḥ śrūyateka lakalaiḥ va dhvani mātra śrutiḥ tadā api syāt atha vācakasya ulabdhi pratyaya bhāvāt upalabdhiḥ tadā kalaka lepi syāt viśeṣa abhāvāt 
[382,i_382,v]	yadi ca indriyāṇām saṃskāra viśeṣāt śabda viśeṣa upalabdhi pratiniyamaḥ tadā katham vā śakti niyamāt bhinna dhvani gatiḥ bhavet śakti niyamaḥ tadā śakti niyamāt indriyāṇām katham bhinna dhvani gatiḥ bhavet śabda viśeṣa vat dhvani viśeṣasya eva grāhakam indriyam syāt tat katham kalakala dhvani pratītiḥ kiñca dhvanayaḥ saṃmatāḥ yaiḥ te doṣaiḥ kaiḥ api avācakāḥ dhvanibhiḥ byajyamānā ismin vācakepi katham na te 
[382,vi_382,vii]	yaiḥ kaiḥ api doṣaiḥ dhvanayaḥ avācakāḥ sammatāḥ te doṣāḥ vyajyamānepi vācakesmin kathat na bhavanti tathā hi yathā pratyekam avācaka tvāt vācaka tve vā dhvani antara vaiphalyāt sāhitya abhāvāt ca dhvanayaḥ avācakāḥ tathā dhvanibhiḥ pratyekam vācaka an abhivyakteḥ abhivyaktau vā dhvani antare vaiphalyāt sāhitya abhāvāt ca na abhivyajyeta śabdaḥ anabhivyaktaḥ ca kam artha pratipādayet varṇṇa ānupūrvī vākyam ced na varṇṇānām abhedataḥ teṣāñca na vyavasthānam krama antara virodhataḥ 
[382,viii]	varṇṇānām ānupūrvī paripāṭi viśeṣaḥ vākyam tat ca upalabhyate eva iti ced na varṇṇānām ānupūrvyāyāḥ abhedataḥ na hi varṇṇebhyaḥ bhinnā ānupūrvī pratīti viṣayaḥ tatas ca varṇṇāḥ eva vākyam iti syāt teṣāñca loka vedayoḥ na viśeṣaḥ iti sarvatra prāmāṇyam atha aprāmāṇi am vā syāt atha viśeṣa anupūrvīkāḥ varṇṇāḥ eva veda vākyam na itaraḥ iti āha teṣāñca varṇṇānām na vyavasthāna krama niyamaḥ krama antarasya laukikasya virodhataḥ tathā hi varṇṇa vat ānupūrvī nityāḥ na ca varṇṇāḥ bahavaḥ santi samāna jātīyāḥ vai eka tvāt varṇṇasya tatas ca agniḥ iti eva ākāra gakāra nakārāṇām ānupūrvī viśiṣṭaḥ syāt nagam iti anyathā na bhavet kṛtakānām api bījāṅtkura patra ādīnām ṛtu saṃvatsara ādīnām viśiṣṭa ānupūrvī na anyathā bhavati kimpunar nityānām 
[383,i_383,iii]	sā ca iyam ānupūrvī varṇṇānām deśa kāla krama abhāvaḥ vyāpti nitya tva varṇṇanāt deśa kṛtā vā pipīlikānām iva paṃktī syāt kāla kṛtā vā bīja aṅkura ādīnām iva dvayoḥ api deśa kāla kramayoḥ abhāvaḥ varṇṇānām vyāpti nitya tvayoḥ varṇṇanāt anyonya deśa parihāreṇa vṛttiḥ hi deśa paurvāparya tat ca sarvagānām asambhavi tathā anyonya kāla parihāreṇa vṛttiḥ kālapaurvāparyañca nityānām asambhavi 
[383,iv_383,vii]	atha ānupūrvī samarthana artham anitya tā avyāpita iṣyate anitya avyāpita āyāñca doṣaḥ prāk eva kīrttitaḥ anitya avyāpita āyāñca doṣaḥ prāk eva uktaḥ anitya tve pauruṣeya tā avyāpi tve ca sarvatra upalabdhiḥ ca na syāt vyakti krama upi vākyam na nitya vyakti nirākṛteḥ vyāpārāt eva tad siddheḥ karaṇānām ca kārya tā 
[384,i_384,iii]	iti nitya vyāpinām api śabdānām vyakteḥ abhivyakte pratiniyata deśa kālāyāḥ kramaḥ vākyam na yuktaḥ nityasya vyakti nirākṛteḥ jñāna utpādana hetūnām ityādinā tasmāt karaṇānām vyāparāt eva teṣām varṇṇānām siddheḥ kārya tā eṣām yuktā na vyaṅgyatā kiñca sva jñānena anya dhī hetuḥ siddherthe vyañcakaḥ mataḥ yathā dīponyathā vā api kaḥ viśeṣaḥ sya kārakāt 
[384,iv_384,vi]	siddhe vidyamāne arthe sva jñānena kāraṇena anyasya jñāna hetuḥ vyañjakaḥ mataḥ pradīpaḥ ghaṭasya yathā anyathā vā api iti yadi vyaṅgyaḥ prāk siddhaḥ na bhavet tadā asya vyañjakasya kārakāt hetoḥ kaḥ viśeṣaḥ na kaścid apūrva pratipatti hetu tva aviśeṣāt tathā karaṇānām samagrāṇām vyāpārāt upalabdhitaḥ niyamena ca kārya tvam vyañcake tad asambhavāt 
[384,vii]	karaṇānām samagrāṇām vyāpārāt niyamena upalabdhitaḥ ca kāryatvam eva varṇṇānām vyañcake dīpa ādau tasya vyaṅgya upalabdhi niyamasya asambhavāt na hi dīpaḥ iti eva ghaṭa pratītiḥ karaṇa sāmagryantu kāryam avaśyam bhāvayati iti karaṇa sāmagrye niyata upalambhasya kārya tā eva tad rūpa āvaraṇanām ca vyaktiḥ te vigamaḥ yadi abhāve karaṇa grāma sāmarthyam kim nu tat bhavet 
[385,i]	teṣām varṇṇānām rūpasya stimita vāyavīya avayava saṃyoga rūpāṇām āvaraṇānām prayatna preritena vāyunā vigamaḥ yadi vyaktiḥ te mī mām sa kaḥ syeṣṭā tadā pūrva avasthā tyāge na atiśayaḥ na vyaktiḥ anitya tva āsakteḥ upalambha āvaraṇa vigamaḥ vā śabda ālambanam jñānam vā vyaktiḥ syāt iti atra āha kāryam vyaktiḥ aśakyā yasmāt āvaraṇa vigame abhāve nīrūpe karaṇa grāmasya kim nu tat sāmarthyam bhavet kvacid karttavye sāmarthyam syāt na tu karttavya abhāve yadi samasta kāryatva sambhavepi śabdānām na kārya tā tadā 
[385,ii_385,iii]	śabda aviśeṣāt anyeṣām api vyaktiḥ prasajyate tathā abhyupagame sarva kārakāṇām nirarthatā śabdāt aviśeṣāt anya vyāpāra antarāt upalabhyamāna tva niyamena anyeṣām ghaṭa ādīnām api vyaktiḥ prasajyeta kārya tā na syāt tathā abhyupagame ca sarveṣām kārakāṇām vyañcaka abhimatānām nirarthaka tā utpādakam hi kāraṇabhiṣyate na tu vyañjakam śabdānām iva sādhanam pratyabhijñānam sat prayoga ādi yat matam anudāharaṇam sarva bhāvānām kṣaṇa bhaṅgataḥ 
[385,iv_385,v]	yat ca nitya tva siddhaye varṇṇānām pratyabhijñānam sat prayogaḥ ādi śabdāt uccāryamāṇa tva ādi sādhanam matam san ā iva hi prayujyate yathā vā asya ādi cchidāyām tatas prayogāt prayogepi vidyamāna tvāt varṇṇāḥ nityāḥ eva tad anudāharaṇam dṛṣṭānta vikalaṃsarveṣa ambhāvānām kṣaṇa bhaṅgataḥ dūṣyaḥ kuhetuḥ anyā upi 
[385,vi_386,iii]	anayā eva diśā paraiḥ ucyamānaḥ kuhetuḥ anyā upi dūṣyaḥ atha buddhiḥ abhivyaktiḥ varṇṇānām sā ca kramavatī vākyam iṣṭam tadā vākyasya apauruṣeya tvena iṣṭa tvāt buddhiḥ apauruṣeyī syāt tatra buddheḥ apuruṣa āśraye bādha abhyupeta pratyakṣa pratīta anumitaiḥ samam buddheḥ apuruṣa āśraye puruṣa an āśrayaṇebādhā kaiḥ iti āha abhyupeta pratyakṣa pratīta anumitaiḥ samam eka kālam eva buddheḥ apuruṣa āśraya tvasya abhyupetena puruṣa guṇa tva abhyupagamena pratyakṣa pratītena ca puruṣa kārya tvena tad prayatnakāḥ ryatvena vā kādācid katva anumitena kāryatvena ca bādhā 
[386,iv_386,vi]	varṇṇānām ānupūrvī vākyam syāt iti āha ānupūrvyāḥ ca varṇṇebhyaḥ bhedaḥ sphoṭena cintitaḥ kalpanā āropitā sā syāt katham vā apuruṣa āśrayā varṇṇebhyaḥ ānupūrvyā bhedaḥ ca sphoṭena cintitena ekatvena hi abhinnasya kramaśas ityādinā cintitaḥ na hi varṇṇebhyaḥ vyatiriktā ānupūrvī kācid upalabhyate abheda pakṣe ca saraḥ rasaḥ iti ādau pratipatteḥ bheda abhāva prasaṅgaḥ prakāra antarasya ca abhāvaḥ tasmāt vastu bhūta ānupūrvyā ayogāt kalpanā āropitā sā syāt tathā ca apuruṣa āśrayā katham ucyate 
[386,vii_386,ix]	katham punar avagamyate dhvaniḥ avaśyam anityaḥ iti āha sattā mātra anubandhi tvāt nāśasya anitya tā dhvaneḥ avināśāt saḥ eva asya vināśaḥ iti ced katham anyorthoni asya nāśoḥ tu kāṣṭham kasmāt na dṛśyate sattā mātra anubandhi tvāt nāśasya dhvaneḥ anitya tā na khalu asatām anyasmāt nāśa utpattiḥ sva hetoḥ eva tu vinaśvara svabhāva tayā utpannāḥ bhāvāḥ vinaśyanti vināśaḥ hi kriyamāṇaḥ bhāvāt vyatiriktaḥ vā bhavet avyatireka pakṣe bhāvaḥ eva kriyate iti syāt tat ca aśakya kriyam utpanna tvāt vyatirekepi agneḥ sakāśāt artha antarasya vināśa ākhyasya utpattau kāṣṭhasya darśanambhavet avināśāt 
[387,i]	saḥ eva agni janmā arthaḥ asi avināśaḥ tena adarśanam iti ced katham anyorthonyasya vināśaḥ yuktaḥ evam hi ati prasaṅgaḥ syāt kāṣṭhe agni kṛtaḥ svabhāvaḥ vināśaḥ na sarve iti ced kāṣṭha vināśayoḥ kaḥ sambandhaḥ na āśraya āśrayi bhāvaḥ niṣetsyamāna tvāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ ced agneḥ api sa vināśaḥ syāt tasya api kāryatvāt tasmāt na bhāva antaram arthasya nāśaḥ astu vā nāśaḥ kāṣṭhañcet apracyuta prācīna svabhāvam kasmāt na dṛśyate 
[387,ii]	nanu yosau artha antara svabhāvaḥ vahni kṛtaḥ sa kāṣṭhasya nāśaḥ nāśa rūpa tayā pratīteḥ vināśaḥ ca abhāvaḥ yaḥ ca abhāvaḥ sa kāṣṭha virodhi rūpaḥ eva kriyate na ca ayam artha antara tvāt ghaṭa vat virodhi rūpa tā kurttum aśakyaḥ na hi ghaṭa vat artha antara tvāt dhūmaḥ agni kāryaḥ na bhavati tasmāt yathā antara rūpa upi dhūmaḥ agninā kriyate tathā virodhi rūpopi vināśīkriyeta yayoḥ ca paraspara parihāreṇa virodhaḥ tayoḥ eka bhāvaḥ eva aparasparasya adarśanam iti katham agni kṛtasya artha antarasya vināśa saṃjñitasya virodhinaḥ bhāve kāṣṭhasya darśanam ucyate 
[387,iii_387,iv]	atra ucyate yosau artha antara svabhāvaḥ nāśaḥ tena saha kāṣṭhasya kaḥ virodhaḥ yadi saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇaḥ sambhāvyatas eva tad bhāvayoḥ nivartti anivarttaka bhāva darśanāt agni śītayoḥ iva kintu bhāva antarasya yadi kāṣṭha vināśaka tvam sa ca nāśaḥ kimartha antara nivṛttiḥ artha antara tve tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ nivṛttiḥ ca niḥsvabhāvāḥ na tatra hetu vyāpāraḥ iti vakṣyate paraspara parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇaḥ ced virodhaḥ evam api atiprasaṅgaḥ yathā kāṣṭhāt bhinnam abhimata padārtha antaram tathā anyat api ghaṭa ādikam iti tat api kāṣṭhasya vināśaḥ syāt nanu yaḥ eva kāṣṭhasya nāśa rūpa tayā virodhi rūpa tayā ca sva hetubhiḥ kriyate saḥ eva nāśaḥ na tu yaḥ kaścid arthaḥ iti katham atiprasaktiḥ 
[388,i]	tat api ayuktam paraspara parihāreṇa hi virodhī nāśaḥ iṣṭam sa ca paraspara parihāraḥ abhimata padārtha vat ghaṭa ādīnām api iti na viśeṣaḥ atha yaḥ eva kāṣṭha nivṛtti rūpaḥ saḥ eva tad nāśaḥ na anyaḥ kim idam nivṛtti rūpa tvam kāṣṭhāt anya tvam nivṛtti mātra ātmaka tvamvā anya tvañced tad itarasya api samānam nivṛtti mātra ātmaka tvañca bhāva antarasya ayuktam svabhāva aviśeṣava tvāt yat utpattau yat nivṛttiḥ sa virodhī nāśaḥ ca iti ced anyā tarhi vināśāt nivṛttiḥ tatra ca samānaḥ sarve eva prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt kāṣṭham svarasa nirodhitayā nivarttate agni kāṣṭha ādi sāmagrayāḥ tu aṅgāra ādikam jāyate iti yuktam artha antara svabhāve tu sati nāśe kāṣṭham kasmāt na dṛśyate iti anivāryaḥ prasaṅgaḥ 
[388,ii_388,iii]	tad parigrahataḥ ced na tena anāvaraṇam yatas vināśasya vināśi tvam tena vināśa ākhyena bhāva antareṇa parigraha tovaṣṭabdha tvāt kāṣṭhā darśanam iti ced na tena bhāva antareṇa kāṣṭhasya anāvaraṇam yatas tatas kāṣṭhasya aparigrahaḥ na hi nāśaḥ vastu āvaraṇam avināśi tva prasaṅgāt na ca pūrva apara eka svabhāvasya varaṇam yuktam iti uktam kiñca 
[388,iv_388,vi]	syāt utpatteḥ tatas punar kāṣṭhasya darśanam bhāva antara bhūtasya nāśasya yadi utpattiḥ iṣyate tadā utpatti liṅgāt vināśi tvam nāśasya syāt ghaṭa ādi vat tatas kāṣṭha nāśasya nāśāt punar kāṣṭha darśanam bhavet hantṛ ghāte caitrāpunarbhavaḥ yathā atra api evam iti ced hantuḥ nna amaraṇa tvataḥ 
[388,vii]	nanu caitrasya hantuḥ vyāghāte kṛte caitrasya punarbhāvaḥ na asti yathā tathā atra api kāṣṭha nāśa nivṛttyā na kāṣṭha punarbhāvaḥ iti ced na hantuḥ amaraṇa tvataḥ na hi hantā maraṇam caitrasya kintu anyaḥ eva indriya āyuḥ nirodhaḥ yena hantṛ maraṇe caitra punar ujjīvana prasaṅgaḥ yadi tu indriya ādi nirodha nivṛttiḥ syāt syāt eva ujjīvanam tat ca tvad mate prāptam nirodhasya utpatti bhāvayoḥ iṣṭaḥ 
[389,i_389,ii]	ananya tve vināśasya syāt nāśaḥ kāṣṭham eva tu tasya asatvāt ahetu tvam na atonyā vidyete gatiḥ atha na bhāvāt bhinnaḥ nāśaḥ kintarhi abhinnaḥ ananya tve vināśasya nāśaḥ kāṣṭham eva tu syāt tasya kāṣṭhasya agni sannidhānāt prāk eva sa tvāt ahetu tvam na aśaka abhimatasya na atas bheda abheda prakārāt anyā gatiḥ utpattimatosti dvidhā api ca nāśa hetu ayogaḥ 
[389,iii_389,iv]	ahetu tvepi nāśasya nitya tvāt bhāva nāśayoḥ sahabhāva prasaṅgaḥ ced asataḥ nitya tā kutas ahetu tvepi nāśasya nitya tvāt ākāśa ādi vat bhāva nāśayoḥ anyonya abhāva svabhāvayoḥ sahabhāva prasaṅgaḥ ced nanu nāśasya asataḥ nīrūpa tvāt nitya tā kutas vastu hi nityam anityam vā syāt yat tu na kiñcid tat katham ucyatām 
[389,v_389,vi]	asatve abhāva nāśi tva prasaṅga upi na yujyate nāśena yasmāt bhāvasya na vināśanam iṣyate atas ca anitya tvāt asatve nāśasya abhāva nāśi tvasya prasaṅga upi na yujyate yasmāt bhāvasya kāṣṭha ādeḥ nāśena hetunā nāśanam na iṣyate yadi hi nāśena nāśaḥ kriyate iti iṣyate tadā nāśa abhāve vastu nāśaḥ na syāt kintu sva hetutaḥ eva bhāvāḥ eka kṣaṇa sthiti dharmāṇaḥ utpannāḥ dvitīye kṣaṇe na bhavanti na tu nāma kaścid bhavati yasya nitya tva anitya tvayoḥ doṣa avakāśaḥ 
[389,vii_390,i]	kathantarhi idānīm ahetukaḥ nāśaḥ bhavati iti ucyate iti āha naśyan bhāvaḥ para apekṣaḥ na tasya jñāpanāya sā avasthā ahetuḥ uktā asyāḥ bhedam āropya cetasā naśyan bhāvaḥ eva kṣaṇa sthiti dharma tayā sva hetoḥ utpatteḥ dvitīye kṣaṇe abhavat na para apekṣaḥ kāraṇa antara nirapekṣaḥ iti tasya kāraṇa antara anapekṣa nāśi tvasya jñāpanāya sā bhāvānām avasthā ahetuḥ uktā ahetukaḥ vināśaḥ bhavati ityādi vacasā eva asyāḥ avasthāyāḥ dharmiṇaḥ sakāśāt bheda antara pratikṣepeṇa cetasā vikalpakena bhedam āropya na tu vastutas nāśaḥ nāma kaścid bhāvāt bhinna svabhāvaḥ bhavati 
[390,ii_390,iii]	svatopi bhāve abhāvasya vikalpaḥ ced ayam samaḥ na tasya kiñcid bhavati na bhavati eva kevalam sva topya bhāvasya bhāve ayantatva anyatva vikalpaḥ samaḥ ced tathā hi yadi bhāvāt bhinna upyabhāvaḥ jñātaḥ bhāvaḥ kim iti na dṛśyate abheda tu bhāvaḥ eva nāśaḥ iti katham naṣṭaḥ atra āha na tasya bhāvasya kiñcid vināśaḥ anyovā bhavati kintarhi saḥ eva kevalam na bhavati vyavaharttavya eka rūpa tvāt tasya tatra ca bheda abheda vikalpān avatāraḥ 
[390,iv_390,vii]	bhāve hi eṣa vikalpaḥ syāt vidheḥ vastu anurodhataḥ hi yasmāt bhāve vikalpaḥ eṣa bheda abheda ātmakaḥ syāt vidheḥ vastu anurodhataḥ nāśaḥ tu prasajya pratiṣedha rūpaḥ niḥsvabhāva tvāt bheda abheda vikalpa akṣamaḥ yadi ca prasajya pratiṣedha ipi vastu antara vidhiḥ tadā paryudāsāt na bhidyeta ubhayatra api vidheḥ prādhānyāt paryudāsaḥ vā na sidhyet eka nivṛttau apara vidhāne sa syāt nivṛtti a siddhau tu katham yuktaḥ na bhāvaḥ bhavati iti uktam abhāvaḥ bhavati iti na yadā ca bhāva nivṛttiḥ vināśa arthaḥ tadā abhāvaḥ bhavati ityādi vākyena bhāvaḥ na bhavati iti uktam abhāvasya bhāva ayogāt atas ca hetuḥ api nāśasya na kaścid 
[390,viii_391,i]	apekṣeta paraḥ kāryam yadi vidyeta kiñcana yat akiñcitkaram vastu kim kenacid apekṣyate yasmāt paraḥ kāraṇa abhimataḥ apekṣya tayadi kiñcana kāryam vidyeta anyathā yat akiñcitkaram vastu tat kenacid kim apekṣyate 
[391,ii_391,iii]	etena ahetuka tvepi hi abhūtvā nāśa bhāvataḥ sattā nāśi tva doṣasya pratyākhyātam prasañcanam etena nāśasya niḥsvabhāva tva kathanena ahetuka tvepi satya bhūtvā nāśasya bhāvataḥ sattā nāśi tva doṣasya prasañjanam ghaṭa ādau iva pratyākhyātam na hi abhāvaḥ nāma kaścid bhavati yasya abhūtvā bhāvāt sattvam nāśitvam vā syāt 
[391,iv_391,v]	yathā keṣāñcid eva iṣṭaḥ pratighaḥ janminām tathā nāśaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhāvānām na anutpattimatām yadi nanu yathā janminām buddhi ādīnām madhye keṣāñcid eva ghaṭa ādīnām pratighaḥ sva deśe vastu antara utpatti vyāghātaḥ iṣṭaḥ na buddhi ādīnām tathā yadi satām utpattimatām eva nāśaḥ svabhāvaḥ syāt na anutpattimatām śabda ākāśa ādīnām tadā katham uktam sattā mātra anubandhi tvāt nāśasya anitya tā dhvaneḥ iti 
[391,vi_392,i]	atra āha svabhāva niyamāt hetoḥ svabhāva niyamaḥ phale na anitye rūpa bheda usti bhedakānām abhāvataḥ hetoḥ svabhāvasya viśiṣṭa kārya utpādana yogya tāyāḥ niyamāt phale kārye svabhāvasya pratigha apratigha ādeḥ niyamaḥ tatas nitya tva abhimata anāñca hetum antareṇa svabhāva niyama ayogāt hetuḥ eṣṭavyaḥ kṛtake punar anitye vā bhāve rūpasya naśvarān aśvarasya bhedaḥ na asti kasmāt iti āha nitya anitya svabhāva tayā kṛtakasya bhedakānām hetūnām abhāvataḥ na hi kaścid eva hetuḥ anityam janayatinā aparaḥ sarveṣām kṛtakānām artha kriyā kāritvāt tasya ca anitya tā vyāpteḥ 
[392,ii_392,iii]	pratyākhyeyā atas eva eṣām sambandhasya api nitya tā sambandha doṣaiḥ prāk uktaiḥ śabda śaktiḥ ca dūṣitā atas sarva bhāva kṣaṇika tva sādhakāt pramāṇāt eva eṣām śabdānām artha sambandhasya api nitya tā pratyākhyeyā sambandhasya vastu tve kṣaṇika tvāt yā ca śabda śaktiḥ yogya tā ākhyā artha pratipatti āśrayaḥ varṇṇyate sā ca śabdāt vyatiriktā eva iti tadvat anityā atha bhinnā tādṛśī ca sambandha doṣaiḥ sambandhi nām a nitya tvāt na sambandhe asti nitya tā ityādinā prāk uktaiḥ dūṣitā iti na punar ucyate 
[392,iv_392,vi]	na tāvat apauruṣā iyam vacanam asti iti uktam bhavatu vā tathā api nā apauruṣeyam iti eva yathā artha jñāna sādhanam dṛṣṭaḥ anyathā api vahni ādiḥ aduṣṭaḥ puruṣa āga sā na apauruṣā iyam iti eva vacanam yathā arthasya avisamvādinaḥ jñānasya sādhanam yasmāt puruṣasya āgasā doṣeṇa aduṣṭopi vahni ādiḥ nīlotpala ādau anyathā apara artha jñāna hetuḥ dṛṣṭaḥ 
[392,vii_392,ix]	kiñca na jñāna hetu tā eva syāt tasmin akṛtake mate nityebhyaḥ vastu sāmarthyāt na ca janma asti kasyacid tasmin śabde akṛtake mate jñāna hetu tā eva na syāt na hi nityebhyaḥ vastu sāmarthyāt kārya janma aśakteḥ kasyacid jñānasya anyasya vājanma asti krama ākramayoḥ vyāpakayoḥ nityāt nivṛtteḥ tat vyāpyasya sāmarthyasya abhāvāt 
[392,x_392,xii]	tasmāt vikalpa vāsanā udbhūtāḥ samāropita gocarāḥ jāyante buddhayaḥ tatra kevalam na artha gocarāḥ tatra anitya ātmani uccarite śabde anādi antena vikalpane citta santatau āropitāyāḥ vāsanāyā vikalpikā buddhayaḥ jāyante samāropita gocarāḥ kalpita artha viṣayāḥ na artha gocarāḥ na sva lakṣaṇa viṣayāḥ tathā artha tve śabda pramāṇa antara vaiphalyasya ukteḥ 
[394,i_394,iv]	nanu mithyātvam kṛtakeṣu eva dṛṣṭam iti akṛtam vacaḥ satya artham vyatirekasya virodhi vyāpanāt yadi hetau asambhave bhāvaḥ tat tasya api śaṅkyate viruddhānām padārthānām api vyāpaka darśanāt mithyātvam artha śūnya tvam kṛtakeṣu eva vākyeṣu dṛṣṭam iti akṛtam vacaḥ satya artham yadi syāt tadā kaḥ doṣaḥ kasmāt evam iti āha paraḥ akṛtaka tvasya sādhanasya virodhinā kṛtaka tvena sādhya viparyayasya mithyātvasya vyāpanāt atra āha vipakṣān mithyā tvāt akṛtakasya hetoḥ asaṃbhave asaṃbhava nimittam hetau bādhaka pramāṇe anukte tasya akṛtaka tvasya api mithyātve vipakṣe bhāvaḥ śaṃkyate bādhaka pramāṇa adarśanāt nanu mithyātvam kṛtakeṣu dṛṣṭam tat akṛtakeṣu virodhiṣu katham syāt iti āha viruddhānām api hi vyāpyānām padārthānām ekasya vyāpakasya darśanāt yathā prayatna anantarīyaka tvayoḥ ekena kṛtaka tvena anitya tvena vā vyāptiḥ 
[394,v_395,i]	kiñca na asattā siddhiḥ iti uktam sarvatonupalambhanāt asiddha āyāma sattāyām sandigdhā vyatirekitā sarvatas vipakṣāt hetoḥ asattāyāḥ anupalambhāt pratibdham antareṇa na siddhiḥ iti uktam prāk na ca adarśana mātreṇa vipakṣe avyabhicārita ityādinā asiddhāyām vāsatyāyām vipakṣāt vyatirekitā sandigdhā kasmāt punar vyatireka niścaya apekṣā na hi sādhana tayā upāttaḥ dharmam iti eva sādhanam 
[395,ii_395,iv]	kintarhi anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ vā sattvam vā sādhya dharmiṇi tad niścaya phalaiḥ jñānaiḥ siddhyanti yadi sādhanam anvayaḥ sa pakṣevyatirekaḥ vipakṣāt sādhya dharmiṇi satvam vā tad niścaya phalaiḥ anvaya ādi niścaya prayojanaiḥ jñānaiḥ pramāṇa ātmabhiḥ yadi sidhyanti tadā sādhanam bhavati niścita trairūpyasya eva hetu tvāt 
[395,v_395,vii]	yat api vyatirekī hetuḥ iti uktam tat ca ayuktam iti āha yatra sādhya vipakṣasya varṇṇate vyatirekitā saḥ eva asya sa pakṣaḥ syāt sarvaḥ hetuḥ ananvayī yatra dharmiṇi sādhya vipakṣasya mithyātvasya sādhana avipakṣa vyatirekāt vyatirekitā varṇṇyate yat kṛtakam na bhavati tat mithyārthañca na bhavati iti saḥ eva sādhya sādhana viparyaya nivṛtti darśana viṣayaḥ dharmī sa pakṣaḥ syāt asya akṛtaka tvasya hetoḥ viparyaya niṣedhena vidheḥ eva pratipādanāt yatra ca sādhya sādhana sattava niścayaḥ saḥ eva pakṣaḥ atas sarvaḥ hetuḥ ananvayī na kevala vyatirekī 
[395,viii_396,ii]	nanu pakṣasya vedasya katham sa pakṣatā sa pakṣa lakṣaṇa yogāt evam tarhi sarvaḥ pakṣaḥ sa pakṣaḥ syāt bhavati eva kim anyena iti ced anyasya api lākṣaṇikam tat katham tyajyatām kiñca samaya tve hi mantrāṇām kasyacid kārya darśanam kiñcid kārya kāriṇaḥ mantrāḥ apauruṣeyāḥ ca iti vyāhatam tathā hikasya cit satya tapaḥ prabhāvataḥ puṃsaḥ samaya tve saṃketa tve mantrāṇām abhyupagamyamāne kāryasya mantra prayoga niṣpaādya tvena iṣṭasya sādhanam siddhiḥ syāt kenacid śakti viśeṣavatā mad praṇītam mantram evaṃprayuñjānasya ayam arthaḥ setsyati iti samayasya kṛta tvāt siddhiḥ syāt kavi samaya ādi vat kāvya apāṭhakasya artha siddhiḥ atha api bhāva śaktiḥ syāt anyathā api aviśeṣataḥ atha api bhāva śaktiḥ sādṛśya pauruṣeyāṇām syāt yayā abhimata siddhiḥ evantar hi anyathā prayuktepi mantre syāt abhimatam aviśeṣatas varṇṇa ātmakasya mantrasya 
[396,iii_396,v]	varṇṇānām krama viśeṣaḥ mantraḥ tatas tad grahaṇena phalam iti ced kramasya artha antara tvañca pūrvam eva nirākṛtam nittyam tad artha siddhiḥ syāt asāmarthyam apekṣyate kramasya varṇṇebhyaḥ artha antara tvañca pūrvam eva nirākṛtam varṇṇa ānupūrvī vākyan cet itya trāntare astu vā kramaḥ tasya nitya tvāt tad arthasya tat niṣpādyasya arthasya nityam siddhiḥ syāt na hi avikale kāraṇe kārya kṣepaḥ yuktaḥ atha prayoga vidhāna ādi apekṣā asti sā api ayuktā apekṣaṇe kasyacid sahakāriṇaḥ asāmarthyam svabhāvataḥ syāt samarthasya anya apekṣā ayogāt apekṣaṇīyāt samartha svabhāva utpattau tu syāt apekṣā 
[396,vi_397,ii]	kiñca sarvasya sādhanam te syuḥ bhāva śaktiḥ yadīdṛśī mantrāṇām bhāva śaktiḥ yat īdṛśī kārya viśeṣa sādhikā tadā sarvasya yajamānasya itarasya ca te mantrāḥ abhimata artha siddheḥ sādhanam syuḥ na hi kārya kāritā teṣām kañcid eva prati na itarān sādhāraṇa tvāt bhāva svabhāvasya atha prayoktuḥ viśeṣam apekṣya phala prāyāḥ tat ca asat prayoktṛ bheda apekṣā ca na asaṃskāryasya yujyate prayoktuḥ bhedaḥ yajamāna tvam tad apekṣā ca nityasya paraiḥ asaṃskāryasya na yujyate 
[397,iii_397,iv]	saṃskāryasya api bhāvasya vastu bhedaḥ hi bhedakaḥ prayoktṛ bhedāt niyamaḥ śaktau na samaye bhavet saṃskāryasya api bhāvasya vastunaḥ saṃskarttuḥ bhedaḥ hi bhedakaḥ bhavitum arhati na tu brāhmaṇa śūdra ādīnām vastutas jāti bhedaḥ kaścid asti vyavahāra mātra tvāt tasya tatas ca prayoktuḥ bhedāt api mantrāṇām śaktau niyamaḥ na sambhavati nanu upalabhyate niyatā mantrāṇām śaktiḥ satyam upalabhyate kintu sā puruṣa kṛte samaye abhyupagamyamāne bhavet na tu akṛta tve yaḥ hi brāhmaṇaḥ iti prasiddhaḥ tasya eva ayam vidhi prayuktaḥ mantraḥ phala pradaḥ na itarasya iti kartrā puruṣeṇa śakti viśeṣavatā samita tvāt mantrasya 
[397,v_397,vii]	kiñca anādheya viśeṣāṇām kiṃkurvāṇaḥ prayojakaḥ prayogaḥ yadi abhivyaktiḥ sā prāk eva nirākṛtā nityānām anādheya viśeṣāṇām prayoktā puruṣaḥ kiṃkurvāṇaḥ prayojakaḥ iṣṭaḥ anupakārakasya prayojaka tve sarvasya tathā tva prasaṅgāt yadi abhivyaktiḥ prayogaḥ ucyate sā abhivyaktiḥ nityānām prāk eva sāmānya prastāve nirākṛtā na hi svarūpa pariṇāmaḥ āvaraṇa vigamaḥ vā sa anityātām ghaṭate 
[397,viii_398,i]	buddhiḥ kadācid sambhāvyate tadā vyaktiḥ ca buddhiḥ sā yasmāt sa phalaiḥ yadi yujyate syāt śrotuḥ phala saṃbandhaḥ vaktā hi vyakti kāraṇam tad vyaktiḥ ca buddhi rucyeta sāyasmāt vaktu rbhavati sa pha lena yujyate yadi tadā na ati prasaṅgaḥ nanvem api śrotuḥ phala sambandhaḥ syāt na vaktuḥ eva vaktā hi vyakteḥ jñānasya kāraṇam iti phale yujyate tat ca jñāna hetu tvam śrotuḥ api asti eva 
[398,ii_398,iv]	kiñca anabhivyakta śabdānām karaṇānām prayojanam manojapaḥ vā vyarthaḥ syāt śabdaḥ hi śrotra gocaraḥ anabhivyaktaḥ aniveditaḥ śabdaḥ yaiḥ teṣām karaṇa ādīnām prayojanam prayogaḥ yadā tadā tālu ādi karaṇa praspanda mātrayā upāṃśu japaḥ kriyate na tu vyaktam ucyate yadā ca tām api vinā manaḥ mātreṇa manojapaḥ vā kriyate tadā dvau api japau imau vyarthaḥ syātām śabdaḥ hi śrotra gocaraḥ ucyate na ca japayoḥ anayoḥ śrotra gocaraḥ kaścid asti 
[398,v_399,i]	pāramparyeṇa tad ja tvāt tad vyaktiḥ sā api ced matiḥ te tathā syuḥ tad arthā ced asiddham kalpanā anvayāt nanu yā api upāṃśu manojapa kāle śabda ābhāsā dhīḥ sā api matiḥ pāramparyeṇa tad ja tvāt tasya vyaktiḥ iti ced yadi evam śabda avikalpavat artha vikalpāḥ api tad prabhavāḥ iti tepi tathā śabda vyaktayaḥ syuḥ paraḥ na kevalāt śabda prabhava tvāt tad vyaktiḥ kintu tad arthā śabda viṣayā sati iti ced na ca artha vikalpaḥ śabda viṣayaḥ śabda vikalpasya śabda viṣaya tvam asiddham kalpanāyāḥ vācya vācaka yojanāyāḥ anvayāt sambandhāt na ca kalpanā vastu viṣaya iti kathyate 
[399,ii_399,iv]	asmākantu mate sva sāmānya svabhāvānām eka bhāva vivakṣayā ukteḥ samaya kāṇṇām avirodhaḥ na vastuni sva sāmānya svabhāvānām śabda sva lakṣaṇa sāmānya lakṣaṇānām pratyakṣa vikalpa buddhi viṣayāṇām ekatva adhyavasāya vaśāt eka bhāvasya ekatvasya vivakṣayā samaya kārāṇām samaya karttṛbhiḥ śaktimat puṃbhiḥ mantrāṇāmukteḥ avirodhaḥ upāṃśu japa manojapayoḥ vaiphalya virodha abhāvaḥ dṛśya vikalpyau eka adhyavasāyāt eka kārya kāri tvena adhiṣṭhita tvāt tat kurutaḥ ye tu vastu bhūtam mantram icchanti teṣām virodhaḥ eva tat āha na vastuni virodha abhāvaḥ na hi upāṃśu japa ādi viṣayaḥ vastu kalpita tvāt 
[400,i_400,iii]	atha tvad matepi ānupūrvyām asatyām syāt saraḥ rasaḥ iti śrutau na kārya bhedaḥ iti ced asti sā puruṣa āśrayā ānupūrvyā varṇṇa vyatiriktāyām asatyām saraḥ rasaḥ iti prasiddha anuloma viloma kramāyām śrutau kāryasya sva jñānasya bhedaḥ na syāt iti ced asti asmad mate sa ānupūrvī puruṣa āśrayā puruṣa kṛtā pratipadaṃbhinnā tatas na jñāna bheda prasaṅgaḥ 
[400,iv_400,vi]	tathā hi yaḥ yad varṇa samutthāna jñāna jāt jñānataḥ dhvaniḥ jāyate tad upādhiḥ sa śrutyā samavasīyate yaḥ dhvaniḥ jāyate tad varṇṇa samutthaḥ jñānataḥ yaḥ ca asau varṇṇaḥ ca yat varṇṇaḥ tasya samutthānam kāraṇam tat ca tat jñānañca yat varṇṇa samutthāna jñānam tasmāt jātam yat varṇṇa samutthāna jñāna jam tasmāt jñānam atas ayam arthe ādyasya varṇṇasya yat samutthāpakam vivakṣā ātmakam jñānam tena samanantara pratyayena satā dvitīya varṇṇa samutthāpakam jñānam janyate tena ca dvitīyaḥ varṇṇaḥ evam dvitīya varṇṇa samutthāpakāt jñānāt tṛtīya varṇṇa itthāpaka jñāna utpattau tṛtīya varṇa utpattiḥ iti kāraṇa kramāt varṇa utpatti kramaḥ uktaḥ punar kārya krameṇa kramam darśayitum āha saḥ uttaraḥ varṇaḥ tad upādhiḥ pūrṇa varṇa viśeṣaṇaḥ tad anantaraḥ iti arthaḥ śrutyā śravaṇa jñānena grāhya varṇa kāryeṇa śrotṛ santāna varttinā samavasīyate krama utpannāḥ varṇāḥ sva sva janita jñānaiḥ asahabhāvinaḥ eva gṛhyante 
[400,vii_401,ii]	nanu krama bhāvinām saha darśana abhāvāt katham pūrva varṇṇa upādhi grahaṇam iti āha tad jñāna janita jñānaḥ sa śrutau apaṭu śrutiḥ apekṣya tad smṛtim paścāt smṛtim ādhattaḥ ātmani tasya pūrva varṇasya jñānena grāhakeṇa uttara varṇṇa sahakāriṇā janitam grāha kaṃjñānam yasmin sa tat jñāna janitaḥ uttaraḥ varṇṇaḥ mandam uccāryamāṇa tvāt śrutau śravaṇa jñāne apaṭa śrutiḥ manda cāri śravaṇa jñānaḥ tasya pūrva varṇṇasya smṛtim apekṣya ātmani smṛtim pūrvavaṇa nintara tvena ādhatte yasmāt pūrva varṇa anantara tvena uttaraḥ smaryate tasmāt tad anantaraḥ eva asau gṛhītaḥ iti arthaḥ 
[401,iii_401,iv]	iti eṣā pauruṣeyī eva tad hetu grīhi cetasām kārya kāraṇa tā varṇe hi ānupūrvī iti kathyate iti evam uktena krameṇa varṇṇeṣu krama bhāviṣu tad hetu cetasām varṇṇa utthāpaka cetasāṃvaktṛ santāna vartinām tad grāhi cetasām varṇṇa grāhaka cetasām śrotṛ santāna vartinām kārya kāraṇa tā eṣā yathāyogam varṇṇa apekṣā kramavatī kāraṇa tā kārya tā ca ānupūrvī kathyate sā ca puruṣa nirvarttya tvāt pauruṣeyī eva 
[401,v_401,vi]	anyat eva tatas rūpam tad varṇṇānām pade pade karttṛ saṃskārataḥ bhinnam sahitam kārya bheda kṛt yatas na nitya tvam tatonyat eva varṇṇānām tad rūpam pade pade pratipadam eka adhyavasāya viṣaya tvepikarttṛ saṃskārataḥ varṇṇa samutthāpaka citta śakti bhedāt jātam bhinnam krameṇa ca anubhūya smṛtyā sahitam smṛtam sat kārya bheda kṛt artha pratipatti viśeṣa kāri 
[402,i_402,ii]	sā ca ānupūrvī varṇṇānām tad hetu grāhi cetasām icchā aviruddha siddhīnām sthiti krama virodhataḥ kārya kāraṇa tā siddheḥ puṃbhyaḥ varṇa kramasya ca sarvaḥ varṇa kramaḥ puṃbhyaḥ dahana indhana yukti vat sā ca varṇānām ānupūrvī tad hetu grāhi cetasām racanā kṛtaḥ puruṣāt pravṛttā iti na sthita kramāḥ varṇāḥ puruṣa icchayā aviruddha siddhīnām varṇṇānām sthitasya kramasya virodhāt na hi sthita kramāṇām himavat vindhya malayānām icchayā viparīta kramaḥ śakyaḥ varṇṇāḥ tu icchayā viparyyāsyante vikalpa krama anuvidhāyi tvāt ca tadvat kalpita upyarthaḥ na pramāṇam kārya kāraṇa tāyāḥ siddheḥ sarvaḥ vaidikaḥ anyaḥ ca varṇṇa kramaḥ puṃbhyaḥ bhavati iti avadhāraṇam dahana indhana yukti vat yathā ekasya dahanasya indhana pūrvakatva dṛṣṭyā sarvaḥ agniḥ indhana pūrvaḥ iti nyāyaḥ 
[402,iii_402,iv]	asādhāraṇa tā siddhā puṃsām ca krama kāriṇām atas jñāna prabhāvābhyām anyeṣām tad abhāvataḥ atas eva ca mantra ākhya varṇṇa krama kāriṇām puṃsām jñāna prabhāvābhyām puruṣa antaraiḥ sahāsa ādhāraṇa tā asamāna tā asiddhā anyeṣa antayoḥ jñāna prabhāvayoḥ abhāvataḥ 
[402,v_403,i]	nanu tantra jñāḥ ratthāpuruṣāḥ api mantram kiñcid kārya samartha praṇayantaḥ dṛśyante tatas mantra karaṇāt na atiśaya siddhiḥ iti āha yepi mantra vidaḥ kecid mantrān kāṃścana kurvate prabhoḥ prabhāvaḥ teṣām sa tad ukta nyāya vṛttitaḥ yapi kecid sādhāraṇāḥ mantra vidaḥ mantra śāstra jñāḥ kāṃścana mantrān viṣa ādi śamanān kurvate teṣām prabhoḥ mantra praṇetuḥ atiśayita śakteḥ sa prabhāvaḥ sāmarthyaṃtat uktasya nyāyasya samaya anuṣṭhāna ādeḥ vṛttitaḥ ārādhitasya prabhoḥ prabhāva ādī dṛgak śakti lābhaḥ iti arthaḥ 
[403,ii_403,iv]	tasmāt kṛtakaḥ pauruṣeyāḥ ca mantrāḥ vācyāḥ phala īpsunā aśakti sādhanam puṃsām anena eva nirākṛtam kṛtakāḥ pauruṣeyāḥ ca mantrāḥ vācyāḥ phala īpsunā sarveṇa yena puruṣāḥ śakti viśeṣavantaḥ mantrān praṇetum īśate anena eva mantra ādi praṇayanam prati puṃsām aśakti sādhanam yat kim api mī mām sa kaiḥ iṣṭam tad nirākṛtam boddhavyam 
[403,v_403,vii]	etat eva sphuṭayitum āha buddhīndriya ukti puṃstva ādi sādhanam yat tu varṇyate pramāṇa ābham yathārtha asti na hi śeṣavataḥ gatiḥ buddhīndriya ukti puṃstva ādi sādhanam śakti viśeṣa nirākaraṇam yat tu varṇyate tat pramāṇa ābham anaikāntikam na hi buddhimataḥ ekasya śakti viśeṣaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ iti anyasya api tathā abhyāsa adhīnaḥ hi prakarṣaḥ guṇeṣu tad abhilāṣāt abhyāsopi sambhavī dṛśyate ca prajñā ādi guṇānām atiśayitaḥ prakarṣaḥ iti buddhimatu ādya sādhanam na hi śeṣavataḥ liṅgāt yathārtha anumeyasya gatiḥ bhavitum arhati 
[403,viii_404,i]	api ca puruṣa atiśayam anicchatām jaiminīyānām mahat duḥśliṣṭam tathā hi arthoyam na ayam arthaḥ naḥ iti śabdāḥ vadanti na kalpyoyam arthaḥ puruṣaiḥ te ca rāga ādi saṃyutāḥ ayam arthaḥ asya śabdasya ayam na iti na tāvat śabdāḥ svayam vadanti tasmāt puruṣaiḥ ayam arthaḥ kalpaḥ te ca rāga ādi yuktāḥ na avadhāraṇa paṭavaḥ 
[404,ii_404,iii]	saḥ ekaḥ tattva vipnna anyaḥ iti bhedaḥ ca kiṃkṛtaḥ tadvat puṃstve katham api jñānī kaścid katham na vaḥ atha rāgiṣu api kaści jjaiminyādiḥ jānāti eva tatra ekaḥ tattva vid anyaḥ na iti bhedaḥ ca kiṃkṛtaḥ eṣaḥ rāgi tva aviśeṣāt sarve eva ajñaḥ prāptaḥ na vā kaścid atha puruṣa tvasāmya īpi jaiminī ādiḥ atīndriya artha darśi tvāt vaidika śabdānām atīndriya artha sambandha vettā kalpyate tadā puṃstve sati api kaścid anyopi jñānī jñāna atiśayavān katham api abhyāsa ādinā tadvat jaiminya ādi vat katham vaḥ mīmāṃsakānām nābhimataḥ 
[404,iv_404,vi]	syāt etat na vayam puruṣa pramāṇyāt vyākhyānam anumanyāmahe kintu pramāṇam avisaṃvādi vacanam sortha vid yadi na hi atyanta parokṣeṣu pramāṇasya asti sambhavaḥ yasya pramāṇam avisamvādi vacanam sa ūrtha vid veda artha jñātā yadi iṣyate nanu atyanta parokṣeṣu veda artheṣu pramāṇasya sambhavaḥ na hi kasyacid asti tat katham samvādāt artha vid vyavasthāpyate 
[404,vii_404,ix]	api ca yasya pramāṇa saṃvādi vacanam tat kṛtam vacaḥ saḥ āgamaḥ iti prāptam nirarthā apauruṣeya tā yasya pramāṇa samvādi vacanam sa yadi vyākhyātā tadā samvādaḥ āgama lakṣaṇam iti tena saṃskṛtam vacaḥ āgamaḥ iti prāptam iti nirarthā apauruṣeya tā vedānām kalpitā 
[405,i_405,iii]	tathā yadi atyanta parokṣerthe anāgama jñāna sambhavaḥ atīndriya artha vid kaścid asti iti abhimatam bhavet yadi atyanta parokṣerthe svarga sambandha ādau jaimini ādeḥ anāgamasya āgama nirapekṣasya jñānasya sambhavaḥ tadā atīndriya artha darśīkaścid asti iti abhimatam bhavet tatas tad pratikṣepaḥ na yuktaḥ 
[405,iv_405,vi]	yadi tu na kaścid atīndriya artha darśī tadā svayam rāga ādimān na artham vetti vedasya na anyatas na vedayati veda upi veda arthasya kutas gatiḥ svayam rāga ādimān pumān vedasya artham na vetti na ca anyatas anyasya api rāga ādimatve ajñāna tvāt veda upi sva artha na vedayati tatas ca kutas veda arthasya gatiḥ na kutaścid iti puruṣāḥ eva yathāpratibham kalpayeyuḥ 
[405,vii_405,viii]	tena agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti śrutau khādet śava māṃsam iti eṣa na arthaḥ iti atra kā pramā tena agnihotram juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ iti śrutau veda vākye śva māṃsam svādet iti eṣa na arthaḥ iti atra kā pramā iti api kalpayitum śakya tvāt 
[405,ix_405,x]	prasiddhaḥ lokavādaḥ ced tatra koti indriya artha dṛś aneka artheṣu śabdeṣu yena arthoyam vivecitaḥ agniḥ dāha ādi samarthaḥ tasmin ghṛta ādi prakṣepaḥ ca havanam iti prasiddhaḥ lokavādaḥ tatas na anya artha kalpanā iti ced tatra loke rāga ādimati kaḥ atīndriya artha dṛś asti yena aneka artheṣu aneka artha abhidhāna yogyeṣu śabdeṣu ayam abhimata ūrthaḥ vivecitaḥ vācya tayā viśeṣaṇa vyavasthāpitaḥ yadi dāhaka dravye ghṛta prakṣepasya svargeṇa sambandhaḥ śva māṃsa bhakṣaṇena ca na asti iti kena api dṛṣṭam syāt syāt ayam artha vivekaḥ tad darśī tu rāga ādima tvāt kaścid neṣṭaḥ iti na asti viparīta kalpanā nirāsaḥ 
[406,i_406,iii]	na ca loka prasiddha anusārāt veda artha vyavasthā tathā hi svarga uḥ vaśya ādi śabdaḥ ca dṛṣṭaḥ rūḍha artha vācakaḥ śabda antareṣu tādṛkṣu tādṛśyeva astu kalpanā svarga urvaśya ādi śabdaḥ ca ārūḍha artha vācakaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ manuṣya atiśāyi puruṣa viśeṣa niketaḥ atimānuṣa sukha adhiṣṭhānaḥ nānā upakāraṇaḥ svargaḥ tad sthā apsarāḥ urvaśī iti prasiddhaḥ loka vādaḥ tam ullaṃdhya duḥkhena asambhinnā niratiśayā prītiḥ svargaḥ urvaśī ca araṇiḥ pātrī vā iti aprasiddha artha kalpanā iti śabda antareṣu agnihotra ādiṣu tādṛkṣu sarva artha yogyeṣu tādṛśi eva aprasiddha arthā eva kalpanāḥ tu nyāyasya tulya tvāt 
[406,iv_406,vi]	kiñca prasiddhaḥ ca nṛṇām vādaḥ pramāṇam sa ca na iṣyate tatas ca bhūyortha gatiḥ kim etat dviṣṭha kāmitam prasiddhaḥ ca nṛṇām vādaḥ eva na tu anyathā kācid sa ca puruṣa pravarttita tvāt pramāṇam na iṣyate bhavatā bhūyas punar tatas janavādāt arthasya gatiḥ iti kim etat dviṣṭhakāmitam lokavādaḥ apramāṇa tvāt dviṣṭhaḥ saṃprati kāmyate iti vyaktaḥ virodhaḥ 
[406,vii_406,viii]	atha prasiddhim ullaṃdhya kalpane na nibandhanam prasiddheḥ apramāṇa tvāt tad grahe kim nibandhanam atha lokasya prasiddhim ullaṃdhya śva māṃsa bhakṣaṇa ādi artha kalpane na nibandhanam asti nanu prasiddheḥ apramāṇa tvāt tasyāḥ grahe kim nibandhanam vicārakasya na kiñcid 
[406,ix_407,i]	kiñca utpāditā prasiddhyā eva śaṅkā śabda artha niścaye yasmāt nānā artha vṛtti tvam śabdānām tatra dṛśyate prasiddhyā eva śabda artha niścaye viparīta artha kalpanāyā śaṅkā utpāditā yasmāt nānā artha vṛtti tvam śabdānām gavākṣa prabhṛtīnām tatra prasiddhau dṛśyate 
[407,ii_407,iv]	tathā anyathā sambhava abhāvāt nānā śakteḥ svayam dhvaneḥ avaśyam śaṅkayā bhāvyam niyāmakam apaśyatām nānā śakteḥ aneka artha pratipādana yogyasya dhvaneḥ svayam ātmanā anyathā sambhavasya eka artha pratipādana yogyatā sambhavasya asambhavāt avaśyam artha antara śaṅkayā bhāvyam katham iti āha niyāmakam apaśyatām aneka arthasya śabdasya eka vṛtti niyama kāraṇam apaśyatām puṃsām 
[407,v_407,vii]	kiñca eṣa sthāṇuḥ ayam mārgaḥ iti vakti iti kaścana anyaḥ svayam bravīmi iti tayoḥ bhedaḥ parīkṣyatām svayam artha pratipādana śūnyaḥ netā anabhimata artha dyotaka tvena pratipādayan karttuḥ nnabhidyate tasya api evam vyāpāra tvāt yathā kenacid kaścana panthānam pṛṣṭhe āha na aham jāne kintu sthāṇuḥ eṣa vakti ayam mārgaḥ iti anyaḥ punar pratyāha aham svayam bravīmi ayam mārgaḥ iti tayoḥ evam vādinoḥ pratipādaka tvasya bhedaḥ parīkṣyatām ekaḥ nirabhiprāya vacanam vaktṛ tvena vyapadiśati anyaḥ tu na iti vacana vaidagdhyam eva anayoḥ bhidyate na upadeśa pravṛtti nivṛttī tathā svayam artha pratipādayatā upi veda artha viśeṣa abhidhāyinaḥ abhidadhat karttaṃva vācaka tāyāḥ 
[407,viii_408,i]	atha tad artha pratipādane yogyāḥ eva śabdāḥ nanu evam sarvatra yogyasya eka artha dyotane niyamaḥ kutas jñātāḥ vā ati indriyāḥ kena vivakṣā vacanāt ṛte sarvatra arthe yogyasya śabdasya eka artha dyotene niyamaḥ kutas jātaḥ puruṣaḥ ced niyāmakaḥ na bhavati syāt etat pratiniyatāḥ eva arthāḥ teṣām na te puruṣeṇa niyamyante evam api jñātāḥ vai atīndriyāḥ pratiniyatāḥ arthāḥkena puruṣeṇa rāga ādimatā vivakṣāyāḥ prakāśakāt vacanāt pratipādanāt ṛte na hi vedeṣu kasyacid vivakṣā asti tad avagatim antareṇa ca pratiniyata artha tā na śakyā boddhum na hi śabdāḥ svayam sva artha niyamam kathayanti saṃketam antareṇa sa ca pauruṣeyaḥ na ca artha niyama avagamam vinā saṃketa karaṇam artha niyama pratītiḥ ca vinā saṃketam na asti iti vyaktam itaretara āśraya tvam 
[408,ii_408,iv]	api ca vivakṣā niyame hetuḥ saṅketaḥ tad prakāśanaḥ apauruṣeye sā na asti tasya sā ekārtha tā kutas vivakṣā arthasya niyame hetuḥ saṃketaḥ tad prakāśanaḥ artha niyama bodhanaḥ apauruṣeye ca vede sā vivakṣā na asti puruṣa prayojya tvāt tasyāḥ tatas tad prasādhyā sā ekārtha tā vedasya kutas 
[408,v_408,vii]	atha svabhāva niyamenyatra na yojyeta tayā punar saṅketaḥ ca nirarthaḥ syāt vyaktau ca niyamaḥ kutas svabhāvataḥ śabdāḥ kvacid arthe niyatāḥ tadā svabhāva niyame anyatra arthe vācaka tvena tayā vivakṣayā na yojyeta punar na hi svabhāvena pratiniyata aviṣayonyathā kartum śakyate saṃketaḥ ca nirarthaḥ syāt svabhāva pratiniyame sati na hi cakṣuḥ indriyam rūpa grahaṇa pratiniyatam tatra saṅketam apekṣate saṅketāt vācaka tāya avyakta aviṣyamāṇāyām niyamaḥ kutas ayam eva asya śabdasya arthaḥ iti niyamaḥ na yujyate puruṣa adhīna saṅketa apekṣāyām 
[408,viii_409,ii]	tathā hi yatra svātantryam icchāyāḥ niyamaḥ nāma tatra kaḥ dyotayet tena saṅketaḥ na iṣṭām eva asya yogyatām yatra puruṣasya svātaḥ ntryam icchāyāḥ tatra niyamaḥ nāma kaḥ saṅgataḥ tena icchā adhīna tvena saṃketaḥ na iṣṭām eva yogya tām uddyotayet anabhimatām api vyañjayet iti arthaḥ tat evam apauruṣeya tvam āgama lakṣaṇam bruvāṇā mī mām sa kāḥ pratikṣiptāḥ 
[409,iii_409,v]	saṃprati vṛddhamīmāṃsakānām matam dūṣayitum utthāpayati yasmāt kila īdṛśam satyam yathā agniḥ śītanodanaḥ vākyam veda eka deśa tvāt anyat api aparaḥ avravīt yathā vaidikam vākyam agniḥ himasya bheṣajam iti satyam śītanodana tvena vahneḥ pramāṇa siddha tvāt tathā annyat api vākyam agniṣṭomena juhuyāt svarga kāmaḥ ityādi veda eka deśa tvāt satyam iti aparaḥ mī mām sa kaḥ abravīt uktavān kila śabdaḥ akṣamāyām 
[409,vi_409,vii]	rasavat tulya rūpa tvāt eka bhāṇḍe ca pāka vat śeṣavat vyabhicāri tvāt kṣiptam nyāya videdṛśam īdṛśam anumānam śeṣavat anaikāntikam vyabhicāri tvāt nyāya vid ācārya di gnāge na pratikṣiptam rasavat tulya rūpa tvāt svādita phalena tulya rūpa tvāt phala antarasya tādṛś rasa anu māna vat eka bhāṇḍa antarga tvāt dṛṣṭa pāka taṇḍula anumāna vat na hi etādṛśasya hetoḥ sādhya pratibandha usti viparyaya bādhaka pramāṇāt iti vipañcitam prāk 
[410,i_410,ii]	dṛśyate ca bahutara viṣaye visamvādaḥ vedasya katham ekasatya tayā sarvatra tathātvam tathā ca nityasya puṃsaḥ kartṛ tvam nityān bhāvān ati indriyān aindriyān viṣamam hetum bhāvānām viṣamām sthitim nivṛttim ca pramāṇābhyām anyat vā vyasta gocaram viruddham āgama apekṣeṇa anumānena vā vadat virodham asamādhāya śāstra artham ca apradarśya saḥ satya artham pratijñānānaḥ jayet dhāṣṭaryena bandhakīm 
[410,iii^1]	paraiḥ anādheya viśeṣasya puṃsaḥ ātmanaḥ krama janmasu karma ādiṣu kartṛ tvam vadat śāstram tathā nityān bhāvān diś kāla ākāśa ādīn artha kriyā rahitān sataḥ vadat vastutas atīndriyān guṇa karma sāmānya ādīn aindriyān pratyakṣān vadat tathā bhāvānām viṣamam hetum prāc ajanakam vadat tathā viṣamām sthitim niṣpannānām bhāvānām āśraya vaśena sthitim vadat nivṛttiñca viṣamām svatas anaśvara svabhāvānām anya kṛtām nivṛttim vadat anyat vāvastu vyasta gocaram pramāṇābhyām pratyakṣa anumānābhyām nirasta avakāśam vadat 
[410,iii^2]	āgama apekṣeṇa āgama siddha liṅga trairūpyeṇa anumānena ca viruddham agni hotra snāna ādeḥ pāpa śamanam vadat na hi rāga ādi prabhavaḥ dharmaḥ tad apanayanam antareṇa snāna ādeḥ nivṛttim arhati evamvidha visamvāda bhājam artham vadat śāstram virodham prāmāṇikam asamādhāya aparihyatya pravṛtti kāmocitam śāstra artham anuguṇa upāyam puruṣa artha lakṣaṇañcā pradarśya sa jara nmī mām sa kaḥ eka deśa samvāda darśanāt satya artham pratijānānaḥ dhārṣṭyena bandhakīm sākṣāt dṛṣṭa vyalīkām sva patim sva śīla prāmāṇya udbhāvanena bhrāntam āvedayantīm jayet 
[411,i_411,iii]	kiñca sidhyet pramāṇam yadi evam apramāṇam atha iha kim na hi ekam na asti satya artham puruṣe bahu bhāṣiṇi yadi evam dṛṣṭa eka deśa samvādasya avayava tvāt anyat api pramāṇam sidhyet atha iha nyāye kim apramāṇam śāstram bhaviṣyati na hi bahu bhāṣiṇi puruṣe satya artham ekam vace na asti kintu asti eva tena eva dṛṣṭāntena tat vacanam pramāṇam syāt 
[411,iv_411,v]	na ayam svabhāvaḥ kāryam vā vastūnām vaktari dhvaniḥ na ca tad vyatiriktasya vidyatevyabhicāritā na ayam dhvaniḥ vastūnām svabhāvaḥ kāryam vā yasmāt vaktari dhvaniḥ bhavati na hi vastunaḥ svabhāvonyatra dharmiṇi varttate kāryamvā anyatas bhavitum arhati na ca tat vyati riktasya kārya svabhāvābhyām aparasya avyabhicāritā vidyate iti niveditam 
[411,vi_411,viii]	syāt etat pravṛttiḥ vācakānāñca vācya dṛṣṭi kṛtā iti ced paraspara viruddha arthā katham ekatra sā bhavet vācakānām śabdānām pravṛttiḥ vācya dṛṣṭi kṛtā abhidheya darśana āgatā tatas paraṃparayā tat kāryatā eva eṣām iti ced evam tarhi sā śabda pravṛttiḥ ekatra vastuni paraspara viruddha arthā katham bhavet 
[412,i_412,iii]	yadi yathā vastu eva śabdaḥ tadā vastutas eka rūpeṇa śabde nityaḥ kim ayam anityaḥ vā ityādi śabda sandarbhaḥ na bhavet vastubhiḥ na āgamāḥ tena kathañcid na antarīyakāḥ pratipattuḥ na sidhyanti kutas tebhyaḥ artha niścayaḥ tena pratibandha abhāvena vastubhiḥ saha na antarīyakāḥ āgamā pratipattuḥ artham śabdāt pratipadyamānasya kathañcid na sidhyanti tat kutas tebhyaḥ āgama artha niścayaḥ 
[412,iv_412,v]	tasmāt na tad nivṛttyā api bhāva abhāvaḥ prasidhyati tena asat niścaya phalā anupalabdhiḥ na sidhyati yasmāt pravarttamānāt āgamāt na asti artha siddhiḥ tsmāt tasya āgamasya nivṛttyā api bhāvasya abhāvaḥ na sidhyati tena pramāṇa traya nivṛtti lakṣaṇā api anupalabdhiḥ arthānām asat niścaya phalā na sidhyati tatas yuktam uktam sat asat niścaya phalā na iti syāt vā apramāṇa tā iti sat vyavahāra sādhane ca adhikṛte vyavasthitā iti avasthitam 
[413,i_413,ii]	sva artha anumānam vyākhyāya para artha anumānam vyākhyātum āha tatra para artha anumānam sva dṛṣṭa artha prakāśanam iti ācāryīyalakṣaṇam svena dṛṣṭaḥ sva dṛṣṭaḥ sva dṛṣṭaḥ ca asau arthaḥ ca iti tri rūpaḥ hetuḥ tasya prakāśanam vacanam anumāna hetu tvāt iti arthaḥ 
[413,iii_413,v]	nanu trirūpa liṅga ākhyānam iti eva astu kim sva dṛṣṭa grahaṇena iti śaṅkāyām para mata nirāsa artha tām asya darśayitum āha parasya pratipādya tvāt adṛṣṭopi svayam paraiḥ dṛṣṭa sādhanam iti eke tad kṣepāya ātma dṛś vacaḥ parasya para artha anumānena pratipādya tvāt sādhana vādinā svayam adṛṣṭā upi pramāṇena paraiḥ prativādibhiḥ āgamāt dṛṣṭa sādhanam liṅgam iti eke sām khyāḥ te hi sukha ādīnām utpattimatvāt anityāt acetana tvam rūpa ādīnām iva bauddham pratyāhuḥ na hi asate utpattimatvam sataḥ ca niranvaya vināśaḥ anitya tvam hetuḥ sāṃkhya asiddhaḥ bauddhasya punar āgamāt siddhaḥ tāvatā eva hetuḥ iti manyante tasya para matasya kṣepāya pratiṣedhāya ātma dṛśra vacaḥ adṛṣṭa vacanam sūtre na prativādi mātra siddhasya hetu tvam kintu ubhaya siddhasya evati arthaḥ 
[414,i_414,iii]	na ca āgamāt prativādinā upi sādhana siddhiḥ yuktā iti vaktum āha anumāviṣaye na iṣṭam parīkṣita parigrahāt vācaḥ prāmāṇyam asmin hi na anumānam pravartate anumānasya vastu bala pravṛttasya viṣaye yasmāt anumāna jñānam utpadyate sa ca trirūpaḥ hetuḥ tatra pratipādye vācaḥ āgama ātmikāyāḥ prāmāṇyam na iṣṭam artha pratibandha abhāvāt iti uktam 
[414,iv]	kiñca pramāṇa antara samvādāt parīkṣitasya pramāṇa upapannasya āgama arthasya parigrahāt svīkārāt na iṣṭam vacana prāmāṇyam yadi vacanam iti eva pramāṇanta dā pratijñāpadāt eva sādhyasya siddheḥ niṣphalam hetu dṛṣṭanta ādi vacanam syāt pramāṇa antara samvāda apekṣā ca na bhavet samvāda jñānasya eva artha bhāva anuvidhāyi tvāt tasmin āgama arthe prāmāṇyam vacanasya tu viparyayāt yadi tu āgamaḥ iti eva pramāṇam tadā pramāṇa antara samvāda apekṣā na syāt hi yasmāt asmin āgama arthe pramāṇa pratipādita tvāt niścite anumānam na pravṛrttate yadi hi āgama arthaḥ sandihyeta tadā tad niścaya arthā pramāṇa antara vṛttiḥ apekṣyeta 
[414,v_414,vi]	bādhanāya āgamasya ukteḥ sādhanasya param prati sopramāṇam tadā asiddham tat siddham akhilantataḥ yadi ca āgamasya sukha ādi caitanya pratipādakasya bādhanāya sādhanasya utpattimatu ā ādeḥ sām khye na param bauddham pratyuktiḥ tatas kāraṇāt saḥ āgamaḥ apramāṇam tadā na hi pramāṇasya bādhaḥ yuktaḥ tatas āgama aprāmāṇyāt tena āgamena sākṣāt pāraṃparyābhyām siddham utpattimatu a ādi sādhyam ca ācaitanyam akhilam idam asiddham 
[414,vii_414,viii]	tat āgamavataḥ siddham yadi kasya kaḥ āgamaḥ bādhyamānaḥ pramāṇena sa siddhaḥ katham āgamaḥ sa ca sukha ādi utpattimatva pratipādakaḥ āgamaḥ ca tad āgamaḥ tadvataḥ tad sambandhinaḥ bauddhasya siddham utpattimat tva ādi liṅgam iti ced kasya puruṣasya kaḥ āgamaḥ sambandhī na tāvat avayavat āgamopi puruṣasya sahaja sambandhena sambaddhaḥ na api yukti upapanna yata upādhinā pratyakṣa anumāna vat sambandhaḥ tathā hi pramāṇena utpattimatu ā ādi liṅga jena anumānena āgama pratipāditasya sukha ādi caitanyasya bādhanāt bādhyamānaḥ āgamaḥ hetuḥ sa katham āgama siddhaḥ yena yukti samvāda upādhinā api puruṣeṇa sambandham anubhavet 
[415,i_415,iii]	syāt etat sukha ādīnām acaitanyam tena eva āgamena pradeśa antare darśitam atas abādhya tvāt pramāṇāt asmāt sādhana vidhiḥ yuktaḥ iti āha tad viruddha abhyupagamaḥ tena eva ca katham bhavet tad anya upagame tasya tyāga aṃgasya apramāṇa tā tasmāt caitanyāt pratipāditāt viruddhasya ācaitanyasya abhyupagamaḥ tena caitanya pratipādakena eva ca āgamena katham bhavet sambhave vā viruddha artha abhidhāyi tvena apramāṇāt āgamāt hetu siddhiḥ ayuktā eva āgama pratītena utpattimat tva ādinā tasmāt āgama ukta caitanyāt anyasya ācaitanyasya upagame svīkāre vā prativādīnā kriyamāṇe tasya āgamasyatyāgāṃgasya apramāṇa tā abhyupagatā syāt yadā eva āgama prāmāṇyasya bādhake hetau ādriyate tadā eva tatra saṃśayitaḥ na ca apramāṇāt hetu siddhiḥ 
[415,iv_415,vi]	kiñca tat kasmāt sādhanam na uktam sva pratotiḥ yat udbhavā yuktyā yayā āgamaḥ grāhyaḥ parasya api ca sā na kim ayamvādī tāvat svayam pratītam eva ācaitanyam parasmai pratipādayati va ca sādhanam antareṇa eva pratītiḥ tatas pratipādayituḥ svasya pratītiḥ caitanya viṣayāḥ yasmāt sādhanāt udbhavaḥ yasyāḥsā yat udbhavā tad sādhanam svāgama ādikam kasmāt pratipādyam prati na uktam svayam pratipanna sāmarthyam eva sādhanam vaktum ucitam tathā niryuktikasya āgamasya aprāmāṇyāt yayā yuktyā upapannaḥ āgamaḥ sādhana tvena gāhyaḥ vādinā sā yuktiḥ parasya pratipādyasya api kinna sādhanayena tat parityajya anyat apramāṇa siddham utpatti ādi ucyate 
[415,vii_416,ii]	atha yoga bala jena pratyakṣeṇa sukha ādīnām acaitanyam pratītam na tat anyathā pratipādayitum parasya śakyate iti para upagatam sādhanam ucyate nanu tathā api na akasmikaḥ buddhi sukha ādya caitanya viṣayasya niścayaḥ tad sākṣāt kāri pratyakṣa tad sādhana yoga anuṣṭhānayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāva avadhāraṇañca avaśya karttavyam tat niścayam antareṇa yoga anuṣṭhāna ayogāt tathā ca prākṛtasya sataḥ prāk yaiḥ pratipatti akṣa saṃbhavau sādhanaiḥ sādhanāni artha śakti jñānesya tāni alam 
[416,iii]	prākṛtasya arvāk darśanasya sataḥ yaiḥ sādhanaiḥ sukha ācaitanya ādi viṣayam tad grāhi pratyakṣa tad sādhanayoḥ sambandhañca niścitya pravṛttasya upāye pratipattuḥ anuṣṭhānasya tad phalasya akṣasya pratyakṣasya ācaitanya ādi viṣaya grāhiṇaḥ sambhavau bhavataḥ tāni sādhanāni arthasya upāya abhyāsasya śakteḥ acaitanya grāhi pratyakṣa janikāyāḥ jñāne karttavye asya pratipādyasya alam samarthāni tatasyāni eva sādhanāni ucyantām kim svayam adṛṣṭa sādhya pratipādana sāmarthyena utpattimatu ā ādinā uktena 
[416,iv_416,vi]	syāt etat pratyakṣasya ācaitanya ādi viṣayasya yoga ādi abhyāsena saha sādhya sādhana sambandhaḥ viprakṛṣṭātvāt sāmānya ākāreṇa api na pratīyate tatosya anupadarśanam iti āha vicchinna anugamāḥ yepi sāmānyena api agocarāḥ sādhya sādhana cintā asti na teṣu artheṣu kācana yepi vicchinnaḥ viprakṛṣṭaḥ anugamaḥ sambandhaḥ yeṣām te pratyakṣa tad upāya ādayaḥ sāmānyena aviśeṣa ākāreṇa api agocarāḥ teṣu artheṣu idam sādhanam idam sādhyam iti ca sādhya sādhana cintā kācana na asti tatas arvāk darśanasya abuddhi viṣayīkṛtayaḥ rūpayoḥ upaya upeyayoḥ ekatra anuṣṭhānau aparatra niṣpādanam iti kutas 
[416,vii_416,ix]	kiñca apramāṇakāt āgamāt icchā mātreṇa pratipādyaḥ hetum kurvan punar icchayā tam eva pariharan hetu tad ābhāsayoḥ icchā adhīna tām svīkuryāt iti ākhyātum āha puṃsām abhiprāya vaśāt tattva atattva vyavasthitau luptau hetu tad ābhāsau tasya vastu asamāśrayāt puṃsām abhiprāya vaśāt icchā anurodhāt tattvā tattvayoḥ hetu tad ābhāsa tvayoḥ vyavasthita āviṣyamāṇāyām hetu tad ābhāsau luptau syātām avyavasthita tvāt tasya puruṣa abhiprāyasya vastu asaṃśrayāt yathāvastu pravṛtti niyama abhāvāt 
[417,i_417,iii]	api ca san arthaḥ jñāna sāpekṣaḥ na āsan jñānena sādhakaḥ satopi vastu asaṃśliṣṭā asaṃgatyā sadṛśī gatiḥ san arthaḥ jñāna sāpekṣaḥ sādhya sādhakaḥ pratītaḥ yathā dhūma ādiḥ na āsannarthaḥ jñānena pratīti mātreṇa sādhakaḥ sādhyasya yathā kalpitaḥ dhūmaḥ atha ācaitanyam vastutosti eva tat yathā kathañcid parasmai pratipādanīyam atas para abhyupagataḥ hetuḥ kriyate iti āha sa topya caitanyasya vastu asaṃśliṣṭā vastu bhūta liṅga apratibaddhā gatiḥ asaṅgatyā asataḥ pratītyā sadṛśī samyak pratīta tva abhāvat anyetu asat gatyā doṣavat pratītyā sadṛśī iti vyācakṣate teṣām sa topya vastu kṛtā pratipattiḥ asat pratipattim na atiśete apratyaya tvāt iti viniścaya granthena saha eka vākyatā na syāt 
[417,iv_417,vi]	kiñca liṅgam svabhāvaḥ kāryam vā dṛśya adarśanam eva vā sambaddham vastutassiddham tat asiddham kimātmanaḥ liṅgam sādhya artha sambaddham na anyat vyabhicārāt tat ca svabhāvaḥ kāryam dṛśya adarśanam anupalabdhiḥ eva anyasya pratibandha abhāvāt iti uktam tad utpatti ādikam yadi triṣu hetuṣu antarbhūtam tadā vastutas paramārthataḥ siddham pratipādyasya kim kasmāt ātmanaḥ sāṃkhyasya vādinaḥ asiddham utpattimatu ādi svabhāva hetuḥ syāt sa ca dharmi grāhakāt pramāṇāt anyatas vā śiṃśapātva vat kṛtaka tva ādi vat arthān prativādinaḥ iva vādinā api sidhyet 
[417,vii_417,x]	atha trividhe hetau na antar bhavati utpatti ādi tadā pareṇa api anyatas gantum ayuktam pareṇa prativādinā api trividhāt hetoḥ anyatas hetoḥ acaitanyam gantum pratyetum ayuktam yadi para abhyupagama siddham asādhanam tadā prasaṅga hetuḥ ahetuḥ syāt iti āha para kalpitaiḥ prasaṅgaḥ dvaya sambandhāt eka apāyeni ahānaye 
[418,i]	para kalpitaiḥ sādhanaiḥ prasaṅgaḥ kriyate yathā sāmānyasya para upagata aneka vṛtti tvāt aneka tvam āpādyate na tu ayam pāramārthikaḥ hetuḥ trairūpya abhāvāt yadi ayam na hetuḥ tadā kimartham ucyate iti āha dvayoḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ sambandhāt vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvāt sphāritāt ekasya sādhyasya apāye anyasya sādhanasya hānaye yathā ca anekaṃsāmānyam tasmāt na aneka vṛtti iti viparyaya prayoge sādhya abhāve sādhana abhāvaḥ kathyate prasaṅga viparyayotra maulaḥ hetuḥ sādhya sādhanya vyāpti grāhaka pramāṇa smārakaḥ tu prasaṅge prayogaḥ iti arthaḥ bhinna deśa kāla ādiṣu anekāsu vyaktiṣu vṛttasya tad atad deśa tva ādi viruddha dharma adhyāsāt aneka tva siddheḥ aneka vṛtta tva aneka tvayoḥ vyāpti siddhiḥ boddhavyā 
[418,ii_418,v]	uktam sva dṛṣṭa grahaṇasya sāphalyam artha grahaṇasya idānīm vaktavyam adṛṣṭa artha prakāśanam iti atra sūtre yat upāttam tad artha grahaṇam śabda kalpanā āropita ātmanām aliṅga tva prasiddhi artham arthāt arthasya siddhitaḥ tad artha grahaṇam śabdena kalpanayā ca āropitaḥ ātmā yeṣām pakṣa sa pakṣa anyatara tva ādīnām teṣām aliṅga tva prasiddhi artham boddhavyam kasmāt punar kalpitasya aliṅga tvam iti āha arthāt vastu bhūtāt liṅgāt arthasya sādhyasya siddhitaḥ 
[418,vi_418,ix]	kalpanā āgamayoḥ karttuḥ icchā mātra anuvṛttitaḥ vastunaḥ ca anyathā bhāvāt tad kṛtāḥ vyabhicāriṇaḥ kalpanāyāḥ āgamasya śabdasya ca karttuḥ puruṣasya icchā mātrasya anuvṛtti tonurodhāt vastunaḥ ca anyathā bhāvāt karttuḥ icchā anuvṛtteḥ tābhyām śabda kalpanābhyām kṛtāḥ hetavaḥ vyabhicāriṇaḥ na aikāntikāḥ uktam artha grahaṇa prayojanam sva dṛṣṭa artha prakāśana śabdena trirūpa liṅga vacanam iṣṭam na pakṣa vacanam api iti vaktavyam 
[419,i_419,iv]	yadi sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa vā pakṣa vacanam sādhya prattipattau upayujyate tadā ucyeta kintu etat na asti iti āha arthāt artha gateḥ śaktiḥ pakṣa hetu abhidhānayoḥ na arthe tena tayoḥ nna asti svatas sādhana saṃsthiti sākṣāt tāvata pakṣa abhidhānasya hetu abhidhānasya ca pratipādye arthe śaktiḥ na vidyate kim kāraṇam iti āha arthāt vacana pratipādyāt artha sādhyasya gateḥ na vacanāt tena sākṣāt artha pratipādaka tva abhāvena tayoḥ pakṣa hetu abhidhānayoḥ svatas sva rūpeṇa sādhana saṃsthitiḥ sādhana tva vyavasthāḥ nāstiyataḥ ca pakṣa vacanam sākṣāt arthe na pramāṇam 
[419,v_419,vi]	tat pakṣa vacanam vaktuḥ abhiprāya nivedane pramāṇam saṃśaya utpatteḥ tatas sākṣāt na sādhanam tat tasmāt pakṣa vacanam vaktuḥ abhiprāya nivedane pramāṇam śabda prāmāṇyam ācāryasya vadataḥ abhimatam iti boddhavyam tad pakṣa vacanāt sādhyertha saṃśaya utpatteḥ aniścayāt na sākṣāt sādhanam arthasya tat 
[419,vii_420,i]	paraṃparayā sādhya sādhanāt pramāṇam pakṣa vacanam vaktuḥ abhiprāya nivedane pramāṇantarhi syāt iti āha sādhyasya eva abhidhānena pāraṃparyeṇa na api alam śaktasya sūcakam hetu vacaḥ aśaktam api svayam pāramparyeṇa api pakṣa vacana malam samartham na sādhya siddhau sādhyasya eva kevalasya abhidhānāt na hi pakṣa vacasā sādhakam kiñcid ucyate sādhya mātrasya eva abhidhānāt trirūpasya hetoḥ vacaḥ vacanantu svayam sākṣāt siddhau aśaktam api śaktasya trirūpa liṅgasya sūcakam pratipādakam iti sādhanam ucitam 
[420,ii_420,v]	nanu ācāryasya pakṣa vacanam asādhana tvena iṣṭam iti katham jñāyate iti āha hetu artha viṣaya tvena tad aśakta uktiḥ īritā śaktiḥ tasya api ced hetu vacanasya pravṛrttanāt hetoḥ arthaḥ sādhyaḥ sa viṣayosya iti hetu artha viṣayaḥ tatvena sādhya artha upadarśaka tvena tasya pakṣa vacanasya sādhya sādhanam pratyaśaktasya uktiḥ īritāḥ nirdiṣṭa ācāryeṇa tatra anumeya nirdeśaḥ hetu artha viṣayaḥ mataḥ iti anena granthena tatas jñāyate pakṣa vacanam asādhanam iṣṭam ācāryasya iti nanu tasya pakṣa vacanasya api sādhya siddhau śaktiḥ asti tad sādhakasya hetu vacanasya pravarttanāt na hi anuddiṣṭerthe sādhana prastāvaḥ tatas sādhana prastāvanā hetu tvena pakṣa vacanasya sādhaka tvam asti iti ced evam 
[420,vi_421,i]	tad saṃśayena jijñāsoḥ bhavet prakaraṇa āśrayaḥ tasya sādhya saṃśayena jijñāsā tasya añca satyām sādhanam ucyate iti jijñāsoḥ puṃsaḥ saṃśayaḥ jijñāsā ca prakaraṇasya sādhana prastāvasya āśrayaḥ nimittam iti bhavet sādhanam pakṣa vacana vat nanu saṃśaya jijñāse pratipādya pravartite pakṣa vacanantu vā ādi pravartitam tat katham tad samudāyasya sādhanasya vādinā nirdeśa saṃbhavaḥ iti āha vipakṣa upagamepi etat tulyam iti anavasthitiḥ 
[421,ii]	evantarhi vipakṣasya sādhya viruddhasya dharmasya upagame para abhiprāyeṇa nitya śabdaḥ iti sādhya nirdeśa kṛte pārśva sthānām tathā saṃśaya nirāsa artham yat kṛtakam tat anityam yathā ghaṭaḥ kṛtakaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti punar vādinā eva ucyate tadā nitya tva pratijñāyāḥ tat anitya tva avi abhicāri kṛtaka tva hetu pravarttaka tvam tulyam iti nitya tva pratijñāpi anitya pratijñāvat sādhanam syāt iti anavasthitiḥ sādhana avayavānām 
[421,iii_421,v]	yatas ca pakṣa vacanasya sādhya siddhau sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa vā sāmarthyam na asti tatas antaraṅgam tu sāmarthyam triṣu rūpeṣu saṃsthitam tatra smṛti samādhānam tad vacasi ā iva saṃsthitam antaraṅgam sāmarthyam tu śabdaḥ avadhāraṇe bhinnakramaḥ ca iti triṣu eva pakṣa dharmatā ādiṣu rūpeṣu saṃsthitam tatra trirūpa liṅge sādhya sādhana śakti smṛteḥ samādhāna m āropaṇaṃtad vacasi trirūpa liṅga pratipādaka vacanaḥ eva saṃsthitam atas tat eva pāramparyeṇa sādhya siddheḥ aṅga tvāt pramāṇan na pakṣa vacanam 
[421,vi_421,viii]	nanu akhyāpite hi viṣaye hetu vṛtteḥ asaṃbhavāt viṣaya khyāpanāt eva siddhau ced tasya śakta tā uktam atra akhyāpite apratipādite sādhanasya viṣaye sādhye hetoḥ vṛtteḥ eva hi asambhavāt tasya pakṣa vacanasya viṣaya khyāpanāt eva sādhyasya siddhau pāramparyeṇa śakta tā iti ced uktam atra saṃśaya jijñāsayoḥ api sādhana pravṛrttaka tvāt sādhana tva prasaṅgaḥ iti 
[421,ix_421,xi]	kiñca vinā api asmāt kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ īdṛśāḥ sarve anityāḥ iti proktā ipi arthāt tat nāśadhoḥ bhavet asmāt pakṣa vacanāt vinā api kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ īdaśāḥ ye kṛtakāḥ te sarve anityāḥ iti pakṣa dharma tā vyāpti vacane proktā ipi arthāt tasya śabdasya nāśadhīḥ bhavet anitya tva avi abhicāri kṛtaka tvam śabde varttamānam anitya tām tatra gamayati eva iti niṣphalam pakṣa vacanam 
[422,i_422,iii]	tasmāt anuktau api pakṣasya siddheḥ apratibandhataḥ triṣu anyatama rūpasya eva anuktiḥ nyūna toditā pakṣasya anuktau api sādhya siddheḥ apratibandhataḥ avirodhāt tri pakṣa dharmatā ādiṣu rūpeṣu anyatamasya ekasya anuktiḥ nyūna toditā sādhana doṣaḥ na tu pakṣa ādya vacanam 
[422,iv_422,vi]	yadi ca pratijñā sādhanam iṣyate tadā sādhya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā iti pratijñā lakṣaṇam ati vyāpi syāt asiddhasya hetoḥ dṛṣṭāntasya ca asiddhasya sādhya tvam sādhana tvañca asti iti pratijñā artham syāt yasya tu mate pratijñā na sādhanam sādhya uktim vā pratijñām sa vadan doṣaiḥ na yujyate sādhana adhikṛteḥ eva hetvābhāsā prasaṅgataḥ sa sādhyoktim sādhya nirdeśam pratijñām vadan anantara uktaiḥ doṣaiḥ na yujyate sādhana adhikṛteḥ sādhana tvena adhikāra deva pratijñā arthasya hetvābhāseṣu aprasaṅgataḥ
[422,vii_422,ix]	yasmāt aviśeṣa uktiḥ api eka jātīye saṃśaya āvahā anyathā sarva sādhya ukteḥ pratijñātvam prasajyate aviśeṣa uktiḥ sāmānya abhidhānam api eka jātīye saṃśaya āvahā tattva artha śaṅkā upa adhikā na sarvatra iti nyāyaḥ tatas asādhanam eva sādhyam pratijñā na tu asiddha hetu dṛṣṭānta ādikam tasya sādhana tvena iṣṭa tvāt anyathā yadi evam na abhyupagamyate tadā sarvasyāḥ sādhya ukteḥ ghaṭam karoti iti ādeḥ pratijñātvam prasajyate jñāpaka hetu adhikārāt tad sādhyasya eva pratijñātvam na kāraka hetu sādhyasya iti ced yadi evam asādhana bhūta sādhya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā na sādhana nirdeśaḥ iti siddham 
[423,i_423,iii]	syāt etat siddha ukteḥ sādhana tvāt ca parasya api na duṣyati idānīm sādhya nirdeśaḥ sādhana avayavaḥ katham parasya api siddha ukteḥ siddhārtha pratipādaka tvāt sādhana tvāt ca pratijñā tvam iṣṭam atas hetvābhāsa ādi pratijñātva prasaṅgena na duṣyati hetvābhāsa ādyasiddha tvāt asādhanam aṃsa adhana tvāt ca na pratijñā idānīm asmin abhyupagame sādhya nirdeśaḥ asiddha tvāt sādhana avayavaḥ katham na hi pratijñā arthaḥ siddhaḥ tad artham eva sādhana upanyāsāt asiddhaḥ ca na sādhanam hetvābhāsa vat 
[423,iv_423,vi^1]	yā ca sva yūthyānām pūrva pakṣa parihāra uktiḥ sa ābhāsokya ādi upakṣepa parihāra viḍambanā asambaddhā tathā hi eṣa na nyāyyaḥ iti sūcitam pakṣa vacanam sādhanam sa ābhāsa artha tvāt iti ced na pratyakṣeṇa anekāntāt pratyakṣam sa ābhāsam api na kasyacid pramāṇasya sādhanam vacana ātma tve sati sābhāsa tvāt sādhana tvam iti ced na dūṣaṇena anekāntāt dūṣaṇam sa ābhā saṃvacana ātma tvepi na sādhanam itisā api sa ābhāsa uktiḥ ādiḥ yasya tausā bhāsa ukti ādī upakṣepa parihārau tau eva viḍamvanā ayukta tayā atas eva āha asambaddhā tathā hi sābhāsa tvasya viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa bhāvāt eva ahetu tvāt asambandhaḥ pūrva pakṣaḥ tatas tam anumatya pratyakṣeṇa anekānta tā pādanam aśobhanam punarvacana ātma tvam viśeṣaṇam para uktam apratikṣipya
[423,vi^2]	dūṣaṇa ābhāsena anekānta tā āpādanam ca ayuktam tat eva hi hetoḥ viśeṣaṇam upayuktam yat vipakṣāt hetum vyāvarttayati na ca vacana ātma tvā asādhana tvayoḥ kaścid virodhaḥ yena asādhanāt vacana ātma tva nivṛtteḥ viśeṣaṇa sāphalyam syāt tathā hi eṣa vipakṣāt avyāvarttaka hetu viśeṣaṇa upanyāsaḥ na nyāyyaḥ iti varṇṇi taṃprāk veda nitya tā sidhyarthaṃmadhyayana pūrvakam iti ukte bhārata adhyayanena anekānta tām āpāditām pratiṣeddhum veda adhyayana tve satī iti viśeṣaṇam mī mām sa kena upanyastam tat api kṛti pūrvakam bhārata adhyayana vat syāt na kaścid virodhaḥ tatas vipakṣāt avyāvarttakam viśeṣaṇam ayuktam iti uktam prāk 
[424,i_424,iii]	nanu yadi pakṣa vacanam asādhanam sāmarthya gamyā abhidheyañca tad ācāryeṇa pakṣa lakṣaṇam kṛtam kimartham iti āha gamya artha tvepi sa adhya ukteḥ asaṃmohāya lakṣaṇam tad catur lakṣaṇam rūpa nipāteṣu svayam padaiḥ sādhya vyāpta pakṣa vacana sāmarthyāt gamya artha tvepi sādhya ukteḥ pakṣa vacanasya lakṣaṇam uktam asaṃmohāya vipratipatti nirākaraṇena sādhya pratipatti artham tathā hi ātma artha tvam sādhyam api sām khyāḥ asādhyam ācakṣate para artha tvam asādhyam api sādhyam iti santi vipratipattayaḥ tat ca sādhyam catur lakṣaṇam uktam sva rūpeṇa eva nirdeśyaḥ svayam iṣṭaḥ anirākṛtaḥ pakṣaḥ iti atra lakṣaṇa catuṣṭaya pratipādakaiḥ rupa nipāteṣu svayam padaiḥ yathākramam 
[424,iv_424,v]	asiddha asādhana artha ukta vādi abhyupagata grahaḥ anuktā upīcchayā vyāptaḥ sādhye ātma arthavat mataḥ asiddhasya asādhanasya artha uktasya vādi abhyupagatasya grahaḥ asiddha svabhāva tvāt sādhyasya na siddhasya grahaṇam tatas siddham cākṣuṣa tva ādi rūpa ādeḥ na sādhyam nipātā eva kārakaraṇena asādhanasya grahaṇam tatas cākṣuṣa tva ādi asiddham api sādhana tvena śabdebhidhīyamānam na sādhyam dṛṣṭa śabdena artha uktasya api grahaṇam tatas anuktam api ātma artha tvam saṃghāta tvāt cakṣuḥ ādeḥ sāṃkhyasya sādhyam svayam śabdena vādi abhyupagatasya grahaṇam tatas śāstra abhyupagatasya ākāśa guṇa tva ādeḥ śabde dharmiṇi vādinā anitya tve sādhayitum ārabdhe asādhyatā alpa vaktavyatayā artha uktasya tāvat sādhyatām samarthayitum āha vādinaḥ anukta upīcchayā vyāptaḥ sādhyaḥ mataḥ ātma artha vat yathā ātmā asti na vā iti vivāde tad sādhana artham sām khye na para arthāḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ saṃghāta tvāt śayana āsana ādi aṅga vat iti uktasya sādhanasya ātma artha tvam anuktam api sādhyam icchā viṣaya tvāt 
[425,i_425,iii]	nanviṣṭa śabdena aniṣṭasya sarvasya nirāsāt śāstra upagatasya api vādya niṣṭhasya asādhya tvam siddham tad niṣphalam svayaṃpadam iti āha vyavaccheda phala tvāt śabdānām iṣṭa śabdāt sarvānyeṣṭa nivṛttau api āśaṅkā sthāna vāraṇam vṛttau svayaṃśrutena āha kṛtā ca eṣā tad arthikā sarvasya vādinaḥ anyena śāstra udinā iṣṭasya nivṛttau siddhāyām api śāstreṇa iṣṭam vādinā upīṣṭam eva iti śaṅkā sthānasya vipratipatti viṣayasya vāraṇam phalam svayaṃśrutena ācāryaḥ vṛttau āha svayam iti śāstra anapekṣam abhyupagaman darśayati evā svayaṃśrutiḥ tad arthikā vipratipatti nirākaraṇa arthā kṛtā 
[425,iv_425,vi]	yaḥ eva icchayā viṣayīkṛtaḥ sa viśeṣaḥ tad vyapekṣa tvāt kathitaḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ anuktau api vāñchāyā bhavet prakaraṇāt gatiḥ viśeṣaḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ sambandhī vyapekṣatvāt icchā racitāt sambandhāt sādhya tvena kathitaḥ cakṣuḥ ādīnām saṃhata viṣayam pārārthyam iti dharmasya viśeṣaḥ sādhyaḥ para arthasya sādhya tvāt para arthāḥ santaḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ asaṃhata arthāḥ iti dharmiṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ sādhyaḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ aneka aṇu sañcaya ātmikāḥ krameṇa eka kālañca saṃhatāḥ jñāna ādi tu kāla bhedena aneka tvāt saṃhatāni teṣām para arthānām satām asaṃhata viṣaya tvam eva icchā viṣaya tvāt sādhyam ātmanaḥ sarva kālam eka tve na asaṃhata tvāt katham punar ātma artha tvasya anuktau tad viṣayāyāḥ vāñchāyāḥ pratītiḥ iti āha vāñchāyāḥ anuktau api mukhyam śabdena prakaraṇāt ātmā asti na asti iti saṃśaye sati tad sādhana upanyāsa prastāvāt gatiḥ pratītiḥ bhavati 
[426,i_426,iii]	ātma artha tvasya vivāde kaḥ doṣaḥ iti āha ananvaya upi dṛṣṭānte doṣaḥ tasya yathā uditam ātmā paraḥ ced saḥ asiddhaḥ iti tatra iṣṭa ghāta vat tasya icchā viṣayasya ātma artha tvasya sādhyān anvayaḥ dṛṣṭānte doṣaḥ api śabdāt vakṣyamāṇaḥ iṣṭa vidhātaḥ ca yathā uditam ācārya vasu bandhunā para arthāḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ iti atra paraḥ ced ātmā vivakṣitaḥ saḥ asiddhaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti tatra anvaye sati iṣṭa vidhāta vat sādhanam iṣṭa ātma artha tva viparyayeṇa anvayāt tad sādhaka tvāt 
[426,iv_426,vi]	atha ātma artha tva na sādhyam iti āha sādhanam yat vivāde na nyastam tat ced na sādhyate kim sādhyam anyathā aniṣṭam bhavet vaiphalyam eva vā yasya ātmanā urthasya vivāde asti na asti iti sandehe na sādhanam nyastam upanyastam tat ced na sādhyate kim idānīm sādhyam syāt anyathā vivāda viṣayaḥ yadi na sādhyam tadā aniṣṭam viparyaya siddhiḥ syāt yathā vyutpanna sarva śabda vādinam pratyavyutpanna saṃjñā śabda vādinā tad arthavatu a siddhi artham sādhanam ucyate 
[426,vii_427,i]	saṃjñi sambandhāt prāc arthavat śabda rūpam vibhakti darśanāt tad anya śabda vat iti atra gacchati iti gauḥ iti eka artha samavāyāt kriyā upalakṣitena bāhya sāmānyena arthavān go śabdaḥ siddhaḥ avyutpanna vādinaḥ na tu sva rūpa mātreṇa arthena arthavān artha mātra jañca sādhya tvena uddiṣṭam na tu sva rūpeṇa arthena arthava tvam tatas dṛṣṭānte vibhakti antasya vākya arthava tvena vyāpti siddheḥ devadatta ādau api pakṣīkṛte saṃjñā śabde devaiḥ dattaḥ devadattaḥ iti vākya arthava tvam svarūpa arthava tve viruddham sidhyati athavā iṣṭasya sādhya tva abhāve para arthāḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ saṃhata tvāt iti atra ātma artha tvasya asaṃhata pāra arthyasya asādhya tvāt jñāna hetu tvena saṃhata pāra arthasya bauddhena api īṣṭe sādhana vaiphalyam eva vā syāt 
[427,ii_427,iv]	sa dvitīya prayogeṣu niranvaya viruddhate etena kathite sādhyam etena sādhya tvena iṣṭasya ananvaya doṣa darśanena sa dvitīya prayogeṣu cā rvā kakṛteṣu yathā abhivyakta caitanya śarīra lakṣaṇa puruṣa sadvitīyaḥ ghaṭaḥ anutpanna tvāt kuḍya vat iti śarīram eva abhivyakta caitanyam puruṣaḥ na ātmā kaścid para lokī tena sa sahāyat tvam ghaṭasya sādhyate iti prayoga phalam tatra ca niranvaya viruddhate kathite tathā hi abhivyakta caitanya deha lakṣaṇa puruṣeṇa sa dvitīya tvam sādhyam tena ca kuḍyenu ayaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ iti niranvayatā ghaṭasya tu kuḍye anvayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti tena sa dvitīya tva sādhanāt viruddha tā syāt sāmānyena atha sammatam tat eva artha antara abhāvāt dehān āptau na sidhyati vācya śūnya pralapatām tat etat jāḍya varṇṇitam 
[427,v]	atha sāmānyena viśeṣam anullikhya sa dvitīya tvam sādhyam kuḍye sa dvitīya tva mātreṇa anvayāt evam api tat sāmānyam eva na sidhyati prativādinaḥ ghaṭāt abhivyakta caitanya svabhāvatayā artha antara abhāvāt artha antara tva asambhavāt dehasya anāptau artha antara tvena asiddhau dvayoḥ bhinnayoḥ anyatarasa dvitīya tvam sāmānyam syāt na hi ghaṭaḥ svarupeṇa eva anyatarasa dvitīyaḥ dehantu nābhi vyakta caitanya lakṣaṇa puruṣam icchati prativāditi bheda abhāvāt tena api na anyatara sa dvitīya tva siddhiḥ yatas ca na ghaṭasya sva rūpeṇa eva sa dvitīya tva sambhavaḥ bheda adhiṣṭhāna tvāt tasya na api dehena anvaya abhāvāt tatas vācya śūnya tvam artha śūnya tvam anyatarasa dvitīya tvam pralapatām para loka apava ādīnām tat etat anyatarasa dvitīya tva sādhya vacanam jāḍyasya varṇṇitam ceṣṭitam 
[428,i_428,ii]	tulyam na āśepi ced śabda ghaṭa bhedena kalpane na siddhena vināśena tadvatas sādhanāt dhvaneḥ na āśepi sādhye śabda ghaṭayoḥ sādhya dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇoḥ sambandhi tayā bhedena kalpane śabda sambandhinaḥ nāśasya ghaṭenvayā bhāvāt asādhya tvam ghaṭa sambandhinaḥ ca śabde asambhavāt asādhyatā iti tulyam idam iti ced na tulyam vānāśena pradhvaṃsa lakṣaṇena siddhena niścitena dhvaneḥ tadvataḥ vināśavataḥ sādhanāt vināśa sāmānyam sādhyam siddham kevalam tadvat tā śabdasya na siddhā iti sādhyate yathā vināśe sāmanyena siddhe satya siddhaḥ tadvān śabdaḥ sādhyate 
[428,iii_428,vi]	tathā artha antara bhāve syāt tadvān kumbhopi tathā artha antara bhāve abhivyakta caitanya svabhāvatayā dehasya ghaṭāt vaijātye siddhe sati tadvān kumbhopi sidhyet na ca etat prativādī bodhiyitum śakyate tena ācaitanyasya bhūta vyatiriktasya eva svīkārāt yadi punar acetana svabhāva tayā ghaṭa jātīyena eva dehena sa dvitīya tvam ghaṭasya sādhyate tadā sidhyati eva tathāvidhasya sa dvitīya tvasya siddha tvāt vināśa vat kintu vādinaḥ na iṣṭi siddhiḥ dehasya cetana svabhāvatayā asiddheḥ anitya tā viśiṣṭāḥ dhvaninā anveti no ca id na ayoga vāṇṇāt atha dhvaninā sva sambandhi tayā viśiṣṭā anitya tā dṛṣṭāntam na anveti iti ced na ananvaya doṣaḥ viśeṣaṇena ayogasya asambandhasya vāraṇāt 
[428,vii_428,viii]	dvividhaḥ hi vyavacchedaḥ viyoga apara yogayoḥ vyavacchedāt ayoge tu vārye na ananvaya āgamaḥ dvividhaḥ hi vyavacchedaḥ viśeṣaṇena dṛṣṭaḥ viyoga apara yogayoḥ ayoga ani ayogayoḥ vyavacchedāt yathā caitraḥ dhanurddharaḥ pāḥ rthaḥ dhanurddharaḥ iti tatra dharmiṇā viśeṣaṇena ayoge vārye anitya tāyāḥ na ananvaya āgamaḥ ananvaya āpattiḥ na bhavati śabdaḥ anityaḥ na vā iti ayogaḥ śaṅkitaḥ viśeṣaṇena vyāvarttyate śabdaḥ anityaḥ iti evamvidhā ca anitya tā na anya sambandhena virudhyate iti na ananvayaḥ dṛṣṭānte 
[428,ix_429,ii]	ukta artha saṃgraham āha sāmānyam eva tat sādhyam na ca siddha prasādham viśiṣṭam dharmiṇā tat ca na niranvaya doṣavat tat anitya tā ādi sāmānyam eva sādhyam na viśeṣaḥ yena ananvaya doṣaḥ syāt nanu anitya tā ādi sāmānyam siddham eva kvacid sādhane vaiyarthyam iti āha na ca siddhasya kvacid sattā mātreṇa anitya tvasya prasādhanam dharmiṇī ayoga vyavacchedasya asiddhasya prasādhanāt na ca dharmiṇā ayoga vyavacchedataḥ viśiṣṭam tat ca anitya tā ādi dṛṣṭānte niranvaya doṣavat na ca ayoga vyavacchedena dharmi viśeṣitasya dharmi antara sambandha avirodhāt 
[429,iii_429,iv]	etena dharmi dharmābhyām viśiṣṭau dharma dharmiṇau pratyākhyātau nirākurvan dharmiṇī evam asādhanāt etena iṣṭasya sādhya tva vacanena dharmi dharmābhyām viśiṣṭau dharma dharmiṇau ananvayāt nirākurvan cārvākaḥ yathā na śabda anitya tvavān śabdaḥ na anitya śabdavān vā śabdaḥ iti na hi śabda anitya tvena anitya śabdena vā kvacid ghaṭa ādau dṛṣṭānte kṛtaka tvasya anvayosti tatas iṣṭa viparyāsinād viruddham kṛtaka tvam iti saḥ evam vadan pratyākhyātaḥ katham iti āha dharmiṇi śabde evam dharmmi viśiṣṭasya dharmasya dharma aviśiṣṭasya vā dharmiṇaḥ asādhanāt anitya tva mātrasya śabde sādhya tvena iṣṭa tvāt anyathā anitya śabdavati śabde siddhepi śabdaḥ na anityaḥ syāt yadi dharma mātram sādhyam tadā samudāyaḥ sādhyaḥ na syāt hetoḥ tad apavādaḥ viruddhasya na syāt iti āha dharma mātrasya dharmi sādhya tvāt 
[429,v_429,vi]	samudāya apavādaḥ hi na dharmiṇi virudhyate sādhyam yatas tathā na iṣṭam sādhyaḥ dharmotra kevalaḥ samudāyaḥ eva sādhyaḥ hi yasmāt tasmāt viruddhasya hetoḥ iṣṭa samudāya apavādaḥ na virudhyate nanu samudāyasya sādhya tve ananvaya doṣaḥ iṣṭa vighātaḥ vā syāt iti āha tathā dharmi dharma samudāyaḥ anya dharmi sambandhi tayā sādhyam yatas na iṣṭam tasmāt na ananvayaḥ viruddha tā vā tathā hi atra śabda ādau dharmiṇi dharmaḥ anitya tā ādiḥ kevalaḥ sādhyaḥ iṣṭaḥ tasya ca anvayoḥ ti iti na doṣaḥ 
[430,i_430,iv]	uktam iṣṭa grahaṇasya prayojanam svayam śabdasya idānīm vaktum āha ekasya dharmiṇaḥ śāstre nānā dharma sthitau api sādhyaḥ syāt ātmanā eveṣṭaḥ iti upāttā svayam śrutiḥ ekasya śabda ādeḥ ddhamiṇaḥ śāstre nānā dharmāṇām amūrtta tva anitya tā ākāśa guṇa tva ādīnāṃsthitau abhyupagamepi vādinā ātmanā eva sādhana upanyāsa kāle sādhayitum iṣṭaḥ dharmaḥ sādhyaḥ syāt na anyaḥ iti svayam śruti tira ācāryeṇa upāttā 
[430,v_430,vii]	yadi punar śāstra abhyupagamāt eva sarva ādānāt prabādhane tatra ekasya api doṣaḥ syāt yadi hetu pratijñayoḥ śāstreṇa abhyupagamāt eva sarveṣām dharmāṇām ādānāt parigrahāt vādinā tatra teṣu madhye ekasya api dharmasya upanyasta hetunā bādhane hetu pratijñayoḥ viruddha tā doṣaḥ ucyate
