[430,viii_430,ix]	yathā śabde śāstra iṣṭam ākāśa āśraya tvam bādhamānasya vādīṣṭam anitya tvam sādhayatopi kṛtaka tvasya viruddha tvam pratijñā virodhaḥ vā abhidhīyate kṛtakam hi kṣaṇikam na ca kṣaṇikam utpāda ānat naram kṣaṇam api asti tatas kṛtaka tvam ākāśa āśraya tva bādhanam śabda nāśe prasādhye syāt gandha bhū guṇa tā kṣateḥ hetuḥ viruddha uprakṛteḥ nna ūced anī atra sā samā 
[430,x]	tathā kṛtaka tvāt śabdasya nāśe sādhyamāne gandhasya kṛtaka tvāt naśvarasya bhū guṇa tāyāḥ pṛthivī āśrita tāyāḥ śāstra iṣṭāyāḥ ca kṣateḥ viparyāsanāt hetuḥ prayatna ānantarīyaka tva ādi viruddhaḥ syāt pratijñā viruddhā syāt upāttaḥ hetuḥ vādinā aniṣṭam śāstra iṣṭam bādhataḥ iti eva yadi viruddhaḥ tadā gandha bhū guṇa tām bādhamānasya kṛtaka tvasyam śabde viruddha tā syāt śāstra iṣṭa bādhaka tāyāḥ aviśeṣāt 
[431,i_431,ii]	atha gandha bhū guṇa tāyā sādhya tvena aprakṛteḥ aprastute tad vādhanepi śabde kṛtaka tvam viruddham no ced sā prakṛtiḥ anyatra ākāśa guṇa tvepi samā na hi vādinā ākāśa guṇa tvam sādhayitum iṣṭam kintu a nitya tvam atas aprakṛtasya asya bādhane na viruddhaḥ syāt hetuḥ atha atra dharmī prakṛtaḥ tatra śāstra artha bādhanam atha vādīṣṭatām brūyāt dharmi dharma ādi sādhanaiḥ 
[431,iii]	atha atra ākāśa guṇa tva ādau dharmī śabdaḥ prakṛtaḥ tatra śāstra arthasya ākāśa guṇa tva ādeḥ sādhanam tat bādhane ca viruddha tā hetoḥ bhū guṇa tve tu gandhaḥ dharmya prakṛtaḥ iti tad bādhanepi na virodhaḥ na eṣa parihāraḥ tathā hi na vādi iṣṭa viparyāsanena doṣaḥ uktaḥ kintu śāstra artha virodhena tathā ca prakṛta tvam anupayuktam atha vādi aniṣṭatayā aprakṛta tvam tat ca ākāśa guṇa tvayoḥ samānam atha ākāśa guṇa tvasya vādīṣṭatām paraḥ brūyāt dharmmi dharmma ādi sādhanaiḥ sādhya dharmi dharma tvāt tad eka deśa tvāt vā akāśa guṇa tvam iṣṭam vādinaḥ anitya tva vat iti 
[431,iv_431,vi]	nanu kaiścid prakaraṇaiḥ icchā bhavet sā gamyate ca taiḥ balāt tava iccheyam iti vyaktam īśvara ceṣṭitam kaiścid prakaraṇaiḥ vivāda ādibhiḥ icchā vādinaḥ kasmiścid dharme bhavet taiḥ eva ca prakaraṇaiḥ sā icchā gamyate pareṇa api na tu tasya dharmiṇaḥ dharmaḥ iti eva vādinā iṣyate tatas dhami dharma tva ādi sandigdha vipakṣa vyatireki tvāt śeṣavat svayam anicchataḥ ca vādinaḥ sādhanasya balāt tava iccheyam iti yat ucyate vyaktam idam īśvara ceṣṭitam iti upahasati 
[431,vii_432,i]	kiñca vadan a kārya liṅgām tām vyabhicāreṇa bādhyate anāntarīyake ca arthe bādhitenyasya kā kṣatiḥ tām icchām akārya liṅga jām kāryā itara liṅgām anumeya tvena vadan paraḥ vyabhicāreṇa bādhyate na hi anyaḥ akāryaḥ anyam na vyabhicarati iti niyama usti api ca sādhyasa anitya tvasya ānantarīyake arthe ākāśa guṇa tva ādau bādhita tvepi anyasya sādhyasya kā kṣatiḥ na hi anitya tvam ākāśa guṇa tvanāntarīyakam yena tad abhāve tat api na syāt kṛtaka tvantu anitvatyatā avyabhicārī iti tasmāt na anumānam anaikāntikam 
[432,ii_432,iii]	uktañca na āgama apekṣam anumānam sva gocare siddham tena su siddha tat na tadā śāstram īkṣyate anumāviṣaye na iṣṭam vācaḥ prāmāṇya mityādinā uktam prāk vastu bala pravṛttam anumānam na āgama apekṣam svasya gocare sādhyaḥ iti tasmāt tena vastu bala pravṛttena āgamānapekṣiṇā anumāne yat siddham su siddhantat tadā ca na śāstram īkṣyate bādhitam na vā iti vastu bala pravṛtta anumānena tad apekṣā bhāvāt tadā anukāle śāstrasya anāśrayaṇāt 
[432,iv_432,v]	vāda tyāgaḥ tadā syāt ced na tadā anabhyupāyataḥ upāyaḥ hi abhyupāye ayam anaṅgam sa tadā api san vāda tyāgaḥ syāt ced na vāda tyāgaḥ sisādhayiṣita eka dharmāt aparasya śāstra abhyupetasya tadā sādhana upanyāsa kāle sādhyatayā anabhyupāyataḥ asvīkārāt nanu śāstra abhyupagamāt yadā vādaḥ kriyate tadā śāstra artha bādhanāt vāda tyāgaḥ syāt eva iti āha śāstrasya abhyupāye ayam vicāra aupāyaḥ tatas tadā vicāra kāle san api abhyupagamaḥ anaṅgam śāstra artha grahaṇe gṛhītasya tyāgaḥ syāt na vicārāt prāk grahaṇam abhyupagamāt nyāyyam 
[432,vi_433,i]	kadā tarhi śāstreṇa bādhā iṣyate iti āha tadā viśuddhe viṣaya dvaye śāstra parigraham cikīrṣoḥ sa hi kālaḥ syāt tadā śāstreṇa bādhanam śāstra upadarśite viṣaya dvaye pratyakṣa parokṣe rūpa nairātmya ādau tadā pramāṇa pravṛttyā viśuddhe nirṇṇīte sati paścāt atyanta parokṣe svarga ādau śāstreṇa śāstra āśrayaṇena anumānam cikīrṣoḥ sataḥ sa hi kālaḥ abhyugamya yadi śāstra bādhaḥ na bhavet atas tadā śāstreṇa bādhanam sādhya sādhana ādeḥ iṣyate 
[433,ii_433,iv]	tat api karamāt śāstra bādha iṣyate iti āha tad virodhena cintāyāḥ tad siddhārtheṣu ayogataḥ tṛtīya sthāna saṃkrāntau nyāyyaḥ śāstra parigrahaḥ tasya śāstrasya virodhena tad siddheṣu artheṣu liṅga ādiṣu asiddha kalpeṣu gamaka cintāyāḥ ayogataḥ yasmāt pratyakṣa parokṣa arthayoḥ na āgama adhikāraḥ tasmāt tṛtīya sthāne atīndriye viṣaye vicāra saṃkrāntaḥ śāstra parigrahaḥ nyāyyaḥ prakāra antara abhāvāt 
[433,v_433,vi]	tatra api sādhya dharmasya na antarīyaka bādhanam parihāryam na ca anyeṣām anavasthā prasaṅgataḥ tatra śāstre parigrahepi tadā sādhayitum ārabdhasya sādhya dharmasya yat na āntarīyakam sambaddham yathā kṣaṇika tvasya nairātmyam tasya bādhanam parihāryam vastutas tāt ātmyāt anayoḥ nairātmya bādhane kṣaṇika tva bādhana prasaṅgāt na tu anyeṣām sādhyasya akāraṇa avyāpaka bhūtānām dharmāṇām bādhanam parihāryam anavasthā prasaṅgataḥ na hi śāstra darśita sambhava dharma vyāpti liṅgasya dṛṣṭānte darśayitum śakyate yena kaścid āgama āśrayaḥ hetuḥ avatiṣṭheta 
[433,vii_433,ix]	nanu śāstram anapekṣya na vādaḥ karttavyaḥ iti vastu bala pravṛttā anumānepi śāstra apekṣā iti āha kena iyam sarva cintāsu śāstram grāhyam iti sthitiḥ kṛta idānīm asiddhāntaiḥ grāhyaḥ dhūmena na analaḥ sarvāsu parokṣa atyanta parokṣa artha cintāsu śāstram grāhyam iti kena iyam sthitiḥ kṛtā na etat anumanyante vidvān saḥ idānīm aviduṣām asmin abhyupagame asiddhāntaiḥ siddhānta viśeṣa āśraya rahitaiḥ gopālaka ādibhiḥ ddhū mena liṅgena na analaḥ grāhyaḥ 
[434,i_434,iii]	na ca kasyacid siddhānta sambandhaḥ yuktaḥ tathā hi sambandhaḥ bhavan sahajaḥ vā bhavet aupādhikaḥ vā dvayam api niṣeddhum āha riktasya jantoḥ jjātasya guṇa doṣam apaśyataḥ vilabdhāḥ vata kena amī siddhānta viṣamagrahāḥ riktasya tucchasya siddhānta rahitasya jantoḥ jātasya anena sahaja sambandha abhāva nimittam uktam guṇa doṣam prāmāṇya aprāmāṇya nibandhanam apaśyataḥ anena aupādhika sambandha nimitta abhāvaḥ uktaḥ kena anartha paṭīyasā siddhāntāeva viṣama grahāḥ duṣparihāra tvāt ime vilabdha avata yeṣu svāmi tvena jantavaḥ vyavaharanti na hi karṇṇa nāsam iva siddhāntaḥ prāṇa sahajaḥ na api doṣa ūrjjita guṇa upapannaḥ pramāṇam iva vicārāt prāk siddhāntaḥ siddhaḥ yena samartha viṣayaḥ syāt 
[434,iv_434,vi]	kiñca yadi sādhanaḥ ekatra sarvam śāstram nidarśane darśayet sādhanam syāt iti eṣā lokottarā sthitiḥ yadi sādhanaḥ ekatra sarvam śāstram śāstra artham nidarśane dṛṣṭānte vādī darśayet tadā tat sādhanam syāt na tu ekasya śāstra darśita dharmasya anvaye etat ca na kvacid sādhane karttum śakyam iti loka atikrāntā sthitiḥ eṣā 
[434,vii_434,ix]	api ca asambaddhasya dharmasya kim asiddhau na siddhati hetuḥ tad sādhanāya uktaḥ kim duṣṭaḥ tatra sidhyati asambaddhasya sādhayitum apravṛttasya dharmasya ākāśa guṇa tva ādeḥ kṛtaka tvāt hetoḥ viparyāsanāt a siddhau satyām sisā dhayiṣitam hetu vyāpakam anitya tvam kim na sidhyati na hi vyāpakam antareṇa vyāpyam bhavati hetuḥ tasya vyāpakasya sādhanāya uktaḥ kinduṣṭaḥtatra sva sādhye sidhyati sādhya pratipādanam sādhya vyāpāraḥ tat ced asti katham duṣṭaḥ 
[435,i_435,iii]	śāstra artha bādhane abhimatasya api na siddhiḥ iti ced āha dharmān anupanīya eva dṛṣṭānte dharmiṇaḥ akhilān vāgdhūma ādeḥ janonvā iti caitanya dahana ādikam dharmiṇaḥ dharmān śāstra darśitān akhilān hetu vyāpaka tvena anupanīya apradarśyam vāgdhūma ādeḥ hetoḥ caitanya dahana ādikam yathākramam sva santāna vat mahān asa vat ca janaḥ anveti pratipadyate 
[435,iv_435,vi]	kiñca svabhāvam kāraṇam ca arthaḥ avyabhicāreṇa sādhayan kasyacid vāda bādhāyām svabhāvāt na nivartate svabhāvam vyāpakam vṛkṣa tva ādi kāraṇam vahni ādi ca arthaḥ vyāpyaḥ śiṃśapā ādiḥ kāryam dhūma ādiḥ avyabhicāreṇa avinābhāvi tvāt sādhayan kasyacid śāstra para adhīnasya vādinaḥ vādasya bādhāyām svabhāvāt vyāpaka kāraṇa gamakān na nivarttate tatas śāstreṣu dharma antara vyāhatau api hetuḥ sādhyīkṛtam sva sambaddham artham pratipādayati 
[435,vii_435,ix]	tatas ca prapadyamānaḥ ca anyaḥ tam na antarīyakam īpsitaiḥ sādhya artha ehetunā tena katham apratipāditaḥ sādhyaiḥ arthaiḥ īpsitaiḥ āptam pratyetum aṣṭaiḥ nnāntirīyakam avinā bhāvinam tam hetum prapadyamānaḥ pratipadyamānonyaḥ prativādī kathantena hetunā apratipāditaḥ sādhyana antarīyaka tayā kvacid dharmiṇi sādhana pratītiḥ eva hi sādhya pratītiḥ sā ca asti prativādinaḥ 
[435,x_436,i]	kiñca hetunā yaḥ śāstra arthaḥ bādhyate kintasmin sādhye vādīnā hetuḥ asādhu uktaḥ āhosvit tatra sādhye hetuḥ ucyatām mā vā vastutas tad vādhakosau hetuḥ iti duṣṭa tā tatra ādya pakṣe bhavati eva doṣaḥ yadi evam iṣyate atha uktaḥ anuktā upi vā hetuḥ viroddhā vādinotra kim na hi tasya ukti doṣeṇa sa jātaḥ śāstra bādhanaḥ uktaḥ anuktā upi vā hetuḥ vastutas eva tasya viroddhā pratighātakaḥ tadā tatra śāstra artha bādhane vādinaḥ kindūṣaṇam na kiñcid hi yasmāt tasya vādinaḥ ukti doṣeṇa sa kṛtaka tva ādi hetuḥ śāstrasya śāstra arthasya ākāśa guṇa tva ādeḥ bādhanaḥ bādhakaḥ na jātaḥ 
[436,ii_436,iii]	bādhakasya abhidhānāt ced doṣaḥ yadi vadet na saḥ kin na bādheta saḥ akurvan ayuktam kena duṣyati śāstra artha bādhakasya hetoḥ abhidhānāt vādinā upi doṣaḥ ced yadi tam hetum na vadet sa vādī tadā kim asau hetuḥ śāstra artha na bādheta vastutas tad virodhi tvāt avaśyam bādhate tatas ca sa vādya kurvan ayuktam kena kāraṇena duṣyati parājitaḥ syāt 
[436,iv_436,vi]	nanu yadi duṣṭa hetu vacanepi na vādinaḥ duṣṭa tā tadā asiddha ādi vacanepi na doṣaḥ syāt iti āha anyeṣu hetvābhāseṣu sveṣṭasi a iva aprasādhanāt duṣyet vyartha abhidhānena na atra tasya prasādhanāt anyeṣu asiddha ādiṣu hetvābhāseṣu vādyukteṣu sva iṣṭasya vādī iṣṭasya eva aprasādhanāt vādī duṣyati vyarthasya sādhya sādhana anupayuktasya sādhanasya abhidhānāt atra kṛtaka tve tu vādi ukte vāñchitasya anitya tvasya prasādhanāt na vādī duṣyati śāstra arthe tu vādya niṣṭe bādhyamāne śāstram eva duṣṭam bhaviṣyati 
[436,vii_436,ix]	yadi api sveṣṭasya tena sādhanam tathā api śāstra arthasya bādhanam iti duṣṭaḥ eva iti āha yadi kiñcid kvacid śāstre na yuktam pratiṣidhyate bruvāṇaḥ yuktam api anyat iti rāja kula sthitiḥ kvacid vaiśeṣika ādi śāstre nirdiṣṭam yadi kiñcid ākāśa guṇa tva ādi bādhyamāna tvāt ayuktam tāvatā anyat anitya tva ādi yuktam api kṛtaka tva hetunā bruvāṇaḥ pratipādayan pratiṣidhyate śāstra artha bādhanāt virodha upanyāsena iti vyaktam iyam rāja kula sthitiḥ rāja śāsanasya eva bala pravṛttasya yukta ayukta vicāraṇa abahis bhāvāt 
[436,x_437,i]	kiñca sarvān arthān samīkṛtya vaktum śakyam na sādhanam sarvatra tena succhannā iyam sādhya sādhana saṃsthitiḥ sarvān śāstra dṛṣṭān arthān sādhya tvena samīkṛtya kiñcid sādhanam vaktum aśakyam dṛṣṭānte śāstra dṛṣṭa akhila dharma vyāpti anupalambhāt tena kāraṇena sarvatra dharmiṇi sādhya sādhanayoḥ saṃsthitiḥ vyavastheyam succhannā syāt 
[437,ii_437,iv]	yadi tarhi ākāśa guṇa tva abhāvepya nitya tvam sidhyada bādhyam śabde tadā śrāvaṇa tva ādi hetunā nitya tvam api sādhyamānam abādhyam syāt iti āha viruddhayoḥ eka dharmiṇī ayogāt aḥ tu bādhanam viruddha aikāntike na atra tadvat asti virodhitā viruddhayoḥ nnitya tva anitya tvayoḥ ekatra śabde dharmiṇī ayogāt viruddha aikāntike viruddha avyabhicāriṇi śrāvaṇa tva ādau nitya tva sādhake bādhanam astu na hi ekatra dharmiṇi viruddhau dharmaḥ bhavitum arhataḥ tadvat nitya tvayoḥ iva atra anayoḥ prakṛta aprakṛtayoḥ anitya tva ākāśa guṇa tva abhāvayoḥ virodhitā na asti tatas kṛtaka tvāt śabde anitya tva siddhau ākāśa guṇa tva abhāvaḥ na bādhyate 
[437,v_437,vii]	syāt etat prakṛta aprakṛtayoḥ anitya tva ākāśa guṇa tva abhāvayoḥ parasparam abādhya bādhaka tvepi tayoḥ śāstra artha vilpavāt asambandha ipi bādhā ced syāt sarvam sarva bādhanam bādhya bādhaka tva abhāvepi ekasmin anitya tve kṛtaka tvāt sidhyati śabde dharmiṇi śāstra arthasya śāstra abhyupagatasya ākāśa guṇa tvasya viplavāt kāraṇāt asambaddhe aprakṛta ākāśa guṇa tva sambandha rahite anitya tvepi bādhā bhavati iti ced evantarhi prayanta anantarīyaka tvāt gandhe pṛthivī guṇa tva bādhane sarvam kṛtaka tva ādi sarvasya anitya tva ādeḥ sādhyasya bādhanam syāt śabda ādau dharmiṇya prakṛta śāstra artha bādhanasya tulya tvāt 
[437,viii_437,ix]	sambandhaḥ tena tasya eva bādhanāt asti ced asat hetoḥ sarvasya cintya tvāt sva sādhye guṇa doṣayoḥ atha tatra śabdaḥ eva dharmiṇi ākāśa guṇa tvasya sattvāt sambandha usti tena kṛtaka tvāt tasya eva bādhanāt virodhaḥ pṛthivī guṇa tvantu śabde dharmiṇya sambaddham tatas tad bādhanepi śabde kṛtaka tvam aviruddham iti ced asat etat sarvasya hetoḥ sva sādhye prakṛte guṇa doṣayoḥ cintya tvāt yat punar aprakṛtam dharmi sambaddham api na tat sādhyam tad vādhanepi na kācid kṣatiḥ 
[438,i_438,iii]	kiñca dharmiṇi sattā mātram na sambandhaḥ kintu na antarīyaka tā sādhye sambandhaḥ sā iha na īkṣyate kevalam śāstra pīḍā iti doṣaḥ sa anya kṛte samā sādhye na antarīyaka tā sādhya avinā bhāvi tvam sambandhaḥ ucyate sā sādhyana antarīyatā iha prakṛta ākāśa guṇa tva bādhane sati na īkṣyate yadi api satvana āntarīyakam ākāśa guṇa tvam śabde syāt na bādhyeta kevalam śāstra abhyupagata dharma bādhanāt śāstra pīḍā iti doṣaḥ sā ca kṛtaka tvāt anitya tva siddhau dṛśyate śāstra pīḍā anyena prayatna anantarīyaka tva ādinā gandhe pṛthivī guṇa tva bādhanepi sameti kṛtaka tvam śabde viruddham syāt 
[438,iv_438,vi]	yat api āhuḥ ācāryīyāḥ śāstram abhyupagamya yadā vādaḥ kriyate tadā śāstra dṛṣṭasya sakalasya dharmasya sādhyatā iti atra āha śāstra abhyupagamāt sādhyaḥ śāstra dṛṣṭaḥ akhilaḥ yadi pratijñā asiddha dṛṣṭānta hetuvādaḥ prasajyate śāstra abhyupagamāt śāstra dṛṣṭaḥ akhilaḥ dharmaḥ yadi sādhyaḥ iṣyate tadā asiddhayoḥ śāstra uddiṣṭayoḥ hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ vādaḥ pratijñā sādhyam prasajyate śāstre dṛṣṭasya asiddhasya sādhya tvāt 
[438,vii_438,ix]	syāt etat kintu uktayoḥ sādhana tvena no ced īpsita vādataḥ nyāya prāptam na sādhya tvam vacanāt vinivarttate vādinā īpsitasya sādhya tvena vādataḥ svayam sādhya tvena īpsitaḥ pakṣaḥ viruddha tvāt nirākṛtaḥ iti ādikāt sādhana tvena uktayoḥ asiddha hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ sādhya tā no ced nanu asiddhasya śāstra abhyupagatasya sādhya tvam nyāya prāptam vacana mātrāt īpsita sādhya tvam pratipādaka tvāt na vinivarttate 
[439,i_439,ii]	anīpsitam asādhyañcet vādinā anya upyanīpsitaḥ dharmaḥ asādhyaḥ tadā asādhyam bādhamānam virodhi kim śāstra abhyupagamepi vādinā anīpsitam asādhyam ced evantarhi ākāśa guṇa tva ādiḥ api dharmaḥ vādinā sādhya tvena anīpsitaḥ asādhyaḥ syāt tadā tad asādhyam ākāśa guṇa tvam bādhamānam kṛtaka tvam kim kasmāt virodhi 
[439,iii_439,v]	kiñca pakṣa lakṣaṇa bāhya arthaḥ svayaṃśabda upyanarthakaḥ śāstreṣu icchā pravṛtti arthaḥ yadi śaṅkā kutonu iyam yadi śāstra abhyupagata tvam pakṣa lakṣaṇam tadā svayaṃśabdopi pakṣa lakṣaṇa bāhya arthaḥ bhinna abhidheyaḥ anarthakaḥ syāt śāstra abhyupagame śāstra iṣṭasya sādhya tā prāptau vādīṣṭa mātram sādhyam na anyat iti hi svayaṃśabdasya prayojanam śāstra iṣṭa mātrasya tu sādhya tve niṣphalam eva tat śāstreṣu icchayā pravṛtti arthaḥ svayaṃśabdaḥ yadi kathyate svayaṃśabdam antareṇa śāstram icchayā na grahītavyam iti śaṅkā iyam kutas nu hetoḥ jātā yena tad nivṛtti arthā svayaṃśrutiḥ varṇyate 
[439,vi_439,vii]	soniṣiddhaḥ pramāṇena gṛhṇan kena nivāryate niṣiddhaḥ ced pramāṇena vācā kena pravṛrttyate sa vādī pramāṇena śāstra artha bādhakena aniṣiddhaḥ śāstram gṛhṇan kena nivāryate na kenacid yatas svayaṃgrahaṇam śāstram grāhayat saphalam syāt pramāṇena ced śāstra artha bādhakena niṣiddhaḥ vādī vācā svayaṃśabdena śāstra abhyupagame kena lakṣaṇa kartrā pravarttyate na kenacid 
[439,viii_439,x]	kiñca pūrvam api eṣa siddhāntam sva icchayā eva gṛhītavān kiñcid anyam sa tu punar grahītum labhate na kiṃm eṣa vādī pūrvam api sveccheyā eva siddhāntam kaṇāda ādi praṇītam gṛhītavān na tu anyapurāṇa ādi balāt sa katham icchayā śāstra uddiṣṭaṅ kiñcid dharma vyabhicāra darśana ādinā śāstreṣu saphala dharma kalāpa sādhya tvāt anyam siddhāntam ākāśa guṇa tva rahita anitya tā ādikam grahītum kin na labhate icchā adhīna tve niyama ayogāt tasmāt svayaṃgrahaṇam śāstra icchā pravṛtti artham iti ayuktam 
[440,i_440,iii]	nanu iṣṭasya api sva icchayā eva sādhya tā parigrahaḥ siddhaḥ iti vyartham svayaṃgrahaṇam iti āha dṛṣṭeḥ vipratipattīnām atra akārṣīt svayaṃśrutim iṣṭa akṣatim asādhya tvam anavasthāñca darśayan śāstra kārasya iṣṭam sādhyam iti vipratipattīnām dṛṣṭeḥ tad nirākaṇa artham atra pakṣa lakṣaṇe svayaṃśrutim ācāryaḥ akārṣīt śāstreṣu ākāśa guṇa tva asiddhau api vādī iṣṭasya akṣatim śāstra iṣṭasya asādhya tvam śāstra iṣṭa dharma antara asiddhau hetu bala prasiddha sādhya bādhane gandhe bhūta guṇa tā ābādhāyām śabde kṛtaka tvam anitya tva sādhanam viruddham syāt ityādi kāmanavasthāñca parasya darśayat ācā ryaḥ svayaṃśrutim akārṣīt iti pūrveṇa sambandhaḥ 
[440,iv_440,v]	samayā ahita bhedasya parihāreṇa dharmiṇaḥ prasiddhasya gṛhi iti arthāḥ jagāda anyaḥ svayaṃśrutim samayena siddhāntena āhitaḥ āropitaḥ bhedaḥ viśeṣaḥ ākāśa guṇa tva ādiḥ yasya tasya dharmiṇaḥ parihāreṇa āgama nirapekṣa pramāṇa balāt prasiddhasya dharmiṇaḥ śabda mātra ādeḥ gṛhītiḥ iti arthaḥ prayojanam yaḥ tāḥ tām svayaṃśrutim anyaḥ jagāda svam prasiddhaḥ dharmī kāryaḥ na āgam a siddhaḥ iti arthaḥ 
[440,vi_440,viii]	atra āha vicāra prastuteḥ eva prasiddhaḥ siddhaḥ āśrayaḥ sva icchā kalpita bhedeṣu padārtheṣu avivādataḥ dharmiṇi sādhya dharmasya bhāva abhāva vicāra prastuteḥ eva āgamam anapekṣya prasiddhaḥ āśrayaḥ dharmī siddhaḥ sva icchayā kalpitaḥ bhedaḥ viśeṣaḥ yeṣām teṣu padārtheṣu avivādataḥ vivāda abhāvāt na hi kalpita bhede dharmiṇi kaścid prekṣāvān kasyacid dharmasya sādhanam bādhanam vehate kintu pramāṇa pratīte vastuni atas tad artham api svayaṃgrahaṇam anupayuktam 
[441,i_441,ii]	asādhyatām atha prāha siddhādeśena dharmiṇaḥ sva rūpeṇa eva nirdeśyaḥ iti anena eva tad gatam atha siddhādeśena prasiddha artha vācakena svayaṃśabdena dharmiṇaḥ asādhyatām prāha yathā asti pradhānam bhedānām anupadarśanāt iti idam api ayuktam yasmāt sva rūpeṇa sādhya tvena eva nirdeśyaḥ iti anena pakṣa lakṣaṇa avayavena eva ca tad dharmiṇaḥ siddhasya asādhya tvam gatam pratītam 
[441,iii_441,v]	tathā hi ayam iṣṭaḥ anirākṛtaḥ pakṣaḥ iti anena siddha sādhana rūpeṇa nirdeśasya hi sambhave sādhya tva ena iva nirdeśyaḥ iti idam phalavat bhavet siddhasya siddha rūpeṇa nirdeśasya dharma vacanasya asiddhasya api sādhana rūpeṇa nirdeśasya asiddha vacanasya pakṣatva sambhave hi tat pratiṣedham vidadhat sādhya tvena eva nirdeśyaḥ iti idam phalavat bhavet sādhyasya eva nirdeśaḥ pakṣaḥ iti siddhasya dharmiṇaḥ asiddhasya ca sādhana tvena uktasya nirāsaḥ 
[441,vi_441,viii]	kiñca anumānasya sāmānya viṣaya tvañca varṇṇitam iha evam na hi anuktopi kiñcid pakṣe virudhyate anumānasya sāmānya viṣaya tvam svayam ācāryeṇa varṇṇitam yadi ca dharmī pakṣaḥ tadā tasya sva lakṣaṇa tvāt sāmanya viṣaya tā vyāhanyeta kiñca iha pakṣa lakṣaṇaḥ evam ukta krameṇa anuktepi svayaṃśabde siddha dharmya siddha sādhana vyavaccheda arthe kiñcid pakṣe pratipādye na virudhyate 
[441,ix_441,xi]	nanu anukte svayaṃśabde pakṣa lakṣaṇam kuryāt ced dharmiṇam sādhyam tatas kintan na śakyate kasmāt hetu anvaya abhāvāt na ca doṣaḥ tayoḥ api dharmiṇam sādhyam kuryāt iti doṣaḥ tatas dharmiṇaḥ pakṣatva prasaṅgāt kindūṣaṇam tad dharmmi pakṣa tvam karttum na śakyate iti aśakyatādūṣaṇam kasmāt kāraṇāt dharmī pakṣaḥ bhavitu na arhati dharmiṇaḥ sādhya tvena asiddha tāyām hetoḥ abhāvāt viśeṣasya dharmiṇaḥ dṛṣṭānte asambhavāt anvaya abhāvāt ca dharmī pakṣaḥ karttum na śakyate 
[442,i_442,iii]	nanu ayam doṣaḥ tayoḥ hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ na tu pakṣasya tathā hi uttara avayava apekṣaḥ na doṣaḥ pakṣaḥ iṣyate tathā hetu ādi doṣa upi pakṣa doṣaḥ prasajyate sādhana vākyasya pakṣāt uttare avayave hetu dṛṣṭānta ādike apekṣā yasya asau doṣaḥ pakṣe na iṣyate hetu dṛṣṭānta sambandhi tvāt tasya yadi tu uttara avayava apekṣā upi pakṣasya bādhanāt pakṣa doṣaḥ ucyate tathā sati hetu ādi doṣa upi pakṣa doṣaḥ prasajyate 
[442,iv_442,v]	sarvaiḥ pakṣasya bādhātaḥ tasmāt tanmātra saṅginaḥ pakṣa doṣāḥ matā na anye pratyakṣa ādi virodha vat sarvaiḥ hetu ādi doṣaiḥ pakṣasya bādhāt tasmāt tanmātraṅginaḥ pakṣa mātra sambaddhāḥ doṣāḥ pakṣa doṣāḥ matāḥ na anye avayava antara apekṣāḥ pratyakṣa ādi virodha vat yathā pratyakṣa ādi bādhita tvam avayava antara anapekṣam pakṣa doṣaḥ 
[442,vi_442,viii]	tasmāt hetu ādi lakṣaṇaiḥ bbādhyam muktvā pakṣasya lakṣaṇam ucyate parihāra artham avyāpti vyatirekayoḥ hetu ādīnām lakṣaṇaiḥ bbādhyam pariharttavyam doṣam anvaya virodha ādikam muktvā pakṣa mātra anuṣaṅgiṇa uḥ avya āpti vyatirekayoḥ parihāra artham pakṣa lakṣaṇam ucyatevyatireke ādhikyam abhivyāptiḥ iti arthaḥ 
[442,ix_442,xi]	tatra yena padena yat dūṣaṇam parihriyate tat āha svayat nipāta rūpa ākhyāḥ vyatirekasya bādhikāḥ saha anirākṛtena iṣṭa śruti ḥ avyāpti bādhanī svayañca nipātañcaḥ evam rūpam sva rūpañcā ākhyā śrutayaḥ saha anirākṛtena padena vyatirekasya ati vyāpteḥ bbādhikāḥ svayaṃśabdena śāstra iṣṭasya nipātena asiddhasya api sādhana tvena uktasya sva rūpa śabdena siddhasya nirākṛta śabdena pratyakṣa ādi nirākṛtasya pakṣa tvam saktam niṣidhyate iṣṭa śrutiḥ avyāpteḥ bbādhanī iṣṭa śabde hi akriyamāṇe nirddiṣṭam eva sādhyam sādhyam syāt na prakaraṇa āpannam iṣṭam 
[443,i_443,ii]	yadi svayaṃnipāta rūpa ākhyāḥ vyatirekasya vā adhikāḥ pramāṇa samuccaya lakṣaṇe nirddiṣṭāḥ tadā nyāya mukhe sādhya tvena īpsitaḥ pakṣaḥ viruddha artha anirākṛtā eti pakṣa lakṣaṇe tāḥ na santi iti kathantena avyāpti vyatirekayoḥ parihāraḥ iti āha sādhya tvena īpsitaḥ pakṣaḥ iti sādhya abhyupagamaḥ pakṣa lakṣaṇam teṣu apakṣatā nirākṛte bādhanataḥ śeṣe alakṣaṇa vṛttitaḥ 
[443,iii]	sādhya abhyupagamaḥ pakṣaḥ iti pakṣa lakṣaṇam avatiṣṭhate tathā ca teṣu śāstra iṣṭa ādiṣu pañcasu vyāvarttyeṣu madhye nirākṛte pratyakṣa ādi bādhite bādhanataḥ apakṣatā viruddha arthāḥ nirākṛtasya pakṣa vidhānāt śeṣe śāstra iṣṭe vādinā aniṣṭe sādhane ca siddhe sādhayitum iṣṭaḥ eṣyamāṇe siddhe ca sādhya viparīte aprastute ca ukta mātre lakṣaṇasya sādhya tvena īpsita tvasya āvṛttitaḥ apakṣatā siddhā iti paripūrṇṇam idam api lakṣaṇam 
[443,iv_443,v]	nanu yathā satyarthebhyaḥ varttamāne ku vidhānāt īpsita śabdaḥ varttamānam icchām āha tathā iṣṭa śabdopi tatra eṣiṣyamāṇe pakṣa tvam aprasaktam eva tat kim pramāṇa samuccaya lakṣaṇe avadhāraṇam kṛtam iti āha svayam iṣṭa abhidhānena gata arthepi avadhāraṇe kṛtya antena abhisambandhāt uktam kāla antara chide 
[443,vi]	svayam iṣṭaḥ iti anayoḥ padayoḥ abhidhānena avadhāraṇe nipāta arthe gate pratītepi kṛtya antena nirdeśya śabdena sarva kāla sambandha yogya abhidhāyinā abhisambandha ādiṣṭa śabdasya āvarttamāna kāla icchā viṣayasya api pakṣa tvam syāt yathā āgataḥ devadattaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ iti yadā gamiṣyati tadā drakṣyate iti arthaḥ atas vartamāna kālāt kāla antarasya bhaviṣyat ādeḥ sādhye sādhya icchā viṣayasya cchide pratiṣedha artham uktam avadhāraṇam sva rūpeṇa eva iti 
[443,vii_444,i]	yasmāt kṛtyā antena abhisambandhāt kāla sāmānya vṛttiḥ iha anaṅga miṣeḥ nniṣṭhā tena īpsita pade punar aṅgam eva tayā asiddha hetu ādi pratiṣidhyate iha pramāṇa samuccaya lakṣaṇe niṣṭhā varttamāna sādhya tva iṣṭi pratipādanam ati anaṅga hetuḥ nyāya mukhe tena kṛtyā antena sambandha abhāvena īpsita pade punar aṅgam eva niṣṭhā varttamāna sādhya icchā bodhane tayā āvarttamāna sādhya icchā bodhikayā asiddha hetu ādi apīṣyamāṇam sādhya tvena pratiṣidhyate tasmāt na dharmiṇaḥ sādhya tā pratikṣepa artham svayaṃgrahaṇam siddha tvena eva tad parihārasya labdha tvāt 
[444,ii_444,iv]	na api śāstreṣu icchā pravṛtti artham icchā mātreṇa eva tad grahaṇasya siddha tvāt iti uktam avācaka tvat ca ayuktam tena iṣṭam svayam ātmanā anapekṣya akhilam śāstram tat vādi iṣṭasya sādhya tā avācaka tvāt ca ayuktam tad artham svaya grahaṇam na hi svayaṃśabdaḥ sva icchayā śāstram grāhyām iti etad artha vācakam kintu vādinaḥ eva vācakaḥ tena tad vācaka tvena svayam vādinā atmanā śāstram akhilam anapekṣya yat iṣṭam tasya vādīṣṭasya sādhyateṣyate na śāstra iṣṭasya iti upasaṃhāraḥ 
[444,v_444,vi]	tena anabhīṣṭa saṃsṛṣṭasya iṣṭasya api hi bādhane yathā sādhyam abādhataḥ pakṣa hetūna duṣyataḥ tena kāraṇena vādinā ūna bhīṣṭena ākāśa guṇa tvena saṃsṛṣṭasya iṣṭasya anitya tvasya api hi bādhane abhidhīyamāne pakṣa hetū na duṣyataḥ kiṅgākāraṇam iti āha yathā sādhyam abādhātaḥ na hi vādinā akāśa guṇa tva eka artha samavāyi anitya tvam sādhayitum iṣṭam yena asya bādhaḥ syāt kintu a nitya tva mātram na ca asya pratyakṣa ādi bādhā asti hetoḥ vā tad apekṣayā viruddhatā ādikam tat evam svayaṃnipāta rūpa ākhyā vyatirekasya bādhikāḥ saha anirākṛtena iti vyākhyātam 
[444,vii_445,i]	anirākṛta padam vyākhyātum āha aniṣiddhaḥ pramāṇābhyām sa ca upagamaḥ iṣyate sandigdhe hetu vacanāt vyastaḥ hetoḥ anāśrayaḥ sa ca ukta lakṣaṇaḥ sādhyasya upagamaḥ pakṣaḥ pramāṇābhyām pratyakṣa anumānābhyām aniṣiddhaḥ iṣyate kasmāt iti āha saṃdigdhe arthe sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa viṣaye hetoḥ vacanāt vyastaḥ pramāṇa pratikṣiptaḥ hetoḥ anāśrayaḥ aviṣayaḥ 
[445,ii_445,iv]	yadi dvividhau pakṣa bādhau tadā pratyakṣa anumāna āptaiḥ prasiddhena iti katham ācāryeṇa caturvidhā sā darśitā iti āha anumānasya bhedena sā bādhā uktā caturvidhā tatra abhyupāyaḥ kārya aṅgam svabhāva aṅgam jagastthitiḥ anumānasya bhedena traividhyena pratyakṣeṇa ca ekena saha sā bādhā caturvidha uktā tatra teṣu bādhakeṣu abhyupāyaḥ āpta sva vacane kāryam aṅgam jagataḥ sthitiḥ vyavahṛtiḥ prasiddhiḥ svabhāvaḥ aṅgam hetuḥ 
[445,v_445,vii]	kasmāt punar āpta vacanam sva vacanañca abhyupāyaḥ ucyate iti āha ātma aparodha abhimataḥ bhūta niścaya yukta vāc āptaḥ sva vacanam śāstram ca ekam uktam samatvataḥ ātma aparodha abhimataḥ bhūtasya arthasya niścayena yuktā prayuktā vāc yasya saḥ āptaḥ ucyate evam paraṃparayā artha kārya tvena sva vacanam śāstrañca samatvataḥ abhyupāyaḥ iti samasya kārya liṅgam ekam uktam 
[445,viii_445,x]	kiñca yathā ātmanaḥ apramāṇa tve vacanam na pravarttate śāstra siddhe tathā na arthe vicāraḥ tat anāśraye vaktuḥ ātmanaḥ apramāṇa tve prāmāṇya nimitta abhāvāt vacanaṃprāmāṇyam na pravarttate na hi asatyā arthena vacanena paraḥ pratipādayitum śakyate visamvādana āśrayasya vacanāt arthāpatteḥ tatas yathā pratipādayituḥ prāmāṇyaḥ eva sati vacanam pravarttate tathā śāstra siddhe arthe tasya śāstra prāmāṇyasya anāśrayeṇa na vicāraḥ pravarttate pramāṇa viṣayaḥ labdhaḥ sākṣāt asya eva pramāṇasya śāstrasya atyanta parokṣa arthe vicāraḥ prastūyate prekṣaiḥ nānasya tatas śāstra sva vacanayoḥ prāmāṇye abhyupagatepi sāmyam uktam 
[446,i_446,iii]	sāmyam eva punar kim artham upadarśitām iti āha tad prastāva āśraya tve hi śāstram bādhakam iti amum vaktum artham su avācā asya saha uktiḥ sāmya dṛṣṭaye hi yasmāt tad prastāvasya vicāra prakramasya āśraya tve adhikaraṇa tve sati śāstram siddhe dharmiṇi śāstram pratijñā artha viruddhaṃbādhakam na vastu bala pravṛtta anumānam iti amum artham vaktum asya śāstrasya sva vācā sāmyasya dṛṣṭaye darśana artham saha uktiḥ anayoḥ abhyupāyatā nirdeśe sva vacanam api hi uccāraṇa sāmarthyāt upagata prāmāṇyam siddhe dharmiṇi vicāra prakrame pratijñā artha viṣaya bādhakam bādhakam dṛṣṭam na vastu bala pravṛtta anumānena idam anayoḥ sāmya darśana prayojanam 
[446,iv_446,v]	udāhāraṇam api atra sadṛśam tena varṇitam pramāṇānām abhāve hi śāstra vācoḥ ayogātaḥ atra śāstra vacanayoḥ vyāghātena ācāryeṇa udāharaṇam api sadṛśam abhinnam varṇṇitam yathā na santi pramāṇāni prameya arthāni iti katham punar atra śāstra artha sva vacanābhyām vyāghātaḥ iti āha pramāṇānām abhāve hi śāstra vācoḥ ayogātaḥ anupapatteḥ pramāṇa sambhave hi śāstra vacanayoḥ para pratipādana artha muktiḥ yuktā tasmāt uccāraṇa sāmarthyāt abhyupagata prāmāṇyāt prayoga vacanāt eva pramāṇa abhāva pratijñā bādhyate 
[446,vi_446,viii]	etat ca udāharaṇam sva vāc virodhe vispaṣṭam udāharaṇam āgame diś mātra darśanam tatra pratyedharmaḥ sukha pradaḥ sva vāc virodhe sva vacana vyāhatau vispaṣṭam tathā hi pramāṇa abhāva pratijñā vacana uccāraṇa sāmarthya abhyupagata prāmāṇyena vacanena eva bādhyate āgame śāstre punar udāharaṇasya diś mātra darśanam upalakṣaṇa mātram etat na tu mukhyam udāharaṇam pramāṇasya dharmiṇaḥ āgama siddha tva abhāvāt idam punar mukhyam udāharaṇam āgame pretya para loke dharmaḥ asukha pradaḥ āgama siddhe dharmiṇi dharme sāmānye asukha pradatvasya viśeṣasya sukha pradatvena viruddhena āgama siddhena bādhanāt 
[446,ix_447,ii]	kintu śāstriṇā upyatadālambe viruddha uktau tu vastuni na bādhā pratibandhaḥ syāt tulya kakṣatayā tayoḥ śāstriṇaḥ abhyupagata śāstrasya atad ālambe śāstra asiddhe pramāṇa siddhe vastuni dharmiṇi śāstra pratijñā viruddhasya dharmasya uktau na sā bādhā yathā mīmāṃsakasya gṛhīta śāstrasya pratyakṣa siddhe śabde dharmiṇi kṛtaka tvāt anitya tva uktau api śāstra pratijñātena nitya tvena na bādhā yadi bādhā kintarhi bhavati iti āha pratibandhaḥ syāt kasmāt iti āha tulya kakṣa tvāt sama bala tvāt yathā mātā me bandhyā ca iti sva vāci tulya kakṣa tvāt padayoḥ parasparam pratibandhaḥ 
[447,iii_447,v]	nanu sva vacanayoḥ tulya kakṣa tvāt yuktaḥ pratibandhaḥ āgama sva vacanayoḥ tulya bala tā eva katham iti āha yathā sva vāci tat ca asya tadā sva vacana ātmakam tayoḥ pramāṇam yasya asti tat syāt anyasya bādhakam tat ca śāstram nitya tva pratijñātasya vādinaḥ tadā prasiddhe dharmiṇi śāstra viruddha pratijñā samaye sva upagama svīkṛta pramāṇa tvāt sva vacana ātmakam jātam vacanam śāstrañca svayam abhyupagata prāmāṇya yuktam tulya kakṣam yathā sva vāci mātā me bandhyā iti vacana mātrayoḥ pratibandha unyonyam tayoḥ śāstra vacanayoḥ virūddha artha abhidhāyinoḥ madhye yasya pramāṇam anuvarttakam asti tat pramāṇa vat anyasya apramāṇakasya bādhakam bhavati yathā anitya tvam nityasya śabde 
[447,vi_447,vii]	pratijñām anumānam vā pratijñā apeta yuktikā tulya kakṣāḥ yathārtham vā bādheta katham anyathā anyathā yadi pramāṇa siddhe dharmiṇi pramāṇān anugṛhītayoḥ parasparam bādhā pramāṇa abhāve kena itarasya na ābādheti iṣyate tadā pratijñā viparītā śāstra vacana ākhyā apeta yuktikā pratijñā pramāṇya abhyupagamāt tulya kakṣā satī katham bādheta yathā śabde nitya tva pratijñā śāstra uktā anitya tva pratijñām vidyamānam anumānam vā yathārtham vastu bhūta kṛtaka tva liṅga samuttham nitya tva pratijñayā katham bādhitam syāt anitya tvāt 
[448,i_448,ii]	prāmāṇyam āgamānāñca prāk eva vinivāritam abhyupāya vicāreṣu tasmāt doṣoyam iṣyate tasmāt viṣaya bhedasya darśana artham pṛthakkṛtaḥ anumāna ābarhiḥ bhūta upi abhyupāyaḥ prabādhanāt tasmāt kārya liṅga tvāt anumānāt abahis bhūta upi abhyupāyaḥ viṣayasya bhedaḥ nānātvam tad darśana artham anumānāt pṛthakkṛtaḥ anumānam sarvatra bādhakam śāstrantu śāstra āśraye dharmiṇī iti bādhaka tva viṣaya bheda upadarśanam pṛthak karaṇa phalam katham jñāyate anumāna abahis bhūtam śāstram iti āha sva siddhe dharmiṇi sva upagama viruddhasya dharmasya prabādhanāt na hi apramāṇamba adhakam pramāṇañcā pratyakṣa tvāt anumānam eva 
[448,iii_448,v]	anyathā atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt vyartha tā vā pṛthakkṛteḥ anyathā yadi viṣaya bheda upadarśana phalam pṛthak karaṇam na iṣyate tadā prabheda darśana artham vaktavyam tathā ca kārya svabhāva anupalambhānām prabhedaḥ yāvat sambhavam vācyaḥ iti atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt atha sat api bheda antaram na ucyate tadā anumānāt śāstrasya pṛthak kṛteḥ vyarthatā vā syāt prabheda vacanasya avivakṣita tvāt sāmānya vacanasya anumānena eva siddha tvāt yadi viṣaya bheda upadarśana artham anumānāt pṛthak vacanam śāstrasya tadā abhyupagamāt sva vacanam ācāryeṇa kim artham pṛthakkṛtam yathā sarva m uktam mṛṣā iti tathā aulūkyasya nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti 
[448,vi_448,ix]	atra āha bhedaḥ vāc mātra vacane pratibandhaḥ sva vācī api sva vāci api bhedaḥ sva vacanasya api śāstrāt pṛthak karaṇam apramāṇakam vacanam vāc mātram tasmin pratibandhaḥ uccāraṇa sāmarthyāt abhyupagata prāmāṇyam sva vacanam anyathā uccāraṇam eva na syāt satya artha tā ca prāmāṇyam tat mṛṣā artha tayā vācyayā niṣedhyate iti tulya kakṣa tayā pratibandhaḥ eva anayoḥ na bādhā tat enam vākyam sva artham pratibadhnāti vākya antara nirdiṣṭam vastu śāstram iti anayoḥ bhedaḥ iti uktam 
[448,x_449,ii]	syāt etat tena abhyupāgamāt śāstram pramāṇam sarva vastuṣu bādhakam yadi na icchet sa bādhakam kimpunar bhavet śāstrasya tena vādinā abhyupagamāt sarvatra vastuṣu dharmiṣu śāstra siddhe vastu bala pravṛtte pramāṇa niściteṣu ca śāstram pramāṇam sat bādhakam eva syāt viparīta pratijñāyāḥ na pratibandhakam tat katham pramāṇīkṛta śāstrasya mīmān sakasya śabde pratyakṣa siddhe kṛtaka tvāt anitya tva pratijñāyāḥ sādhyamānāyāḥ śāstreṇa pratibandhaḥ na bādhā iti uktam atha sa vādī yadi śāstram pramāṇam na icchet tadā kim punar ddharmasya asukha pradatvasya bādhāyām pramāṇam bhavet na hi apramāṇam kvacid pramāṇīkṛta śāstrasya śabde pratyakṣa siddhe bhavitum arhati 
[449,iii_449,v]	dharmasya sukha pradatvena nirdeśāt asukha pradatve sādhye sva vacana virodhaḥ eva iti ced evam tarhi svavāc virodhe abhedaḥ syāt sva vāc śāstra virodhayoḥ puruṣa icchā akṛtā ca asya paripūrṇṇā pramāṇa tā svavāc virodhe abhyupagamyamāne sva vāc śāstra virodhayoḥ abhedaḥ eva syāt dvayoḥ abhyupagama siddha pramāṇa tvāt puruṣa icchā kṛtā ca asya śāstrasya paripūrṇṇā pramāṇa tā iti upahasati sati api āgamasu a vacanayoḥ abhyupagamāhita prāmāṇyāt abhede bheda darśana nimittañca uktam 
[449,vi_449,viii]	yasmāt śāstram tat siddhaḥ eva dharmiṇi liṅge ca bādhakam na tu pramāṇa siddhepi tasmāt prasiddhaṣu artheṣu śāstra tyāgepi na kṣatiḥ parokṣeṣu āgamā aniṣṭau na cintā eva pravarttate tasmāt pratyakṣa anumānābhyām prasiddheṣu dharmi liṅga sādhya sambandha ādiṣu satsu śāstra tyāgepi na kṣatiḥ yathā śabda kṛta tva anitya tva sambandha ādiṣu pramāṇa siddheṣu śāstrasya ākāśa guṇa tva pratipādakasya tyāgepi na aniṣṭam parokṣeṣu dharma adharma ādiṣu punar āgamasya pramāṇa tvena aniṣṭau cintā eva na pravarttate na hi asiddhe dharmiṇi vicāraḥ 
[449,ix_450,ii]	nanu śāstrañced na pramāṇam kathantad siddhe dharmiṇi liṅga ādau vā vicāraḥ iti āha virodha udbhāvana prāyā parīkṣā api atra tat yathā adharma mūlam rāga ādi snānañca adharma nāśanam atra śāstre parīkṣā api yā kriyate sā pūrva aparābhyām virodha udbhāvana prāyā na vāstavī tat yathā adharmasya mūlam rāga ādi iti kvacid uktam snānañca adharma nāśanam iti atra ucyamānam viruṇaddhi rāga ādayaḥ hi pāpanidānam na ca nidāna avirodhe nidāninaḥ bādhā tat katham rāga ādi avirodhi snānam pāpa virodhi syāt apramāṇe śāstre virodha udbhāvana prāya api cintā kasmāt pravarttyate iti ced dāna ādi cetanānām pravṛtteḥ mahā anuśaṃsā śravaṇāt hiṃsā ādi cetanānām mahā pāpa śravaṇāt ca apekṣita phaleṣu dāna ādiṣu ayam puruṣaḥ pravṛtti kāmaḥ na āgama prāmāṇyam anāśritya asitum samarthaḥ 
[450,iii_450,v]	tatas śāstram yat siddhayā yuktyā sva vācā ca na bādhyate dṛṣṭe adṛṣṭepi tat grāhyam iti cintā pravarttyate yat śāstram dṛṣṭe pramāṇe viṣaye yuktyā pratyakṣa ādi ākhyayā na bādhyate adṛṣṭe pramāṇa viṣaye ca sva vācā agama āśrayeṇa anumānena na bādhyate tad pramāṇa tvena adṛṣṭe viṣaye pravṛtti kāmasya grāhyam na tu yat kiñcid iti anena prayojanena śāstre virodha udbhāvana prāyā cintā pravarttyate 
[450,vi_451,iii]	śāstra sva vacana virodhau vyākhyātau pratīti bādhām vyākhyātum āha artheṣu apratiṣiddha tvāt puruṣa icchā anurodhinaḥ iṣṭa śabda abhidheyasya āptaḥ vā akṣata vāc janaḥ iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tvasya abhimata vācya tvasya puruṣa icchā anurodhinaḥ puruṣa icchā adhīnasya artheṣu apratiṣiddha tvāt na hi puruṣa icchāyām api śaśī candra śabdam vācaka tayā na svīkaroti tatas ca atra iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tve viṣaye āptaḥ vyavaharttā janaḥ akṣata vāga pratiṣiddha iṣṭa vacanaḥ anena śabdena ayam arthaḥ mayā abhidhātavyaḥ iti kalpanā viṣaya tvam iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tvam tatra ca puruṣasya āropeṇa sva icchā adhīnā vacana pravṛttiḥ tasmāt iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tva bādhaḥ pakṣī kriyam āḥ tena eva sva samvedana siddhena bādhyate 
[451,iv_451,v]	uktaḥ prasiddha śabdena dharmaḥ tad vyavahāra jaḥ pratyakṣa ādi mitāḥ māna śruti āropeṇa sūcitāḥ candraḥ candraḥ iti ādi śabda vyavahārāt jātaḥ dharmaḥ kalpanā viṣayaḥ yogyatā ākhya ācāryeṇa prasiddha śabdena tat yathā śābda prasiddhena ityādinā uktaḥ śābdī prasiddhiḥ vyavahāraḥ śābda prasiddhiḥ tad bhavaḥ viṣayaḥ śābda prasiddhaḥ tena bādhā iti arthaḥ na kevalam iha eva pratyakṣa ādi bādhāsu api māna śratau meyasya āropeṇa pratyakṣa ādibhyām anumāna āgamābhyām mita arthāḥ eva virodhinaḥ vācaka tve pakṣasya sūcitāḥ 
[451,vi_451,viii]	na hi pratyakṣa anumāne puruṣa citta vartinī āgamaḥ ca bādhyamāne dharmiṇi sambhavanti tad upalabdha tad dharmmāḥ santaḥ yujyante bādhakāḥ tasmāt tad āśraya bhuvām icchā anurodhāt aniṣedhinām kṛtānām akṛtānām ca yogyam viśvam svabhāvataḥ tasya lokasya āśrayeṇa bhuvām bhavatām śabdānām vyāvahārikāṇām icchā anurodhinām artheṣu vācaka tva pravṛtteḥ kāraṇāt kvacid api viṣaye aniṣedhinām niṣedha rahitānām kṛtānām saṃketitānām asaṃketita anāñca viśvam idam vācya tvena svabhāvāt eva yogyam 
[451,ix_452,ii]	yatas ca iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tva yogya tā sarvatra sambhavati atas viśeṣa anapekṣaṇāt artha mātra anurodhinyā bhāvinyā bhūtayā api vā bādhyate pratirundhānaḥ śabda yogya tayā tayā artha mātra anurodhinyā tayā śabda yogya tayā bhāvi saṃketa apekṣayā bhāvinyā atīta saṃketa apekṣayā bhūtayā api vā vyavasthitayā tām eva yogyatām pratirundhānaḥ yathā acandraḥ śaśī satvāt iti bādhyate 
[452,iii_452,iv]	tad yogya tā balāt eva vastutas ghaṭitaḥ dhvaniḥ sarvosyām apratītepi tasmin tad siddha tā tatas yogya tā balāt eva vastutas sāmarthyāt sarvaḥ saṃketitaḥ asaṃkitataḥ ca dhvaniḥ asyām yogyatāyām ghaṭitaḥ sambaddhaḥ sākṣāt vācaka tvena tasmin śabde apratītepi vastuni aprātikūlya lakṣaṇasya yogya tvasya sarvadā sthiteḥ yatas evam tatas tasyāḥ yogyatāyaḥ śabda prasiddha tā ācāryeṇa uktā yat yatra samartha tad asaṃmukhībhāvepi tat tena vyapadiśyate yathā pācakaḥ iti samarthañca vastu iṣṭa śabda abhidheyatvaḥ iti kṛtvā śābda prasiddhaḥ iti 
[452,v_452,vi]	asādhāraṇa tā na syāt bādhā hetoḥ iha anyathā tad niṣedhaḥ anumānāt syāt śabda arthe anakṣa vṛttitaḥ anyathā yadi śabdaḥ asaṃmukhībhavan api yogyatāyām na sambaddhaḥ tadā iha śabda yogya tā pratiṣedhe karttavye bādhā hetoḥ a candraḥ śaśī satva ādeḥ iti ādeḥ asādhāraṇa tā uktā na syāt sarvasya candra śabda yogya tve sa pakṣa abhāva ātma tva sādhāraṇam syāt na anyathā śabda arthe yogya tā lakṣaṇe kalpite anakṣa vṛttitaḥ akṣa vṛtti abhāvāt pratyakṣa bādhaka mititasyāḥ yogyatāyāḥ niṣedha unumānāt syāt 
[452,vii_452,viii]	asādhāraṇa tā tatra hetūnām yatra na anvayi sattvam iti asya udāhāraḥ hetoḥ evam kutas mataḥ tatra yogyatā pratiṣedhe karttavye sarveṣām hetūnām sa pakṣa abhāvāt asādhāraṇa tā katham etat iti āha yatra sādhye sattvam api liṅgam sarva vastu vyāpi nā anvayi sādhāraṇam bhavati tatra anyasya kā kathā iti hetoḥ kṛtaka tvasya udāhāraḥ ācāryesya evam phalaḥ sarva hetu asādhāraṇa tva pratipādana prayodanaḥ mataḥ 
[453,i_453,iii]	katham gamyate sarveṣām śabdānām sarvatra arthe siddhiḥ iti āha saṃketa saṃśrayāḥ śabdāḥ sa ca icchā mātra saṃśrayaḥ na asiddhiḥ śabda siddhānām iti śābda prasiddhi vāc saṅketam antareṇa vācaka adṛṣṭeḥ saṃketa saṃśrayāḥ śabdāḥ sa ca saṃketaḥ puruṣa icchā mātra saṃśrayaḥ tad atiriktasya apekṣaṇīyasya abhāvāt tasmāt śabda siddhānām abhidheya tva ādīnām kvacid api arthe na asiddhiḥ iti hetoḥ śābda prasiddhiḥ ācāryasya 
[453,iv_453,vi]	etat ca śābda prasiddhi vacanam anumāna prasiddheṣu viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ abhāvaḥ darśayati evam pratīteḥ anumātvataḥ vastu bala pravṛttena anumānena prasiddheṣu artheṣu viparīta dharma upasthāpakasya viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ sādhana antarasya abhāvan darśayati kasmāt iti āha evam īdṛśyāḥ śabda siddhāyāḥ yogyatāyāḥ pratīte svabhāva liṅga samuttha tvāt anumātvataḥ yathā śabda siddhā yogya tā anumāna siddhā iti bādhyā satva ādi hetunā tathā anyopi vastu bala pravṛtta anumāna viṣayaḥ samāna tvāt nyāyasya iti arthaḥ 
[453,vii_453,viii]	athavā bruvataḥ lokasya anumā abhāvaḥ ucyate kintena bhinna viṣayā pratītiḥ anumānataḥ athavā acandraḥśaśī satvāt iti vipratipadyamānam pratipad pratipādana artham lokasya bruvataḥ śābda prasiddhena asādhāraṇa tvāt anumāna abhāvaḥ ācāryeṇa ucyate pāramārthikasya bādhya tvasya abhāvāt kalpitam niṣedhyam tat ca puruṣa icchā mātra adhīna tvāt sarvatra sambhavati iti sarvasya candra śabda yogya tā yogāt na kaścid acandraḥ pakṣosti yatra varttamān aṃsattvam asādhāraṇa tām jahyā evandarśite kimbhavati iti ced tena anumāna abhāva abhidhāyinā śabda prasiddha abhidhānena śabda siddhā pratītiḥ vastu bala pravṛtta anumānataḥ bhinna viṣaya uktā bhavati vastu viṣayam hi anumānam kalpita gocara antarā śābdī pratītiḥ iti arthaḥ 
[454,i_454,ii]	tena anumānāt vastūnām sat asat ta anurodhinaḥ bhinnasya ātad vaśā vṛttiḥ tat icchā jā iti sūcitam tena viṣaya bhedena vastūnām sat asat ta anurodhinaḥ anumānāt bhinnasya kalpitasya arthasya śabda yogya tvasya vṛttiḥ atad vaśā vastu anāyattā tasya puruṣasya icchā jā iti sūcitam bhavati 
[454,iii_454,v]	kiñca candra tām śaśinaḥ anicchān kām prati iti sa vāñchati iti tam pratyadṛṣṭāntam tat asādhāraṇam matam śaśinaḥ sarva jana siddhām vyāvahārikī candra tā candra śabda vācya tām anicchan paraḥkām anyām pratītim sa vāñchati yayā vācya tā siddhiḥ kvacid syāt matā ca pāramārthikī vācya tā pratītiḥ na kvacid asti vastutas sarvasya avācya tā pradarśanāt kalpiva ācyatā pratītiḥ tu puruṣa icchā mātra prabhava tvāt sarvatra avyāhata eva atas sarvasya candra śabda vācya tā yogāt sa pakṣaḥ na asti iti tam candra tā palāpinam vādinam prati satvam liṅgam adṛṣṭa antam asādhāraṇam uktam ācāryeṇa na tu candrasya ekasya anyatra asambhavāt sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ abhāvāt asādhāraṇa tvam abhipretam ācāryasya acandra tve sādhye ghaṭa ādeḥ sa pakṣasya satvāt candraḥ tu vipakṣaḥ mā bhūt tathā api hetu nivṛttiḥ asmāt avyāhata eva asatā upi hetu nivṛtteḥ sādhanāt 
[454,vi_454,viii]	apica na udāharaṇam eva idam adhikṛtya idam ucyate lakṣaṇa tvāt tathā vṛkṣaḥ adhātri iti uktau ca bādhanāt acandraḥ śaśī sattvāt iti etat eva udāharaṇam adhikṛtya idam śabda vācya tva pratikṣepa heta urasādhāraṇa tvam na ucyate lakṣaṇa tvāt lakṣaṇena hi lakṣyam vyāptam darśanīyam na ca dvitīya candra abhāvena usādharaṇa toktiḥ udāharaṇa antaram vyāpnoti yathā vā candra tāyāḥ pratītyai bādhā iṣyate tathā adhātrī vṛkṣaḥ sattvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti udāharaṇa uktau sarva loka siddhayā puruṣa icchā adhīnayā ghaṭa ādau api vṛkṣa śabda yogya tā pratītyā sa pakṣa abhāvena asādhāraṇa tvāt vṛkṣa śabda vācya tva abhāvasya sādhanāt yathā uktam eva asādhāraṇa tvam ācāryasya iṣṭam 
[455,i_455,iii]	yat api ucyate dvitīyasya candrasya abhāvāt asādhāraṇa tā iti tatra āha atra api loke dṛṣṭa tvāt karpūra rajata ādiṣu samayāt vartamānasya kā asādhāraṇa tā api vā loke karppūra rajata ādiṣu gāndhika vācika ādīnām samayāt varttamānasya dṛṣṭa tvāt atra acandraḥ śaśī sattva āt iti udāharaṇe hetoḥ asādhāraṇa tā api kā vā yadi dvitīya candraḥ na bhavet evam asādhāraṇa tā syāt vastu tvasya 
[455,iv_455,ix]	syāt etat tad samayāt api varttamānasya candra tva ādeḥ na śabda vācya tā tatas yathā na vahni śabda vācya tā karppūrasya tathā candra śabda vācya tā ca na syāt iti asādhāraṇa tā eva iti āha yadi tasya kvacid sidhyet siddham vastu balena tat tasya evaṃvādinaḥ sati api sāmayike candre kvacid artha viśeṣe candra śabda vācya tvam yadi sidhyet na tu sarvatra karpūra rajata ādau tadā tat candra śabda vācya tva vastu balena siddham syāt na tu evam dṛśyate sarvasya karpūra ādeḥ ca śabda abhidheya tva darśanāt atha yatra eva kalpyate candra tvam tat eva tad śabda vācyam pratīyate iti tathā abhyupagamyate tadā pratīti siddha pagame aśaśini api anivāraṇam sāmayike candra tve kvāpi pratītyā siddhasya candra śabda vācya tvasya upagame śaśini api tad śabda vācyasya anivāraṇam 
[455,x_455,xi]	tasya vastuni siddhasya śaśini api anivāraṇam tat vasttu a bhāve śaśini vāraṇepi na duṣyati śukla tā ādike nimitta bhūte vastuni tasya candra śabda abhidheya tvasya siddhasya śaśini api nimitta sadbhāvāt anivāraṇam tasya nimitta bhūtasya vastunaḥ śaśini abhāve tu candra śabda vācya tvasya vastu tvāt hetoḥ vāraṇepi na kiñcid duṣyati nimitta abhāve naimittika abhāva asya iṣṭa tvāt sāmayikantu sarvatra aśakya vāraṇam iti tad śabda yogya tāpya bādhyā 
[456,i_456,ii]	tasmāt avastu niyata saṃketa bala bhāvinām yogyāḥ padārthāḥ dharmāṇām icchāyāḥ anirodhānāt tasmāt avastu niyataḥ vastuni aniyate icchā adhīna tvāt saṃketaḥ tasya balāt bhāvinām dharmmāṇām vācya tva ādīnām padārthāḥ sarve dharmi tvena yogyāḥ icchātaḥ puṃsaḥ kenacid vācya tva ādi utthāpikāyāḥ icchāyāḥ anirodhāt 
[456,iii_456,iv]	tām yogyatām virundhānam saṃketa apratiṣedha jā pratihanti prati iti ākhyā yogya tā viṣaye anumā tām iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tva yogya tām padārthānām sattva ādikāt hetoḥ virundhānam pratikṣipantam vādinam prati iti ākhyā pratīti saṃjñitā anumā pratihanti saṃketa apratiṣedha jā iti svabhāva liṅga ja tvam āha icchā adhīna tvāt yogya tā viṣaye viparīta dharma upasthānam āha prayogaḥ punar yaḥ puruṣa icchā anubhidhāyī sa sarvatra sambhavī tat yathā vikalpaḥ puruṣa icchā anuvidhāyi ca artheṣu iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tvam iti 
[456,v_456,vi]	śabdānām artha niyamaḥ saṃketa anuvidhāyinām na iti anena uktam atra eṣām pratiṣedhaḥ virudhyate anena ceṣṭa śabda abhidheya tva yogya tā pratiṣedha bādhanena darśitena śabdānām saṃketa anuvidhāyinām artha niyamaḥ pratiniyata vācaka tvam na iti uktam bhavati tatosya sva icchā kalpitaḥ arthe eṣām śabdānām vācaka tvasya pratiṣedhaḥ sattva ādi hetoḥ kriyamāṇaḥ virudhyate 
[456,vii_457,i]	yadi evantadā kvacid arthe niṣedham kurvatā śabdaḥ bādhyaḥ syāt tatas ca guṇa ādikam nimitta bhūtam guṇa ādi śabdānām guṇa guṇi sambandha ādi pāramārthikam artham guṇi śabda ādīnām niṣedhan bādhyaḥ syāt iti āha yena kalpitam artham śabdānām bādhamānaḥ pratikṣipyate na tu guṇa ādikam tena naimittikyāḥ śruteḥ artham artham vā pāramārthikam śabdānām pratirundhānaḥ abādhana arhaḥ hi varṇṇitaḥ naimittikyāḥ vastu bhūta guṇa ādi nimittavatyāḥ śruteḥ artham guṇa ādikam pāramārthikam artham guṇi guṇa ādi sambandham śabdānām guṇyādi vācinām pratirundhānaḥ abādhana arhaḥ bādhām na arhati iti uktaḥ bhavati 
[457,ii_457,iv]	yasmāt ca sāṃketika artha nirākaraṇe pratīti bādhā tasmāt viṣaya bhedasya darśanāya pṛthakkṛtā anumāna abahis bhūtā pratītiḥ api pūrvavat tasmāt svabhāva liṅga ja tvena anumānāt abahis bhūtā pratītiḥ api tasmāt pṛthakkṛtā kimartham iti āha viṣayasya bhedaḥ kalpita akalpita tvam tasya darśanāya kalpita artha viṣayā pratītiḥ vastu viṣayantu anumānam iti arthaḥ pūrvavat iti yathā āgama sva vacane abhyupagata prāmāṇye apratyakṣa tvāt anumāna antargatepi viṣaya bheda darśanāya pṛthak darśite vastu bala pravṛttenu mānam sarva viṣaya vicāre tu āgama sva vacane adhikṛte tathā prati iti anumāne api bhinna viṣaye iti arthaḥ 
[457,v_457,vii]	anumāna bādhāyām antarbhāvāt anayoḥ abhyupagama pratīti bādhayoḥ siddhayoḥ pṛthak ākhyāne darśayan ca prayojanam ete sa hetuke prāha na anumā adhyakṣa bādhane siddhayoḥ api pṛthak ākhyāne viṣaya bheda lakṣaṇam prayojanandarśayannā cā ryaḥ ete abhyupagama pratīti bādhe sa hetuke prāha na santi pramāṇāni prameya arthāni iti pratijñā mātreṇa iti atra pratijñā mātram śāstra sva vacanayoḥ siddhayoḥ aprāmāṇya pratijña ābādhakam uktam atopya sādhāraṇa tvāt anumāna abhāve śābda prasiddhena apodyate na sa pakṣaḥ iti atra śābda prasiddhena śaśinaḥ candra tvena acandra tva pratijñāyāḥ bādhanam uktam anumādhyakṣa bādhane tu na sa hetuke prāha aśrāvaṇaḥ śabdaḥ nityaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti tasmāt viṣaya bheda upalakṣaṇa artha sa hetu tvā hetu tva darśanam pratyakṣa anumāna bādhe sarva aviṣaye abhyupagama pratīti bādhe tu niyata viṣaye iti arthaḥ 
[457,viii_458,iv]	uktā pratīti bādhā pratyakṣa bādhā vaktavyā na kevalam śābda prasiddhe vyavahāra dharma prasiddhau tad pratiroddhā bādhyate kintu atra api adhyakṣa bādhāyām nānā rūpa tayā dhvanau prasiddhasya śrutau atra api adhyakṣa bādhāyām vyāvahārika kalpanā vaśāt nānā rūpa tayā loke prasiddhasya khyātasya dhvanau śrutau śravaṇa jñāne rūpam yat eva pratibhāsate advayam śabala ābhāsasya adṛṣṭeḥ buddhi janmanaḥ tad artha artha uktiḥ asya eva kṣepe adhyakṣeṇa bādhanam 
[458,v]	yat eva rūpam advayam dharma ādi dvaya śūnyam pratibhāsate śabala ābhāsasya nānā ākārasya buddhi janmanaḥ adṛṣṭeḥ yadi nānā kara tā śabdasya vāstavī syāt tathā eva śruti jñāne pratibhāseta tad arthā tad pratipādana phalā acāryasya pratyakṣa anumāna artha prasiddhena nirākṛta eti atra artha uktiḥ artha grahaṇam asya adhyakṣa siddhasya eva rūpasya kṣepe adhyakṣeṇa bādhanam iṣṭam 
[458,vi_458,vii]	tat eva rūpam tatra arthaḥ śeṣam vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇam avastu bhūtam sāmānyam atas tat na akṣa gocaraḥ tatra śruti jñāne bhāsamānam tad rūpam arthaḥ sva lakṣaṇam tat atiriktam śeṣam dharmi dharma ādi vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇam anya vyavaccheda svabhāvam avastu bhūtam sarvatra sambhavāt sāmānyañca atas avastu tva ādeḥ tad guṇa jāti ādi na akṣa gocaraḥ 
[459,i_459,ii]	tena samānya dharmāṇām apratyakṣa tva siddhitaḥ pratikṣepa ipi abādhā iti śrāvaṇa uktyā prakāśitam tena avastu tvena kāraṇena sāmānya dharmāṇām prameya tva ādīnām apratyakṣa tvasya siddhitaḥ kenacid vādinā pratyakṣa siddhitaḥ pratikṣepa ipi kriyamāṇe na bādhya bādhaka bhāva iti aśrāvaṇaḥ iti atra śrāvaṇa uktyā niṣedhya darśikayā prakāśitam sva lakṣaṇa bādhane pratyakṣa bādhā iti arthaḥ 
[459,iii_459,v]	evam tarhi śabda sva lakṣaṇam na asti iti eva kasmāt na ucyate kim śrāvaṇa tva mukhyam niṣedhya yuktiḥ iti āha sarvathā avācya rūpa tvāt siddhyā tasya samāśrayāt bādhanāt tad balena uktaḥ śrāvaṇena akṣa gocaraḥ sva lakṣaṇasya sarvathā kenacid śabdena avācya tvāt mukhyam abhidhānam na asti eva atha sāmānya vṛttiḥ api sva lakṣaṇa śabdaḥ adhyavasāya anurodhāt sva lakṣaṇam upalakṣayati evam śrāvaṇa śabda upīndriya grāhya tā upalakṣaṇam śabdasva lakṣaṇam upalakṣayiṣyati iti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ athavā asti eva śrāvaṇa śabdena abhidhāne prayojanam iti āha śrotra indriya viṣasya yā siddhiḥ tathā bhāvaḥ tayā siddhyā tasya indriya jñānasya samāśrayāt śabdasya svarūpa vyavasthityā hetunā tena vyapadeśaḥ indriya jñāna balena śabda svarūpa pāvasthitaḥ tathā abhidhānam iti arthaḥ kiñca tasya indriya jñānasya balena śabda sva lakṣaṇa viparyaya bhāvasya bādhānāt kāraṇāt śrāvaṇena akṣa gocaraḥ sva lakṣaṇa muktaḥ nityaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti anumāne nitya tva viṣayeṇa kṛtaka tva liṅga bhuvā bādhitaḥ pakṣaḥ sa ca asakṛt darśitaḥ eva iti na iha vipañcitaḥ 
[459,vi_460,i]	idānīm pratyakṣa anumāna āpta prasiddhena svadharmiṇī iti svadharmi grahaṇasya sāphalyam ākhyātum āha sarvatra vādinaḥ dharmaḥ yaḥ sva sādhyatayā upsitaḥ tat dharmavati bādhā syāt na anya dharmeṇa dharmiṇi sarvatra vāda kāle sādhya kāle vā vādinaḥ sva sādhya tayā yaḥ dharmaḥ īpsitaḥ tat harbhavati dharmiṇi bādhā syāt yathā śrāvaṇa tvavati śabde bādhite bādhā pakṣasya na tu vādīṣṭāt dharmāt anyena dharmeṇa dharmavati dharmiṇi bādhite bādhā pakṣasya syāt iti dharmi graha prayojanam yathā ākāśa guṇa tvavati śabde bādhitenam pakṣa bādhā 
[460,ii_460,iii]	anyathā asya uparodhaḥ kaḥ bādhitenyatra dharmiṇi gata arthe lakṣaṇena asmin svadharmi vacanam punar anyathā yadi evam na iṣyate tadā anyatra dharme dharmiṇi bādhite asya prakṛta dharma viśiṣṭasya dharmiṇaḥ kaḥ uparodhaḥ bādha nanu sva rūpeṇa eva nirdeśyaḥ svayam iṣṭaḥ anirākṛtaḥ pakṣaḥ iti pakṣa lakṣaṇena eva aniṣṭa dharmavataḥ dharmiṇaḥ bādhā na pakṣa bādha iti labhyate eva iti āha pakṣasya lakṣaṇena asmin vādi iṣṭa dharmavati dharmiṇi bādhya tvena gata arthe punar svadharmi vacanam yat kṛtam 
[460,iv_460,v]	bādhāyām dharmiṇopi syāt bādheti asya prasiddhaye āśrayasya virodhena tad āśrita virodhanāt dharmiṇā api bādhāyām dharmasya bādhane pakṣa bādhā yathā syāt iti asya arthasya prasiddhaye kvacid āśrayasya dharmiṇaḥ virodhena pratikṣepeṇa tad āśritasya dharmasya virodhanāt dharma dvāreṇa dharmi dvāreṇa vā samudāya bādhāyām pakṣa bādhā iti arthaḥ 
[460,vi_460,vii]	anyathā evaṃvidhaḥ dharmaḥ sādhyaḥ iti abhidhānataḥ tad bādhām eva manyeta svadharmi grahaṇantataḥ anyathā dharmi dvāreṇa samudāya bādhāyāḥ saṃgraha artham svadharmi grahaṇam yadi na kriyate tadā evamvidhaḥ sādhya tvena eva iṣṭaḥ dharmaḥ sādhyaḥ iti abhidhānataḥ tasyam dharma mātrasya eva bādhām manyeta pratipattā na tu dharmi bādhām api tatas ubhaya saṃgraha artham svadharmi grahaṇam ācāryasya 
[460,viii_461,ii]	nanu etat api artha siddham satyam kecid tu dharmiṇaḥ kevalasya uparodha īpi doṣavattām upāgatāḥ nanu etat ubhaya saṃgrahaṇam api arthataḥ sāmarthyaṃtaḥ siddham na hi kevalaḥ dharma usti kvacid tad vādhane tad viśiṣṭasya dharmiṇā api bādhanāt samudāya bādha evaiṣitavyā sā ca dharmi dvāreṇa vā bhavatu dharma dvāreṇa vā na kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti arthaḥ atra āha satyam etat kecid tu vādinaḥ dharmiṇoḥ kevalasya uparodhe sādhya dharmasya ābādhāyām api pakṣasya doṣavattām upāgatāḥ pratipannāḥ 
[461,iii_461,iv]	yathā paraiḥ anutpādya apūrvarūpan na kha ādikam sakṛt śabda ādi ahetu tvāt iti ukte prāha dūṣakaḥ yathā paraiḥ saha kāribhiḥ anutpādya āpūrva rūpam na kha ādikam ākāśa diś kāla ādi na bhavati api tu utpādya pūrvarūpam eva bhavati sakṛt eka kālantad utpādyasya kārya kālapasya śabda ādeḥ ahetu tvāt aviśiṣṭa eka rūpāt kāraṇāt sakṛt sarva kārya utpatti prasaṅgāt iti vādinā ukte dūṣakaḥ prativādya āha 
[461,v_461,vi]	tadvat vastu svabhāvaḥ asan dharmī vyomādiḥ iti api na evam iṣṭasya sādhyasya bādhā kācana vidyate tadvat yathā anutpādya apūrva rūpaḥ ākāśa ādiḥ na bhavati tathā vastu svabhāvaḥ dharmī vyoma ādirasan iti api syāt artha kriyā asamarthasya vastu tva abhāvāt iti dharmiṇaḥ kevalasya bādhanam na dharmasya evam dharmi bādhana īpi iṣṭasya sādhyasya kācana bādhā na vidyate hetoḥ vā asiddhiḥ asatī api kārya anutpādasya vyavacchedasya siddheḥ 
[461,vii_462,ii]	tatas dvayasya api hi sādhya tve sādhya dharma uparodhi yat bādhanam dharmiṇaḥ tatra bādhā iti etena varṇṇitam dvayasya dharmi dharma samudāyasya api hi sādhya tve sati yatra dharmiṇaḥ bādhanam sādhya dharma uparodhi tatra pakṣa bādhā yuktā iti etena svadharmi grahaṇena varṇṇitam na hi sādhya dharma mātra sādhana artham kaścid sādhanam anveṣate tasya jagati kvacid sattāyām vivāda abhāvāt tathā niścaye pravṛtti ayogāt ca kintu dharmi viśeṣa niṣṭham sādhyam iṣṭam 
[462,iii_462,v]	tathā eva dharmiṇā upyatra sādhya tvāt kevalasya na yadi evam atra bādhā syāt tatra yathā dharmi viśiṣṭasya sādhya tvam dharmasya tathā eva sādhya tva viśiṣṭa tvena dharmiṇopi sādhya tvāt kevalasya dharmasya na kvacid sādhya tā tatas na kevalasya dharmiṇaḥ bādhane pakṣa bādhā yadi sādhya dharma uparodhini dharmiṇi bādhite pakṣa bādha iṣyate evam satyatra hetau sāṃkhyam prati bauddhena ukte dharmi bādhā dvāreṇa dharma bādhā syāt na anyā anutpādya śaktikaḥ sakṛt śabda ādi ahetu tvāt sukha ādiḥ iti pūrvavat virodhitā bhavet atra hetuḥ aikāntikaḥ yadi 
[462,vi]	tat yathā sukha ādiḥ sukha duḥkha moha ātmakam pradhānam na anyena sahākāriṇā anutpādya śaktikaḥ anādheya sāmarthyaḥ sakṛt śabda ādīnām kāryāṇām ahehetu tvāt iti atra pūrvavat paraiḥ anutpādya ityādi prayoga tvāt ca sukha ādi ātmakasya nitya tvasya bādhanāt sukha ādau dharmmiṇi bādhite tad dharmmasya nitya tvasya virodhane viparyaya sādhane bādhā syāt anitya svabhāvaḥ hi sukha ādiḥ sādhayitum iṣṭaḥ sukha ādi svabhāva bhūta nitya tva bādhane ca sukha ādiḥ eva bādhitaḥ iti dharma uparodhini dharmiṇi bādhite pakṣa bādhā syāt atra āha bhavet atra hetau pakṣa bādhā yadi na sakṛt śabda ādi anutpādāt iti hetuḥ sādhyasya vastu bhūta sukha ādi anitya tvasya viparyaye sukha ādi dharmya bhāvāt anitya tva abhāvena aikāntikaḥ avyabhicārī bhavet 
[462,vii_463,ii]	yāvatā yā ca krama kriyā anitya tayoḥ avirodhāt vipakṣattaḥ vyāvṛtteḥ saṃśayān na ayam śeṣavat bhedaḥ iṣyate krama kriyāḥ hetuḥ yā ca sādhya anitya tā tayoḥ avirodhāt avastu bhūta dharmi sukha ādi dharma anitya tve viparīte sādhye vastu bhūta sukha ādi dharma anitya tvam vipakṣaḥ tatas hetoḥ krama karaṇa vyāvṛtteḥ saṃśayān na ayam viruddhaḥ hetuḥ śeṣavat bhedaḥ anaikāntika viśeṣaḥ tu iṣyate sati ca viruddha tve dharmi bādhā dvāreṇa dharma bādhā syāt 
[463,iii_463,iv]	svayam iṣṭaḥ yatas dharmaḥ sādhyaḥ tasmāt tad āśrayaḥ bādhyaḥ na kevalaḥ na anya saṃśrayaḥ vā iti sūcitam yatas kāraṇāt svayam vādinā iṣṭaḥ dharmaḥ sādhyaḥ tasmāt sādhya dharmasa āśrayaḥ yaḥ saḥ eva bādhyaḥ kevalaḥ na bādhyaḥ yathā vastu bhūta ākāśa bādhāyām api nitya eka rūpatva abhāvasya sādhya dharmasya na kṣatiḥ sādhya dharmāt anyasya ca dharmasya āśrayaḥ na bādhyaḥ iti svayaṃśabdena sūcitam yathā anitya tve sādhye śabde ākāśa guṇa tva āśraya tvena bādhāyām api na doṣaḥ 
[463,v_463,vii]	tasmāt svayaṃśrutya ani adharmāṇām bādhā abādhā iti kathyate tathā svadharmiṇā anyasya dharmiṇā upī iti kathyate svayaṃśrutyā sādhyāt dharmāt anyeṣām dharmāṇām yathā bādhā yā sā abādhā iti kathyate tathā svadharmiṇā sva dharmi vacanena sādhyāt anyasya dharmasya dharmiṇaḥ bādhā abādhā iti kathyate 
[463,viii_464,i]	tathā aparepi pakṣa ābhāsāḥ santi te kasmāt na ucyante tathā hi aprasiddha viśeṣyaḥ kaścid pakṣaḥ yathā vibhuḥ ātmā ātmanaḥ eva bauddha syāsiddha tvāt kaścid prasiddha viśeṣaṇaḥ yathā vināśī śabdaḥ sāṃkhyam pramāṇam prati tasya vināśa asiddheḥ kaścid aprasiddha ubhayaḥ yathā samavāyi kāraṇam ātmā bauddhasya ubhayā siddheḥ iti nanu asiddha upya ātmā pakṣī bhaviṣyati tad lakṣaṇa yogāt na hi asiddhasya pakṣatā nirastā āśraya asiddha tvāt hetoḥ na pakṣaḥ iti ced na 
[464,ii]	sādhana doṣoyam na pakṣa doṣaḥ tathā śabde anitya tvam viṣeśaṇam asiddham iti guṇaḥ eva ayam na pakṣa doṣaḥ asiddhasya eva sādhya tvāt atha viparyaya siddhyā asiddham ucyate tathā api mūḍhasya viparyaya siddhau api na ayam pakṣa doṣaḥ virodhaḥ nāma hetu doṣaḥ eva ayam pramāṇena ca viparyaya siddhau pramāṇa bādhita tvam eva pakṣa doṣoḥ tu alama prasiddha viśeṣaṇa tva abhidhānena aprasiddha ubhayasya tu ubhaya doṣāt ca sarve amī hetu doṣāḥ eva iti kim pakṣa doṣāḥ vaktavyāḥ atha 
[464,iii_464,iv]	sarva sādhana doṣeṇa pakṣaḥ eva uparudhyate tathā api pakṣa doṣa tvam pratijñā mātra bhāvinaḥ sarveṇa sādhanasya doṣeṇa asiddha tva ādinā pakṣaḥ eva uparudhyate tena pakṣa doṣāḥ asiddha viśeṣya ādayaḥ abhidhīyante yadi api pakṣa uparodha phalāḥ sarve doṣāḥ tathā api pratijñā mātreṇa bhavana śīlasya doṣasya pakṣa voṣa tvam uktam iṣṭam 
[464,v_464,vii]	yasmāt sākṣāt uttara avayava apekṣaḥ yaḥ doṣaḥ sonubadhyate tena īyuktam atas apakṣa doṣaḥ asiddha āśraya ādikaḥ uttaraḥ avayavaḥ hetu dṛṣṭānta ādiḥ tad apekṣaḥ yaḥ doṣaḥ sa tena hetu ādinā anubadhyate ātmani sambadhyate iti uktam prāk uttara avayava apekṣaḥ na doṣaḥ pakṣaḥ iṣyate ityādinā atas asiddha āśraya ādikaḥ āśraya asiddha tva ādiḥ uttara avayava apekṣaḥ na pakṣa doṣaḥ mataḥ 
[464,viii]	nanu aśrāvaṇaḥ śabdaḥ nityaḥ ghaṭaḥ na anumānam pramāṇam acandraḥ śaśī iti udāharaṇaiḥ ebhiḥ ddharma svarūpa nirākaraṇena bādhā darśitā yathāpratijñāta dharma mātrasya viparīta dharma upasthāpanena nirākaraṇāt dharmi viśeṣasya dharma viśeṣasya dharmi svarūpasya ca bādhanena pakṣa bādhā asti sā katham avagantavyā iti a āha 
[465,i_465,ii]	dharmi dharma viśeṣāṇām svarūpasya ca dharmmiṇaḥ bādhā sādhya aṅga bhūtānām anena eva upadarśitā dharmi dharmayoḥ viśeṣāṇām vyakti bheda apekṣayā bahuvacanam dharmiṇaḥ svarūpasya ca sarveṣām eṣām sādhyam pratyaṅga bhūtānām bādhā anena eva dharma svarūpa nirākaraṇa pareṇa udāharaṇena sādhyate pakṣa lakṣaṇa tvāt vādha upadarśitā 
[465,iii_465,iv]	tatra udāhṛti diś mātram ucyate arthasya dṛṣṭaye dravya lakṣaṇa yuktonyaḥ saṃyogerthosti dṛṣṭi bhāj tatra āśrāvaṇaḥ śabdaḥ iti ādiṣu udāharaṇa diṅa mātram ucyate sādhyāṅaga bhūtasya sarvasya eva bādhā bhavati iti arthasya dṛṣṭaye darśana artha tatra parasya avayavebhyaḥ avayavinaḥ guru tva ādi guṇa yoginaḥ anya tve abhimate yadā ucyate na anyaḥ avayavi avayavebhyaḥ tulān ati viśeṣa agrahaṇāt iti etad dharma viśeṣa nirākaraṇena udāharaṇam boddhavyam tathā hi na atra anya tva mātram niṣeddhum iṣṭam tathā tve dharma svarūpa nirākaraṇa udāharaṇam etat syāt tasmāt anya tvasya sādhya dharmasya na antarīyakāḥ gaurava ādayaḥ viśeṣāḥ nirākarttum iṣṭāḥ tathā ca dharma viśeṣa udāharaṇam eva tat tathā hi paraiḥ ekasya avayavasya anyān i āvayava saṃyoge sati tad anyaḥ arthaḥ avayavi saṃjñitaḥ dravyasya lakṣaṇena kriyāvat guṇavat samavāyi kāraṇañce tyanena yuktaḥ dṛṣṭi bhāj dṛśyoḥ ti iti iṣṭam eva 
[465,v_465,vii]	anyathā adṛśyasyāḥ viśiṣṭasya pratijñā niṣprayojanā iṣṭaḥ hi avayavī kāryam dṛṣṭvā adṛśyeṣu asambhavi adṛśyasya saṃvyavahāra aviṣayasya dravya lakṣaṇena viśiṣṭa sāmānya mātrasya astitva pratijñā niṣprayojanā bhavet tathā hi paramāṇuṣu adṛśyeṣu adarśana āvaraṇa pratighāta ādi kāryam asaṃbhavi dṛṣṭvā avayavī ceṣṭaḥ tasmin darśana ādi kārya yogāt 
[465,viii_466,i]	aviśiṣṭasya ca anyasya sādhane siddha sādhanam guru tva adhas gatī syātām yadi asya syāt tulā ānatiḥ yadi punar anindriya grāhya tvam dravya lakṣaṇena aviśiṣṭanta davayavi dravyam sādhyate tadā aviśiṣṭasya anyasya ca sādhane bauddhasya na kācid kṣatiḥ iti siddha sādhanam syāt tasmāt dṛśyaḥ dravya guṇavān bhāvaḥ avayavī iti sādhyam tatas ca asya avayavinaḥ guru tvam guṇaḥ adhas gatiḥ ca karma yadi syātām tadā mṛd ā ādi khaṇḍayoḥ saha tolitayoḥ yāvatī tulānati gaurava vaśāt dṛṣṭā tatodhikā tulā ānatiḥ syāt yadā tayoḥ mṛd ā ādi khaṇḍayoḥ saṃyoge sati dravya antaram utpadya te tadā tayoḥ pūrva avasthitayoḥ pūrva avasthitam gauravam tadā utpannasya ca dravyasya adhika gaurava viśeṣāt tulā an ati viśaṣaḥ dṛśyeta na ca evam tasmāt na tatra kārya dravya sambhavaḥ iti avayavī nirguṇaḥ niṣkriyaḥ ca syāt 
[466,ii_466,iii]	tad nirguṇa kriyaḥ tasmāt samavāyi na kāraṇam tatas eva na dṛśyosa avadṛṣṭeḥ kārya rūpayoḥ tasmāt nirguṇa kriya tvāt guṇa karmaṇoḥ na samavāyi kāraṇam avayavī tatas eva dravya lakṣaṇa yogāt na tasya āvaraṇa ādi kāryam svarūpam vā kiñcid dṛśyate adarśanāt ca na dṛśyaḥ avayavī 
[466,iv_466,vi]	tad bādhāni aviśeṣasya na antarīyaka bhāvinaḥ tat tasmāt asau avayavinaḥ bādhā anyasya viśeṣasya gaurava adhas gati ādeḥ na antarīyaka bhāvinaḥ sādhya anya tva avinā bhāvinaḥ bādhā iti dharma viśeṣa nirākaraṇe nirdeśaḥ yuktaḥ āsūkṣmāt dravya mālāyāḥ tolya tvāt aṃśu pāta vat dravya antara guru tvasya gatiḥ na iti aparaḥ abravīt 
[466,vii_467,i]	āsūkṣmāt dvi aṇukāt ārabhya dravya mālāyāḥ sthūla avayavi paryantāyāḥ tolya tvāt tat dadravya mālā varttinaḥ sthūlasya dravya antarasya na gatiḥ bhavati tulāyām aṃśu pāta vat karpāsa bhāra patitasya aṃśoḥ ekasya yathā guru tvam sat api na pratīyate tathā dravya mālā varttinaḥ sthūla dravyasya iti aparaḥ abravīt tasya krameṇa saṃyukte pāṃśu rāśau sakṛt yute bhedaḥ syāt gaurave tasmāt pṛthak saha ca tolite suvarṇa māṣaka ādīnām saṃkhyā sāmyam na yujyate 
[467,ii]	tasya evaṃvādinaḥ mate krameṇa sūkṣma avayava saṃyoga abhivṛddhi paripāṭyā saṃyukte sthūla avayavi tām gate pāṃśurāśau ava yava saṃyoga abhivṛddhi kramam anapekṣya sakṛt eka kālam yukte sthūla avayavi tām gate bhedaḥ gaurave syāt tathā hi dvi aṇuka ādi krameṇa kārya dravya saṃyoga paraṃparayā ca dravyam utpadyate tatra aneka dravya bhāra sadbhāvāt mahat gauravam bhavet yatra tu ekaḥ eva sakṛt pāṃśu rāśiḥ saṃyogāt jāyate tatra ekasya dravyasya alpīyaḥ gauravam bhavati na ca asti etat kiñca tasmāt gaurava bhedāt pṛthak pratyekam māṣaka ādau tolite piṇḍa avasthayoḥ saha ca aparaiḥ māṣaka ādibhiḥ tolite suvarṇṇa māsaka ādi bhinnāyāḥ saṃkhyāyāḥ sāmyam na yujyate māsaka avayavinām vināśe tad saṃkhyānām gauravāṇām ca nāśāt ekam suvarṇṇam iti eva syāt dṛśyate ca pratyekam māṣaka ādīnām tulāyām yāvatī saṃkhyā tāvatī eva saha tolitānām api 
[467,iii_467,iv]	sarṣapā dāmahāra āśeḥ uttara uttara vṛddhimat gauravam kārya mālāyāḥ yadi na eva upalabhyate atha raktikāyāḥ caturthaḥ bhāgaḥ sarṣapaḥ tasmāt ārabhya āmahārāśeḥ sthūla avayavinam yāvat krama vṛddhimatām kāryāṇām mālāyāḥ uttarottara vṛddhimat gauravam sat api na upalabhyate iti yat ucyate tadā 
[467,v_467,vi]	āsarṣapāt gauravantu durlakṣatam analpakam tolyam tad kāraṇam kārya gaurava anupalakṣaṇāt āsarṣapāt sarṣapāt ārabhya dbyaṇukam yāvat pūrvam pūrvam gauravam tat durlakṣatam analpakam iti sutarām anupalabhyam syāt sarṣapāt uttarantu gauravam svayam eva durllakṣam iṣṭam iti kārya dravya gaurava anupalakṣaṇāt tasya kārya dravyasya kāraṇam paramāṇavaḥ pāriśeṣyāt tolyam syāt na ca paramāṇūnām guru tva ādi guṇa upalambha usti tad anupalakṣaṇena ca na avayavinaḥ paramāṇūnām va upalambha uḥ ti iti sarvathā arthānām apratipatiḥ syāt 
[467,vii_468,ii]	nanu adṛṣṭaḥ ṃ aśu vat sorthaḥ na ca tat kāryam īkṣyate nanu guru tva apratītau api aṃśuḥ pratīyate tadvat avayavi ādikam api pratyeṣyate iti āha na ca guru tva anupalakṣaṇa ipi aṃśuḥ iva saḥ arthaḥ avayavi ādiḥ īkṣyate na ca tat kāryam gaurava āvaraṇādiḥ īkṣyate tasmāt apratyakṣa tā eva sarvathā syāt kiñca 
[468,iii_468,iv]	gurutva āgati vat sarva tad guṇa anupalakṣāṇāt māṣaka ādeḥ anādhikyam guru tva ādi guṇa āgati vat sarveṣām rūpa ādīnām adhikānām tasya dravyasya guṇānām anupalakṣaṇāt avayavebhyaḥ bhāṣakādeḥ avayavinoḥ anādhikyam yadi hi avayavebhyodhikam tadā guru tva ādi vat rūpa ādi vat avayaveṣu varddhamāneṣu varddhamānam dṛśyeta 
[468,v_468,vii]	nanu tulānati viśeṣa agrahaṇāt iti uktamā cā ryeṇa tat kim rūpa ādi grahaṇa abhāvaḥ ucyate iti āha anatiḥ sa upalakṣaṇam yathāsvamakṣeṇa adṛṣṭe rūpa ādau adhika adhike anatiḥ ācāryeṇa yā nirddiṣṭā sa upalakṣaṇa mātram na tu niyamaḥ anatiḥ kva upalakṣaṇam iti āha rūpa ādau dravya abhivṛddhyā adhika adhike yathāsvam yasya yat ā ātmīyam grāhakam tena akṣeṇa indriya jñānena adṛṣṭeḥ yad rūpa ādi viṣayam yat indriya pratyakṣam tat eva tasya dharmi viśeṣasya pakṣa bādhakam iti arthaḥ tasmāt guṇa kriyā vat dṛśya avayavi abhāvaḥ eva iti dharma viśeṣa vāc dvāreṇa udāharaṇam uktam 
[468,viii_468,ix]	abhyupāya sva vāc ādi a bādhāyāḥ saṃbhavena tu udāharaṇam api anyat diśā gamyam yathā uktayā abhyupāyaḥ abhyupagamaḥ sva vāc ādiḥ yasya tena ābādhāyāḥ saṃbhavena tu anyat api udāharaṇam dharmi viśeṣa nirākaraṇena dharmi svarūpa nirākaraṇena yathā uktayā anayā udāharaṇa diśā gamyam 
[468,x]	tatra pareṇa avayavinaḥ sakāśāt avayavānām anya tve pratijñāte yat ucyate na anye avayavāḥ avayavinaḥ apratyakṣa tva prasaṅgāt iti tad dharmi viśeṣa nirākaraṇa udāharaṇam tathā hi avayavānām bhedam icchan pratyakṣatām api icchati anya tve ca nirākṛte pratyakṣatāyāḥ ca nirāsāt avayavānām dharmi viśeṣa nirākaraṇa udāharaṇa tvam vyaktam abhyupagamaḥ eva ca atra bādhakaḥ avayava adarśane dravya adarśana svīkārāt guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam asti iti pareṇa ukte yadā ucyate na asti dravyam guṇa dravyāṇām dravya adravya tva prasaṅgāt tad dharmi svarūpa nirākaraṇa udāharaṇam 
[469,i_469,iii]	tathā hi dharmiṇaḥ eva dravyasya svarūpa mātram nirākriyate guṇa dravyāṇām anyonyam bhedaḥ svīkṛtaḥ guṇa upi dravyam syāt dravyañca guṇaḥ bheda aviśeṣāt iti abhyupāyasya bādhaka tvam nanu sādhya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā iti pakṣa lakṣaṇam naiyāyikānām tatra kaḥ doṣaḥ asiddha hetu dṛṣṭāntasya api pakṣatva prasaṅgaḥ iti uktam nanu sādhyate iti sādhyam hetu dṛṣṭāntau tu sādhayiṣyate tatas na anayoḥ pakṣatva prasaṅgaḥ iti āha tri kāla viṣaya tvāt tu kṛtyānām atathā ātmakam tathā param prati nyastam sādhyam na iṣṭam tadā api tat 
[469,iv]	kṛtyānām pratyayānām kāla sāmānya vihita tvena tri kāla viṣaya tvāt sādhya śabdena kṛtyā antena na sādhya mātrasya grahaṇam sādhayiṣyamāṇasya api grahaṇāt tathā ca nityaḥ śabdaḥ mūrta tvāt buddhi vat ityādi prayoge tadā vāda kāle tad hetu dṛṣṭānta ādikam atathā ātmakam vastutas atad svabhāva ātmakam param prati tathā atad rūpa tvena nyastam upanyastam vādinā yatnatas sādhyam yadi api śabde mūrtta tvam na asti aniṣṭañca sādhya tvena tathā api hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ upanyāsāt avaśyam sādhyam sādhya nirdeśaḥ ca pratijñā iti pratijñā tvañca durvāram 
[470,i_470,ii]	pratyāyana adhikāre tu sarva asiddha avarodhinī yasmāt sādhya śrutiḥ na iṣṭam viśeṣam avalambate pratyāyanasya jñāpakasya hetoḥ adhikāre tu sādhanasya sarvasya abhyupagama hetu dṛṣṭānta ādera siddha avarodhaḥ saṃgrahaḥ tadvatī yasmāt sādhyaśrutiḥ iṣṭam viśeṣam na sādhya tvena avalambate parigṛhṇāti 
[470,iii_470,v]	yena pratyāyana adhikāre sādhanasya asiddhasya pakṣatva prasaṅgaḥ tena aprasiddha dṛṣṭānta hetu udāharaṇam kṛtam anyathā śaśaśṛṅga ādau sarva asiddhe api sādhya tā tena aprasiddhābhyām dṛṣṭānta hetubhyām pratijñā prasaṅgāt udāharaṇam kṛtam prāk tathā ca asiddha dṛṣṭānta hetuvādaḥ prasajyate iti anena anyathā yadi sādhanam asiddham vivakṣitam na syāt tadā śaśaśṛṅga ādau api sarvasya asiddhasya pakṣatva prasaṅgaḥ 
[470,vi]	nanu sādhyam karma karmaṇi kṛtya vidhānāt karma ca īpsitatamam tat ca kriyā apya mātram payasā udanam bhuktam iti atra kriyā apyatvepya nīpsitatama tvāt payaḥ karaṇam tatas sādhanīya tvepi vādinaḥ anīpsitatama tvāt hetu dṛṣṭānta ādikam na pratijñā bhaviṣyati tathā caturvidhaḥ siddhāntaḥ sarva tantra siddhāntaḥ prati tantra siddhāntaḥ adhikaraṇa siddhāntaḥ abhyupagama siddhāntaḥ ca tatra abhyupagama siddhānta tvaṃśa astra dṛṣṭasya iti tad āśrayeṇa sādhyasya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā na hetu dṛṣṭānta ādeḥ pakṣatva prasaṅgaḥ iti āha 
[471,i_471,ii]	sarvasya ca aprasiddha tvāt kathañcid tena na kṣamāḥ karma ādi bheda upakṣepa parihārā vivecane sarvasya pratijñā hetu dṛṣṭānta ādeḥ ca aprasiddha tvāt sādhayitum īpsitatama tvena abhyupagamāt karma tvam karma ca sādhyam pratijñā iti pratijñātva prasaṅgaḥ durvāraḥ abhyupagamaḥ ca yathā nitya tve tathā mūrttattva ādau api śāstra abhyupagamayoḥ ca bhedaḥ prāk uktaḥ tena karma tva aviśeṣeṇa sādhyam karma sādhanam karaṇam iti karma ādi bhedasya upakṣepeṇa upanyāsena parihāra avivecane sādhya viśeṣa avagamāpane kathañcid na kṣamāḥ 
[471,iii_471,vi]	yadi api ucyate yaḥ sādhyaḥ avayavaḥ tasya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā tatas hetu ādeḥ siddhasya avayavasya na pratijñātvam iti tat api asat kiñca prāc asiddha svabhāva tvāt sādhyaḥ vayavaḥ iti asat tulyā siddhānta tā te hi yena upagama lakṣaṇāḥ lakṣaṇa vacanāt prāk sādhya asādhyayoḥ asiddha svabhāva tvāt lakṣaṇena hi sādhya tā pratipattavyā tri kāla viṣaya tvāt kṛtya pratyayasya sādhayiṣyamāṇepi sādhyaḥ iti sādhanam ca sādhyam syāt siddhānta tā hetu dṛṣṭānta ādeḥ api tulyā te hi pratitantra ādi siddhāntāḥ yena kāraṇena upagama lakṣaṇāḥ abhyupagama svabhāvāḥ yathā hi nitya tvam abhyupagamyatetathā mūrtta tva ādikam api iti na viśeṣaḥ 
[471,vii]	kiñca sādhyaḥ dharmaḥ dharmī dvayam vā syāt yadi dharmaḥ tadā sādhya sādharmyāt tad dharma bhavī dṛṣṭānte udāharaṇam iti dṛṣṭānta lakṣaṇam virudhyate na hi sādhya dharmasya anitya tvāt eḥ ddharmaḥ utpattimatu ādiḥ kintu śabdasya tatas sādhya dharmeṇa sādharmyāt dṛṣṭāntasya tad dharma bhāvi tvam sādhya dharma utpattimatu ā ādi bhāvava tvam na asti atha dharmī sādhyaḥ tadā udāharaṇa sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam hetuḥ iti hetu lakṣaṇam na yujyeta na hi śabdaḥ dharmma siddhaḥ yena tad sādhanāt sādhya sādhanaḥ hetuḥ syāt 
[472,i_472,iii]	atha ubhayam sādhyam tadā ubhaya pakṣa bhāvi doṣa prasaṅgaḥ samudāyasya asiddha tvāt saḥ eva sādhyaḥ iti āha samudāyasya sādhya tva ipi anyonyasya viśeṣaṇam sādhyam dvayam tadā asiddham hetu dṛṣṭānta lakṣaṇam samudāyasya sādhya tvepīṣyamāṇe anyonyasya parasparam viśeṣaṇam vaktavyam dharma viśiṣṭaḥ dharmi viśiṣṭaḥ vā asādhyaḥ yathā śabda viśiṣṭam anityam iti tathā ca dvayam sādhyam syāt tadā dvaya sādhya tva abhyupagame tu hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ lakṣaṇam asiddham syāt na hi dharmi dharma viśiṣṭena dharmeṇa anitya śabda sambandhinā utpattimatu ādinā ghaṭa ādeḥ sādharmyam asti yena dṛṣṭānta tā bhavet tathā dharma viśiṣṭe dharmiṇi prāk anumānāt hetuḥ api na kasyacid siddhaḥ iti hetu lakṣaṇam ca na syāt 
[473,i_473,ii]	asaṃbhavāt sādhya śabdaḥ dharmi vṛttiḥ yadi iṣyate śāstreṇa alam yathāyogam lokaḥ eva pravarttatām yathā utpattimatu a ādeḥ samudāya dharma tva asaṃbhavāt dharmi dharma tva saṃbhavāt ca sādhya śabdaḥ yadi dharmi vṛttiḥ upacāra āt iṣyate tadā śāstreṇa durvihitena alam loke eva yathākramam yathāyogam yasya yādṛśam lakṣaṇam yuktam tat avadhārya pratijñā hetu ādiṣu pravarttatām yat tu pakṣaḥ dharmī avayava samudāya upacārāt iti asmābhiḥ ucyate tat sarvam dharmi dharma pratiṣedha artham upacāra yogya parigraha artham tasmāt ayuktam parasya pratijñā lakṣaṇam 
[473,iii_473,v]	kiñca sarva vākyānām avadhāraṇa phala tvāt sādhya nirdeśaḥ eva pratijñā iti pūrva pada avadhāraṇam vā syāt sādhya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā eva iti uttara pada avadhāraṇam vā syāt tatra prathama pakṣe siddha nivṛtyā asiddha parigrahaḥ prayojanam tat ca anyathā api labhyate tathā hi sādhana ākhyāna sāmarthyāt tad arthe sādhya tā gatā hetu ādi vacanaiḥ vyāpteḥ anāśaṅkyam ca sādhanam 
[473,vi_474,i]	siddhe api sādhana upanyāsaḥ anupayuktaḥ iti sādhana ākhyāna sāmarthyāt tasyāḥ pratijñāyai arthe asiddhe sādhya tā pratītā pratijñā lakṣaṇam vinā api naca asiddhe hetu dṛṣṭānta ādike pratijñā artha prasaṃgaḥ tathā hi hetu ādi vacanaiḥ pṛthak lakṣaṇa pratipādakaiḥ vyāpteḥ viṣayi kṛta tvāt sādhanam hetu dṛṣṭāntam asiddham ca pratijñā arthe vā anāśaṅkyam 
[475,i_475,ii]	pūrva avadhāraṇe tena pratijñā lakṣaṇa abhidhā vyarthā vyāptiphalā soktiḥ sāmarthyāt gamyate tatas tena ati prasaṃga abhāvena pūrvasya padasya avadhāraṇe pratijñā lakṣaṇa abhidhā vyarthā tatas pāriśeṣyāt sāmarthyāt sādhya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā eva ityayoga vyavaccheda phalam uttara pada avadhāraṇam syāt tathā ca asiddha hetu dṛṣṭānta ādau api pratijñātvam durvāram asiddhasya sādhana aṅgasya katham api pratijñātvā ayaḥ gatā virahāt nirastam pratijñā lakṣaṇam 
[475,iii_475,iv]	parasya pratijña ābhāsa lakṣaṇam saṃprati nirākaraṇīyam hetu pratijñayoḥ vyāghātaḥ pratijñā doṣaḥ mataḥ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ sarvasya nitya tvāt yadi sarvam anityam tadā śabdasya api sarvatra antarbhāvāt kutas nityatā atha śabdaḥ nityaḥ katham sarvasya anitya tā iti pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhāt pratijñā viruddha tā doṣaḥ viruddha teṣṭa asambandhaḥ anupakāra saha āsthitī evam sarva aṅga doṣāṇām pratijñādoṣa tā bhavet 
[475,v_476,i]	viruddha tā ceṣṭasyā sādhya dharmasya dharmiṇī asambandhaḥ nāma sa ca vicāryamāṇaḥ hetunā sādhya dharmasya anupakāraḥ aniścāyanam vā syāt dharmiṇi sādhyena saha āsthitiḥ vā syāt tatra yadi hetoḥ sādhye pratipādaka tva abhāvāt pratijñā doṣaḥ ucyate evam sati sarveṣām aṅgasya hetoḥ doṣāṇām pratijñādoṣa tā bhavet sarvaiḥ hetu doṣaiḥ pratijñāyāḥ eva vyāhananāt pakṣa doṣaḥ parāpakṣaḥ na iti ca pratipāditam iṣṭa asambhavya siddhaḥ ca saḥ evam syāt nirākṛtaḥ 
[476,ii_476,iii]	pratijñā mātra bhāgī ca pakṣa doṣaḥ para apekṣaḥ sādhana ādi sāpekṣaḥ na doṣaḥ iti ca pratipāditam prāc uttara avayava apekṣaḥ na doṣaḥ pakṣaḥ iṣyate ityādinā atha saha asthiti svabhāvaḥ virodhaḥ tadā iṣṭe pakṣe asambhavī hetu doṣaḥ eva ayam na pakṣa doṣaḥ atha tena hetunā pratijñā artha nirākaraṇāt pratijñā virodhaḥ pakṣa doṣaḥ eva tat ca ayuktam tathā hi sādhya dharmaḥ dharmiṇī evam nirākṛtaḥ syāt anitya tva sahetu tve śabdaḥ evam prakīrttayet dṛṣṭānta ākhyān ataḥ anyat kim asti atra artha anudarśam 
[476,iv]	yadi śabde dharmiṇī anitya tvena dharmeṇa sa hetu tve pratipādye evam sarvasya anitya tva ādi prakīrttayet na ca īdṛśam vādinaḥ vivakṣitam sarvasya parasya anitya tvāt śabdaḥ nityaḥ iti vivakṣita tvāt tathā ca sāmānya viśeṣa bhāvāt virodha bhāvaḥ bhavatu vā śabde anitya tva nirākaraṇam vivakṣitam tathā api pramāṇa bādhā eva apakṣatā iti na pratijñāvirodhaḥ nāma pakṣa doṣaḥ tasmāt hetu artha tā anupapatteḥ sarvasya anitya tvāt iti atra vaidharmyeṇa dṛṣṭānta ākhyān ataḥ anyat artha anudarśanam kim asti vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ eva su śikṣitaiḥ ittham ākhyātaḥ sarvasya nitya tve vyāpti darśana artham yadi punar vaidharmya dṛṣṭānta upadarśanam etat na bhavati tadā 
[476,v_476,vi]	viśeṣebhinnam ākhyāya sāmānyasya anuvarttane na tad vyāptiḥ phalam vā kim sāmānyena anuvarttane viśeṣeṇa śabde bhinnam nitya tvam ākhyāya sarvasya anitya tvāt iti vyāpi tvā at sāmānyasya anitya tvasya anuvarttane kriyamāṇe tasya anitya tvasya vyāptiḥ aśeṣa padārtha grahaḥ na bhavati yathā kauṇḍinyasya takra dānam vihitam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ sāmānyena vihita dadhi dānena na bādhyate prakalpya apavāda viṣayam utsargasya pravṛtteḥ tathā śabde nitya tvasya viśeṣa vihitasya sarva anitya tvena sāmānya vihitena bādhā āśaṅkā na asti iti katham pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ yadi śabda vyatiriktasya sarvasya anitya tvam iṣṭam na syāt tadā sarvasya anitya tvāt iti sāmānyena anuvarttane kim phalam syāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ śabdasya anitya tvāt iti eva vācyam evam virodhasya vaktavya tvāt śabdaḥ eva udāharaṇam bhaviṣyati iti ced na anunmattaḥ evam brūyāt yadi ātmanaḥ anitya tvam hetuḥ siddhaḥ katham tat viruddham sādhyam tatra eva pratijānīyāt atha asiddhaḥ tadā hetu doṣaḥ eva asau na pratijñā doṣaḥ tasmāt na asti śabde nitya tvam atas sva virodhinam api nirākarttum aśaktam 
[477,i_477,iii]	syāt nirākaraṇam śabde sthitena eva iti atas bravīt atas eva ācārya śabdesthitena eva anitya tvena nirākaraṇam nitya tvasya syāt iti abravīt tadā ca syāt atra pratijñā arthasya nirākaraṇam yadi nityaḥ śabdaḥ sarvasya anitya tvāt iti vaidharmya dṛṣṭānta upadarśanam etat yathā nitya tva viśiṣṭa śabdaḥ iti tadā hetu nirdeśaḥ na syāt iti āha asarvaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti upanayāt hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ 
[477,iv_477,vii]	viruddha viṣayeni asmin vadan āha anyatām śruteḥ tathā hi nitya tvasya viruddham śabdāt anyasmin vadan sarvasmāt anya tām śruteḥ śabdasya āha sa ca bheda upratikṣepāt sāmānyānāt na vidyate sa ca sarvasmāt bhedaḥ asarva lakṣaṇaḥ śabdasya na vidyate sāmānyānām vyāpinām bhedasya apratikṣepāt svīkārāt niḥ śeṣa artha saṃgṛhīta tvāt sarva śabdaḥ na kiñcid pariharati 
[477,viii_478,i]	nanu sāmānyānām viśeṣa pratikṣepaḥ dṛśyate eva yathā kim śiṃśapā eva vṛkṣaḥ na vā iti praśne kathyate na śiṃśapā eva vṛkṣaḥ tadā śiṃśapā vṛkṣa tva pratikṣepaḥ bhavati eva asat etat na hi tatra śiṃśapā vṛkṣa tvam niṣidhyate kintu śiṃśapā eva vṛkṣaḥ iti niyamaḥ pratikṣipyate tad itarasya api vṛkṣa tvāt vṛkṣaḥ na śiṃśapā eva iti yathā prakaraṇe kvacid sarva śruteḥ eka vṛtti niṣedhaḥ syāt na ceyatā sosarvaḥ sarva bhedān ām a tattve tad asambhavāt 
[478,ii]	yathā ca kvacid prakaraṇe śiṃśapā mātra vṛkṣa tva praśna hetau yathā vṛkṣaḥ na śiṃśapā eva iti śiṃśapā mātra vṛkṣa tva niṣedhaḥ iṣṭaḥ tathā niḥśeṣa vastu saṃgrāhikāyāḥ sarva śruteḥ ekatra śabda mātra vṛtti niṣedhaḥ syāt na ceyatā sa śabdaḥ asarvaḥ sarva antargamāt tasya pratyekam sarveṣām bhedānām viśeṣāṇāmatatve asarva tve tasya sarvasya asambhavāt 
[478,iii_478,v]	atha pāribhāṣikam sarva tvam śabda āditara tvam tathā asarva tvam śabde siddham eva iti ced tat ayuktam evam hi sarva tvam eva sarva śabdena uktam syāt tathā aprasiddha tā eva tathā hi jñāpya jñāpakayoḥ bhedāt dharmiṇaḥ hetu bhāvinaḥ asiddheḥ jñāpika tvasya dharmya siddhaḥ sva sādhane jñāpya jñāpakayoḥ bhedāt kāraṇā t sādhya abhinnam sādhanam vaktavyam tatas dharmiṇaḥ hetu tvena bhāvinaḥ hetuḥ bhaviṣyataḥ nitya tvena sādhya tvāt jñāpakasya asiddheḥ kāraṇāt dharmī sādhya tvāt svasya sādhane asiddhaḥ asiddham hi sādhyam siddhañca sādhanam anayoḥ katham aikātmyam 
[478,vi]	nanu śabda tvam siddham eva nityavat tayā tu tat asiddham sādhyate na ca tathā eva tad sādhanam śabda tva mātreṇa sādhana tvāt tad kathandharmī sva sādhane asiddhaḥ ucyate ayam abhiprāyaḥ na śabda tvam iti eva gamaka tvam kintu sa adhyapi āptam tasya ca asādhāraṇa tvena na anyatra vyāpti upalambhaḥ tatas ca anyatra anitya tva niyamāt śabde śabda tvam nitya tā vyāptam sat hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ tathā ca yaḥ eva sādhyaḥ saḥ eva hetuḥ iti sādhya siddheḥ hetu asiddhiḥ ca iti yuktam uktam dharmya siddhaḥ prasādhanaḥ iti 
[478,vii_479,i]	dharma dharmi vivekasya sarva bhāveṣu asiddhitaḥ sarvatra doṣaḥ tulyaḥ ced na saṃvṛtyā viśeṣataḥ nanu evam sati sarvatra bhāveṣu dharmayāḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ ddharmiṇaḥ ca vivekasya bhedasya asiddhitaḥ sarvatra tulyaḥ doṣaḥ na hi śabdāt anyat nitya tvam kṛtaka tvamvā anitya tva asiddhau ca yathā nityaḥ sādhyaḥ tathā tad ātmavān kṛta kopi śabdaḥ asiddhaḥ aivati ced na eṣa doṣaḥ saṃvṛttyā bhinna vyāvṛtti viṣayayā sādhya sādhana dharmiṇaḥ viśeṣataḥ bhedāt yathā svam vikalpaiḥ saṃketa vāsana anugama niyamita ekaika vṛtti mātra viṣaya arthaiḥ śabda tva kṛtaka tva nitya tva ādi asaṃkīrṇṇāni eva dharmi sādhana sādhya tayā vyavasthāpyante iti na doṣaḥ 
[479,ii_479,iv]	yadi dharma dharmi vivekaḥ asti eva tadā tattva anyatva pratiṣedhaḥ katham kṛtaḥ iti āha parama artha vicāreṣu tathābhūta aprasiddhitaḥ tattva anya tvam padārtheṣu sāṃbṛteṣu niṣidhyate sāṃvṛteṣu kalpanā viṣayeṣu dharmi dharma ādiṣu tattva anya tvam parama arthasya tattvasya vicāreṣu niṣidhyate tathābhūtasya yathākalpanam para sparataḥ bhinnasya dharmi dharma ādeḥ pramāṇena aprasiddhitaḥ na tu sāṃvṛtopi teṣām bheda abhāvaḥ na ceyatā kalpite dharmiṇi kalpitāt sādhanāt kalpitasya sādhyasya siddhiḥ iti anumānāt avastu pratītyabhāva prasaṅga aśabda vyāvṛttyā niścitasya vastunaḥ eva dharmi tvāt evam kṛtaka tva anitya tvābhyām niścitasya tasya eva sādhana tvāt sādhya tvāt ca iti ukteḥ anyonyasya teṣām bhedaḥ punar kalpitaḥ eva 
[479,v_479,vii]	anumāna anumeya artha vyavahāra sthitiḥ tu iyam bhedam pratyaya saṃsiddham avalambya ca kalpyate atonumāna hetu tvāt anumānasya liṅgasya anumeya arthasya anayoḥ upalakṣaṇa tvāt dharmiṇaḥ ca vyavahāra sthitiḥ tu iyam anityaḥ kṛtaka tvāt ityādau kriyamāṇā teṣām para sparataḥ bheda pratyatena vikalpakena eka vyāvṛtti mātra viṣayeṇa saṃsiddham niścitam avalam vyāśritya ca kalpyate
