[479,viii_479,ix]	yathā svam bheda niṣṭheṣu pratyayeṣu vivekinaḥ dharmī dharmāḥ ca bhāsante vyavahāraḥ tad āśrayaḥ tathā hi yathā svam yasya yaḥ ātmīyaḥ grāhyaḥ bhedaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ tad niṣṭheṣu vikalpeṣu vivekinaḥ dharmī dharmāḥ ca sādhya sādhana ādayaḥ bhāsante tad āśrayaḥ vikalpa gocara āśrayaḥ dharmi dharma ādi bhedasya vyavahāraḥ pravarttate 
[480,i_480,v]	evantarhi nityaḥ śabdaḥ asarva tvāt iti atra api vyāvṛtti bhedāt eva sādhya sādhana bhāvaḥ bhaviṣyati iti āha vyavahāra upanītotra saḥ eva āśliṣṭa bheda dhīḥ sādhyaḥ sādhana tām nītaḥ tena asiddhaḥ prakāśitaḥ atra prayoge sa śabdaḥ eva sādhyaḥ aśliṣṭa bheda dhīra saṃspṛṣṭa anyādṛśa buddhiḥ dvābhyām api śabdābhyām ekasyāḥ vyāvṛtteḥ pratipādanāt vyavahāreṇa vyāvṛtti samāśrayeṇa upanītaḥ pratyupasthāpitaḥ yena kāraṇena sādhana tām nītaḥ tena asiddhaḥ prakāśitaḥ nanu saṃskṛta śabdaḥ anityaḥ saṃskṛta tvāt iti pratijñā artha eka deśasya yathā hetu tvam tathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ śabda tvāt iti asya api syāt iti āha bheda sāmānyayorddharma bhedāt aṃgāṃgitā tatas yathā anityaḥ prayatna utthaḥ prayatna uttha tayā dhvaniḥ 
[480,vi]	sādhya dharmi mātra niṣṭha tvāt sarva dharma gocara tvāt ca bheda sāmānyayorddharma bhedāt vyāvṛtti bhedāt sādhya dharmaḥ hi sādhya dharmi niṣṭha tvena sajātīyāt vijātīyāt ca vyāvṛtta tvāt viśeṣaḥ sādhana dharmaḥ tu vijātīya mātra vyāvṛtta tvena sāmānyam tatas bheda sāmānya bhāvena bhedāt aṅga aṅgitā hetu sādhya tā yuktā viśeṣaḥ sādhyaḥ sāmānyam hetuḥ iti kutas pratijñā artha eka deśa tā yathā anityaḥ prayatna utthaḥ dhvaniḥ iti pratijñā prayatna utthatayā iti hetuḥ śabdaḥ punar abhinna viṣayaḥ hetuḥ sādhyaḥ ca iti pratijñā artha eka deśa tvam 
[480,vii_481,i]	prayatna anantarīyaka tvasya dharmi viśeṣaṇa tvāt pratijñā artha eka deśa tvam asti eva iti āha pakṣa aṅga tvepi a bādha tva at na asiddhiḥ bhinna dharmiṇi yathā aśvaḥ na viṣāṇi tvāt eṣa piṃḍaḥ viṣāṇavān pakṣa aṅga tve viśeṣaṇa tvepi na asti eva tāvat sādhanasya pakṣa aṅga tvam viśeṣa sādhya tvāt bhavatu vā tathā api na asiddhasya tena viśeṣaṇena bhinne viśeṣite dharmiṇi dharmmi antara vyāvṛtte prayatna anantarīyaka tvasya avirodhāt abādha tvāt dharmiṇam viśeṣayat api prayatna uttha tvam śabde prasiddham eva yathā bahuṣu piṇḍeṣu dṛśyamāneṣu kim ayam aśvaḥ navā iti saṃśayaḥ abhidhīyate viṣāṇavān eṣa piṇḍaḥ dharmī na aśvaḥ viṣāṇi tvāt iti viṣāṇi tvam dharmiṇam viśeṣa yat ipa pramāṇa pratīta tva at na asiddhaḥ hetuḥ sādhya kāla aṅga tā vā na nivṛtteḥ upalakṣya tat viśeṣa upi pratijñā arthaḥ dharma bhedāt na yujyate 
[481,ii_481,iii]	athavā viśeṣaṇasya prayatna uttha tva ādeḥ tad śabda rūpam viśeṣya tvena upalakṣya anumānāt prāk eva nivṛtteḥ sādhya kāle anumeya pratīte kāle aṅga tā viśeṣaṇa tā na asti eva apratītam hi anumānāt pratyetavyam prayatna uttha tvāt iti ca pratītam na ca tatra vivādaḥ tatas dharmi mātra upalakṣaṇantat yathā kākaḥ devadatta gṛha upalakṣaṇa tvāt na kārya upayogī yadi api viśiṣṭe dharmiṇi pratijñā artha eka deśa tvam hetoḥ tathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ śrāvaṇa tvāt iti śabda svabhāva bhūtasya śrāvaṇa tvasya śabda tva vat pratijñā artha eka deśa tā syāt nāsā ādhāraṇa tā iti āha na kevalam viṣāṇi tva ādiḥ viśeṣaḥ śrāvaṇa tva ādiḥ api pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ na yujyate dharmasya vyāvṛtteḥ bhedāt śrāvaṇa tvam śravaṇa grāhya tā aśrāvaṇa vyāvṛttiḥ tat ca śabdepi kvacid kañcid puruṣam apekṣya bhavati aśabda vyāvṛttiḥ tu śabda tvam tat ca sarvatra asti tatas vyāvṛtti bhedāt śabde siddhasya śrāvaṇa tvasya anyatra ananuvṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā eva yuktā iti uktam sa parikaram pakṣa lakṣaṇam iti pakṣa lakṣaṇam 
[481,iv_481,v]	hetu lakṣaṇam idānīm vaktavyam tatra hetu lakṣaṇam eva tatra yaḥ san sajātīyeiti ādikam yuktam vaktum sa pakṣe sannasan dvedhā pakṣa dharmaḥ punar tridhā ityādinā navadhā pakṣa dharma prabhedaḥ tu kasmāt uktaḥ iti āha pakṣa dharma prabhedena sukha grahaṇa siddhaye hetu prakaraṇa arthasya sūtra saṃkṣepaḥ ucyate 
[482,i_482,ii]	pakṣa dharmasya navadhā prabhedena hetu prakaraṇa arthasya hetu hetu ābhāsa lakṣaṇa ātmakasya sukhena grahaṇasya siddhaye tad artha vācakānām sūtrāṇām saṃkṣepataḥ saṃgrahaḥ ucyate sa pakṣe san ityādinā yadi pakṣasya dharmaḥ hetuḥ tadā tad viśeṣaṇa apekṣasya dharmasya anyatra dharmiṇī ananu vṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā syāt atha pakṣeṇa na viśiṣyate tadā na pakṣa dharmaḥ hetuḥ syāt asat etat na hi anya yoga vyavacchedena eva viśeṣaṇam anyathā api sambhavāt iti darśayitum āha 
[482,iii_482,v]	ayogam yogam aparaiḥ atyanta ayogam eva ca vyavacchinatti dharmasya nipātaḥ vyatirecakaḥ nipātaḥ eva kāraḥ vyatirecakaḥ niyāmakaḥ kvacid dharmasya viśeṣaṇasya ayogam vyavacchinatti kvacid aparaiḥ viśeṣyāt anyaiḥ yogam vyavacchinatti kvacid atyanta ayogam vyavacchinatti nanu nipātaḥ na svayam vācakaḥ kintu dyotakaḥ tat asya katham ayam artha prabhedaḥ iti āha 
[482,vi_482,ix]	viśeṣaṇa viśeṣābhyām kriyayā ca saha uditaḥ dyotaka tvāt eva nipātaḥ viśeṣaṇena saha uditaḥ ayogasya vyavacchedakaḥ viśeṣyeṇa saha uktonya yogasya kriyayā ca saha uktaḥ atyanta ayogasya iti viśeṣaṇa ādi pada vācyaḥ eva ayoga vyavaccheda ādiḥ tad saha ukta nipāta dyotyaḥ iti arthaḥ bhavatu tāvat nipāta prayoge vyavaccheda viśeṣasya pratītiḥ pakṣaḥ iti ādau tu katham iti āha vivakṣātaḥ aprayogepi sarvaḥ arthoyam pratīyate vyavaccheda phalam vākyam yatas caitraḥ dhanurdharaḥ pārthaḥ dhanurddharaḥ nīlam sarojam iti vā yathā 
[482,x]	aprayogepi nipātasya vaktuḥ vivakṣātaḥ sarva uṃyama yoga vyavaccheda ādiḥ arthaḥ pratīyate yatas vyavaccheda phalam vākyam iti uktam prāk vākyañca upalakṣaṇam padam api vyavaccheda phalam na hi ghaṭena udakam ānaya iti pratipādam anavadhāraṇe aghaṭena ānayana pratiṣedhaḥ pakṣaḥ iti ādau tu katham iti āha aprayogepi nipātasya vaktuḥ vivakṣātaḥ sarvaḥ yam ayoga vyavacchedaḥ anudaka ānayana pratiṣedhaḥ anānayana nivṛttiḥ vā śakya upadarśanā ayoga vyavaccheda ādīnām udāharaṇam āha yathā caitraḥ dhanurddharaḥ pārthaḥ dhanurddharaḥ nīlam sarojam iti caitre dhanurddharatu asan dehāt viśeṣaṇena ayoga mātram vyavacchidyate pārthe dhanurddhara tvam prasiddham eva kintu tādṛśam anyasya api kim asti iti sandehe anya yoga vyavaccheda phalam viśeṣaṇam na khalu sarvam eva nīlam sarojam yena ayoga vyavacchedaḥ syāt na api sarojam eva nīlam yena anya yoga vyavacchedaḥ bhavet kintu nīlam sarojam saṃbhavati na vā iti anta ayoga saṃdehe viśeṣaṇena saḥ eva vyavacchidyate 
[483,i]	nanu bhavatu tāvat caitraḥ dhanurddharaḥ eva pārthaḥ eva dhanurddharaḥ sarojam nīlam saṃbhavati eva iti nipāta prayoge vivakṣā vaśāt viśeṣaṇa ādi padānām eva vā vyavaccheda pratipādaka tvāt aprayoge api nipātasya caitraḥ dhanurddharaḥ iti ādi prayogeṣu yoga vyavaccheda ādīnām pratītiḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ iti atra punar pakṣaḥ viśeṣaṇam dharmaḥ viśeṣyaḥ tat yadi pakṣasya eva dharmaḥ iti viśeṣaṇena saha nipātaḥ ucyate aprayogepi vā viśeṣaṇasya tad artha vṛttita iṣyate upabhayathā api anya yoga vyavaccheda pratipādaka tvam eva syāt 
[483,ii]	atha dharmaḥ eva viśeṣyaḥ nipāta sahacaraḥ tad artha vṛttiḥ veṣṭaḥ tadā ayoga vyavacchedaḥ labhyate eva param viśeṣaṇa sahitaḥ anya yogam vyavacchinatti iti ukteḥ virudhyate atra ucyate bāhyaḥ nipātaḥ śrūyamāṇā upi viśeṣya ādibhiḥ saha vaktṛ vivakṣa avaśāt gamyamānaḥ vā ayoga vyavacchedakaḥ bhavati iti dṛṣṭānta pradarśana artham uktam tathā eva caitraḥ dhanurddharaḥ iti ādi udāharaṇa pradarśanāt vyavaccheda phalam vākyam iti ukteḥ ca samāse tu viśeṣaṇam eva ayoga ādi vyavacchedakam vivakṣā vaśā ādiṣṭam ayoga vyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt iti ukteḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ iti pakṣa śabdaḥ ayoga vyavacchedakaḥ pakṣa asambaddhaḥ na bhavati iti arthaḥ cākṣuṣam rūpam iti cākṣuṣa tvasya rūpe vivāda abhāvāt śabda ādīnām viśeṣaṇena vyavacchedaḥ kriyate nīlotpalam iti utpale nīlatva niyama abhāvāt pareṣu abhāvāt ayoga ani ayogayoḥ vyavaccheda abhāvāt nīla śabdena atyanta asambhava mātram vyavacchidyate iti na kaścid virodhaḥ 
[483,iii_483,iv]	nanu yathā pārthaḥ eva dhanurddharaḥ iti viśeṣaṇasya sannidhānāt nipātasya viśeṣya antara vyavacchedaḥ tathā viśeṣaṇa sannidhānāt avadhāraṇasya caitraḥ dhanurddharaḥ eva iti guṇa antara vyavacchedaḥ syāt iti āha pratiyogi vyavacchedaḥ tatra api artheṣu gamyate tathā prasiddheḥ sāmarthyāt vivakṣā anugamāt dhvaneḥ 
[483,v_484,ii]	tatra viśeṣaṇa ādiṣu artheṣu vyavaccheda īpi kriyamāṇe prakaraṇāt buddhi viṣayīkṛtasya pratiyogina vyavacchedaḥ viśeṣaṇena gamyate na anyasya tathā prasiddheḥ pratiyoginaḥ eva buddhi sthīkṛtya viśeṣaṇena vyavacchedaḥ na itarasya iti loka prasiddheḥ vivakṣāyāḥ anugamāt dhvaneḥ vyavacchet ādau sāmarthya anna avivakṣita vyavacchedaḥ yatas eva ayoga vyavaccheda upyasti tad ayoga vyavacchedāt dharmī dharma viśeṣaṇam tad viśiṣṭa tayā dharmaḥ na niranvaya doṣa bhāj tat tasmāt dharmī pakṣaḥ dharmasya ayoga vyavacchedāt viśeṣaṇam dharmiṇaḥ na adharmaḥ hetuḥ iti arthaḥ ayoga vyavacchedāt tena dharmiṇā viśiṣṭa tayā dharmaḥ niranvaya doṣa bhāj na bhavati 
[484,iii]	sa pakṣe ghaṭa ādau san śabda anitya tve sādhye kṛtaka tvam hetuḥ asan sa pakṣe vyoma ādau śabda anitya tve sādhye kṛtaka tvam hetuḥ sa pakṣe dvedhā san asan ca śabda anitya tve sādhye yatna ja tvam hetuḥ ghaṭa ādau sa pakṣe san vidyut ādau ca āsan punar tridhā sa pakṣe san asan sadasan ca śabdasya yatna ja tve sādhye sa pakṣe ghaṭa ādau anitya tvam hetuḥ san śabda anitya tve sādhye yatna ja tvam hetuḥ asan vidyut ādau sa pakṣe śabde ayatna ja tve sādhye anitya tvam hetuḥ sa pakṣe vidyut ādau san vyoma ādau ca āsan evam pratyekam asapakṣepi san asan dvedhā ca iti yojyam śabda nitya tve sādhye prameya tvam hetuḥ asapakṣe ghaṭa ādau san śabda nitya tve sādhye śrāvaṇa tvam hetu rasa pakṣe asan śabda nitya tve sādhye asparśava tvam hetu rasa pakṣe ghaṭāt āvasan buddhi ādau san iti dvidhā pakṣa dharma nirdeśaḥ kimartha hetu prakaraṇe navadhā pakṣa dharma nirdeśaḥ 
[484,iv_484,vi^1]	samyak hetuḥ asiddha viruddha anaikāntika hetvābhāsāḥ eva yukta nirdeśāḥ iti āha svabhāva kārya sidhi artham dvau dvau hetu viparyayau vivādāt bheda sāmānye śeṣaḥ vyāvṛtti sādhanaḥ svabhāva kāryayoḥ eva hetu tvena siddhi artham tatra dvau śabde anitya tva siddhi artham kṛtaka tva prayatna ānantarīyaka tva ākhyau hetū nirdiṣṭau tathā śabdaḥ eva nitya tva sādhane dvau hetu viparyayau viruddhau hetu bhāve ca uktau yathā hi samyak hetoḥ sva sādhye vyāpya kārya tayā pratibaddhasya gamaka tvam tathā sādhya viparyaye vyāpya kārya tayā pratibaddhasya eva tad gamaka tvena viruddha tā na anyasya iti arthaḥ vyatirekī anvayī ca hetuḥ iti pareṣām vivādāt tad pratiṣedha artham bheda sāmānye asādhāraṇa sādhāraṇe
[484,vi^2]	śrāvaṇa tva prameya tve nirddiṣṭe yadi vipakṣe na asti iti sa ātmaka tve sādhye prāṇa ādima tvam hetuḥ tadā śrāvaṇa tvam api syāt na ca evam tasmāt na vyatirekī hetuḥ yadi ca kevala anvayinaḥ darśana mātra adhyavasita avyabhicārasya hetu tvam tadā prameya tvasya ākāśa ādau darśanāt avyabhicāra niścaye sati śabde nitya tva gamaka tvam syāt na ca evam tatas na kevala anvayī hetuḥ śeṣaḥ aprayatna utthaḥ śabdaḥ anitya tvāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśava tvāt prayatna ānantarīyaḥ śabdaḥ anitya tvāt iti hetu trayam vipakṣāt hetoḥ vyāvṛtti sādhanaḥ 
[485,i_485,ii]	yadi hi sa pakṣe darśana mātreṇa gamaka tvam tadā ete hetavaḥ prāptāḥ sarveṣām sa pakṣe satvāt tasmāt na anvaya sambandha mātreṇa gamaka tvam kintu vipakṣāt vyatireka niścaye na ca asti vyatireka niścayaḥ pradhānam hetu tva nibandhanam iti arthaḥ katham punar jñāyate svabhāva hetuḥ kṛtaka tvam kārya hetuḥ prayatna ānantarīyakam iti āha na hi svabhāvāt anyena vyāptiḥ gamyasya kāraṇe sambhavāt vyabhicārasya dvidhā vṛtti phalam tatas 
[485,iii]	na hi svabhāvāt hetoḥ anyena hetunā gamyasya sādhyasya vyāptiḥ yatra yatra anitya tvam tatra kṛtaka tvam iti dṛśyate ca vyāptiḥ tasmāt svabhāva hetuḥ eva na avaśyam kāraṇāni kāryavanti bhavanti iti kāraṇe kāryasya vyabhicāra sambhavāt kāryam kāraṇa vyāpakam na bhavati tatra sa pakṣe dvidhā vṛtti bhāva abhāvāt pratyatna ānantarīya tvam phalam kārya hetuḥ prayatna kāryasya tathā abhidhānāt 
[485,iv_485,vi]	nanu prayatna jena jñānena anityaḥ śabdaḥ anumeyaḥ iṣṭaḥ śabdāḥ ca nityāḥ eva tad viṣaya jñāna utpāda ādinā yatnena te vyajyante tat katham kārya hetu udāharaṇam idam iti āha prayatna anantaram jñānam prāc sataḥ niyamena na tasya āvṛtyakṣa śabdeṣu sarvathā anupayogataḥ prayatnāt prāk sataḥ śabdasya niyamena prayatna anantaram jñānam na yajyate prayatnam vinā api kadācid upalabhyeta na ca prayatna vyajyatā śabdānām yuktā tasya prayatnasya āvṛtau upalambha āvaraṇe śabda viṣaya jñāna janake śrotre śabdeṣu ca viṣayeṣu sarvathā akiñcitkara tvena anupayogataḥ iti uktam prāk 
[486,i_486,iii]	kiñca kadācid nirapekṣasya kāryā akṛti virodhataḥ kādācid ka phalam siddham tat liṅgam jñānam īdṛśam sahakāribhiḥ anādheya atiśaya tvet nityasya kadācid prayatna kāle kāryasya jñānasya ākṛti virodhataḥ kāraṇāt tat śruti viṣayam jñānam kādācid kasya anityasya śabdasya phalam liṅgam kāryam īdṛśam niyamena prayatna anantara bhāvi siddham 
[486,iv_486,v]	etāvatā eva siddhepi svabhāvasya pṛthak kṛtiḥ kāryeṇa saha nirddeśe mā jñāsīt sarvam īdṛśam etāvatā prayatna anantarīyaka tvena eva svabhāva hetu nirdeśa ipi siddhe prayatna anantaram utpādasya abhivyakteḥ ca tathā abhidhānāt tathā api svabhāvasya kṛtaka tvasya hetoḥ yā pṛthakkṛtiḥ sā kāryeṇa saha śleṣeṇa nirdeśe mā jñāsīt pratipattā sarvam svabhāva hetum īdṛśam sa pakṣe dvidhā vṛttim kṛtaka tva ādeḥ viparyaya vyāpti sambhavāt 
[486,vi_486,viii]	kiñca vyutpatti arthā ca hetu ukti rukta artha anumitau kṛtā atra prabhedaḥ ākhyātaḥ lakṣaṇantu na bhidyate anumitau sva artha anumāne hetu ukti rukta arthā abhihita lakṣaṇā api pratipattṝṇām vyutpatti arthā ca para artha anumāne kṛtā atra ca prabhedaḥ ākhyātaḥ lakṣaṇam punar hetoḥ na bhidyate tathāvidha lakṣaṇa hetu vacanasya para artha anumāna tvāt 
[486,ix_486,x]	tena atra kārya liṅgena svabhāva upi eka deśa bhāj sadṛśa udāhṛtiḥ ca atas prayatnāt vyakti janmanaḥ tena prayatna antarīyaka tvena kārya liṅgena śleṣa nirdeśāt svabhāva hetu dharma bhājā svabhāvopi sa pakṣa eka deśa bhāj bhavati iti aktaḥ bhavati atas eva kārya svabhāva tayā sadṛśasya prayatna anantarīyaka tvasya udāhṛtiḥ ācāryeṇa kṛtā prayatnāt vyakteḥ janmanaḥ ca bhāvāt yadā prayatnāt vyaktiḥ tadā kārya hetuḥ yadā janma tadā svabhāva hetuḥ 
[487,i_487,iii]	kārya svabhāvayoḥ prabheda nirdeśasya kim phalam iti āha yat na antarīyakā sattāḥ yaḥ vā ātmani avibhāgavān sa tena avyabhicārī syāt iti artham tad prabhedanam yat na antarīyakā sattā bhede sati yam antareṇa hetuḥ na bhavati yaḥ vā sve ātmīyaḥ sādhyāt avibhāgavān ātmā svabhāvaḥ sa tena kāraṇena vyāpakena vā avyabhicārī vyabhicāra rahitaḥ syāt na anyaḥ iti artham etat prayojanam tayoḥ kārya svabhāvayoḥ prabhedanam 
[487,iv_487,vi]	evañca sati saṃyogi ādiṣu yeṣu asti pratibandhaḥ na tādṛśaḥ na te hetavaḥ iti uktam vyabhicārasya sambhavāt saṃyogi samavāyi eka artha samavāyi ākāśa ādiṣu para abhimateṣu hetuṣu yeṣu pratibandhaḥ tādṛśaḥ tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇaḥ na asti na te hetavaḥ iti uktam bhavati atada ātmanaḥ atad utpatteḥ ca sādhya vyabhicārasya sambhavāt 
[487,vii_487,ix]	atha saṃyogi ādiṣu tad utpatti pratibandha usti tadā sati vā pratibandheḥ tu saḥ eva gati sādhanaḥ niyamaḥ hi avinābhāvaḥ aniyataḥ ca na sādhanam sati pratibandhe saḥ eva gati sādhanaḥ sādhya pratipatti hetuḥ astu niṣphalā saṃyogi ādi kalpanā niyamaḥ niyata tvam hi sādhanasya sākṣāt avinābhāvaḥ ucyate sa ca tādātmya tad utpattibhyām na anyathā sa ca tad vikala tvāt sādhye aniyataḥ na sa sādhanam yathā saṃyogi tvepi sa vahniḥ ddhūmasya iti svabhāva kārya siddhi artham dvau dvau hetu viparyayāvi ti vyākhyātam 
[488,i_488,iv]	vivādāt bheda sāmānyaḥ iti vyākhyātavyam syāt prāṇa ādima tvam hetuḥ yadi vipakṣāt hetu vyatirekaḥ syāt saḥ eva tu na sidhyati iti āha aikāntika tvam vyāvṛtteḥ avinābhāvaḥ ucyate tat ca na apratibaddheṣu tatas eva anvaya sthitiḥ vipakṣāt bhedaḥ vyāvṛtteḥ bbādhaka pramāṇa niścita tvāt aikāntika tvam avinā abhāvaḥ ucyate tat ca vyāvṛtteḥ aikāntika tvam sva sādhya apratibaddheṣu prāṇa ādiṣu na asti yadi hi ātmani pratibaddhāḥ prāṇa ādayaḥ tad ātma nivṛttau nivṛttāḥ vipakṣāt gamyeran anyathā tu pakṣaḥ eva sandehaḥ kim amī ātmā abhāvepi varttante uta na iti yathā ca pratibandhāt vyatireka niścayaḥ tathā tatas pratibandhāt eva anvayasya sthitiḥ na tu saha darśana mātreṇa 
[488,v_488,vii]	tasmāt sādhyasya sva ātma tve hetu bhāve vā siddhe hi vyatirekitā sidhyet atas viśeṣe na vyatirekaḥ na ca anvayaḥ sva ātma tve hetu svabhāva ātmaka tve hetu bhāve vā siddhe sati tad abhāve niyamena vyatirekāt vipakṣāt vyāpaka kāraṇa vyatireke svabhāva kārya hetvoḥ vyatirekitā sidhyet na anyathā iti nyāyaḥ eṣaḥ yatas pratibandhena eva anvaya vyatireka siddhiḥ atas viśeṣe asādhāraṇe hetau na anvayaḥ na vā vyatirekaḥ sidhyati 
[488,viii_488,x]	evam tarhi sa pakṣa vipakṣa vyatirekābhyām vyāvṛtteḥ viśeṣaḥ katham ācāryeṇa uktaḥ iti āha adṛṣṭi mātram ādāya kevalam vyatirekitā uktā anaikāntikaḥ tasmāt anyathā gamakaḥ bhavet adṛṣṭi mātram bādaka pramāṇa rahitam ādāya para abhiprāyeṇa sa pakṣāt vyatirekita uktā tasya adarśana mātreṇa vyatireka aniścayāt anaikāntikaḥ ācāryeṇa uktaḥ anyathā vipakṣāt vyatireka niścaye gamakaḥ hetuḥ bhavet tatas ca anaikāntika varge na prakṣipyeta 
[489,i_489,iii]	nanu sādhya nivṛttau niyamena sādhanam nivarttate iti sādhya abhāvaḥ sādhana abhāvena vyāptaḥ tatas ca prāṇa ādi abhāvaḥ nairātmya vyāpī iti vinivarttane ātmanaḥ vinivartteta prāṇa ādiḥ yadi tat ca na prāṇa ādeḥ sādhanasya abhāvaḥ nairātmyasya sa ātmaka tva sādhya abhāvasya vyāpi iti hetoḥ ātmanaḥ ghaṭa ādeḥ vipakṣāt vinivarttane sati prāṇādiḥ vinivarttate na hi anyathā sādhana abhāvaḥ sādhya abhāvasya ca vyāpakaḥ bhavati tatas yatra prāṇa ādi bhāva nivṛttiḥ tatra sa ātmaka tva bhāva nivṛttiḥ api iti yadi ucyate tat ca na yuktam 
[489,iv_489,v]	anyasya vinivṛtya anya vinivṛttyeḥ ayogataḥ tad ātmā tad prasūtiḥ ced na etat anyasya kāraṇasya ātmanaḥ vinivṛttyā prāṇa ādeḥ vinivṛtteḥ ayogataḥ tādātmya tad utpattau eva hi sādhya nivṛttau sādhana nivṛttiḥ yuktā tad svabhāva tvāt tad āyatta tvāt ca sati ca sādhya sādhanayoḥ niyamena nivartti a nivarttaka bhāve sādhya abhāvaḥ sādhana abhāvena vyāpyate prāṇa ādiḥ tasya ātmanaḥ ātmā svabhāvaḥ tasmāt prasūtiḥ vā asya iti ced na etat asti yuktam tathā hi 
[489,vi_489,vii]	ātma upalambhane tasya upalabdha avagata avagatau ca prasidhyati te ca atyanta parokṣasya dṛṣṭi adṛṣṭī na sidhyataḥ ātmanaḥ upalambhane sati tasya prāṇa ādeḥ upalabdhau satyām ātmanaḥ agatau prāṇa ādeḥ agatau ca satyām kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ prasidhyati te ca dṛṣṭi adṛṣṭī kārya kāraṇa bhāva sādhane atyanta parokṣasya ātmanaḥ na sidhyataḥ atyanta parokṣasya katham adṛṣṭiḥ api na sidhyati iti ced abhāva sādhikā dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ na sidhyati eva adṛṣṭi mātrantu na abhau a sādhakam tatas prāṇa ādeḥ ātmanā saha pratibandhā siddheḥ na ātma nivṛttyā prāṇa ādi nivṛtti siddhiḥ 
[489,viii_490,ii]	kiñca anyatra adṛṣṭa rūpasya ghaṭa ādau na iti vā kutas ajñāta vyatirekasya vyāvṛtteḥ vyāpitā kutas ātmanā uni atra jīvat śarīre adṛṣṭa rūpasya ghaṭa ādau na sattvam iti yat ucyate tat kutas siddham dṛśya anupalabdhyā hi abhāva siddhiḥ na ca adṛṣṭa care tad sambhavaḥ ajñātaḥ vyatirekaḥ abhāvaḥ yasya tasya ātmanaḥ yā vyāvṛttiḥ ghaṭa ādau tasyāḥ prāṇa ādi nivṛttyā vyāpitāḥ vyāpanam kutas sambhavi yena jīvat śarīre prāṇa ādi nivṛtti abhāvāt sa ātmaka tva nivṛtti abhāve satya ātma siddhiḥ syāt 
[490,iii_490,v]	nanu yathā ghaṭa ādau prāṇa ādi abhāva niścayaḥ tathā ātma abhāva niścayopi kim na bhavati iti āha prāṇa ādeḥ ca kvacid dṛṣṭyā sattva asattvam pratīyate tathā ātmā yadi dṛśyeta sattva asattvam pratīyate prāṇa ādeḥ kvacid jīvat śarīre dṛṣṭyā sattvam pratīyate mṛta dehe ca upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya asya adṛṣṭyā asattvam pratīyate tathā yadi kvacid dehe ātmā dṛśyeta tadā tatra sattvam asya pratīyeta anyatra upalabhya svarūpasya asya anupalabdheḥ asattvam pratīyeta na ca ātma upalabdhiḥ asti kvacid iti na tad abhāva niścayaḥ 
[490,vi_490,viii]	yat api ucyate yadi na sa ātmakam jīvat śarīram tadā asya prāṇa ādi viraha prasaṅgaḥ narātmyāt ghaṭa vat iti prasaṅga sādhanam tat ca ayuktam darśayitum āha yasya hetoḥ abhāvena ghaṭe prāṇaḥ na dṛśyate dehepi yadi asau na syāt yuktaḥ dehe na sambhavaḥ yasya buddhi deha atiśaya prayatna ādeḥ hetoḥ a bhāvena ghaṭe prāṇaḥ na dṛśyate dehepi yadi asau buddhi deha atiśaya prayatna ādiḥ na syāt tadā dehepi hetu virahāt prāṇa ādeḥ na saṃbhavaḥ yuktaḥ yathā mṛta śarīre jīvat dehe tu buddhi ādi sadbhāvāt eva prāṇa ādi rucita saṃbhavaḥ iti na ātma abhāve tad abhāva prasaṅgaḥ saṅgataḥ 
[490,ix_491,i]	atha ghaṭa jīvat śarīra ādīnām nairātmyena yathā sādharmyam tathā prāṇa ādi rahita tayā api syāt na ca bhavati tasmāt nirātmake ghaṭa ādau prāṇa ādiḥ adṛṣṭaḥ yatra varttate tatra sa ātmaka tvam sādhayati iti āha bhinnepi kiñcid sādharmyāt yadi tattvam pratīyate prameya tvāt ghaṭa ādīnām sa ātma tvam kinna mīyate ghaṭabhinnepi jīvat dehe kiñcit mātreṇa nirātmaka tvena sādharmyāt yadi tattvam prāṇa ādi virahita tayā ghaṭa sadṛśa tvam pratīyate tadā aprameya tvāt hetoḥ ghaṭa ādīnām jīvat śarīrasa ātmaka tvam kinna mīyate 
[491,ii_491,iii]	aniṣṭeḥ ced pramāṇam hi sarva iṣṭīnām nibandhanam bhāva abhāva vyavakthām kaḥ karttum tena vinā prabhuḥ aniṣṭeḥ ced nanu pramāṇam hi sarva iṣṭīnām nibandhanam tad vaśena arthān na sthiteḥ tena pramāṇena bhāva abhāvayoḥ vyavasthām karttum kaḥ prabhuḥ yadi ca kiñcid sādharmya mātrāt sādhanam sādhya sādhakam tadā prameya tvāt ghaṭasya api sa ātmaka tva sādhanāt aniṣṭiḥ anupayuktā 
[491,iv_491,vi]	yadi tarhi na ātmā prāṇa ādeḥ hetuḥ kaḥ tarhi bhaviṣyati iti āha yathā yogam smṛti icchā āyatna jaḥ prāṇa nimeṣa ādiḥ tad udbhavaḥ viṣaya indriya cittebhyaḥ smṛti icchā prayatnebhyaḥ jātaḥ prāṇa nimeṣa ādiḥ samāhitasya niruddhavāyoḥ samādhi vyutthitasya smaraṇāt prāṇa vṛttiḥ gāḍha prahāra ādibhiḥ vyāhata prāṇasya icchā prayatnābhyām prāṇa pravṛttiḥ svasthasya sādguṇyāt nimeṣa ādeḥ icchā prayatna ja tvam vyaktam teṣām ca smṛti icchā āyatnānām udbhavaḥ viṣaya indriya cittebhyaḥ yathāyogam kvacid viṣayāt vadarāde rasanā srava ādi hetaḥ rasa ādi smṛtiḥ bhavati indriyāt vā vilādera paṭu jāna hetoḥ pradīpa maṇḍala ādi smaraṇam bhavati buddheḥ eva atad viṣayasya atīta anukūla tā ādi smṛtiḥ udbhavati 
[491,vii_492,i]	nanu ṣaḍ pravṛtti buddhayaḥ eva ātmajāḥ pravṛtti buddhi jāḥ ca smṛti ādayaḥ tad bhavāḥ ca prāṇa ādayaḥ iti paraṃparā atma hetukāḥ eva iti āha tāḥ ṣaṣ buddhayaḥ tāḥ sva jāti samudbhavāḥ anyonya pratyaya apekṣā anvaya vyatireka bhāj etāvatī ātma bhāvoyam anavasthāni akalpane anyonya pratyaya apekṣā yasyāḥ yaḥ ātmīyaḥ pratyayaḥ sahakāri kāraṇam indriya ādi tasmin apekṣā ayat tiḥ yāsām tāḥ tathā satyaḥ sva jāti samudbhavāḥ samanantara prabhavāḥ na tu paraṃparayā api ātma apekṣiṇyaḥ iti arthaḥ etāvati kāraṇa kalāpe ayam ātma bhāvaḥ ṣaṣ āyatanam gṛhītaḥ anvaya vyatireka bhāj pratibaddhaḥ kāraṇa tvena tatonyasya kalpane anavasthā kāraṇānām tasmāt na adṛṣṭa sāmarthyasya ātmanaḥ nivṛttau prāṇa ādi nivṛttiḥ yuktā 
[492,ii_492,iv]	kiñca śrāvaṇa tvena tat tulyam prāṇa ādi vyabhicārataḥ na tasya vyabhicāri tvāt vyatirekepi ced katham tat prāṇa ādi sādhanam śrāvaṇa tvena hetunā vyabhicārataḥ anaikāntika tvāt tulyam na etat asti tasya śrāvaṇa tvasya vipakṣāt bahulam vyatirekepi vyatirekasya vyabhicārataḥ na hi śrāvaṇa tvam anityebhyaḥ prāyas vyāvṛttam iti anitya tva vyatireka avyabhicāri śakyam avasātum pakṣaḥ eva anityena saha akārya virodhāt prāṇa ādi tu niyamena vipakṣāt vyatireka avyabhicāri iti na yuktam śrāvaṇa tvena tulyam iti ced pṛcchatyā cā ryaḥ prāṇa ādi śrāvaṇa tvena atulyam katham iti 
[492,v_492,vii]	itaraḥ āha na asādhyāt eva viśleṣaḥ tasya nanu evam ucyate sādhyenu vṛtya bhāva ūrthāt tasya anyatra api asau samaḥ tasya śrāvaṇa tvasya asādhyāt vipakṣāt eva na viśleṣaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ kintu sa pakṣāt api prāṇa ādeḥ tu sarvasya jīvat śarīrasya sa ātma tvena sādhya tvāt sa pakṣaḥ eva na asti iti kathantataḥ vyāvṛttiḥ iti atra āha nanu evam asādhyāt eva śrāvaṇa tvasya na viśleṣa eti ākhyānesādhya sādhyavati sa pakṣe anuvṛtteḥ anvayasya abhāvaḥ arthāt uktaḥ syāt yaḥ hi vipakṣa mātrāt avyāvṛttaḥ sa sa pakṣāt api vyāvṛtteḥ anvaya rahitaḥ uktaḥ bhavati tathā ca prāṇa ādeḥ asau sa pakṣa anuvṛtti abhāvaḥ samaḥ na hi prāṇa ādi sapakṣe kvacid siddham sarvaṃsya jīvat śarīrasya pakṣa tvāt 
[492,viii_493,i]	asādhyāt eva vicchedaḥ iti sādhyeḥ titā ucyate artha apatyā atas eva uktam ekena ubhaya darśanam asādhyāt vipakṣāt eva sādhanasya vicchedaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ iti abhidhānena artha apatti asāmarthyena sādhye sa pakṣe astitā ucyate yadi tu sa pakṣāt api vyāvṛttiḥ tadā vipakṣāt eva vyāvṛttiḥ iti asaṅgatam yatas vipakṣāt eva vyāvṛttiḥ iti vyatirekaḥ ākṣipta anvayaḥ eva bhavati atas eva ācāryeṇa ekena vyatirekeṇa anvayena vā niyamavatā dṛṣṭena ubhaya darśana m uktam arthāpattyā anyatareṇa ubhaya darśanāt iti 
[493,ii_493,iv]	yasmāt aikāntikaḥ vyatirekaḥ ākṣipta anvayaḥ eva bhavati atas īdṛś avyabhicārotaḥ ananvayiṣu na sidhyati pratiṣedha niṣedhaḥ ca vidhānāt kīdṛśaḥ aparaḥ īdṛś vipakṣe vyatirekaḥ avyabhicāraḥ ananvayiṣu hetuṣu na sidhyati yaḥ eva sādhyena anvitaḥ hetuḥ tasya eva vipakṣāt eva vyatirekaḥ yadi tu sati api sādhye hetu abhāvaḥ tadā sa pakṣāt api vyatirekāt katham vipakṣāt eva nivṛttiḥ kiñca prāṇa ādeḥ sa pakṣe pratiṣedhasya nivṛtteniṣedhaḥ vidhānāt aparaḥ kīdṛśaḥ pratiṣedha niṣedhaḥ hi vidhiḥ eva paraspara parihāreṇa avasthiteḥ tatas prāṇa ādeḥ sa pakṣāt nivṛttiḥ na asti iti arthāt vṛttiḥ eva uktā syāt iti na vyatireki tvam 
[493,v_493,vii]	syāt evam yadi sa pakṣaḥ bhavati kintu nivṛttiḥ na asataḥ sādhyāt asādhyeṣu eva no tatas na iti sā eva nivṛttiḥ kim nivṛtteḥ asataḥ matā sa ātmaka tve sādhye sa pakṣaḥ na asti iti asataḥ sādhyāt sa pakṣāt prāṇa ādeḥ nivṛttiḥ na asti tatas asādhyeṣu vipakṣeṣu eva naḥ vṛttiḥ iti vyatireki tvam iṣṭam evantarhi sa pakṣāt asataḥ hetoḥ nivṛtteḥ nivṛttiḥ asmākam astitvena yeṣṭā sā eva kinna iti bhavataḥ matā yadi hi asat nivṛtteḥ na adhikaraṇam tadā nivṛtta nivṛtteḥ katham bhaviṣyati 
[493,viii_493,x]	kiñca nivṛtti abhāvaḥ tu vidhiḥ vastu bhāvaḥ asatā upi san vastu abhāvaḥ tu na asti iti paśya bāndhya vijṛmbhitam asatā upi sa pakṣāt hetu nivṛtteḥ nīrūpāyāḥ abhāvaḥ tu vidhiḥ vastu bhāvaḥ hetu sambhavaḥ sa na iṣyate yadi asati sa pakṣe hetu nivṛttiḥ na asti tadā hetuḥ eva asti iti uktam syāt vastunaḥ hetoḥ abhāvaḥ tu nivṛtti śabda vācyaḥ na asti iti paśya bāndhya vijṛmbhitam pareṣām asatya sattavam aviruddham viruddhantu sattvam iti arthaḥ 
[494,i_494,iii]	api ca nivṛttiḥ yadi tasmin na hetoḥ vṛttiḥ kim iṣyate sā api na pratiṣedha uyam nivṛttiḥ kim niṣidhyate hetoḥ tasmin asati sa pakṣe nivṛttiḥ yadi na asti tadā kim vṛttiḥ iṣyate vidhi niṣedhayoḥ anyonya vyavaccheda ātma tvāt eka pratiṣedhasya tad apara vidhinā antarīyaka tvāt tatas ca anvaya vyatireki tvāt prāṇādiḥ na vyatirekī sā vṛttiḥ api na asati sa pakṣaḥ iti ced nanu vṛtti niṣedhaḥ pratiṣedha uyam nivṛtti ātmakaḥ tatas ca asataḥ vṛtti nivṛtteḥ adhikaraṇa tvāt tasmin nivṛttiḥ kim niṣidhyate satyāñca nivṛttau śrāvaṇa tva vadasādhāraṇam prāṇa ādi syāt 
[494,iv_494,vi]	atha adhikaraṇa tayā apādāna tayā vā sataḥ pratītiḥ na asti iti na tasmāt nivṛttiḥ iti ucyate etad artham hi vidhānam pratiṣedhañca muktvā śābda usti na aparaḥ vyavahāraḥ sa ca asatsu na iti prāptā atra mūka tā vidhānam pratiṣedhañca muktvā aparaḥ śābdaḥ vyavahāraḥ na asti tayoḥ eva śabda pratipādya tvāt sa ca vidhi pratiṣedha vyavahāraḥ asatsu na asti iti atra āsatsu mūka tā eva prāptā tathā hi asati vidhi vyavahāraḥ tāvat na asti eva pratiṣedhopi tvad mate na asti iti yuktam mūka tvam 
[494,vii_494,ix]	kiñca sa tāñca na niṣedhaḥ asti saḥ asatsu ca na vidyate jagati anena nyāyena nañarthaḥ pralayam gataḥ sa tāñca padārthānām na niṣedha usti vidyamāna tvāt sa pratiṣedhaḥ asatsu na tvad abhiprāyāt vidyate anena nyāyena nañorthaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ jagati viṣaye pralayam gataḥ 
[494,x_494,xi]	deśa kāla niṣedhaḥ ced yathā asti sa niṣidhyate na tathā na yathā sosti tathā api na niṣidhyate kvacid satām eva arthānām anyayoḥ deśa kālayoḥ nañādinā niṣedhaḥ iṣṭaḥ ced yathā yad deśa kāla sambaddha tvena saḥ arthaḥ na asti tathā niṣidhyate tvad abhiprāyāt atas niṣedha ayogāt yathā ca asti sa tathā api na niṣidhyate satvāt 
[495,i_495,ii]	tasmāt āśritya śabda artham bhava abhāva samāśrayam abāhya āśrayam atra iṣṭam sarvam vidhi niṣedhanam tasmāt śabdasya artham āropita bahīrūpam anya vyavacchedam abāhya āśrayam bāhya viṣaya rahitam yaḥ eva bhāva abhāvayoḥ vidhi pratiṣedha vikalpa pratipādyayoḥ samāśrayaḥ tam āśritya vyavahāre sarvam vidhi niṣedhanam iṣṭam 
[495,iii_495,iv]	yadi vastu śabda vikalpābhyām viṣayīkriyate sarvathā pratīteḥ śabda pramāṇa antara vaiphalya prasaṅgaḥ tatonya apohaḥ eva vidhi niṣedha sambandhayoḥ viṣayaḥ tathā śabdāt sattva asattvābhyām vastunaḥ pratītau vidhi niṣedhayoḥ avaiphalya prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt bhāva abhāva sādhāraṇaḥ anvaya vyavacchedaḥ vidhi pratiṣedhābhyām sambadhyate iti tābhyām sa dharmī sambaddhaḥ khyāti abhāvepi tādṛśaḥ śabda pravṛtteḥ asti iti sa upīṣṭaḥ vyavahāra bhāj 
[495,v]	tābhyām vidhi pratiṣedhābhyām sa śabda arthaḥ dharmī sambaddhaḥ khyāti vastutas abhāvepi tādṛśaḥ vidhi pratiṣedha sambaddhasya arthasya na hi śabda arthaḥ eva kaścid bāhya abāhya arthayoḥ ayogāt tad itarasya ca abhāvāt iti ukteḥ kutas eva vidhi niṣedhābhyām tasyāḥ sambandhaḥ syāt tathā api sa vidhiḥ pratiṣamadhas ca śabda pravṛtteḥ asti iti vyavahāra bhāgiṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ hi pravarttamānaḥ vidhi pratiṣedha vyavahāram vastutas asantam api avidyā abhyāsataḥ vāsanā vaśāt upadarśayati iti tad anurodhāt san ucyate 
[495,vi_495,vii]	anyathā syāt padārthānām vidhāna pratiṣedhane eka dharmasya sarva ātma vidhāna pratiṣedhanam anānātma tayā anyathā yadi evam na iṣyate tadā padārthānām vidhāna pratiṣedhane abhyupagamyamāne yadi dharmāḥ dharmiṇaḥ abhinnāḥ tadā ekasya dharmasya vidhāne pratiṣedhane vā kṛte sarveṣām dharmāṇām dharmya ātma bhūtānām vidhāna pratiṣedhanam syāt teṣām dharmāṇām eka dharmi svabhāva tvena ānānātma tayā eka svabhāvatayā ekasya dharmasya vidhiḥ pratiṣedhaḥ vā sarvasya bhavet 
[496,i_496,ii]	bhede nānā vidhi niṣedha vat eka dharmiṇī a saṃhāraḥ vidhāna pratiṣedhayoḥ dharmiṇaḥ sakāśāt dharmāṇām bhede abhyupagamyamāne ekasmin dharmiṇi dharmāṇām vidhāna pratiṣedhayoḥ asaṃhāraḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam na syāt nānā vidhi niṣedha vat svatantra aneka padārtha vidhi niṣedhau iva na ekatra vastuni sāmānya adhikaraṇya bhājau 
[496,iii_496,v]	asmad mate tu eka dharmiṇam uddiśya nānā dharma samāśrayam vidhau ekasya tad bhājam iva anyeṣām upekṣakam niṣedhe tad viviktañja tad anyeṣām apekṣakam vyavahāram asatya artham prakalpayati dhīḥ yathā śabda artha dharmiṇam ekam nānā dharma samāśrayam ekasya dharmasya vidhau kriyamāṇe tad bhājam eka dharma sambaddham iva anyeṣām vidhi pratiṣedhābhyām aparāmṛṣṭānām dharmāṇām upekṣakam tathā eka dharmasya niṣedhe kriyamāṇe ekam dharmiṇam nānā dharma samāśrayaṇam tena niṣidhyamānena dharmeṇa viviktam eva tad anyeṣām niṣidhyamāna dharma itareṣām dharmāṇām apekṣakam uddiśya yathā kalpikā dhīḥ vyavahāram paramārtha taḥ asatya artham kalpayati 
[496,vi_496,vii]	tam tathā eva avikalpa artham bheda āśrayam upāgatāḥ anādi vāsanā udbhūtam bādhante artham na laukikam tathā eva kalpanā anatikrameṇa tam vyavahāram artha bheda āśraya manya vyāvṛtti viṣayam anādi vāsanāyāḥ udbhūtam yathā tattvena vikalpa upagatāḥ pratipannā vyavaharttāraḥ laukikam bauddham artham śabda pratipāditan na bādhante vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgāt 
[496,viii_496,x]	katham punar ddharma bhedaḥ vyavahriyate iti āha tat phalaḥ atad phalaḥ ca arthaḥ bhinnaḥ ekaḥ tatas tatas taiḥ taiḥ upaplavaiḥ nīta sañcayā apacayaiḥ iva arthaḥ śabda ādiḥ tad phalaḥ śrotra vijñāna ādi hetuḥ atad phalaḥ cakṣuḥ vijñāna ādi ahetuḥ tatas gandha ādeḥ śrotra jñāna ahetoḥ tatas rūpa ādikāt cakṣuḥ vijñāna hetoḥ bhinnaḥ vyāvṛttaḥ tad tad vyāvṛtti viśiṣṭa tayā kalpita dharmi dharma nānātvaḥ paramārthataḥ ekaḥ taiḥ taiḥ upaplavaiḥ kalpita dharma bheda vidhi niṣedhayoḥ gocaraiḥ vikalpaiḥ yathākramam dharmi dharmāṇām nīcaḥ prāpitaḥ sañcayaḥ apacayaḥ ca yaiḥ taiḥ iva yathā adhyavasāyam 
[497,i_497,iii]	vastutas atadvān api sambandhāt kutaścid upanīyate dṛṣṭim bheda āśrayaiḥ tepi tasmāt ajñāta viplavāḥ bheda āśrayaiḥ vyāvṛtti viṣayaiḥ atadvān dharma bhedena tad sañcaya apacayābhyām rahitopi śabda ādi dṛṣṭim pratīta vyavahāram upanīyate vikalpāḥ tāvat vāsanā vaśāt tathā upadarśayanti vyavaharttāraḥ tu kasmāt vimṛśya na nivarttante iti āha arthe teṣām vyāvṛtti āśrayeṇa kalpita dharmāṇām kutaścid sambandhāt tad artha kriyā prāpteḥ paritoṣāt artha kriyā arthinām vyavahāriṇām dharma bhedāt yathārtha tvena vimarśāt ādaraḥ iti te vyavahartta āropya jñāta viplavā dharma bheda vidhi pratiṣedha vyavahārasya iti yathārtham eva tat manyante iti tasmāt paramārthataḥ asati eva dharmiṇi vidhi pratiṣedha vyavahārāt asatā upi sa pakṣāt vipakṣāt vā hetu nivṛttiḥ sandigdhā 
[497,iv_497,vii]	kiñca prāṇa ādeḥ sa pakṣaḥ na asti iti tatas na vyatirekaḥ iti yadi ucyate tat asaṅgatam iti āha sattā sādhana vṛtteḥ ca sandigdhaḥ syāt asat na saḥ asatvañca abhyupagamādapramāṇan na yajyate ātmanaḥ sattāyām sādhanasya prāṇa ādeḥ vṛtteḥ kāraṇāt vādi prativādinoḥ ātmā sandigdha syāt na hi asat tayā niścite arthe kaścid sādhanam āha prativādī ca tad sādhanam śṛṇvan katham asandigdhaḥ nāma ātma sandehāt ca sa pakṣaḥ na āsan tat katham ucyate sa pakṣa asatvāt na tatas vyāvṛttaḥ iti vyatirekī prāṇa ādiḥ syāt etat prativādinaḥ sātma tvena kasyāścid aniṣṭeḥ sa pakṣa abhāvaḥ ucyate nanu para abhyupagama pramāṇam apramāṇam vā pramāṇañcet nairātmyam eva tarhi siddham alam ātma sādhana upanyāsa prayāsena atha apramāṇam parasya abhyupagamāt apramāṇakāt sa pakṣa satvam ca na yujyate tasmāt 
[497,viii_497,ix]	asataḥ vyatirekepi sa pakṣāt vinivarttanam sandigdham tasya sandehāt vipakṣāt vinivarttanam asataḥ sa pakṣāt hetoḥ vyatirekepi upagamyamāne prāṇa ādeḥ sa pakṣāt vinivarttanam sandigdham tasya sa pakṣa sandehāt yadi sa pakṣa abhāvaḥ asandigdhaḥ evam hetu vyāvṛtti bhāva upyasandigdhaḥ syāt tad sandehe tasya api sandehaḥ sa pakṣāt vyāvṛtti sandehe vipakṣāt vinivarttanam prāṇa ādeḥ sandigdham 
[498,i_498,iii]	katham iti āha ekatra niyame siddhe sidhyati anya nivarttanam dvairāśye sati dṛṣṭeṣu syāt adṛṣṭepi saṃśayaḥ ekatra sa pakṣe sattvasya niyame siddhe sati anyatas vipakṣān nivarttanam sidhyati yaḥ hi pakṣaḥ eva bhavati sa niyamāt vipakṣe na bhavati yadi tu vipakṣepi syāt sa pakṣe sattā niyamaḥ vyāhanyeta 
[498,iv]	nanu sa ātmaka tvānātmaka tvābhyām dvairāśyam bhāvānām tatra nirātmakeṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu dṛṣṭaḥ prāṇa ādiḥ arthāt sa ātmakeṣu vyavatiṣṭhate iti prāṇa ādeḥ atas yuktam sa ātmaka tva anumānam iti āha dvairāśye sati bhāvānām ghaṭa ādiṣu nirātmakeṣu dṛṣṭeṣu bahulam prāṇāt āva dṛṣṭepi deśa ādi viprakṛṣṭeṣu prāṇa ādi sattā saṃśayaḥ kadācid kvacid nirātmakāḥ api prāṇa ādi yuktāḥ syuḥ bādhaka abhāvāt tathā hi 
[498,v_498,vi]	avyakti vyāpinā upyarthāḥ santi tad jāti bhāvinaḥ kvacid na niyama udṛṣṭyā pārthiva āloha lekhya vat tasyām ekasyām jātau sambhavinā upyarthāḥ dharmāḥ avyakti vyāpinaḥ niḥśeṣa tad vyakti asambhavinaḥ santiḥ tatas kvacid ghaṭa ādau nirātmake prāṇa ādiḥ nān ti iti adṛṣṭyā darśana mātreṇa samasteṣu nirātmakeṣu na prāṇa ādi abhāvasya niyamaḥ bahuṣu pārthiveṣu kāṣṭha pāṣāṇa ādiṣu loha lekhya tva darśana īpi pārthiva eva vajre aloha lekhya tva darśanepi pārthivaḥ eva vajre aloha lekhya tva vat aloha lekhyasya iva na asambhavasya niyamaḥ 
[498,vii_498,viii]	bhāve virodhasya adṛṣṭeḥ kaḥ santeham nivārayet nirātmaka tvena saha prāṇa ādeḥ virodhasya adṛṣṭeḥ nirātmakeṣu api bhāveṣu prāṇa ādeḥ bhāve sattāyām kaḥ sandeham nivārayet na hi prāṇa ādeḥ nairātmyena saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇaḥ virodhaḥ kvacid nivartti a nivarttaka bhāva anupalabdheḥ na api anyonya parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇaḥ paraspara vyavaccheda ātmaka tva abhāvāt 
[498,ix_499,i]	syāt etat nairātmya viruddhena ātmanā vyāpta tvāt prāṇa ādeḥ paramparayā nairātmyena virodhaḥ iti āha kvacid viniyamāt konyaḥ tad kārya ātma tayā sa ca tasya ātmanaḥ kārya tayā ātma tayā prāṇa ādeḥ kvacid ātmani viniyamāt niyata tvāt konyaḥ paramparayā virodhaḥ ca uktaḥ syāt tādātmya tad utpattibhyām eva kenacid kiñcid vyāpyate na anyathā 
[499,ii_499,vii]	na ca ātmanaḥ atyanta parokṣa tayā te sidhyataḥ tad kathantad nimittaka virodha sthitiḥ nairātmyāt api tena asya sandigdham vinivartanam tena sākṣāt paramparayā ca virodha abhāvena nairātmyāt vipakṣāt api śabdāt na kevalam sa pakṣāt asya prāṇa ādeḥ nivarttanam sandigdham sandigdha anvaya vyatirekaḥ prāṇa ādiḥ iti arthaḥ na asti tāvat ukta krameṇa nairātmyāt prāṇa ādi nivṛttiḥ astu nāma tathā api ātmā na anairātmyāt prasidhyati astu nāma aṅgīkārāt tathā api jīvat śarīre anairātmyāt nairātmya abhāvāt prāṇa ādima tva sādhitāt ātmā na sidhyati 
[499,viii_499,x]	yat na viruddhayoḥ eka abhāvāt anyatarasya avaśyam siddhiḥ bhati eva iti āha yena asau vyatirekasya na abhāvam bhāvam icchati yathā na avyatirekepi prāṇa ādiḥ nna sa pakṣataḥ yena kāraṇena asau vādī vyatirekasya abhāvam bhāvam anvayam na icchati yathā prāṇa ādirasataḥ sa pakṣataḥ avyatireke vyatireka abhāvepi na sa pakṣe satvena iṣṭaḥ tathā nairātmya nivṛttau api ātma bhāvaḥ jīvat śarīre na syāt 
[499,xi_499,xiii]	tasmāt sa pakṣāvyatirekī ced hetuḥ hetuḥ atonvayī na anvayya vyatirekī ced anairātmyam na sa ātmakam sa pakṣāvyatirekī prāṇa ādiḥ nairātmye nivarttamānaḥ sattām ātmanaḥ gamayan hetuḥ ced iṣṭaḥ tadā atas eva nyāyāt prāṇa ādi hetuḥ anvayī syāt sa pakṣāt prāṇa ādeḥ nivṛtti abhāvaḥ eva bhāvaḥ sa ca anvayaḥ sa pakṣāt avyatirekī vyatireka rahitaḥ prāṇa ādiḥ na anvayī ced iṣyate tadā tat vat anairātmyam nairātmya rahitam śarīraṃna sa ātmakam syāt 
[499,xiv_499,xvi]	kiñca yat na antarīyakaḥ sva ātmā yasya siddhaḥ pravṛttiṣu nivarttakaḥ saḥ eva atas pravṛttau ca pravarttakaḥ yasya sva ātmā svabhāvaḥ yat na antarīyakaḥ yat anvaya vi atireka anuvidhāyī pratibandhakasya vahni ādeḥ pravṛttiṣu vidhiṣu siddhaḥ saḥ eva nivarttamānaḥ tasya anuvihita anvaya vyatirekasya nivarttakaḥ atas pravṛtti viṣaya tvāt pravṛttau sva sattāyāñca tasya avaśyam pravṛtteḥ karttā hetuḥ bhavati yathā dhūmaḥ dahanana āntarīyaka tayā siddhaḥ dahana nivṛtti pravṛttibhyām nivarttate pravarttate ca 
[500,i_500,ii]	na antarīyaka tā sā ca sādhanam samapekṣate kārye dṛṣṭiḥ adṛṣṭiḥ ca kārya kāraṇa tā hitā sā ca na antarīyaka tā sādhanam niścāyakam mānam apekṣate gamaka tva hetu adhikāre aniścita gamaka tva nibandhasya ahetutvāt sādhanañca kārye kāraṇa anvayavati dṛṣṭiḥ tat vyatirekavati ca adṛṣṭiḥ na tu sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ darśana adarśana mātrakam hi yasmāt tad kārya dṛṣṭi adṛṣṭī kārya kāraṇa tā kāraṇa bhāva abhāva prayukte kārya bhāva abhāva darśane kārya kāraṇa tā uktā anya niścaya upāya tā darśana artham 
[500,iii_500,vii]	tatas ca artha antarasya tad bhāve abhāvāniyamataḥ agatiḥ akāraṇasya artha antarasya ātmanaḥ tasya prāṇa ādeḥ bhāve abhāva aniyamataḥ avaśi ambhāva abhāvāt agatiḥ apratītiḥ nanu ātma anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt prāṇa ādayaḥ ātmānam tad kāryatayā anumāpayiṣyanti iti āha abhāva asambhavāt teṣām abhāve nitya bhāvinaḥ 
[500,viii]	tasya ātmanaḥ nitya bhāvinaḥ sarva kāla sthāyinaḥ kadācid abhāve sati teṣām prāṇa ādīnām abhāvasya asambhavāt yadi vyatirekam antareṇa anvaya mātrāt ātma kārya tā prāṇa ādīnām tadā kāla akāla ādi kārya tā api syāt yā yasya samāna tvāt tatas ca tān api anumāpayeyuḥ kāla ādi nivṛttiḥ ca prāṇa ādi nivṛttyā vyāpyate tatas yatra prāṇa ādi nivṛttiḥ asti tatra kāla ādi nivṛttiḥ api syāt evam vyāpya sadbhāvāt na ca kāla rahitaḥ kaścid asti 
[500,ix_500,x]	kiñca kārya svabhāva bhedānām kāraṇebhyaḥ samudbhavāt taiḥ vinā bhavataḥ nyasmāt tad jam rūpam katham bhavet kārya svabhāva bhedānām yathā svam kāraṇebhyaḥ samudbhavāt kāraṇāt kevalāt anvayāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvepi kārya bhāva aṅgīkārāt taiḥ kāraṇaiḥ vinā bhavataḥ kāryasya rūpam tad jam katham bhavet na hi vahnijam yuktam pratyekam vyabhicāra ādeḥ hetu tva prasaṅgāt 
[501,i_501,ii]	sāmagrī śakti bhedāt hi vastūnām viśva rūpa tā sā ced na bhedikā prāptam eka rūpam idam jagat sāmagrīṇām śakti bhedāt hi vastūnām kāryāṇām viśva rūpa tā nānā ātma tā sāmagrī ced sva bhedena kāryāṇām na bhedikā jagat idam eka rūpam prāptam 
[501,iii_501,v]	nanu kāraṇāni kāryaṇāni kārya mātrāṇi janayanti na teṣām para sparataḥ bhedam api tatas dhūmaḥ pāvakāt iva śakra mūrdhnopi jāyeta iti āha bhedaka abhedaka tve syāt vyāhatā bhinna rūpa tā ekasya nānā rūpa tve dve rūpe pāvaka itarau asyāḥ sāmagrayā bhedaka tve bhinna tve bhinna sāmagrī kārya vilakṣaṇa kārya janaka tve abhedaka tve ca sāmagrayantara kārya janaka tve abhyupagamyamāne ekasyāḥ sāmagrayā bhinna rūpa tā nānā ātmā abhyupagatā syāt sā ca vyāhatā tathā hi dhūma agni ādi sāmagrī sāmagrayantara kārya vilakṣaṇam janayantī tasya bhedikā pratītā yadi ca sāmagrayantara kāryam ca sā janayet tadā abhedikā ca syāt tathā ca ekasya śakra mūrdhnaḥ nānā rūpa tve dve rūpe pāvaka itarau syātām dhūma janaka tvāt vahni tvam vilakṣaṇa rūpa tvāt ca avahni rūpa tvam na ca ete ekasya yukte rūpa bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt vastu bhedasya 
[501,vi_502,i]	tat tasyāḥ jananam rūpam anyasya yadi sā eva sā tat tasmāt tasyāḥ śakra mūrddha ādi sāmagrayā jananam dhūma utpādakam rūpam yadi vidyate tadā sā eva dahana ātmikā eva sā śakra mūrddha ādi sāmagrī agni dhūmayoḥ anvaya vyatireka darśanāt saḥ eva agniḥ yaḥ dhūmajanakaḥ saḥ eva dhūmaḥ yaḥ agni janyaḥ iti niścita tvāt na tasyāḥ jananam rūpam tat tasyāḥ saṃbhavet katham atha tasyāḥ śakra mūrddha ādi sāmagrayā jananam rūpam na asti iti tadā tat dhūma ākhyam rūpam vahni janyam asyāḥ katham saṃbhavet na hi adhūma hetorddhūma janma yuktam yatas dhūma janakaḥ eva vahniḥ vahni janyaḥ ca dhūmaḥ 
[502,ii_502,iii]	tatas svabhāvau niyatau anyonyam hetu kāryayoḥ tasmāt sva dṛṣṭau iva tat dṛṣṭe kāryā ipi gamyate tatas hetu kāryayoḥ agni dhūma ādyoḥ svabhāvau niyatau anyonyam tad janakatva tat bhāvi tvābhyām tasmāt kāraṇa kāryayoḥ niyamāt avyabhicāra hetoḥ yathā svasya kāraṇa ātmanā vahneḥ dṛṣṭau tad kāraṇa tvam gamyate tadvat sākṣāt darśana abhāve kāryā ipi dhūme dṛṣṭe tad kāraṇe parokṣam anumāna buddhyā gamyate sākṣāt paraṃparayā vā tad utpannena jñānena pratīyamānasya vyabhicāra abhāvāt 
[502,iv_502,vi]	ekam katham anekasmāt kleda vat dugdha vāriṇaḥ na yadi ekam ekasmāt eva bhavati tadā ekam kāryam katham anekasmāt bhavati udāharaṇam āha kleda vat taṇḍula ādi avayava śaithilyam iva dugdhāt vāriṇaḥ ca agni sahakāri dugdham vāri ca svayam pṛthak taṇḍula ādeḥ viklittim janayat dṛśyate drava śakteḥ yatas kledaḥ sā tvakā eva dvayoḥ api 
[502,vii_502,viii]	ayuktam etat anyaḥ hi dugdhena janitaḥ kledaḥ anyaḥ ca vāriṇā rasa vīrya pariṇāma ākāra bhedāt tat katham ekasmāt aneka utpādaḥ atha sati api avāntara bhede vijātīya vyāvṛttyā kledaḥ ekaḥ ucyate tadā dugdha vāriṇoḥ yato yasyāḥ dravya janikāyāḥ śakteḥ kledaḥ jāyate sā śaktiḥ tu dvayoḥ api vijātīya vyāvṛtteḥ ekā eva tat katham anekasmāt eka utpattiḥ 
[502,ix_502,xi]	bhinna abhinnaḥ kim asya ātmā bhinnotha drava tā katham abhinnā iti ucyate buddheḥ tad rūpāyāḥ abhedataḥ yadi dugdhasya kleda janana śakti ātma tayā vāriṇā saha abhedaḥ iṣyate tadā bhinna abhinnaḥ asya ātmā kim abhyupagantavyaḥ śakti ātma tayā abhedāt ākāra bhedāt ca bhedāt uttaram āha na bhinna abhinnaḥ ātmā kintu bhinnaḥ eva kathantarhi dvayoḥ api dravatā abhinnā kleda hetuḥ iti ucyate drava tu asya abhedāt abheda uktiḥ bheda uktyā virudhyate 
[503,i]	yadi nāma sva svabhāva sthita tvāt bhāvānām bhedaḥ eva pāramārthikaḥ tathā api kecid bhāvāḥ bhinnāḥ api sva hetu bala āyāta sva rūpa viśeṣāt eka kārya kṛtaḥ iti buddheḥ vikalpikāyāḥ tad rūpāyāḥ eka pratyavamarśa ākārāyāḥ abhedataḥ kāraṇāt drava tā kleda hetuḥ abhinnā iti ucyate tad eka vyāvṛtti viṣayasya avasāyasya anurodhāt eka tva vyavahāraḥ na pāramārthikaḥ iti arthaḥ 
[503,ii_503,iii]	tadvat bhedepi dahanaḥ dahana pratyaya āśrayaḥ yena aṃśena adadhat dhūmam tena aṃśena tathā gatiḥ tadvat kṣīrodaka vat avāntara bhede sati api dahanaḥ yena aṃśena svabhāvena svarūpa uṣṇa sparśa ādi ātmakena anagni vyāvṛttena dahanaḥ iti pratyayasya vyavahārasya śrayaḥ viṣayaḥ tena svabhāvena dhūmam ādadhat janayat dhūma āśrayaḥ bhavati tena dhūma āśraya tvena kāraṇena dhūma āliṅgāt dahanaḥ hetuḥ tathā anagni vyāvṛtti tvena gamyate 
[503,iv_503,vi]	tathā hi dahana pratyaya aṅgāt eva anya apekṣāt samudbhavāt dhūmotat vyabhicārī iti tadvat kāryam tathā aparam dahana pratyayasya aṅgāt nimittāt eva agni lakṣaṇāt anya apekṣāt ārdra indhana ādi sahāyāt samudabhavāt utpatteḥ kāraṇāt dhūmaḥ atat vyabhicārī iti tadvat dhūma vat aparam api kāryam tathā sva kāraṇa avyabhicāri boddhavyam 
[503,vii_503,ix]	kim punar ddhūmaḥ vahrim na vyabhicarati iti āha dhūma indhana vikāra aṅga tā pade dahana sthiteḥ anagniḥ ceda dhūmaḥ asau sa dhūmaḥ ced sa pāvakaḥ dhūmasya indhana vikāra ādeḥ aṅgam hetuḥ tasya bhāvaḥ dhūma indhana vikāra aṅga tā tasyāḥ pade āśraya vastuni dahana sthiteḥ agni tā vyavahārāt śakra mūrdhā anagniḥ ddhūma indhana vikāra kārī na ced iṣyate tatas jāyamānaḥ padārtha ūsau dṛśyamānaḥ adhūmaḥ vā aṣpādiḥ eva na hi agni janyaḥ anagniḥ bhavati sarvathā sāmyāt sa dhūmaḥ cediṣyate tarhi sa valmīkaḥ pāvakaḥ eva dhūma janakasya eva pāvaka tvāt deśa kāla svabhāva pratīti niyamaḥ hi bhāvānām na akasmikaḥ tathā tve ati prasaṅgāt na ca nānā hetukaḥ pratyekaḥ vyabhicāre ahetu tva prasaṅgāt tasmāt niyata hetukaḥ yadi ca anvaya vyatirekābhyām upalabdha agni kāraṇa bhāvaḥ dhūmaḥ śakra mūrdhnaḥ jāyate tadā vahneḥ eva śakramūrddhā atha anagniḥ tathā adṛśyamāna tvāt tathā sā upi na dhūmaḥ vā asi ādiḥ eva ākāra sāmyāt tu dhūma ābhaḥ tasmāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya na antarīyaka tā iti sthitam 
[504,i_504,ii]	na antarīyaka tā jñeyā yathāsvam hetu apekṣayā svabhāvasya yathoktam prāk vināśa kṛtaka tvayoḥ svabhāvasya ca hetoḥ na antarīyaka tā sādhyā avinā bhāvitā jñeyā yathāsvam yasya svabhāva hetoḥ yaḥ ātmīyaḥ tādātmya sādhakaḥ hetuḥ sādhanam tasya apekṣayā yathā prāk uktam vināśa kṛtaka tvayoḥ tādātmya sādhanam avaśyam hi kṛta kānām vināśaḥ na ca artha sāpekṣāṇām avaśyam bhāvaḥ tatas svabhāvataḥ eva kṛtakān annaśvarāṇām vināśam pratyanapekṣi tvāt iti darśitam tat eva svabhāva kāryayoḥ avyabhicāri tvāt hetu tvam na ca prāṇa ādeḥ ātma kārya tvam siddham iti katham hetu tā 
[504,iii_504,v]	nanu ayam prāṇa ādeḥ uktaḥ doṣa kalā api ācāryeṇa iṣṭaḥ iti katham gamyate iti āha ahetutva c ati nyāyaḥ sarva uyam vyatirekiṇaḥ abhyūhyaḥ śrāvaṇa tva ukteḥ kṛtāyāḥ sāmya dṛṣṭaye sarvasya āsādāraṇasya doṣa duṣṭa tvena sāmya dṛṣṭaye tulya tā upadarśanāya ācāryeṇa śrāvaṇa tvasya asādhāraṇasya yoktiḥ kṛtā tasyāḥ eva ayam vyatirekiṇaḥ prāṇa ādeḥ anyasya ca hetoḥ ahetu tva gati nyāyaḥ sarvaḥ abhyūhyaḥ 
[504,vi]	nanu yathā svabhāva kārya siddhi artham dvau hetū uktau tathā anupalabdhiḥ api vaktum yuktā hetu tvāt svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ tāvat tādātmya pratibandhāt svabhāva hetoḥ na bhidyate iti svabhāva hetuḥ nirdeśāt eva nirddiṣṭā kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhibhyāñca niṣedhya anupalabdhiḥ eva pratipādyate iti na tepi svabhāva anupalabdheḥ bhidyante udāharaṇantarhi kasmāt na uktam iti āha 
[505,i_505,ii]	hetu svabhāva nivṛttyā eva artha nivṛtti varṇanāt siddha udāharaṇa iti ukta anupalabdhiḥ pṛthak na tu trividhā api anupalabdhiḥ vipakṣāt hetoḥ kāraṇasya svabhāvasya vyāpakasya nivṛtya eva arthasya kāryasya vyāpyasya ca nivṛtteḥ varṇanāt siddha udāharaṇa iti na pṛthak uktā svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ kāraṇa vyāpaka abhā a sādhikā tayoḥ anupalabdhiḥ tu kārya vyāpya abhāva sādhanī iti trividha anupalambha uda āharaṇam siddham 
[505,iii_505,v]	upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta viṣaya tvam anupalabdheḥ viśeṣaṇam katham siddham iti ced āha tatra api adṛśyāt puruṣāt prāṇa ādeḥ anivartanāt sandeha hetu ta ākhyātyā dṛśyerthe sā iti sūcitam prāṇa ādeḥ hetoḥ adṛśyāt puruṣāt ātmanaḥ anivṛtteḥ nivṛtti asiddhe jīvat śarīre sandeha hetu tayā ākhyātyā kathanena tatra anupalabdhau api dṛśye arthe yā anupalabdhiḥ sā bhāva sādhikā na anyā iti sūcitamā cā rye ṇa yadi tu anupalabdhiḥ iti eva pramāṇam tadā atmani prāṇa ādeḥ nivṛttiḥ sidhyet tatas ca jīvat śarīre varttamānam ātmānam gamayet iti na sandeha hetuḥ syāt 
[505,vi_505,viii]	nanu yathā vyavaccheda viṣayā anupalabdhiḥ tathā kārya svabhāvau apī iti anupalabdhiḥ eva ekaḥ hetuḥ syāt iti āha anaṅgīkṛtavastu aṃśaḥ niṣedhaḥ sādhyatenayā vastuni api tu pūrvābhyām paryudāsaḥ vidhānataḥ anayā anupalabdhyā na kevalam vastuni avastuni api niṣedhaḥ kevalaḥ na aṅgīkṛta vastu aṃśaḥ kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhibhyām vastu vyavaccheda mātram abhāva vyavahāraḥ ca sādhyate yathā pradeśe dharmiṇi ghaṭa abhāvaḥ pūrvābhyām kārya svabhāvābhyām tu anya vyavacchede na ekasya vidhānataḥ paryudāsaḥ sādhyate yathā anagni vyavacchedena agniḥ nitya vyavacchedena anitya tvam 
[505,ix_505,xi]	nanu svabhāva anupalabdhau katham tādātmyam pratibandhaḥ iti āha tatra upalabhyeṣu asti tvam upalabdheḥ na ca aparam tatra upalabhyeṣu bhāveṣu vicāryamāṇam astitvam upalabdheḥ aparam na bhavati yadi hi upalabdhiḥ karma dharmaḥ tadā upalabhyamāna tā astitvam atha kartṛ dharmaḥ jñānam tadā tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt bhāva sattā vyavasthānasya upacārāt sā eva sattā yathā ca upalabdhiḥ eva sattā tathā anupalabdhiḥ eva asat tā iti tādātmyam anayoḥ sambandhaḥ 
[506,i_506,iii]	evam tarhi anupalabdhiḥ eva abhāva siddhiḥ iti alam liṅgi liṅga bhāvena iti āha ityajña jñāpanāya eka anupākhyā udā hṛtiḥ matā abhāvaḥ siddha tvāt na sādhana arhaḥ tasmāt abhāvam paśyatā upya vyavaharataḥ ajñasya mūḍhasya jñāpanāya abhāva vyavahārāya ekā svabhāva anupalambha uda āhṛtiḥ matā sā ca anupalabdhiḥ anupākhyā vastutas abhāva ātmikā 
[506,iv_506,vi]	yadi abhāvaḥ svabhāva anupalabdhyā na sādhyate kintarhi sādhyate iti āha viṣaya asattvataḥ tatra viṣayi pratiṣidhyate jñāna abhidhāna sandeham yathā adāha āt apāvakaḥ tathā anyāḥ na upalabhyeṣu na astita anupalambhanāt tad jñāna śabdāḥ sādhyante tad bhāvāt tad nibandhanāḥ tatra svabhāva anulambhe viṣaya asa tvataḥ jñāna abhidhāna sandehānām viṣayasya asattvataḥ kāraṇāt viṣayi pratiṣidhyate kintat viṣayī iti āha jñānam abhidhānañca sandehaḥ ca jñāna abhidhāna saṃdeham sat iti jñānam sat iti abhidhānam asti na vā iti sandehaḥ ca anupalabdhi lakṣaṇāt abhāvāt niṣidhyate sattva viṣayāḥ hi sat jñāna ādayaḥ tad abhāve niṣidhyante iti nyāyyam dṛṣṭāntam āha yathā guñjā ādau vahni tva san dehe kaścid āha pāvakoyam iti dāha ādi nimittaḥ hi vahni tva vyavahāraḥ tad abhāvāt pratiṣiddhaḥ yathā upalabdheḥ anyā na astitā tathā upalabhyeṣu upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpteṣu anupalambhāt anyā na astitā na bhavati kintu anupalabdhiḥ eva nāstitvam tasmāt tad nibandhanāḥ anupalabdhi nimittāḥ tat jñāna abhidhāna vyavahārāḥ tasya anupalambhanasya bhāvāt sādhyante 
[506,vii_507,ii]	yadi anupalambhena nimittena naimittikaḥ asat jñāna ādiḥ sādhyate tadā nimitte sati naimittika bhāva niyama abhāvāt sati anupalambhe asat jñāna ādi vyavahāra aikāntikaḥ na syāt iti āha siddhaḥ hi vyavahāroyam dṛśya adṛṣṭa avasan iti tasyāḥ siddhau asan digdhau tad kāryatvepi dhī dhvanī sarvasya eva hi dṛśya adṛṣṭa avasan iti vyavahāroyam nimitta antara nirapekṣaḥ siddhaḥ tasyāḥ dṛśya adṛṣṭeḥ siddhau satyām asat iti dhī dhvanī kārya tvepi asa digdhau niyata pravarttanau siddhau yadi api kāryam na kāraṇena niyata bhāvam tathā api yadi kvacid bhāva vyavahāraḥ pravarttyate tadā anupalabdhi māna nimitta tvāt anyatra api anupalabdhau satyām sa pravarttanīyaḥ iti arthaḥ 
[507,iii_507,iv]	vidyamānepi viṣaye mohāt atra ananubruvan kevalam siddha sādharmyāt smāryate samayam paraḥ abhāva vyavahārasya viṣaye dṛśya adarśane vidyamānepi kevalam mohāt asat jñāna śabda vyavahārān ananubruvan na anuvadan paraḥ asat vyavahāra viṣaya tayā siddhena ghaṭena dṛṣṭāntena dṛśya adarśana vattāyāḥ sādharmyāt samayam vyavahāram smāryate pūrvam api tvayā dṛśya adarśana mātrakaḥ asat vyavahāraḥ pravarttitaḥ tad sadbhāvāt iha api pravarttayā iti paraḥ pratipādyate 
[507,v_507,vii]	dṛṣṭāntam āha kārya kāraṇa tā yadvat sādhyate dṛṣṭi adṛṣṭitaḥ kārya ādi śabdāḥ hi tayoḥ vyavahārāya kalpitāḥ kārya kāraṇa tā dṛṣṭi adṛṣṭitaḥ darśana adarśanābhyām anvaya vyatireka grāhakābhyām yadvat sādhyate na hi vastutas darśana adarśanābhyām anyā kārya kāraṇa tā kintu tayoḥ darśana adarśanayoḥ hi saṃkṣepeṇa vyavahārāya kārya ādi śabdāḥ kalpitāḥ tatas ca 
[507,viii_507,ix]	kāraṇāt kārya saṃsiddhiḥ svabhāva antargamāt iyam hetu prabheda ākhyāne na darśita udāhṛtiḥ pṛthak kāraṇāt dṛśya adarśanāt asat jñāna śabda vyavahāra kārya yogya tā saṃsiddhiḥ svabhāva hetau antargamā atra hetu antaram tena iyam svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ hetunā prabhedasya ākhyāne kriyamāṇe svabhāva hetunā eva darśita udāhṛtiḥ na pṛthak nirddiṣṭā 
[507,x_508,ii]	bhavatu tāvat dṛśya anupalabdheḥ asat vyavahāra yogya tā siddhiḥ sā eva tu katham sidhyati iti āha eka upalambha anubhavāt idam na upalabhe iti buddheḥ upalabhe vā iti kalpikāyāḥ samudbhavaḥ eka jñāna saṃsargiṇaḥ ekasya pradeśa saya upalambha anubhavāt sva samvedanāt anantaram ghaṭa ādi na upalabhyate idam pradeśa ubhyupala bhyatas iti kalpikāyāḥ buddheḥ sva vedana viṣayī kṛta vidhi pratiṣedha anukāriṇyāḥ samudbhavaḥ bhavati iti sva samvedanā t eva anupalambha siddhiḥ 
[508,iii_508,v]	bhavatu jñānam sva samvedana viṣayayoḥ jñānayoḥ anyonya bhedaḥ tu kena jñāyate iti āha viśeṣaḥ gamyate arthānām viśiṣṭāt eva vedanāt tathābhūta ātma saṃpattiḥ bheda dhī hetuḥ asya ca arthānām viśeṣaḥ anyonyam bhedaḥ gamyate viśiṣṭa pratiniyata ākārāt eva vedanāt asya samvedanasya tayoḥ bheda aniyata ākāra tvam tasya dhiyaḥ samvedanasya tu sādhanaṃtathā bhūtā pratiniyata ākārā para nirapekṣa prakāśa ātma saṃpattiḥ aparokṣa tā 
[508,vi_508,vii]	tasmāt svatas dhiyoḥ bheda siddhiḥ tābhyām tad arthayoḥ anyathā hi anavasthātaḥ bhedaḥ sidhyet na kasyacid tasmāt dhiyaḥ bhedasya svatas pratiniyatāt aparokṣa prakāśāt svarūpataḥ eva siddhiḥ tābhyām bhinna tayā siddhābhyām tayoḥ arthayoḥ sārūpya janakayoḥ bheda siddhiḥ anyathā yadi evam na iṣyate tadā aparābhyām bheda siddhiḥ vaktavyā tayoḥ ca bheda siddhau bheda grāhaka tā yuktā iti tad bheda grāhakam aparam dvayameṣṭavyam evam apara apara apekṣāyām anavasthātaḥ na kasyacid bhedaḥ sidhyet 
[508,viii_508,ix]	viśiṣṭa rūpa anubhavāt anyathā anya nirākriyā tad viśiṣṭa upalambhotaḥ tasya api anupalambhanam atas viśiṣṭasya niyatasya rūpasya anubhavāt an yathā anyasya nirākriyā na bhavati atas tasmāt pratiṣedhyāt viśiṣṭasya bhinnasya pradeśa ādeḥ upalambhaḥ tasya pratiṣedhyasya api anupalambhanam 
[509,i_509,ii]	tasmāt anupalambhoyam svayam pratyakṣataḥ gataḥ sva mātra vṛtteḥ gamakaḥ tad abhāva vyavasthiteḥ tasmāt ayam jñāna ātmakā anupalambhaḥ svayam ātmanā pratyakṣatas sva samvedanād gataḥ pratītaḥ san sva mātra vṛtteḥ ātma mātra pratītāyāḥ tasya anupalabhyamānasya abhāva vyavasthiteḥ gamakaḥ anupalambhaḥ hi nimittam viṣayaḥ vā abhāva vyavahārasya iti ubhayathā api sva sattā mātreṇa abhāva vyavahāra hetuḥ 
[509,iii_509,iv]	anyathā arthasya nāstitvam gamyatenu palambhataḥ upalambhasya na astitvam anyena iti anavasthitiḥ anyathā yadi svatas na anupalambha siddhiḥ tadā arthasya na astitvam anupalambhaḥ tatas gamyate upalambhasya na astitvam anupalabdhiḥ anyena anupalambhena gamyate sa upyanapalambha antareṇa iti apekṣāyām anavasthitiḥ syāt 
[509,v_509,vii]	bhavatu tāvat dṛśyeṣu anupalabdhau abhāva pratītiḥ adṛśye punar katham iti āha adṛśye niścaya ayogāt sthitiḥ anyatra bādhyate yathā aliṅgaḥ anya sattveṣu vikalpa ādiḥ na sidhyati anyatra dṛśya anupalabdhau satyām adṛśye viṣaye abhāva niścaya ayogāt sat vyavahārasya sthitiḥ bbādhyate upalambha pūrvaka tvāt tasyāḥ yathā anyeṣu sattveṣu prāṇiṣu rāga ādi viṣayaḥ vikalpaḥ para citta jñāna ādiḥ ādinā aliṅgaḥ liṅga rahitaḥ sat vyavahāra viṣaya tvena na sidhyati 
[509,viii_509,xii]	kim punar adṛśya anupalabdhau satyām api na sidhyati iti āha aniścaya phalāḥ hi eṣā na alam vyāvṛtti sādhane eṣā hi sati api arthe sambhavantī abhāvasya aniścayaphalā tasmāt vyāvṛtteḥ abhāvasya sādhane na alam śaktā ādya adhikriyate hetoḥ nniścitena eva sādhane ādyā dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ punar vyāvṛtti sādhane adhikriyate kasmāt iti āha hetoḥ vipakṣāt kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhibhyām vyāvṛtteḥ niścitena eva sādhya artha sādhane adhikārāt na hi vipakṣāt aniścita vyāvṛttikaḥ hetuḥ gamakaḥ na hi kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhibhyām anyaḥ vyāvṛtti sādhanaḥ kāraṇa viruddha upalambha ādiṣu api kāraṇa abhāvāt abhāvaḥ pratipādyaḥ 
[510,i_510,ii]	tasyāḥ svayam prayogeṣu svarūpam vā prayujyate artha bādhana rūpam vā bhāve bhāvāt abhāvataḥ tasyāḥ anupalabdheḥ prayogeṣu svayam śabda pratipāditam vā svarūpam prayujyate yathā svabhāva kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhi ādiṣu niṣedhyasya arthasya bādhanam viruddham vā prayujyate yathā svabhāva kāraṇa vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhi ādiṣu prayujyate iti āha avikala kāraṇa tayā śītasya bhāve sattāyām satyām dahanasya bhāvāt abhāvataḥ nivṛtteḥ yathā śīta abhāva sādhane saha anavasthāna viruddhaḥ vahneḥ prayujyate na atra śīta sparśaḥ vahreḥ iti 
[510,iii_510,iv]	anyonya bheda siddheḥ vā dhruva bhāva vināśa vat pramāṇa antara bādhāt vā sa apekṣa dhruva bhāva vat niṣedhya vidhīyamānayoḥ anyonyasya abhāva ātma tayā bheda siddheḥ vā artha bādhana rūpam prayujyate dhruva bhāva vināśa vat nitya tva anitya tvayoḥ anyonya abhāva ātmaka tvena bheda siddhau paraspara parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇa tayā viruddham vināśi tvam nitya tva bādhane prayujyate yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ vināśi tvāt sa ca ayam paraspara parihāra sthiti viruddhaḥ kvacid sākṣāt vā prayujyate yathā nitya tvasya vināśi tvam kvacid dharma antara virodha grāhiṇā pramāṇa antareṇa paramparayā bādhanāt abādhita viruddha bhāvaḥ vā prayujyate sa apekṣa dhruva bhāvi tva vat yathā sa apekṣa dhruva bhāvayoḥ sākṣāt virodha abhāvepi dhruva bhāvi tvasya yat vyāpakam tena viruddham sa apekṣa tvam vyāpya vyāpakayoḥ ca vastutas tādātmya ādayaḥ yat vyāpake virudhyate sa tat vyāpyena api iti pramāṇa antara bādhanāt eva avadhṛta viruddha bhāvam sa apekṣa tvam dhruva bhāvi tva bādhane prayujyate yathā na dhruva bhāvī kṛtakasya vināśaḥ hetu antara sāpekṣa tvāt iti 
[510,v]	kasmāt punar hetu antarasā apekṣaḥ na dhruva bhāvi iti āha 
[511,i_511,v]	hetu antara samutthasya sannidhau niyataḥ kutas utpādakāt hetoḥ hetu antara samutthasya dharmasya sannidhau sannidhāne niyataḥ kutas yathā kāraṇa antara sāpekṣasya vāsasi na avaśyaṃbhāva niyamaḥ rāgasya syāt etat bhāva hetuḥ eva anitya tva ākhyam dharmam bhāva nāśakam janayati tena naśvara svabhāva niyataḥ bhāvaḥ iti āha bhāva hetu bhava tve kim pāramparya pariśramaiḥ bhāva hetu bhava tve anitya tva ākhyasya dharmasya bhāva nāśakasya iṣyamāṇe pāramparye pariśramaiḥ ebhiḥ svīkṛtaiḥ kim prayojanam 
[511,vi_511,viii]	tathā hi nāśanam janayitvā anyam sa hetuḥ tasya nāśakaḥ tam eva naśvaram bhāvam janayet yadi kimbhavet sa bhāva hetuḥ anyam anitya tva ākhyam dharmam bhāva nāśanam janayitvā tasya abhāvasya na aśakaḥ iṣyate paraṃparayā yadi tu tam eva naśvaram bhāvam sākṣāt bhāva hetuḥ janayet tadākiṃndūṣaṇam bhavet na kiñcid 
[511,ix_511,xi]	api ca ātma upakārakaḥ kaḥ syāt tasya siddha ātmanaḥ sataḥ na ātma upakārakaḥ kaḥ syāt tena yaḥ samapekṣyate yaḥ yāvān anitya tva ākhyaḥ dharmaḥ ātmā bhāvasya sa kim upakārakaḥ san vināśakaḥ bhāvasya uta anupakārakaḥ eva tatra ādye pakṣe siddha ātmanaḥ bhāvasya sataḥ sarvatas nirāśaṃsi asya kaḥ ātmā anitya ākhyaḥ dharmaḥ anyaḥ vā upakārakaḥ syāt atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā anātmā upakārakaḥ syāt tena bhāvena yaḥ na aśaka tvena samapekṣyeta upakārakaḥ eva hi apekṣyate anupakāraka tve kā tasya apekṣā na aśaka tā vā 
[512,i_512,iii]	atha nāśa hetu ayogāt anapekṣyaḥ eva bhāvaḥ naśvara tāyām tadā anapekṣaḥ ca kimbhāvaḥ atathābhūtaḥ kadācana yathā na kṣepa bhāj iṣṭaḥ saḥ eva udbhūta nāśakaḥ anapekṣaḥ ca nāśe bhāvaḥ kim kasmāt kadācanā tathābhūtaḥ anaśvara svabhāvaḥ sarvadā eva naśvara svabhāva tā asya yuktā yathā tvad mate saḥ eva kṛtakaḥ bhāvaḥ udbhūta nāśakaḥ unmukha nāśaka anitya tva svabhāvaḥ nāśa kāle akṣepa bhāga cira vināśī iṣṭaḥ tathā utpāda anantaram naśvara svabhāva tayā vinaśyet iti 
[512,iv_512,v]	kṣaṇam api anapekṣa tve bhāvaḥ bhāvasya na iti ced bhāvaḥ hi sa tathā bhūtaḥ abhāve bhāvaḥ tathā katham kṣaṇa kṣayi svabhāvāḥ bhāvāḥ sva hetoḥ eva jāyante vināśam pratyanapekṣa tve bhāvasya yathā dvitīye kṣaṇe bhāvaḥ na asti tathā prathamepi kṣaṇe na syāt iti kṣaṇam api bhāvasya bhāvaḥ na syāt iti ced ayuktam etat hi yasmāt sa bhāvaḥ tathā naśvara svabhāvaḥ iṣyate yadā tu bhāvaḥ eva na asti tadā abhāve bhāvasya bhāvaḥ tathā naśvaraḥ katham ucyate tatas labdha janmataḥ bhāvasya kṣaṇa antarānanuvṛtteḥ naśvara tā 
[512,vi_512,viii]	tasmāt ye apara apekṣa tadbhāvāḥ tad bhāva niyatāḥ hi te asambhavat vibandhā ca sāmagrī kārya karmaṇi ye bhāvāḥ anapekṣa tadbhāvāḥ para apekṣām vinā sambhavat dharma viśeṣa saṃbhavāḥ te tasya bhāve dharmasya niyatāḥ kāraṇa sāmagrī va asambhavat vibandhāḥ vibandha kāraṇa rahitā kāryasya karmaṇi kriyāyām niyatā para nirapekṣāḥ ca bhāvāḥ sva nāśaḥ iti kṣaṇikāḥ sarva saṃskārāḥ iti akampyaḥ sau ga taḥ siṃhanādaḥ 
[512,ix_513,iii]	na yat iha tat na nyāyyam tena uditena ca kim phalam yadim bahuśas tasyāḥ vṛttau guṇaḥ katham kasya kaḥ yadi paramasau vyākhyeya artha grahasya virodhinī vivṛtti racanā mātre tasmāt kṛtotra bhaya ādaraḥ ācārya śrīmanoratha nandi kṛtāyām vārttika vṛttau caturthaḥ paricchedaḥ samāptaḥ likhitā iyam paṃḍita vibhūti candreṇa yat atra puṇyam tad bhavatu a ācārya upādhyāya pūrvaṅgam asakala satva rāśeḥ anuttara jñāna phala avāptayaḥ iti
